dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul zhal skong bcas bsdoms shing lhag par dus mchod bla brang pa'i gdung rabs kha yod lag yod du bgrangs pa gdan rabs bcas
kyi lo rgyus ngo mtshar srid na 'gran bral bzhugs/bshad par dam bca' ba/na mo gu ru tri ku la nA thA ya/mkhyen brtse nus ldan rgyal sras rigs gsum mgon/'od gsal lha dang
'khon ston sa skya pa/rab snyan mtshan 'chang gdung rabs mkhas grub la/gus pas phyag 'tshal snying po'i rnam bzhag bri/

'od gsal lha dang 'khon ston sa skya pa'i gdung rabs/gzugs khams lha gnas gsum pa 'od gsal nas/spyi ring g.yu ring g.yu se mched rnam gsum/'dzam gling mi yul spyi dang gangs
ljongs pa'i/bsod nams mgron du byon pa'i gcung po las/sras bzhi byon pa yab bcas lha yul gshegs/bar pa g.yu ring dmu bza' yab yum las/sras mchog ma sangs spun bdun gcen
po drug/yab bcas lha yul gshegs shing bdun pa ni/ma sangs spyi rje thog lcam 'ur mo'i sras/dpa' bo stag dang klu lcam dra ma'i sras/stag po 'od can 'di rnams bar snang bzhugs/de
dang mon bza' mtsho mo rgyal gyi sras/g.ya' spang skyes gcig byon rnams lha'i gdung rabs/gang des srin po skya rengs khrag med bsad/chung ma g.ya' 'brum 'phrogs
bzhes lha srin 'khon/bar du byung bas sras ni 'khon bar skyes/de dang bstan bza' lcam bu sgron gyi sras/dkon pa rje gung stag gam dpal po che/

'di yan bon lugs rjes 'brangs yin nam snyam/de dang rlangs bza' ne chung ma yi sras/klu dbang gcen dang rdo rje rin chen gcung/phyi ma'i lcam mo 'gro bza' g.yang len skyid/bzhes
par sras bdun byon pa'i gcen drug las/che ba mang yul de 'og gung thang dang/de 'og srad dang de 'og gnyal lo ro/de 'og myang shab byon las so so ru/sku brgyud 'phel
yang 'di yin ngo ma shes/bdun pa'i sku brgyud ma 'khrigs sde gsum grags/drug pa shes rab yon tan g.ya' lung bzhugs/sras gnyis chung ba khab so stag byon las/la stod byang
gi 'khon tsho 'phel zhes grags/che ba yon tan 'byung gnas sras gsum gras/tshul khrims rgyal por sras gsum bar pa ni/brdal gyi chang tshang byon zhing thog mtha' gnyis/g.ya'
lung bzhugs pa'i che ba gtsug shes la/sras bdun gcung bcas 'khon tsho brgyad ces grags/bdun pa'i lnga pa dge skyabs shab tu byon/sras gnyis byung ba'i gcung las shab
stod kyi/'khon tsho gyes shing gcen po dge mthong sras/bal po de sras shAka blo de yi sras/gcen yan 'khon gyi gdung rabs snga 'gyur bdagdpal po che nas shes rab tshul khrims
bar/

dbu bla ma nges 'on kyang klu dbang mched/mkhan chen zhi ba mtsho dang slob dpon che/padma'i zhal slob yin cing de dus kyi/mkhas grub gzhan yang yod mod 'di yin ces/gsal ba'i
lo rgyus kho bos sngar ma mthong/phyi ma shing khyi re dgu chu rtar gshegs/yab dang gcen po khyin lo 'od snang dang/bla chen shAkya ye shes bse kun rig'gos lo bsod nams
rtse mo auTyan gyi/paNDi shes rab gsang ba rma lo tsA/mal lo ba ri kha'u sku mched dang/'khon ston sgyi chu skyu ra a seng sogs/dam pa rnams las gsan pa'i pha rol phyin/bzhi
bcu'i dgung lon rgyal bstan lnga brgya pa/phrag bcu'i bdun pa mngon dus lnga brgya las/nyis brgya bdun lon chu glang khrums zla'i 'gor/sa dpyad gzigs nas gzim spyil
dkar po btabs/gu ru zhang mor lnga bcu nga dgu'i lo/chu spre sa chen kun dga' snying po 'khrungs/re bdun sa stag gshegs de'i dbu bla ni/'jam dbyangs sgrol ma mi g.yo birwa
pa/nag po gha ya nags khrod ko tra li/yab dang ba ri lo tsA dar ma snying/byang 'chad khyung dang khyung gzhan rin chen grags/me dig lhang 'tsher kha'u chos rgyal mtshan/sgyi
chu dgra lha 'bar dang mal lo tsA/spu hrang lo chung skyu ra a skyabs dang/padma shrI dznyA na badzra dang/

bha dra rA hu dge bshes rngog dang ni/zhang ston chos 'bar dpal chen rga lo sogs/lha dang mi yi dam pa du ma'o/ /gang des btsun mo gnyis bzhes dang po ni/tsha rong jo lcam
phur mor kun dga' 'bar/gnyis pa tsha rong 'od sgron bsod nams rtse/grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal chen 'od po gsum/zhal slob zhu yas paN chen grags rdor ba/zung gis tshigs bcad
mdzad pa 'di lta ste/gdul bya mtha' dag smin par mdzad pa la/zhang ston sgyi chu ba yi lung bstan ltar/tshe 'dir phyag chen thob pa rnam pa gsum/singga gling gi rnal 'byor
byang sems stag/sgom pa skyi 'bar gsum du gsal bar grags/bzod pa thob pa bdun du grags pa ni/rje btsun chen po zhu yas dngos grub dang/nang sgom bsod rgyal tshar kha'i
rnal 'byor pa/bsgom pa 'od grags dga' ston mang chung ma/gzhon nu'i sa la gnas pa'i slob ma ni/mkha' spyod dbang po bsod nams rtse mor grags/gzhan yang bdag nyid che de'i
slob ma ni/brtul zhugs grub pa dpal chen rga lo'i zhabs/byang chub sems dpa' zla ba rgyal mtshan dang/dpal ldan phag mo gru pa chen po dang/sgom pa rta rgan rnal 'byor
phag ston sogs/grub pa brnyes pa'i skyes chen du ma dang/rta

nag 'khrungs pa'i rgyal tsha tal phug pa/'u yug 'khrungs pa'i dbyar ston sbu ma ba/g.yor ston byon pa'i gshen ston rdor seng dang/yar klung 'khrungs pa'i gshen ston dgon dkar
ba/'on du byon pa'i zhang ston gsum thog pa/brag dmar zhu dang zhang ston spe dmar ba/skyu ra a skyabs de sras a seng dang/gnam du byon pa'i ne tso wal ston dang/lha brag
dkar ston lcags kyi rdo rje dang/gsang phu'i mkhas pa mdzangs ston mdza' ne dang/thugs sras dam pa bsod nams rdo rje dang/snyags ston dbang rgyal rgya sgoms tshul khrims
grags/mi nyag ston pa pradznyA dzwa la dang/kham pa rga thang 'a 'u ma la sogs/rmi lam na yang 'dod la ma chags shing/rgyud sde'i snying po rim gnyis lhur len pa'i/mkhas
grub dam pa mu mtha' bral ba yis/rgya mtsho'i gos can dpal dang ldan par byas/rga lo'i slob ma g.yu brag pa la sogs/zla rgyal slob ma nyin phug pa la sogs/phag gru'i
slob ma 'bri stag gling gsum sogs/rgyal tsha'i slob ma ri ma lce sgom sogs/a seng slob ma phyag gtsang nyang ran sogs/rje pa'i slob ma sa skya paN chen dang/grags pa'i mtha'
can brgyad la sogs pa ste/shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mtha' klas dam pa rnams/thugs rje che

ldan de yi slob brgyud lags/de sras dpal chen 'od po yab nga dgu/lcags rtar 'khrungs shing nga bzhi chu phag gshegs/yab sogs dbu bla kha shas zhal slob rnams/gsal bar ma mthong
'dir ni smos su med/gang de'i lcam mo gar phu nyi khri las/sras gnyis byon pa'i gcen po sa paN rje/gcung po bzang tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan ni/yab rje so lnga shing
'brug nga drug pa/sa phag gshegs des mkhas grub bla ma dang/zhal slob ma zin grub par bzhugs de yi/btsun mo lnga dang tsha sna kun skyid sras/chos rgyal 'phags pa 'gro
mgon phyag na gnyis/phyag na'i btsun mo mam gal chos 'bum dang/zha lu mkha' 'gro 'bum gsum phyi ma'i sras/dharma phA la de lcam dpal stag gnyis/phyi mar ratna bha dra sras
su bltams/bzang tsha'i btsun mo gnyis pa chu mdo ma/jo 'gror rin chen rgyal mtshan lcam bcas byung/gsum pa gung thang lha gcig mdzes ma las/bsod 'bum nyi 'bum zhes pa'i
lcam gnyis so/ /bzhi pa g.ya' lung hor lcam sras mo gcig/lnga pa mdzes ma'i nye gnas rdo rje gdan/zhes par yab rje nga lnga sa khyi lor/ye shes 'byung gnas 'khrungs shing
so bdun pa/shing khyir gshegs de'i dbu bla zhal slob rnams/ma nges btsun mo khab

smad 'bum me las/dgung grangs nyer lnga chu pho khyi lo la/bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal bltams nas/re gsum shing byi bar bzhugs dbu bla ni/rje btsun sgrol ma 'phags pa rin
po che/la sogs du ma'i bdud rtsi bzhes yod snyam/zhal slob rigs dang chos 'khrungs mang yod kyang/rkang grangs smos pa re zhig ma mthong ngo/ /sman tse ma dang lung phud
btsun mo drug/sman tse ma la sras gcig chung ngur gshegs/lung phud dang po rgyal lcam mu da gan/bsod nams bzang po lcam sring gnyis kyi yum/bsod bzang btsun mo buddha
gan gyi sras/ratna bha dra lung phud gnyis pa ni/mang mkhar sog spe ngang mor bla chen pa/ti shrI kun dga' blo gros byon pa ste/spyi la dbang sgyur gdung rabs zhes su grags/bzhi
thog bla brang gi gdung rabs/de las gyes pa bzhi thog gdung rabs ni/lung phud gsum pa glang mtsho na spe ma/nam mkha' rgyal mor yab rje zhe bzhi pa/shing sbrul mkhas
btsun nam mkha' legs 'khrungs

nas/so dgu chu lug bar bzhugs dbu bla ni/yab dang mkhas pa nor bzang dpal la sogs/zhal slob chos rje bla ma dam pa sogs/de gcung bgres pa nam mkha' bshes gnyen dang/gzhon pa
nam mkha' rgyal mtshan rnam gnyis so/ /mkhas btsun btsun mo ngam ring khang gsar ma/dge 'dun 'bum la yab rje so lnga pa/sa yos kun dga' rin chen sa yos bar/re gcig bzhugs
des chos rje bla ma dang/mnyam med grags rgyal zhang ston dbang phyug rgyal/mgon rgyal 'jam sngon gung ru shes rin sogs/bsten nas mdo sngags sbyangs shing zhal slob kyang/mang
du byung 'dra btsun mo gnyis bzhes sngon/nyi thog nam par blo gros rgyal mtshan te/de yi btsun mo sa skya rgyal mo skyid/kun dga' dbang phyug yum yin gnyis pa ni/mnyam
med dbon mo ma gcig dge ma la/grags pa blo gros kun dga' blo gros dang/lcam gcig 'khrungs shing grags blo'i btsun mo ni/brag dkar ma la blo gros dbang phyug ste/bzhi
thog bla brang pa yi gdung rabs so/ /

rin chen sgang bla brang gi gdung rabs/de nas bla brang rin chen sgang gdung rabs/lung phud btsun mo drug pa zha lu ma/gzhon nu 'bum sras kun dga' nyi ma dang/don yod rgyal
mtshan bsod nams rgyal mtshan gsum/don yod rgyal mtshan yab rje zhe dgu pa/lcags khyir 'khrungs shing so lnga shing sprer gshegs/yab dang bsod nams grags pa dpal ldan seng/dpang
lo grags pa sengge bsod nams dpal/rgyal sras thogs med chos dpal bzang sogs bsten/tshogs chos gsungs pas zhal slob shin tu mang/btsun mo zha lu yon tan dpal 'bum
la/nyi zla rgyal mtshan rnam gnyis phyi ma la/bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhes grags de/yab rje so lnga shing sprer 'khrungs nas su/sa khyi don lnga'i bar bzhugs dbu
bla ni/chos rje bla ma mnyam med grags rgyal sogs/zhal slob sa bzang 'phags pa kun bkras sogs/btsun mo zha lu nam mkha' rgyal mo las/yab rje nga lnga sa stag 'jam dbyangs
che/nam mkha' rgyal mtshan

'khrungs shing don lnga pa/chu 'brug gshegs des yab dang theg chen rje/bsod nams rgyal mchog rdo rje rgyal mtshan sogs/bsten cing zhal slob gdung sras sku mched sogs/gcung
po bdag chen zha lu bsod rgyal ba/lcam mo gnyis dang btsun mo khro mda' ma/dpal 'byung rgyal mor lcam bzhi sras che ba/rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan chung ba ni/bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang dbang blo gros mtshan/bdag chen zha lu'i btsun mo ldan yul ma/kun dga' 'bum la grags pa rgyal mtshan te/bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs so/ /lha
khang bla brang gi gdung rabs/de nas lha khang bla brang gdung rabs ni/lung phud btsun mo bzhi pa sha zug ma/kun dga' nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan ma yi sras/kun dga' legs pa'i
'byung gnas zhes bya dang/kun dga' rgyal mtshan gnyis las phyi ma 'di/yab rje zhe dgu lcags khyi zhe dgu pa/sa khyi bar bzhugs dbu bla zhal slob rnams/ma nges btsun mo
gnyis dang kha char ma/dpal

ldan bzang mor yab rje nyer gsum pa/chu sprer chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'khrungs nas ni/nyer brgyad sa phag gshegs de'i dbu bla dang/zhal slob ma gsal gcung po blo rgyal ni/btsun
mo gnyis pa ra lung bsod dpal sras/chos rgyan btsun dang chu mdo rgyal mo mtshor/theg chen rje dang btsun mo gnyis pa ni/nyang stod sras skyabs dharma dhwa dza dang/rdo
rje rin chen rnam gnyis gsum pa ni/lho pa dpal ldan 'bum las bsod bkras rje/yab nyid nyer gcig chu 'brug lor 'khrungs shing/nga drug me phag gshegs des bzhi thog bdag/kun
dga' rin chen sa bzang ma ti dang/chos rje bla ma sogs bsten zhal slob mang/byang mo ma gcig nam par yab gshegs pa'i/phyi lo sa byir bde legs bkra shis 'khrungs/dgung
grangs dbu bla zhal slob mi gsal zhing/byang bdag sras mo mtshan dngos mi gsal bar/bsod nams rgyal mtshan shAkya seng ge dang/don grub rgyal mtshan bsam grub rgyal mtshan
bzhi/shAkya seng ge'i btsun dang gcung dpon mor/kun bkras kun rgyal kun dga' snying po gsum/gnyis pa ma gcig yum par rin rgyal mtshan/sku mched mtshan byang 'dra ba rnam
gnyis bltams/kun dga' rgyal mtshan btsun mo gling kha dpon/

dkar mor chos kyi rgyal mtshan kun dga' legs/lha khang bla brang pa yi gdung rabs so/ /dus mchod bla brang gi gdung rabs/de nas dus mchod bla brang gdung rabs ni/lung phud
lnga pa re mda' nyi rin la/nyi dpal lcam gcig kun dga' legs 'byung gsum/phyi ma yab rje zhe bdun sa sprer bltams/nyer dgu me byir gshegs de'i bla slob rnams/mi gsal btsun
dang gung thang kun skyong mar/lcam gcig gnyis pa ngam ring dge 'bum mar/bsod nams blo gros sku 'bring chung ngur gshegs/grags pa rgyal mtshan rnam gsum byon pa las/grags
rgyal yab rje gshegs pa'i me byir bltams/zhe gnyis sa sbrul gshegs des chos rje dang/gcen dang brag phug mnyam med la sogs bsten/zhal slob mi gsal btsun dang lha ring mar/kun
dga' legs blo rnam sras rgyal mtshan mched/gnyis pa stag tshang sras 'dren chos rgyal yum/rnam sras rgyal mtshan yab rje nyer lnga pa/lcags byir 'khrungs shing zhe
dgu sa

byir gshegs/chos rje bla ma bsod blo dpal ldan pa/bsten cing zhal slob mi gsal btsun dang ni/rta nag gru gur legs blo gnyis pa ni/yang 'brog bsod nams 'bum las yab bzhi bcu/sa
yos nam legs 'khrungs nas zhe drug pa/shing byir gshegs des 'brom ston seng ge sogs/bsten cing zhal slob du ma yod dam snyam/sku mched gtogs pa'i lcam lnga btsun dang
ni/yar 'brog dpal chen lcam gnyis gnyis pa ni/mi nyag btsun ma skyid la nam rgyal ba/ yab rje so bdun shing yos 'khrungs pa de/nyer dgu chu lug lor gshegs bla slob rnams/mi
gsal lcam lnga btsun dang shangs mthong smon/bgres par lcam gcig gzhon par rin rgyal ba/gsum pa gnam gling dpal 'byor bzang mo la/yab rje nyer bzhi sa stag nam bkras
'khrungs/zhe drug chu phag gshegs des stag tshang lo/shes rab rin chen mi nyag grags rdor sogs/dbu blar bzhes shing zhal slob du ma byon/btsun mo dma' ze hor mo tshe brtan
la/sa lo 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams dang/ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dpal grags pa dang/sangs rgyas tshe brtan sku mched rnam bzhi las/phyi ma yab rje so lnga chu byir
'khrungs/lnga bcu lcags

glang gshegs des mus pa rje/sangs rgyas rin chen sa lo sku mched sogs/bsten cing zhal slob du ma byon yod snyam/yar 'brog bu 'dren skyid ces khab bzhes las/gdung sras mched
gnyis byon pa'i dang po nas/phyi byon rtse gdong bla brang gi gdung rabs/phyis byon rtse gdong bla brang gdung rabs ni/bdag chen kun dga' bsam grub yab nyer bzhi/shing phag
'khrungs shing nga brgyad chu sprer gshegs/sa lo ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub dang/kun dga' legs grub sman sding lo chen sogs/bsten cing zhal slob du ma bskrun yod
snyam/btsun mo bde skyid gling pa ma gcig la/kun dga' bde legs yab rje so lnga pa/sa byar 'khrungs shing bzhi bcu sa byir gshegs/kun dga' legs grub kun dga' rgyal mtshan
dang/yab rje dkon mchog dpal ldan thar rtse ba/paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang thub bstan pa/byams pa rab brtan sogs bsten zhal slob mang/btsun mo rta nag bya bzang dpal bu
khrid/de

las rtse gdong khri chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs/kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub gcung bgres pa/tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang/gzhon pa 'jig rten rgya hor rnam gnyis
las/phyi ma yab rje sum cu sa stag 'khrungs/zhe brgyad shing glang gshegs des gcen bgres dang/thar rtse paN chen byams pa rab brtan dang/thub bstan mkhan chen chos kyi 'od
zer sogs/bsten cing zhal slob kha shas byung tshod dang/btsun mo stag lung nor 'dzom bu khrid las/bsod nams blo gros byams pa bsod lhun dang/ngag dbang bsod lhun gsum
las phyi ma 'di/yab rje so drug chu glang 'khrungs nas ni/re bzhi me 'brug gshegs des gcen mched dang/'jam mgon a mes zhabs sogs dam pa bsten/zhal slob kha shas btsun mo
yol gdong ma/nor bu bu khrid las 'khrungs bstan 'dzin dbang/bsod nams 'phags pa bsod nams dbang rgyal gsum/lcam gnyis byung min the tshom 'dir ma bkod/phyi ma yab rje so
gsum shing byar 'khrungs/re drug lcags stag gshegs des gcen bgres dang/ngag dbang brtan rdor sogs bsten slob kha shas/btsun mo stag lung bkra shis tshe ring la/gcen po kun
dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin

dang/gcung po ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan dang/phal mo zhig las sras bcas gsum byon zhing/nor bu rgyal mtshan btsun mo bya sgo ma/tshe ring bu khrid bzhes mod bstan gegs
kyis/yab sras lcam bcas thog la gdan sa 'thor/sku tsha nged rang kun dga' blo ming pa/bcu drug shing byir gdan sa lag 'byor skor/phyis byon rtse gdong bla brang gdung rabs
so/ /kun dga' bsam grub gcung po bka' drin can/sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po bdud kyi gshed/ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis dang/grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
'byor bzang po zhes/mtshan don mthun de yab rje nyer drug pa/me glang lor 'khrungs re brgyad shing sprer gshegs/sa lo chen po ngor chen lhun grub mtshan/'phags chen dpal
ldan bkra shis spyan snga ba/ngag dbang chos grags ngor chen sangs rgyas seng/thub bstan lha chen mkhan dang legs blo sogs/bsten cing zhal slob ris med nor 'dzin rdul/btsun
mo gsum bzhes dang po shar gling mar/sras mo gnyis dang gnyis pa gdong dga' ma/bgres pa bsod nams legs 'dzoms dkar mo las/'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po lcam gsum bcas/gsum
pa gzhon pa bkra shis dpal bu khrid/de

las yab rje zhe bdun chu phag lor/sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros zhes bya'am/mtshan gzhan bsod nams rgyal mtshan 'khrungs nas lo/nga lnga bar bzhugs me sbrul gshegs de yis/yab
dang gcen po spyan snga dkon rgyam dang/thar rtse paN chen sogs bsten zhal slob ni/nor 'dzin ma 'di ngal bar ma gyur ram/btsun mo byang bdag lha sras bsod nams ni/rgyal
mo'i mtshan las sras gnyis chung ngur gshegs/gsum pa sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug dang/bzhi pa chung ngur gshegs shing lnga pa ni/sngags 'chang kun dga' dbang rgyal
drug pa ni/sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i chos srid bstan/spel la bsam bzhin byon pa'i a mes zhabs/mtshan dngos ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams dang/grags pa rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po zhes pa'i/snyan pas kun yid 'phrog des yab rje mchog/so lnga me bya lor bltams re gsum pa/sa phag bar bzhugs khu bo sku mched dang/rtse gdong bsod nams
lhun grub gcen po gnyis/gcig chog mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang/thar rtse paN chen spyan snga kun dga' don/nags dgon sbyin grags 'bum chen kun dga' dpal/dbang phyug
rab brtan ngag

dbang chos grags sogs/bsten cing zhal slob nyi zer rdul la 'gran/sku mched gsum la sde srid lhun rtse ma'i/nye gnas tsha shod mthong smon bu sring ma/bkra shis dpal gyi bu
bskyed ces bya las/lcam gcig gdung gcig byung yang chung ngur gshegs/de nas ko chag 'gro mgon 'jigs bral ba'i/sras mo auTya na skyabs ma bzhes pa las/yab rje zhe gnyis sa
stag 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug bltams nas lo/zhe brgyad shing glang bar bzhugs de nyid kyis/yab rje ngag dbang rnam rgyal zha lu pa/rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub ka spe ba/bstan pa rab rgyas lhun grub dpal ldan pa/byang bdag bsod nams grags pa la ru ba/ngag dbang dpal bzang sogs las gsan mthar phyin/nyid kyi rigs
sras la sogs slob tshogs ni/kun gsal skar grangs lta bu'i bdag nyid des/bdag chen shar mo pad dkar bu khrid las/yab rje bcu dgu me sprer rigs kyi sras/ngag dbang kun dga'
bkra shis 'khrungs nas lo/nga drug lcags yos bar bzhugs dam pa des/'jam mgon a mes zhabs dang yab rje mchog/ngag dbang rnam rgyal bstan pa rab rgyas dang/lhun grub dpal
ldan bzang po rgyal mtshan dang/

sangs rgyas phun tshogs smin grol gling lo chen/dza lung bco brgyad chen mo la sogs las/zab rgyas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son cing/rigs sras la sogs slob grangs nyi zer
rdul/de'i gcung gzhon nu'i dus su gshegs skad dang/btsun mo dang po sngon dus rlabs bza' ma/ne chung la sogs gnyen dang dus phyis ni/si tu byang rgyal la sogs bstan dgra'i
brgyud/sne gdong bkra shis dbang mor sras mi mnga'/phyi ma sku zhang rnga sgra'i sras mo ni/mkha' 'gro 'bum nas sa skya'i sku zhang rang/bzhi tsam mdzad brgyud 'phan yul
bco brgyad pa'i/sras mo bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo zhes/dpal ldan sa skya'i gdung yum bsam bzhin du/skye ba bzhes der thog mar gdung gnyis bltams/snyigs ma'i rang mdangs
chung ngu'i dus su gshegs/de nas bdag gi bla ma rje btsun drung/yab rje lnga bcu shing byar lnga bdo'i mgon/drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma rdo rje 'chang/ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams rin chen dang/bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/mtshan don mthun bltams so bdun lcags bya'i bar/ngo mtshar rnam thar mnga' des yab rje dang/bstan
'dzin phun tshogs lha btsun kun bzang pa/bco brgyad mkhyen brtse

rab brtan stag rtse ba/byams pa lha dbang rig rigs  'dzin mchod dpon pa/dkon mchog rgyal po sgro lung mang thos dang/bsod nams chos 'phel zhes grags gong dkar ba/blo gros dbang
phyug ngor chen bsod nams bzang/thar rtse rdo rje 'chang dang thub bstan pa/byams pa tshul khrims bzang po gdan sa che'i/mkhan chen dbang phyug phun tshogs dza lung
pa/phrin las rdo rje gsang sngags bstan 'phel sogs/dam pa nyer bsten zab don bang mdzod 'dzin/thar rtse rje dang gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang/brag rtsa rje sogs bstan 'dzin grangs
med bskrun/mgon de'i btsun mo snga ma bzhad chos ma'i/sras gnyis chung ngur gshegs shing phyi ma ni/nam yang bka' drin 'khor med 'gro mgon ma/bsod nams dpal gyi dbang
mor bdag cag gi/a lce gnyis dang dkor zan rang nyid dang/nu bo sring mo nu bo sring mor bcas/bdun las drug pa'i lcam ni lcags zam pa/sgar pa'i sras mo bkra shis dbyangs
can las/'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma 'di nyid do/ /gsum pa dkor zan kun blo nga rgyal can/yab rje nyer lnga sa byar skyes nas ni/mkhas grub gdan sa'i ming 'dzin rang lo ni/bcu
gsum nas bzung da lta nga gsum pa/

lcags glang 'di'o yab rje thar rtse rje/gnas gsar rje dang brag rtsa rje btsun drung/zhe dgon rab brtan bzang dang rta nag mkhan/tshul khrims bzang dang ngor chen bsod nams
bzang/sangs rgyas ye shes dpal ldan chos skyong zhabs/gong dkar bsod nams blo gros rnam mkhyen grong/chos dbang rgya mtsho chu ri bkra shis don/kun dga' chos 'phel rin chen
bzang po ste/gong dkar rnam lnga rin chen mi 'gyur zhabs/'gro mgon mthu dbang de sras rigs 'dzin mtshan/mkhan chen dbang phun mkhan chen kun dga' zla/seng ge rgyal mtshan
sha ri mnga' bdag che/rgyal dbang bskal bzang rje dang mchog sprul zhabs/dpal ldan no min han dang 'on rgyal sras/lo nas sems dpa' chen po smin grol gling/khri chen
rin chen rnam rgyal sras mchog bcas/'bri gung rje dang bsam sdings yang zab rje/kun dga' sangs rgyas zha lu ye shes grags/dngos grub sdings dang kun dga' don gsal sogs/gus
pas bsten nas ris med chos rgyun zhus/nyams len med kyang dbang lung man ngag 'khrid/gzhon dus brtson khul slob ma bstan phan dang/btang snyoms dam nyams gsog pa grangs
med yod/gdan sa'i 'khur gyis lus sems don med

mnar/byas pa rjes med thang chad grangs su bsdad/phyi ma de 'di yong re ba'ang ga la mchis/ru thog rgyal po'i sras mo sems ma'i ngo/gzhon par bu mo gcig byung rgan par ni/lhalta'i
gdung brgyud mched byon drin can ma/rtsa brgyud bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs gyur cig/sku mched lcam ni gnya' nang sngo ra ba/'chi med dpal 'byor bzang mo 'di nyid
las/gdung brgyud chu klung chen po ltar byon nas/mkhas btsun bzang po sku tshe'i rig 'dzin can/thos bsam sgoms pas thugs grol 'chad rtsod rtsom/rje btsun gong ma'i rnam
thar khongs nges rnams/chos srid zhabs 'degs lugs zung shes yon can/lhag bsam smon lam rnam dag kho nas bteg/rang gzhan don gnyis sgrub la 'di 'dra las/ngo mtshar gzhan
yod ma yin snyan grags kyis/srid mtha'i bar du bstan 'gro'i mgon kho na/'byung bar mdzod cig bla ma yi dam dang/dam can rgya mtshor gdung dbyangs snying nas 'bod/brtse chen
mthu stobs dus las g.yel med mkhyen/de ltar rmad byung gdung rabs rgya mtsho las/ngo mtshar nying khu snying por sgril 'di lta/'jam mgon gnam lha bar pa g.yu ring dang/dmu
bza' ldem sras bdun gyi mtha' ma ni/ma sangs spyi rje thog

lcam 'ur mo'i sras/dpa' bo stag dang klu lcam dra ma'i sras/stag po 'od can mon bza' mtsho mo'i sras/g.ya' spang skyes rnams lha yi gdung rabs yin/de dang srin 'khon g.ya'
'brum si li'i sras/'khon bar skyes dang btsan lcam bu sgron sras/dkon pa rje gung stag gam dpal po che/de dang rlangs bza' ne chung ma yi sras/rdo rje rin chen 'gro bza'
g.yang lon sras/bdun gyi drug pa shes rab yon tan te/de nas dkon mchog rgyal po'i bar byon yum/sngon gyi gtam dang yig tshang ngas ma mthong/yab sras rim can smos pa 'di
lta ste/yon tan 'byung gnas tshul khrims rgyal po dang/gtsug tor shes rab dge skyabs dge mthong dang/bal po shAkya blo gros dkon mchog rgyal/rim bzhin snga ma'i sras ni phyi
rnams yin/dkon mchog rgyal po yan gyi dgung snying dang/lo grangs 'di bzhugs ma gsal dkon mchog rgyal/shing khyi re dgu chu rtar gshegs de dang/gu ra zhang mo skyid la
nga dgu pa/chu sprer sa chen 'khrungs nas re bdun pa/sa stag gshegs de'i dgung grangs bcu gcig ni/yab kyi khongs bsdus lhag ma nga drug lus/btsun mo tsha rong bgres pa
'od sgron las/yab rje nga dgu lcags rtar dpal chen 'od/'khrungs nas nga bzhi

chu phag gshegs de'i dgungs/dgu ni yab kyi khongs bsdus lhag zhe lnga/de dang gar phu nyi khri lcam la ni/yab rje so lnga shing 'brug bzang tsha 'khrungs/nga drug sa phag gshegs
de'i nyi shu bar/yab kyi khongs bsdus so drug lhag ma lus/de dang rdo rje ldan las yab nga lnga/sa khyir ye shes 'byung gnas 'khrungs nas ni/so bdun shing pho khyir
gshegs lo gnyis ni/yab kyi khongs bsdus lhag ma so lnga lus/de dang khab smad ma las yab nyer lnga/chu khyir bzang po dpal 'khrungs re gsum pa/shing byir gshegs de'i bcu
gsum yab khongs so/ /lnga bcu lhag lus de dang nyi rin mar/yab rje zhe bdun sa sprer kun legs 'khrungs/nyer dgu me byir gshegs de'i bcu bdun ni/yab khongs bcu gnyis lhag
lus me byir ni/grags rgyal bltams shing zhe gnyis me sbrul gshegs/nyer lnga lcags byir lha rin rnam sras rgyal/zhe dgu sa byir gshegs de'i lo bco brgyad/yab khongs lhag
ma so gcig lus de dang/bsod nams 'bum la yab rje bzhi bcu pa/sa yos nam mkha' legs pa 'khrungs nas lo/zhe drug shing byir gshegs de'i lo bcu ni/yab khongs lhag ma so drug
lus de dang/btsun ma skyid las yab rje so bdun pa/shing yos nam mkha'

rgyal mtshan 'khrungs nas lo/nyer dgu chu lug gshegs de'i lo bcu ni/yab kyi khongs dang lhag ma bcu dgu ni/lus dang de lcam dpal 'byor bzang mo las/yab rje nyer bzhi sa stag
lor 'khrungs pa/nam mkha' bkra shis zhe drug chu phag gshegs/lo drug yab khongs lhag ma bzhi bcu lus/de dang dma' ze bza' las yab so lnga/chu byir sangs rgyas tshe brtan
'khrungs nas lo/lnga bcu lcags glang gshegs de'i lo bcu gnyis/yab kyi khongs gtogs de lhag so brgyad lus/de dang bu 'dren skyid las yab nyer drug/me glang bstan pa'i gsal
byed sngags 'chang che/kun dga' rin chen re brgyad shing spre'i bar/nyer lnga yab kyi khongs dang lhag zhe gsum/de dang bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid las/yab rje zhe bdun
chu phag grags blo 'khrungs/nga lnga me sbrul bar bzhugs lo nyer gnyis/yab khongs lhag ma so gsum lus de dang/lha sras bsod nams rgyal mor yab so lnga/me bya 'jam mgon
a mes 'khrungs nas lo/re gsum bzhugs de'i nyer gcig yab khongs dang/lhag ma zhe gnyis lus dang auTya na skyabs/rnam gnyis las byon sa stag yab zhe gnyis/bzhes tshe 'jam dbyangs
bsod nams dbang phyug 'khrungs/zhe brgyad shing

glang gshegs de'i lo nyer gnyis/yab khongs lhag ma nyer drug lus de dang/pad dkar bu khrid las ni yab bcu dgu/me sprer ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis bltams/nga drug lcags yos
gshegs de'i lo sum cu/yab khongs lhag ma nyer drug lus de dang/bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mor yab lnga bcu/shing byar rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa 'khrungs/so bdun lcags byar
gshegs de'i dgung bdun ni/yab khongs lhag ma sum cu bzhugs dang ni/drin can bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo las/yab rje nyer lnga sa byar kho bo btsas/rab byung bcu gsum
lcags glang 'di yan la/nga gnyis 'das shing da lta nga gsum pa'i/bcu gsum yab khongs lhag ma bzhi bcur slebs/g.yu ring nas bzung dus mchod bla brang brgyud/kho bo yan du
so bzhi byon zin cing/so lnga kho bo dkon mchog rgyal po nas/da bar mi thog nyi shu'i lo sdoms ni/bdun brgya zhe bdun 'das shing zhe brgyad slebs/rang lo so lnga chu lug
gdung bgres pa/da lta bcu dgu lon dang so brgyad pa/me khyir gdung gzhon da lta bcu drug pa/'di gnyis bskal bzang bde skyid bu khrid las/legs 'khrungs de dag las byon ngag
dbang lha/ti la kar gsungs legs bshad

bye ba ni/ngag lam nas spel mkhas dbang kun dga' ba/snyan grags pas khyab la sogs 'byon 'gyur gyi/gdung rabs srid mtha'i bar du 'byung gyur cig/de ltar dus gsum ngo mtshar
gtam gyi gzhi/gangs khrod rdo rje'i gdan mchog dpal sa skya'i/gdan rabs lo grangs dad pa'i gsos bris par/chu glang nas ni chu rta sum cu'i bar/dkon mchog rgyal po nyid do
chu lug nas/lcags pho stag bar ba ri rin chen grags/lo brgyad bar mdzad lcags yos sa stag bar/bzhi bcu sa chen kun dga' snying pos mdzad/de sras bsod nams rtse mos mdzad
min la/lo rgyus sna tshogs 'dir ni chos kyi rje/bla ma dam pas lam 'bras chos 'byung ni/ngo mtshar snang ba'i rjes 'brangs sa yos nas/shing phag bar gyi lnga bcu nga bdun
lo/rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gdan sar bzhugs/me byi nas ni chu mo yos kyi bar/nyer brgyad 'jam mgon sa skya paN chen po/de nas lo grangs nyer gcig 'das bar du/gdan
sa ma bkod shar pa shes 'byung dang/'u yug rig seng dpon chen shAka bzang gsum/spyi mir bzhugs shing shing glang me stag gnyis/'phags pa rin po ches mdzad me yos nas/shing
phag bar dgu rin chen rgyal

mtshan zhes/'phags pa'i gcung pos mdzad cing me byi nas/lcags 'brug bar lnga slar yang 'phags pa nyid/lcags sbrul me phag bar du lo ngo bdun/dhar ma pha la rakShi ta yis mdzad/sa
pho byi nas me mo bya yi bar/lo bcu shar pa 'jam dbyangs rin rgyal po/sa pho khyi nas shing pho byi ba'i bar/nyer bdun bzang po dpal zhes mus srad lugs/de nas bla
brang go bzhi'i bzhi thog pa/mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pas shing glang nas/chu lug bar la bcu dgu gdan sa mdzad/rin sgang don yod rgyal mtshan shing spre nas/me khyi'i bar
gyi gdan sa lo gsum ma/me phag nas bzung chos rje bla ma yis/gdan sa mdzad kyang lo grangs re zhig med/lha khang gdung brgyud ta dben blo rgyal gyis/bco brgyad mdzad cing
bzhi thog kun rin gyis/yun ring mdzad ces grags kyang lo ma 'khod/de nas bzhi thog blo rgyal rin sgang pa/nam rgyal bzhi thog kun dga' dbang phyug dang/rin sgang rgya
gar shes rab rgyal mtshan te/'di rnams la yang lo grangs 'di song med/rin sgang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang dbang gis/nyer gnyis lo yun gdan sa mdzad nas ni/me sbrul nas ni
chu sprelsbrul bar so brgyad/sa lo 'jam dbyangs kun dga'

bsod nams bzhugs/de 'phros nas ni shing spre'i bar nga gcig/sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos bstan srog bzung/de 'phros nas ni sa glang bar lo drug/'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang
po gdan sar bzhugs/sa stag nas bzung me sbrul bar so bdun/grags pa blo gros gdan sar bzhugs nas kyang/de 'phros nas bzung sa lug bar lo gsum/sku 'bring ngag dbang kun
dga' dbang rgyal po/de 'phros nas brtsis sa phag bar zhe gcig/'jam mgon a mes zhabs bzhugs de 'phros nas/shing glang bar du nyer bdun bsod dbang phyug/de 'phros nas ni
lcags yos lo yi bar/nyer bdun ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis bzhugs/de 'phros nas bzung lcags bya lo yi bar/so gcig yab rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad/de 'phros nas ni 'di lo'i
lcags glang bar/zhe gcig rta lam bong gzung kun blo'o/ /da ni de ring tshe tshad rdzogs nas kyang/do nub 'chi'am yang na rang nyid kyi/tshe tshad bar der dus min 'chi
med na/lo shas sdod pa'ang srid do mos ldan rnams/dga' bar mdzod cig bdag la lan chags rnams/'chi dus mi 'dug sgug yun a re ring/nyams ldan 'di 'dra bdag gi gshis lugs te/tshig
sgra legs

po byung song bla ma'i drin/dpal ldan sa skya'i dgon gnas de 'dzin bcas/rmad byung lo rgyus snyan ngag gis ma sgrib/drang po'i gtam mo bzo khyad 'dir ma dgos/'dzam gling 'di
na rlung ltar grags nas 'dug/de ltar gleng la dgos pa 'dug na ni/dges par mdzod cig 'jam dbyangs thob phyir bsngo/dgos pa med na bdag gi gtam 'chol dang/sprang po'i kha
ni 'brel med yin 'dug pas/nyi ring bskyel thabs tsam du gzigs nas kyang/nyes kun mkha' mnyam sdig dang lhan bshags 'bul/rmongs mkhas kun gyis bkra shis gnang rogs zhu/sarba
mangga laM/

rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod dgos 'dod kun 'byung gi kha skong rin chen 'dzad med srid zhi'i dpal 'byor
lhun grub bzhugs so/ /mchod brjod dang bshad par dam bca' ba/oM swasti/ phyogs bcu dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi yab/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang 'phags mchog pad dkar 'dzin/ gsang
ba'i bdag po'i sgyu 'phrul rol pa'i gar/ dpal ldan sa skya'i gdung rabs rnams la 'dud/ zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po
che'i rnam

thar ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod dgos 'dod kun 'byung zhes bya ba sku drin mtshungs med sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa
de nyid du ngor chen mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i dpal sa skya'i gdung rabs tshigs bcad ma ya rabs kha rgyan rtsa 'grel gyi tshul du mdzad pa
las/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi rnam par thar pa yan gyi thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung rab dgongs 'grel yongs su
rdzogs nas/ de'i rjes su kha skong 'di ltar gsungs te/ da ni de nyid kyi kha skong cung zad brjod par bya ste/ de la yang gnyis te/ rtse gdong pa'i gdung rabs byung tshul
bstan pa dang/ dpal ldan sa skya 'di nyid du gdung rabs rgyun mi chad par byon pa'i tshul bshad pa'o/ /rtse gdong bla brang gi gdung rabs byung tshul bstan pa/dang po
la yang tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang/ de'i don cung zad phye ba gnyis las/

dang po ni/ kun dga' bsam 'grub btsun mo ma gcig sras/ kun dga' bde legs bkra shis zhes bya 'khrungs/ kun dga' bde legs btsun mo bya bzang ma'i/ sras la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
lhun grub dang/ tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang/ 'jig rten rgya hor zhes bya rnam gsum byon/ 'jig rten rgya hor btsun mo stag lung mar/ sras gsum 'khrungs
pa da lta bzhugs 'di'o/ / zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don cung zad bshad pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsam grub kyis btsun mo zhig khab tu bzhes pa la sras 'jam dbyangs kun
dga' bde legs bkra shis 'khrungs pa ni/ gzhon nu nyid nas dam pa'i skyes bu mang po las gsan pa ci rigs pa mdzad de thugs dam la brtson par bzhugs shing/ rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gis rjes su bzung bar yang grags la/ mthar dgung lo bzhi bcu bzhes pa'i tshe bde bar gshegs so/ /bdag chen des bya bzang pa'i sras mo dpal bu khrid bya ba btsun
mor bzhes pa la/ da lta dgung lo nga dgu pa'i steng na bzhugs pa'i 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub dang/ gzhon nu la gshegs pa'i tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal
mtshan zhes bya ba dang/ 'jig rten rgya hor dang

gsum 'khrungs pa de dag gis mdzad pa'i cha rnams ni so so'i rnam thar du blta'o/ /de gsum gyi nang nas gcung 'jig rten rgya hor pas stag lung pa'i sras mo khab tu bzhes pa
la sras gsum 'khrungs pa ni da lta yod pa'i gdung sras sku mched 'di dag go/ /de dag gis rtse gdong pai' gdung rabs byon tshul bstan zin nas/ zhes gsungs pas na/ 'dir de
min gyi kha skong brjod pa la/ tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang/ de'i don cung zad phye ba gnyis las/dang po ni nged rang gis brtsams pa'i sa ska skor dpon par
nye bar mkho ba'i yi ge 'gro don bzang po'i gdung rabs kha skong las/ 'jig rten rgya hor btsun mo stag lung mar/ sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i gcen po gzhon nur gshegs/ bar pa
ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang/ chung ba ngag dbang lhun grub rnam gnyis byon/ ngag dbang lhun grub btsun mo yol gdong ma/ nor bu bu khrid sras ni bstan 'dzin dbang/
bsod nams 'phags pa bsod nams dbang rgyal gnyis/ dbang rgyal sras gnyis tshe dbang rig 'dzin dang/ ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan zhes bya ste/ phyis su byon pa'i rtse
gdong bla

brang pa/ zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don cung zad bshad pa la/ spyi don dang gzhung don gnyis las/ dang po ni/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi gsung rab de nyid na/ 'jam dbyangs kun
dga' bde legs nas/ 'jig rten rgya hor gyi sras sku mched gsum gyi bar la rnam par thar pa nyung ngu las ma gsungs pas na/ de rnams la rnam thar cung zad rgyas tsam re brjod
na/ de yang gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po kun mkhyen mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng ges 'debs par mdzad pa'i dpal thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi gdan rabs bcu bzhi
pa shar mdo khams kyi paNDi ta chen po ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i rtse gdong khri chen 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub kyi rnam par thar pa yon
tan yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che'i za ma tog bkod pa las gsungs pa bzhin la cung zad kha bkang ste 'dri ba ni/ de yang lha rigs 'khon sa skya pa'i gdung rabs las rje
btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po la sras bzhi byon pa'i chung ba'i sras sku mched gnyis kyi gcung gi sras 'phags pa sku mched bzhi'i chung ba ye shes 'byung gnas
kyi sras bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal la sras du mar byon pa bla brang khag bzhir gyes

pa las/che ba bzhi thog bla brang pa la mkhas btsun chen po nam mkha' legs pa la sogs pa'i skyes chen du ma byon/de 'og bla brang rin chen sgang pa la 'jam dbyangs don yod
rgyal mtshan dang/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la sogs pa'i skyes chen du ma byon/de 'og lha khang bla brang pa la theg chen chos kyi rgyal po la sogs pa'i skyes
chen du ma byon no/ / bla brang de gsum gyi gdung brgyud ni ding sang mi bzhugs so/ /chung ba dus mchod bla brang pa la rtse gdong bla brang pa zhes grags shing bla chen
bsod nams blo gros dang/ dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan la sogs pa'i skyes chen du ma byon/ khyad par du bdag chen nam mkha' bkra shis pas gdung spel gyi go sar bzhugs skabs/
mdo rgyud rgya mtsho lta bu'i mnga' bdag paN chen shes rab rin chen stag tshang lo tsA bar grags pa dang/ gnas lnga rig pa'i paN chen mi nyag grags pa rdo rje rnam pa
gnyis kyis rdo rje 'dzin pa du mas dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje sa lug kyi sgrub mchod nar ma dang/ dge 'dun du mas 'jam dpal mtshan brjod kyi rgyud la zhal 'don
mdzad pa'i rgyun

'dzugs pa dang/ bdag chen nyid la sogs pas dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi sgrub mchod dang/ rdo rje phur pa dang chos skyong gur zhal la sogs pa'i
mchod gtor gyi rnal 'byor gyi rgyun 'dzugs pa la sogs pa'i zhal bkod dang mthun rkyen mdzad cing/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gdung rabs kyi phreng ba ji snyed pa 'byon pa'i
gsol gdab dang rten 'brel mdzad pa la brten nas/ shing mo sbrul gyi lo la dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta gnyis pa mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug dpal sa skya lo tsA ba chen po 'jam
dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po byon/ bdag nyid chen po 'di'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar ba ni/ ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod du gsungs
pa bzhin yin lags/de'i gcung bdag chen rin po che ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni me mo lug gi lo la 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas thugs rje
che zhing thugs rgyud dul ba ngo mtshar ba zhig byon pa des/ yongs 'dzin dam pa dkon mchog 'phel/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ kong ston
dbang phyug grub pa/ zhwa lu lo chen rin po che chos skyong bzang po/ gcen sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams

sogs mkhas grub du ma las phar tshad 'dul mngon dbu sdom rig gnas dbang lung man ngag sogs gsan sbyong mthar phyin par mdzad de/ dgung lo nyer gsum bzhes pa sa mo sbrul gyi
lo la gdan sa chen po dpal rtse gdong nyid du mkhan po thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po las kyi slob dpon gnas lnga
rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po kong ston dbang phyug grub pa dpal bzang pos mdzad de/ dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa bzhes/ bsnyen sgrub
mthar phyin cing 'gro don rgya cher mdzad/ khyad par sa lo chen po zhing gzhan du gshegs rjes dpal nA lendrar kun mkhyen rong ston chen po'i rgyal tshab mdzad de bstan pa
bskyangs/ dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe dgu pa shing mo lug gi lo la dpal thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i chos kyi grwa chen por mdo rgyud rgya mtsho lta bu'i mnga' bdag mkhyen
rab gzhan dang mi mnyam pa'i blo gros mnga' ba kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa chen po bsod nams seng ge'i gdan sar mnga' gsol te/ sde snod gtso bor gyur pa'i mdo sngags kyi
'chad nyan rlabs che ba mdzad/ nA lendra dang thub bstan rnam rgyal sogs su gsung ngag rin po che tshar du ma gnang zhing/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags

lugs kyi rim lnga'i khrid dang gzhung phran rnams kyi lung la sogs pa yun ring po'i bar du ma nyams par bzhugs pa ni rje btsun 'di'i bka' drin las byung ba yin no/ / de ltar
bstan pa dang sems can gyi don mtha' yas pa mdzad nas dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa brgyad pa shing mo phag gi lo nag pa zla ba'i nyer dgu la zhing gzhan du gshegs so/ /de'i gcung
bdag chen 'jam dpal grags pa dpal bzang po ni bla ma dam pa rnams bsten cing rdo rje theg pa la mkhas par mdzad/ khyad par thugs dam la shin tu brtson pa zhig te/ rtse
gdong gi gzim chung lcang lo can gyi mgon khang gi thog la dbu lo bcings te mtshan mo thugs dam la rtag 'grus mdzad pa'i lcags gzer deng sang gi bar du'ang bzhugs shing/
mdo khams kyi yul du 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa ste/ bdag chen a 'jam pa zhes grags so/ /gcung sku gzhon pa bdag chen rin po che dbang nam mkha' 'dod grub sangs rgyas tshe
brtan bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ skyes thob kyi mkhyen rab phul du byung zhing bla ma dam pa gzhan du ma dang sa lo sku mched bsten te chos kyi sgo du ma gsan
cing bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin nas nag po chen po la sogs

pa'i zhal yang gzigs te 'gro phan du ma mdzad pa'i sngags 'chang mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug chen por gyur/ gdung brgyud gnyis 'khrungs rjes su rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen
dang sa lo sku mched sogs kyi drung du bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa bzhes te/ dpal nA lendra'i gdan sa yang mdzad cing thub bstan rnam rgyal du yang phebs te gu drag
gi dbang dang sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang mgon po'i chos skor du ma gsungs so/ /kun dga' bsam grub/bdag chen de nyid dang yar 'brog pa'i khri lcam bu 'dren skyid la sras
gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba bdag chen rin po che kun dga' bsam grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste/ 'di ni shing mo phag gi lo la 'khrungs/ skyes thob kyi
mkhyen rab che zhing sa lo tsA ba sku mched rnams dang/ rdo rje 'chang dkon mchog lhun grub 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ lo chen ratna bha dra la sogs pa'i bla ma
rnams bsten nas gsan sbyong mdzad/ dbu bla rnams la gus 'dud shin tu che zhing rang nyid kyis kyang bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin par mdzad/ rtse gdong du

bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun rnams kyis kyang dkyil 'khor du ma'i sgrub mchod dang bsnyen sgrub la brtson pa'i sgrigs rim dang dus mchod kyi gzhi rten rgya cher mdzad/ rdzu 'phrul
la sogs pa'i grub pa'i mtshan ma phal pa'i blo yul du mi shong ba zhig ste/ de yang dper mtshon tsam brjod na/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar ngo mtshar rgya
mtsho las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ dus de nyid kyi tshe rtse gdong nas gcen rin po che kun dga' bsam grub nyid blo bur du byon te/ mdzo mo zhig la sil snyan chung ngu gcig sogs
rgyab khal dang bcas skas son drug bdun yod pa'i skas shig la thogs med 'khrid nas gzim phug gi nang du thal byon nas/ ngas o lo 'phrad par yong ba yin/ mdzo 'di gang
du 'dogs gsungs pa la/ sngags 'chang bla ma de nyid kyis brag la phyag mdzub kyis bug pa zangs thal du btod nas/ 'di la 'dogs par zhu zhes gsungs pas/ sku 'khor ba rnams
ha las par gyur cing/ bdag chen sku mched gnyis ka grub pa'i gtsug rgyan du thag chod pa yin no ces kyang thos/ zhes dang/ yang de nyid las/ bsam yas su byon pa'i rnam thar
gyi thad nas 'di ltar gsungs te/ sngags 'chang bla ma yab sras kyi drung du/ bsam yas pa'i zhal ngo/ blon po gros dbang rnams dang/ gzhan

yang skya ser bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus pa'i dbus su/ chos skyong chen po'i gsung gis/ da lta bod na gang zag 'khrul pa zad pa mang po med/ sa skya pa chen po'i gcen hor yul
du byon nas nyi ma re la yang rdzu 'phrul mang du ston par 'dug ste/ de grub rtags su shes pa gdug 'dre min pa mi 'dug da stag lung na byon yod pas zab yangs mthil gyi
gtsug lag khang 'di rnams la/ sa skya pa chen po dang/ dge bshes gcen po gnyis kyis rab tu gnas pa dang/ sems can la bde skyid 'byung ba'i slob dpon padma la gsol 'debs
rgyas par mdzad na/ bstan 'gro la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung ba'i rten 'brel khyad par can yod pas/ sa skya pa chen po'i gcen po nyid gdan 'dren par gtong dgos/ zhes gsungs
pa la brten nas/ rtse gdong bdag chen pa'i drung du/ bsam yas pa'i lha mi rnams kyis spyan 'dren gyi zhu yig dang/ khyad par sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i zhu yig
mi sna dang bcas pa gnang ba'i tshe bdag chen kun dga' bsam grub kyang sku mched mjal ba la thugs shin tu spro bar gyur nas/ spyan 'dren pa rnams zhabs drung du slebs ma
thag stag lung pa rnams la slar gang myur phebs pa'i bka' bzhes gnang nas/ de ma thag chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te bsam yas su phebs pa'i tshe/ der bzhugs kyi

skya ser byings kyis ser phreng phebs bsu sogs rgyas pa dang/ khyad par gdung sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i zhabs dpon slob rags bsdus gzab gshom dang bcas dal
la gong du phebs bsu'i slad du phebs pa na/ rtse gdong bdag chen nyid dang mjal ba'i tshe/ de ma thag bdag chen pa nyid dang/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can gnyis
ka yun ring 'grogs pa'i mdza' bo ltar thugs yid shin tu 'dre bar gyur cing/ de nas rim par bsam yas su phebs pa na/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos kyang phyag dang
bsu ba'i slad du dkar zhal mthil du phyags phebs cing/ de nas bsam yas dbu rtse'i bar khang du spyan drangs te/ sku mched gnyis ka dges bzhin tu bzhugs gral mdzad pa la/
bsam yas pa rnams kyi dkar spro sogs bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs shing/ de nas dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i bla brang bkra shis sgang du 'dren pa dam pa sku mched
khu dbon gsum gyis gdan chags te/ de'i sang nyin snga ba'i char pe har lha'i pho brang nas sku mched khu dbon gsum ka spyan drangs pa'i tshe/ dung rgya gling/ spos sna sogs
dang/ gzhan yang rol mo dang bcas chos skyong rang nyid kyi gar 'chams mdzad pa sogs gus pa chen po'i ngang nas phebs

bsu rgya che ba dang bcas lcog tu phebs pa na/ mkhan tshang par chos skyong chen po'i gsung gis/ sa skya pa chen po mched gnyis la gdug 'dre'i gzhi len byed pa yin pas/ ja
rgyu yag pa/ gar po yin pa/ sla mo min pa sbyor bdun phrag gcig bkral khog bdun tshugs la 'phral du yong bar gyis zhes gsungs shing/ de nas chos skyong gi gsung las/ slob
dpon padmas gdug 'dre la bod gangs ri'i khrod kyi bstan pa'i bsrung ma bka'i bya ra ba la bskos pa de yin/ khyed sa skya pa rnams bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong spel ba la bka'
bsgos pa yin pas/ khyed sa skya dge bshes mched gnyis kyis sems can la phan bde 'byung ba'i gnas gzhis mchog tu gyur pa lha sa bsam yas sogs su sems can bde thabs kyi rten
gsum sogs la rab gnas dang/ bstan pa dar zhing rgyas pa'i smon lam rgya chen po mdzad dgos/ gdug 'dres kyang bstan dgra thams cad myur du tshar gcod cing/ khyad par sa
skya pa'i dbang gi khrims ra stag tshang rdzong kha dmag gis bskor nas 'phrog mi rnams/ lo zla tshes grangs dus btab nas myur du tshar gcod pa'i khas blang gi yi ge chos
skyong chen po nyid kyi dam kha 'byar ba/ bdag nyid chen po sku mched kyi phyag tu 'bul zhu ba bzhin/ de ltar phul ba ltar de dang mthun par yun ring

ma lon par bstan dgra rnams la rtags mtshan myur du byung ba yin no zhes thos la/ de ltar stag tshang rdzong kha gzhan lag tu 'chor ba'i rgyu ni/ snga gong zhig rtse gdong
bdag chen pas sde pa thob rgyal ba la dpung khyer khrid gnang ba tshabs su ma song ba la brten nas/ bdag chen rang yang btson lam du phebs dgos shar zhing/ de mthun stag
tshang rdzong dang bcas pa yang mi lag tu shor ba la/ rtse gdong pa rnams kyis lan lon pa zhig ma byung kyang/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyi bka' bzhin bsam yas
chos skyong chen pos/ bdag chen kun dga' bsam 'grub nyid la 'phrin las sgrub par zhal gyis bzhes shing dam bca' phul ba 'di yang/ grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po nyid la
phrin las mgon po sogs bstan bsrung dam can rgya mtshos bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i mtshan ma yang dag par rtogs shing/ de skabs chos skyong gi sprul pas dgra bgegs tshar gcod
pa'i gzigs snang ngo mtshar can byung ba rnams ri mor mdzad pa ni/ da lta rtse gdong srid gsum rnam rgyal gyi 'du khang chen mo'i sgo nang na bzhugs pa de dag yin par grags/
de ltar mkhas grub kyi sgo nas bstan 'gro'i don rlabs po che mdzad de/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa brgyad pa chu pho sprel lo sbo zla ba'i nyer dgu la zhing gzhan du gshegs/

de'i gcung ni sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen te/ bdag nyid chen po 'di'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rgya mtsho dang/ ngo mtshar rin po che'i
bang mdzod sogs su gsungs pa ltar ro/ /kun dga' bde legs/bdag chen kun dga' bsam grub kyi btsun mo rtse gdong ma la sras gcig 'khrungs pa ni/ bdag chen kun dga' bde legs
bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste/ 'di ni sa mo bya yi lo la sku 'khrungs/ mkhyen rab shin tu che bas chos mang po thugs su chud/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs
grub kyi drung du dgung lo bcu bzhi pa chu pho khyi lo hor zla bdun pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin dge bsnyen mdzad de mtshan gsol/ dus 'khor gyi dbang/ sbyor drug gi khrid kyai
rdor gyi dbang la sogs pa chos kyi sgo bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan cing thugs dam dang gsan pa phul du byung bar mdzad pas ting 'dzin gyi sgo du ma 'khrungs/ chos rje rin
po che kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa la gsung ngag gsan/ gzhan yang yab 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsam 'grub pa dang ngor chen

dkon mchog dpal ldan/ brang ti pa nam mkha' dpal bzang/ thub bstan mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan la sogs las chos du ma gsan/ bsnyen sgrub du ma mdzad cing nus mthu bsam gyis
mi khyab rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sprul par grags/ dgung lo bzhi bcu pa sa pho byi ba'i lo sa ga zla ba'i tshes lnga la zhing gzhan du gshegs/ sku gdung zhugs pa phul
bas sku'i rtsibs rus la bde mchog phyag bcu gnyis pa yab yum sen mo'i khyon tsam pa ngo mtshar ba 'bur dod dang/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sku dang ring bsrel grangs med byon/
me tog re la 'ja' gur re yod pa mang po'i char babs so/ /kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/bdag chen de la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba ni 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun
grub ste/ bdag nyid chen po 'di ni/ yab dpal sa skya pa chen po bdag chen kun dga' bde legs zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug de nyid dang/ yum ni lha mo nor rgyun
ma'i rnam 'phrul yin par bdag chen kun dga' bsam grub pas lhums su yod dus bya bzang du lung bstan

pa ltar/ rigs khyad par can du 'khrungs shing byams dang snying rjes mgon med skyong ba bla ma dang dkon mchog gi zhabs tog la brtson pa/ lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa rab tu rgyas
pa ye shes mkha' 'gro'i mtshan dang ldan pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang mo dpal bu khrid ces bya ba'i sras su skyes bdag ces bya ba lcags mo lug gi lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes
brgyad kyi tho rengs res gza' lhag pa dang rgyu skar dbyug pa 'dzom pa'i tshe/ gdan sa chen po dpal rtse gdong gi bla brang chen po'i gzim khang du sa lo thams cad mkhyen
pa sku 'khrungs pa'i gnas gzim chung phun tshogs gling gi shar phyogs gzim chung zil gnon zhes bya bar sku 'khrungs so/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di yum gyi lhums su bzhugs
pa na yum sku ldang ba yang ba dang lhag par yang byams pa dang snying rje che bar gyur pa dang/ sras 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa gsum 'byung bas dge la tha mi'i ming nas smos
pa'i mtshan btags na dge zhes bya ba'i mnal ltas byun bar grags pa sogs mtshan ltas ngo mtshar ba du ma byung bar nges shing/ sku bltams pa'i tshe yang yum la gnod pa med
cing bde bas brgyan pa dang/ rje nyid kyang mngal nas 'byung ba'i sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba med par bsam bzhin du srid par skye ba bzhes pa'i rnam par thar pas bde bar bltams
shing

bde bar 'khrungs par gyur to/ /gzhon nu de ni shin tu mdzes shing yid du 'ong la mtshan dpe ngo mtshar ba dang ldan pas mthong na dga' ba bskyed cing lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig
rten gyis phyag bya ba'i 'os su gyur pa bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams kyis dus de nyid nas gtsug gi rgyan du 'dzin pa zhig tu gyur pa ste/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs rabs
nas rabs su brgyud pa'i gdung brgyud dam pa 'di dag tu 'khrungs tsam nyid nas yon tan de lta bu dang ldan par gor ma chag cing lhag par rje btsun dam pa 'di gzhan las ches
phul du byung bar dang po nyid nas mngon du gyur pa'i phyir ro/ / mtshan yang yum gyi mnal bltas dang bstun te/ rdo rje rgya sog ces gsol to/ /de nas rim gyis sku bskyed
bsrings te cung zad nar son pa nas tha mal pa'i byis pa'i spyod pa las yang dag par 'das shing thub gcod la sogs pa mi mdzad par dul zhing yid gzhung ba chos kyi bag
chags shin tu gsal bas de dang mthun pa'i spyod pa mdzad pa zhig ste/ sku na phra mo'i dus shig nyin gcig yab drung la/ bdag la khang pa legs po yod lags zhus byung ba la/
yab kyis ci 'dra zhig yod ces gsungs pas/ shing dang 'jim pa

las byas pa 'di 'dra min lags/ zhes zhus 'tshams su yum phebs nas byung bas gsung 'phro bcad song zhes zer ba dang/ yum la nga la dung mang po yod ces gsung ba dang/ rje 'di
lug lo rgyal zla'i tshes brgyad la 'khrungs nas lo hril po gnyis dang zla ba gnyis tsam song ba'i khyi lo'i dpyid 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsam grub kyi dgongs rdzogs la/
sa skya nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po spyan drangs te rtse gdong du bzhugs skabs dus rtag tu sngags 'chang rin po che'i sku drung rang du bzhugs shing/ dgong mo gsung
bskang mdzad pa'i yun thams cad la phyag rnga chung chung bzo ba 'dra mo zhig yod pa de brdung gin rgyun ring po ci 'dra byung yang ngal ba med par sku drung du bzhugs
pa zhig byung bas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po shin tu dges te 'di la yag po rang zhig yong ba 'dug ces yang yang gsung ba byung zhes thos/ rje ngor chen dkon mchog dpal
ldan pa rtse gdong du phebs skabs shig rje 'di byis pa chung ngu der bzhugs pa la/ rje ngor pas yab yum gnyis la/ gdung brgyud 'di sku skyed yag po byung 'dug sa lo thams
cad mkhyen pa'i sku rjes zin pa zhig e yong/ zhes gsungs pa la/ rje 'dis yong yong zhes gsung byung bas chos rje ngor chen dang yab yum rnams ha las pa lta bur gyur/

bdag chen ngag drung gi grwa pa drung ram pa dge 'dun dar rgyas zhes pa la/ dge dar ba zhes 'bod pa gcig yod pa de nam gzigs pa na thugs shin tu dgyes pa'i tshul mdzad pa dang/
rje dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i thugs sras rin po che kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa zhal ngo'i sku srung la bzhugs pa/ khong gis ri khrod lo ma can gyi khrus chog mdzad pa
gzigs pas/ khong la pi sha zhes 'bod pa gnang zhing nye 'khor du bzhugs nas/ khong gi sku chos de sku la mi rdzogs bzhin du bzhes/ dbu zhwa dbu thog tu 'jog par mdzad pa
la/ khong gis de 'dra ma mdzad 'bags nas 'gro zhus kyang mi gsan par de bzhin mdzad/ de skabs shig khong pa 'gro tsa na/ da pi sha ma byung zhes yang yang gsungs/ rin po
che kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas/ gdung brgyud 'di gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i ngo mtshar che ba zhig 'dug 'di la sku yon zhig 'bul ba'i zhabs thog nged kyis byed rgyu byung na
tshogs bsags par 'dug ste/ nga myur du 'chi'am zhes gsung zhing/ khong bdun cu don lnga bzhes sa phag lo sku gshegs/ de dus rje 'di dgung lo lnga pa yin pas lha bzo ba dang/
shing bzo ba dang/ mgar ba rnams bos nas/ nga'i pi sha ma byung/ khyed tshos nga'i pi sha yag po shig bzos shog ces gsungs/ cung zad sku nar son pa na

klog yig phul bas brda' tsam bstan pas tshegs med du mkhyen pas ngo mtshar du 'dzin cing rim gyi chos spyod kyi rim pa rnams dang rdo rje phur pa la sogs pa'i sgrub dkyil gyi
cho ga sogs la thugs sbyong mdzad do/ /de skabs yab bdag chen kun dga' bde legs pa'i dbu blar e waM chos ldan nas brang ti pa paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang pa bzhugs pa
la kyai rdor la sogs pa'i dbang bskur ci rigs pa gsan pas smin par mdzad cing rjes gnang la sogs pa'i dbang bka' ci rigs pa gsan pa nas bzung sum cu rtsa gnyis su phebs
pa'i stag lo rje brang ti pa zhing brjes pa'i bar du rje btsun de nyid dus skabs phal che bar rtse gdong du spyan drangs te gsung chos rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan
cing/ de yang nged rang gi zhu ba la ma ltos par/ 'di dgos pa yong gsungs nas dgongs pas dpyad nas chos tsho gnang ba zhig yod ces gsungs zhing/ rje dgung lo nyer gcig
pa yos lo bsnyen par rdzogs pa gnang grub 'phral/ da thar pa rtse rang du bzhugs la gsung chos 'chad pa la brtson pa mdzod gsung ba'i bka' lung nan che ba phebs byung ba
la/ nged rang de kha bzhin du zhu rtsis yod/

de dus chos 'chad rgyu'i ca lag yang dga' mo yod de/ stabs shig gis/ de bzhin byed pa'i thabs ma byung bas/ cung zhig ma dgyes zhes gsung/ de dus yum gyi thugs rtsis che bas
thugs kyis ma btang ba dang/ dpon slob chen mo lhun grub dpal bzang pa sku yon 'bul ba sogs lugs gnyis kyi zhabs thog pa'i sku dbang che shos yin 'dug pas/ khong gi blo
la'ang med 'dug pa'i stabs kyis thar rtser bzhugs pa zhig ma byung 'dug e waM du khams phyogs nas bla ma dpon slob mang po zhig gis yang dag he ru ka'i dbang sogs rje brang
ti pa la gsol ba btab 'dug pa la/ da nged las kyang rtse gdong zhabs drung 'di pa la thugs 'dris che ba yod cing/ nged kyis gsung chos gang yod phul ba yin pas/ rtse
gdong du zhus gsungs 'dir brdzong ba gnang byung bas/ khong tshos blo la gang yod kyi chos rnams byas pas/ thugs dgyes pa byung 'dug ces gsungs/ de ltar rje btsun chos kyi
rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa de nyid zhal bzhugs pa'i skabs rnams su zhabs thog bsnyen bkur phul du byung bas mchod cing/ stag lo sku zhabs thog bsnyen bkur phul du byung
bas mchod cing/ stag lo sku gshegs pa na phyis sprel lo'i bar lo bcu dgu'i bar dus chen steng/ e waM tshogs chen du mang ja re chag med du gnang zhing/ phal cher la 'gyed
dang rgyab chas gnang bar mdzad pa

dang/ de nas kyang dus skabs la dgongs pa rdzogs thabs kyi mang ja sogs gnang ba dang/ rje de nyid kyi bris sku dang 'bur sku du ma bzhengs pa dang/ rje de'i sku 'dra gang
na 'dug kyang dbu gtugs nas byin rlabs zhu bar mdzad pa dang/ tshogs su rje'i sku bstod thugs rjes nam yang ma 'don pa'i skabs/ na bza'i sbugs su phyag thal mo sbyor bar
mdzad pa dang/ dus 'gol ba'i tshe/ rje de nyid kyi mdzad spyod dang yon tan gyi cha rnams dges bzhin du gsung 'phros mdzad pa sogs thugs dad gus bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo
nas/ thugs dam dang 'chad nyan gang mdzad kyang/ rje 'di nyid kyi phyag bzhes ji lta ba bzhin mdzad cing/ phyag mdzod kun legs pas bka' lung gnang dgos kyi 'phros tshul
zhus pa'i skabs shig rin po che paN chen gyis/ mi gzhan gyi nor de nga la dgos zer nas blangs na sdom pa 'chor ba yin gsung byung zhes bka' stsal 'dug pa sogs/ bla ma dam
pa de nyid kyi sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las dang bcas pa'i rnam thar gyi rjes su slob par mdzad pa zhig snang ngo/ /yang rje 'di dgung lo lnga pa shing mo phag lo'i
dbyar/ rje dkon mchog dpal ldan rtse gdong du gdan drangs nas yab

'jam dbyangs kun dga' bde legs la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras cha lag dang bcas pa dang/ gzhan yang bde mchog lU yi pa sogs kyi dbang/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa rgya mtshos
gtso byas pa'i rjes gnang du ma/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i bka' 'bum sogs lung gi tshogs du ma gnang ba rje 'di nyid kyis ma tshang ba med par gsan/ lung sogs re re
nas 'di byung rang gsal po mi 'dug kyang/ phal che ba da lta'ang gsal po 'dug ces rje de nyid kyi gsungs/ de dus chos yun ring ba dang sku phra bas bzhugs mi nus pa'i rnam
'gyur cung zad byung dogs nas chab tog na bza'i khud du 'jog dgos byung zhes gsung yang/ sngon legs par sbyangs pa'i bag chags sad pa'i skyes bu dam pa 'di ni de tsam
na dran shes bzhin dang ldan pas don gnyer de lta bu mdzad pa ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su snang zhing/ yol ba'i phyi nas nang du re re bzhin 'gro ba'i brda chig brgyud gnang
ba sogs da lta yang gsal po 'dug ces gsungs so/ /lo de'i ston mjug nas/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis dgung lo bco brgyad pa'i dus rtse gdong gi gzim khang bsam gtan 'phel
rgyas su gzhi bsnyen mdzad 'dug phyag g.yog la chos rje lha sdings pa 'dug/

byi ba lo gzhi bsnyen grol ba'i gtang rag gi bskang gso mdzad pa'i skabs/ nged byis pa yin kyang gral dbu la byon gsung phyin bdag bskyed kyai rdor lam dus mdzad 'dug bskang
gso he ru ka dpal ma gnang 'dug lha mchog ma'i tshig gi khyad par/ zhing skyong dbang phyug chen po'i thugs dam bskangs/ gsung ba zhig 'dug ces gsungs te/ de dus rje 'di
dgung lo drug pa yin 'dug kyang sku na phra mo de tsam gyi dus nas/ bskang gso sogs la thugs gzhol ba dang/ mkhyen rab kyi 'jug pa de lta bu ni ngo mtshar che bar snang/
de lta bu'i ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba de dus nas mnga' ba'i rnam thar la thugs yis ches te/ phyis shar chen kun dga' bkra shis pa nyid kyis dad gus chen po'i sgo nas
dbu bla'i mchog tu bzhes par mdzad do/ /dgung lo brgyad bzhes pa 'bru mang po zhes grags pa sa pho stag gi lo'i dbyar phur sgrub chen lo'i dus 'cham gsar mdzad de sku 'chams
kyi rigs gang dgos pa rnams 'khrul med du mdzad pas kun ya mtshan du 'dzin par gyur/ dgung lo dgu pa myos ldan gyi lo yab dang lhan cig e waM du phebs te smin drug zla
ba'i yar tshes bdun zla ba lha mtshams kyi 'grub sbyor bzang po yod pa'i snga dro'i cha la mkhan po yongs 'dzin dkon mchog dpal ldan

las slob paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang/ grib tshod pa mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang/ dbu mdzad mgon po bkra shis sogs dge slong lnga'i dbus su rab tu byung ste/ mtshan kun
dga' bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gsol te tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rin po ches thugs kyi bang mdzod yongs su gang bar mdzad/ na bza'
brjes pa'i tshe yum la nga'i go lag rnying pa de dgos gsung/ ma phul bas 'o na de'i nang na shig 'dra 'dug na yum gyis de tsho sha yag po dang mnyam du gos nang du 'jog
rogs mdzod ces gsungs/ mkhan slob gtso bor gyur pa'i der bzhugs kyi las gral ba rnams la'ang 'bul ba gnang sbyin rgya che ba dang/ dge 'dun tshogs pa la'ang mang ja 'gyed
dang bcas pa'i dga' ston mdzad/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bde legs pas tshogs chos dang sgos chos 'ga' zhig gnang/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis rgyal ba khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang
chen po'i seng ge'i khri ga la ba der zhabs sen bkod nas der bzhugs kyi dge 'dun brgya phrag du ma 'dus pa la 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i rjes su gnang ba mdzad/ phyis
rje'i zhal nas nga mi 'kham ches zer dgos sam lo dgu pa la ngor tshogs chen du 'jam dbyangs kyi rjes gnang byas zhes gsungs so/ /

de nas slar rtse gdong du phebs pa dang dus cher mi 'gyang bar/ 'brug lo nas rje dkon mchog dpal ldan pa rtse gdong du sku mtshams lo gsum pa'i ring la/ nyin mo'i dus thams
cad du rje de'i sku gzhogs rang du bzhugs nas thub pa dgongs gsal dang/ sdom gsum rab dbye la sogs pa'i gsung rab dang/ kyai rdor la sogs pa'i smin grol skor gyi gsan sbyong
phyag khrid dang bcas pa rgyun ldan du mdzad pa dang/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid la sogs pa'i khrid che chung du ma dang/ dbang rjes gnang lung la sogs pa'i chos
gsan pa 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad/ phyis gdan sa chen por che 'don gyi skabs su yang gsung chos gsan pa sogs/ rje 'di nyid thugs kyi sras dam par gyur te/ thugs dad
bsam gyis mi khyab pas rigs kyi bdag po dam par dgongs pa mdzad do/ / sku phra mo'i dus rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa la tshe dbang sogs chos thos yod 'dug kyang nged rang
gis cher mi dran par 'dug gsungs/ rje dkon mchog dpal ldan pa yab kyi dbu blar bsten pa las kyang snga bar rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa dbu bla gnang ba snga zhes gsung
ngo/ /de dus rje ngor pas thugs 'dun rtse gcig pa'i sgo nas zhal ngo yab yum la gdung brgyud rin po che sku mched rnams gdan sa

chen po dpal ldan sa skyar khri 'don mdzad dgos pai' snyan zhus yang yang 'bul bar mdzad nas/ che 'don gyi yo byad la dmigs pa'i rtse gdong nas 'bul sdud pa rdzong bda' gnang
ba'i bka' gros gsal 'debs mdzad de/ mdo khams phyogs kyi ngor pa la gtogs pa'i bla ma slob dpon dgon sde che chung sbyin bdag drag zhan thams cad la rje de nyid kyi phyag
dam mdzad de/ rtse gdong nas gdung brgyud rin po che sku mched rnams dpal ldan sa skya'i bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol rgyu yin pas/ khyed rnams kyis sa skya pa'i bstan
pa'i zhabs tog dang rang rang gi 'di phyi'i don sgrub pa'i phyir du 'bul ba gang drag byed dgos/ zhes sogs kyis bskul ma mdzad de/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po lhun grub
dpal bzang pa dpon slob rnams khams phyogs su brdzong bar mdzad/lo gsum gyi sku mtshams grol nas rta lo'i mjug tu e waM du phebs/ de dus rje 'di dgung lo bcu gnyis pa yin
la/ de dag gi mu nas sngar smos pa'i sgrub dkyil sogs dang kun rig tshe dpag med/ mi 'khrugs pa la sogs pa'i rgyud sde 'og ma'i cho ga dang dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud
dang rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i tshul gsum mdzes rgyan la sogs pa'i rgyud gzhung rnams thugs la bzung nas rgyud 'don gyi dbur phebs pa dang/

sgrub mchod dang bskang gso la sogs pa'i rim pa gang ji snyed pa dag gi gral du yang phebs te shin tu byang chub par mdzad/ bstan bcos chen po thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal ba la
sogs pa la thos bsam yang rgyun chags su mdzad do/ / de nas skabs shig rje btsun byams pa rab brtan pas dbu mdzad thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas
pa bsam grub rtser mtshan brjod la phebs skabs/ mkhan chen de nyid rtse gdong du spyan drangs nas 'phel rgyas su bzhugs skabs/ yab sras rnams kyis tshe dpag med lha dgu'i
dbang dang grub rgyal ma'i byin rlabs/ zhag bdun ma dang sgra mi snyan pa'i tshe sgrub/ lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang rnams gsan/ srid gsum rnam rgyal gyi grwa rgyun du dmigs
pa du ma rab tu byung bar mdzad/ byams pa rab brtan pas bdag nyid chen po 'di'i drung du 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang gsan pas sku na phra mo la thugs spobs pa
chen pos gsung chos thogs med du stsal ba de la yum dges te bzhad shor bas de 'dra ma mdzad gsung/shing mo bya lo khams nas 'bul sdud pa 'khor dang bstun rtse gdong nas
kyang yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas yab sras bzhi la dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma dang/ dpon skya las

sne sogs zhabs 'bring ba du mas bskor te dpal sa skyar chibs kha bsgyur ba'i lam zhor bsam grub rtse/ e waM chos ldan sogs rim gyis brgyud ngor chen dkon mchog dpal ldan dang
bcas gdan sa chen por phebs par nye ba na/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po dpon g.yog brgya skor gyis ga ra'i maNDal sgang du phebs bsu mdzad de khu dbon lhan rgyas de
nub bkra shis mthong smon du bzhugs/ sang nyin dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen por chos grwa lho byang gi ser phreng/ chos skyong gi 'cham sku byin rlabs can rnams kyis phebs
bsu sogs mdzad de gzhis len zhabs tog rgyas par mdzad/me khyi rta zla'i tshes gcig nas bzung sku mched gsum char chos khri mkhas pa zil gnon du khri bton mnga' gsol mdzad
de/ mkhas grub 'dus pa rgya mtsho dang skye bo'i tshogs stong phrag du ma 'dus pa'i dbus der bdag nyid chen po 'dis rgyal sras lam bzang gi chos 'khor rgya chen po bskor
bar mdzad de/ thams cad dad pa'i spu long dbang med du g.yos shing zang zing gi 'bul ba nam mkha' mdzod kha phye ba lta bu dang/ mchod pa bsnyen bkur sbyin gtong blo'i
ra ba las brgal bar mdzad cing khu dbon dam pa rnams kyis thog drangs skye rgu thams cad thugs dgyes pa

dang rangs pa'i mchog tu gyur te/ slar yang bdag nyid chen po rang nyid kyi gdan sa dpal rtse gdong du chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur ba na phebs skyel gyi rim pa'ang phebs bsu dang
'dra bar mdzad de/ rim gyis bsam grub rtser mi dbang sku mched la chos 'brel stsal zhing/ de sa nas kyang bsnyen bkur rgya chen po mdzad de chos grwa chen po thub bstan
rnam rgyal du phebs pa na mkhan slob dge 'dun rnams kyi bsu ba dang bsnyen bkur rgya chen po mdzad de kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po'i chos khri'i steng nas rje byams pa
rab brtan dang/ kun mkhyen chos 'od zer sogs mkhas grub 'dus pa rgya mtshor drag dmar gyi dbang sogs chos kyi sbyin pa dang 'bul ba gnang sbyin phul du phyin par mdzad de
gdan sa chen po rtse gdong nyid du phyag phebs so/ /de ltar e waM pa chen po rje btsun dkon mchog dpal ldan de nyid las dge bsnyen dge tshul gyi sdom pa/ brgyud pa'i khyad
par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ kyai rdor yab bka' yum bka'i rgyu lam dang/ bde mchog lU hi pa/ tshe dpag lha dgu/ mi 'khrugs lha dgu rnams kyi dbang lam zab byin rlabs/
sgrub thabs brgya rgyam/ gur lha brgyad/ zhal/ dur khrod bdag po/ pu tra/ bran bdud/ dkar bdud rnams kyi rjes gnang/ lam

'bras/ do lugs gcod khrid/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid sogs dang/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum sogs lung gi tshogs du ma gsan te/
sdom gsum stsol pa'i bla ma dam pa bka' drin che ba zhig tu 'dzin par mdzad do/ / yang rje btsun yab las rdo rje phur pa'i dbang gsan te de phyin chad sangs rgyas dngos
kyi 'du shes mdzad/ yang paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang las rdo rje phur pa stod las smad las kyi dbang dang rjes gnang/ sgrub thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi lung rnams
gsan te/ de'i dus grangs kyi ljags bsnyen mthar phyin pa'i tshe/ ngor nas rje dkon mchog dpal ldan gyis theg chen rin po che'i mgul phur zhu yig bcas gnang/ slar yang
phur pa'i 'chams dbyangs sogs sbyangs pa mdzad de/ de'i chog dpon lo ltar mdzad/dgung lo bcu bdun pa me phag smin drug nas bzung/ zla ba drug gi bar du bzhugs stan thog gcig
tu mi tshig gis bar ma chod par kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen bcu cha'i sbyin sreg bcas mdzad/ sa byi lo yab sku gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs rnams rgya cher mdzad/ de sku gsung
thugs rten gsar bzhengs rnams la rje byams pa rab brtan rab gnas la spyan 'dren mdzad/ de'i drung du lam 'bras

dbang lung byin rlabs cha tshang dang/ gur mgon brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gsang gsum dang/ rtsa gsum 'khor lo bzhi'i gsang khrid/ de dang rjes 'brel gyi rjes gnang/ tshe bka'
'ga' zhig dang bcas pa gsan te/ bla ma 'dis chos gsung ba rnams thugs la shin tu 'jems pas grol dus zin byung snyam pa byung gsungs/ yang paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang
pa'i drung du bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang dang rim bzhi'i khrid gsan nas de'i ljags bsnyen mdzad de yab kyi dus mchod la de'i sgrub mchod lo re bzhin mdzad/ gnas skabs
thams cad du nyams bzhes dang chos 'chad la thugs brtson che ba'i ngang nas rje brang ti pa yang yang spyan drangs te gsan pa rgya mtsho ltar gyur pa mdo tsam brjod na/ rdo
rje phreng ba kri ya'i dkyil 'khor gsum/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor/ spyan gzigs/ gshed dmar lha lnga dang bcu gsum ma/ 'jigs byed ra lugs ro langs brgyad bskor dang/ bcu gsum
ma/ bde mchog lU nag dril gsum/ kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi/ gur sam gnyis/ kyai rdor bcu bdun ma/ ku ru kulle lha lnga gur mgon lha bcu gnyis ma/ yang phur/ gur drag kun
rig 'chi 'joms/ sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis/ mi 'khrugs pa/ tshe dpag lha dgu rnams kyi dbang dang rjes gnang

rigs gtad du ma/ 'og nas byung ba'i khrid bka' rnams dang/ phreng ba skor gsum/ bka' gdams glegs bam/ rin spungs skor gsum/ sa skya bka' 'bum/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/
rje sangs rin/ glo bo mkhan chen/ sa lo/ paN chen nyid kyi bka' 'bum sogs lung gi rigs du ma ste zhib pa gsan yig rin chen phreng mdzes su gsungs pa ltar ro/ /chu sbrul
lo'i dpyid ka paNDi ta snying rje bzang po rtse gdong srid gsum rnam rgyal gyi slob dpon dang nyid kyi zhabs 'bring pa'i gtso bor bsko bzhag mdzad de sku yon zhabs bskul
dbu bla rnams la chos gsan pa/ phral gyi mdzad pa rnams la spyan ltos bzang po 'bul ba sogs zhabs tog tshul bzhin mdzad cing/ dpon slob gnyis ka thugs zhi dul che bas
thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi thugs mthong che zhing/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ snying rje bzang po 'dir phebs tsam gyi dus bzhugs gral nyung ngu zhig la btsun pa 'ga' zhig chang
la 'dzem gyin 'dug pa na/ 'dzem mi dgos 'thung pas chog byas pas/ bzhugs gral grol phral snying rje bzang pos ma thungs gsungs pa phar zhog 'thung gsung mkhan byung dogs
med gsung byung bas nged shin tu 'jigs pa byung gsungs shing/ dbu bla zhig dang mnyam pa'i thugs mthong mdzad nas phyag thal mo

sbyor ba mdzad/ snying rje bzang pos kyang rje 'di la 'jam pa'i dbyangs dngos kyi thugs dad mdzad cing/ 'dis rnam par thar pa'ang rtsom par mdzad do/ /lo de'i dgun e waM nas
rje brang ti pa thub bstan du spyan drangs/ rje nyid dpon slob rnams kyang der phebs te paN chen brang ti pas mkhan po/ rje byams pa rab brtan gyi las slob/ mkhan chen
chos 'od zer gyi gsang ston/ chos rje bsod nams chos 'phel gyi grib tshod/ mkhas grub snying rje bzang pos zhu ba/ rje bsod nams don grub kyi kha bskongs mdzad de dgung lo
nyer gsum pa la bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag pa gsan nas yongs 'dzin rnams la 'bul ba/ las gral ba gzhan la gnang sbyin/ dge 'dun tshogs chen
la mang ja'i dga' ston mdzad de chos 'od zer gyi drung du gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang gsan nas rtse gdong du phebs/ slar yang mkhan chen brang ti pa las so thar mdo/ me
tog phreng brgyud/ mdo rtsa/ karma sha ta/ gsum brgya pa/ 'od ldan/ bu ston las chog rnams gsan te 'dul ba 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur/de nas shing pho rta lo
na lendrar she'u lo tsA ba gsher pa'i

gdan tshab rje 'di la gsol ba btab pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes te dgung lo nyer lnga pa shing lug khrums zla'i nang dbus phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur te rim bzhin lha bu/ 'u yug
zam tsher/ ri sding ma/ stod lung bde chen/ grub rgyal sogs su phebs pa'i tshe lam bar na 'khod pa'i lha sde mi sde kun gyis mchod cing bsnyen bkur dang chos 'brel gyi tshim
par mdzad/ de nas na lendra nas bla ma slob dpon sde pa mkhar rtse ba sogs kyis chibs bsu dang/ dge 'dun gyi ser phreng bcas phebs pa'i tshe gnam gshis 'jam zhing nyi
ma nyis 'gyur gyi ring la me tog gi char 'babs pa sogs dge mtshan du ma dang bcas bla brang gzim chung du phebs te tha skar zla ba'i bcu bzhi sa mchod nyin gzhis byes kyi
dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su kun mkhyen smra ba'i seng ge rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan gyi chos khri la zhabs zung bkod de rgyal tshab dam par mnga' gsol gyi
me tog gtor/ chos sde dang sbyin bdag spyi sgos kyi legs 'bul phul zhing gnang sbyin mang 'gyed sogs kyi so so'i re ba bskangs/ der bzhugs ring phur pa sa lugs kyi dbang
dang/ yi dam gyi rjes gnang du ma sogs smin grol chos kyi char pa phabs/ mkhar brtse ba sogs dpon rigs dang/ stag lung sde pa/ gling zhabs drung/ spyang lung chos sde/ dga'
mo grong

pa sogs kyis spyan drangs pa bzhin phebs te dbang rjes gnang mang 'gyed/ gnang sbyin sogs kyis tshim par mdzad nas gtsang phyogs la chibs kha bsgyur te/ chos 'khor lha sar
jo zhal rnam gnyis la mchod 'bul gser chab/ snyan dar/ phyag dang zhabs bskor bstan 'gror phan pa'i thugs smon mdzad pa'i tshe mi skyod rdo rje'i thugs kar phyag nas 'byar
ba kun gyi mthun snang du grub/ de nas snye phu dang 'jun sogs brgyud gong dkar rdo rje gdan du 'dus tshogs kyi ser phreng sogs bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstar zhing mang 'gyed
gya nom dang/ bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang stsal/ de nas rim gyis yar 'brog tu phebs skabs dgun yin kyang dpyid dus ltar dro zhing mtsho sman 'brog chen 'khor 'dul ma
dang/ gnod sbyin gang bzang gnyis kyi bsu ba'i rnam pas sprin khog lnga pa gdugs rgyal mtshan sogs mchod rdzas kyi rnam pas nye 'khor gyi nam mkha' khyab cing/ de nas rim
gyis rin spungs su spyan drangs shing mchod/ gdan sar phebs nyin ser phreng gi bkod pa dang bstun klu sdings mgon khang du rol mo'i sgra rang khrol yun ring byung bar grags/
'di ni chos skyong dngos su bzhugs pa'i mtshan mar nges te/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge zhing brje kha ma'i mnal ltas su/ rta sga bstad pa gcig rta pa

gsum 'dug pas gcig sa skya nas 'ong pa'i mgon chen/ gcig kha'u'i zhal/ gcig bya gshong gi rnam sras mdung dmar de dag gi 'khor du rtse gdong nas 'ong pa'i mi gsum gyi bsrung
mdud mang rab zhus song gsungs pa ltar/ 'phags pa'i shel dam che ba rtse gdong gdung brgyud rnams kyi phyag na bzhugs pa de la dkar bdud lcam dral 'phreng nas dngos su
bzhugs par bshad pa bzhin/ bdag chen kun dga' bsam 'grub la rnam rgyal rtser dkar bdud kyi zhal gzigs pa sogs bstan tshigs du ma snang/ lo de'i rgyal zla'i nyer lnga la mkhan
chen byams pa rab brtan gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs thub bstan du mang 'gyed gdung 'bul rgya cher mdzad/me spre lo sku mtshams dang sgrub mchod so so'i tshogs dpon/ dbyar
chos gnang ba sogs bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad/ me bya dbo zla'i nang slar yang brang ti pa spyan drangs te lam 'bras kyi dbang lung khrid byin rlabs man ngag zhal shes phyag
len tshang ma gsan/ nA lendra nas spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin ston ka der chibs kha bsgyur te dgung lo nyer brgyad pa sa khyi dpyid kha nas bzung spyan snga rin po che
sogs gzhis byes kyi bla ma slob dpon gra bu slob dge 'dun tshogs pa lnga brgya tsam la gsung ngag dbang lung khrid byin

rlabs yongs rdzogs stsal nas rtse gdong du phebs te/ sa phag lo dbyar brang ti pa spyan drangs te zla ba bcu lhag tsam la khrid bka' bcu gsum sogs gsan/lcags glang lo dbus
su chibs bsgyur dus gling stod chos rje kun dga' 'byung gnas kyi mnal lam du gsang mda' na byams mgon gyi sgar yin zer ba mang po shar ba nas zla ba gnyis tsam song tshe
der rje 'dis bzhugs sgar phebs byung gsung ba dang/ nA lendra'i bkras phug tu phebs dus smyon ma zhig gis byin rlabs zhus gzhan gyis khyod gar phyin dris pas mi pham mgon
la byin rlabs zhur song ba yin zer/ nA lendrar phebs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi dngos slob chos rje sangs rgyas rin chen gyi rje 'di rnal 'byor dbang phyug
rus pa'i rgyan drug can du yun ring por gzigs shing gzim khang du phebs nas da lta'i skur gzigs/ de nas nA lendrar gsung ngag dang rdo rje phreng ba sogs stsal te rtse
gdong du phebs/chu stag mgo zla'i bcu gsum gyi tho rengs paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang zhing khams brjes te de'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub par e waM thar rtser phebs nas dpon
slob lngas sku gdung gi drung snga dro kyai rdor sgrub mchod dang phyi dro bla mchod mdzad/ rgyal

zla'i nyer bdun tho rengs sku gdung kyai rdor sbyin bsreg gi sgo nas zhugs 'bul mdzad de/ yos lo rta zla'i bar kyai rdor sgrub mchod dang bla mchod chag med mdzad/ bco brgyad
nyin gdung rus bsdus shing sku khrus gsol te gdung tsha shin tu phon che bar gnang/ dgongs rdzogs tshogs chen gyi dbur rjes 'jug rnams kyi spyan drangs nas rim bzhin 'du
khang dang/ 'du khang steng dang/ rong po ka drug ma'i tshogs dbur byon te yon bshad sngon 'gro'i gsung bsngo shin tu rgyas pa 'khor gsum yongs dag gi sgo nas paN chen
dam pa de nyid kyi thugs kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs par mdzad/ 'dus tshogs la mang ja gdan bzhes gral 'gyed tshad med dang/ rgyal tshab shar chen drung bsngo rten spang
mtho mdzad/de skabs shar chen la tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang stsal zhing thar rtser tshogs chen la'ang tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang dang/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i dbang sogs chos
char phabs/ drung chen bsod nams shes rab pas sa skya bka' 'bum sogs thar rtse'i phyag rdzas khyad nor rnams phul/ dor gyi thugs brel rnams grub 'phral thub bstan rnam
rgyal du phebs nas kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer ba las bde mchog dril bu rim lnga'i byin rlabs dang 'khrid sogs

chos bka' 'ga' zhig gsan pa dang tshogs chos kha shas stsal nas rtse gdong du phebs/ma 'gyangs par shar chen kun dga' bkra shis kyi rje dkon mchog dpal ldan gyi dgongs rdzogs
bka' 'gyur gser chos grub pa dang paN chen brang ti pa'i dngul gdung gsar bzhengs la rab gnas kyi phyir e waM nas spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin phebs skabs 'dus tshogs kyi
ser phreng dang shar chen gyi rdo gcal nas phebs bsu mdzad pa sogs kyis bsnyen bkur te thog mar gtsang khang du paN chen dngul gdung la rje nyid/ shar chen/ zur 'chad pa/
srid gsum slob dpon sogs dpon slob nyung shas kyi rab gnas mdzad par drung chen bsod shes kyis zhabs tog 'bul ba gya nom btab cing/ tshogs chen du'ang dga' ston rgyas
par sgrub/de nas gza' skar bzang po la gong gi dpon slob rnams kyi steng dbu mdzad drung 'khor bsnyen song sogs dpon slob mang pos ka drug mar bka' 'gyur la rab gnas nyin
gsum ma mdzad dus sbyin bdag gi 'dus tshogs su mang ja gdan bzhes dkar spro'i dga' ston dang slar yang 'du khang du rje 'di dpon slob mkhan zur sogs drag bsdus la bur ston
sogs mdzad de

dngos 'bul shin tu rgya cher bstar te gdan sa nas rtse gdong du phebs/ shar chen gyis shing 'brug ngor du gsung ngag gnang skabs snang gsum rdzogs tsam nas bzung yun ring bsnyung
ste sku khams cung zad dwangs pa na thugs dam chag med rnams gso ba'i phyir spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin nag zla'i nang e waM du phebs te rgyu lam gyi dbang dang lam
zab sogs thugs bzhed bzhin gnang nas klu sdings bka' 'gyur lha khang dang gzim khang gsar bzhengs la rab gnas mdzad cing phyis kyang chag med kha gso lan kha shas gsan/
gang ltar ngor gyi thugs brel rnams grub 'phral gdan sar phebs/shing sbrul dpyid thub bstan nas chos 'od zer spyan drangs te gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ 'jigs byed sa lug bde
mchog bong zhal rnams kyi dbang dang mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid sogs gsan/ slar yang me lug dgun spyan drangs te kyai rdor rgyud gsum gyi
bshad bka' dang/ bde mchog rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang/ rgyu ma chen mo'i dbang/ tshe bka' dang rjes gnang du ma gsan/sa spre chu stod tshes brgyad la chos 'od zer gshegs pa'i
dgongs rdzogs thub bstan du mang ja gdan non gdung 'bul

snyan dar/ gdung chog pa nyi shu skor la bsnyen bkur sogs dgongs rdzogs rlabs chen mdzad/ de skabs tsam la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i drung nas gsung ngag yongs rdzogs/
phur pa'i stod las smad las gur zhal sogs kyi rjes gnang/ tshe bka'/ jo bo'i chos 'byung brgya rtsa'i lung rnams gsan no/ /gzhan yang dbus su yang yang phebs skabs nA
lendrar gsung ngag tshar du ma dang dbang bka' grangs mang/ sems bskyed rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sogs kyi sgo nas bstan 'gro'i don mdzad cing/ mkhar rtse/ stag lung/ grub
rgyal/ mtsho kha dga' ldan rtse/ spyang lung chos sde/ dga' mo/ lo dgon pa/ rgya ma rin chen sgang/ 'chad kha sogs su'ang spyan drangs te mchod cing lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas
kun gyi re ba bskang/ spyang lung pa dang rin sgang pa gnyis kyis mchod gzhis mang po yang phul/ skabs shig zhwa dmar mchog sprul rin po che drug pa gar dbang chos kyi
dbang phyug khams phyogs nas za dam du phebs pa la sngar nas thugs 'dris yod pa bzhin/ mtshams zhu gnang zhing/ rgyal ba karma pas kyang sku khyos gya nom phul/ yar lam
sne gdong chos sde/ snye phu/ 'jun/ chu shur sogs nas kyang bsnyen bkur

zhing/ yar rgyab dang skyid shag phreng gsum sogs sbyin bdag rnams dang gong dkar chos sdes spyan drangs te mchod cing chos 'brel stsal/ gnas der rjes sor phebs skabs zhig
dge slong bsnyen pa mang po song ba zhig gi rmi lam du/ sang 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs 'dir phebs rgyu yin zer ba'i phyi nyin rje 'di phebs par grags shing/ gar phebs phal
cher du me tog gi char babs pa ni kun la gsal/de nas rim gyi rgyal mkhar rtser dpal 'khor rtser dpal 'khor chos sde'i ser phreng dang bcas spyan drangs nas bsnyen bkur
