gya nom dang/ mang 'gyed chos dang zang zing gi bka' drin rgya chen bstsal/ me tog char shin tu 'babs bzang bar byung bas sku 'khor rnams kyis gos steng du'ang skya chil
ba byung/ de nas rtse chen/ 'brong rtse/ ram pa/ dga' bde/ byams chen sogs su rim gyis phebs shing/ lha sde/ mi sde tshang ma'i re ba bskang zhing byams chen la mchod 'bul
snyan shal smon lam mdzad/ rin spungs mi dbang sku mched kyi bsnyen bkur zhing bka' chos bstsal/ mgon sku ngo mtshar can sogs phul/ gzhan yang bya bzang du 'ang lan du
mar phebs shing/ mchod yon 'brel shin tu zab pa dang/ pho brang bsam grub rtser mi dbang

kun spangs karma lha dbang rdo rje/ karma mthu stobs rnam rgyal/ karma bstan srung dbang po/ dpon sa yar rgyab ma/ rgyal bu karma phun tshogs rnam rgyal rnams kyis yang yang
spyan drangs shing 'byor pa rgya chen pos mchod/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas dbu bla'i mchog tu 'dzin cing/ mchod gzhis 'ga' zhig kyang 'bul bar mdzad do/ /skabs shig gser
mdog can du rten chen rab gnas la spyan drangs te bsu ba dang zhabs tog bla med sgrub cing/ paN chen rin po che'i chos khri'i steng nas gsung chos du ma gnang ba dang/
rab gnas mang 'gyed sogs kyi re 'bras bstsal/ lha khud/ zha lu/ ri shing/ tshong 'dus/ lcags stod sogs kyis kyang mchod cing chos sbyin mdzad/ gdan sar phebs nas rdo rje
'jigs byed dang nag po chen po la sogs pa'i ljags bsnyen mdzad cing/ gcung 'jig rten dbang phyug gis gsol ba btab nas dbyar chos la gong ma lnga/ ngor chen/ sa lo rnams
kyi bka' 'bum lung dang/ dbang rjes gnang du ma mdzad/ gra rgyun rnams la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sogs yid bzhin du stsal zhing/ bar skabs su bdud rtsi ril sgrub 'ga' yang
gnang bar 'phel che zhing dri'i phyogs kun khyab pa sogs mkha' 'gro mnyes pa'i mtshan

ma du ma bsnyes so/ /de nas dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa lnga pa shing yos shar chen kun dga' bkra shis sku khams shin tu ma bde bas gsung ngag gnang ma thub pa'i tshab tu spyan
'dren byung ba bzhin e waM du phebs te/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi chos khri'i steng nas 'dus tshogs la gsung ngag yongs rdzogs cha lag dang bcas pa gnang/ nag zla'i tshes brgyad
la shar chen gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs tshogs dbu dang/ sa ga'i sgrub mchod chen mo'i tshogs dpon/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po rnams mdzad pas 'dus tshogs kyi
gdan sa mdzad par gsol yang/ re zhig rtse gdong du phebs nas lo de'i ston rje nyid kyis mkhan po/ dkon mchog rgya mtshos las slob/ snying rje bzang pos gsang ston/ shes
rab rgyal mtshan gyis grib tshod pa mdzad de/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas la bsnyen rdzogs stsal/ ston chos dang bstun e waM du phebs nas 'dus tshogs la rdor phreng dge
legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor dang bcas pa'i dbang bskur mdzad pa'i tshe lha ngo ston pa na mngon rtogs rgyas pa gsung pa sogs phyag len zhib mos zla gcig gi bar du chos
'khor bskor/ de nas dgun chos gsung ngag gsung ba dang bstun rje rdo rje 'chang gi gdan sar mnga' gsol te/ lo gsum

gyi bar la gnas mchog de nyid du mnga' ris dbus gtsang khams dwags kong sogs nas 'dus pa'i tshogs pa dgu brgya tsam la gsung ngag smin grol yongs rdzogs tshar re dang/ lo re
bzhin rab byung bsnyen rdzogs don gnyer nyis brgya tsam re'i mkhan po dang/ phur dbang sogs dbang bka' sgrubs brgya rgyam sogs spyi bka' zur bka'i rjes gnang du ma/ 'dul
ba'i las chog gi lung sogs lung gi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pas so so'i re ba skong shing/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba dang gsung 'phros khyad par chags sdang can gyi gtam la
thugs mi 'jug cing/ zang zing gi dngos po bzang ngan la rtog dpyod mi mdzad par chos mi gsung ba'i dus thams cad du thugs dam dang/ phyag dpe gzigs rtog kho na mdzad cing/
khrims mthun tshogs skad gnang dgos rnams kyang phog thug byung dwogs gzhan la gyis gsung ba dang/ mkhan pos cis kyang gsung dgos rnams gzhan gyi yi ger bris nas phul
ba de ljags klog tsam las dngos su mi gsungs pa sogs snyom chung chos mthun kho na'i mdzad pas bstan pa bskyangs pas thams cad dad cing/ dam tshig gi nyes pa med par gyur/
chos gzhis 'dzin skyong sogs 'jig rten dang 'brel ba'i bya ba rnams drung chen bgres gzhon gyis mdzad do/ /

sa rta sa ga sgrub mchod grol nas mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub gdan sar bskos te rtse gdong du phebs/ e waM du phebs pa'i yar mar snga phyi du mar bsam grub rtser mi dbang
phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis yang yang spyan drangs nas brgya 'bul mang po dang dbus gtsang gi chos gzhis 'ga' zhig kyang phul te/ dbang rjes gnang sogs chos char rgya cher
phabs shing/ mi dbang chen po nyid rje 'di'i yon tan la thugs nges shes 'drongs te sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes mdzad do/ /rta lo'i dgun brag rdzong ma'i ljags bsnyen
yun ring mdzad pa'i tshe srod thun gyi thun gtor bya rog gis rgyun du len zhing/ snga dro bzhengs phyis na zhabs pus nas bteg nyams zhig yang yang byung bas/ sku drung
pa rnams la khyed tshos bteg pa min nam gsungs shing/ lhun po rtse'i ltag tu sgrub chu thon te 'khyag ba gsum byung ba sogs grub pa'i mtshan ma brnyes so/ /lug lo gcung 'jig
rten dbang phyug gi gtso mdzad gzhis byes dad 'dus rnams la rtse gdong du gsung ngag gnang/ spre lo nA lendrar phebs nas rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang dang gsung ngag sogs
chos 'khor bskor/ rgya ma rin chen sgang du gsung ngag gnang ba sogs bka' chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa stsol ba'i ngang nas dbus

su zla ba bcu gsum bzhugs te yar phebs/ lcags bya mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags spyan drangs nas gur gyi mgon po'i dbang rjes gnang lung 'khrid rnams
dang/ zhal gyi rjes gnang lung 'khrid/ dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang dang lung/ mkha' spyod ma'i khrid/ dud gsol pod chung/ rnam sras/ bka' gter du ma/ shangs chos ni
gu'i skor dus 'khor gyi dbang tshe bka' sogs chos bka' phon che bar gsan cing/ rje 'dis kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi'i sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis rnams kyi dbang dang/ zur bka'
'ga' zhig sa paN bka' 'bum gyi lung sogs 'bul bar mdzad do/ /chu khyi lo tsher lung pa karma kun dga' rnam rgyal zhes rgyal ba zhwa dmar ba chos kyi dbang phyug dang chos
phar gsan tshur gsan mdzad pa de nyid la rje zhwa dmar bas bkas bskul zhing/ rang nyid kyang thugs dwangs kyi sgo nas gsung ngag zhu bar byon par lam 'bras smin grol cha
lag tshang ma gnang ba bzhin de nyid kyi drung du rgyal ba zhwa dmar bas gsan pa ni gzhan las rmad du byung ba'i rnam thar ro/ / tsher lung pas gcung 'jig rten dbang phyug
la dud sol pod chung gi lung gsan/ shing byi khams nas sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug sa skyar phebs zhor rtse gdong du phebs

te/ kyai rdor rgyu lam gyi dbang sogs dgos gsungs pa bzhin 'bul bar mdzad cing/ chos srid kyi sgo nas khu dbon thugs shin tu mthun par gyur/yang shing glang lo ngag dbang chos
grags phebs te rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang dang kun mkhyen sngags 'bum gyi lung sogs gnang/ tshur tshe bka' sogs 'bul ba mdzad/ gcung 'jig rten dbang phyug zhi bar gshegs
pa'i dgongs rdzogs dang/ rten bzhengs rab gnas sogs mdzad de lo de'i khrims zla'i bcu'i nyin rje nyid kyis mkhan po/ ngag dbang chos grags kyis las slob/ spyan snga kun
dga' don grub kyis gsang ston/ snying rje bzang pos gribs tshod pa/ shes rab rgyan mtshan gyi zhu ba/ chos sku rdo rje ba sogs dad dge'i dbus su gdung brgyud rin po che
byams pa bsod nams lhun grub bsnyen par rdzogs/me stag dpyid ka hor chos rje gshegs nas zam tsher du rje 'di spyan drangs te rjes sgrub rnams mdzad/ de nas rin spungs bdag
mos spyan drangs te mchod cing chos bka' dang rab gnas gtor sgrub sogs mdzad cing 'bras yul skyid tshal 'dus tshogs la'ang chos 'brel gnang/ snron zla'i nyer lnga la snying
rje bzang po dgung lo brgyad cur phebs pa de gshegs/ me yos dpyid nA

lendrar phebs te 'du khang gsar pa'i logs bris zhal bkod dang lam 'bras gnang zhing dga' ston mdzad/ dbyug zla'i bcu gcig gza' skar sbyor ba bzang po nyin sku'i dbon rin po
che byams pa bsod nams lhun grub rong ston chen po'i gdan sar mnga' gsol nas khu dbon gnyis gas chos kyi bka' drin 'ga' zhig stsal te yar phebs/'brug lo'i dbyar dbon rin
po che sku mched kyis gtsos 'dus tshogs la sgrub thabs brgya rgyam gyi rjes gnang stsal/ ngag dbang chos grags spyan drangs te rje nyid la brtan bzhugs dang tshe bka' phul/
rje 'dis mkhan chen de nyid dang dbon rin po che sku mched la rje btsun sku mched dang 'phags pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung gnang/ mkhan chen gyi drung du dbon rin po ches
sa paN bka' 'bum gyi lung sogs chos bka' du ma gsan/ dbon rin po che sku bgres pas ngag dbang chos grags la sa chen gyi bka' 'bum dang rje 'di'i rnam thar snying rje bzang
pos mdzad pa'i lung gnang ste phan tshun chos 'khor rgyun mi chad du bskor/ rje'i dbon mo bsod nams rnam rgyal bu khrid bsam 'grub rtse'i mi dbang chen po'i lcam du bzhugs
pa de la sras 'khrungs te mi dbang chen pos bsam 'grub rtser spyan drangs/ yum sras gnyis la dbang rjes

gnang bsrung 'khor sogs mdzad/rta zla'i mjug sde srid chen po rgyal mkhar rtse nas tshur phebs te sde srid chen po nyid la tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs bka' chos bsam gyis mi
khyab par mdzad cing/ yab sras sku bsrung la sku 'khor nyung shas dang bcas sku mtshams la bzhugs/ dbo zla'i 'gor rgyal ba karma pa bcu pa chos dbyings rdo rje dang/ rje
zhwa dmar ba drug pa gnyis ka bsam rtser phebs te phan tshun dag snang shin tu che bar mdzad/de ltar zla ba drug bzhugs ring lam 'bras bla brgyud bris thang la rab gnas
sogs bstan 'gror phan pa du ma mdzad cing/ mi'i dbang pos zhabs tog rgya cher bzhes nas nyid kyi gdan sar phebs te phur sgrub la sogs mdzod de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'dis
mkhas grub dam pa rnams las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu gson nas/ nyid kyi thugs nyams su bzhes pa dang/ gzhan la spel ba'i tshul ni gong du bshad pa de dag dang 'dir
yang cung zad tsam bsdoms na rgyun gyi nyams bzhes kyi rim par bir bsrung phyi nang/ lam zab phyi nang/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i phyi nang gi bskyed rim dbang rgyas 'bring dang
bcas pa la ljags bzlas du ma/ mkha' spyod ma'i bsgom zlas/ nag po chen po'i bsrung 'khor nang

'khrid nyams len rnams snga thun dgongs thun gyi tshul dang/ phur chung gtor bsngo/ bskang ba sogs chag med mdzad cing/ sgrub mchod/ dus gtor/ gtor bzlog dbang rjes gnang la
sogs pas dus 'da' bar mdzad pa'i gnas skabs thams cad du lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi sgo nas snod bcud thams cad lha dang ye shes kyi rol par gzigs pas bla ma yi dam
mkha' 'gros byin gyis brlabs pa'i dag snang dang mngon par shes pa la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba gdon mi za yang sbas pa'i brtul shugs kho na gtso bor mdzad
cing/ thugs dam gyi tshe mnal lam la ji 'dra byung zhus kyang/ nged lo rta lug yin pas/ lug 'di rmongs pas rmi lam sogs ci yang mi shes phal cher sa lug rang yin pa 'dra
gsung zhing/ gzhan gyis nyid kyi yon tan brjod kyang/ de mi zer ba'i thabs dbyibs kyi bka' phebs pa dang/ gsung brtag zhu ba rnams la'ang/ ngas de 'dra mi shes zhes thag
chod kyi bka' phebs pa las nyis 'gro'i rigs gtan mi mdzad mod/ 'on kyang shugs 'byung du byung ba ni sde srid karma bstan bsrung pa thugs dran med du 'gro ba la gur drag
gi dbang dang/ khro bo bcu'i bsrung 'khor gnang ba tsam gyis sku khams dngas ba dang/ mkhar rtse dpon mo gdon gnod kyis dran pa ma

zin pa la gzhan gyi thabs zhi drag ci byas kyang ma phan par/ rje 'dis gur drag gi dbang gnang ma thag phan pa sogs gdon gnod can rnams la dbang tsam gyis phan thogs pa shin
tu mang ba dang/ dpal gnas pas khang pa la phyag nas zhus pas/ phyis me gnod byung tshe phyag nas kyi sa dang/ bka' shog gdung la 'byar ba rnams ma tshig pa dang yos lo
thang sag chu rags la phyag nas mdzad pas/ de nas chu 'gyur te stod du rdzing chos pa dang/ gzhan yang yul phyogs mang por chu yis khang pa sogs la gnod tshe/ 'dis phyag
nas gtor ba tsam gyis 'gyur 'gro ba dang/ thol byung du bka' gang gnang bzhin nges pa ni/ sbrul lo sde srid karma phun tshogs pas dbus su dpung chen bteg skabs rtse gdong
lhun po rtse'i gro bo lung du snying rje bzang po dang lhan rgyas bzhugs skabs zhig nyi ma shar lhod tsam la/ rje 'dis 'an/ da lta 'khrug pa dang mi bsad stobs chen byed
kyi yod par 'dug gsungs pa la snying rje bas skad cha e gsan ci 'dra zer 'dug zhus pas/ a a nges 'brel med de 'dra zhig lab shor song men men gsungs/ phyis skad cha byung
ba na de nyin dus tshod de tsam la dbus kyi khyung tshang brag gi ldeb la 'khrug pa byung ste thob rgyal phyogs kyi mi du ma rkyen lam du song ba de mkhyen par 'dug zer/

she'u lo tsA ba'i slob ma lcags mo chos mdzad ma'i g.yog mo de nA lendrar gsung ngag zhu ba la yong dus chu nad kyis 'chi la khad pa la bsrung mdud dang byin rlabs mdzad skabs
lcags mo bla ma blo gros brtan pas do dgong sang dgong tsam 'chi ba 'dra zhus pas khams mo da res mi 'chi gsung ba bzhin nad las grol nas gsung ngag yongs rdzogs thob/
yang bsam 'grub rtser mda' dpon sgog lung pa na dus tshe dbang brgya rtsa dang/ 'chi bslu mdzad tshe zhabs phyi 'ga' res/ da lan mda' dpon 'gro ba 'dra zhus pas/ a kha
mda' dpon mi 'chi gsungs pa bzhin nad las grol ba dang/ 'og nas 'byung ba ltar chos sde gsar pa'i sa chog skabs bka' gnang ba rnams de bzhin du gyur pa dang/ 'grul pa sogs
'ong gsungs pa'i nyin 'ongs shing/ mi 'ong gsungs pa'i nyin mi 'ongs pa sogs mdor na thugs mkhyen thogs pa med pa'i rnam thar dpag med yod kyang de tsam las brjod par ma
nus la/ de ltar rnam 'dren dam pa rang nyid mkhas grub kyi go sa mthon por gshegs te gzhan rjes su bzung ba'i tshe smin byed dbang ngam/ grol byed kyi lam mam/ mtha' drug
tshul bzhi'i rgyud don 'chad dam/ zab mo'i byin rlabs stsol lam/ rnam dag sdom pa 'bog pa la sogs pa gang mdzad kyang de

kho na la sbyang pa ltar thogs pa med pa'i sgo nas nA lendrar gsung ngag tshar brgyad/ rgya ma rin chen sgang du gcig e waM chos ldan du bzhi/ rtse gdong tu gnyis te kun sgril
bco lnga gsung ba re re la yang rgyu lam gyi dbang grangs med lta bu dang/ rdo rje phreng ba nA lendrar gnyis/ e waM dang rtse gdong du re re ste bzhi/ sa skya bka' 'bum
tshar gnyis/ rdo rje 'chang dang kun mkhyen bka' 'bum sogs lung du ma/ spyi bka' dang zur bka'i rjes gnang du ma/ sbyong dkyil sogs dbang bka' du ma/ rab byung bsnyen
rdzogs sogs grangs med kyi mkhan po mdzad de gnas skabs de dag tu yang las sla cung zad kyang mi mdzad par nyin mtshan du ma sbrel nas chos 'chad dang thugs dam chag med
rnams la rtag 'grus su mdzad kyang bsnyun mi mnga' zhing/ sku mdangs je rgyas su 'gro ba dang bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub sems kyi kun la bu gcig pa ltar brtse bas gdol
spyod khro gtum can dag sku mdun du slebs ma thag zhi mal gyi 'gro ba sogs bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ /de nas dgung lo nga dgu sbrul lo'i ston dbon rin po cher nA lendra
nas spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin phebs skabs gang ci'i bka' bkod rgyas pa dang/ gye re mdo chod bar phebs skyel

mdzad/ slar bsam 'grub rtser phebs te lcags rta nag zla'i nang kun mkhyen chos rnam pa'i thub bstan du spyan drangs pa bzhin phebs par chu mig mgron lhar mkhan chen nyid phebs
te thab bsu mdzad/ dgon par phebs tshe 'dus tshogs gi ser phreng gis bsus te zhag bcu bzhugs ring mkhan chen nyid la 'jigs byed sa lugs kyi dbang sogs bka' chos che phra
du ma dang/ tshogs chos tshe bka' rjes gnang sogs nyin re bzhin gnang zhing bye spe shag sgang du skya ser du ma la khrom dbang tshe bka'i zhor rtse gdong spyi khang
dang khams pa gra tshang du spyan 'dren zhus te spyi sgos 'bul ba zhabs tog zab cing/ mang ja gnang sbyin gya nom mdzad nas tshur lam bsam 'grub rtse nas rtse gdong du phebs/
thar rtse'i dbon rin po che nam mkha' sangs rgyas rtse gdong du byon par glo bo mkhan chen gyi bka' 'bum lung sogs stsal/de nas bsam 'grub rtser phebs skabs sa skya
nas 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyang der phebs te mjal 'dzom gnang zhing khu dbon phan tshun shin tu dges par gyur te rje nyid kyis 'jam mgon a mes zhabs la tshe dpag lha dgu/
yang dag 'jigs byed sa lugs kyi dbang rnams dang/ 'jigs byed yig cha'i lung/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi 'khrid dang byin rlabs/ kun

mkhyen chen po'i sdom gsum spyi don gyi lung dang/ sdom gsum TIkka'i lung las/ de lta'i ri dwags rgyal po de/ dpal ldan sa skya'i gangs rir gnas zhes pa'i mtshams su chos mtshams
mdzad/ de phyin gsan 'phror lus pa dang/ a mes zhabs kyi sku 'khor rnams la bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhig gnang/de nas rgyal rtse gur pa gra tshang gi 'du khang gsar bzhengs
rab gnas la drung chen sgrub gnyer bas spyan 'dren byung yang sde srid kyi dgongs pa ma bzhengs par rtse gdong nas dbon rin po che byon nas rab gnas grub bstun gzhis
rtser khu dbon lhan rgyas thog rje nyid kyis bka' chos 'ga' zhig bstsal zhing/ dbon rin po ches phur bzlog drug bcu pa'i gtor bzlog mdzad/ sde srid la tshe dkar gyi rjes
gnang dang/ sde srid kyis dpag bsam 'khri shing dang me long TIkka'i thog nas rtsom rgyugs sogs pu ti gsum phul/ dbon drung rtse gdong du phebs/ rje nyid der bzhugs te
sde srid kyi dgongs pa sgrub pa dang/ phan tshun mjal 'phrad zhu ba rnams la bka' chos stsal/lug lo nag zla'i nyer bdun la/ dbon mo sde srid kyi lcam gshegs pa'i rjes kyi
bya ba rnams mdzad de/ dbon mo gzhon pa sde srid kyi btsun mor bzhes pa la bka' chos sogs gnang nas

rtse gdong du 'khor tsam phebs/ ma 'gyangs par bsam rtser phebs te ngag dbang chos grags spyan drangs nas tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs gsan/spre lo'i dpyid shes rab 'byung gnas
kyis e waM du spyan drangs/ ser phreng sogs zhabs tog rgyas par mdzad de/ thar rtse klu sdings gnyis kyi sger du spyan 'dren zhabs tog dang/ rje nyid kyis mang ja bdud
rtsi ril 'gyed sogs gnang sbyin bzang zhing shar chen la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang/ tshogs chen la ri khrod ma'i rjes gnang sogs mdzad de zhag lnga tsam bzhugs nas lcags
nang brgyud de bsam rtser zhag shas dang rtse gdong du phebs nas kyai rdo rje'i ljags bsnyen kha gso zla gcig mdzad de sa ga'i nang ril sgrub mdzad par 'phel che ba sogs
byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma shar zhing slar bsam grub rtser phebs/ dbon drung sa skyar phebs zhor bsam rtser bka' chos 'ga' zhig zhu bar mdzad/ rje nyid rgyal po'i pho brang
du bzhugs par mi dges kyang thugs dbang ma 'dus par lo gsum bzhugs/phag lo gdung brgyud sku gzhon la gsung ngag rtse gdong du gnang bzhed yod kyang sde srid kyi dgongs
pa ma grol bar bsam rtser yar phebs te gdung brgyud/ dbon drung/ mi dbang karma

bstan skyong dbang po/ lcam bsod nams tshe brtan bu khrid rnams la gsung ngag smin grol yongs rdzogs gnang bar thog mtha' bar gsum du tshogs 'khor dang 'bul nod bsam gyis mi
khyab pa bcas grol/ gdung brgyud rtse gdong du phebs nas gzhis bsnyen mdzad/ rje nyid der bzhugs pa la slar yang 'jam mgon a mes zhabs dang mjal 'dzom gyi gsung chos sogs
mang du 'bul bar mdzad nas rtse gdong du spyan drangs te khu dbon mjal 'dzom zhabs tog bla med mdzad de slar gzhis rtser phebs/ de'i dgun sog po a sa lang gi dmag gis
bod 'brog 'joms shing/ 'brum dogs che ba bcas byi lo'i mgo la rtse gdong du phebs te lhun rtser sku mtshams kyi thugs dam shin tu 'phel zhing/ bdud rtsi ril sgrub dang/ skabs
mtshams rnams su dbon drung/ gdung brgyud sku gzhon sogs la sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung sogs bka' chos 'ga' zhig gnang zhing/ yum bgres mo dang nyin ltar lhan rgyas byung
bas yum sras gnyis char gyi thugs kha rdzogs/byi lo'i ston gdung rin po che'i bdag mor yul gdong sras mo nor bu bu khrid bzhes te gsung chos 'ga' zhig gnang/ glang lo'i
dbyar gdung sku mched sogs zhal ngo rnams dang bya bzang pa yab sras/ rtse gdong slob grwa yongs rdzogs la smad las drag po'i

rjes gnang mdzad/ ngag dbang chos grags spyan drangs te tshe bka' sogs gsan/ ston mjug rje nyid gzhis rtser phebs/ ngag dbang chos grags kyi yum bgros mor gsung chos gnang
mur yum sku ma bde bar je lod du song tshe rje nyid rtse gdong du phebs nas zhag bcu song ba glang lo smin drug nyer lnga la yum dgung lo brgyad cu gya bdun pa'i thog tu
sku gshegs rjes/ rje nyid khu dbon dang ngag dbang chos grags kyi gdung chog lam ston sogs dgongs rdzogs dang/ dbus gtsang gi chos sde che phra mtha' dag la mang 'gyed bsngo
rten/ rtse gdong du ser 'du mang 'gyed dpag med mdzad de gsung bsngo'i rgyas 'debs kyi sgo nas rgyal yum dam pa'i dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs pa mdzad/rgyal yum de nyid
ni gzhan las khyad par du 'phags pa zhig ste/ dgung lo bdun pa la bya bzang du ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub la kyai rdor rgyu dbang gsan/ bco lnga ma la rtse gdong du
bdag mor byon nas rje 'di sogs gdung sku mched gsum 'khrungs/ mkhas grub du ma las chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan/ lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa che bas yab sras rnams kyis bka'
bkod ltar/ rgyal rtse nas bka' 'gyur yongs rdzogs spyan drangs te rtse gdong du sbyar nas lo re bzhin tshar du ma 'don pa

dang/ 'dus sder zhabs tog gzab ma dang bcas rje btsun rin po che'i sku bstod yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'jam dpal mtshan brjod/ sgrol sher rnams 'bum ther du ma dang/ rje 'di'i yab
kyi dgongs rdzogs su lam 'bras brgyud thang bcu bdun/ skyes rabs so bzhi/ gnas bcu/ rigs 'dzin bla brgyud rnams kyi bris thang mang po dang/ bka' 'gyur/ dngul gdung/ dbon
drung sku gzhon gyi dgongs rdzogs/ tshe dpag med kyi gser sku/ dbon drung sku bgres kyi zhal bkod mdzad pa'i phur sgrub kyi tshogs rnga shin tu legs pa sum cu so bgrangs/
'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i dgongs rdzogs gu ru rin po che'i gser sku dang/ dbang rdzas sku 'dra chung ngu du ma/ 'jig rten rgya hor gyi dgongs rdzogs bka' 'gyur/
dpag bsam 'khri shing gi zhal thang/ de'i glegs bam gsar bzhengs rgyun sgrog rje 'dis sku rim gser zangs rnam rgyal mchod rten mi tshad/ gur gyi bris sku 'phyar dar che
ba/ yi dam chos skyong gi gtor mgron thang ka che ba grangs mang/ gtsang sde srid kyi lcam bsod nams rnam rgyal bu khrid kyi dgongs rdzogs de nyid kyi sku rgyan la gzhi
byas bzhengs pa'i dngul gdung sogs sku gsung thugs rten mchod cha phon chen gsar bzhengs mdzad skabs rab gnas rgyas pa dang

bzo bo rnams la gla lto yon rdzong phang med du stsol ba zhig go/ /yang rje 'di nyid kyis gsar bzhengs mdzad pa la/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gi gzims mal sku 'dra gser
zangs kyi mda' tshad ma/ shing gi khri rgyab na bza' bcas dang/ dus thang che ba rnams e waM lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs shing/ nyid kyi phyag nas rgyu cha dang gzhan
gyi zhal 'debs bcas rtse gdong dang nA lendra'i 'du khang gi logs bris yum gyi dgongs rdzogs sbyong rgyud zhing khams ma/ mkha' spyod ma sogs kyi gser thang rdor phreng/
sbyong dkyil/ kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi/ bde gsang/ kun rig tshe dpag mi 'khrugs/ yang phur 'jigs byed sogs kyi dkyil 'khor ras bris du ma/ lam zab brgyud thang gser thang
bcu bdun dang/ de'i kha skong gser thang lnga/ dpal sa skya'i gdung brgyud rgyun mi chad par 'byon pa'i rten 'brel du gsang 'dus 'jam rdor brgyud rim bcu gcig mgon po'i
brgyud rim gser thang bcu bdun rnams la gong gsham zhal khebs rnams gos dar shin tu bzang ba dang/ tog ngo mtshar can gyis spras pa la rab tu gnas pa'i byin rlabs kyi gzi
'od 'bar bar sgrub cing mchod rgyun shin tu bzang bas bsnyen bkur/

gzhan yang nyid kyi 'phrin las kyi rgya dkar nag dbus gtsang khams sogs nas rol sil dril gting ngo mtshar can du ma dang/ thar rtse'i sa skya bka' 'bum/ gzhan yang ngor chen/
kun mkhyen/ rje sangs rin/ glo bo mkhan chen/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang rnams kyi bka' 'bum dang/ lam 'bras glegs bam/ sgrub dkyil/ rjes gnang gi po ti/ me 'bar/ snyan
brgyud kha skong gyi ljang dud gsol/ zhal rnams kyi be bum dang/ rje nyid kyi gsan yig sogs gsar bzhengs dang phyag 'byor po ti phon shin tu che bar bzhugs shing/ zang
zing gi dgos po ni char gyi rgyun ltar babs pas de dag kyang log 'tshor mi 'gyur bar yab kyi dgongs rdzogs bde mchog nag po pa/ gcung 'jig rten dbang phyug gi dgongs rdzogs
gsang 'dus 'jam rdor sgrub mchod sogs sngar yod dang gsar 'dzugs kyi sgrub mchod du ma rnams dang/ dus ja/ bla mchod/ dus gtor/ gtor bzlog rnams gzhis su mdzad pa dang/
'brug lo nas bzung gzhis rtse'i ser 'du la grub mtha' ris med kyi dge 'dun stong phrag du ma tshogs pa rnams la mang ja/ grwa tshang so so'i bla mar bsngo rten dang/
dbus gtsang gi dgon sde du mar mang ja bsngo rten 'bul ba rnams la thim par mdzad cing/

sa phyogs gang du phebs kyang mchog dman bar ma'i lha sde mi sde kun gyis mchod cing bsnyen bskur yang khengs dregs cung zad kyang mi mnga' ba dman cha kho na 'dzin par mdzad
cing sku tshe ril por gzhan sems dkrug pa'i tshig rtsub tshig gcig kyang zhal nas gsung ma myong ba sogs byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi rnam par thar
pa kho na mnga' ba yin no/ /de nas dgung lo re bdun pa me glang tha skar zla ba'i tshes bcu gcig la gzhis rtser phebs skabs sde srid chen po'i gsung las/ nged rang gzhon
nu'i dus rgyal rtser phyin pa des yid drangs nas 'dir yang chos sde dang rten bzhengs de 'dra zhig byung na snyam par grwa tshang lngas gtso byas pa'i spos khang byes pa
dang/ phur pa grwa tshang/ thar pa ba/ 'gro don gling pa/ theg mchog gling pa rnams kyis 'dus tshogs kyi gtso bor gtsang gad pa'i sras jo gdan 'di mkhan por bkod rgyu yin
pas tshes bcu gsum la sa chog mdzad dgos de yang ltas mo sogs kyis khyad rdo rje phur pa'i sgo nas gnang bar zhu gsungs pa bzhin/ de phral rtse gdong nas 'chams chas sogs
bzhes te dpon slob nyi shu skor gyi bcu gsum bi spen 'grub sbyor nyin sa chog mdzad de nub smad spre'u'i thog tu sa bskos pa las sol ba thon pas rten 'brel ma legs shing
sde

srid nyid nas lto 'phye'i thig sogs mdzad 'dod yod kyang smin drug bcu gcig bum gter sba ba'i nyin bar thugs snyel bas rten 'brel ma 'grig rje nyid kyi bum gter sgrub mjug
mdzad/ mgo zla'i nang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags gzhis rtser phebs te grwa lnga'i dbang dang/ gdugs dkar legs ldan gyi rjes gnang/ tshe dbang mda' 'phel ma/ brag rdzong
ma'i 'khrid sogs gsan/ phar tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang gnang/ thub bstan mkhan chen don grub dpal bzang gzhis rtser bzhugs pa la kyai rdor rgyu dbang sogs gnang/slar
yang sa stag rta zla'i bcu gnyis la dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis phur pa'i sa chog rgyas pa mdzad skabs bka' bsgo'i tshe dbu gdugs chag pas rje nyid shin tu ma dgyed par
gyur te sa chog grol 'phral zhal ras nag por gyur nas gzim chung du phebs/ dbu zhwa bzhugs lding khar skyur stabs su mdzad nas khyel bzhugs kyi gsung las sde srid kyi sku
tsher bar chad mi yong yang mtshan jus yag po mi yong ba thag chod 'dug gsungs/ de nas sde srid kyis rje nyid la zhal bkod cher ma zhus par gsar bzhengs rtag 'grus su mdzad
pa'i rten gtso sman bla'i gser sku/ klu sgrub/ thogs med sogs rgya gar gyi paN grub du ma'i rdo sku che

ba/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi sku 'dra mi tshad ma sman sku'i rigs che chung du ma bzhengs pa rnams la rab gnas mdzad/ thugs dam rgyun bskang gi dkar mo ba'i gtor
ma las bur chu'am sa zhag 'dra ba'i chu zhig yun ring por zegs/lo de'i nag zla'i nyer gsum la dbon drung bgres bsod nams blo gros dbang phyug gshegs/ dgongs rdzogs rnams
dbon drung sku 'bring byams pa bsod nams lhun grub kyis zhal bkod mdzad/ sde srid kyi ngor nas bzhes pa'i gos sku dang/ gsar bzhengs bzo grwa gong 'og nang bzhugs rten brgya
phrag mang po/ dmar po skor gsum gyi sku che ba/ de dag gi 'khor lo rnams la bgegs skrod rab gnas sogs mdzad/ de dgun stod rtse gdong du 'khor tsam zhig phebs/ mgo zlar
gzhis rtser phebs zhor gser mdog can mkhan chen rdo rje lhun grub kyi chos grwa der rab gnas la spyan 'dren zhus te/ pan mdar thab bsu'i sar mkhan slob bzhi'i chibs bsu
dang/ dgon par gos sku zhal 'byed/ 'dus tshogs kyi ser phreng bcas bya rgod phung po'i chos khri'i steng nas mkhan slob dge 'dun skye bo du ma dang bcas pa la spyan ras
gzigs kyi sgom lung dang/ phyi nyin byams pa'i gser sku chen mo lha khang dang bcas pa la rab gnas mdzad

cing/ 'bul ba zhabs tog rgya chen dang/ mang ja gnang sbyin gya nom mdzad nas gzhis rtser phebs/sa yos sa ga'i nyer lnga pa shes 'grub sbyor nyin/ spang gcal du chos sde gsar
pa'i 'du tshogs thog ma dang/ snron zla'i tshes dgu dang/ bcu la gos sku zhal 'byed/ ston mo mang ja bsnyen bkur rgya cher mdzad skabs rdzong pan bad la me shor/ chos
sde gsar pa'i mtshan la chos 'khor bde chen zhes sde srid kyis gsol/ dge 'dun lnga brgya tsam 'dus nas chos spyod sgrub mchod bskang ba sogs shin tu dar zhing/ bya gshongs
mkhan slob dang/ chos 'khor lhun po'i tshogs pa bzhugs pa'i bka' ram sum cu tsam la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs dang/ mkhan chen sogs la gsung chos 'ga' zhig dang/ bstan 'dzin
sprul sku/ glang bu chos rje sogs la lam 'bras pod dmar ma'i lung gnang/ ston sa skya sgar chen dbus la phebs zhor sde srid kyis spyan drangs te khu dbon dgyes mjal gyi
tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs gnang/ smin drug nyer dgur rtse gdong du gdung brgyud bgres pa sku 'khrungs shing/ dbon drung bgres pa sku khams nyog pas rtse gdong du phebs
te/ de dang yum sras la rkyen sel gnang nas sku khams dang 'phral gzhis rtser phebs/

'brug lo'i nang rten gtso thub dbang/ dngul gdung chen mo rnams la kyai rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dang 'brel ba'i rab gnas zhi rgyas kyi sbyin bsreg bcas mdzad/ glang bu chos rjer
sa lo'i bka' 'bum gyi lung gnang/ sa ga zla nang chos sde gsar pa'i mkhan po jo gdan pa dang/ 'jam mgon sku skye sogs la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sogs gsung chos du ma
gnang/ sku dbon gzhon pa sa skyar phebs zhor yar mar du sde srid kyis spyan drangs ste khu dbon zhal rgyas chos bka' mdzad cing/ dbon drung gi phur bzlog mdzad nas rtse gdong
du phebs/ snron zla'i nang lha khang lho ma'i yum chen mo'i sku la rab gnas dang/ e waM mkhan gsar nam mkha' sangs rgyas zur 'chad pa dang lhan rgyas thog chog grwa
dgu'i lha khang chung ngu rnams la rab gnas mdzad cing gsung chos du ma gnang/ de sngon sa ga'i gos sku zhal 'byed skabs gos sku'i dbu gdugs lcags rting lhungs nas gos sku'i
zhal ras ral/ rgyun du sde srid gzim chung kho nar bzhugs dgos deng rab gnas sogs thugs g.yeng shin tu che yang sku bgres nyams kyi thugs ngal mi mdzad par glang bu chos
rje/ lcags zam pa dang/ ngos bzang dbon po rnams la bka' chos dang/ lha btsun kun bzang rnam rgyal la bsnyen rdzogs dang/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs

rgyas la lam sbas bshad kyi 'khrid sogs lam 'bras skor du ma gnang zhing/ brang ti pas chos sde gsar pa'i bla slob mang po la sbyong dkyil sogs gnang ste ngor du phebs/de nas
chos sde gsar pa'i gtsang khang gi rten gtso gser bzang thub dbang zhal ras la dpangs rgyangs mtho lnga tsam yod par/ 'khor nye sras sman sku thog so do tsam yod pa dang/
lho'i glo 'bur du yum chen mo/ byang du gnas bcu lha khang dang/ lho'i glo 'bur du yum chen mo/ byang du gnas bcu lha khang dang/ 'du khang chen mo/ steng gi g.yab ring
la rdo rje gdan gyi bkod pa'i steng li ma lha khang/ rdo chal khyon shin tu che ba g.yas g.yon mdun rnams su lha khang bco brgyad mdzad pa'i byang shar mgon khang gi steng
nad sel lha khang gi gtso bo gser bzang sman bla mched bdun/ slob dpon dpa' bo dang g.yu thog pa sogs sman brgyud 'bur sku/ zhi mdzad lha khang na seng ge sgra sems
nyid ngal gso/ don zhags lha lnga sogs/ nor lha khang na nor rgyun ma dzam ser nag sogs/ shar lhor g.yos khang/ phyir bzlog lha khang na gtsug tor gdugs dkar sogs/ rnam sras
khang na ser can rta bdun brgyad sogs/ thugs rje lha khang na spyan ras gzigs/ rgyal sras thogs med/ bu dol/ karma dus gsum mkhyen pa sogs karma brgyud rim/ rigs brgyud
lha khang na grwa lnga

sogs/ kun gzigs lha khang na 'jam dbyangs/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paNDi ta/ rje bo dong pa/ rje tsong kha pa/ rje dge 'dun grub sogs/ mkhas grub lha khang na gon gi rdo
sku rnams dang lo chen rin chen bzang po/ chos rgyal lha khang na srong btsan sgam po yab yum dbon blon sogs/ o rgyan lha khang na gu ru mtshan brgyad sogs/ tshe lha khang
na tshe dpag lha dgu/ dbang khang na dmar po skor gsum sogs/ bdud 'dul lha khang na 'od zer can ma sogs/ mgon khang na gur mgon thog so phyed do tsam dang/ yum chen sogs
thog tshad ma/ sgo ma ru 'dren zhal gtso 'khor lnga rnams mi tshad/ mchod gtor spyan gzigs bcas/ myur skyobs lha khang na sgrol ma gtso 'khor/ mda' dpon lha khang na
bka' 'gyur tshar gnyis dang gu ru rin po che sogs/ bgegs 'jom lha khang na 'byung 'dul sogs/ grib sel lha khang na rdor sems rnam 'jom sme brtsegs sogs bzhugs te ming dang
bkod pa thams cad sde srid rang gis mdzad/ grwa tshang so so na gtsang khang thub chen dang/ g.yas su yi dam/ g.yon du mgon khang/ steng du bla ma lha khang/ sgo 'phyor
du li ma lha khang re re dang/ grwa shag mang pos bskor ba/ gos sku spel gyi byang bsil tshal mgon khang nang na traka shad dang phyag drug pa

thog tshad la 'khor phyogs skyong dang bcas pa/ g.yab la stag 'brong sogs kyi sob dang/ gtsug lag khang mgon khang bcas thams cad la logs bris rgyas pa/ phyi sgor rgyal chen
bzhi'i 'bur sku che ba sogs mdzad pas spyir las 'khyon che zhing/ 'ga' zhig la yang yang bzo dgos sogs shin tu 'gor che bas rje 'dis gsung las sde srid kyi mdzad pa 'di
dkar phyogs kho nar 'dug kyang ha cang rang rgya che zhing bkod pa mang grags pas ci 'dra zhig 'ong ngam zhes yang yang gsungs pa dang/'brug lo smin drug tshes gnyis la
thub chen rgyab yol rab gnas dang/ 'go zla'i tshes bdun sogs nas thar phur 'gro gling theg gling rnams kyi gtsug lag khang rten bcas la rab gnas rim can dang/ jo gdan par
gur mgon dang rnam sras phur pa bar zhal dang dkar bdud/ theg gling par ma ning dang phyag bzhi yul 'khor bsrung/ 'gro gling par phyag bzhi ber nag thar pa bar phyag drug
trag shad rnams kyi rjes gnang mdzad cing/ gtsug lag khang yongs rdzogs zhal la gtad chog mdzad nas smin drug nyer gsum la rtse gdong du phebs te/ dbon drung la thugs dam
kha gso'i dbang byin rlabs dang/ zhal ngo so sor bka' chos gdung brgyud la mtshan gsol/ mgon khang rnams su gsung

bskang mdzad de gzhis rtser phebs/ ser 'du grub nas rgyal zla'i tshes bzhi la sku 'bum chen mo'i sa chog skabs gtsang gzhung thal 'tshub kyis khengs pa sogs rten 'brel ma legs/
de skabs rab byung bsnyen rdzogs dad chag med gso dgos rnams la de bzhin gnang/lcags sbrul ngag dbang chos grags phebs nas tshe dbang brtan bzhugs sogs phul zhing/ rje
nyid kyis sde srid zhal ngo rnams la tshe bka' sogs mdzad de rtse gdong du phebs/ dbo zla'i nang ljags bsnyen kha gso dang/ ril sgrub/ mgon khang so sor gsung bskang bcas
mdzad skabs rin spungs dpon pos spyan 'dren byung yang gtsang nas dgongs pa ma grol bar thugs cung zad ma dgyes/ nag zla'i tshes bdun la gdung sku mched sku 'khor bcas
kyis zhabs brtan phul bar rten 'brel cung zad ma legs/ sa ga'i tshes bcu bzhi la rtse gdong nas phebs te gdung sku mched kyis phebs skyel mdzad par phyag dbang bka' bsgo
bslab bya rgyas par gnang zhing/ dpon slob rnams sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i phan tshun thugs shin tu 'phreng bar byung/ sang nyin grur phebs skabs ri dur gyi sgra chen po
dang bcas gzhis rtser phebs nas/ sa ga'i tshes brgyad la mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen

pa ngag dbang chos grags dgung lo bdun cu'i thog zhing khams brjes pa'i dgongs rdzogs 'bul mi slebs par ljags bsngo mchod 'bul sogs rgyas par mdzad skabs sog po'i skad cha
che bar byung bas lo de'i smon lam khrum zla'i bar 'gyangs pa'i bka' bkod gnang kyang ji bzhin ma byung bar chos sde gsar par grwa tshang lnga la grwa grangs stong phrag
gnyis gsum yong ba'i mi brtsi btsun khral/ lha khang gi mjug skyong sogs la sde srid thugs yengs skabs snron zla'i tshes dgu nas bzung gug shri rgyal po'i dmag gis gzhis
rtse yongs rdzogs bskor te 'thab rtsod shi don sogs zla ba gsum lhag tsam byas rjes dga' ldan pho brang pa'i phyag mdzod chen mos gtsos dbus dmag rnams kyang yar slebs zhor
gtsang dmag kyang kha shas bskul nas rta lo dbo zla nas bzung zla ba dgu lhag tsam rdzong bskor te dmyal khams ji lta ba bzhin byung skabs rje nyid rdzong gi rtser thugs
yid 'byung drag pos thugs dam la brtson zhing dus 'khrug myur du zhi ba'i gsol 'debs rtag 'grus dang/ dgra gnyen thams cad la nye ring med pa'i byams snying rje chen pos
bde 'jags yong ba'i thabs kho na lhur mdzad kyang/ sems can gyi las 'phags pa'i thugs rjes bzlog dka' ba der snang/

de skabs zhabs 'bring pa bstan 'dzin lhun 'grub la mgon po me 'bar ma dang/ glang bu chos rje la bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma'i lung gnang 'gro yod pa de mdzad bzhed yod kyang sde
srid kyi bkas glang bu bar zhu long ma byung bar bstan lhun la 'phro nyan pa legs gsungs pa la/ zhabs phyi dag gis slar glang bu ba dang lhan gcig gnang chog zhus pas/ da
glang bu ba la byed dgos mi yong gsungs shing/ de skabs sku la snyun med kyang phyag rtsa mi bde ba zhig byung nas/ sku rim spong dag ltos chen rdzong nang gi dge 'dun
stong phrag tsam la yang yang gnang/ mchod pa 'phar ma gshom gsungs shing/ mtshan mo yang mnal mi mdzad par bzhugs khrir phebs nas thugs dam dang zhabs skor sgron me'i 'od
la ljags klog sogs mdzad do/ /de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di zhing khams gzhan du phebs pa'i snga ltas gong du cung zad bshad pa de dag dang/ chu rta rta zla'i tshes gsum
nas rtse gdong gi chos dung gsung mi 'byin zhing/ chu mig che chung rnams skam/ de dus rje 'dis bsod nams don 'grub sogs tshe 'das du ma la lam ston gsung bsngo rnams mdzad
nas/ 'o cho ga de rnams tshar bas blo bde gsungs/ zhabs phyi rnams kyis sku rim nar mar sgrub kyang sku nyams je chung du song

rung sde srid zhal ngo gsum la tshe bka' sogs gang dgos gnang/ dbo zla'i tshes drug la sku shin tu dub par gyur pas sku rim rgya cher sgrub/ tshes bdun la rtse nas phyogs thams
cad du gzigs te rgyal khams bde ba'i thugs smon gnang/ tshes brgyad la snyun med pa'i tshul mdzad nas zhal 'don kho nar rtag 'grus su bzhugs te dgung lo don gnyis pa
chu rta dbo zla'i tshes dgu'i nyi ma phyed tsam la 'da' kha ma'i nyams bzhes mdzad nas dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan to/ /de'i mtshan 'das pa'i tho rengs
gtsang blon rnams nang rul nas chos sde gsar pa'i 'dzin cha rnams shor te grwa tshang lnga'i sku gsung thugs rten mchod cha phod ka thang thebs/ gser rnga gra 'grig grwa
pa'i gzab spros rnams skad cig la 'phrogs te gsod gcod 'phrog 'joms kyi sgo nas bstan 'gro'i bde skyid thams cad 'joms pa'i las la mngon par brtson par gyur to/ /de nas
sku 'khor dge bshes 'ga' zhig gis bla mchod gsol mchod mdzad cing tshes dgu nas bzung nyi 'od gsal la me tog gi char babs pas gshegs pa gsang kyang phyis dmag mi blo rno
ba 'ga' zhig gis shes te/ kha sang nas bla ma des bsrung 'khor bzang bas rdzong ma phebs par 'dug da bla ma gshegs pas

rdzong thob byung zer ba sogs gsang ma thub bo/ / thugs dam ma grol yang dus 'gyur gyi stabs chos rje glang bu ba chos skyong dbang phyug gi zhu ba bslus bskul gyi thugs dam
bkrol te tshes bcu gnyis kyi srod kyi cha la chos rje de dang dbu mdzad lhun rgyal bas sku gdung chas su bcug nas spur sgam du bzhugs nas mchod pa phul/'jam mgon a mes
zhabs bkra shis lhun por bzhugs pa la dbu thebs/ gsol phod/ phyag ting/ zhal dkar 'bras shel/ 'phags pa rin po che'i gsol spang/ sil snyan bzang ba sogs thugs dam gsal 'debs
bsngo rten rgya spangs che ba dang/ thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pho brang pa'i phyag mdzod chen mo/ gug shri rgyal po rnams la'ang
dngos po rgya cher phul te dgongs pa bkrol nas lam srung mgo dkar ba dang bcas sku gdung rin po che nyer gsum la rdzong nas thon te gnas rnying rgyal khang du bzhugs/ de
nas nyer lnga'i snga dro sde srid rin po che bkra shis lhun por phebs dgos shar/ de nyin sku gdung rtse gdong lhun po rtser phebs te nag zla'i bcu bzhi'i bar bzhugs pa la
brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas dang/ gdung sku mched gnyis kyis tshogs dpon mdzad de kyai rdor sgrub

mchod tshar gnyis re dang/ ban tshang pa rnams kyis sku gdung drung rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub mchod dang/ bla mchod/ 'du khang/ zur chen/ bla brang sde yangs rnams su gzhis byes
kyi gser tshogs rgya chen pos smon lam mdzad par mang ja gdan non 'gyed sogs spyi sgos la gya nom zhus/bcu bzhi'i nub mo rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis kyai rdor gyi sgo
nas gdung zhu mdzad par/ bud shing tsan dan dkar dmar kho nas bgyis pa sogs mchod pa'i tshogs rgya chen po'i mchod pa'i nyin thar rtser 'bul chen/ sgrub mchod pa gzhan
la yon/ tshogs chen la mang 'gyed/ mnga' zhabs la nas sogs skam 'gyed mdzad/bcu dgu la gdung khang dang gdung rus bsdus pas phal cher gdung log dang/ 'ga' zhig la ring bsrel
kyang thon/ klu sdings su sman sku mda' khang gang ma dus ja thang ka che legs gsum rnams grub rim bzhin rab gnas dang gro bzhin tshes gcig nas bal po mgon po dang dzi
na sogs brgyad kyis dngul gdung bzhengs par zangs rtse gdong gi khal zhe brgyad dang nyag bcu gnyis/ dngul khal drug dang nyag dgu srang drug zho lnga/ gser srang so bdun/
g.yu khra ltos che ba sogs kyi shin tu sgros

gtsang bar sgrub/de skabs sde gzar gyis dbus gtsang la 'grim 'grul shin tu dka' bar yod kyang bsod nams rig 'dzin dpon g.yog dbus phyogs su dgongs rdzogs do dam par thon te
jo zhal rnam gnyis la gser zhal/ thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang rgya mtsho dang/ sa skya sgar chen rnams la gsung bsngo'i rten/ ser 'bras nA lendra sogs grub mtha' ris med
kyi dgon par mang 'gyed ltos che ba dang/ gtsang du'ang dgongs rdzogs do dam pa mngags te sa skyar chos dung gsung bskul gyi mang 'gyed/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs la bsngo
rten/ e waM du rje rdo rje 'chang gi dus mchod chen mo de lo cung dka' bar yod 'dug pa la 'dis dgongs rdzogs kyi gzhi bzung ste ngor lugs sgrub mchod lnga nyin du mar btsugs
par mang ja gnyis dang tsam khal 'gyed/ mkhan chen shar chen la bsngo rten spam mtho ba/ bkra shis lhun por mang ja rgyab bcas thog rje blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan
la 'bul chen/ thub bstan rnam rgyal/ gser mdog can/ 'bras yul skyid tshal sogs dgon sde mang por mang 'gyed/ rgyal ba karma pa chos dbyings rdo rje/ drung rgyal tshab sprul
sku/ stag lung khu dbon/ 'brug gdung brgyud sogs mkhas grub rnams la bsngo rten spam

mtho ba dang sku tshigs lo zla dus dran gyi mchod par dgon sde mang por mang 'gyed mdzad/dngul gdung rin po che ring bsrel rnam bzhi'i snying po can rtse gdong srid gsum rnam
rgyal gyi gtsang khang mthil du bzhugs pa la mgo zla'i tshes bzhi'i nyin lhag gnas kyi me tog gtor te snyan dar mchod tshogs rgya chen pos mchod cing zla mchod rnal 'byor
ma'i sgrub mchod dang bla mchod/ lo dus kyi mchod par kyai rdor sgrub mchod zhag bdun rnams sgrub pa ste/ de thams cad dbon rin po che sku mched dang phyag mdzod kun
dga' legs pas dad gus chen po'i ngang nas sgrub pa yin no/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'dis sku tshe hril por 'chad nyan kho na mdzad pas zhal slob nor 'dzin dpal mo'i rdul
snyed bzhugs pa rnams las/ cung zad tsam zhig smos na/ gcung rin po che 'jig rten dbang phyug gdung brgyud gsum dang bcas pa/ zhabs drung sgar chen dang/ 'jam mgon a mes
zhabs/ thub bstan mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan dang/ chos 'od zer/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis dang shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas
grub dpal ldan don grub/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ thub

bstan pa rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ gser mdog can gyi mkhan chen shAkya bstan 'dzin/ spyan snga kun dga' don 'grub/ shangs brgya tsho bla ma dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rje snying
rje bzang po/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje dbon bcas/ 'brug gdung brgyud mi pham bstan pa'i nyi ma/ ri shing zhabs drung/ tsher lung karma kun dga' rnam rgyal/ stag lung
zhabs drung ngag dbang bkra shis dpal grub la sogs pa mkhas grub dang chen po'i gdung 'dzin pa du ma dang/ sde srid karma phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ karma bstan skyong dbang
po sogs chos bzhin du spyod pa'i rgyal po du ma ste mdor na bstan 'gror sman pa'i zhal slob bgrang bar mi bzod pa bskrun par mdzad do/ /tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/de'i gcung tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal mtshan nam ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni chu mo bya la 'khrungs/
gsan sbyongs dang thugs dam mdzad nas dgung lo bco brgyad pa lcags stag rta zla'i bcu gnyis la gshegs/

'jig rten rgya hor/de'i gcung 'jig rten rgya hor ni sa stag lo sku 'khrungs pa'i tshe rtse gdong gi nags shing rnams la bya rigs mi gcig pa du ma 'dus nas skad snyan par bsgrags/
gzhon nu nas paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang/ byams pa rab brtan/ chos 'od zer/ gcen sku bgres pa rnams las gsung ngag smin grol/ bde mchog gi dbang/ sa skya bka' 'bum
gyi lung sogs chos du ma gsan cing/ bla ma dam pa rnams la sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes mdzad de ci gsung dang len dang/ phyag dang ldang ba chos dgug bsnyen bkur sogs
phal pas sgrub par mi nus pa'i zhabs tog mdzad cing/ gzim khang dben par thugs dam kho na la bzhugs pas ting nge 'dzin dang nyams rtogs kyi mthar son/ rig gnas kun la
thugs byang chub cing/ byams snying rje byang chub sems kyi thugs rgyud phyug cing zhi dul brtan pa'i yon tan mnga' bas mtshan yang ngag dbang 'jig rten dbang phyug bkra
shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes grags shing/ gzhon nu'i dus sku mched gsum gyis paN chen nam mkha' dpal

bzang la chos gsan skabs shig dam pa 'dis jo lags ni zla ba gsum rang yin pa gda' lags so/ / gsung ba paN chen dang drung chen bsod shes thugs la bzhag pas zla ba gsum nas
sku 'bring sku gshegs pas de mngon shes kyi mkhyen par 'dug gsung/ de ltar dgung lo zhe brgyad kyi bar skyes bu dam pa'i mdzad pa du ma mdzad nas shing glang sa ga'i nyer
dgu la gshegs/ sku gdung zhugs la phul bas ring bsrel du ma byon no/ / de rnams kyi spyi don bstan zin pas/ngag dbang bsod nams blo gros/gnyis pa gzhung gi don ni/ 'jig
rten dbang phyug gi btsun mor stag lung pa'i sras mo nor 'dzom bu khrid bzhes pa la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba ni/ ngag dbang bsod nams blo gros bkra shis grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po sa mo phag gi lo 'khrungs/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa'i dus rdo rje la phyag g.yas kyi rjes 'dam brdzis ltar bzhag pa sogs grub rtags mang po mdzad de
gzhon nu la gshegs/byams pa bsod nams lhun grub/gcung byams pa bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po chu mo glang shing sbrul zhes pa'ang snang
bas dpyad gi lo sku 'khrungs te/ gsan bsam dang nA lendra'i gdan sa mdzad pa sogs gong 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub kyi rnam thar dang 'og tu bsod nams bstan 'dzin
dbang po'i rnam thar du thor tsam bshad pa ltar mdzad de/ gcung ngag dbang bsod nams lhun grub ni chu mo glang gi lo sku 'khrungs te gcen sku mched dang 'jam mgon a mes
zhabs sogs dam pa du ma las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son te rnam dkar lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pa rgya chen po'i sgo nas spyi sgos bstan 'gro'i don mtha' yas par mdzad
de 'og nas 'byung ba ltar mdzad pa mthar phyin to/ /'jam mgon bstan 'dzin dbang po/bdag chen de nyid kyi yul gdong pa'i sras mo nor bu bu

khrid khab tu bzhes pa la sa yos smin drug nyer dgu lhag pa lha mtshams kyi 'grub sbyor thog 'jam mgon bstan 'dzin dbang po rtse gdong rnam sras klu sdings gzim chung nyi 'od
'khyil par yum la gnod pa med par 'khrungs/ rje 'di lhums su bzhugs pa'i tshe yum sku khams bzang zhing thugs chos la 'jug pa dang/ mnal lam du bla ma gong ma'i gdung
tsha yin snyam pa'i lha sku dang/ sAtstsha chung ngu gser gsol ma 'thu ba dang sku'i rgyab mdun thams cad de 'dras gtams shing/ tshe dpag med kyi sku zhig lhums su bzhugs
pa shar ro/ /'khrungs ma thag khu bo 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub kyi tshe bka' sogs rkyen sel du ma dang/ 'jam dbyangs kyi ljags bzlas ljags mar zhu bar mdzad cing
mtshan zhus pa'i tshe thog mar 'og rab byung mdzad skabs kyi mtshan de gnang ba la rkyen cung zad zhig gi 'gyur nas kun dga' bsod nams grags pa tshe dbang rdo rjer gsol/
'brug sbrul gyi lo gnyis dang gsum bzhes skabs kyang tshe bka' sogs rkyen sel du ma gsan/dgung lo lnga pa chu lug tha skar nas bzung thub bstan mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan
pa'i rdo rje dbu blar bzhes te khu bo dang yab yum sras bcas la rnam rgyal/ tshe dpag med dkar po/

'jam dbyangs kyi rjes gnang sogs dang/ sa chog nas brtsams te dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa bdun ldan gyi sgo nas kyai rdor rgyu dbang dang/ gzhan yang dbang rjes gnang lung
man ngag du ma gsan/dgung lo drug pa sgrol byed kyi lo sa ga'i bcu gcig nas zla ba bzhi'i ring gsung ngag smin grol lung bcas tshang ma gsan/dgung lo bdun pa sa skyong gi
lo sbyongs dkyil bcu gnyis/ kyai rdor gzhung 'grel la brten pa gsum rnams kyi dbang dang/ sgrub thabs brgya rgyam gyi rjes gnang/ de'i rgya bod kyi yig skor gyi lung rnams
gsan/ bdag chen khu bo las phur dbang gsan te me khyi dgung lo brgyad par phur sgrub la byon par 'chams sogs brda' bstan pa tsam gyis mkhyen te 'chams sbyong skabs 'chams
dpon mdzad/ mi 'jigs spobs pas 'chams dang 'chams skad thams cad 'khrul med dang/ dngos gzhi'i tshe bdag chen khu bo dang yab gnyis 'chams dpon du phebs pa'i 'chams sne
ba sku chung ngu des mdzad pa na/ mkhas dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje sogs mchog dman thams cad ha las te/ 'di 'dra ngo mtshar can yin pa 'dug zhes snyan grags kyis khyab/
ston ka rje bstan rdor las gsang 'dus 'phags lugs dang/ gur sam sogs kyi

dbang gsan/dgung lo dgu pa me phag rta zla'i tshes 'gor 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang chos 'chad kyi thog mar gnang/ dbo zla'i bcu gcig la mkhan slob rje bstan rdor/
grib tshod pa chos bka' rnam rgyal/ dbu mdzad lhun rgyal sogs kyi dbus su rab byung zhus te mtshan brje ba'i skabs mkhan po'i gsung las/ sngar gzhon nu'i dus bdag chen khu
bos mtshan gnang ba rkyen cung zad kyi gzhan du 'gyur bas/ da lam sngar gyi mtshan de gsol dgos gsungs nas/ bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po rdo rje rgyal mtshan grags pa
dpal bzang po zhus na sngar gyi mtshan kyang tshang ba 'dra gsungs pas de bzhin gnang/ nag zlar mkhan po las rdor phreng kri ya dang bcas pa'i dbang gsan tshe mkhan po'i
gsung las 'di rdor phreng gi phyag len rgyas pa'i lugs yin pas gdung rin po ches kyang slad nas de bzhin dgongs dgos gsungs/ gzhan yang grub thob sa ru bya bral ba'i lugs
kyi spyod skor yig cha gsar rnying yongs rdzogs kyi lung byin rlabs dang/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar 'khrid sogs gsan/byi glang gnyis la rtse gdong srid gsum dang klu sdings
su bzhugs nas gsan sbyongs gtso bor mdzad/ khyi phag byi glang gi

lo la rje 'di mnal rkyen gyi thugs dran med la 'gro ba zhig byung bar/ mkhan chen gyis gur drag gi dbang yang yang stsal bas dwangs shing/ gur drag gi zhal yang gzigs/ lhag
lha'i gtso bo gur drag la mdzad/ lcags stag dbo zla'i tshes lnga nas bzung khrums zla'i bcu bzhi bar mkhan chen las slar yang gsung ngag dang/ ni gu sbyong dkyil/ rigs gsum
spyi dang a ra pa tsa na'i dbang rdul tshon/ bka' gdams glegs bam sogs gsan te mkhan chen thub bstan du byon/ lo der thub bstan mkhan chen gnyis btud nas gshegs pas rje
bstan rdor gyi slar yang gdan sa mdzad/yos lo rta zla'i nang rje 'dis thub bstan du byon par 'dus tshogs kyi ser phreng sogs zhabs tog zab cing mkhan chen nas zab chos
du ma dang/ brda' sprod kyi gzhung 'bul bar mdzad de ston rtse gdong du phebs/ dgun mkhan chen rtse gdong du 'khor tsam phebs nas dpon slob lhan gcig thub bstan du phebs
te gsan sbyong rgyun ma chad par mdzad/ de skabs mkhan chen nas ratna bha dra'i gdan sa rkyang phu dang/ yon tan dpal 'byung gi dgon pa tsha lung gnyis kyang zhal 'dzin
mdzad pas/ dpon slob lhan cig rta nag phur yang yang byon tshe g.yag 'brog dad pa can

rnams kyis mchod cing bka' chos stsal/sbrul lo khra zla'i nang e waM du shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub mchod tshogs dbur mkhan chen dang rje nyid
rtse gdong du phebs/ de lo gcung ngag dbang nor bu bsod nams dbang gi rgyal pos phur sgrub 'chams gsar mdzad/sbrul rta'i lo der bzhugs nas rta lo'i dbyar bkra shis legs
pa phebs bsur 'byor te thub bstan du phebs/ dbyar ston dgun stod rnams bzhugs nas mkhan chen las lam sbas bshad/ nag po rim bzhi blo sbyong don bdun sogs 'khrid mang po
dang dbang lung rjes gnang du ma gsan/ mgo zla'i nang rtse gdong du phebs/lug lo mchu zla'i mjug nas zla ba phyed bzhi'i bar phur bsnyen sbyin bsreg dang bcas pa dang/
spre lo'i nang kun rig dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi ljags bsnyen sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bla brang mchog legs su mdzad/ lo de'i chu stod nyer brgyad la rje bstan rdor ba
zhing brjes pa'i dgongs rdzogs blos mi 'khyud pa dang/ khyad par rje nyid la zhal dkar phyag dril sogs sku chas dngos gtsang ba rnams 'bul ba dang chabs cig rtse gdong chos

sder zhabs rtog nyin gang ma/ slar yang mang ja 'bru 'gyed sogs zhus/ dngul gdung dang bka' 'bum bzhengs skabs khams pa shis ngan rnams kyi rgyu ngan la brten drung chen yang
bsnyung nas dngul gdung ma 'grub par thub bstan ngor rtse gdong rnams su rgyu rnams mang 'gyed la btang/ rtse gdong nas kyang gnas de nyid dang/ thub bstan du dgongs rdzogs
mchod 'bul dang dus mchod kyang 'dzin par mdzad do/ /de nas rje nyid dgung lo bcu dgur phebs pa me bya'i dpyid srid gsum chos sder dang phyogs 'dus la kun rig gi dbang
du ma gnang/ dbyar byams pa bsod nams lhun grub lho bod 'ching dan la chibs bsgyur dang/ rje 'dis phur sgrub sogs mdzad de/ de'i dbang dang khyi lo bdag chen khu bo dbus
la chibs bsgyur skabs rje 'dis sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang tshar kha shas mdzad cing/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs dbus nas rong brgyud rtse gdong du phebs par zhal ngo
rtse rgyas drung 'khor rags bsdus bcas kyi chibs bsu dang/ ser phreng rgyas pa bcas klu sdings su byon te zhag gsum bzhugs skabs zhal ngo chos sde'i bla slob grwa rigs bcas
la kyai rdor rgyu lam/ bde mchog rnams kyi dbang dang/ tshe bka' mang po/ o rgyan bla ma'i rnal 'byor/

lam zab/ sa 'jam sbags sgrub/ khyung khra nag 'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ spyan gzigs sgom lung/ 'od dpag med kyi nyal 'pho/ gur zhal/ dur khrod bdag po/ pu tra/ dkar bdud/ bran
bdud rnams kyi rjes gnang/ lung gi rigs 'ga' zhig bcas gsan cing/ khu dbon phan tshun shin tu mnyes par gyur pas bkur sti dang zang zing gi mchod pas phan tshun thugs kha
shin tu tshim zhing/ yar phebs skabs chibs skyel la'ang zhal ngo rnams phebs te chibs gyes kyi tshe a mes zhabs kyis lugs gnyis bslab bya rgyas par bstsal bas thugs shin
tu 'phreng ba'i sgo nas bskal brgyar zhabs pad brtan pa dang/ slad nas mjal thog gsung gi bdud rtsi bzhes pa'i gsol 'debs mdzad de rtse gdong du phebs/ sa ga'i nyer dgu
nas zla brgyad ring phyogs las rnam rgyal du kyai rdor gzhis bsnyen sbyin bsreg bcas dang/ chos skyong gi ljags bsnyen mdun bskyed la brten pa mdzad/dgung lo nyer gcig tu
phebs pa sa phag khra zla'i tshes gsum snga dro'i char khu bo bdag chen byams pa bsod nams lhun grub kyis mkhan po/ rgyal rtse bdag po ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan
gyis las slob/ 'bum phrag gsum pa dge 'dun rgya mtshos gsang ston/ chos dkar rnam rgyal gyis grib tshod/ rtse

gdong srid gsum slob dpon kun bsod pas kha skong mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs skabs mtshan yongs rdzogs bsgyur bzhed la sngar gyi lo rgyus de zhu bar mdzad pas/ 'o na bsod nams bstan
'dzin dbang po zer ba de brjes na mi yong ba e yin gsungs nas/ de'i rjes su byams pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes gnang/de skabs las slob las bu ston las
chog gi lung dang/ gur lha brgyad/ bcu gnyis/ gri gug lha lnga/ kyai rdor rgyu lam rnams kyi dbang dang/ lam zab byin rlabs/ zhen pa bzhi bral dang brag rdzong ma'i 'khrid
sogs gsan/ phar sme brtsegs rjes gnang sogs gnang/ gsang ston las kyai rdor rgyu lam/ lam zab dang bir bsrung/ thun mong ba'i byin rlabs/ gur lha brgyad thun mong ma yin
pa'i rjes gnang/ me 'bar snyan brgyud/ kha skong rnams kyi lung/ gur mgon gsang 'khrid rtsa gsum dril sgrub kyi dbang sogs gsan/ phar sbyong dkyil gnang zhor dbang cha
'ga' zhig dang/ dbyar chos kyai rdor rgyu dbang sogs mdzad de ston dbus phebs kyi thog mar sa skyar phebs skabs chibs bsu ser phreng sogs rgyas par mdzad nas lha chen phun
tshogs gling du phebs phral bzhi thog tu a mes zhabs yab

sras mjal bar mdzad dus/ phan tshun thugs dgyes pa'i gsung gleng rgyas kyang a mes zhabs sku khams zhan pas bka' chos gnang ma thub par/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug
gis 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang mdzad cing gzhis lan zhabs tog rgyas pa dang/ mkhan chen bsod nams bkra shis kyis sne shan mdzad nas gtsug lag khang thams cad dang
skyed lhas byas 'gyur/ bsam brling rnams gnas gzigs mdzad de mchod 'bul stobs che ba dang phyag skor smon lam mdzad cing/ sgo rum dang kha'ur lam gtor/ chos dung gsung
bskul gyi mang 'gyed sogs mdzad de gdan sa'i phebs skyel ba dang bcas rim gyis chu mig sogs brgyud rtse gdong du phebs/lcags byi yab sras lhan cig sa ga'i tshes bcu gcig
la byang lam brgyud dbus phebs mdzad de rje zhwa dmar ba bzhi pa'i dgon pa yangs pa can du bla slob grwa ris kyis spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur 'bul ba rgya chen dang/ mchod
'bul gnas gzigs/ rje bzhi pa'i dus mchod dus 'khor dang mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i thog drangs chog gra sum cu zin tsam la mang 'gyed gzigs tog bcas rim gyis stod lung brgyud
phebs par rgyal lha khang mdun chos rje bco brgyad pa sogs dgon de'i bla slob che gras phebs bsur

'byor te/ de nub dpal ldan rtser bzhugs/nyer drug snga char ser phreng gis bsus te nA lendrar phebs par bla brang khang tshan so sos zhabs tog gzab mas mchod cing/ snron zla'i
tshes lngar pho brang chen po po ta la nas rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen pos bsko mjal khri 'don legs skyes khri 'bul gya nom bcas gleng phu ba dgra 'dul sku
tshab tu mngags te 'dus tshogs dang bcas pas kun mkhyen rong ston chen pos chos khrir mnga' gsol zhing/ lha mi tshang ma'i dga' ston 'bul ba rgyas pa'i thog a ra pa tsa
na'i rjes gnang mdzad/ re zhig yab sras lcang lung chos sdings su phebs/ slar yang de gar bzhugs nas rje 'dis nA lendrar rdo rje phur pa'i dbang bskur cha du ma mdzad/ yab
rje'ang sha ra 'bum chung brgyud gnas der phebs te yab sras lhan cig 'jog po'i nang nas yer pa'i gnas gzigs la phebs te phyag mchod smon lam mdzad nas sang nyin gzhung
zhabs rin po che'i chibs bsu thab 'dzin sogs bdag rgyan bzang ba dang bcas lha sar phebs nas thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por mjal phyag 'bul chen dang po ta la dang lha
sa'i gtsug lag khang rnams su phyag mchod smon lam mdzad de yab rjes stod lung brgyud gtsang dang/ rje nyid sgo la brgyud nA lendrar

phebs te ston bcag grwa rigs rnams la kun rig dbang cha du ma/ phu mda' bar gsum gyi sbyin bdag rnams kyi spyan 'dren bsnyen bkur/ dgun stod chos sdings su zla skor tsam la
spyi sgos chos 'chad rong ston dus mchod dang bstun nA lendrar phebs/mgo zla'i bcu bzhi nas bzung lcags glang nag zla'i bco lnga'i bar tshogs pa nyis brgya lhag tsam la
gsung ngag smin grol yongs rdzogs mdzad pa'i tshe rta zla'i tshes lnga la sems bskyed chen mo'i nyin gnam gshis shin tu dro bas grog po phan tshun gyi chab rom thams cad
zhu nas chu chen rdol bar skyid tshal mkhan chen shes rab rin chen pas/ 'di 'dra thugs rje'i byin rlabs rang yin 'dug ste nged tsho rdzong shar du chu la mi thar ba 'dra
khu tA man sag gsung/ gsung ngag grol nas nyan po ba sku mched kyi spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur 'bul ba rgya che zhing phebs zhor grog mkhar nang so dang bkras sbug jo gdan
pa rnams kyis kyang gdan 'dren zhus/ thams cad du shi gson so so'i re ba bskangs/ zla skor chos sdings su bzhugs/ yul snga sding gi rten gsar la rab gnas dang/ rtsa gsum
dril sgrub kyi dbang sogs chos bka' 'ga' zhig stsal nas/ slar yang lha sar thams cad mkhyen pa mjal phyag mdzad de snron zla'i bcu bdun la chibs kha bsgyur nas bon

grong nang so'i sngon 'gro kun rig stong chog tshogs dbu sogs mdzad de rim gyi chu stod tshes drug la ser phreng dang bcas gdan sar phebs nas gzhis byes zhal ngo lhan rgyas
thog gzhis len sku 'khyos/ 'dus sder mang 'gyed sogs mdzad de mgon khang so sor gtang rag dang phur sgrub mdzad/ e waM nas shar chen dang thar rtse dpon slob chag med gso
bar phebs par de bzhin dang/ rtsa gsum dbang lung sogs gnang/ sa mchod/ gtor bzlog tshe chog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi dus mchod/ mdos chen/ gtor spod rnams mdzad/chu
stag rta zla'i nang sku mtshams dang/ dpyid ka sgrub mchod so so'i tshogs dbu/ dbyar chos gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang cha du ma/ phur sgrub/ ston gnam rtser drug
cu dang rten mdos 'dzugs pa/ gtor bzlog chen mo/ tshe chog sogs rim bzhin mdzad de li thang grwa rgyun mang 'byor rnams la gu ru zhi drag dang kyai rdor rgyu dbang rnam
'joms rjes gnang sogs mdzad cing/ mdos chen rol dpon sogs mdzad/ chu yos rta zla'i mjug gi kyai rdor sgrub mchod tshogs dpon sogs rgyun bzhin mdzad de khra zla'i nang las
slob rgyal rtse ba las chag med gso ba dang lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi 'khrid gu ru drag dmar mthing/

mda' 'phel dang grub thob tshe dbang/ tshe ring ma'i rjes gnang/sa lo'i bka' 'bum dang bsod nams dbang po'i pad ma'i rnam thar gyi lung gsan/ nag nya'i bco lnga la ril sgrub
mdzad pas dus tshod kyang bsil dus bsil ba dang dro dus dro ba/ 'ja' 'od kyi gur dang dri bzang 'phel che ba sogs byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma gsal/snron zla'i nang nA lenaDa
nas spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin zhal gyis bzhes te dbyug zla'i bcu gsum nyin klu sdings rgyab tu dkar 'dzin dang bcu bzhi'i sa skor mdzad de bcu bdun la chibs kha bsgyur
bar yab yum sras bcas kyis phebs skyel mdzad de rong brgyud byams chen mjal ba sogs dang 'bum phrag gsum pas brag dkar du gdan 'dren zhus kyang dgongs pa bkrol nas yul
lhar zhal 'dzom dang/ dpal di sogs brgyud phebs lam la rang gzhan gyi re 'bras smin par mdzad nas yos lo smin drug 'gor nA lenaDar phebs skabs sngar bzhin bsnyen bkur te
mgo zla'i bcu bzhi rong ston dus mchod dang grwa tshang la 'dod chos/ lcang rgyab glo gong sogs brgya tsho so sos spyan 'dren bsnyen bkur/ chos sbyin/ chos sdings su zhag
bcu skor tsam la lugs gnyis de

kha'i 'dod sbyar dang/ 'brug lo rta zla'i nang nA lenaDar gsung ngag tshugs par nag zla'i tshes gsum la rtse gdong du yum gshegs pa'i gnas tshul nyer gcig la 'byor yang yum
sras brtse drags pas phyag g.yog rnams kyis zhu ma nus pa bla ma so so dang dge rgan kha cig gis bsnyen 'bul zhus pas thugs 'byung drags po shas mi bzod pa 'khrungs nas/
spyir 'dus byas mi rtag pa'i ngang tshul yin kyang/ da lam gshegs khar mjal ma thub pa 'di 'dra yong ba tshe 'di'i spros pa bcad de 'bras mo gshongs lta bur tshe dang sgrub
pa mnyam pa zhig byed snyam kyang de'i spros pa ni chod song gsungs/ de nyid dang nye 'khor gyi dgon pa so sor mang 'gyed bsngo rten rnam dag phon che ba dang/ bsam yas
la jo dar snyan dar zhal zas dkar me'i rgyur drel rgyab gnyis/ rab grar mang 'gyed bcas mdzad chos 'phro zhus par tshe ring na slar bshad chog gsungs te de phral yar phebs
rtsis dang/ bsam yas/ la mo/ gzims 'og chos skyong rnams nas kyang yar phebs sku dog chung bar lung bstan pas chibs kha bsgyur te/ rim bzhin brgya grong du zhag gsum
tshe chog mdzad pa sogs phebs lam gyi thugs brel rnams bcad de gdan sar phebs skabs 'khangs kyang da ni ci bya cha med du 'dug pas/ dgongs rdzogs gang drags byed gsungs

te nyid kyi sku chas steng nas/ yum gyi sku tshigs so sor chos sder mang ja gdan non rgyas pa'i dbur thub bstan mkhan chen kun dga' bsod nams byon pa la 'khor drug dang rta
sogs bsngo rten zab pa/ ngor thub bstan/ gser mdog can/ skyid tshal rnams su'ang 'gyed rnams mdzad/snron zla'i bcu dgu nas gu ru mtshan brgyad sman sku'i bzo tshugs par/
de sngon than pa che yang de nub nas char babs shing/ sngar sku rgyu'i 'jim pa dkon kyang rang rdol lta bu dang/ gser mtshal/ spang ma sogs kyang 'bul tshong 'bad med 'byor
zhing/ 'bum phrag gsum pa'i phyag na sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung bzhugs pa nas zhur btang bas/ sngar phebs pa ni med/ 'on kyang da lam chos 'khor bskor ba'i dus chen
dang thug pas gsol ba btab na phebs pa e srid gsungs nas mchod pa dang gsol ba btab pas yung 'bru tsam zhig phebs pa de gnang skabs/ nyid kyi thugs rjes 'di bzhin byung gsungs
pa las 'phel te sku 'dra re la re re dang/ gu ru rin po che'i zab ber gyi dum bu sogs ring bsrel rnam bzhi'i gang ba'i rten rnams la pra rtsis skabs nyi 'od shin tu
gsal ba sogs lugs 'gro bcas zla ba nyis brtsegs kyi rting ma'i nang du yongs rdzogs grub nas

tshes bdun la rje nyid dpon slob brgyad gras rab gnas mdzad pas 'ja' sprin gur phub pa lta bu dang/ rten gtso'i zhal ras sngar bas gzi brjid che ba phyag g.yog 'ga' zhig gis
mthong ba'i rten rnams la na bza' mchod tshogs dang bcas bzhugs shing/ lha bzo bar yon rdzong rta gsum ja gos dar g.yu byi ru gos lham sogs la gong dma' bzung byas pas
khyon Tam stong phrag gcig dang brgyad brgya lhag tsam thob pas kun dga' mgu yid rangs shing/ gtang rag mchod 'bul bskang gso sogs mdzad de/ yum gyi thugs dam bzhin tshes
bcu'i rgyun bzung/ lo mjug dang shing sbrul lo gang dang me rta'i 'go'i sgrub mchod sogs thugs brel 'char can mdzad de me rta nag zla'i nyer bdun la sa skyar phebs/ de sngon
rlung 'tshub che yang chibs bsgyur nas bzung gdugs 'jam zhing gdan sa'i ser phreng 'grig pa dang me tog gi char babs pa sogs bkra shis shing zhab bcu skor tsam gyi bar
bzhugs par bzhugs spro ba bcas 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug gi phur pa'i smad las rjes gnang dang/ yang dag dbang sogs stsal nas sa ga'i tshes brgyad la chibs kha
bsgyur te rim gyis e waM du phebs skabs ngor nang zin tsam nas 'ja' gur ya mtshan can zhig byung bas zhabs phyi rnams kyis de

bzhin zhus par rje rdo rje 'chang mnyes pa yin go bcad gsungs/ me tog gi char sogs gdan sa gong bzhin dang zhag gsum bzhugs ring mchod mjal chos 'brel bla brang so so'i zhabs
tog mang ja sogs mdzad nas gdan sar phebs/ snron zla'i dgu nas gro bzhin nyer gsum bar rtse gdong du gsung ngag gnang ba grol ba'i gtang rag rtse gdong gi mgon khang so
so dang/ ge re mdo chod mgon khang du mdzad pas ge tshar gnyis kyi legs 'bul dang/ de skor mi dmangs la gu ru zhi drag dang tshe dbang gnang/ khrums zla'i nang rtse gdong
'du khang steng gis gtsug lag khang du dkar po rnam gsum dang thub dbang/ gnas rten 'khor bcas kyi sku rnams sgrig par mdzad de dkar me rgyun 'bar sogs mchod tshogs kyis
bskor bar dbyug zlar khu dbon yab sras rtse rgyas ban tshang dang bcas pas rab gnas mdzad/ gcung gi drag po sgrol dbang zhus pa bzhin nyer gsum rgyal phur nyin klu sdings
tshoms chen du skya ser lnga brgya tsam la gnang/lug lo tha skar nang chos sde'i sgo 'phyor steng lha khang gsar bzhengs/ lo de'i smin drug zla nang shing rtsi tsam ma
gtogs grub/ nA leN Da nas spyan 'dren byung ba bzhin bcu gcig la chibs kha bsgyur te bdag chen khu bo dang yab gcung rnams kyis ge re mdo

chod bar phebs skyel mdzad de/ mgon khang du khu dbon ban tshang pas gsungs bskang mdzad/ gcung gis tshar bar phebs skyel zhus/ dgun dus byang brgyud yin kyang dbyar dang 'dra
ba'i gnam gshis legs shing sbyin bdag so so'i zhabs tog dang phur dbang sogs mdzad mu nas chos skyong rnam gnyis dang bco brgyad pa'i gtso mdzad chibs bsu ba dpal ldan
rtser 'byor te nyin gsum bzhugs nas gsung bskang rgyas pa dang/ nyer bdun dgon par phebs pa sogs sngar phebs dang cha 'dra bar chos skyong gi lung las dpal rtser zhag bdun
sku mtshams dang ban tshang pa'i bskang ba rgyas par mdzad rjes gsung ngag tshugs na legs tshul bzhin mdzad nas/ chos sdings su zhag lnga bzhugs te khrom dbang dang/

la phur dbang dngos sta drug re/ bco brgyad pa'i gsol ba bzhin dbang mi lnga brgya tsam la drag po sgrol dbang gnang/nag zla'i tshes brgyad nas nyid kyis mkhan po mdzad
de rab byung bsnyen rdzogs gang dgos mdzad par gzhung zhabs rin chen

nas sku tshab gdong legs skyes rgyas par stsal/ de nas lhun grub rdzong la spyan 'dren bang phyin 'byor kyang gyang ra nang so dang chos sdings su phebs pa'i zhal bzhes bzhin
de dag tu chibs bsgyur skabs slar yang bang mi nyis sbrel gyi zhu yig nan cher byung ba bzhin phebs te khong tsho'i re ba bskang nas nA leNDar shar phebs gnang rtsis yod

mdar gsol tshigs dang/ spel mkhar bzhugs zhag mdzad de/ de'i sang ser phreng dang bcas yab rje'i sku drung du thog mar phebs/ de phral lhun po rtser bdag chen

khu bo'i drung du phabs te khu dbon gnyis ka thugs shin tu dgyes kyang sku mdangs zhan pas cung zad ma bde bar yang gyur/ de gong yab sras rnams dang 'bum phrag gsum pa rtse
gdong tshogs chen rnams kyi zhabs brtan mdzad pas legs lam byung 'dug pa ltar/ nged rang nas de bzhin bgyid gsungs nas mdzad pas sku khams gzhi med du dngas/ de nas spyir

byang sems/ chos srung nor lha'i sku rgya dkar nag bal bod 'dres pa nyis brgya bzhi bcu tsam dang/ bris thang byin rlabs can du ma bzhugs pa la mchod tshogs kyi bskor
te rab gnas mdzad/dbyug zla'i tshes bcu bzhi la rje sa skya pa chen po'i dus chen sa mchod/ dus mdos chen mo'i rnga 'chams grub 'chams gnyis kyi 'chams dpon gnang/ bya
lo'i mgon khang so so'i gtor spod rnams dang/ gong ma na rim gyi dus mchod kyai rdor/ gsang 'dus/ gshed dmar/ bde mchog sgrub mchod rnams dang/ zla ba bzhi pa'i drug cu pa'i
tshogs dbur phebs/ tshes bcu bzhi'i snga char khu bo rin po che sku khams je lod du song bas rje

nyid la snyan zhus phul phral yar phebs te/ mjal bas dgyes te bslab don phra rags kun gnang/ de 'phral gzhan don la phebs/ de nas dgongs rdzogs kyi rim par/ sku gdung sku zhabs
su dge slong bzhi dang/ gzhan dge 'dun byings kyis mchod 'bul rgyas par gnang/ sku tshigs dang po'i snga char mkhan chen byams pa dge 'dun rgya mtshos sku gdung zhugs
'bul skabs rang zhabs kyi them che chung thams cad la phyi 'gyed gnang/ nam mkhar 'ja' gur sna tshogs kyis khyab pa/ gdung khang la'ang 'ja' zug pa me tog gi char kha ba

lha khang tshang mar zhal gser dkar me/ mar khal stong dang nyis brgya gdal tsam dang/ snyan dar shin tu zab pa/ rgyal ba yab sras sa skya stag lung rnams kyis mtshon dbus
gtsang gi bla ma slob dpon rnams la bsngo rten/ dgon so sor mang 'gyed rgyas pa gtong ba'i bka' khyab gnang/ nang rten dngul gdung rnam rgyal mchod rten ches che ba phra
rgyan phun sum tshogs pas spras pa dang/ sman 'dam las grub pa'i gzims mal sku 'dra che legs/ dus mchod thang ka shin tu che ba

sogs dang/ sku 'dra dngul gdung dang bcas par rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i gzungs cha tshang/ ring bsrel sogs bla ma gong ma'i byin rten gyis phyur bur gtams pa'i nang bzhugs phun
