sogs mchod rdzas bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul te/ rab tu gnas pa legs par mdzad do/ /yang lo de nang du rje btsun de nyid kyi dgongs rdzogs su/ rig 'dzin brgyud pa lha mgron
dang bcas par gras thang nyer bdun gong gsham zhal khebs tog bcas khyad mtshar du bskrun te rje nyid dpon slob bcu gsum skor gyis rab gnas rgyas par mdzad/ rten bzhengs
gegs med du grub pa'i chos skyong rnams la gtang rag gsung bskang rgyas par mdzad do/ /khyi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du a lu chos rje bsod nams bstan 'dzin bzang po dpon
slob drug cu skor 'byor te/ chos sder mang 'gyed/ gong ma rin po cher bsngo rten 'bul ba tshad med phul/ kyai rdor/ phur pa stod las/ smad las/ kun rig tshe dpag med lha
dgu rnams kyi dbang dang/ rjes gnang skor blo

'dod dang/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs rnams grub nas/ byin rlabs dang dngos po'i gnang sbyin sogs kyis tshim par mdzad/'di lo gtsug lag khang gi steng du mgon khang gsar bzhengs
gis rten gtsor mgon sku rgya nag ma zhal ngo na rim gyi thugs dam ma dang/ khri chen kun dga' bsod nams kyi phyag nas ma sogs sman sku dang/ rdo sku/ bris sku sogs mgon
sku mang po dang/ sa lo'i zhal 'bag dgra gegs zil gnon/ phyag rnga snyan dar spyan gzigs sogs/ mchod rdzas du mas brgyan te/ rab gnas dang/ gtor bsngo bskang rgyun sogs
'dzugs par mdzad de/ ding sang gi bar du yang ma nyams par bzhugs/ sgrub mchod dus ma rnams dang/ don gnyer slob bu rnams la chos sbyin mdzad/ dus mdos 'chams sna gsum ka'i
'chams dpon gnang/phag lo khrums zla dang byi lo dbyug zla'i nyer gsum la zab lung mjal bar lan re re phebs/ rjes ma'i tshe gter lung du gzigs snang khyad mtshar can
byung yang gab sbas tshul gyis zhib par ma gnang/ mchod 'bul rgyas par mdzad/ der bzhugs rnams la tshogs 'khor mang ja/ chos sbyin sogs gnang/ yar lam ras dkar thang du dbang
mo che gnang ba'i dbang yon rnams

dkar me'i thebs su sbyor 'jags mdzad/ slar gdan sar phebs phral sa mchod dus chen sogs dang/ chu glang lo a lu chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan dbon slob mang tsam la/ rab byung
bsnyen rdzogs/ kyai rdor rgyu lam/ kun rig tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang/ gur drag rjes gnang sogs 'dod sbyar ltar gnang/ phyogs nas don gnyer chos zhu ba gzhan rnams
la'ang chos sbyin gyis tshim par mdzad do/ /de nas shing stag zla ba bzhi pa'i nang/ gdung brgyud sku mched dang/ chos sde'i grwa rigs rnams la bde mchog nag po'i dbang
dang/ zla ba bdun pa'i nyer gsum la gdung brgyud sku mched/ thub bstan mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ srid gsum grwa rigs rnams la dbyar chos su sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i
rjes gnang dang/ khrums zlar de rnams la phur pa stod las dang/ smad las gnang/yang de skabs su rig 'dzin chos rgyal rdo rje rtse gdong du spyan drangs te/ gter ston 'ja'
tshon snying po'i gter chos skor la/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi dbang tshe dbang dang bcas pa/ lung skor la gter ston rnam thar nyung ngu bsdus pa/ yang zab nor bu'i lde
mig kha byang nyi ma'i snying po/ padma'i zhal lung

'od 'phro/ lung bstan 'od kyi me long/ le'u brgyad ma/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang/ dka' 'grel ri rgyal lhun po/ rig 'dzin 'ja' tshon snying pos mdzad pa'i rig 'dzin drag po'i sgrol
las/ bla ma'i rnam thar/ dbang gi rim pa/ tshe sgrub lcags kyi pho brang/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi las byang/ drag po zer bzlog gu ru drag po/ gter bsrung seng gdong
ma/ seng gdong ma'i las mtha'/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi kha skong zor bzlog a nu yo ga'i rdzogs rim/ 'phrin las bzhi sgrub/ yo ga gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ ma hA yo ga'i bskyed
rim/ gtum mo bde drod 'od 'bar/ 'pho ba dkar khung mda' 'phangs/ ting 'dzin bzang po'i zhus lan/ lta sgom spyod khrid/ nam mkha'i 'od klong bskang bshags rim par dkon
mchog spyi 'dus kyi gsol 'debs/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus sgrub pa byed lugs/ rdor sems bsgom bzlas rnams dang/ gter ston nyang ral gyis spyan drangs pa'i bla ma drag po'i chos
bskor gyi lung/ gter ston padma gling pas bla ma drag po'i chos tshan bzhi bcu'i skor tshang ma'i lung gza' dbang dang sgrub thabs kyi lung/ rdo rje gro lod dang padma
'byung gnas/ dzamabha la rnams kyi sgrub thabs/ rnam thar dri med/ dri med bshags rgyud/ na rag dong sprugs kyi

rgyud/ bdud rtsi bum pa'i dbang lung sogs gsan/zla ba bcu pa'i tshes lnga la dbus phyogs la chibs kha bsgyur/ byang lam brgyud tshes bco brgyad nyin dan dpag rin chen sgang
du sku zhabs yas phyin nas phebs bsu/ thab bsu sogs zab rgyas stsal/ lha sar phebs nas rgyal dbang mchog gi mjal 'dzoms skabs chos kyi gleng mo sogs zhib rgyas gnang/ bzhugs
gral tshe dkar gyi bka' 'grel dang gnang cha sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang/ nyer lnga la phan yul gzhung skor gyi nA leNDar chibs kha bsgyur/ glang ra'i bar ja rgyugs
dang chibs skyel ba sogs gnang/ tshes lnga la dgon par phebs/ der 'dus dge 'dun sogs la rgyu lam sgrub thabs sogs 'dod chos rnams stsal shing/ shi gson thams cad kyi
re ba bkang ste zla ba gsum bzhugs/shing yos rta zla'i nyer brgyad la chibs kha sgyur te khra zla'i bcu bzhi'i nyin rtse gdong du phebs/ mgon khang so sor gtang rag bskang
gso rgyas par gnang/ slob dpon padma/ tshe dpag med/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub sogs kyi sku brnyan mang du bzhengs shing rnam rgyal pho brang du bzhugs
te/ snron zla'i tshes lnga la rab gnas stsal zhing/ rten rnams la na bza' mchod rdzas sogs kyis bka' 'doms mdzad/ chu stod

tshes brgyad la phur sgrub tshogs dbur phebs/ smin drug zla ba'i bcu dgur bla brang rnam rgyal rtser phebs nas/ me 'brug khra zla'i bar yang dag gi sgrub pa mdzad pas zhal
gzigs dang dngos grub kyi mtshan ma sogs mang du brnyes/ gro bzhin zla ba'i nang yab rje ngag dbang bsod nams lhun grub bsnyun gzhi cher med par dag zhing du gshegs par/
sku'i gcung dang bcas pas dgongs rdzogs rgya cher bstar/ khams 'grul dang gzhis byes kyi tshogs la kyai rdor/ bde mchog phur pa/ kun rig tshe dpag med sogs dbang bka' du
ma dang/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho sogs kyi rjes gnang/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs/ rnying lugs chos bka'i ljags lung sogs mtha' yas par gnang/lho bod gzir skabs gdan sa nas 'jam
dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug skyid shod khag gnyis/ bkra shis lhun po'i phyag mdzod rnams dbyug zla'i nang du chings la phebs zin/ smin drug zla ba'i nyer bdun la lho
bod kyi zhu chings la chibs kha bsgyur bas rgyal zla'i tshes brgyad nyin lho bod mtshams kyi sprel mo lar phebs pa gong gi chings khag rnams kyi gsan pas/ phebs bsu ba rta
pa du ma byung ba rnams dang bcas sho rmug tu bzhugs sgar 'jags/ phebs bsu rnams la ja gral dang gsung gleng gang

'tshams gnang nas so sor log rjes/ de 'phral khu dbon mjal 'dzom la phebs nas/ gang ci'i gsung gleng zhib rgyas mdzad do/ /de nas chings khag zhal ngo tshang mas sems can bde
thabs kyi bka' gros kyi 'go btsugs/ gnam gang la chings khag tshang ma sku 'khor nyung bsdus dang bcas zhabs thang dka' tshegs la ma gzigs par shar nang du phebs/ btsan
gdong dbu mdzad dmag dang bcas 'byor/ zhag bco brgyad bar der bzhugs nas 'dzom rgyas lan gsum tsam byas/ chu gzar du bzhugs skabs rje nyid gur drag gi skur bzhengs pas/
gnas de'i gzhi bdag 'o dod bdud po zer ba de dam la btags/ lha chen brag skyes sogs mon phyogs kyi gzhi bdag phal che bas phrin las sgrub par khas blangs/khrums zla'i tshes
brgyad la 'brug sku tshab dang 'dzoms rgyas skabs zhu chings ha lam 'grig ngo dod/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog dang 'brug gzhung gnyis nas chings khag bla
dpon rnams 'o brgyal bas ci gsung gyis gsungs pa nas/ sa rta rgyal zla brtsegs pa'i tshes lnga'i nyin 'brug pa'i sku tshab rnams dang dmag mi dos skyel 'u lag bcas byung
bar/ 'brug

phyogs kyi dbu brtsis bzhes/ zhabs drung khu dbon gnyis su 'brug sku tshab nas khyed gdan sa yas phyin gyi zhal ngo gser gyi pha bong sgor 'dril yin/ nged lho mon gyi mis zhal
mjal ba lta ci/ gsung thos pa tsam yang mi yong bas/ dga' ldan pho brang pa bka' drin chen po yin/ dmag mi rnams la phyag dbang zhu zer ba bzhin khu dbon gnyis nas gnang/de'i
sang bod sgar la phebs/ bod phyogs kyi dbu brtsis bzhes/ gzhung 'brug gnyis char nas chings khag so sor bdog pa'i dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab pa drin gzo'i tshul
du phul/ chings khag so so nas sku tshab mngags pas bod dmag rnams phyir slog lho bod gnyis phyogs su bka'i 'khor lo gnang ba rnams don thog tu 'khyol zhing lhag lus med
par mdzad/ zhabs drung rin po cher yang dag gi ljags lung tshe bka' sogs gsan/ de nas chod yig sogs ma grub kyang/ gzhung 'brug sku tshab dang/ chings khag zhal ngo rnams
la log phebs chog pa zhus/rta zla'i tshes bcu bzhi la dpal rtse gdong la chibs kha bsgyur te/ dpal 'khor bde chen pas phebs bsu ser phreng bcas te zhag gnyis bzhugs shing
gnas gzigs dang/ ser skya thams cad la grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang sogs 'dod chos

ci rigs gnang/ de nas rim bzhin gru thog dang/ gtsang 'gram lha khang sogs su sku'i gcung ngag dbang rig 'dzin dbang po/ gdung brgyud sku mched yum mchog dam pa sogs 'khor
dang bcas pa'i phebs bsu thab 'dzin sogs gzab rgyas mdzad/ rta zla'i nyer bdun gyi snga char 'dus tshogs ser phreng gis bsus te/ thog mar bsam gtan 'phel rgyas dang/ de nas
lhun rtse sogs su phebs/ mnga' khul mi dmangs rnams dang/ phyogs nas kyang legs skyes tshar du dngar ba/ rje nyid nas kyang gzhis bzhugs tshang mar dngos po'i gnang skyes
dang/ 'dus tshogs su mang 'gyed 'bras 'jam sogs stsal zhing/ mgon khang so sor gtang rag gi mchod gtor snyan shal sogs 'bul bar mdzad/ a lu chos rjer kyai rdor rgyu dbang/
phur pa stod las/ smad las/ gur drag lha brgyad/ dkar bdud rnams kyi rjes gnang/ rab byung sgrub pa sogs chos dang zang zing gi gnang sbyin stsal/ tshoms chen sogs
pho brang la nyams gso/ tshon rtsi sogs mdzad/zla ba bzhi pa'i nang 'u yug zam 'tsher chab 'dugs la phebs shing/ lam bar ser skya rnams la lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas re 'dod
'gengs par mdzad/ zla phyed tsam nas gdan sar

phebs te/ bla ma bsod nams rab rgyas sogs la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ kun rig tshe dpag med/ rnam 'joms/ lha brgyad/ dkar bdud rjes gnang/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ chab klu/ 'pho
ba sogs kyi lung gnang zhing/ bla ma bsod nams rab rgyas khams phyogs 'bul dpon du bskos/ de nas mon phyogs sku tshab rnams 'byor ba'i stabs/ khrums zla'i nyer brgyad la
chibs kha bsgyur zhing rim gyis phag rir phebs/rgyal zla'i tshes bco lnga la sprel mo'i la rtsa brag stod rgod por gzhung 'brug gi sku tshab rnams 'dzoms nyin chod yig thebs
nas gzhung 'brug gnyis nas chings khag zhal ngo thun mong du legs so rgya cher phul/ nyi shu la phag rir phebs/ nyer gnyis la gdan sar chibs kha bsgyur/ rgya rong brgyud
gur pa grwa tshang gi ser phreng sogs kyis bsus te zhag gnyis bzhugs/ zha lu pa chen po dang mjal zhing 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang stsal/ zha lu pa chen pos
tshe dbang lcags sdong ma dang/ brtan bzhugs 'bul bar mdzad de rim gyis rnam rta chen sogs brgyud gdan sar phebs skabs zhal ngo rnams kyis phebs bsu ser phreng sogs mdzad/sa
lug rta zla'i tshes gsum la pho brang lhun rtser phebs nas

legs 'bul sogs bzhes shing/ 'dus tshogs su mang 'gyed/ chos srung la gtang rag sogs phebs skor snga ma bzhin/ nag zla'i tshes bcu gsum la gtsug lag khang gi seng g.yab shing
rtsi dang ldebs bris su thub pa gtso 'khor/ rgyan drug mchog gnyis/ sor sdom brgyud pa gzhan yang yi dam chos srung/ nor lha sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang/ gtsug lag
khang gi sgo 'phyor rnying bcos sogs gnang nas rab gnas mdzad/ byams pa bsod nams lhun grub kyi dus mchod dang/ nang rten dngul gdung/ phun tshogs lha khang/ gnas bcu lha
khang sogs rten gsum rnams la mar me'i thebs su sa zhing dang/ ri phyugs mang po sbyor 'jags gnang/sa lug zla ba bcu pa'i tshes lnga la dbus su chibs kha bsgyur zhing gcung
rin po che nas phebs skyel sogs mdzad/ sku zhabs rtse shod mjal bar chag chag la brgyud pa'i mdo chod du phebs/ de nas rim phebs kyi lam bar du 'khod pa'i ser skya hor
sog 'brog pa sogs skye 'gro shi gson rnams kyi re 'dod bkang te/ tshes bco brgyad la skyar po gzhis kar phebs/ sde srid nas thab bsu gong sa yas phyin nas phebs bsu ba
ser skya bzhi bcu skor gnang/ tshes bcu dgu la lha sar dpal 'byor rab brtan gyi

gnas tshang du phebs/ sde srid nas gsol ja phebs chas sogs stobs che ba dang/ rtse shod nas mgron gnyer sogs sku 'khor ser skya bco lngas phebs bsu bcas/ gong sa yas phyin
lhan rgyas su mjal 'dzoms gnang zhing/ kyai rdo rje'i sku rgya nag ma zhig gis gtsos dgu tshan bco lnga'i 'bul ba dang/ gsol ja bzhi'i bar lho bod legs spel skor nas brtsams
pa'i bka' 'dri sogs gnang bar rje nyid nas kyang gsung lan gang 'jems phul rjes mgron khang du gdan 'dren thog gsol ston gzab rgyas gnang/ de'i sang nyin gong sa mchog
nas grub rgyal ma'i tshe bka' shin tu rgyas pa stsal/ gnang sbyin rgya dpyad khyad mtshar/ rgya sbub sogs dngos po stobs che ba gnang ba dang chabs cig da cha dpal 'chi
med dbang por phebs pa gzhir bcas gsung ngag lam 'bras kyis gtsos pa'i bka' chos gang la'ang thogs med yod 'dug pas bstan 'gro'i don du rgya gang che gnang dgos tshul dang/
bsam yas phyogs la'ang da lam nges par phebs pa'i phyag nas sogs gnang lugs ngos lugs gnyis kyi khur bzhes mdzad dgos stabs nA lendra sogs dbus phyogs su bka' chos gnang
dgos rnams kyang gdan sa'i thugs brel dang bstun nas gnang chog gsung ba sogs lugs gnyis kyi bka' stsal thugs rje che bar

gnang/nyer lnga'i snga char jo zhal rnam gnyis sogs gnas mjal rnams grub bstun sku zhabs yas phyin nas phebs skyel du sku 'khor ser skya snga ma'i phebs bsu las ches mang ba
dang bcas chibs kha bsgyur zhing/ glang rar thab skyel thog sku 'khor rnams la gnang cha gzab rgyas bcas so so'i thugs 'dod skong bar mdzad nas 'phan yul gzhung 'ded kyis
rim gyis phebs/ ja yul gzhis kar chos sdings nas khang steng pa bstan 'dzin dpal 'byor sogs ser skya mang pos phebs bsu dang/ grwa mang gis ser phreng bcas chos sdings
bla brang du phebs/ de phyogs kyi ser skya mchog dman rnams la spyi dbang dang sgos chos gsung chog bsngo smon rgyas 'debs sogs re blo bkang/ 'dus tshogs la mang 'gyed bsgrigs
lam kun spyod gtsang dag dgos pa'i bslab ston mthil phyin bca' yig dang bcas pa gnang/ nyer dgu'i nyin chos rje bco brgyad pas gtsos nA lendra'i las 'dzin bzhi bcu
skor phebs bsur 'byor/[rgyal zla'i tshes la chibs kha phyogs pa'i lam bar gyi mchog dman so so'i re blo 'gengs par mdzad/ phebs bsu ser phreng sogs kyis ring po nas bsus
te bla brang du phebs/ de'i sang

'dus tshogs su ser ja sbyor sbrel/ 'bras tsha dam rdzas dang dngos po'i 'gyed spam mtho ba sogs stsal/ tshes bcu bzhi rong ston gyi dus chen la mang ja 'theb gtong dang / nyer
gsum la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i mgo 'dzugs gnang ba'i chos rje bco brgyad pa sogs gzhir 'azhugs dang / phyogs grwa grub mtha' ris su ma phyed
pa lnga brgyar nye ba zhig la/ zla ba phyed gsum gyi khongs su gsung ngag grub par stsal/ bsnyen rdzogs brgyad cu skor dang / rab byung nyi shu skor/ mi dmangs ser skya
stong tsho gsum du nye bar spyi dbang tshe bka' rtsa gsum gyi dbang / le'u bdun ma/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus sogs dang / bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa 'bogs pa sogs chos dang zang
zing gi sgo nas so so'i blo'i rdzing bu yongs su 'gengs par mdzad/ de nas dpal ldan rtser phebs/ zhag gsum ring gsung bskang 'phrin bcol smin rgyas dang / gnyan mgon dngos
dang mtshungs pa'i sku de dbu sngas su spyan drangs nas 'phrin bcol smin rgyas su gnang bar thugs bzhed 'grub pa'i mtshan ma mngon du gyur kyang snod min rnams kyi spyod
yul du mi 'gyur bas su la'ang ma 'chad gsung / der ser skya pho mo stong phrag gsum du nye bar tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / kha shas la

lcags sdong ma sogs gnang ste de phyogs kyi skye rgu rnams phan bde la bkod/ bcu bzhir nA len drar phebs/ bco lnga'i nyin chos skyong rnam gnyis sku phebs zhus par legs nyes
kyi lung bstan 'ga' zhig dang / phral du gdan sar phebs pa legs tshul byung bas gong sa rtse shod du gsung ngag sogs 'di skor gyi 'dzin skyong rnams grub cing da cha lho
kha brgyud gdan sar phebs bzhed sogs kyi zhu yig phul bar/ rtse shod nas kyang de bzhin gnang chog pa'i thugs dam dang / gong dkar rdzong nas zur chas gtos chen gnang ba'i
bka' 'dzin bcas gzab rgyas stsal/ rtse gdong nas phebs bsu ba rnams kyang 'byor/ mgon khang so sor lam gtor rgyas pa dang / khyad par mgon khang chen mo'i sku la 'di
bzhes shig gsungs nasakha btags zhig 'phangs pa gnang ba snyan g.yas par bzhes/ bstan 'gro'i don du 'phrin bcol rgya chen mdzad/rta zla'i nyer gsum la nA lendra nas chibs
bsgyur/ bco brgyad du gdan 'dren zhus/ rgyal dbang mkhyen gzigs chen pos mdzad pa'i brtan bzhugs 'od gsal ma 'bul ba'i rten 'brel du bkra shis kha btags kyi gtsos dgu tshan
gsum phul/ bsnyen bkur gya nom pa mdzad/ de nyin nA lendra'i chos grwar yang

'dzugs par gnang zhing / nam mkha'i lhas kyang shin tu ngo mtshar bas thugs dgyes/ bco brgyad chos rjes mtshon dge 'dun rta pa bzhi bcu skor gyi g.yag rong gdong bar phebs
skyel zhus/ de rnams la dngos po'i gnang sbyin gya nom pa dang / bstan lar ljang bsam chen po so so nas mdzad dgos pa'i bka' khyab gnang bas chos rje bco brgyad khra zla'i
tshes gcig snga dro bsam yas nas rta pa sum cu skor rdo mchod thang du phebs bsu'i thog rab byung tshogs pa'i ser phreng dang bcas bsam yas nang pa rtsas mang pa'i khyim
du phebs/ stag rtse nas gsol ja dang zur chas gzab rgyas/ rtswa shing rnams zla skor bzhugs kyang 'bul rtsis dang / sang pho brang du phebs pa'i slob dpon chen po srin
yul la phebs khar mu khri btsan po la gnang ba'i zhabs rjes sogs nang rten mjal ba dang bcas gsol gong du phebs dgos pa'i snyan gsan phul bar/ de bzhin

byed cing gnas mjal skabs sne shan pa zhig dgos tshul gnang bas/ de'i sang snen shan par gnyer pa chos mdzad dang bcas dbu rtse rigs gsum gyi byang chub chen po'i sku/ bo dhi
satwa'i dbu thod / g.yu'i jo bo rnams dang / bar khang gi dus gsum sangs rgyas 'khor bcas rnam snang kun tu zhal 'khor bcas dang / 'jam dpal gling nas bzung / ma chags
pad ma can gyi bar gyi gnas gzigs rnams gnang / so sor snyan shal sogs mchod rdzas du ma tshar du dngar/ pho brang du phebs/ zhabs drung nas mjal dar dang / phar gnang skyees
tshan grangs 'ga' zhig mdzad/ mchod yon lhan rgyas bzhugs gral thog gung tshigs ston mo dkar spro sogs bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa zhus/ slob dpon gyi zhabs rjes
kyis mtshon nang rten rnams zhib mjal gnang / tshes gsum sku phebs thog chos skyong dang mjal 'dzom mdzad skabs/ rje nyid nas dbu chings gnang skyes legs par mdzad/ spyi
bye brag gi bstan pa dang sems can la dgongs pa'i bka' bsgo dam gzhag gnang bas chos skyong nas kyang 'o dge bshes de yin de byed zhus te zhal gyis bzhes/ ngos

mjal yang yang byed 'on kyang da nas dge bshes rang gis nges pa ltar/ gur drag gi las tshogs ni btsan po dang chos rgyun chad 'grob la thug na ma gtogs bzhag na 'gab 'dug 'di
bzhag phyin gdug 'dres kyang bka' dang mi 'gal ba'i phrin las sgrub cing ngos mjal kyang byed do gsung / sku phebs rting ma'i thog lha dung gser shog ma shin tu legs pa/
ba dan dar lce dang bcas pa brten pa'i dam rdzas su phul/ bkur zos khyad par canaphul lo/ der 'dus tshogs la 'jam dbyangs dang phyag rdor gyi rjes gnang sogs bdod chos
dang bsam yas su bzhugs ring nang rer mang ja/ dam rdzas/ dngos 'gyed sogs gya nom pa gnang / bka' 'gyur ma Ni 'khar lo ltar bskor chog pa rnams la phyag nas mdzad/tshes
bzhi'i nyin mchims phu'i gnas gzigs la phebs/ sne shan par kong po'i grwa pa rgyus yod zhig gis byas/ rje nyid nas kyang 'di 'dra zhig yod 'dug pa de ga na yod pa sogs sngon
gnas rjes dran tshul du mjal/ brag dmar ke'u tshang du bya dmar khra zhig skad sna tshogs sgrog pa la rje nyid nas kyang bya 'di ci zer snying rje sdug gi gsung / sku
'khor rnams la bya skad mang ba

zhig 'dug snyam pa las rtog pa ma byung/ phyis brtags pas 'og tu bshad pa bzhin bse khrab can yin 'dug/ tshes lnga drug la bsam yas mthil gyi lha khang dbu rtse nas bzung gnas
gzigs phros rnams dang / yang skyar mjal bar mdzad/ tshes bdun gyi nyin chibs kha bsgyur te sngar gyi phebs bsu ba rnams kyis phebs skyel zur mkhar rdo mchod bar zhus/
der mchod rten rnams la zhabs rkor dang thugs smon mdzad/ phebs skyel ba rnams dad rten dang bdog pa'i dngos pos mgu bar mdzad do/ /de nas bye rdzing tshogs pa'i phebs
bsu ba rnams dang bcas bye rdzing tshogs su phebs/ bla ma grwa tshang bcas kyis 'bul ba rgya che'i mchod/ ser skya phomo stong phrag lngar nye ba la tshe dbang lcags sdong
ma/ gzhan yang spyi chos sgos chos sogs chos dang zang zing gnyis kas tshim par mdzad/ rnam sras sgrub mchod kyi zhal 'debs sogs kyang stsal/ skye bo pho mo skra phud 'bul
ba mang du byung/ lcog la rab gnas sogs gnang / tshes bcu'i nyin sngar gyi phebs bsu ba rnams dang bcas/ grwa thang phyogs su phebs der phebs bsu ser phreng sogs kyis
bsus te/ chos 'brel mang 'gyed gnas gzigs sogs mdzad nas gdung phud chos 'khor du phebs/ bsnyen bkur 'bul ba dang bcas zhabs

brtan zhal bzhes gnang dgos pa'i gsol ba btab/ rje nyid nas lo du ma'i bar sdod do zhes zhal bzhes gnang/der gdan sar phebs stsol dgos pa'i zhu yig bcas rtse gdong nas bang
chen 'byor bas/ de phyogs kyi ser skya rnams la spyi chos gos chos mtshan bskyangs te gnang / brtan bzhugs 'od gsal ma btsugs mang 'gyed logags stsal te/ sang nyin ra ba
smad du phebs bsu ser phreng bcas byon/ chos skyong gis phebs bsu mjal dar sogs dang rje nyid nas kyang snyan dar phyag ral sogs gnang nas gzim chung du phebs/ slar yang
spyan 'dren zhu bar mdzad skabs gsung las lcog tu dge bshes rong ston gyi chos khri'i steng nas lam 'bras gnang ba de legs shing / sngon dur khrod bsil ba tshal du dge bshes
dang rang re gnyis kyi rdo rus sbal 'dra ba zhig gi 'og nas zab gter spyan drangs pa ma bsnyel 'dug gam/ 'bras sjongs kyi gnas sgo phye ba'i skabs grub thob rdzogs chen
pa dang bcas rang re gsum yod pa ma bsnyel 'dug gam zhes sogs dang/ ngas brag dmar ke'u tshang du bya dmar khra zhig tu rdzus nas 'ongs pa ngo mkhyen nam gsungs/ spyi
bye brag gi lung bstan dang / rgyal mtshan legs pa zhig chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'dzugs pa'i rten 'brel du phul/ 'dus sder

mang ja dngos 'gyed sogs stsal/ de nas gong dkar du chos sde'i phebs bsu ser phreng bcas pas bsus zhabs tog bsnyen bkur gzab rgyas zhus/ 'dus tshogs su mang 'gyed dang bcas
spyi chos sgos chos stsal zhing / gnas gzigs sogs mdzad/ de nas shad rtsol gyis phebs pa lam bar na 'khod pa'i skye 'gro kun la phan bde'i sa bon bskrun pa'i ring nas thob
rgyal gru brgyud lcags spre khra zla'i nyer gsum la ge rer phebs/ phyag mdzod lhun grub chos dkar 'khor bcas phebs bsur byon gzhis byes dgyes pa'i gsung gleng rgya cher
stsal/ nyer bzhi'i nyin rgyan mchog rin po che gdung brgyud mched yum dang bcas zhal ngornams dang chos sde'i las tshan sogs ser skya rnams kyi phebs bsus grwa dmangs kyi
ser phreng dang bcas 'phel rgyas su gung tshigasadang/ grub 'phral lhun rtser pebs pa'i dga' ston rdzogs ldan gyi sprin bzhin gyur/ chos srung la gtang rag gi mchod gtor
kyang rgyas par mdzad do/ /de nas tshes bco lnga la rje 'di nyid dpon slob byang pa dang / gzim dpon mtshungs med gnyis kyis tshogs chen du spyan drangs te/ dpon gzim
gnyis phyag mdzod spyi chen rnams kyi mang ja gsum sbrel steng zhabs brtan 'od gsal ma 'dzugs par mdzad/

rgyan mchog rin po yum dpon slob/ gzims phyag spyi grwa dmangs sogs nas dngos po'i tshan grangs kyis mchod nas bskal brgyar zhabs pad brtan pa'i gsol 'debs dang / rten 'brel
legs bsgrigs su mdzad/ gnang cha sogs kyang che thob chung thob kyi slog rnams bka' drin che bar mdzad/ nyer gsum snga dro bsangs dang dar 'phyar gnang thog bsam yas chos
skyong gis ngos mjal yang yang byed gsung pa ltar/ gdan sa 'di nyid du bsod nams chos mchog la khog zhugs gnang ba'i sku phebs dang po byung / sa ga'i bde mchog sgrub
mchod dang / mgon po drug cu pa'i rdo rje slob dpon du pebs/ nyer gsum la bsangs sogs gong bzhin/ chos skyong sku phebs thog lhun rtse'i mkhar las kyi sa 'dul dang las mi
rnams la phyag nas bar chad mi yong ba'i lung bstan mdzad/ nyer bzhi la mkhar las tshugs zla khongs su grub 'di skabs mtshan mo rdo 'jo ba dang / sa skyel ba dang 'khun
pa sogs sngon bsam yas bzhengs tshul dang mthun par byung / nyer drug la phyag mdzod gser khang sogs rgyan mchog gi phyag nas rtsis bzhes pa'i deb nang bzin rim 'bul gnang
/ de skabs gdung brgyud sku mched du na bza' cha tshang sku ber lam 'bras glegs bam/ mgon pod rol sil rdor

dril chibs sga rigs lnga nyer gcakig sogs dngos po'i gnang cha dang/ lha khang sogs su'ang sbyor 'jags spams mtho bar gnang / thugs 'gan bzhes pa nas bzung zhal ngo spyi'i
sku rim dus mchod/ dge 'dun gyi zhabs tog sogs sngon gyi phyag deb las rim spor mdzad/chu stod zla'i tshes gcig la sku'i dbon kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin rab byung bzhes
pa'i mkhan po rje nyid dang/ slob dpon thub bstan mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan sogs dgi slong drug gi dbus su rab byung mdzad cing gzhan yang de nyin rab byungabasnyen
rdzogs mang po gnang / gdung brgyud sku mched/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan sogs la 'jam dpal smra seng gi rjes gnang / dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum dmar po
skor gsum sogs kyi ljags lung dang/ gro zhun zla nang bsam yas chos skyong nas gu ru pad ma'i zhal gzigs sgrub pa mdzad dgos yod gsung pa dang / bse khrab can nas kyang
de bzhin byung bas/ rje nyid nas kyang chos grwa chen po'i 'dzin skyong sku'i dbon la gtad/ tshogs chen du mang ja 'gyed sogs stsal/khrums zla'i nang chibs khyon pa'i tshes
bcu la/ slob dpon

gyi sgrub gnas zab lung du phebs/ grwa btsun rnams la mang 'gyed tshogs 'khor sogs stsal/ le'u bdun ma sogs gsol 'debs lan mang du mdzad/ tshes bcu gsum nas zhabs skor 'bum
ther 'go btsugs nyin rer zhabs skor sum brgya nyi shu re gnang / gdul bya las can 'ga' zhig gis zhabs sa la mi reg par phebs 'dug zer ba'ang mang du byung / sngon skor ba
stong phrag bcu gcig rer 'bum ther brtsi yang rje nyid nas stong phrag bcu gnyis kha skong bcas dang / zhabs skor ma grub bar la dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi nyams bzhes dang
mchod rgyun nar mar 'bulab/ zhabs skor thon nas 'phan sogs mchod rdzasargya che dang / der bzhugs ring 'bul ba gsum tshan re byung yang dar kha re snyan dar du phul/ de
skabs sku'i dbon kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin/ sa mchod thog srid gsum rnam rgyal bzhugs khrir mnga' gsol mdzad bzhed la ma 'grig par smin drug gi bcu bzhi la khrir phebs
rje nyid nas kyang thub dbang gi sku'i gtsos dgu tshan gsum gyi legs skyes bcas rgyal tshab tu dbang bskur/ rje 'di gter lung gsum pa dang / bdun pa'i gnas gzigs su phebs/
gter lung bdun par sku 'khor rnams phyir slog nas brag g.yab zhig tu bzhugs/ gnas mjal ba 'gas rje 'di

mi zhig dang / gsung gleng yun ring gnang 'dug par dbu'i gtsug na mar 'ja' mdung tshugs dang / 'ja' 'od kyi gur/ me tog gi char sogs ltas khyad mtshar can byung ba mthong bas
khong rnams dad pa'i yus kyi ngu chom dang phyag 'tshal ba sogs ku co dir byung / sku 'khor rnams nas kyang tshul de bzhin mthong / sngon chos skyong rnam gnyis kyi lung
bstan ltar/ slob dpon gyi zhal gzigs der byung ngam snyam zab bu gnas mthil du sku mtshams bdun phrag gcig gnang rjes rig 'dzin brgyud pa dang rdo rje gzhon nu'i lha tshogs
tshang ba'i sku thang lnga / yang dag gi lha tshogs tshang ba'i thang ka gcig bcas bzhengs te phur pa'i sgo nas rab gnas mdzad/ rgod tshang bla ma sogs la tshe dbang
dang bka' bsgo sogs stsal/ tshur kyang ri phyugs sha mar sogs gzab rgyas phul/ gnasader rgyun ring bzhugs pa'i thugs 'dun gtad kyang/ rtse gdong pa rnams nas myur phebs
dgos tshul dang/ chos skyong chen pos kyang de bzhin nan chen byung bas mgo zla'i tshes gcig la chibs khyon/ de nyin ma tshor gyi gnas gzigs/ der bzhugs rnams la mang ja
sogs tshim par mdzad/de nas rim gyis gdan sar tshes lnga'i nyin gsang stabs su lhun rtser shar mar phebs/ de nas re zhig bcad rgyar bzhugs/

sngar bzhengs phur pa'i thang ka rnams la rgyal zla'i tshes gsum la kyai rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa slob bcas kyi mdzad/ gsung chog phyag phyi ba/ lha bris pa lnga
/ dngul tog brdung mi lag g.yog gos bzo ba bcas la yon dang ston mo sogs kyis tshim par stsal/ bcad rgya grol bstun rdza dmar bla ma dang tshe dbang bkra shis gnyis la
kun rig dang dmar po skor gsum gyi ljags lung/ gung brgyud sku mched dang bcas par gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang rnams mdzad gtor spod drug cu pa sogs kyang rgyas par mdzad
/ bya lo thub bstan drung gnas su byams pa lhun grub/ ngor khang gsar dbon po/ sde dge bla ma kun dga' chos 'phel rnams la phur pa/ kun rig/ tshe dpag med lha dgu rnams
kyi dbang / lha brgyad dang / 'byung 'dul rjes gnang / dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi tshe dbang rnams gnang / bdag bskyed gtor chog bcas kyi lung gadzad/de nas khra zla'i tshes
brgyad la thub bstan mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ drung gnas gnyis rnams la/ dmar po bskor gsum gyi rjes gnang / mnga' rigs drung gnas la de'i be'u bum lung rnams
gnang / de mtshungs slob dpon gyi dngul sku padma gser zangs las grub padang/ gong ma byams pa bsod nams

pa'i sku brkyang khru gang lhag tsam gser zangs las grub pa zla ba drug khongs su bzhengs/ de bstun chos skyong gi lung bzhin nyid kyi phyag mdzod dang / gzim dpon sogs phyag
phyi rnams nas khur bskyed/ rje nyid kyi 'dra sku gser zangs las grub pa'i bzo khyad phul phyin zhig kyang bzhengs pas/ de skabs su lhag bsam gyis kun nas blangs pas zhal
'debs dang bsnyen bkur zhu mi sogs khyon sdom mi brgya dang drug cu skor sogs kyi dpal 'byor lha'i 'dod yon la 'gran par gyur/ gro zhun gyi tshes brgyad la nyid kyi 'dra
sku/ lhun rtser spyan drangs/khrums zla'i tshes drug la sku gsar bzhengs gnyis kyang lhun rtser spyan drangs nas gzungs gzhug gi rten rnams rje nyid nas phyag bzhes su
bstar/ shel brag nas nyi ma 'od zer gyis gdan drangs pa sloob dpon gyi sku bye ma a krong du grags pa dang/ o rgyan gtso 'khor gsum sku sgyur sangs rgyas 'phel gdung sogs
sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung gu ru yab yum gyi byang sems dkar dmar mkhas grub du mas byin rlabs/ lo paN du ma'i ring bsrel/ dbu lo na bza'/ lam zab brgyud pa sogs ma tshang
ba med par ma 'khrul bar 'bul bar mdzad/tshes bcu la kyai rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas rje nyid slob

tshogs dang bcas pas mdzad pas/ ye shes pa zhugs pa'i rtags thon pa byung zhing / rab gnas phyag phyi dge 'dun rnams dang / bzo bo'i mgo pa gnyis lag g.yog dang bcas pa rnams
la/ bsod btags/ gos dar/ gser dngul dkar zhags/ rta dre'u/ rta sga/ gos stod/ gos slog sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang/ sku gsum bzhugs khri'i shing bzo ba/ lha bris
pa bcas la'ang gsos ras gzab par stsal/ de rnams la mchod rgyun mar me'i thebs su ri phyugs pho mo brgya dang nyi shu lhag tsam mar dkon gnyer du shar mar rtsis sprod pa'i
bka' khyab gnang / de nas khams 'a zhur gyi grwa pa sum cu tsam la bsnyen rdzogs/ gser mdog can mkhan po brtson 'grus phun tshogs la lam dbang dang/ gzhan yang phyogs nas
byon pa'i dge 'dun rnams la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs dbang bka' rjes gnang / skye bo phal pa rnams la tshe bka' gang 'dod sogs kyis tshim par stsal/ khams glang dgon gyi
bla mar phur pa stod las/ rnams 'joms rjes gnang byabs bkrus/ dgon pa'i bca' yig gdan sa chen po nas gnang ba'i rgyab bsnon bcas stsal/sa ga zla ba'i tshes lnga la phyag
mdzod chos dkar nas zhabs

brtan phul/ snon zla'i tshes lnga la lhun tse'i bde yangs su grub rgyal lugs kyi khrom dbang stsal/ chu stod tshes lnga la srid gsum slob dpon bslab gsum bstan 'dzin sogs la
phur pa'i stod las/ gzhan yang srid gsum rnam rgyal grwa rigs rnams la gang 'dod kyi rjes gnang lung sogs stsal/ khrums zla'i tshes bcu gnyis la mnga' khul gyi bzo bo rnams
kyis bskal brgyar bzhugs pa'i rten 'byung phul/ me tog char pa 'bab pa'ang 'ga' zhig gis mthong /dbyug zla'i tshes lnga la nyid kyi gzim dpon bkra shis mtshungs med
kyi gsol ba btab nas/ mnga' khul gyis gtsos thob rgyal/ pa rnam tshun/ shangs rnam gling man gyi skye 'gro ser skya khri tshor nye ba zhig la rtsa gsum dril sgrub kyi chos
bka' zhig stsal/ de'i sang sku'i gcung rgyan mchog rin po che'i gtsos mchog dman snga brgya tsam la dril sgrub stsal/ gzim dpon nas 'bul ba dgu tshan gnyis dang/ bdun tshan
bcas phul bar rje nyid nas ting shags/ gsol slog mchod 'phro/ ras dar sogs tshan grangs gnang bar/ 'di 'dra mi zhu 'di nas zhus nas gang du 'bul zhus song bar/ nan chags
len dgos tshul phebs/ ting shags dang gsol slog zhus/ ras dar phul/

dbyug zla'i tshes bcu gsum la chab tshan du phebs/ chab zhag bdun gnang ba'i zhag gsum thog tu/ bco brgyad nas kyi chab la phebs pa lam du gsan pas / khong dpon slob der phyag
mjal du phebs/ phyag dbang dang gsol tshigs zhig stsal/ khong dpon slob sgo la phyogs kyi gang 'byor du phebs/ rje nyid nas gling mkhar rdzong dpon dang / sdings ma spyi
sogs ser skya mchog dman stong tsho gcig tsam la ras chung tshe dbang/ dol gnas chung par lcags sdong ma'i tshe dka'/ gzhan yang 'dod chos ljags lung sogs so so'i re
skong mdzad/ bsnyen bkur ba sogs mang du byung / nyer gnyis kyi gung tshigs snga grol la chibs khyon pa'i phebs zhag gsum gyi mdo chod du phebs lam bar gyi gdul bya rnams
sbyin pa rnam bzhis tshim par mdzad/ mdo chod du bzhugs zhag gsum dang gsung bskang smin rgyas gnang/ de nas gdan sar phebs bsu ser phreng sogs kyis bsus te lhun rtser phebs/
de nas sde dge zhal ngo kun dga' rab brtan sogs la bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang glegs bam lung / klu dbang rgyal po/ tshe dkar/ rta mgrin lcags ral can rnams kyi
rjes gnang / kun rig gi dbang rnams gnang / bco brgyad byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub dpon slob

rnams la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma dang / bsnyen bkur rgyas par gnang zhing / rdor phreng dbang chas dang phyag dpe sogs g.yar por stsal/mag zla'i tshes lnga la chos skyong
gi lung bstan du byung ba bzhin 'dus tshogs nas bskal brgyar zhabs pad brtan par gsol ba btab/ sku mtshams zhag bdun gnang / drug cu pa'i tshogs dbur phebs/ rgyal zla'i
nang rje nyid dang gcung rgyan mchog rin po che bcas nas dus kyi gtor spod rnams mdzad/de nas chu khyi rta zla'i mgor ngor khang gsar dbon po bsod nams phun tshogs sogs la
drag po mthing kha'i sku gsung thugs dbang / phur pa sa lugs dbang / rta mgrin lcags ral can gyi rjes gnang / yang gcung rgyan mchog rin po che sogs la thugs sgrub drag
po mthing kha'i dbang gnang/ de nas nA lendra'i grwa rgyun 'ga' dang gzhis grwa 'ga' zhig dang dred gdan sa bsod nams gzhan phan grwa slob rnams la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs
dang / srid gsum slob dpon bslab gsum bstan 'dzin la pu tra'i zur bka' dang bran bdud rjes gnang stsal/ grags pa zla dbang / mchod dpon bkra shis chos 'phel sogs la gshed
dmar lha lnga'i dbang stsal/ bla ma ma Ni ba sogs la thugs rje

chen po'i rjes gnang dang / phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug nyams su len tshul gyi bsgom lung / ban tshang pa sogs la a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i gnod sbyin tse dmar gyi gsol
kha le tshan gnyis/ kun bzang smon lam/ spyod 'jug smon lam/ spyan ras gzigs phyag bzhi pa'i brgyud 'debs/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus brgyud 'debs/ chab gtor / klu gtor / rje nyid
kyi brtan bzhugs/ bsod nams rgyas bskrun ma/ 'od gsal ma/ phanabade'i dkyil 'khor ma/ kun rig gzhan phan mtha' yas/ sbyin srig ro srig tsha tsha'i cho ga 'byung 'dul
sgrub thabs gtor chog rnams kyi lung/ 'byung 'dul dang dkar bdud rjes gnang /snron zla'i nyer bzhi la nA lendra'i grwa rgyun bzhi dang / gzhis grwa rnams la rab byung bsnyen
rdzogs/ klu bum sgrub pa rnams gnang ste lhun rtse sogs su 'jug par gnang /chu stod zla'i bco brgyad nyin nA lendra'i grwa rgyun mang por bsnyen rdzogs dang / gcung rgyan
mchog rin po che/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ srid gsum slob dpon sogs la kyai rdo rjer man ngag 'grel pa/ mtsho skyes lugs sogs kyi dbang gnang /

yang gro bzhin zla ba'i tshes gcig nas mkhan chenabazang po rgyal mtshan sogs la bka' gdams glegs bam dang / gcod skor dpe tshan kha cig slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la brten
pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor rnams kyi lung stsal/ chos skyong gi lung bzhin rje nyid ban tshang pa dang bcas pa'i mgon khang so sor bskang gso smin rgyas gnang / nyer bdun
nyin chos skyong thog phebs kyi dge bshes su zhabs brtan 'bul dgos yod gsung pa ltar khrums zla'i bcu bdun la zhabs brtan 'bul ba'i cho ga dang/ lha bsangs sogs ban gtsang
pa rnams kyis mdzad de/ rgyan mchog rin po che nas tshe dpag med kyi gser sku/ bzhugs gdan sogs kyis thog drangs tshan pa dang / chos skyong nas bzhugs 'ding khar bkra
shis kha btags la rdo rje rgya gram dang rtags brgyad bris pa/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i skus thog drangs tshan pa kha shas bcas phul/ gzhan ser skya so so nas 'bul
spom che ba bcas/ de nyin nyi ma ldab 'gyur tsam gyis ring bar 'ja' 'od sogs bkra shis pa'i mtshan ma dpag med byung /de nas zhag bdun sku mtshams dang / dbyug zla'i tshen
gsum la chos skyong chen por gtang rag gzab par stsal/ tshes

lnga'i nyin rgyan mchog rin po che zab sog la phebs par drung 'khor rnams ja rgyugs bcas rdzong bda' gnang/ bcu gsum nyiin gdung brgyud rin po che mched dbus phyogs su phebs
par phebs skyel du drung 'khor tshang ma rdzong bda' mdzad/ nyer gsum nyin 'jam dbyangs rnam rgyal la dkar bdud rjes gnang dang phur chung sbyin sreg lung bcas kyi lung
stsal/smin drug gi tshes gcig la rgyan mchog rin po che tshur phebs skabs drung 'khor tshang ma ja rgyugs dang bcas phebs bsur rdzong bda' mdzad/ ngor grwa bco lnga sde
dge gnyer pa sogs la 'byung 'dul rjes gnang dang bsnyen rdzogs stsal/ dar mdo ya ma tsho nang mir dkon mchag spyi 'dus dang dad rten sogs stsal/ rgyan mchog rin po cher padma
bka' thang shel brag ma'i lung / rdzong ri bla mar 'byung 'dul rjes gnang rnams stsal/ drug cu pa dang gtor spod sogs gcung rgyan mchog rin po che dang ban tshang pa
rnams kyis mdzad/ grags pa zla dbang la kun rig dbang dang/ nA lendra'i grwa rgyun rnams la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs gnang / ge re phu'i tshes bcu ba las tsho gcig sogs brgya
phrag lhag tsam la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ tsa gsum/ le bdun sogs kyi lung / yang rdzong ri bar mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang dang/

phyogs grwa rnams la bsnyen rdzogs gnang /nag zla'i gnam gang nas nyin gsum srid gsum pa/ rin sgang pa sogs grwa rigs rnams la kun rig gi dbang / gzhan phan mtha' yas brgyud
'debs sbyin sreg ro sreg tsha tsha'i rab gnas/ dbang chog rnams kyi lung dang / sa ga'i nang bla ma ma Ni skor chen pas bskul bar gdan sa 'di nyid du 'gu yul/ rgyal rtse/
pa rnams chu lho brgyud phal cher/ thob rgyal yan/ shangs mkhar chen rtse man mi stong lhag tsam la rtsa gsum dril sgrub dbang dang / tshe dbang lcags sdong ma stsal/
snron zla'i tshes gsum la gter ston gter bdag gling par phebs bsu ja rgyugs bcas rdzong bda' / lhun rtser phebs thog mjal 'dzom legs par mdzad cing tshes lnga'i nyin chos
bka' 'bul ba'i dbu tshugs/ de nyin kha btags nyin bde/ sgrol dkar gyi dngul sku/ g.yang tri'i sder ma/ gos yug sogs dgu tshan bzang ba gsum phul/ thog mar gter gsar la brag
dmar g.ya' ma lung nas spyan drangs pa'i rig 'dzin thugs thig gi dbang lung khrid sogs yongs rdzogs/ gnam brag nas spyan drangs pa'i rdor sems dang gur drag khro mo rag
gdong ma sogs dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ shel brag nas spyan drangs pa'i gshin rje dregs 'joms gter

srung dang bcas pa'i dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ sha 'ug nas sprangs pa'i thugs rje chen po bde gshegs kun 'dus gter srung dang bcas pa'i dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ khyad par rje
'di gnubs nam snying gi sprul pa yin pa dang / gnam lcags dang sha 'ug gnyis kyi chos bdag yin pa sogs gter kha so so nas lung gis zin pa bcas/ gter ston chen po yang chos
bdag por 'phrod pas dges tshor dpag med mdzad/ gzhan yang gshin rje tshe bdag gi dbang / las byang padma'i ljon shing gi lung / zlum po bzhi'i dbang / mkha' 'gro snying
thig gi dbang dang lung skor la yang gsang gnad kyi man ngag kha byang/ btags grol 'grel pa/ sangs rgyas 'das rjes/ rigs lnga phyi nang gi sgrub thabs bum dbang dang bcas
pa/ dbang gsum pa'i lag len/ rigs lnga'i ngo sprod/ bum sgrub/ dkyila'akhor/ gsang dbang shes rab ye shes dang bcas pa'i lhan thabs/ rig pa ngo sprod/ rigs lnga phyi
nang gsang gsum gyi sgrub pa/ rta phag kki'i las byang / tshogs mchod/ rgyab yig rigs lnga mchod 'bul tshogs mchod/ zhal gdams gnad 'bebs/ DAkki'i nor sgrub/ lam gyi don
khrid/ ti la gsal byed/ lung gi phreng ba/ rtags tshad yi ge khregs chod khrid/ mkha'

'gro snying thig chen po/ DAkki'i zhal gdams gsang ba'i dum bu/ rnal 'byor bzhi'i gdams pa/ zhus len gser phreng / DAkki'i lam 'bras/ zhal gdams gnad kyi thigs pa/ rdo rje
chu 'thung gi man ngag dbang sdud yang khol/ don gsal me long / zhi ba bar do/ khro bo bar do/ bar do'i zhal gdams/ 'chi rtags bsal ba/ gtum mo'i gdams pa/ rdo rje'i bcud
len/ bka' srung nag mo'i rgyud/ le'u/ srog sgrub nag mo'i sgrub thabs/ shan sgrub kyi dbang dang rjes gnang / rtsa gsum dril sgrub/ tshe sgrub 'chi bslu/ rta phag mkha'
'gro'i tshe sgrub/ gsang sgrub/ gsol 'debs le tshan gnyis/ gter bdag mchod thabs rnams/ le bdun dang rten bskyed brgyud 'debs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ rje 'bangs nyer lnga/ gter
ston gsol 'debs/ gter ston gsung rtsom/ thugs thig las byang / thugs thig sngon 'gro gur drag gi las byang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ gtor bzlog/ gter ston sku bstod/ ja mchod
gsum/ byang gter thugs rje chen po'i bdag bskyed bsdus pa/ mkhyen brtse nus mnga' ma/ gter ston brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ gnod sbyin rtse dmar gyi rgyud sgrub thabs rnams
kyi lung / rta mgrin rje khol ngar po'i dbang rnams gsan/

tshes bcu gsum nyin rje nyid nas gter ston chen por gzungs grwa lnga/ sgrol ljang / tshedakar rnams kyi rjes gnang stsal/ de nyin gter ston chen pos/ mchog gsum 'di nyid la
zhabs brtan bsod ye ma tshigs bcad dang/ 'bul ba sogs legs par phul bas rten 'brel legs tshogs che bar 'grig gter ston chen por yang ston mo gzab rgyas phebs rdzong gi gnang
cha sogs rgya cher stsal/ phyag mdzod sogs zhabs phyi rnams la'ang gnang cha shin tu rgyas par mdzad/ tshes bcu bdun nyin gter ston phebs skyel ba phyag mdzod sogs drung
'khor bco lnga gnang /lo sngon ma'i nang sras yum dpon g.yog dbus su phebs/ tshes bcu dgu'i nyin gdan sar phebs rgyu la/ phyag mdzod sogs drung 'khor bco lnga phebs
bsur gnang/ sang nyin lhun rtser phyag dbang la phebs par phebs bsu gzab rgyas stsal/chu stod zla'i tshes gsum la sdings ma dang srid gsum gyi dge 'dun brgya phrag brgal
tsam la thugs rje chen po'i dmar 'khrid tshem bu lugs kyi dpe lung / thugs rje chen po dang phyag chen zung 'jug nyams len/ gtor chog/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus/ gter ston 'ja'
tshon snying po'i rnam thar/ rnam thar dri med/ 'byung 'dul bdag bskyed/ gter ston gol 'debs gnyis/

rje 'di'i sku bstod gnyis/ chos rgyal rdo rje'i sku bstod gnyis/ ye shes sku mchog thugs thig sngon 'gro dang las byang sogs kyi lung / rab byung bsnyen rdzogs/ kun rig gi
dbang / 'byung 'dul rjes gnang bcas snod ldan rnams kyi re ba tshim par mdzad/ gzhan yang 'dod chos zhu mi so sor gnyan sgrol rjes gnang / phyag 'tshal nyir gcig gi lung
phur pa'i dbang sogs gnang/dbyug zla'i bcu dgu la gter ston gyi sku bstod mchog tu mi 'gyur ma ban tshang par 'dzugs par gnang thog tshogs dbur phebs/ yang gsol 'debs rgyang
'bod ma zhig kyang mdzad/ yab rjer zhabs brtan gsol 'debs sho lo ka gsum ljags bsgrigs gnang / yang chos skyong chen po'i lung bzhin gro bzhin gyi tshes bcu dgu'i nyin
zhabs brtan phul/khrums zla'i tshes lnga'i nyin byang gnam mtshor chibs kha phyogs/ gcung rgyan mchog rin po che/ gdung brgyud sku mched yum bcas sku 'khor ser skya rnams
kyis phebs skyel zhus/ 'gro rnams smin grol gyi lam la 'god bzhin pas/ se sa lha sa sogs su tshe dbang gnang / rim bzhin bye dkar sbug tu phebs par phyis nas phyag phyi
rnams nyon mongs pa na/ rje 'di la bsnyel

med par byang shar la gzigs nas phyag smon du ma mdzad/ go ra lcags 'phrang gdong nyin gyi khrus sgor sku khrus dang / gsol 'debs rgyas par gnang skabs nam mkhar stas bzang
sna tshogs kun dang ba 'dren pa byung / de nas bkra shis do bo cher phebs/ slob dpon gyi gzim phug sa skya phug ces grags pa'i mdun na zhabs rjes/ brag la tshe bum rang
byon/ tshe chu sogs phug pa dang / phyag rjes zhabs rjes du ma yod pa mjal/ ri sbob brag na phyag rjes yod pa 'di gnas bshad pas karma pa'i phyag rjes yin zhus par/ gsung
las nga ni slob dpon gyi phyag rjes su ngos 'dzin gsungs nas smon lam mdzad/ khrus sgo'i rtsar phebs nas gsol 'debs le'u bdun ma dang / phyag mchod mdzad/ mtsho la phyag
rjes lan bzhi gzigs/ g.yon gyi phyag rjes yin 'dug gsungs/ rdo rje phag mo dang dkyil 'khor du ma gzigs/ de nas zhang sna'i gzhung du skye bo'i tshogs la tshe dbang lcags
sdong ma dang slob dpon gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor gnang / de nas khong khyim mdor bra'u rdo rje rnam rgyal sogs kyis mchod/ bsngo ba rgyas par mdzad/ la rgan la rtsar phebs
pa na gzhi bdag rnams 'phrang nas rtsub 'gyur che bar phur pa'i bskyed rim mdzad pas srog snying phul nas bran du khol/ rams sdings ma dang brag dkar ba ste dge

'dun ma dang gling dkar rdzong dpon sogs skye bo'i tshogs la chos char phab/ mdor na byang phyir 'brog chos kyi sgra mi thos pa rnams la chos kyi sgron me sbar te sangs rgyas
kyi bstan pa rgyas par mdzad do/ /de nas rim bzhin dbyug zla'i nyer lnga'i nyin gcung rgyan mchog rin po ches gtso mdzad lha sde mi sdes phebs bsu/ 'dus tsogs kyi ser
phreng bcas gdan sa chen por phebs so/ de nas rgyan mchog rin po che/ gdung brgyud sku mched sogs gzhis bzhugs rnams la sku 'khyos dang 'dus tshogs su mang ja 'gyed bcas/
phyogs dgon ngor thub bstan sogs sa dge rnying 'brug karma pa sogs ris med kyi dgon gnas nye skor tshang mar mang ja 'gyed bcas gzab rgyas stsal/ nA lendra'i grwa rgyun
rnams la so thar sdom pa 'bogs pa/ tshe dbang kun rig dbang sogs dang / ngor dang thub bstan gyi khams 'gros pa 'ga' la'ang dbang dang rjes gnang lung sogs gnang / drug cu
pa'i tshogs dpon mdzad cing / phyag mdzod mtshungs med nas nyid kyi zhabs brtan du phur sgrub zhag bdun sgrub pa'i tshogs dbur phebs/rgyal zla'i tshes brgyad nas nyer gsum
bar lhun rtse'i mgon khang gtor spod du phebs/ 'dus tshogs su bka' 'gyur gsung

sgrog nyin gsum gnang /rta zla'i tshes gsum nas rnam rtser gter gsar thugs thig gi sku mtshams tshugs/ yi dam lha'i byin rlabs mtshan ltas khyad par can mang du mnga'/rta zla'i
tshes bcu la mar me mtshan thub gcig gi zhag lnga thub pas phyag phyi kun ngo mtshar du gyur/ khra zla'i tshes brgyad la sku mtshams grol/ tshes bcu la gnam rtse'i grwa
rigs la mang ja 'gyed dang bcas rtsa gsum le bdun gyi lung / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang / bstod pa 'ga' re dang / za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg gi lung rnams gnang
/ gzhan yang lhun rtse'i drung 'khor rnams dang / srid gsum slob dpon sogs la tshe dbang scags sdong ma dang sgrol dkar sgrub thabs gtor chog bum chog rjes gnang bcas
dang / bum gter 'jug tshul sogs kyi lung / snye mo ba gcig la dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi lung /nag zla'i tshes lnga la gter gsar thugs thig las byang btsugs/ mchod pa tshogs
'khor gzab rgyas mdzad/ nam mkhar 'ja' gur phub pa sogs kyi mtshan stas byung / de nas phur bzlog nyin gsum gnang /sa ga'i tshes bcu gnyis la chos gling dbon po sogs grwa
bcu

bdun la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs dang / lha brgyad/ sme btsegs/ ri khrod ma/ seng ge sgra/ thub pa gtso 'khor gsum/ spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum/ rnam rgyal/ gshed dmar/
seng gdong ma/ sher phyin dkar mo rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / thugs sgrub gnad kyi gzer lnga drag po'i las byang / dbang chog 'jam nag sgrub thabs las tshogs grub gnyis bsam
'phel/ rnal 'byor ma'i 'pho ba/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi 'pho ba/ pa ru bya bral lugs kyi 'pho ba rnams kyi lung stsal/ tshes nyi shu la sram sa dpon sogs ser skya nyis
brgya tsam la tshe rta zung 'bral gyi dbang / ban tshang pa rnams la phur dbang dang / khro bo bcu'i rjes gnang stsal/ yang se pa'i grwa pa rnams la kun rig 'byung 'dul/
rnam 'joms/ tshe dbang lcags sdong ma rnams gnang / shing byi nas bzung lhun rtse nas phur sgrub nyin bdun chag med btsugs pa bzhiin tshogs dbur phebs/ de skabs sil snyan
'dzam gling 'brug sgra phyag tu 'byor/chu stod zla'i tshes gcig la chos skyong chen pos rje nyid la zhabs pad bskal brgyar brtan phyir/ kha btags nyin bde ma gsum/ tshe
thang / gos g.yog gsum/ dar yug gsum rnams kyis mgo byas dgu tshan gsum/ gsol ja/ tshogs 'khor

sogs rgya dpangs shin tu che ba dang bcas zhabs brtan phul bar/ de nub nas brtsams zhag bcu gcig bar sku mtshams dam par mdzad/ grol bstun bskang gso smin rgyas/ tshes bcu
bdun nyiin lhun rtser phebs/ tshul khang bla mas ya ju 'khor drug gsum/ dre'u/ gzhan yang ja gos dar sogs 'bul ba zab par phul/ tshul khang bla ma dpon slob sogs grwa bzhi
bcu tsam la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs dang / tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ kyai rdor rgyu dbang / byin rlabs phyag mdud/ gyon pa sogs kyis mgu bar mdzad/zla ba bdun pa'i nang
rdo brkos byed zer ba'i sgrub pa gnyis byung nas/ gzungs sngags 'dra brkos gsungs/ de snga rdo brkos len dkon pa las med kyang khong rang gnyiis kyis sngon bdag chen kun
dga' bsam grub kyi spyan ras gzigs kyi sku 'dra brkos pa'i rdo 'di nas thon zer nas btsal bas lha lung phur rdo brkos len spus gtsang gter bton pa bzhin byung bar/ rigs
gsum mgon po o rgyan gtso 'khor gsum/ gu ru mtshan brgyad/ sa bir/ thub pa drug tshe 'jam/ yang o rgyan gnyis/ gter bton 'gyur med rdo rje; rje 'di nyid bcas kyi sku rnamasadang
/ thugs rten mchod rten gsum/ gzhan gzungs sngags badzra gu

ru/ rigs gsum mgon po/ kyai rdor/ phur ba/ yang dag mi g.yo ba/ sgrol ma/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal/ gdugs dkar/ mgon po la sogs pa'i gzungs sngags mang du brkos/ gzhan yang dpon
g.yog ser skya tshang ma'i sku gsung thugs kyi rten tu mang bar brkos pa'i ya mtshan du byed pa byung ba yang rje nyid la chos srung rnams kyis rdo gter phul ba gdon mi
za zhing / rdo brkos gnyis la yang gnang sbyin mgu bar stsal lo/ /de yan gyi thub bstan pa byams pa lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i rje 'di'i rnam thar le tshan gsum las 'byung
ba bzhin bstan zin nas de'i 'phro ni/ de dus phyag mdzod mtshungs med dang / chos dkar gnyis kyi thog skabs shig khri chen gong ma nyid kyi zhabs phyir ru gnyer rdo rje
lhun grub khrid de dpon g.yog gnyis kyis lhun rtser bcad rgya mdzad yod tshul gyi zab phu mjal bar gsang stabs kyis phebs zab bu gter lung du sgrub pa mdzad skabs gsol chas
rnams shin tu bkren par byung mus/ rin sgang gi grwa pa gsum tsam zhig gi zab bu mjal bar phyin pas khong rnams zab bu mthil du 'byor bstun zab bu mthil pa rnams kyis/
rtse gdong gong ma gter lung na sku mtshams la bzhugs yod pas rtse gdong pa 'dra byung tshe gter lung du shog zhes lon

sprod gsung byung bas khyed rnams 'gro dgod yod do zer bas khong tsho'i sems la gong ma lhun rtser bcad rgya gnang yod gang yin nam snyam nas phyin pas / gter lung du 'byor
bstun gong ma bcad rgya grol ba dang stabs mtshungs byung ste mjal phyag zhus pas gsung las/ rtse gdong nas yong mi 'dra e 'dug nged la chas 'dra skyel rtsis yin pas da
dung ma byung / phyag mdzod rnams kyis nged la lto chad gtong rgyu yin pa 'dra zhes gsungs shing / khong tsho'i chas 'phros yod pa rnams phul bas shin tu mnyes/ tshang mas
lhan cig zab bu mthil mjal bar phebs dus gtir ston bdud 'dul gling pa rdo rje gro lod rtsal dang mjal/ sgrub gling gong du gter ston dpon g.yog tshang ma gdan 'dren zhus
te gsol ja zhig gi thog gter ston nas phreng ba byin rlabs zhig zhus shing / de nas gter ston dpon g.yog rnams kyis zab bu shin tu zhib par mjal skabs gnas rten rnams kyi
bshad pa sku gnyer la med pa kun kyang / zhabs drung gong ma nyid nas dwangs gsal 'khrul zad du gnang bas kun ngo mtshar shing / nyii ma'ang ldab 'gyur gyi ring ba byung
'dug pas/ der yod tshang mas mgrin gcig par bla ma nam mkha'i snying poo'i rnam par sprul pa yin pas bzung ba yin 'dug zer ba sogs nges don gyi dad

pa thun mong ma yin pa thob cing / rin sgang grwa pa rnams sog po mjal bar byon/ dpon g.yog gnyis slar yang gter lung du phyag phebs/ de skabs bya bral ba 'ga' zhig la 'bru
sogs kyi gsol ras yong bas len par shog gsungs pas/ khong bya bral rnams rtse gdong du 'byor/ zhag shas nas dpon g.yog gnyis kyang lhun rtser phebs shing phyag mdzod rnams
la zab bu'i bya bral ba rnams la gsol ras 'dra sprod bka' phebs par phyag mdzod rnams kyis gtan nas ma sbyin pas bla ma zhal shin tu skyengs pa zhig byung /gzhan yang
bka' chos 'chad nyan mang po dang / lhag par skabs der bdud rtse ril bu sgrub par mdzad pas sngon dus las 'phel shin tu che zhing / 'phur ba lta bu'i phu shar gyi chu 'go
dang / lhun rtse sde yangs sogs nye bskor rnams nas mang po rnyed pa bcas ya mtshan che bar byung gdug cing / spre lor skye tshogs rnams la mu ge lta bus shin tu bkren pa
zhig byung bas/ khri chen nyid nas phyag mdzod rnamasal srid gsum bka' rgya'i thog nas mi ser la 'bru khal re tsam sprod bka' phebs par/ phyag ma dzod rnams kyis ma sbyin
pa sogs phyi nang gi gnas tshul ngan pa 'ga' zhig gi rkyen byas kyang snang ngor lho bod 'khrugs skabs ngos nas

chings la phyin dus sems can mang po'i blo gtad yod pas lus kyi dka' thub ma bcad na nyes pa mi byang bas 'bras ljongs gnas skor zhig la 'gro gsungs shing / lhun rtser bcad
rgya gnang yod tshul gyi kun la gsang stabs kyi zhabs phyir mgron gnyer tshangs pa/ dpon tshang sman phrug pa/ gzim dpon rdor don/ chos skyong sku bsten rgyal khang pa bsod
nams chos mchog ban tshang pa lnga drug tsam dang / gzhan thor bu bcas thog mar sku chas rnams lhun rtse sde yangs byang du sa srib la phebs te dpon g.yog rnams nam gung
la phebs par lhun tse'i nub kyi phebs lam sogs la chos srung 'phreng bas khal g.yag rnams har 'grogs kyis khal rnams log pa sogs byung zhing / phyag mdzod chos dkar gyis
lhun tse'i sde yangs dang / mtshungs med kyis brag chen rgyab tsam gyi bar phebs skyel zhus/ dpon g.yog rnams brag chen bud tsam 'thon pas blo bde'o/ /zhes gsungs shing
/ ru bzhi ma'i gru brgyud de dpal rnam dga' ba gdong / gzhis rtse rin rtse sogs brgyud de 'bras ljongs su phebs nas 'bras ljongs kha stod kyi gnas brten rnams mjal gnang
thog tshur phebs lam bar gyi la chen gangs la dang zer ba'i mdun du phebs tshe do nub la 'di

cis kyang babs pa 'gro gsungs par mgron gnyer tshangs pas do nub thang yang chad cing tshang mas 'gro mi thub khyed rang rnams 'byon na yang nga ni 'di gar sdod zhes zhus par
brten de nub der bzhugs pas/ kha ba nyin mtshan sbrel bar babs te/ dpon g.yog rnams phar tshur gar yar phebs ma thub par zhag shas de khar bzhugs pa 'bras ljongs kha stod
pa rnams kyis shes nas g.yag mang po dang bcas phebs lam bcags/ slar yang 'bras ljongs gting la phebs te gnas brtan mtha' dag zhib gzigs gnang rjes dpon g.yog phal cher
tshad pas bsnyung zhing / gong gi zhabs phyi rnams dang ban tshang pa gsum tsam ma gtogs phyir log yong nye'i skabs chos skyong tse dmar ba thog phebs byung ste gsol ja
zhal dkar gang mchod nas zhal dkar kha bub tu bzhag chos skyong nyid shin tu mya ngan dang bcas dge bshes nub phyogs o rgyan gyi yul du dgongs pa gtad song bas gdug 'dre'ang
re zhig zhabs phyir 'gro rgyu yin pas khyod tshang mas dge bshes kyi sku chas rnams bor zegs su ma song bar gdan sar 'byor ba ma byas tshe gdug 'dres rta pa'i nyin
lam bco brgyad kyi sa nas bltas pa'i tshar gcod pa yin no zhes gsungs shing mthar dgung grangs lnga bcu nga gnyis su phebs pa khyi lo zla ba drug pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin ngo

mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te gzhan don la dgongs nas zhag bdun song rjes spur zhu bas thugs ma tshig par kha dog cung zad nag pa pad ma 'od 'bar gyi sku'i dbyibs can
phyi shun pad ma 'dab brgyad kha zum pa lta bu'i rtser ldem phru gsal ba nyug ge 'thon pa'i ngo mtshar shin tu che ba dang / spur rus spur thal tshang ma khong rnams kyis
lus med du khyer te gdan sar 'byor bstun dgongs rdzogs rnams gcung bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po nyid nas thugasangs rgyas phun tshogs gdan 'dren thog dge 'dun tshang mar
mang 'gyed sogs rgya che mu med mdzad pa dang chabs cig nyid kyi skus 'gan che bzhes kyis ngor sogs dbus gtsang dgon khag tshang mar mang 'gyed rgya che dang / rtse gdong
tshogs dbur ngor chen brnyan gtsor bzhugs kyi nang rten dus thang chen mor grags pa dang / dngul gdung rin po che shin tu che zhing bzo dbyibs phra rgyan sogs so skye'i
blo yul las 'das pa gsar bskrun gyi gzungs bzhugs su gong gi thugs ngo mtshar can de yang bzhugs shing / de skabs bal po bzo pa rnams kyis gser dngul sogs dngos po sbas
skums byas pa nub gcig khong rang tshang ma'i rmi ltas su ban btsun gzugs 'bong shin tu che zhing sma ra sogs me ris su yod pa zhig byung nas dngos po rnams

'di na 'di 'dug lta bu'i rang rang gi snod nas bton te khyer/ mi rnams la mig gcer gcer lta ba sogs tshubs 'gyur che ba byung bas bzo pa thams cad 'jigs par gyur te/ 'gyod
bshags dang bcas dngos po gang khyer phul zhing / rab tu gnas pa sogs rjes kyi bya ba tshang ma mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad do/ /// bsod nams 'phags pa/de'i
gcung bgres pa bsod nams 'phags pa grags pa lha dbang rdo rje ne chu lug gro bzhin nyer bdun la 'khrugangs nas chung ngur gshegs/// bsod nams dbang rgyal/gcung gzhon
pa ngag dbang nor bu bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po ni shing byar 'khrungs/ chung ngu'i dus nas gcen gong ma khri chen nyid kyi drung du srid gsum grwa rigs dang bcas gsung
ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa yongs

rdzogs dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa la sogs pa rjes gnang mtha' yas par gsan zhing / gzhan yang ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje sogs khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po'i
dbu'i cod pan du gyur pa rnams la'ang chos rnams gsan cing / yi dam chos srung gi ljags bsnyen kha shas mthar phyin/ gong ma na rim gyi thugs dam rten rdo rje gzhon nu'i
sku gtsor bzhugs kyi gong ma lnga'i gser sku byin can rnams dang / da lta rin sgang na bzhugs pa'i lam 'bras bla brgyud kyi sku sman 'dam las grub pa sogs rgya chen bzhengs
pa dang / stag lung pa'i sras mo bkra shis tshe ring dbang phyug khab tu bzhes/ gzhan la dbang lung man ngag 'chad pa dang/ sgrub mchod bskang ba gtor bzlog sogs gong
ma rnams kyi phyag rgyun bzhin mdzad/ bstan gegs kyi yab yum thugs ma mthun par tsho gnyis su bzhugs dgos byung bas yab kyi phyag mdzod kun blo dang sras yum gyi phyag
mdzod kun dga' don grub kyis byas rjes mi ring bar yum bkra shis tshe ring dbang phyug gshegs/ de nas kun blo'ang 'das pa btsan du skyes te da lta btsan rgod du grags pa
bar skabs su rtse gdong par phan shin tu thogs pa byung / 'das tshab rgyal khang bkra shis bstan pa bsko bar mdzad do/ /

// kun dga' tshe dbang rin 'dzin/de'i sras bgres pa 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyii rnam sprul du grags pa kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin ne me lugs sa ga zla ba'i tshes bco lngar
ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas bla brang gzims shod du sku bltams nas nar son pa dang gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen por dbu phud phul/ khri chen byams pa bsod
nams lhun grub kyi drung du tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ grub rgyal ma/ 'byung 'dul rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / bka' bsgo byin rlabs/ ngag dbang bsod nams lhun grub kyi
drung du tshe dkar/ grub rgyal ma/ 'byung 'dul rnams kyi rjes gnang dang/ khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po'i drung du gu ru drag dmar/ bde mchog nag po pa/ gsang
'dus 'jam rdor/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i stod las smad las/ kyai rdor/ je tA ri lugs kyi tshe dpag lha dgu ltsagasasdong ma/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus rnams kyi dbang / 'jam dbyangs
dmar ser smra seng gnyis kyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang lung bcas/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang / rgya gzhung de'i 'grel pa ngag dbang bstan rdor gyi mdzad pa/ gsang

'dus 'jam rdor gyi dkyil chog gtor chog mchod 'phreng / bkra shis/ spyan ras gzigs la brten pa'i 'pho ba spros bcas spros med/ bar do ngo sprod/ kun rig bsnyen thabs/ kyai
rdor man ngag lugs kyi bsnyen thabs rnams ngag dbang brtan pas mdzad pa/ lcags sdong ma'i mtshams sbyor/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi sgrub thabs/ sa los mdzad pa'i kun rigs
brgyud 'debs/ mdzad bcu'i bkra shis/ myang ral nasabargyud pa'i drag dmar rjes gnang / dkar bdud rjes gnang lung bcas/ bdag chen rgya gar bas mdzad pa'i dkar bdud bskang
gso/ slob dpon padmas mdzad pa'i rdo rje las rim/ kun dga' bsam grub kyis mdzad pa'i phur pa'i dkyil chog dang bdag 'jug sa los mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub gsal byed/ brgyud
'debs rgyas bsdus/ dkonamachog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i kyai rdor dkyil chog rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa danDa ka dang bkra shis/ slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo
rjes mdzad pa'i bstod pa nyi shu pa/ ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lha brgyad rjes gnang/ dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum nas gur rigs bsdus zur 'debs/ 'jigs byed

bcu gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil tho/ las gshin gtor chog rjes gnang / kyai rdor gtor chog mdzes rgyan ma gtogs bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs/ dmar po bskor gsum gyi be'u bum nas dpe sna
kha yar ma gtogs tshang ma/ mkhyen rabs byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyi drung du rdo rje phreng ba dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor bcas kyi dbang / bde mchog bong zhal
gshed dmar lha lnga rnams kyi dbang/ seng gdang ma/ 'jam nag khyung khra/ rta mgrin dbyug tho can/ phyag rdor gos sngon/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ grub chen brgyad bcu/
dzam dmar srog sgrub/ sgrol ma dmar mo rnams kyis rjes gnang/ bla ma zhi khro dang grub rgyal tshe dbang/ de rnams kyi yig lung kha yar dang bcas pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i
byin rlabs/ gsung ngag slob bshad lugs rtar gsan skabs lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang bir srung thun mong ba/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ brda' chig brgyud/ brda' don gsal
ba/ bla ma riin 'byung rnams kyi byin rlabs/ lung la brgyud 'debs bla ma rdor 'dzin ma/ kun bzang ma/ rje btsun gong ma lnga/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ tshogs nyan gnyis/ dkar
brag pa/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dal pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ buddha shrI/ ngor chen/ sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis rnam thar/

uShNi Sha'i bsrung 'khor sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ rtsa lhung rnam bshad rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa pod dmar ser gyi lung / mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa'i jo lugs sgrol ma nyer
gcig gi rjes gnang / rta mgrin lcags ral/ sme tsegs dud kha/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang / rnam sras ser chen 'khor mang / sgrol dkar/ sangs rgyas klu dbang / 'byung 'dul 'jam
dbyangs/ seng ge sgra/ gur lcam dral lha gsum/ dkar po tshe 'phel rnams kyis rjes gnang bcas gsan/ rdo rje brag rig 'dzin padma 'phrin las kyi drung du gsol 'debs le'u
bdun ma rgyal 'phrin don bcu pa/ rnying lugs gtor ma brgya rtsa/ grub thob tshe dbang / 'chi med dpal ster gyi nyams len rgyun khyer/ thugs rje chen po 'gro ba kun sgrol
dang / drag mthing thugs rje'i rtsal dbang / sgrub chen bka' brgyad mgyogs dbang bum rgya can/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub/ dur khrod bdag po rnams kyi rjes gnang gsan pa sogs
yongs 'dzin du ma las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son gzhon nu nas sku mched gnyis ka'i gdan sa'i 'khur bzhes lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pa rnams gong ma so so'i phyag bzhes star
te skabs shig dpal sa skyar byon dus mangga'i mtshan can las zab chos 'ga' zhig gsan pa'i tshe/ drag po sgrol dbang gi dus thub bstan lha

chen gyi mkhan rin po che bsam gtan lhun po la/ khyed mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi sku skye yin pas kho bos gral 'gor bzhugs gsungs pa sogs 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi
rnam sprul du zhal gyi bzhes shing / a mes zhabs kyi yol mo sprul sku rin po che bstan 'dzin nor bu la gsung brtag zhu bar mdzad pa'i mkha' 'gro'i gsang lung du/ sbas
tshul gyi yang srid gnyis phebs par gsungs pa'i gcig 'di yin zhing / gcig yab rje rdo rje 'chang ratna'i mtshan can yin par kho bos gdung rabs gsol 'debs kha skong lhun grub
rgyun skyong su smos pa ltar ro/ /de dus bzhugs tsher du lha bsangs rgyas pa zhig mdzad de de'i chas sogs nyer mkho rnams zhag shas bar ma bsdu zhig gsungs kyang / gzhan
dbang gi blo bur du bsdus pas yab rje so bdun gyi skabs zhing khams brjes pa sogs ma 'ongs pa'i rten 'brel de ltar du gyur/ mthar dgung grangs nyer bzhir phebs phebs
skabs khri chen gong ma gzhan don la dgogs pa'i dgongs rdzogs rdo rje gzhon nu'i dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod tshugs pa'i tshes gsum gyi tho rengs mnal lam du o rgyan mkha' 'gro'i
gling du dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyi khrod na khri chen de nyid khri stan mthon po'i steng na bzhugs shing da dung khri stong pa zhig kyang 'dug pa las khri

chen nyid kyigasungs las da tsha bo rang yang nga'i tsar shog rtse bdong du bsdad tshe skyid po mi yong zhes gsungs pa'i mur mnal bsad phul gdung dbyangs 'di yang mdzad do/
/na mo/ bsod nams ye shes tshogs gnyis rgya mtsho'i gter/ / bstan 'dzin gtsug rgyan yid bzhin nor bu che/ /dbang gi rgyal po 'gro ba'i mgon po mchog /byams pa'i dpal mnga'
chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /lho nub rnga yab zangs mdog dpal gyi ri/ /mtshan nyid ldan pa'i rin chen gzhal yas su/ /rtsa gsum dkyil 'khor sprin phung ltar gtib cing
/ /me tog 'ja' tshon dri zhim spos ngad can/ /de ltar phun sum tshogs pa'i gzhal yas su/ /dbyer med mtsho skyes rdo rje thod phreng rtsal/ /gnyis su med pa rtsa ba'i bla
ma la/ /sgo gsum mi phyed dad pas gsol 'debs na/ /bdag sogs ma gyur 'gro ba'i tshogs rnams kun/ /khyed nyid bzhugs pa'i zhing mchog dam pa der/ / phyir mi ldog pa'i go 'phang
thob gyur cig /bza' bca'i snying po dpag bsam ljon 'bras dang / /btung ba'i bcud du bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun bcas/ /bgo ba'i gos su rnam dag tshul khrims gos/ /de ltar
mi zad gter la longs spyod cing / rtag tu 'bral med byin gyis rlabs tu gsol/ /

zhes gsugs shing / de nas zla shas song rjes zhing brje bar nye ba na nyin gcig glo bur du gnang nyin 'o skol 'grul chen po zhig la 'gro dgos yong gsung bar/ zhabs phyi rnams
kyis de ltar na thugs gra gang yang ma sgrigs pas ji ltar phebs legs zhus pas/ dngos kyi 'grul min pa zhig yong zhes gsungs pa bzhin gnang dus de la bsnyun gzhi glo bur
ba zhig bzhes pa'i tshul gyi lcags lug zla ba lnga pa'i nyer lnga'i nyin dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan pa'i tshe/ dpal sa skya'i rigs 'dzin pho brang
la 'ja' zug de nas ma 'gyangs par rje btsun mkha' spyod dbang mo kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma 'khrungs pas sku skyer ngos 'dzin byed kyang kho bo ni gong ltar ro/ /de nas
dgongs rdzogs grub mtha' ris med dgon khag mang por mang 'gyed mchod 'bul sogs zab cing rgya che ba dang nang rten dngul gdung rin po che shiin tu che zhing bzo dbyibs
phra rgyan gyiis phyug pa sogs zhabs rjes dngos gtsang bar mdzad do/ /

ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan/sras gzhon pa ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan ni sa bya dbo zla'i tshes gnyis la sku bltams ma thag zhabs rdo rje skyil krung / phyag chos 'chad
kyi phyag rgya dang bcas te saM kr-i ta'i skad du chos gsungs shing / sku nar son nas kyang mkhen rab shin tu rno bas/ lan re klags pa tsam gyis nges pa thugs su chud
pa zhig ste/ sku na phra mo'i skabs rnying lugs la cung zhig mi dgyes pa'i tshul bstan cing / gter bdag gling pa chen po rtse gdong du phebs skabs/ zhabs drung nas bdag gi
pu ti rgya khab tshad ma zhig gi tshad tsam nyin gcig la 'dzin thub gsung bar/ de 'dra rang e bden nam gsungs pas/ 'o na sku zhabs thugs yid ches phyir sang nyin nyi ma
shar ba nas dgong ja bar la 'dzin thub par byed/ de yang thugs yid ches phyir sngar rnying lugs kyi dpe cha lta rtog ma myang bas gter chen rin po che'i phyag dpe zhig dgos
gnang bar/ gter gsar rig 'dzin thugs thig dang/ gshin rje dregs 'joms kyi pu ti sdom par khab tshad longs pa zhig gnang bar/ nyi shar nas dgong ja'i bar la ljags 'dzin
grub ste

rgyugs 'bul mdzad pas thugs ha las/ 'jam dbyangs dngos su rang phebs 'dug gsungs shing legs 'bul sogs rgya spom che bar gnang zhing / gong du bshad pa ltar gzhon nu nas gcen
dang lhan cig gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen por dbu phud phul zhing dbu bla rnams kyang phal cher gcen dang mtshungs/ mdo sngags rig gnas sgra tshad sogs gang la'ang
phyag thogs med pa'i mkhas pa chen par gyur/ lkog gyur thogs med du mkhyen cing grub pa'i mtshan ma yang mang du brnyes/ lhag par 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i ljags
bsnyen mdzad skabasarje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po mngon sum du zhal gzigs/ sa phyogs 'dir rang re'i bstan pa 'di ni mthar thug pa yin pas da ni gnas dang
chos lugs sde dgon bcas par chags pa spongs shig zhes sogs zhal lta lung bstan gnang zhing / khyod skye bar phyi mar rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal mthong ste rjes
su 'dzin par gyur ro/ /zhes dbugs dbyung thob pa dang/ gter ston bdud 'dul gling pa rdo rje gro lod rtsal gyi lung byang las/ g.yu sgra snying po'i skye ba bcu gsum pa/
/nor bu'i mi can de la gtad rgya gyis/ /zhes g.yu sgra'i rnam sprul du gsungs shing / snye mo bya sgo ba'i sras mo tshe ring bu khrid khab tu bzhes/

de ltar bstan 'gro'i don rlabs chen mdzad skabs snyigs ma'i rang mdangs zlog med lta bus rtsee gdong chos srid la 'pho 'gyur byung tshul ni/ de yang gter ston bdud 'dul gling
pas spa gro stag tshang brag nas lung bstan rigs gsum bzhes pa'i lung byang las/ gtsang gi rtse gdong du ru kha'iH gdung la nyams chag 'byung nyen cheH zhes gsal ba dang/
gzhan yang dpal mgon zhal gyi rnam sprul g.yag rwa lnga grags pa 'di snga thog mya ngan las 'das tshul bstan skabs zhal ngo rnams kyis ma mkhyen par gzhan gyis de'i dbu
spyod lam ngu skyur bas rtse gdong bar skabs nyams chag tu 'gro ba'i rten 'brel shar shing / slar dbu gar song 'dri bar mdzad pas/ las byed rnams kyis rgyu mtshan zhus
pa bzhin/ spyod rten dang bcas par byi dor gyis gtsang ba mdzad pa dang chabs cig de nyid la khrus dang mnga' gsol rab gnas bskang ba sogs rgyas pa'i sgo nas rten 'dzugs
mdzad pa der/ sde srid zangs ri ba lha sa rdzong pa'i skye bas snyan shal phul ba'i rkyen gyis/ zhal khyim gyi spu rnams gyen du langs shing / shangs thad kyi rlon gsher
yod pa cung zad skam pas zhal ngo rnams la mi shis pa dang / rtse gdong sku rim chen mo'i 'chams kyi skabs su pu tra'i sku 'bag gi zhal nang nas khrag gi rgyun

'dzags pa dang / rkang gling 'bud mi rnams kyi byad bzhin la tshon byug pa'i phyag lon gnang bar tshon de dam ches pa lta bu'i 'bud mi rnams kyi mchu zum ma thub par rkang
gling 'bud ma thub pa dang / dge 'dun rnams kyi tshogs gral la bong bu pho mo gnyis kyi 'bros 'ded byas pa dang / na khra zer ba'i na ra rtswa brnga'i skabs bong bu rnams
kyis bzhas byas pa dang / gzhan yang skye bo rnams kyis tshig shin tu mi shis pa'i glu sgrog dang / shing spre sa skya'i dus mdos nyer dgu'i zor 'phang grub nas yar lam
'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug gi thugs dam ma mgon po'i 'chams sku 'gyel bas rdul thon pa sogs byung 'dug cing / rkyen ni phyag mdzod mtshungs med du grags pa des khri
chen gong ma'i zhabs 'gyur ji bzhin ma byung bas khri chen gshegs rjes rje de nyid kyi gcung gi phyag mdzod rtsis bzhes kyi kho par tsha len mdzad pas dam nyams de dang
de'i rjes 'brel la btsun srang smad shar phyogs pa/ 'dren dpon pa/ thong dga' ba sogs kyi zhabs 'dren sgrub 'dod kyi kha phyir ltas ngos mtshungs med kyi tsha bo ban log

bcas

rtse gdong du yong ste thugs bsun zhus par dam nyams de dag la dmigs gtor bzlog mdzad pa na de dag gis byang brgyud rgyal por mthu byas so zhes btsun mo chos skyid la zhu log
byas pas rgyal po'i drung du bdag chen bsod nams dbang rgyal nyid byon pa sher sbyang gi dag yig rgyal po'i tham ka can mdzad 'dug cing / lo rgyus 'di la mkhas rmongs
kun gyis shes par / rtse gdong pa'i gdung brgyud rnams bon dang mu stegs sogs kyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i rgyu 'bras mi shes pa'i nges pa yod na/ rgyal po mkhyen rgya can rnams
la'ang tshig zur tsam gyi dgongs par 'char bde min yong ba thugs dag kyang / de 'dra yin min ni bod tsam du ma zad rgya sog kun la rlung ltar grags shing/ ris med bstan
'dzin thams cad kyang 'khon gyi gdung brgyud zhes tshad mar rjes 'dzin mdzad pa thugs rgyus yod bzhin du/ rtse gdong pa'i mi 'khyams gal te rgyal po rang gi'ang zhabs
gras su chud nas thugs blos bkal na nam zhig nas phyi nang gi la rgya tshang ma dkrug shing byed pa de dag kha 'chal la rgyal ba'i bka' ltar tshad mar mdzad de de ma thag
kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i dbang po yab sras sogs bstan 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi dbu 'phangs dmod pa dang / gong ma bdag po chen po sogs rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin

po che gces par skyong ba'i chos kyi rgyal po rnams kyi bka' khrims la rkang 'og gi rdul tsam du'ang mi brtsi bar rtse gdong na sku gsum dang dkon mchog gsum gyi rten ji snyed
bzhugs pa rnams dang / srog chags nyes med dge ba'i ngang tshul can rnams skad cig nyid la thal ba'i rdul du rlog pa la ches shin tu dpa' ba'i dpung 'jug mdzad tshul
'og nas 'byung ba 'di rnams la dpags na/ rgyas sras bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal btsun mo chos skyid bcas sku gegs chen pos bcings pa'am/ yang na zhing bcu tshang ba'i bstan pa'i
dgra bo de bdag cag kho na'o zhes zhal gyi bzhes par nges te/ rgyud sde rin po che rnams nas gsungs pa'i las sbyor de bzhin zhing bcu tshang ba'i skye bo rnams thar pa'i
lam du 'god pa'i ched du gsung gi de las gzhan du na byed pa po rang gi srog gi gshed mar 'gyur ba'i phyir gnas skabs 'dir ni rtse gdong tsam du'ang ma zad gzhan gyi
gtor ma 'phangs pa'am/ sbyin sreg dang mnan pa sogs bstan 'gror gnod pa'i dgra bgegs gdug pa can rnams 'dul thabs byas de yang rgyal sras bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal dang btsun
mo chos skyid la byas so zhes mkhar ba dang slong phor 'dzin pa'i skye bo rku rgyag don gnyer rnams kyis zhus na/ de la'ang dpung 'jug mdzad pa the tshom med pa ni

gzur gnas kun gyis mkhyen nus pas/ des na rtse gdong par dpung 'jug mdzad pa'i rgyal khag 'dis ni rang sde la'ang thugs bskyed smon lam ji 'dra mdzad rtogs nus so/ /gang ltar
bdag chen yab sras gnyis nas gong sa rdo rje 'chang tshangs dbyangs rgya mtshor zhu gnang gi 'gyangs min gtsang du rgyal ba rin po che chibs bsgyur dus dam nyams rnams
'dzin bzung gi rtse gdong dang shangs rnam gling sogs su khri mun du bcug thog mtshungs med tshe'i dus byas/ rgyan drung ngag dbang non bur gong sa rin po che'i thugs rtsis
kyi pho brang chen po po ta lar phebs gnang ba bzhin/ 'phral phebs skabs yab rje zur bzhugs mdzad mu dang / bla brang du bdag mo bya sgo ba tshe ring bu khrid/ phyag
mdzod kun don/ phyag mdzod ma nA bcas la bla brang snang srid dang po ta la rnams la nyams gso'i bka' khyab dang yul lha'i rten mkhar zab bzor rab gnas skabs ma 'ong lung
ston lta bur baN zhA ser po bzhes te mdzad nas chibs kha bsgyur/gong gi zug pa rnams mthar phyin nyer rtse gdong du bang phyin ched rdzong gi sog dmag thon tshul dang 'on
seng skor zhib mthus mdzad kyang / las dbang bzlog med lta bu'i dmag ba so thang du 'byor phral paN chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po blo bzang

ye shes kyi dgongs zab rin po che'i ma bzod par dpung 'jug mi byed pa'i bka' khyab mthar phyin bka' drin che yang rtsi med kyi mtshan 'jug byed rtsis byas rung rgyu 'bras bslu
med kyi bden pas rtse gdong mdor mun 'khor te mtshan 'gebs ma thub pas yab rje bsod nams dbang rgyal nyid sku chas 'ga' zhig dang bcas mtshan 'gribs kyi bkra shis lhun
po'i ba so spyi khang du phebs/ bdag mos rta mgrin brag khung du zhag gcig bzhugs/ de nas gsang stabs kyis yab gzhis su 'byor/ phyag mdzod kun don gyis 'khur blang ste
bsdad pas shing bya dbyug zla'i tshes bcu dgu'i tho rengs dmag dpon thA ja'i dpung gis bla brang / ja go can gyis 'phel rgyas/ e ke dbon po'i dpung rnams kyis chos sde rtsis
blang / phyag mdzod kun don gyisgyi mgo btags stas te dag sbyangs kyi rtse gdong rang 'jags yong bar byas kyang de skabs rang srog skyob thub tsam las gzhan phan ma thogs/sog
dmag dang nye 'khor yul grus bod dmag rtse gdong rang gi g.yog ngan bdud kyi rlams pa rnams kyis gdan sa phyi nang tshang ma nyams chags su btang zhing / phyag mdzod
kun don bsad/ chos sde gtor/ zhag bdun nas dmag log cing / ba so spyi khang du bdag chen la thugs sun zhus tshe der bzhugs dge

'dun rnams kyis khra bzung yang dag mdzad pas sku srog la skyon ma byung / des na bkra shis lhun po'i ba so spyi khang 'di shin tu drin che/ sku chas rnams 'thor zegs su gyur
pa las dpag bsam 'khri shing gi zhal thang dre'u'i rgyab gcig dang / sil snyan 'dzam gling kun grags/ chos kyi rgyal po blo chen 'phags pa rin po che'i bzhugs khri ye
bha'u/ skya bo pa'i phyag mtshan tshang ma yu ba rnams shel las grub pa/ rgya nag gser tham rin po che/ 'phags pa rin po che'i dbu zhA nyi lde mar grags pa mkha' 'gro ma
bye ba'i dbu skra las grub par grags pa dang / phyag dril bcas rgyal mtshan thon por phul skad 'dug pas srang dbar gyi sa rdo'i gras la bzhugs ma dgos pa 'di yang rgyu 'bras
kyi gden par go /de ltar dmag mi rnams kyis mtshams med kyi las tshad med bsags pas dpon mo chos skyid bzang ngan gang yin rtogs nus shing / rtse gdong pa'i dam nyams
rnams kyi zer dbang la nyan pas byang brgyud rgyal por su las su snod mkhas rmongs kun gyi dgongs 'gro zhing / tshe rabs kun gyi bde skyid 'grub 'dug pas thugs spro bar
mdzod cig dpon mo'i tugs bskyed kyi thams cad la mi 'dod pa ji ltar byung tshul ni/ dmag gras

gzungs 'dus zer bas dung chen rdzong dga'/ sil snyan 'chi med sgra dbyangs/ gnas brten thang sku si thang mar grags pa dang bla bre sogs dang / rol mo pu tra snyan sgrog bcas
khyer te nag chu'i dgon pa zhig tu 'byor 'jags thog nyin mo mis 'bud dkrol byas tshe sgra skad mi 'byin zhing / mtshan mo don med du skad 'byin pa sogs mi shis pa'i ltas
ngan sna tshogs byung bar rten slar rtse gdong rang du phyir 'bul byung ba da lta'i bar du 'dug cing / yang sog po zhig gis rin chen sgang gi tshogs dung dang mgon khang
gi snyan dar drag bsdus khyer bar lam du dung gi rkyen med par sgra 'byin pa dang / de phral sna khrag 'dzags pas snyan dar rnams kyis phyis shing mthar sna khrag rgyun
ring 'byams pa'i rkyen byas te tshe'i dus byas rjes snyan dar rnams khrag dang bcas rin chen sgang mgon khang gi mgon sku byin can stag tshang lo tsA ba'i thugs dam mar
da lta'ang na gzar sgron yod cing / de skabs phyag rdzas la 'bags skyon che chung gi khyad las la lar mi brgyud rtsad nas chod cing shul med du song ba dang 'ga' zhig nas
bshags sdom gyi gzung gso gtor bzos 'bul ba sogs dang / dgon par mang ja lo ltar zhu dgos kyi rgyun 'dug cing / er khe dbon po'i bu zhig chos sder btsun pa byas pa'ang
bdud

'dul mgon khang ngam gsang ba'i mgon khang gi 'gag nas tshogs khang gi gsang g.yab la lhung skabs mthong snang du mi nag shin tu che ba zhig gis skyur tshul/ lha lung las dam
can pu tra'i 'tshubs yin pa dang / gzhan yang sog pa'i rigs rnams thog kha nas lhungs shing las mgon pu tra ming sring rnams khog zhugs kyi smyo 'bog sems 'khrugs ltas
ngan sna tshogs byung 'dug pa dang / sog po rgod ma zer ba zhig gis gtsang bdag mo'i nang rten dngul gdung rin po che'i phra rgyan 'ga' zhig 'khyer ba/ lam bar du smyo zhing
ngag nas cal col sna tshogs dang / rtse gdong pa'i lug nag des brdung gi 'dug pas de phyir 'thon zer ba sogs chos skyong rnams kyi 'tshubs 'gyur che ba dang / dpon mo
nas rtse gdong btsan 'phrog byas rjes mi shis pa'i stas ngan sna tshogs byung bar brten/ bshags par da lta dga' ldan lha khang na bzhugs pa'i rgyal gsung bka' 'gyur rin
po che tshar gcig dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i byams mgon gyi sku brnyan/ bla brang mgon khang na bzhugs pa'i gur mgon gyi 'jim sku chung ngu bcas bzhengs/'gyangs min
'jun dkar dpung gis rgyal po lha bzang dkrongs te/ dpon mo chos skyid rang yang bar khrid do/ /

yab rje ba so spyi khang nas slar zha lur phebs te gnas brten rnams mjal/ de nas sa skyar phebs pa'i phur sgrub skabs sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis dang zhal dgyes gnang
zhing zhabs tog gi bzhugs 'jags gnang dgos lugs mdzad kyang ma bzhugs par rim bzhin phebs/ sku khang rnying gras su gyur pa rta nag sding kha bya bzang du zla ba lhag tsam
bzhugs/ de nas slar paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpon khag rnams la yab rje nyid rtse gdong du bzhugs mthus gnang don bzhin la rin sgang du lcags pho stag lor phebs
gsol phogs bzhes te sa lo'i gzim khang du bzhugs/ sku chas 'gangs che gras rol mi 'brug sgra gzil gnon/ dbyangs can bzhad sgra/ khrus bum dngul 'gril ma cha dang bcas phyi
'khyar med par chos sder sbyor 'jags mdzad/zla ba drug tsam song rjes chab chu'i sku brten pa'i tshul bzhes te mthar lcags stag zla ba dang pa'i tshes bcu bdun nyin ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas me tog gi char chen po dang bcas dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan zhing / spur zhu sogs kyang der byas te spur tshwa 'debs pa dang dgongs
rdzogs su chos sde'i grwa bgres rnams kyis lcang hrag gi sa 'bum che ba de bzhengs

shing/ dus chen rnams la'ang 'ja' gur dang me tog gi char 'babs pa sogs yun ring po'i bar du byung / de nyid kyi zur sras bkra shis lhun por bzhugs par sog pos 'o brgyal zhus
pa las skyobs phyir paN chen thams chad mkhyen par zhu rten 'phags pa rin po che'i phyag ting sems nyid ngal sor grags pa phul zhing mthar rta nag gro khud 'bum par gshegs
so/ /de nas nor bu rgyal mtshan po ta lar bzhugs skabs 'gro ba'i las dbang gi mchod yon nyi zla zung gcig gi chos srid la 'pho 'gyur gyi rgyal dbang tshangs dbyangs
rgya mtsho dang / de mo gong ma rin po che zhabs drung nyid dang bcas la rgyal po lha bzang nas dpung 'jug gis tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho dang de mo gong ma rin po che bcas
rgyar phebs dgos byung zhing / zhabs drung nyid rgyud smad pa'i chos grwar yib nas bzhugs pas/ grwa pa zhig gis khyed gang nas yin/ nga'i shag tu phebs zhes yang yang
zer bar brten de'i shag tu phebs te zhag shas bzhugs/ de nas zhabs phyir gsol dpon sangs rgyas/ bstan 'dzin kun bzang / gzim dpon rdor don/ ma chen 'dzam gling / nor bu rin
chen dang bcas dpon g.yog rnams kyis rgyal zhabs tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho dang / de mo gong ma'i phebs rjes e non dgongs

pa'i smad khams phyogs la phebs te thog mar sde dger phebs bzhugs 'jags gnang dgos lugs zhus kyang zhabs drung nyid ma bzhugs par chibs bsgyur gnang / mtsho kun dga' nor bu
phebs dus rje tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho gshegs/ de mo gong ma rgyar phebs pa'i phebs rjes kyang ma non/tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho gshegs pa'i mtsho 'gram der zhabs drung
nyid kyis lcang ma zhig 'dzugs par mdzad pas shin tu legs par skyes 'dug pa rgyal mchog gong sa rin po che'i mchog sprul thams cad mkhyen pa myur phebs kyi rten 'brel khyad
par can 'grig pa dang / mtsho kha'i rgyal po am zlum zhes pas sbyin bdag mdzad bzhugs mus rgyal po nyid nas zhabs drung rang gi gdan sa tshang ma phyir 'bul dgos lugs
kyi phyag dam rten gri ba so'i yu can dang / gsol zhal bcas lha bzang khang la rdzong bda' mdzad pa/ zhag bco brgyad nas lha sa 'khor ba'i lan du sngar khung gang yin rtsis
