bzhes la phebs zer ba yod 'dug na'ang zhabs drung nas ma phebs pa dang de mur sku 'brum bzhes shing rgyun ring tsam bsnyung rjes/ gong sa rin po che'i sku skye li thang
du 'khrungs pa'i grags snyan mtsho mkhar gsan ma thag rgyal ba'i yang srid gzhan dbang du shor dogs smad khams rgyal khag chen po tshang

ma dang / lhag par sde dge sogs la grags snyan bsgrags pa de bzhin gyi dbus gtsang khyab par brten/ mchog sprul rin po che sde dger bzhugs thog lha bzang khang nas ngos 'dzin
dmag 'jug zung 'brel btang bar/ rgyal po am zlum nyid nas rgyal ba'i yang srid rin po cher lha bzang khang nas ngos 'dzin dmag 'jug yod 'dug pas mtsho khar gdan 'dren
zhus tshe ji bzhin gegs med du zhu nus yin zhabs drung nyid la zhus pas/ lan du/ 'gyur med blo yi bdag po gser gyi khri la bzhugs nas/ /las su bya ba thams cad rig pa'i blon
pos byas yong / /sa gcig sa la 'khor ba'i rlung gi gshog pa min te/ /pho shes rig pa'i gshog pas ga nas bskor bskor yin 'dug /dbyar chu rgyas pa'i dkyil nas nya ltar
mchongs nas yong yod/ /dgun chu rgyas kyang rgyas shog gser gyi zam pa btsugs chog /rin chen gling yang mjal myong rgya mtsho'i rgyus yang yod la/ /chu srin gdug pa'i lus
po dung dkar ngar mas phug song / /'dod 'jo ba yi 'o mas dung dkar gso mkhan yod na/ /nor bu len pa'i khas len nga ras byas pa'i mchog lags/ /zhes 'gur du gsungs sheng /
phan tshun khams sog rgyal khag rnams la 'di skor lhings cha dgos pa'i bka' 'doms mdzad de/ rgyal ba

rin po che sde dge nas mtsho mkhar spyan drangs so/ /rtsed gdong tshang ma dpon mo chos skyid nas bdag pa'i dgon pa dge lugs su bsgyur/ chos gzhis thog nas sngags chod gang
yin bstan 'dzin dbang gi dge 'thebs su phul ba dang / gzhan yang shangs khong lam tshar bcas bla brang gzhung chod dang / rtsed dang rtse gdong bde gleng pa/ phu nub dud
chung gcig bcas gru tshang la chod/ 'phan yul nA lendra dang bde ba can bcas phyi 'khyar du song zhing / phogs ja tshugs sogs dge dgon dpe 'dra'i mur/ dpon mo chos skyid
dang rdor rgyan gnyis kyis lo bco lnga tsam 'dzin bdag byas skabs rdor rgyan gyi dge rgan dge slong zhig yod 'dug pa des lhun rtse rten gras nas 'gangs che ba rnams dbye
ba'i dre'u'i rgyab gsum tsam khyer skad dang /gzhan yang me bya 'jun dkar thon skabs rtse gdong pa rnams nas lhun rtse dngul sku chen mor grags pa slob dpon padma'i sku
brnyan de bshig cing / de tshab tse dpag med kyi sku da lta rten gras su bzhugs pa dang / gu ru mtshan brgyad kyi sku brnyan gras nas shAkya seng ge ma gtogs gzhan tshang
ma spang phu mtshor bskyur zhing/ shAkya seng ge'i sku da lta lhun rtser bzhugs/ gzhan yang

sku gsung thugs rten phon che ba gong gi mtshor skyur 'dug pa sogs gyar tshab shin tu che ba dang / de rjes 'jun dkar gyi dpung phyir log pa'i zhor du chos skyid ltos bcas
rnams kyang khrid/ zhabs drung nyid nas rgya mtsho sde gzhi mjal bar phebs/ rje tsong kha pa chen po'i sku 'bum rgya phibs sogs tshang ma'i nyams gso zhabs tog gnang bar/
sku 'bum dge 'dun mang pos zhabs drung nyid rje rin po cher mngon sum du mthong ba dang / rje rang gi sprul pa zhig gis nyams gso byed pa'i lung bstan yod gsung ba sogs
dang / de skabs thugs dam bskang gso'i gtor ma dpal mgon zhal nyid bram ze'i rnam pas dngos su len pa dang / lha srin sde brgyad rnams kyang nyid kyi bka' las cung zad kyang
me 'da' ba sogs grub pa'i mtshan ma mang du brnyes pa dang / gzhan yang byams pa'i sku brnyan chen po zhig gi rgyab yol dreg pa can 'khrud par mdzad pas rgyab yol 'od
shin tu che ba dang bcas mtsho nang du shor bar/ der yod tshang mas thabs gang gi'ang byas kyang 'don ma nus par/ zhabs drung nyid kyis klu la bka' shog sho lo ka gcig mdzad
de rdo dang lhan cig mtshor bskyur bas rgyab yol de phral 'thon pa sogs grub pa'i mtshan ma kun gyi mngon du gyur/ sku 'bum nyams gsor gser

btul ma srang dgu brgya bdun cu don gnyis zho lnga song / tshe dpag med/ 'jam dbyangs/ sa paN/ sgrol dkar/ rje rin po che/ bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad sogs kyi par gsar bzhengs
'debs gnang la gser gsol dang gzungs 'bul rab gnas sogs tshang ma phyag len rgyas par mdzad de sku 'bum grwa tshang rnams la phyag mchod 'bul ba'i rten du gnang ba
sogs bstan pa'i nyams gso mthar phyin thog rgyal po am zlum nas kyang rgyal gsung bka' 'gyur rin po che'i mtshon legs 'bul rgya cher mdzad pa dang / zhabs drung nyid kyi
rab byung kyang tsha khang no mo khang la bzhes shing mtshan gsol dus ngag dbang blo bzang don yod rgya mtshor gnang / bsnyen rdzogs de skabs chu bzang rin po che las bzhes
shing gong gi bka' 'gyur kyang phul/de nas gong ma bdag po chen pa'i dbu bla khal kha rje btsun dam pas gong ma chen por rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud phyogs mthar
'khyar ba de lam du lus tshe bod khams tshang ma'i bde skyid la shin tu gnod tshabs che bas gdan sa 'dzin par phebs dgos gsung pa bzhin/ gong ma'i lung gi gong sa rin
po che bod la chibs bsgyur dang chabs cig 'byon par gsungs yang bka' 'gyangs zhu bar mdzad de/ slar zla gsum tsam nas yar

phebs kyang jag pas sku chas rnams khyer/ lcags khyi rgyal zla'i nyir lnga la lha sar phebs nas lha sa dpal grong shag tu bzhugs thog yab rje rdo rje 'chang dbus phebs dang
'grig kyang lha sar mjal 'dzoms ma byung zhing / gong dkar chos sder phebs thog bang mi ched rdzong gi zhu shog dang chabs cig gzhung sa mchog nas gsol chas zhu rgyu'i bka'
'dzin mang po dang bcas gnang bar zhabs drung nyid nas rtse gdong phyi nang bar gsum gyi 'dzin khres tshang ma gdan sa gong nas rtsis bzhes 'phral la gnang dgos pa yod
do gsungs shing / zhabs phyi rnams la gsung sgros su nga ban rgan la pha gzhis kyi dgos pa med pas gdan sa gong rang du 'bul 'byor thub pa zhig cis kyang bya rgyu yin gsungs
pa ltar/ rtsis sprod sku tshab don grub lbang / mtsho kha'i rgyal po blo bzang bstan 'dzin/ gong ma'i sku tshab bcas nas zhabs drung nyid la rtsis bzhes la phebs dgos
zhu mur/ sa skya nas zom lus skabs zhabs drung glo bur du ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas lcags glang dbo zla nyis brtsegs kyi phyi ma'i tshes bdun la gzugs sku chos
dbyings su thim zhing / spur zhu sogs gzhung sa mchog nas thugs khur che bzhes kyi rgyud grwa rin po che nas ser phreng dang bcas ral mkhar spur mchod mdzad cing / gzhung
sa mchog nas

dbus gtsang dgon khag tshang mar mang ja 'gyed sogs rgya che ba dang spur thal tshang ma sa skyar 'byor bar rdo rje 'chang gi sku bzhengs te da lta 'jag khang na bzhugs/rtse
gdong bdag chen na rim gyi phyag dam 'gro mgon phyag nar se chen rgyal pos phul ba'i dngul dam de gzim dpon rdor don gyis bka' shag nas phyag dam zhus te sa skyar bskur/
dA chings ba dur gyi dpon mdzad skabs rtse gdong 'di yin med par gzhung sog gi lo phyed gsum/ gzhung 'dzin lo bzhi lhag tsam/ 'gag pa stobs ldan gyi lo drug mgroon gnyer
rdza nyag gi lo gnyis tsam zin no/ /zhabs drung gshegs nas gang yin med par lus skabs gzim dpon rdor don gyis sprul sku ma phebs bar sa skya nas zhal 'dzin dang / de nas
sprul sku'i sa skyar thugs gnyer grub bstun sprul skur 'jags pa zhig rgyal yab la mgo 'dren zhus te de phral gong ma bdag po chen por zhu shog phul yang gnas skabs 'ga'
zhig gi ma 'grig de nas chu stag zhabs drung gi sprul sku 'phan yul du 'khrul med phebs pas sku zhang tshe sgrub bla mas rgyal ba rin po cher rgyu mtshan zhus pa'i rtse
gdong phyag 'byor yong khar rtse gdong mkhan po blo bzang stobs ldan gyi rgyab nga phod blo bzang

sogs kyis byas te sku zhang sog po'i bla mar brdzangs pas phyag 'byor ma byung / de dang dus mtshungs rtse gdong lha mi tshang mas kyang mkhan por sprul sku gdan 'dren gyi
mgo 'don zhus pas mkhan po'i thugs la ma song bar sde mkhan kha mchur thug rgyal yab kyis bcad mtshams mdzad/ re zhig mkhan gras bzung slar sprul skur 'bul rgyu mdzad mur
dbus gtsang sde gzar gyi dbang gis ma 'grig par lus/ sde gzar 'jags nas tshe sgrub bla mar gong ma'i sras bcu bdun pa'i bdag rgyab byung bas rtse gdong skor sprul skur rang
'jags zhus/ mkhan po stobs ldan kyang sems ma zin pas dgongs phog gi 'phos/ sa skyong mi dbang de nyid la sras bcu bdun pas bka' khyab thog phyag tu 'byor bas rnying
dus ltar nyams gso ci 'grub dang/ khyad par rnam rtse'i jo bor nyams gso rab gnas dus thugs kar 'ja' dkar zug cing / mdong chod nas rdzong ri jo bo rang gnas su spyan drangs/
shing stag sa skyar byon yab rje rdo rje 'chang dang gtsug lag khang rnams mjal zhu mdzad/ de nas sa lugs kyi bla ma du ma las chos gsan cing thugs rab che bas mkhas
grub chen por gyur/ rtse gdong sogs su gsung ngag rdor 'phreng bka' 'gyur gyi lung sogs chos 'khor bskor zhing 'chad rtsod gsum la thogs pa

mi mnga'/ gser mdog can gyi gdan sa lo du ma mdzad skabs nA lendrar bco brgyad sku mched sogs don gnyer du mar gsung ngag slob bshad kyi chos 'khor bskor ba mdzad pa'i tshe
me khyi dbo zla'i nyer lngar glo bur du gshegs shing / zhabs rjes rnams gcung sku mched zhabs phyi bcas nas mthar phyin pa mdzad nas/ slar yang sprul sku 'khrul med mkhas
grub kyi gdan sa zin pa zhig re ba mdzad mu yin no/ /gang ltar de nyid kyis rtse gdong zhal 'dzin mdzad mur nged rang lo bco lnga'i thog dbus la phyin dus rtse gdong sa
skyar gnang 'dod bzhin gzhung sa mchog nas stsal ba'i bcu drug nas bzung yab mes gong ma'i gdan sa rang 'jags byung ba bzhin rtsis blangs ste/ me stag lo ngos bskyod kyi
gnas rang nyams gso'i tshul du kye rdor zhi ba'i sbyin sreg du ma dang / rab gnas rgyas pa thug gso rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog gtsug lag khang dang mgon khang rnams la mchod
'bul bkang gso/ de skabs thar rtse rdo rje 'chang phebs pa dang 'grigs pas rje de nyid dang spul sku rin po che'i gtso mdzad rtse gdong chos sde dang phyogs 'dus kha shas
la yang phur kyai gsang sogs dbang bka'/ sgrol dkar sogs rjes gnang / chos spyod bskang ba'i lung sogs chos bka' du ma tho

zur bzhin spel zhing mi sder phyag dbang khrom dbang sogs bgyis par tshang ma gus spro yod tshul byed cing / de nas bzung grwa tshang nas dpal sa skyar sgrub dkyil bskang ba
gtor bzlog rnams sbyangs/lcags lug lo ngos bskyod kyi phur sgrub 'dzugs pa dang chabs cig mgon khang gi gtso bo g.yag rwa lnga mgon sku byin can kha shas dang bcas pa mgo
khang gsar par spyan drangs pa sogs bstan pa'i me ro rmangs nas gsos te yar lam ngor du 'byor skabs rgya sbug gur mgon lha dga' bdud 'dul 'brug sgrar grags pa 'di dngul
srang bcu bdun gyi rtsol med lag 'byor byung ba sogs slad kyi dge mtshan dang bcas deng sang gi bar du dar zhing rgyas pa 'di lags/ de rnams kyi lha rigs 'khon dang sa
skya pa ste mtshan mchog gsum dang ldan pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul las/ gdan sa che po'i bla brang so sor dbang bsgyur ba'i gdung rabs kyi nang nas/ phyis byon rtse gdong
bla brang pa'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul legs par bstan zin to/ /'dir smras pa/ phun tshogs tshogs gnyis mthar phyin yon tan rtse/ /spangs rtogs rtogs pa'i dbang
phyug go 'phang rtse/ /'gro 'dren 'dren pa dam pa skyabs kyi rtse/ /srid na srid pa

mchog gyur gdung rabs rtse/ /mkhas grub gdong lnga'i dbang po rim byon rnams/ /rgyal bstan gdong lnga'i sgra dbyangs cher sgrog cing / /mthu stobs gdong lnga'i mche sder rab
grub pas/ /phyogs las rnam rgyal rtse gdong pa zhes grags/ /khyad par mi dbang nam mkha' bkra shis kyis/ /gtsug lag sku gsung thugs rten bshad sgrub sde/ /gsar du bskrun
zhing mkhas dbang sa lo tsA/ /grub dbang bsam grub zhabs dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ /kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub skye dgu'i mgon/ /mtshan doon mthun pa bsod nams bstan 'dzin
dbang/ /mkhyen brtse nus ldan nor bu rgyal mtshan sogs/ /bstan 'dzin rim byon rnam thar bsam bzhin dad/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o/ /de dag gis rtse gdong bla
brang pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul gyi kha skong ma tshang bar med par bstan zin/dpal ldan sa skya 'di nyid du gdung rabs rgyun mi chad par byon pa'i tshul bshad pa/da ni
dpal ldan sa skya 'di nyid du gdung rabs rgyun ma chad

par byon zhing 'byon par 'gyur ba'i tshul gsung ba la/ mdor bstan rgyas bshad mdzad pa der/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen kyi btsun mo gdong dga' ma sku mched la 'jam dbyangs
sku mched 'khrungs pa nas bzung / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs nyid kyi bar gsung rtsom mdzad grub pa las/ 'jam dbyangs sku mched la rnam thar bsdus pa las ma gsungs pas/ des
na 'dir sgar chen rin po che nas bzung kho bo cag rigs kyi myu gu'i bar du 'phel ba'i rnam thar dang lo rgyus rnams kha skong du bris te/ slar yang srid pa ji sriid bar
rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che 'byon par 'gyur ba'i rten 'brel du ma 'ongs pa'i kha skong rnams kyang de dang de dus su so so'i gsung rtsom gnang bde bar
'dri ba la/ tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/dang po ni/ nged rang gis brtsams pa'i sa skya skor dpon par nye bar mkho ba'i
yi ge 'gro don bzang po las/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis btsun mo bzhes tshul gyi mur/ btsun mo gnyis pa slar yang gdong dga' ma/ /bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid
zhes bya'i sras/ /'dzam gling rgyan mchog grags pa'i

mtshan can 'khrungs/ /gang de'i btsun mo byang phyogs rgyal po'i lcam/ /lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo zhes bya'i sras/ /'jam dbyangs sprul pa mthu stobs dbang phyug dang/ /rgyal
sras ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal mtshan/ /thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam mgon a mes zhabs/ /mkhyen yang kun dga'i mtshan can bstan 'groo'i dpal/ /dpa' ldan de yi btsun
mo 'gro mgon ma/ /o rgyan skyabs la bsod nams dbang phyug bltams/ /gang de'i btsun mo ma gcig zhed chos ma/ /pad dkar bu khrid sras ni mangga'i mtshan/ /de yi btsun mo sngon
ma gnas gdong mar/ /gdung brgyud ma byon phyi ma bco brgyad pa'i/ /ma gcig bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo la/ /kho bo'i skyabs gcig khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon/ /ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen zhes/ /snyigs dus mgon de skye ba'i cho 'phrul bstan/ /mgon de'i btsun mo snga ma zhed chos pa'i/ /lha mdzes bu khrid sras gnyis chung ngur
gshegs/ /phyi ma sku drin can gyi 'gro mgon ma/ /ma gcig bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo la/ /yon tan kun bral kun dga' blo gros dang/ /nu bo mched bcas byung ba'i mched
gnyis gshegs/ /kho bos bstan 'gro spyi dang khyad par du/ /sa skya'i rje btsun

bstan pa rin po cher/ /lhag bsam rab dkar gdung rabs bzung ba las/ /da lta'i gdung brgyud sku mched rnam gnyis byon/ /de nas rgyal dang rgyal sras thugs rje dang / /gdul bya'i
bsod nams dad gus 'dzoms pa las/ /deng nas bzung ste 'khor ba ji srid bar/ /'chi med 'khon rigs rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /gdung rabs gangga'i rdul snyed byon gyur nas/
/sku tshe mdzad phrin bzhed dgongs mthar phyin pa'i/ /bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon rim par 'byon gyur cig//ces so/ /mthu stobs dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/gnyis
pa dee'i don rgyas par bshad pa la/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa ni gang
gi dpal gyi mgul nas byon pa'i lam glu ngo mtshar phun tshogs ma las bsdus te kha skong cung zad dang bcas 'dri ba la/ de yang sngon byung skyes rabs kyi phreng ba che
ba dang / sku tshe 'di nyid kyi rnam par thar pa mdor bsdus te bstan pa'o/ /

dang po ni/ 'jig rten na mchog gi sprul pa'i sku gcig gis mdzad pa bcu gnyis bstan pa'i tshe/ ston pa nyid 'khor dang sdud po'i tshul snang ba sogs lung khungs bcas rgya cher
spro ru mchis kyang spros pa bskyungs te dgos don snying por dril ba/ nye sras byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po nyan thos kyi tshul bzung ba 'phags pa kun dga' bo
nas bzung ste sngags 'chang chen po'i bar ni de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal zhing / rje 'di nyid kyi lam glu las kyang / tsha ba'i rong du bai ro tsa nar grags/ /rtsod pa'i
dus su sngags 'chang dag dbang mtshan/ /zhes dang / gzims spyil dkar por grags pa rgyal mtshan skabs/ /phug chen bzhi sogs ri brag sgrub gnas bcas/ /zhes dang / yab chos
kyi rgyal po sngags 'chang rje/ /bo dhi sa twa'i rnam 'phrul grags pa'i mtshan/ /mnal lam nyams snang dag tu 'di ltar gzigs/ /sngags 'chang chen pa'i sku gdung zhabs drung
nas/ /'od zer kha dog lnga ldan phril le ba/ /'phros nas yum chen bsod nams rgyal mo yi/ /sku lus nyid la thim pa'i rtags mtshan gzigs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar sngags 'chang
chen po de nyid bstan 'gro spyi dang bye brag gi phan bde spel ba'i ched du slar yang rigs sras grags pa blo gros nyid kyi sras su bsam bzhin

'khrungs pa ni 'phags yul grub dbang rnams kyis brtul zhugs spyod pa'i ya gyal du gyur pa'i grub pa'i khyu mchog rje btsun mthu stobs dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po 'di nyid yin par yang yang zhal gyis bzhes pa'o/ /gnyis pa sku tshe 'di nyid kyi rnam thar mdor bsdus te bstan pa ni/ yab rje dgung lo nyer drug tu son pa sa pho
byi ba'i lo rgyal yum lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo la zag med kyi bde ba rgyas shing nyams snang spro bzhin pa'i ngang nas ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas 'khrungs shing
/ sku'i gegs sel dang 'khrungs ston gyi tshul du 'dus sde rnams su mang skol sogs legs par bsgrubs/ /dgung lo lnga par yig klog bslab tshulazhus par tshags med dang / sgrol
ma'i mtshan brgya ma bslab par zhal 'don gnang / dgung lo brgyad par yab chos phur pa'i 'cham rol phyag len sogs phul bas bde blag tu mkhyen/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa la 'jam
mgon rim byon gyi chos khri skye dgu'i 'dud gnas chen por mnga' gsol/ phyogs kyi mkhas btsun che gnyen dam pa phal bcas nas khri ston mnga' dbul thog theg chen lam gyi
gzhung shing thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal bar byed pa'i tshogs chos nyin gsum gnang / mgo zla nyi ma thung tshad yin kyang / kun la dbyar nyi

ring ba tsam gyi mthun snang byung bas/ nyi ma bzung bar grags pa dang / phyogs kun tu 'ja' tshon 'khrigs shing / nyi zla skar gsum lhan 'dzom mthong ba sogs lha mi'i yid 'phrog
pa'i dpal du gyur pas snyan grags 'gro don phyogs mthar rgyas pa'i mgo 'di nas tshugs/dgung lo bcu bzhi pa lcags glang lor bde mchog pho brang du phur pa'i bsnyen pa
tshad smin gnang skabs gcung 'jam mgon sku mched la rtseg ge'i bsnyung gzhi byung ba rje 'di nyid kyis gsan na bar chad byung dogs gsang rgya byas skabs/ gtso gtor dang
dkar mo nyi zla'i mar rgyan nyi zla gnyis phyed gas pa byung tshe zhal ngo rnams la bsnyun gzhi 'dra med dam zhes yang yang gsungs kyang 'phros 'bul mkhan ma byung tshe/
tho rengs zhig gi mnal lam du mtsho dkar dngas zhig gi nang nas lha mo dkar mo dar dkar gyi 'jol ber dang nyi zla'i rgyan byas pa zhig thon nas dngos grub gling du bskang
gso brgya rtsa thong zhes lung bstan nas yal song bar yum chen mdun du de bzhin bka' tho stsal bas gcung gnyis kyi bsnyun gzhi yang 'phral dngas byung / mar rgyan yang
rim gyis sos pa kun gyis gsal/ gzhan yang skabs der sngon sngags 'chang chen po'i sku dus spa gro stag tshang du bla ma dang yi dam

dkyil 'khor mngon sum gzigs pa sogs sngon gnas sgrib med thugs dran gsos pa sogs rtags mtshan phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas mthar phyin/ de lo phur bsgrubs kyi tshogs dbur phebs
te slob ma rjes 'dzin sogs gnang / 'di skor snga phyi lo ngo lnga tsam la gdan sa'i khur bzhes te sgrub mchod rigs kyi dbu bzhugs dang / dbyar chos dgun chos sogs gnang
bas yab yum khu dbon tshang ma dgyes tshor yong bar mdzad/bcu dgu pa la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po phu ri nas spyan drangs te sku mched gsum gtsor gyur pa'idage
'dun 'dus tshogs bcas pas bka' chos tshan che bar gsan/ slar yang dgung grangs nyer gcig pa la 'jam dbyangs de nyid kyi drung nas yab sras bzhi gas gsung ngag rin po che
cha lag dang bcas pa dang gzhan yang rje btsun gong ma lngasagatsos pa'i rgya bod bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar sogs chos bka' rgya cher gsan nas snyan brgyud bstan pa'i bdag
po mdzad/ de lo byas 'gyur du gzhi bsnyen rgyas par gnang skabs tho rengs kyi cha zhig rje btsun rdo rje bdag med mas phyis 'byung lung bstan gyi brda' dang / 'gro don
'phrin las rgyas pa'i smon lam bcas stsal/dgung lo nyer gnyis pa la yi dam gur drag gi bsnyen pa

tshad min gnang zin pa dang / rgyas sde la phebasate mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi drung du rab tu byung / yab rje'i sku zhang gdong dga' sde pas gdan drangs te mgon
po drug cu pa'i gtor rdzongs shig gnang ba'i pu tra'i bskul chen tshugs nas phyogs kyi mjal mi dang dad 'dus kyi khrom tshogs che ba kun gyi mthong snang la nam mkha' nas
gtso chen rgyu ba sogs drag sbyor gyis rtags mtshan mthun grub tu byung / spyi sger la tshe dbang sogs 'dod chos 'ga' zhig gnang tshe 'ja' gur dang me tog gi char lta
bas chog me shes pa byung /de nas dgung lo nyer gsum pa la sa dkar dang / 'dam thog dgon mchod gzhis logs sa skya'i chos srid rin po che'i rgyun la dgongs te mdo khams su
'byon bzhed la/ 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar bas mtshon pa'i lha dang srung ma'i rten mchog rnams nas kyang de ltar legs pa'i brda' rtags rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa thob
par brten nas gdan sa nas chibs bsgyur gnang nyin 'ja' 'od 'khrigs pa sogs srung mas skyel ba'i rnam pa dang bcas phebs te bsam 'grub rtse'i pho brang du 'jam dbyangs bsod
nams dbang po dang mjal te snga sor rang lugs kyi yi dam rnams la bsnyen sgrub tshad du bskyal bas las tshogs zhi

drag gang mdzad kyang bar gcod med pa'i khag theg sogs 'byung 'gyur lung bstan shin tu mang po stsal zhing thugs 'phreng ba ltar mdzad/ rim gyis dbus gtsang gi lam bar bla
dpon dgon sde mtha' dag la rang skal bzhin gyi chos sbyin stsal ba dang bsnyen bkur 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pas mdun bsu bzhin par khra 'brug lha khang mjal du byon skabs
tshangs pa lha'i thor tshugs dngos su phebs nas byang phyogs sogs kyi lung bstan rgya chen dang mjal dar bcas gus pas btud/ bsam yas su phebs skabs sprul pa'i chos skyong
chen pos brgyud pa 'od zer can du mtshan gsol ba sogs gus 'dud lhur blangs/ de nas rim par brgyud de lam bar hor gyi sde nang nas rta drel la rkun po byung bar/ chos
srung la rbad bskul gnang bas pu tra lcam sring gi gras sring mo dngos su byon te bstan dgra de'i rgyu ma khyer nas phul ba dang / spu dogs gzhung grang ngar che tshad la
dgun sgang der yar mar ltang 'ju ba'i drod byung ba sogs ya mtshan du ma da bcas 'dam thog tu chag phebs/ der yang ljags bsnyen kha gsos bcas chos srung gi dus gtor mdzad
pas dge ltas phun sum tshogs pa byung / de nas byang phyogs gser kha na sa paN gyi lung bstan pa'i bskal bzang dgon du phebs skabs/ rga a gnyan

pag sha'i chos dung rgyang grags 'di nyid srung mas dngos grub kyi tshul du sbyin bdag gur mgon gyis phul/ de nas yar byon pa'i lha rtags mdor rdo la zhabs rjes gsal ba phyogs
de'i skye dgu'i bsod nams kyi rten du bzhag lha ri gsum mdor phebs tshe sa gnas kyi byang sems yul lha'i tshul 'dzin pa/ jo bo sgyogs chen ldong ra lha bu nor bu'i gtsug
rgyan can du sprul nas/ kwa ye 'jam dbyangs bla ma bka' drin can/ /byang phyogs mun pa'i smag rum 'thims 'dra bar/ /dam pa chos kyi bdud rtsi stsal du gsol/ /rdo rje
theg pa'i sgron me sbar du gsol/ /zhes sogs kyi gzhan don la thugs rje bskul ba'i tshigs bcad lung bstan mang du phul ba'i mthar/ bya rgod gcig tu sprul nas mkha' la 'phur
tshul byung ba dang / de yang rdo la sku chos kyi rjes gcig gnang ba sogs zhib par yi ge mangs kyis dogs pa las gzhan du grub pa'i rtags mtshan dpag tu med par stsal/de
nas slar yang bdag chen kun legs zhabs drung mjal zhing gser srang gang sogs 'bul bar mdzad nas bka' bgros bstun rgya yul du phebs bzhed kyis zhag gsum lam gtor gyi gtor
'bul mdzad skabs dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyis me tog gi char zim phab pa mthun grub tu byung / de nas spe yi chu

tshan du phebs skabs thab mdzo zhig dang rgod ma gcig rkun mas 'khrid tshe mdzo rwa la me 'bar ba sogs srung mas 'phral du cho 'phrul btang bas phyi nyin sgar thog tu tshur
phul/ lu thang du zhag shas bzhugs tshe bi ri ru thog nas brgya 'bul byung / rim gyis rtsa mdo dpal 'bar du phebs/ dpon slob nyung shas byams mdun mjal du phebs par byams
mgon gyi zhal nas 'gro don la bsku' ba'i gsung dngos su gnang / yar phebs pa'i sgrol ma ri gdong du sgrol ma'i sku brnyan sngon med pa zhig kun la mjal kha gnang bas ya
mtshan pa mdzad/ sgar gzhis su phebs khar bzhugs sgar ban tshang par bya rog zhig gis skad gtong zhing / gzims gur gyi sgo mchu yis phye tshul byed pa sogs 'byon pa'i brda'
ston byung ba bzhin phebs/ de nas sgar btegs skam bu gnas nang du chos rgyal 'phags pa'i 'cham mgon rta thog gnyan po'i sku brnyan la rten gtor btsugs nas snyan shal
gnang tshe/ dngos su lung bstan las/ 'di nas shar phyogs 'dod dgu 'byung ba'i gnas/ /grags pas mkha' khyab srid zhi'i dpal 'byor yongs/ /bar chad sel zhing lus dang grib
mar 'grogs/ /bsten cing bsgrub la mchod gtor brtson par byos/ /zhes pa phul/

de nas ka bzhi dgon du phebs/ dgon pa'i spyi rim du phur bzlog gcig gnang / gzas kha nas drel gcig rkun mas khyer bas rjes rnyog tu/ khram pa'i mthong snang la rlung nag gcig
gi gseb na mi nag bong bu la bzhon pa zhig gis 'ded snang byung bas 'phral du sgar thog phul ba'i drel de la dgra 'dul lhas gnang du gsung / 'bom kha dgon du spyi rim
dmar chen gtor bzlog cig gnang nas rim gyis rgya bod kyi tshong 'dus dar rtse mdo ru phebs te/ sgar chen gangs chu khar gnang/ lcags la'i nang blon yul skad du ya rud grags
pa gu ru rdo rje dang / sngon smon bzang po'i mtshams sbyor lta bus mchod yon nang gtsang gi zhabs 'degs byung / phyogs der rims tshad 'go yams shig byung ba'i rkyen gyis
dpon chung grags pa rdo rje zhes pa glo bur du grongs par/ rje 'di nyid kyis dgongs pa brtul zhugs dang ldan pas phung po dmar bsregs dang bdun tshigs kyi cho gas rjes
'dzin gnang bar grwa 'khor rnams shin tu bred kyang gcig la yang ma 'gos par ma zad nad rims gzhan yang chad pas snyan pa phyogs mthar khyab pa byung / de skabs la mo rtse'i
lha mos 'di skad du/ gangs can lngongs kyi gtsug rgyan rta bdun khyod/ /'od zer bye bas stong gsum khyab par byas/ /mun pa'i tshogs

bcom bdud sde kun las rgyal/ /slar yang mjal shing skal ldan re ba skong / /dam chos sgrog cing grags pas sa kun khyab/ /bsam don sgrub cing bar chad kho mos sel/ /zhes sogs
kyi lung bstan dang dam bca' phul lo/ /de nas yang nam mkha' rgyal po'i rim gror phur bzlog gnang ba sogs gdul bya kun gyi re bskangs nas slar yang yar 'byon rgyur dgongs
pa gtad te li thang brgyud nas phebs lam rnams su grub mtha' gcig min sogs skye dgu mtha' dag gis zhabs 'degs rgya chen la rang skal bzhin gyi chos 'brel stsol bzhin pas
'dam thog chos sder phyag phebs/ bdag chen zhabs drung dang mjal 'phrad thugs snang gshin pa'i bka' bgros dang bcas spro bzhin pa nas dbus ljongs su chibs bsgyur brtsams
pa'i lam bar rnams su de skabs rdza chu la ko ba gtong dgos skabs la rje nyid phebs gdong chu rab bde mor bgrod thub pa dang / skabs shig lam nor en byung ba bya rog gnyis
kyis lam sna bstan pa dang / mnal lam du lung bstan byung ba bzhin/ slob dpon chen po'i phyag rjes zhig kyang 'don par mdzad pa da lta dpal sa skya'i bstan sgam na bzhugs
pa sogs thun mong ma yin pa'i mdzad pa blo'i ra ba las brgal bzhin pas lha sar

phebs nas jo shAka rnam gnyis sogs la mjal mchod mdzad/de yan gyilam du yang lha sde/ mi sde kun la chos dang zang zing gi sbyin pas tshim par mdzad pa dang / gzhis ka phreng
po zur bus sde pa ngos ma bsad pa'i gshin po'i gnas 'dren dang / gson pa'i srog bslu mdzad pa sogs thugs rje dang / phrin las tshad med pa'i ngang nas rim gyis phebs pa'ii
gdan sa nas ser phreng mgon 'chams sogs gzab spros dang bcas pas bsus te/ dgung lo nyer lnga chu byi'i steng la gzhir bzhugs zhal ngo rin po che rnams dang phan tshun
thugs spro ba'i ngang nas mjal te khyad nor thams cad yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs drung du phul/ lha dang srung ma rnams la gtang rag mchod sprin rgyas pa dang / chos
sder yang mang skol 'gyed bcas rgya cher stsal te/ dgyes bzhin pas bzhugs thog dgung lo nyer drug gi skabs shig mnga' ris gong ma chen po khri sde bsod nams dbang phyug
nas gdan 'dren nan zhu byung bar/ zhal ngo thams cad thugs gros bstun pa'i sgo nas 'byon pa shar te/ rdzong khar phyag phebs thog gong ma chos rgyal chen po phebs bsur
'byor ba nas bzung pho brang khyung rdzong dkar por zla gcig tsam bzhugs te rdo rje phur pa'i gtor bzlog dang mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog sogs gnang ba gnad

smiin gyi mtshan ma ya mtshan pas dad 'bul rgya chen po dang bcas chos rgyal nyid kyis skyel thung mdzad nas gdan sar phebs te rnam dkar gyi phrin las rgya cher skyong mur/slar
yang bdag chen kun dga' legs pa'i dgongs pa rjogs phyir dgung lo nyer bdun shing stag lor mdo khams su 'byon pa'i dgongs pa gtad nas chos srung la lam gtor dang / zhal
ngo rnams la bka' bgros thugs smon mdzad/ sku mched gnyis pos kyang glang dkar bar thugs 'phreng ba'i skyel thung mdzad cing phyir lam ngor du phebs/ de nas kyang bsam
grub rtser sde srid kyi sku rim drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog gnang / khrom la tshe dbang mdzad/ rim gyis phebs te dpal 'byor rab brtan du re zhig bzhugs/ dbyangs can bsod nams
rgyal mor phur pa'i dbang bka' gnang / bstan pa spyi sger gyi rim gror phur bzlog mdzad/ mngon spyod kyi rtags mtshan mthun grub tu byung / yar rgyab chu 'phrang la bgegs
bskrod mdzad pas chu chen rgyang du bros pa dang / mchims phur zhabs rjes stsal zhing / nyi ma bzung ba thams cad mthun snang du byung / rim gyis 'phan yul brgyud dur
khrod klu mo rgyal gyi bam gdan rdo leb kyi steng du o rgyan rin po che dpa' bo mkha' 'gro chos srung bcas la mchod gtor

phul nas mnyes par mdzad/ slob dpon 'khor bcas dngos su zhal gzigs pa dang 'ja' tshon me tog gi char sogs ya mtshan pa dang / de nas lha sar phebs lam sgo la'i gzhi bdag brag
phug tu phyag rjes shig gnang / jo bo rin po che mjal/ 'bras spungs sprul sku ri po che nas ja 'dren dang rgya sbug legs pa stsal/ gnas chen yer pa mjal/ lo dgon par phebs/
spyan snga kun dga' don grub la snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa mang zhig gsan/ de nas lho lam brgyud nas rwa rgo sum mdor phebs sgar tshugs su rgyun bskang grub rjes dad
ldan 'ga' la khro lo nas nye brgyud 'jam dkar gyi rjes gnang mdzad tshe kha char bu yug gi thugs sun par byung tshe mgyogs gtor rkang gling snyan dar g.yab pas 'phral dwangs
byung / lcags ra dpal 'bar du chos rgyal 'phags pa'i dgon par phebs/ o rgyan sbas lung gangs ri mi ro rus khom gangs seng sogs lam 'phrang ya nga yod sa nas sgar dmangs
bcas phebs par skyon med du bde bar byung / de nas yang yid 'ong shis ring / ka rnam ri bo che'i phyogs rnams su gdul bya che bar byung / mdo khams sges mdor phyag phebs
tshe/ sa dkar nas bdag chen kun legs zhabs drung sku bsnyel ba'i tshul bstan par rgyu mtshan zhu 'bul dang gdan 'dren pa 'byor

'phral zhal mjal ma byung dogs pas 'phral bshad du phebs te bdag chen de nyid dang dngos mjal gsung gleng thugs dgongs rdzogs pa byung / sku ngos nas nan zhus dang / sku 'khor
rnams kyis dbu tshugs kyi ngo ma chog par dgon ma bu dang phyag rdzas gang yod rtsis bzhes lugs mdzad zin 'phral slar yang sku rim zhabs brtan gseng shor med pa bsgrub
kyang zhing khams gzhan gyi gdul byar gzhigs pas rdo la bsnyung bu btsugs pa'i lugs las ma byung bar thugs yus pa'i ngang nas sku gdung zhu ba dang dbus gtsang phyogs su
mang bskol gser gdung bzhengs pa sogs thugs dgongs rdzogs thabs rmad du byung ba gnang bzhin pas gdan sa de nyid du lo ngo bzhi bzhugs nas/dgungs grangs so gcig bzhes tshe
mtha' 'khob sog po 'dul ba'i dus la gzigs te chibs btegs nas rim pas phebs te mtsho khri shod rgyal mo'i lho phyogs sa'i dpyad phun sum tshogs shing chos ldan gyi rgyal
poo 'khor lo chen po zhes bya bas skyong ba'i yul gyi cha sha ra jur ge zhes bya bar bzhugs sgar btab/ sa bya lo zla ba gnyis pa'i dus tshes phun sum tshog pa'i nyin mor
sa dbang de nyid dang mchod yon mjal 'dzom rten 'brel gyi sgo brgya phye/ sngar phan rgyal po'i btsun mo bog tho ma zhes par rigs

brgyud ma byung bar zhabs drung du srung rim skyabs 'jug zhus pa bzhin/ lha srung rnams la phriin bcol gnang bas phyi lo rgyal brgyud 'khrungs par rje nyid nas ming nor bu
mgon skyabs gnang / gzhan yang rgyal blon phal che ba dag rdo rje phur pa'i dbang bskur gyis smin par mdzad/ spyi sger gyi rkyen sel gtor mdos sogs mang du gnang zhing re
ba'i shing rta bkang nas slar yang 'dam thog phyogs la chibs bsgyur mdzad tshe rgyal po 'khor bcas gus zhen gyis 'bral mi phod pa'i rnam pa byung / tshur lam yang shos kun
dga' thas ji'i sa phyogs su lha 'dre'i cho 'phrul rtsa 'bu gdug pa can zhig gis rtswa rnams thams cad zos pas dud 'gro dpag med mu ges 'chi rkyen byung 'dug par gzhan
phan gyi thugs rje tshad med pas sa phyogs der rdo rje phur pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dkyil chog gnang bas de 'phral nasartswa 'bu'i 'tshe
ba nam yang ma byung bas kun gyis dad brgya'i gsol 'debs lhur len par gyur pa sogs thun mong ma yin pa'i rnam thar ya mtshan du ma dang bcas sa dkar gdan sar phebs/de
nas kyang ri zhig nas shar phyogs su 'byon pa'i dgongs pa shar te/ rim brgyud kyis sde dger phyag phebs pa dang / sde

dge sgrub dbang kun dga' rgya mtsho dpon g.yog gis dad gus tshad med pa'i zhabs 'degs rgya cher zhus/ de nas tre bo'i sa cha rong pa tshar phyag phebs/ brag sdod gangs ri dkar
po zhes pa'i gzhi bdag che gnyan de yis zhabs la btud de phrin las bsgrub par dam bca' phul/ khram pa gnyis kyis sgar mdzo gnyis brkus te bshas pa'i khong nas sbal sbrul
mang po thon pa dang / mgon rta la pho rog gis zhon nas khram pa'i sgo drung du dngos su chas pa sogs cho 'phrul drag po du mas sna drangs te khram pa gnyis kyi khyim
la me 'bar bas thal bar brlag de nas yang rim par phebs pa'i lam bar hor pa dang lcags mdud lo star gyi 'khrug pa shor bas srog chags du ma 'chi ba la thugs rje chen pos
bzlum par mdzad/ a gnyan paka shis bzhengs pa'i kre'i rde'u mgon khang du rang lugs kyi srung ma dngos su bzhugs par rten gtor dang hor lcags bzlum pa'i phrin bcol gnang
skabs rtags mtshan ngo mtshar bas thams cad yid ches bka' nyan pa byung / 'di skabs rdo rje nag po chen pos dngos su 'di ltar/ nga ni 'bral ba med do 'di ltar soms/ sangs
rgyas bstan pa bsrung zhing dam ldan skyongs/ /dus kyi mchod gtor dag la brtson par byos/ /bar du gcod pa thams cad nga yis sel/ /

zhes sogs zhal bzhes phul/de nas shes khog stod smad rim brgyud mchod rten dkar por phyag phebs tshe sa yangs dang lcags la gnyis 'khrug rtsod shor ba'i gtan gsan ma thag sngon
gyi sbyin bdag rnying mar gyur pa dang / 'phral gyi thugs rje shugs drag 'khrugs pas bskul te/ nyin mtshan ltos med du dar mdor phebs tshe/ phal pa'i blos mi 'khyud
pa'i lha min gyis 'khrug long lta bus gnam sa khengs pa'i bar du thog brdzis kyi byon te lugs gnyis char dang bstun pa'i bar 'ching gnang bas bde 'jags su btang / chu log
chen pos tshong 'dus 'jig la nye ba'ang bden smon gyis bzlogde skabs shig na dpal lha sgang shes bya ba'i gnas chen du dge 'dun khri phrag mang tshogs mdzad nas rje nyid
tshogs dbur phebs/ rten mchod 'dus pa rnams la 'bul 'gyed rgya che ba stsal/ 'di khongs su rdo rje phur pa'i gtor bzlog rgyas pa zhig gnang ba'i skabs/ rdo la zhabs rjes
shig kyang stsal zhing / me tog gi char sogs kyis kun kyang ngo mtshar bar mdzad/ gzhan yang snga phyir dar mdor rang du rdul tshon la brten pa'i rdo rje phur pa'i dkyil
chog 'chams sogs gdan sa'i phyag len las khyad

par med pa dang / dus mdos gzab spros/ rgya gdung dpon gyi rim gror mgon po'i gtor bzlog dar mdo'i spyi rim du sgar thog tu phur bzlog sogs bstan pa'i mig rgyan du 'gyur nges
kho na gnang/ lha mi kun gyi gtsug gis bkur zhing zang zing gi 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ste/ slar bod la chibs bsgyur gyi lam gtor rim gror phur bzlog tshug
par zor bkra sogs legs par byung /mi nyag gi lam bar gyi sa dge dkar dgon ris med kyi 'chos sder gnam rgyan re dang 'dus tshogs la bsnyen bkur phul/ 'bam kha'i chos sde
zhes pa thog mar gnas brtan ba ku las sprul zhing/ phyis su rig pa'i seng ge byang chub dpal bas dgon btab pa der bka' 'gyur tshar gcig gsung sgrogs gnang / glegs bam dgu'i
dril tshes sngon dus bstan bshig 'gas khyer ba'i tshab la gos chen gyi na bza' phul/ phyu mo dgon par dbon po ngag dbang sogs la gur drag gi bka' dbang stsal/ de kha'i
mgon khang du mgon sku gsar bzhengs dang rab gnas gnang/ ka bzhi dgon du sa mchod la ser phreng yo byad thogs pa sogs kyis bskor ba mdzad/ slar yang 'bam kha dgon du drug
cu pa'i gtor bzlog mdzad/ lha 'bri dgon par dpon slob bu lung

tshul khrims rgya mtsho sogs lha sde mi sde byings la ras chung tshe dbang gi khrom chos gnang bar 'ja' gur sogs ya mtshan pa'i ltas byung / slar ka bzhi chos sder phebs nas
dus mdos lo gsar sogs mdzad/de skabs kyang dar mdo na lcags la'i las tshan phan tshun nang 'khrugs kyis tshong 'dus stong la khad byung ba gsan pasarje nyid kyis bdag gzhan
bde sdug gtong len phyag thog tu bkal ste 'o brgyal la je mi snyam par dpon slob drag bsdus 'phral bshad la phebs te so sor bde 'jags su mdzad/ phyis su yang dmag 'khrug
ar jag sogs mi byed par rje 'di nyid nas jeng 'dren lta bur gnang ste grub mtha' tha dad pa dpag tu med pa dag nas kyang gtor bzlog mdo sgrub bzhes khra bcas pas rgyal
khams 'jam dar yug gcig la bkod par mdzad nas/ phyir ka bzhi dgon par chibs bsgyur/ ka bzhi'i dge 'dun tshogs dang sgar gzhis kyi sku 'khor ban tshang rnams kyis ser phreng
gi bsu ba sogs shin tu spro ba phul/ de nas ma 'gyangs par phyag rjas stobs che bas spyir gyis dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing dang / sgos su gdan sa chen por bstan pa'i
btsas su 'gyur ba zhig la dgongs pa rbad gcad gnang /

dgungs grangs so bdun pa horazla gsum pa'i dus tshes dge bar chibs btegs te ka bzhi dgon pas skyel thung dang bcas rim pas nyag rong gru brgyud/ li thang du nye bar phebs tshe
li thang dpon de thor pa'i nad kyis grongs pa rje nyid sngar phebs skabs yon bdag rnying pa yin pas thugs smon dang thugs bskyed kyis mtshams sbyar te kho rang gi kha
chems su bdag gi 'pho 'debs de bdag chen mthu sdobs zhabs drung la zhus byas pa ltar gdan 'dren 'byor bar sgar dmangs hor chu tshur ka thang dkar du bzhag rags bsdus zhig
'brum nad la the tshom med par myur du phebs nas shi gson gyis re ba rdzogs par rjes su bzung 'ja' sa dpon gyis gdan drangs par phebs/ khrom chen la 'byung 'dul dang tshe
dbang sogs gnang bas 'brum pa rbad kyis chad pas yul phyogs de ha las pas dad spro thob/ slar sgar thog tu phebs/ thang dkar bla ma 'phrin las pas gsol ba btab ngor chos
'khor mang du bskor/ de nas chibs btegs te ljang rdzong dkar por phebs/ yul de'i jag mi rnams kyis gus pas btud par phyag rdor la sogs pa'i dbang bka' gnang / de nas rim
par bka' phur phebs/ de kha'i mgon khang du gsung bskang gnang skabs dpal mgon nag po chen po'i zhal nas/ da lo

dbus gtsang phyogs su rta kha bsgyur/ /bar chad phran bu 'dug ste kho bos sel/ /zhes sogs lung bstan kha shas bstsal/ de nas rim brgyud rgya skabs gdan sar phebs/ de phyogs
skye dgu mtha' dag chos dang zang zing gis tshim par mdzad/ ram 'bur mgon khang du chos rgyal 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam rten gras/ gnyen mgon bram gzugs chen por
bskang ba 'phrin bcol gnang tshe gnyen mgon gyis dngos lung bstan du ma stsal/de nas dngol hreng steng du phebs lha sde mi sde khrom tshogs la thugs rje chen pa'i bsgom lung
gnang / de nas ab bra thang du dge lugs zhal snga sogs la bla ma'i rnal 'byor la sogs pa'i chos 'khor bskor/ de bzhin du lam bar rnams su 'gro ba rnams smin grol gyi
lam la 'god bzhin pa nas dom nag gru don tshe yul phyogs kyi gzhi bdag gis thog ser shA 'od sogs tshub kyi rnam pa byung bar lha dang srung mar 'phrin bcol gnang tshe glo
bur du gur mgon gyi rnam 'phrul mi nag chen po gcig dang / zhal gyi sprul pa mi nag ag tshom ras lcog dkar po byas pa gnyis kas phub re khur nas rbab dang chu log mngon
sum skyabs nas mdun gyi nam mkhar yal zhing 'phrang gi lam ring la gzi bdag gi sprul pa ri dwags gnyis kyis rba rdo phabs pas pu tra'i sprul pa a tsa ra

zhig gis rbab de bar lam nas blangs te chu rongs la 'phangs/de nas tsha ba'i sgang du phyag phebs 'brong pa dpon sogs kyis bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa zhus gshed dmar la
sogs pa'i zab chos 'ga' zhig kyang stsal/ khra rgan phug tu phebs tshe sa dkar/ 'dam thog gnas nang gis gtsos pa'i lha sde mi sde kun gyis bzhugs dgos kyi nan bshol zhus
kyang ma gsan par shar gyis phebs/ lho rong rdzong nas sde pas bsnyen bkur legs par zhus lam skabs dge lugs dgon pa 'ga' la'ang mang bskol gnang / tshal brag dgon pa'i zhing
khar rta drel shor ba'i rkyen gyis sgar dgon 'thab 'dzing thug kyang / sgar pa'i grwa rigs rnams bla ma lha yis skyabs te cang ma skyon/ dgon pa'i grwa pa gsum tsam
la rdo sogs thebs pa byung yang slar bshags pa'i tshul du gdan drangs nas zhabs tog zhus/ de nas khams stod lcags ra dpal 'bar du phebs/ dge ldan pa'i yon bdag dbang drag
gis bsnyen bkur 'bul ba rgya cher zhus/ tshe dbang sogs kyi 'dod chos gnang /de nas gong la brgyud rim pas rdza la'i rtsar phebs tshe khams kyi gzhi bdag rnams kyi sgor
bsgyil gyi tshul du kha bas phebs dka' tsam byung / de nas jo mo snar mang bskol gnang / lba

rang sgang sogs brgyud nas snye mda' bon dgon sogs su phebs tshe hor gyi mi sna yin zer ba'i khram pa 'ga' zhig nya mgo gnon mkhan dang / ha ri lung skyog tu phebs tshe karma
sa skyong zer ba'i mi sna slebs te gnang sbyin dgos zer ba dang / khyad par du bdud mo ga cha'i ming can gyis/ khram pa mang po bskul nas sgar pa blang bar chas tshe/
rje 'di nyid nas sgar thams cad thugs blos btang kyang zil che bas blang ma nus pa dang / slar mer gzhung du phebs tshe/ chos srung rnams kyis mngon spyod kyi rtags mtshan
'phral du bstan nas khram pa mang po bsgral ba'i nye du rnams dang ga cha 'khor bcas kyis thugs rjes 'dzin par zhu ba'i bsngo rten rjes bsnyegs su phul ba rjes su bzung
/ 'bri gung tshal du dar 'phan dang mang bskol gnang / bkra shis na thang du phebs tshe spyan snga byams pa kun dga' don grub phebs pa las zab chos 'ga' zhig gsan/ mang
ra'i dgon pas ser phreng 'cham mgon gyis phebs bsu zhus/ der slob dpon zhi drag sogs gsar rnying gi chos bka' dang dar 'phan bskol 'gyed gnang /lha sar phebs te jo zhal rnam
gnyis kyis gtsos pa'i rten mchog 'ga' la bla re snyan dar dar chen sogs smon lam bcas

gnang / gnas der nwa lendra'i bco brgyad dbon po sogs la khrom chos rgya cher gnang / sa dge bka' 'brug ris med kyi chos sder mang skol sogs phun sum tshogs par stsal/ gsang
mdar gling stod mkhan po mjal khar byon pa dang thugs spro mdzad/ gsang phu sogs dgon gnas kha shas la mang skol gnang / bsam yas gnyer pa mkhan po grags pa dpal 'byor
slebasashing / chos skyong chen po'i zhu yig dang ngag lam mtshungs par brgyud pa 'od zer can rang bsam tshad de byas na gegs med 'grub par 'gyur sogs kyi lung bstan phul
bar skyes len du snyan dar ja phud dar chen sogs stsal/ dbu rtse chen mor sgyan gnam rgyan 'dus tshogs la mang ja ja 'gyed sogs bskur gnang mdzad/ rim gyis skyid tshal sogs
la mang skol dang / gong dkar du mang ja skol 'gyed sogs tshan che ba dang / chos 'khor dpag med bskor/ de phyogs kyi chos sde rnams la mang skol gnang / brag thog pa'i
gzims phug mjal/ yar 'brog dpal de sde pas gus 'dud zhus shing chos dang zang zing gis ngoms par mdzad/sna dkar rtse nas gdan 'dren slebs pa ltar byon/ ser phreng sogs
bsu ba rgyas par bstar zhal ngo rnams la rdo rje phur pa'i dbang bskur sogs thugs 'dod bskang / dgon par mang

skol mdzad/ slar gong dkar du tshogs khro gnang / rong byams chen la gnam sa'i rgyan dang / der yang mang skol gnang / rin spung du dpon sa tshe brtan dpal mos dad spro dpag
tu med pas bsnyen bkur/ sku rim phur bslog mdzad/rtse gdong gdan sa nas 'jam mgon bsod nams lhun grub khu dbon gyis gdan 'dren nan can bzhin der byon/ khu dbon rnams kyi
sku rim du drug cu pa'i gtor rdzong gnang bar mngon spyod kyi bkra ltas legs rab byung / phan tshun bka' chos gnang bzhes rgya cher mdzad/ zhal ngo rnams la skyes gnang
dang / chos sde la dar 'phan mang skol sogs stsal/ gser mdog can du gnam rgyan mang 'gyed sogs dang / thugs rje chen po'i sgom lung yang stsal/de nas bsam grub rtse ru nye
ba na chos rgyal karma bstan skyong gis chibs bsu dang bcas thog mar klu sding du zhag shas bzhugs/ tshe dpag dkar po sogs kyis bka' dbang du ma dang gnang skyes kyang
rgya cher stsal/ de nas pho brang chen po'i shar stengs su rgyun ring bzhugasashing sbyin bdag gi sku rim du phur bzlog dang lo gsar dus mdos gzab spros lugs kyi 'chams
sku sogs gdan sa nas gdan 'dren zhus pa nyer bdun nyin 'byor

bar sde brgyad dregs pa mngon sum gyi rnam pas 'tshub lhong dang rlung 'tshub sogs shin tu 'jigs kyang / nyer brgyad 'chams kyi nyin dang nyer dgu gtor rgyag gi skabs gnam
yul 'jam shing rten 'brel legs par byung / slar yang gdan sa'i phyag len bzhin gyi phur bsgrub zhus pa bzhin rdul tshon la brten pa'i stod las kyi sgrub pa btsugs/ dpon slob
drung 'khor rags rim la dbang bka' kha yar gnang / mchod yon thugs snang gshin stabs 'bral miphod pa tsam byung /de nas rim par lhun rtse klu sdings/ dge sdings/ bar
sdings/ ber chen glang dkar brgyud/ tsher chen du ga ya dha ra'i rnam sprul mjam dbyangs kun dga'i mtshan can dang mjal 'phrad thugs spro gnang / de nas gdan sa'i nye cha
bkra shis lha khang gi mchod rten rtsa ba'i zhing ring du phebs tshe lha chen pho brang nas dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i ser phreng / 'cham mgon lcam dral gyi sku brnyan dang /
mnga' ris kyi skye bo pho mo gzab 'phyor gyi glu gar bcas pas bsus tshe rje nyid kyi gzigs snang la gdan sa 'di nyid kyi bla ma lha yis dngos su bsu ba gnang ba yang dbu
rtse rnying ma'i drang thad na 'ja' 'od dbus su 'jam dbyangs gtso 'khor lnga dang / g.yas su dkar po rnam gsum/ g.yon du

gsang ngag chen po/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ bla brang bzhi thog chen mo'i steng char yab rje grags pa blo gros dang / g.yas su ngag
dbang mtshan can/ g.yon du rgyal yum chen mo sogs gsal por gzigs shing thugs nyams shin tu spro bas/ rdo rje'i nyams dbyangs kyang mdzad/ de nas bzhi thog tu sku mched
zhal 'dzom phebs spro dga' ston dang bzhugs gnas phun tshogs gling du gnang / lha khang chen mor ka khongs gcig gi mtha' grur mnyam pa'i bla bre dang sil snyan tshangs
dbyangs 'brug sgras mtshon/ gzhan yang gtsug lag khang thams cad la gos dar gyi 'phan dang gnam rgyan sogs shin tu mang po dang / khyad par du mgon khang gong 'og bsam brling
bcas rdo rje'i chos srung rnams la gtang rag gi gsol mchod spyan gzigs rgyas par stsal/ phyag rdzas khyad nor gang yod thams cad gdan sa nyid du gnang / dge 'dun 'dus
pa'i tshogs la yang mang skol ja 'gyed gos 'gyed sogs dpag tu med pa gnang /skabs 'dir 'jam mgon a mes zhabs dang / rnam 'dren kun dga' don grub/ mkhan chen rin chen rgyal
mtshan rnams las zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi dpag tu med pa yang

gsan bzhes mdzad/ gdan sa'i sku rim du drug cu pa'i gtor rdzong zhig kyang gnang ba sogs gdan sar zla ba lnga tsam bzhugs shing / de mtshams lha sar zhabs bskor dam bca' yod
mdzad sogs kyis sku mched bka' bgros thog dbus su 'byon bzhed kyis lha chen dang srung ma khang rnams su bskang ba 'phrin bcol dang / gzhi byes kyi sku rim du phur bzlog
rgyas par mdzad de 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis phebs skyel zhu ba mdzad de gdan sa nas chibs bteg snar thang du phebs skabs ngor nas gdan 'dren 'byor ba bzhin phebs/ dbon
po 'byung gnas mtshan can mkhan por bsko bzhag dang / tshogs par mang ja kha shas kyi thog bstan don la phan slebs gtan 'jags yong ba'i zhal ta phebs/ snar thang la yang
mang skol dang rten mjal gnang nas gzhis ka klu sdings su phebs/ mchod yon thugs spro tshad med kyi ngang nas bka' dbang kha shas gnang / sgrub gnas khyad 'phags phung
po ri bo cher gnas mjal la phebs skabs dag pa'i snang ba 'byams su klas pa gzigs/ rin spungs su dpon sa nyid la che dbang brgya rtsa gnang zhing / spyi sger khrom dbang sogs
chos kyi char pa 'beb par mdzad de/ skal ldan smin grol la 'god kyin yar 'brog g.yu mtshor ko sbrel gyis phebs tshe/ mtsho rlabs kyi

rnam pas klu rnams kyis bstod pa gsan pa'ang 'di ltar/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir gdul bya'i snang tshul du/ /rdo rje gdan nas dpag tshad brgya bgrod pa'i/ /gtsang stod grom pa
dpal ldan sa skya de/ /'jam dpal dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul 'byon pa'i gnas/ /gnas chan de ru blo gtad ma 'chugs pas/ /lha klu la sogs sems kyi re ba khengs/ /slar yang 'gro
don phyogs med byed par smon/ /zhes so/ /rim pas chu shul skyed tshal du phebs tshe zhabs kyi dreg ro 'phar nas re shig 'byon 'phro bshol te/ spyan snga'i zhabs drung nas
tshe bka' brgya tshar dang / ljags lung sogs mang bar gsan/ gong dkar sogs chos sde mang por mang skol mdzad/ sman dpyad sogs kyis 'phral dngas gyur/ rnam rgyal gser khang
du chos skyong chen po'i lung bstan bzhin bcad rgya zhag bdun gnang / lha sar jo shAka mjal zhing / dkar me mchod 'bul gser gsos sogs rgyas par phul/ bsam yas chos skyong
chen pos gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs sgo dod de/ mnye thang du a ti sha'i sku 'bum mjal/ dge 'dun la mang ja bsnyen bkur dang bla ma'i rnal 'byor gnang / gsang phu gling
stod zhabs drung dang / 'brug pa lcog grwa dpon slob mjal khar 'byor/ rdo rje

brag tu phebs tshe zhabs 'degs legs par zhus/ de nas rdo mchod du phebs tshe sprul pa'i chos rgyal sku 'khor yul bdag lha klu sogs kyis glu gar rol mor bcas pas bsus pa'i pi
lbang gi sgra las bstod dbyangs gsan pa'i thugs nyams gsal po dang / sngon dus bai ro'i sku tsher slob dpon chos rgyal lo paN sogs mjal phrad kyis tshul thugs dran gsal
por gsos shing / dbu rtse chen mo'i mkhan slob rab byung tshogs kyis ser phreng bsu ba ngo mtshar dang bcas nas phebs/ chos skyong chen por gtang rag bskang bshags rgyas
par phul/ bu tshal gser khang du gdan phab/dgung lo so brgyad shing glang lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes gsum nyin lcog steng du bsangs chen mdzad tshe chos skyong chen po
sku pheb sa te/ glang nas glang lo'i bar sogs kyi lung bstan gdeng khel phul/ de skabs lo nas spyan snga byams pa kun dga'i mtshan can gdan drangs nas bka' chos yun ring
por gsan/ phar yang / sa lo'i bka' 'bum gsung ngag khrid yig snyung gnas cho ga rdo rje gur/ rtsa brgyud brtag gnyis/ rje nyid kyi lam glu ring mo sogs kyis ljags lung
stsal/ 'di lo dam nyams kyis rgyud dkrug pa kha shas kyi byed spyod la brten bar skabs 'tshubs zing zhig byung bas rten rnams la nyams grib byung tshod

kyis chos skyong chen pos mdo sde mchod pa'i thog tu dbu rtse'i sku 'dra rnams la rten khrus dgos tshul dang / lcog steng gi byang shar du sngags 'chang chen pos gnang ba'i
thug dmar la nyams gsos dgos tshul zhus pa ltar rten la khrus gsol rgyas pa dang / thug dmar gsar du btsugs nas bstan pa rgyas pa'i 'phrin bcol rgyas par mdzad/ bsam yas
gling bzhi gling phran jo mo gling gsum ka bcu lha khang sogs zhib mjal gyi dbu rtser gnam rgyan dang gzhan rnams la snyan shal dbul/ de nas yar rgyab phyogs su phebs tshe
chos skyong chen por lam gtor gnang ba'i spyan 'dren gyi skabs su sku sten la pu tra dngos su bab nas yid ches gdeng khel gyi lung bstan du ma phul/ de nas grwa pa mngon
shes kyi gtsug lag khang chen gra thang du phebs/ mang skol gnas mjal rgyas par mdzad/ grub rgyal gyi bka' dbang khrom chos su stsal/ gdung phud la byon nas mang skol
dang tshogs pa la 'jam dkar sogs bka' chos kha shas dang khrom tshogs la tshe dbang gnang / rim par spre shing phebs nA ro'i sku rgyan thugs dam padma rA ga sogs yod pa'i
gdung rten dang dud sol lha mo'i drung du bskang ba rgyasapa mdzad/ mang ja dang snyan dar thugs smon gnang tshe mkha' la mja' 'od 'khrigs pa kun gyi mthun snang du gyur/

dgas po grwa tshang du yang chos 'brel sogs gnang zhing / tshur la dad spro'i bsnyen bkur dpag med zhus/de nas gong dkar du phebs te re zhig bzhugs rtsis gnang / khrom la tshe
dbang lan gnyis stsal ba'i skabs snga phyir 'ja' dang me tog kun gyis mthong ba byung / than pa ches par gzhi bdag la phrin bcol gtor ma phul bas char chen zhag grangs
su phab/ rgan mo 'chi nges chu la 'phen khar slebs pa zhig la tshe dbang gnang bas gsos/de nas sngon gyi dam bca' mi 'gal ched du lha sar phebs nas jo shAg rin po cher
dkar me snyan shal dang zhabs skor kha shas mdzad nas yar phebs te/ bde mchog srin po ri sogs la gnas mjal mdzad/ klu dbang gling gi skyid tshal du rdo la zhabs rjes gnang
/slar yang chos rgyal bstan skyong dbang pos zhus ngor gtsang phyogs su chibs bsgyur te/ dpal di/ sna dkar rtse/ ra lung rnams nas bsnyen bkur zhabs 'degs phun sum tshogs
par zhus/ thong lcags mgon khang du bcad rgya bdun gcig bzhugs par dag snang gzigs mo ngo mtshar ba shar/ rgyal rtse chos sder phebs te/ rig 'dzin bla brgyud gsar bzhengs
la rab gnas

zhus par kyai rdor la brten pa'i nyin gang ma zhig gnang / grub rgyal dang 'byung 'dul rjes gnang stsal/ bla brang dkar po'i mkhan chen gyis gdan drangs par byon 'dod chos
'ga' zhig gnang / rgyal mkhar rtser dpon sa yum sras kyis gdan drangs par tshe bka' brgya tshar gnang / chos rgyal bstan skyong dbang po'i sku rim du phur bzlog de skabs
chos rgyal bstan skyong de nyid dbus phyogs su phebs bzhed kyis rgyal mkhar rtse bar/ gtsang phyogs lha sde mi sde thams cad kyis zhu tshig dngos chas gang gis kyang ma bshol
bar/ rje nyid nas dam tshig dran bskul gyi tshul du bka' stsal lci mos bshol tshe dad pa'i stobs kyis bka' bzlog ma nus pas gtsang phyogs kyi skye dgu'i re skong du
gyur/ slar yang re zhig bar sbyin bdag gi sku rim dang bstan pa spyi rim dus mdos sogs legs par mdzad/ chos rgyal de nyid la yi dam chos skyong kha yar gyi rjes gnang mdzad/
dpal 'byor rab brtan gyis gzhis ka dang / grwa thang sgrub sde sogs phul/ de skabs shig thob rgyal yum ched gtad 'byor bar/ rdul tshon la brten pa'i rdo rje phur pa'i
stod las dbang bskur sogs gnang / chos rgyal bstan skyong dbang po'i sku rim 'ga' zhig kyang tshugs par mdzad nas/ chos rgyal de nyid kyis skyel thung bcas rim phebs kyis

skyid khud chu tshan 'phrod bzhes gnang / gong dkar du mang skol mdzad cing zhag shas gdan phabs/rim pas chibs bteg ra ba smad gtsug lag khang la shis brjod stsal/ sa 'bor
gzhis kar tshe dbang zhig gnang / gra thang chos sdes ser phreng dang bcas gzhis ka chen po dpal 'byor rab brtan du phebs zhag shas song nas/ gra thang du mthong smon gzim
spyil du bzhugs/ gra thang gnod sbyin chen por phrin bcol rgyas par gnang/ thams cad mkhyen pa zha lu lo chen gyi dngul gdung zhabs drung dang / lam 'bras bla brgyud sogs
la rten mjal dang / bla brang mgon khang du bskang gso dang gtsug lag de nyid mi nyams pa'i gnyer gtad phrin bcol mdzad/ gra mda'i khrom tshogs ser skya la dbang bka'
gnang / byams gling mchod rten mjal/ sgrub sde bla brang du bzhugs nas chos 'khor bskor mang ja bsnyen bkur sogs rgya cher stsal/ chos srung la bskang gso dang chos sde dar
ba'i phrin bcol rgyas par gnang / bstan pa spyi dang bye brag rje 'di nyid la gus zhen chen pos zhabs 'degs phul phyin zhus pa'i sbyin bdag bsam dar bas 'di res kyang
dpal rab tu bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa zhus/de nas dgung lo zhe gcig bzhes pa sa 'brug lo dus tshes

dge bar chos srung tshogs la sngar bcol gtang rag dang / da bcol zhu 'debs kyis lo gsar mnga' gsol mchod pa phul/ ras chung tshe dbang khrom chos su gnang / 'di skabs 'jam
mgon a mes zhabs kyis gdan sa skor tsam phebs dgos gnang ba ltar/ hor zla dang po'i gza' skar dge bar chibs bsgyur te/ gong dkar du mang ja bsnyen bkur dang / khrom tshogs
la tshe dbang gnang / 'du khang du chos sbyin dang tshogs bsngo gnang / rdo rje gdan pa'i dngul gdung mdun du sil snyan dang / byu ru'i rgyal lag phul/ gong dkar rtser
mi dbang bstan skyong dbang po'i bka' blon chos mdzad rgyal po don 'grub kyis gus pas gdan drangs nas dad 'bul rgya chen dang skyel thung sogs thugs spro zhus/ dpal di ba/
sna dkar rtse pa/ rong ram pa rnams su sgar tshugs la thab bsu sogs zhabs 'degs rim 'thud du byung ba rnams la chos sbyin gyis byang grol la bkod par gnang / thob rgyal
nas gdan 'dren 'byor/ rin spungs dpon sa'i sku rim du phur bzlog dang tshe dbang sogs stsal/ 'brug pa'i sku zhabs gsung rtsom gra tshang ba dpon slob mjal du 'byor bar re
ba bkang / khrom dbang stsal/ de nas yang rim pas skyil pa 'tsho byed kyis bsnyen bkur phul/ 'am phug gru khar dkar spro

zhus/ gru khar dpon sa rin chen 'dzom pas thabs bsu rgyas par zhus/ de nub dpon tshang ri gdong du bzhugs/ sang snga bar thob rgyal rtser phebs/ ser skya thams cad kyi gzab
spros kyis bsus/ pho brang du dpon sa'i sku rim phur bzlog mdzad/ sger spyi la tshe dbang sogs chos sbyin rgya cher stsal/ rje nyid 'khor bcas la bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa phul/ pad gling gsung sprul mkhas grub tshul khrims rdo rjer chos 'brel gnang / dgon khag gsum la mang ja stsal/slar chibs 'khor bar chos rgyal bstan skyong dbang
pos chibs bsu dang bcas bsam rtse'i skyid tshal du zhag shas bzhugs nas chos rgyal nyid la sgrol dkar sogs yi dam kha yar gyi rjes gnang dang/ gzhan yang chos 'khor du ma
bskor/ de nas rim brgyud glang dkar du 'jam mgon ngag dbang dku na dga' bsod nams kyi chibs bsu 'byor ba dang sku mched sdeb nasalha chen rig 'dzin pho brang du phebs gsol
ja dkar spro rgyas par bzhes/ de nas bde mchog pho brang du gdan phab nas/ gnangs nyin phun chogs gling gi tshoms chen du phebs ston rgyas par mdzad/ a mes zhabs la sa
skya bka' 'bum rin po che dang 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang pos mdzad pa'i slob

dpon padma'i rnam thar gyi ljags lung gnang / 'di skabs bde mchog pho brang du rdo la zhabs rjes gsal por gnang / byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag tu phebs nas re zhig thugs dam gyi
rgyun bskyangs tshe thugs la 'khrungs pa'i nyams dbyangs kyang mdzad/'di lo hor zla bdun pa'i tshes bcu bzhi sngags 'chang chen po'i dus chen gyi tho rengs mnal dang 'od
gsal 'dres pa'i gzigs mor/ dpon po ri'i rgyab phyogs 'ja' sprin 'khrigs pa'i khrod na/ rje btsun dkar po rnam gsum/ sngags 'chang chen po/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang
po o rgyan gyi cha lugs can/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ gur zhal pu tra bcas gsal por gzigs/ dus mdos chen mor nye ba'i tshe 'jam mgon kun dga'i zhabs nas sku 'chams
sogs byang chub kyang bar skabs cung zad bsnyel tshul la/ rje 'di nyid dang dbu byed byams pa dpal 'byor dpon slob la dran gso 'bul dgos tshul gnang ba ltar rje nyid nas
zhib par phul bas 'di ltar yin zhes dgyes tshor chen po gnang / de nas mgon khang rnams dang bsam brling bcas par lam gtor smin rgyas gnang nas/ nyer bzhi'i gnas kyi dpa'
bo mkha' 'gro 'du gnas ming don mthun pa'i yul chen la phebs te/ rtsa khu lung du byang pa'i dpon pas

bzhes ston 'bul ba rgya cher zhus ras chung tshe dbang sogs chos sbyin bstsal/ e ru phebs tshe gnyer pa blo bzang sogs phebs bsur 'byor/ sang dkar leb dgon pa sogs kyis ser
phreng bcas pas mdun bsus te gzhis kar phebs/de na sngon dus snga phyir thugs kyi dam bca' yod pa bzhin sprul pa'i bzo bo dzi na zhes pa'i sku brnyan bzo khyad 'phags shing
myur du grub pa dang / la na bkra shis zhes pas rgyal mtshan/ dung chen sogs bzo khyad phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs/ gzhan yang tshe dbang grub rgyal dang / rta mgrin/
'byung 'dul/ sgrol dkar sogs rjes gnang chos sbyin mang du stsal/ khyab bdag byams pa phun tshogs gdan drangs nas bka' chos rgya cher gsan/de nas dbus phyogs su chibs bsgyur
lam bar ar po sogs grang ngar che yang dbyar sgang ltar dro bas thams cad ngo mtshar skyes/ ngam ring nas gdan 'dren 'byor ba bzhin zhal gyis bzhes te rim gyis phebs
par/ dgun chos skabs yin pas sa dge'i dge 'dun sum stong drug brgyas ser phreng gis mdun bsus/ 'bul ba bsnyen bkur dpag med zhus/ phar yang mang 'gyed dang bka' chos rgya
cher stsal/

'di res dgung grangs zhe gnyis sa sprul lor phebs pa'i lo gsar du mkha' 'gro chos srung la mnga' gsol rgyas par phul/ rim gyis bkra shis sbug tu phebs pa dang gdan sa nas thabs
bsu 'byor/ sang snga bar sku mched mjal spro gnang ste bde mchog tu bzhugs/ snga sor chos rgyal chen por slar mi 'gyangs bar phebs pa'i zhal bzhes yod kyang gdan sa'i
lha mi thams cad yid phreng ba'i bsgor bsgyil lha bus spyan mig an tsam snyun tshul byung bar sman dpyad dang lha bsangs gnang zhing gzugs med 'byung po'i tshogs la bka'
bsgo mdzad pas 'phral dngas byung / de nas gdan sa nas chibs btegs te dong rtse na khar phebs tshe chos rgyal chen po'i thab bsu dang bcas rim phebs kyis skyed tshal du
bzhugs gnas gnang / chos rgyal nyid nas dpon tshang tsha rong tshe dbang rig 'dzin par bkod pa dang bcas spyan gyi snyun gzhi slar mildang ba'i 'phrod bsten phul/ de nas
sde srid kyi sku rim du mgon po drug cu'i gtor bzlog gnang / khyab bdag kun dga' lhun grub kyi zhabs drung nas rjes gnang 'ga' zhig gsan/ sde srid srung 'khor sger spyi
dang/ zhol par khrom chos bcal dbang bka' 'ga' zhig stsal/ mda' dpon sa phud che bas dbang bka' zhus par brten mang rab cig

la ras chung tshe dbang zhig gnang / slar yang sde srid kyi sku rim du dmar chen gtor bzlog btsugs pa'i gtor rdzong nyin char chen 'beb 'phro chad cing nam mkha'i mtha' rnams
sprin nag dang 'tshub mas bskor ba'i dbus na nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor tsha bar 'ja' dkar pos bskor bar byung / sde srid nas gzhis kar ser tshogs su 'dzugs rgyu'i tshogs zangs
blugs pa'i bzo rnams la bkod pa thong tsam rje nyid la bar chad bsrung bar zhus nas blugs su nye ba dang gnam sa sprin 'tshub 'brug glog sogs lce 'bab tu nye ba'i 'tshub
byung bar/ rkang gling btang zhing g.yab dar g.yo pa bcas/ bka' bsgo gnang bas dngos gzhi blug skabs mtshan mo nam mkha' dwangs shing skar bkra rgyas pa dang bcas zangs
chen ngo mtshar lugs pa'i rab gnas kyang gnang /slar yang mi dbang chen pos skyel thung dang bcas dbus phyogs su chibs bsgyur/ lha khud du phebs tshe rtse gdong du gdan
'dren 'byor yang chu ches pas bshol/ de nas rim gyis chos sbyin gegs med stsal bzhin pas rin spung su phebs/ dpon sa nas bsnyen bkur phun tshogs zhus dbang bka' kha shas
gnang ba nas bzung zhag bcu tsam la char chen babs/ rim gyis rong chen brgyud nas phebs par yul mi rnams lam 'phreng ngan pa dang

chu che bas 'jigs snang tshad med byed par rje nyid brtul zhugs kyi ngang nas yud kyi bde bar phebs/ rim brgyud gong dkar du dge 'dun rnams la mang ja 'bras thug 'gyed bcas
dang / khrom la ras chung tshe dbang gnang / dol gyi sa 'bor du phebs/ dad ldan dgos dgos ma bu 'khor bcas kyis gus pas mchod chos sbyin yang gnang / dbang phyug 'bar gyi
gnas gzhir phebs tshe dge 'dun sgang pa dang / byams gling chos sde'i mkhan zur gyis chibs bsu dang / gra thang 'dus sdes/ ser phreng sogs bkod pa phul du byung bas gnas
nang mthong smon du zhag shas bzhugs/ de nas gzhis kha dpal 'byor rab brtan du phebs nas gdan phab te bzhugs/ gong ma sde srid kyis phul ba'i sog po la sogs pa'i chos gzhis
rtsis len mdzad/ 'di lo'i dus mdos kyi skabs la babs pas gzab spros gnang bar de skabs spyan dang zhabs en mi bde ba'i rnam par yod kyang sku 'chams sogs kyi skabs sku
gzugs shin tu bde nyams dang nam mkha' dngas ba sogs spro bar byung bas khrom rnams kyis sku khams rnyog pa mi bden pa 'dug zer ba byung / slar yang srung ma'i tshogs
la bskang gso rgyas par gnang /dgung lo zhe gsum lcags rta lor son pa'i lo gsar dang

chos srung la mnga' gsol rgyas pa sogs phul/ de skabs kyang sde srid nas sku rim sgrub zhus bzhin phur bzlog sogs gnang / de mtshams rin spung nas bang chen snga phyir gdan
'dren nan zhus bstud pas sku 'khor rags bsdus phebs/ sku rim che phra mang du gnang / slar sgar gzhis kyang yar bsdongs nas thob rgyal du gdan drangs pa ltar phebs/ dbang
bka' phur bzlog sogs 'dod don rdzogs par mdzad/ de mtshams hor yul nas chos dar 'bum gyis nan zhus ltar byon nas shi gson rjes 'dzin re ba rdzogs par mdzad/ de phyogs re
zhig bzhugs tshe 'gro don 'phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab zhig 'ong tshod kyang thol skyes rbad chod kyis dgongs pas zhag cig nas thob rgyal phyogs su phebs/ de mtshams kyang
spyan mig en ma bde yang rtse gdong nas gdan 'dren 'byor ba bzhin phebs/ sku mched bgres gzhon gnyis kyi bsu ba dang bcas mjal 'phrad thugs spro gnang / sku rim phur
bzlog sogs tshugs spyan yang rim gyis dngas / rtse gdong rgyal yum gyi gcung mo bsnyun bar sngags chu srung mdud sogs stsal bas sang dngas byung /de nas gzhis ka bsam grub
rtse nas sde srid kyis gdan 'dren 'byor bar thogs med phebs nas re zhig gdan phabs te

bzhugs/ de ras kyi sku rim du dbang bka' dang phur bzlog sogs mdzad/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' lhun grub las tshe dbang brgya rtsa gsan/ gzhis ka rin spungs nas gdan 'dren 'byor
ba bzhin phebs/ tshe brtan dpal mo an tsam bsnyung bar rim gro thugs dgongs bzhin gnang bas phral dngas byung / lam du 'brug sgron tshe dus byas par lam bstan dang lhar
skye bar gzigs slar yang dbus phyogs phebs/ gong dkar chos sder mang ja bsnyen bkur gnang / de nas phebs te bla brang dpal 'byor rab brtan du gdan phabs te 'di gong bstan
pa spyi sger rgyas pa'i 'od gsal lung bstan byung ba bzhin dus mdos chen mo tshugs te grol nyin srid zhi dpal 'byur ma'i bkra shis skabs thugs nyams 'ur zhing spyi sger
gyi bstan dgra 'ga' zhig mngon spyod 'phriin las kyis byang grol la bkod pa gsal bar gzigs/ chos skyong yid bzhin nor bus mi mgo rlon pa dar gyis bstum pa rnams dngos su
phul/dgung lo zhe bzhi lcags lug lor phebs pa'i thog sku phreng sngon ma sngags 'chang chen mo'i sku dus bzhengs bzhed kyang skabs su ma babs pas sku tshe 'dir bzhengs dgos
pa bzhin bzo rigs pa lngas mgon khang yid bzhin nor bu rten dang brten par

bcas pa khyad par grub 'tshams sde srid nas kyang sku rim sgrub dgos kyi rten 'brel rang 'grig tu mgon po rab brtan 'byor bar phur bzlog phral 'dzugs gnang zhing / slar mgon
khang la rab gnas mnga' gsol shis brjod nyin/ 'ja' gur dang me tog gi char mthun snang du byung / bla ma sgo mo bas gdan drangs pa bzhin gson gshin rjes 'dzin re skong
gnang / skabs shig nas sde srid kyis sku rim ser tshogs chen mo'i tshogs dbur phebs dgos 'byor bar/ bshad rtsol ngang nas rgyal khab tu phebs te phur bzlog gnang / bstan
pa spyi sger dang sbyin bdag gi rim gror dgongs gtad kyis dus mdos gzab spros lugs kyi gnod sbyin rnams dang ru 'dren rnams kyi chas bzo bkod brtsam tshe/ thog mar 'tshub
lhong che zhing bzo bo zhig 'bags btsog gi rkyen gyis tshe dus byas/ gzhan mar bka' bsgo phrin bcol sogs gnang bas gegs med grub/ de nas dus mdos tshugs shing zor 'phen
nyin chos srung rgyud gsum dregs pa gnam sa khengs pa dang/ khyad par tse'u dmar po/ gnas rnying rgyal po sogs kyis rang phyogs srung zhing gzhan sde 'joms pa'i rnam 'gyur
gsal po dang / sog 'dre'i 'tshub kyi rnam pa rlung dmar gyis rdzong la bskor ba'i gseb tu mi dkar ber dkar can rta dkar la bzhon

pa g.yas g.yon dgra sta zhags pa thogs pa zhig la 'khor rgya 'dre mdog gos lag cha sna tshogs can mang po 'dug pa rtsa gsum chos srung rnams kyis byang phyogs su bskrad pa
gsal por gzigs pa bzhin/ kun gyi mthong snang la'ang gnas rnying rgyal po'i khang pa nas rlung dmar g.yas bskor byang phyogs du song bas gtor rdzong grub nas slar log tshe
drung 'khor rnams kyi rlung dmar sogs 'tshub 'gyur de 'dra sde srid la sku dog 'dra med dam zhus pas/ spyir gyis chos rgyal nyid thugs dang brtan pas skyon chen gtan mi
'ong yang mtha' mi'i dmag gis thugs bsun phran bu zhig 'phral du yong dogs yod pas zor skyor dgos zhes gsungs/dgung lo zhe lnga chu sprel lor phebs pa'i lo gsar dga' ston
sogs zhib rgyas gnang / sog bzlog la dgongs pa'i klu sdings su bdun gsum la bcad rgya gnang nas phur bzlogs tshad smin mdzad/ slar yang shar pyogs su chibs bsgyur te/ lam
bar skal ldan du ma smin grol la 'god bzhin pas rgyal mkhar rtser phebs/ bdag chen blo gros pa'i gnas mchog khyad par 'phags pa der mgon khang du gtor spod gnang ba sogs
re zhig bzhugs/ sbyin bdag sde srid mchog gi rim gro dang sogs bzlog la zil gnon mgon khang du bdun phrag gcig tu bcad rgya

gnang / de nas re zhig nas sog po'i zing sne byung bar sde srid nas bde dog gi thugs dam zhus par zab mo bdud kyi spyod yul gyi sgo nas 'od gsal gyi dgongs pas gzigs par tho
rengs kyi char mnal lam du/ sog 'dre mdog skya ber smug gon pa dgra sta thod pa thogs pa 'khor yang de 'dra mang po dang bcas byung nas mtsho mkhan kha'i rgyal po 'dir
slebs yod pas khyed rang yon mchod rnying par song bas sog po'i nang la bskor tsam 'byon dgos/ gal te mi 'byon na ded rnams gtsang pyogs 'dir re zhig sdod rgyu yin zer byung
bar/ rje nyid nas sngar dpon po 'khor lo che'i skabs su khyod tsho la chos dang gtor ma'i sbyin pa 'brel ba'i dam tshig dran par byos la song zhig ces stong nyid lta
ba'i phags skor mdzad pas re zhig yal nas/ slar yang sngar gyi gzugs byad las nyams zhan za 'dod gyi tshul du mdung dang khug ma thogs pa mang po byung nas ded rnams log
'gro lam rgyags gtor ma dgos zer byung bar ting nge 'dzin gyis sprul te bsngo bar mdzad pas tshims te rin chen sgang brgyud nas byang phyogs su shar gyis song ba gzigs pas/
zhus lan du/ hor sogs 'jigs pa'i dmag tshogs dgra che yang / /khyod kyi sku yi stobs dang mi mnyam par/ /rgol ba ngan pa'i klad pa 'gems nus pas/ /

g.yul gyi dpung 'degs cher ni mi dgos 'dra/ /zhes sogs lung bstan gnang /skabs der dmigs pa'i phur bzlog gcig kyang mdzad/ de skabs than pas gdungs pas dad ldan sbyin bdag
rnams kyis zhus ngor bden brjod gnang bas char chen 'phral du phebs/ de mtshams sde srid nas ched zhus kyis pa rnams kun dga' phun tshogs dpal mo'i rkyen sel du phebs skabs
gong du byad gtad sogs yod chod la sku rim dang bsod nams kyis ma tshugs par nye 'khor la 'gyur ba'i byed ngo rgyal ltas cho 'phrul dngos su mthong rgyu byung ba'ang tshegs
med du bzlog par gnang / de nas chibs bteg te 'byor rgyas dang / khri khang tshong 'dus rnams nas bsnyen bkur dang bcas bkra shis dge tshal klu sdings su sde srid nyid
phebs bsur 'byor/ phebs ja dkar spro sogs rgyas par zhus/ slar gnas chen rnams la rab gnas skyor ba dang bstan pa gso chog la 'byon par zhus pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes/
rin spungs su dpon sa bsnyung ba'i rim gror tshe dbang gnang bas 'phral dngas byung / gong dkar du zhag shas gdan phabs bstan pa gso chog mdzad/ bde mchog srin po ri/ 'or
gyi gtsug lag khang / lha sa jo zhal rnam gnyis/ yer pa lha ri/

bsam yas/ khra 'brug yum bu bla mkhar/ gra thang rnams su'ang bstan pa gso chog rgyas par mdzad/ de dag gi tshe srin po ri'i bde mchog dang / jo zhal rnam gnyis nas dngos su
lung bstan stsal/ yer pa o rgyan phug nas tshe chu babs/ bsam yas chos skyong chen pos dbu rmog phud nas phebs bsu zhus/ sku gsob chen mor zhig gsos rab gnas dgos tshul
dang bar chad mi yong tshul nan zhus bzhin gnang / khra 'brug tshangs pa dung gi thor tshugs can dang / de'i las mkhan bse khog zer ba dag gis yid lus spongs pa'i smon lam
zhig zhus pa bzhin ljags rtsom gnang ste 'deb la sbyar ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa rgyun chags kyis slar dpal rab tu phebs/ 'dren mchog kun dga'i mtshan can byon
par bka' chos mang zhig gsan/ phar la sa skya bka' 'bum rin po che'i ljags lung gnang /snyan pa dang 'phrin las dkar phyogs rnams kyis spel ba ltar lho phyogs mon yul nas
gdan 'dren 'byor/ bstan don la dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed rbad chod kyis phebs pa shar/ rim pas phag ri brgyud/ jo mo lha ri'i gangs la bsangs mchod mdzad/ sprel mo lha rgyab
nas 'oo dod 'phrang gi bdud mo la gtor ma gnang / nyang spe dbon po sdod sar phebs/ dngul sogs

'bul ba spom mthor bteg spa gro gzhung brgyud/ 'brug chos sdings su phebs/ 'brug pa spyi bla dang spa gro'i yon bdag gi dad 'dun bsnyen bkur bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhus/ de
nas mi pham ngag dbang rnam rgyal drung du phebs pa'i lam khar gzhi bdag gi 'tshub nyams bu yug gis thugs bsun pa zhig byung yang / nyes pas ma gos par dpe med thang du phebs/
'tshub rkyen 'gyur ba'i rnam pas gnas mo de thog so gnyis nas brul yang skyon ma byung / phyir nyin snga bar gdung brgyud dang mjal 'phrad mdzad cing / 'phang ye dgon
nas bla ma spyi dpon rnams kyis nan can gyis gdan 'dren 'byor ba ltar/ lam 'phrang tshad nad mi dang za ma gang sar ya nga bar gyur kyang bstan 'gror dgongs te shar gyis
phebs/ bstod pa'i la rgyab/ 'phan steng nas ser phreng bcas zhabs tog rgyas par zhus/ lo ru byon tshe yang thed pa mi log rnams kyi 'bul ba bsnyen bkur legs pa byung /
bar grong zam pa sogs la sku phreng sngon ma'i smon mthu btsan pas nyes med du phebs/ 'phang ye bla spyi'i rta thab bsu/ ser phreng bcas phun sum tshogs pa byur / gnas de
bla ma gong ma'i zhabs kyis bcags shing / sngags 'chang chen po'i phyag bris kyi mgon khang bar chad kun sel sogs kyang bzhugs/ chos kyis sbyin pa rgya cher

stsal/ chags sdang kha mchu sogs kyang bde 'jags mdzad/ spel shing / mang rtse/ spo tog sogs dgon khag mang po'i gdan 'dren 'byor/ gnas de'i sngags 'chang chen po'i bzhugs
khri kha gsos gnang / phyag bris mgon khang rnams la phrin 'chol mdzad nas rim gyis phebs te bar grong lcags zam khar mang rtse spo tog dga' se yon mchod rnams mjal khar
slebs par byin brlabs bsngo smon sogs chos 'brel gnang / 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / rnyil du phebs tshe snar thang bla ma dpon slob rnams kyis zhabs 'degs tshad
med phul/ rang lugs sho mangs dgon par ri bong tshang log dgos pa'i dam bsgrags gnang / rnyil ma'i la chen brgal/ rim gyis sa skya'i dbu chen nam mkha' bsam grub pas gsar
btab kyi dgon ming bkra shis dar rgyas gnang / spel shing dgon pas gdan drangs par byon/ ser phreng sogs kyis mdun bsus nas chos khri gsar brtsigs kyi steng du phebs/
'bul ba bsnyen bkur tshad med byung zhing chos sbyin rgya cher bstsal nas re zhig bzhugs/ spa dkar du pha tshan nang 'khrug gis yul khams stongs su nye bar/ lam 'phrang tshad
pa sogs ya nga ba'i yul yin kyang bstan 'gror dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed sbar bcangs gnang ste phebs nas bde 'jags su

mdzad/ yul der sngags 'chang chen pos byin gyis brlabs pa'i mgon khang sogs mjal/ sngags 'chang bzhugs khrir dar chen phyar/de nas bod phyogs su chibs bsgyur/ chu mdo'i rab
brgal/ g.yul gsum du bzhugs/ slar spa gro choos sding du phebs/ 'brug bla rab 'byams pas 'bul chen phul te skyel thung zhus/ nya spe dpon po rnams kyis zhabs tog dang dos
skyel sogs zhabs 'degs rgya cher bsgrubs/ spa gro stag tshang du bzhugs zhag gnang smon lam zhib rgyas mdzad/ spe shing sku skye dang yon bdag dmangs mas dad gus 'bral
mi phod pa tsam zhus/ 'o dod 'phrang gi bdud mo shin tu gdug rtsub che bas 'grul pa rnams kyi dmar mchod rgyas pa sogs dgos kyang rje nyid nas gzhi bdag gtor ma gnang bas
tshim zhing gus 'dud phul/ de skabs gzigs snang la sangs rgyas byang sems 'ga' zhig dang / khyad par o rgyan rin po che mkhan po dang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po sku
chas dkar rkyang la dbu skra dkar sangs/ g.yas thugs kar rdo rje rtse lnga dang / g.yon thod pa bdud rtsis gang ba bsnams pa'i g.yas phyogs na 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang
po bcas gsal po dang / yab yum gnyis kyang lam pa zhig

gzigs/ de'i tshe sngags 'chang chen por gdung shugs mtshan 'bod kyi nyams dbyangs mdzad tshe/ nga yis rjes bzung ras chen mthu stobs khyod/ /dus rnams kun tu o rgyan thugs
rjes bskyang/ /zhes sogs rdo rje'i gsung du mas dbugs dbyung gnang / phag ri brgyud pa'i lam bar rnams su 'bul ba dpag med byung / gdan sa ra lung gi gnyer pas gus 'dud zhus/
rim gyis gong dkar chos sder phebs nas mang ja 'bras thug 'gyed bcas stsal/ dus tshes legs pa dang bstun gra thang du phebs/ dpon slob mkhan pos phebs spro rgyas pa
dang bcas mthong smon bla brang du bzhugs/ phyir nyin dpal rab gdan sar phebs/ chos srung la sngar mdzad gtang rag dang slad kyi 'phrin bcol rgyas par gnang / dbus phyogs
chos sde rnams la 'bras 'jam stsal/skabs 'dir bzo rig pa drug gis rten bzhengs tshugs pa'i bzo rgyab do dam pa dpon tshan rnam gnyis bskos te/ gser zangs gis rdo rje 'chang
gi sku brnyan/ dngul gyi mgon po'i bla brgyud mtho tshad gras gcig rnams zla ba lnga'i nang du gegs med grub/ grub mtha' ris med kyi byin rten sogs gzungs gzhug dang
rab gnas bcas mthar phyin gnang / gra byams gling chos

sde chen po'i khrir phebs bstan pa'i me ro legs par gsos/'di skabasakyang sde srid nas 'phral dgos kyi yo byad rgyas pa dang bcas gnas chen rnams la rab gnas zhal gso mdzad
par zhus pa bzhin/ lha sa jo zhal rnam gnyis kyi mdun du mchod sprin dang bcas bden smon sogs zhib par stsal/ phyogs der than pas nyen pa rnams kyis gsol bar btab ngor bden
brjod mdzad pas char rgyun nyin zhag gsum babs/ jo bo'i sku mdun dkyil 'khor sdings du rgyud sde'i yang snying phur par brten pa'i bzlog chog mdzad pa'i gtor rdzong gi
nyin thebs rtags ya mtshan pa byung / de ga'i khyams gra chen mor dgyes rdor la brten pa'i zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg gnang tshe 'od zer 'phro ba'i lha rnams las ngo mtshar
ba'i ltas byung / chos sbyin yang rgya cher stsal/ zhabs skor gnang tshe nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char pa mthun grub tu byung / rim pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor
bzhin pas 'phan yul glang thang / sman rtse / bde chen rdzong / zhang gi gnas chen/ yang rdzong shel phug rnams su mchod sprin zhal gso rab gnas mdzad/ shel phug tu
phyag rjes shig kyang stsal/ de nas dpal gyi bsam yas su lha mi'i bsu ba dang bcas phebs pho brang gong du bzhugs/ lha mi'i dam tshig gi 'brel pas char rgyun

chen po babs/ bstan pa spyi sger la dmigs pa'i phur bzlog gnang / rab gnas zhal gso'i nyin dge mtshan phun sum tshogs pa byung / 'jam dpal gling dang byams pa gling du zhi
rgyas kyis sbyin sreg gnang / bar khang g.yu zhal du zhal gso'i cho ga mdzad tshe char rgyun chen po babs par bka' bsgo gnang bas phral du dngas shing 'ja' gur lta bas chog
mi shes pa byung / chos skyong gi lung bstan ltar lha mo'i 'cham sku dang / padmas rab gnas mdzad pa'i sdig khrab dang dbu rmog la zhig gsos dang / skar chung lha khang
la bye chu'i 'jigs pa srung ba'i las thabs dang / gtsug lag khang gling dang gling phran mtha' dag la mchod sprin dang bstan pa gso chog zhib par mdzad/ phyi bskor mdzad
tshe ngo mtshar ba'i ltas byung / skal ldan rnams la chos sbyin yang rgya cher stsal/slar dpal rab tu chibs bteg tshe/ yul lha gzhi bdag phreng bas rlung 'tshub sogs byung
bar/ grun khar phebs pa dang gzhi bdag gtor ma gnang bas nam mkha' dngas pa dang / 'ja' 'od 'khrigs pa byung / bye ma rdzing pas spyan drangs par lha khang la rab gnas
gnang / 'bul ba bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa byung / byams gling du phebs nas re zhig bzhugs

te bstan pa gso chog dang mchod sprin spro bar mdzad/ gra thang gtsug lag khang du rdo rje bdud 'dul la bskang gso dang bstan pa gso chog mdzad/ phyi nyin dpal rab tu phebs/
gsar bzhengs gtsug lag khang la ri mo ba ngag dbang rin chen gyis logs bris mgo brtsams nas bzo ris mkhas pa bcu phrag gis zla ba lnga tsam gyi khongs su legs par grub
ste/ hor zla dgu pa'i bcu bzhi sa mchod nyin mo dgyes rdor rab gnas nyin gsum ma mdzad/ mtha'i rgyal po mchog thus bsam yas gtsug lag tu gser dngul gyi maNDal phul ba'i rab
gnas dang shis brjod gnang 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / chos skyong chen po'i sku rten tshe 'phos par slar gang 'os lha sde mi sde kun gyis gsol ba btab pa bzhin
'di 'os bstsal/'di skabs snga pyir gdan sa gong nas gdan 'dren zhus pa bzhin gtsang phyogs su chib bteg lam bar du chos sbyin rgya cher stsal zhing lha mi'i bsu ba dang
bcas gdan sar phebs/ sku mched zhal 'dzoms thugs spro tshad med dang / mgon khang rnams su bskang gso rgyas par gnang / bzhugs gnas bde mchog tu mdzad de skabs 'jam mgon
a mes zhabs nas dkon mchog mchod pa dang dmangs la sbyin pa'i phyag ring nam mkha'i

mdzod sgo phye ba'i skabs rje de nyid mchod yul gyi gtso bor gdan 'dren zhu bar mdzad/ rab rgyas phrin las gling pas sngags kyi phyag len mtha' dag zhus pa gnang skabs ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas byung / skyed lhas su gtor 'bul 'phrin bcol rgyas pa dang / byas 'gyur dang khru ma lha khang du'ang mchod 'bul smon lam rgya cher stsal nas bde mchog tu
phebs/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i dus mchod phur sgrub 'cham sogs rgyas par sku mched lhan cig spro bar mdzad/ 'dren mchog kun dga' don grub las chos bka' rgya cher
gsan/dus tshes dge bar mgon khang nye 'gyangs rnams su bskang gso snyan shal sogs phul nas slar yang dbus phyogs la chibs bteg chos rdzong du 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang
po'i gzim chung mgon khang bcas la phyag mchod smon lam gnang / dar lung gnyen gyi pho brang du sde srid kyi sku rim phur bzlog dge sding du phebs/ dben gnas ti ri mjal/
rab rgyas phrin gling pas bsnyen bkur zhus/ snar thang byams pa la snyan shal phul/ bstan pa gso ba'i cho ga dang shis brjod mdzad/ dong rtse'i sa ru sde srid chibs bsur
'byor ba dang yon mchod lhan cig phebs/ gtsug lag khang dang dgon gnas gsar pa la me tog dor/ 'dren

mchog kun dga' lhun grub las gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang gsan/ rim gyis rin spungs su phebs/ dpon pa'i rim gror phur bzlog sogs gnang / rim pas dga' bde ram pa dag nas
kyang zhal 'degs phul byung zhus shing smin grol la bkod/ dpal de rdzong du zhal ngo rnams la smin byed stsal/ bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa byung / rim gyis chos sbyin
stsal bzhin pas gze mar phebs thog rdo rje gdan pas thab bsu dang / gong dkar nas bsu ba ser phreng / tshe dbang khrom chos su gnang / 'dus tshogs la mang 'gyed bsgrubs
skyid gshong grags chen sogs su skye dgu smin grol la bkod par gnang /gdung phud brgyud nas dpal rab tu phebs te slar yang mkhas dang grub pa'i rnam par thar pa rmad du
byung ba kho nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don rlabs po che gnang bzhin pa'i mthar dgung grangs lnga bcur phebs pa'i me glang lor bsam yas chos skyong chen po nas 'di lo
brgyud pa 'od zer can la sku dog chen po yod pas bcad rgya yun ring dang dgon sde mang por rgya ja'i 'du skol sogs dgos tshul nan zhus phul 'dug kyang / thun mong gi ngor
rten 'brel khyad du mi gsod tsam du bcad rgya bdun phrag gcig tsam dang / dgon kha shas la mang skol tsam gnang /

zhal nas kho bos rim gro mtshan tshe zhig byas na gdan sar 'gyur dogs yod/ de 'dra byung na kho bos gdan sa'i khur mi theg nga rang 'chi yang bzod ces sogs stsal/de mus sku
la bsnyun gyi rnam pa sogs gang yang med par lo de'i hor zla lnga pa'i 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po'i dus chen tshes bcu gnyis kyi nub mo sku dngos kyis zhing 'di'i gdul
bya rdzogs nas gtso bor zangs mdog dpal ri sogs mkha' spyod DA ki'i grong du bde chen gar gyis rtsen pa'i ched du re zhig gzugs sku chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan/zla
ba de kha'i tshes nyi shu la rgyu mtshan 'bul mi gdan sar 'byor ba dang / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs nas gzims dpon rab 'byams pa bsam gtan rgya mtsho sku tshab tu rdzong
bda' mdzad de/ gdung mchod du rab kyai rdor sgrub mchod rdul tshon ras bris ci rigs/ min kyang 'ga' zhig gis bla ma'i gdung mchod la kun rig 'os min zer rigs tshos don ma
