go ba yin zhing / dgos rgyu dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dang bla ma tha mi dad pa la bsgrub cing mchod pa yin pas de mthun gyis kun rig ras bris kyi cho ga yun mi thung tsam
zhig ni nges par dgos shing / gzhan ser tshogs kyi mchod 'bul phyag rdzas dang bstun pa'i gang

'khyer gyis/ dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi gdan sa 'dir zhal ngo gong ma rnams ltar mdzad rgyu yin zhing / slar rten bzhengs shig kyang dgos pa dpal rab nas e grub mi shes pas de
lugs phan sleb yong ba'i zangs dpyad sogs byung na bsrings lugs gyis/ khyod rang tsho blo mthun ngos dgongs rdzogs kyi brel ba chod bstun rgyal po mchod yon du bslab ston
zhu lugs go ma logs pa dgos tshul sogs gsung bkod bka' tho bcas phebs pa bzhin rab 'byams pa dpal rab tu 'byor tshe sku gdung rin po che sgam zhigs tu bzhugs su gsol nas
ban tshang pa rnams kyis bla mchod kho na gtong ba las sgrub mchod 'dra ni ma byung 'dug der sku gdung re zhig khang bu brtsegs pa'i mchod rten zhigs tu bzhugs su gsol/
ban tshang byings kyis kun rig zla phyed tsam dang / drag pa bzhi bzhis kyai rdor sgrub mchod star chags kyi bar seng du bla mchod ma chag par phul/ de mtshams gra nang
chos sde/ gong dkar/ bye rdzing rnams la bsnyen bkur rgya chen dang / gra nang gi dgon che chung sogs mchod sbyin gyi yul stong prag longs par mang 'gyed bsgrubs/ ngor/
gser mdog can/ thub stan gong 'og bya gshongs sogs su mang 'gyed/ gdan sa nas gdung brgyud rin po che'i yum gshegs pa dang stabasagacig tu gyur pas

'dres med ldab phar lugs kyis dgongs rdzogs rgya cher mdzad/ dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi'i nyin 'jam mgon a mes zhabs khri thog tu phebs nas gsung bsngo sogs zin gyi bar nam mkha'
'ja' 'od kyis khyab pa sogs ya mtshan pa'i ltas rgyun chags su byung /gzhan yang gdan sa dang gong dkar bcas la zla dus kyi mchod pa rgyun 'dzugs mdzad/ de mtshams dpal
rab tu sku gdung zhugs 'bul grub nas gdung rus phal cher gdan sar gdan drangs par/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs nyid kyis phyag tsha gnang ste gser zangs las grub dbang de nyid
kyi sku 'dra sku tshad gcig dang / dngul gdung phal thog phyed gnyis yod pa bzhengs par mdzad de nang rten gyi gras su bzhugs su gsol/me glang snron zla'i gza' tshes
dge bar 'jam mgon a mes zhabs nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa sha stag gi 'khor dang bcas pas dgyes pa rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas par mdzad de sku tshab dbu rtse dang / dngul
gdung bzhi thog rig 'dzin lha khang du bzhugs pa 'di nyid do/ /dpal rab tu rten rnying gras nas grub mchog nyid la yab rjes gnang ba'i mgon sku shel spyan ma 'jam mgon
a mes zhabs kyi gzim chung rten gras su bzhugs pa

'di dang / mgon brgyud kyi bris thang gras/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs nas 'bul bar mdzad pa'i lam zab bla brgyud sa lo chen po'i phyag nas can/ 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po'i thugs
dam rten gras mgon thang lnga tshar/ de nyid kyi phyag sbug tshangs dbyangs bde chen chos 'khor grub dbang nyid kyi phyag sbug bka' brgyad ma sogs rol mo drag gras lnga
tsam/ phyag dril dril smyon du grags pa sogs phyir 'khyar mi 'os pa kha shas gzim dpon rab brtan dang / dpon sa tshe brtan bu khrid gnyis kyis do dam byas nas slar gdan
sa 'di nyid du phul ba yin no/ /gzhan yang sku tshe 'di nyid kyi mdzad pa tha ma'i bar du mnga' ris gtsang dbus lho mon khams kong rgya sog yul gru mtha' dag pa rnams
su/ chos srid stobs 'byor gyis che gnyen du gyur pa'i bla dpon rigs dang dmangs phal bcas skal ldan grags med pa smin grol la bkod pa dang / mchod sbyin gyi yul ris su med
pa la zang zing gi dngos po lhug par rtsol ba dang / che gnyan nga rgyal gyis dregs pa'i sems brgyud zhe sdang gis kun nas dkrugs pas skye 'gro phal mo che'i lus srog longs
spyod brlag par byed pa'i sde ris phan tshun 'khrug longs du ma bde 'jags su mdzad pa'i chos dang zang zing mi 'jigs skyabs kyi sbyin pa brjod

kyis mi lang ba stsal ba dang / sa phyogs gar yang dbang bka' dkyil chog gtor mdos sogs gang btsugs kyang bstan pa'i mig rgyan du 'gyur nges kyi thig tshon bca' bzo dbyangs
rol sku 'cham sogs gdan sa dang khyad med pa'i phyag len rnam dag rgyas spros kho na ma gtogs sla chos dang khungs med rtogs bzo sogs gtan nas mi mdzad pa dang / mtha' 'khob
gdul dka'i 'gro ba rnams kyis kyang gang gi zhal mthong gsung thos tsam gyis rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar ba dang thugs rje chen po'i rgyud bskul te rtse gtsig tu gus
pa lta bur byed pas rgyal bstan rin po che phyogs mthar rgyas pa'i gzhir gyur pa dang / bka' dbang khrid lung sogs gang gi skabs kyang me tog gi char dang 'ja' 'od kyi gur
ni phal che bar 'byung zhing / drag gtor zor mdos sogs kyi skabs su'ang mngon spyod kyi thebs rtags mngon gyur mthun grub sha stag yong zhing / gdul bya yul dman pa gang
gis kyang dad pas gsol ba btab phyin byams dang snying rje tshad med pas rjes 'dzin rkyen sel gang 'dod bzhin shar mar gnang ba sogs 'phags pa mchog gi rnam thar so skye'i
blo yul las 'das pa dag da lta thun mong phyii'i rnam thar mdor bsdus phyogs mtshon tsam rje nyid kyi gsung la sgro skur dbri bsnan med par brjod pa ste/

gzhan du 'bras bu nye rgyu'i lam la brten nas lhan rgyas kyi bde ba lam du mdzad pas sku tshe 'di nyid kyis rdo rje 'chang chen po zung 'jug kha sbyor yan lag bdun gyi go 'phang
dam par gshegs pa'i tshul thun mong ma yin pa ni rje nyid kyis/ bde bas bde ba chen po kun/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gcod byed cing / /mya ngan 'das pa'i go 'phang mchog
/thob par 'gyur zhes rgyal bas gsungs/ /zhes dang / bde stong lhan cig ye shes chen po'i nyams/ /bde ba bde drod me 'bar gtum mos smyo/ /de yang thabs shes zung 'jug
chen pos smyo/ /zhes dang / dbab bzung bzlog dgram la sogs rlung dang sres/ /dga' bzhi'i ye shes mngon du gyur pa byung / /zhes sogs gsungs pas rgyud sde'i dgongs pa lon
pa rnams kyis phal cher rtogs pa nus shing / zhib par bkod pa ni 'dir skabs su ma bab la/ zhing 'di'i bkod pa bsdus 'phral dag pa ye shes kyi sku slob dpon chen po dang
dbyer med du bzhugs pa yang / dar mdor rjes mar phebs skabs kyi nyams dbyangs su/ zangs mdog dpal gyi ri bo cittar dran/ /skye 'chi gnyis spangs gu ru nus ldan dran/ /srin
po srin mo lha yi gzugs can dran/ /dpa' bo mkha' 'gro du ma sprin ltar 'thibs/ /'on kyang rnam dkar bsam pa mthar phyin

bar/ sems kyis sdug sgur bskyed de thang gcig bshol/ / zhes sogs skye 'chi la rang dbang thob pas bstan 'gro'i don 'bad med du mdzad pa sogs dad ldan bskal bzang rnams kyis
zhib tu rtogs par 'dod na rje 'di nyid kyi lam glu ring mo ma bu rnams las shes par bya'o/ /kun dga' dbang rgyal/de'i gcung kun dga' dbang rgyal ni yab dgung lo sum cu pa
chu 'brug la bstams/ dgung lo bcu gcig pa chu stag lor khrir 'don mdzad/ bcu gsum par phur sgrub la phebs/ bco lnga par bsod nams dbang po'i zhabs drung du sgrub thabs
brgya rgyam/ sa lo/ sngags 'chang/ bsod nams dbang po rnams kyi bka' 'bum dang rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis kyis lung / bcu drug la byas 'gyur du bsod nams dbang po la lam 'bras
gsan/ bcu bdun par byas 'gyur du kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen sbyin sreg dang bcas pa dang bcu dgu par bde mchog tu phur bsnyen mdzad/ nyi shu par gcung a mes zhabs dang lhan
du gdan sar phebs te bdag po dgra 'dul drung la bka' chos kha shas gnang / yab rje

gshegs skabs 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po dang / rje nyied kyis kyai dor sgrub mchod sku gdung zhugs 'bul dgongs rdzogs mdzad pa sogs bstan 'gro'i don du ma mdzad yod 'gro
yang / de skabs kyis lo rgyus zin bris zhib pa ma zhugs shing / nyung ngu 'di ni a mes zhabs kyi rnam thar nas btus pa ste gang ltar spre lo hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes bco brgyad
la zhi bar gshegs / thugs dam gsal 'debs su kyai rdor sgrub mchod dge 'dun brgya phrag tsam gyis sgrub pa dang / dgon che phra mang por mang ja zang zing gi dngos 'gyed
dang bcas pa bstsal zhing / dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi'i skabs tshogs dbur grub mchog bsod nams dbang po spyan 'dren mdzad de gdan sa chen po'i tshogs chen mor dge 'dun
khri phrag du long pa dang / skye bo'i tshogs bgrangs las 'das pa la bsnyen bkur sbyin gtong 'bul nod dngos po dpag med bcas sgrub par mdzad de/ de nas bzung lo zla'i dus
dran mchod 'bul du bla mchod sgrub mchod sogs da lha'i bar du mdzad pa yin no/ /

ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/sku'i mched zla gsum pa bstan 'gro spyi dang bye brag la phan dang bde ba'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun rlabs po che spel ba'i sku drin can mkhas dang
grub pa'i dbang phyug 'jam pa'i dbyangs sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan snyan lha'i
rnga gsang srid pa'i khongs su ldir ba de nyid ni/ spyir gyi rigs dang chos kyi che bas mngon par mtho ba'i gdung rabs rin po che 'di nyid du gang dag byon pa thams cad
ston mchog nyid dam de sras 'phags chen dam pa'i sar gnas nyag gcig ma gtogs tha mal rang rgyud pa 'byung ba'i go skabs nam yang med pa ni gzur gnas yongs kyi yid ngor
gsal ba bzhin la/ khyad par rje 'di nyid ni/ kong po gter ston rig 'dzin hUM nag me 'bar ram 'ja' tshon snying po'i gter byon/ thugs rje chen po ngan song rang grol las:
sna nam skye ba sa skya'i thil du 'byung: 'tha' dmag bzlog pa'i rten 'brel de la yod: ces dang / yang de nyid kyi gter byon mgon po ma ning gi lung byang du/ gzhan yang

zab gter 'di yi bka' babs ni: gnam sa chos 'byung 'dra ba'i sa phyogs su: sa yi ming can gsang sngags chos la mos: khyad par padma bdag la gus pa'i mi: bya yi lo pa thugs kar
sme nag ldan: 'brel tshad don ldan de la gtad rgya gyis: zhes dang sprul sku rig 'dzin padma 'byung gnas nyid long sku'i sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi skabs rgyud gsum
dregs pa'i gnyen po padma rigs kyi khro bo rta mgrin dbang gi skur bzhengs pa'i tshe ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur zhing / phyis su slob dpon padma nyid kyis rgya
gar dang bod kyi yul du rdo rje'i tha tshig gnyen pos gcun te bstan pa'i srung mar bskos pa ngo bod sa gnas dag pa'i 'khor la rnam pa gdul bya gdug pa rnams drag po'i
stobs kyi sgrol ba'i dam ldan gnod sbyin chen po tse dmar pa mi khog tu brlabs nas zhu yig phul bar/sa dkar po'i yul na rig 'dzin brgyud pa spel ba'i pho brang dam pa der
rgya nag po'i yul gyi rtse lnga nas smra ba'i seng ge'i ming du btags/ 'ja' tshugs su ldan pa'i rta pho de la zhon/ gu ru padma'i dus su zhi ba 'tsho dang bstun/ mkhas pa
shrI sidha'i ming du btags/ bkod pa yar la gcig byas na ston pa shAkya'i dus su maungga la gyi bu/ rim par brgyud pa gnam ri srong btsan de la

gces pa mgar ba'i ming / nye bar brgyud pa'i chos ni dar ba'i dus/ sgra sgyur rnams kyi gral la 'khod bar ma do yi 'ga' shes su/ rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul du sprul pa brung
/ rgya gar yul nas tshur la log bod yul sa dkar kun dga' ming can de la zlo ba/ zhes dang / yang de rjes skabs shig tu phul bar/ khri srong lde btsan dus su lo tsA ba klu'i
rgyal mtshan/ da lta'i dus su kun dga'i ming can 'di/ bstan pa rgyas shing smon lam 'phel bar 'ong / gsol ba thob cig skye 'gro sems can rnams shis par gyur cig phyis
dus klu'i ming can du skye ba blangs pa'i tshul ni dge bshes rang gi blo la gsal/ zhes dang /gzhan yang paNDi ta sgo mtha' yas pa dang kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sogs yin
pa dge bshes rang zer ma bde ba ma gtogs gdug 'dre las dge bshes rang gsal/ zhes sogs gsal bar bstan pa 'di nyid kho na khung du ma zad/ slob dpon chen po'i gter lung
gzhan dag gi shugs bstan mang po dang / rje 'di nyid kyis yongs 'dzin mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis gsung rjen par bstsal ba 'ga' zhig dang / rje nyid kyis sngon
gnas rjes dran zhal gyis bzhes pa phal cher dang / gzhan yang yol mo sprul sku la sogs sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pho mo mang po'i

thugs nyams spyan ltas su shar ba mtha' dag dgongs pa gcig par mtshungs pa'i don hril gyis dril na/ lha rigs 'khon gyi gdung brgyud dri ma med pa phal che ba dag gi sprul gzhi
'jam dpal dbyangs kho na yin pa spyi khyab ltar la khyad par ston pa'i dus su rdzu 'phrul can gyi mchog 'phags pa maunggal gyi bu dang / de dang thugs rgyud gcig pa dge
bsnyen litstsha bi gzhon nu 'jig rten thams cad kyis mthong na mngon par dga' ba dang / de rjes rgyu 'bras bya rtsol las 'das pa rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po'i bka' bab
gsum pa rig 'dzin shI sidha dang / thugs rje chen po srong btsan chos rgyal gyi 'phrul blon mi bzhi'i nang tshan 'gar stong btsan yul bzung dang / gangs can bstan pa'i
gzhi ma thub dbang gnyis pa mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho dang / de dang thugs rgyud gcig pa dge bsnyen li tstsha bi'i skye sprul lo chen cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / de dag
dang rgyud gcig rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i nang tshan mkha' la thogasamed rgyu ba sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms dang / skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang phyug gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer
dang / lo chen cog ro de nyid la slob dpon padmas khyod ma 'ongs pa na sa zhes bya bar rnal 'byor pa bsod nams rtse mo zhes bya bar 'gyur ro zhes pa ltar slon dpon rtse
mo'i zhabs dang / slob

dpon 'di nyid 'di'i gong du 'phags yul du paN chen mi thub zla ba sogs pa paNDi ta bcu gcig tu skye ba bzhes pa dang / yang sgo mtha' yas pa yin pa ltar na rje btsun rin po
che yang yin pa'i phyir sku mched thugs rgyud gcig pa dang / mkhan chen bo dhi sa twa'i rnam sprul dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / chos srid 'phrin
las gyis mnga' bdag 'khon ston theg chen chos kyi rgyal po dang / rig 'dzin shrwi sidha'i rnam 'phrul rang gzhan grub mtha'i pha rolatu son cing rdzogs chen snying tig gi
bka' bab bsam yas pa ngag gi dbang po'am kun mkhyen klong chen rab 'byam pa dang / sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms kyis yang srid rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i srog 'dzin
gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal bzang po dang / dri med thub stan smra ba'i khyu mchog 'jigs bral go ram bstan pa'i nyi ma bsod nams seng ge dang / lo chen
cog ro'i skye brgyud lung rigs smra ba'i dbang po mang thos klu grub rgya mtsho sogs rim brgyud sku phreng snga phyi dang / sku dus mnyam par thugs rgyud gcig pa'i rnam
'phrul 'gog med yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa'i mtshan can sogs mkhas dang grub pa sha stag tu byon pa de dag so so'i 'khrul spong lung khung shes byed bcas zhib
par mkhan chen

thams cad mkhyen pa bsam gtan rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i rtogs brjod chen mor gsal bas 'dir don bsdus las ma bkod la/ sku tshe 'dir yang gangs can gyi gdul bya 'dul ba'i dus la
bab pas dkar phyogs srung ma'i tshogs kyis zhing 'dir gdan drangs pa ma gtogs bar srid dag pa ye shes kyi skus 'phags yul du 'khrungs par dgongs pa gtad pa'ang / rje nyid
kyis gsung las kho bo rgya gar du skye ba len rgyu yin pa la ce spyang 'dra ba'i sems can mjug ma ring po byas pa gnyis kyis lam bkag nas rgya gar phyogs la 'gro ma thub
pa log pa zhig dran gyin 'dug gsungs pa 'di dang gnod sbyin chen pos rgya gar yul nas tshur la log ces pa'ang mtshungs par snang ngo / /de ltar sngon byung sku'i phreng
ba cha tsam dad pa'i gsos su gleng nas/ skabs don sku dngos 'di nyid kyi rnam par thar pa mdor bsdus pa sde tshan sa bcad du ma phye bar chu babs su bstan pa ni/ rje 'di
nyid rgyal yum dam pa bsod nams rgyal mo de nyid kyi lhums su zhugs nas re zhig na yum gyi mnal lam du mi smug nag ral pa'i gseb tu po ti bcings pa zhig gis yum nyid nam
mkha'i dbyings mthon por bteg nas cung zad bzhad nyams dang / sku mnga' nasagasung mi che tsam zhig lhang gis byung ba/

de tshul yab rje rin po cher zhus par/ lod rgyu rang med dpal mgon zhal gyi cho 'phrul zhig yin 'dug pas bskang gso gyis phebs pa ltar/ zhal gyi bskang ba gtso bor bton pa'i
bskang gso mdzad pa sogs gnas skabs 'di nyid nas bzung rdo rje'i chos srung rnams 'bral med du 'khor ba'i dge mtshan dang / rgyal yum nyid kyang sku khams dngas shing phal
cher ting nge 'dzin la 'byams pa dang bcas/ yab rje rin po che nyid dgung grangs sum cu rtsa lngar phebs pa gser 'phyangs zhes pa me bya lo'i hor zla dang po 'gro ba'i
bla mas cho 'phrul chen po bstan pa'i yar tshes bcu bzhi res gza' phur bu'i nyin dpal sa skya'i bla brang phun tshogs gling du ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te bltams
par/ sku dbyibs mdzes shing zhal mdangs gsal ba sogs lus can mtha' dag yid 'phrog pa'i ngo mtshar du bzhugs/ gsung mkhyen tsam na lan cig yum gyis na bza'i sbug tu
mnal bas 'od gsal gyis gzigs mor/ gzhan gyi lus ngag gi bya ba thams cad mngon sum ltar gsan gzigs byung ba mnal sad tshe gzhan la gsungs pas kun ya mtshan pa byung / 'di
nas bzung ste chos thams cad bden med sgyu mar mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyang thugs rgyud du 'bad pa med pa 'khrungs/

de mtshams yab rje nyid nas sku mched gsum ga'i slob dpon gyi tshul du ban gtsang dbu byed chen mo bsod nams lha dbang bsko gnang mdzad de 'dri klog sogs kyang tshags med du
mkhyen cing / yab chos yang phur rnam gnyis nas bzung / bde kyai sogs yi dam chos srung phal che ba'i sgrub 'phrin phyag bzhes kun la byang chub par mdzad/dgung lo lnga'i
bar du yab rje rin po che'i drung du tshe dpag lha dgu dang / rdo rje phur pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du smin byed sogs chos bka' 'ga' zhig gsan/ e waM chos ldan
nas thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gdan drangs te rje 'di nyid yab yum lhan cig pas/ tshe dpag kunarig sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis nas kha shas sogs dbang
lung 'ga' zhig gsan/dgung lo lnga pa 'phar ba zhes pa lcags glang lor sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos bzhengs par mdzad pa'i lha khang rtse'i lam 'bras bla brgyud mjal
bar phebs pa'i tshe sku 'khor rnams la nga yar theg cig dang khyod tsho la rten bshad gtong ngo phebs pa bzhin zhabs rim pas sku bteg nas da gsung bar zhu zhus pas sku gnyen
so so la phyag mdzub kyis brda' sbyar nas/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag

med ma/ birwa pa/ zhes sogs sngags 'chang chen po'i bar yongs rdzogs rim pas 'doms par mdzad pas thams cad shin tu ngo mtshar zhing gsung ngag zab mo'i bka' bab ltar du yid
ches pa byung / yang de skabs gzhan zhig tu sa paN gyi rnam thar zhal thang la'ang chos rgyal ma zhal 'don gnang ba dang bstun so sor ngo sprod stsal ba sogs sku na shin
tu phra yang mkhyen rab ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar gsal ba dang / thugs zab cing sgam la dul ba dang / mang po'i tshogs dbus su gsung mi rtab par bag yangs lhod por gnang
ba sogs blo chen rgan po'i ngang tshul 'chang bas thams cad kyis 'di ni 'jig rten gyi a mes chen po zhig go zhes bsgrags pas a mes zhabs su grags/dgung lo drug tu phebs
pa dge byed ces pa chu pho stag gi lo gsar dang khad nyer yab rje sku mched bka' bgros kyis rgyal sras dam pa sku mched gsum ga khri 'don gyi sgo shar bas/ dus mdos chen
mo yang gzab spros rgyas pa'i lugs su gnang / de mus cho 'phrul zla ba'i yar tshes bcu gsum gyi nyin gzhis byes kyis bla ma grwa rigs ngur smrig 'chang ba khri phrag tu nye
ba dang / dad 'dus mchog dman gyi skye bo pho mo gzab 'phyor bcas kyi dbus na mchod pa'i yo byad du ma dang zhabs rim chas gzab mtshar du

dngar ba dag gis mdun bdar bzhin pas/ sku mched gsum po bgres rim gyis chos kyi khri 'phang ga la bar phebs te bzhugs par/ gsung chos dngos gzhi nyin gsum ga gcen sku bgres
rje btsun mthu stobs dbang phyug zhabs nas gnang ba'i chos mtshams rnams su/ phyogs mtha'i che gnyen dmangs phal bcas kyis khri ston legs 'bul blo'i ra bar mi shong ba phul/
nyin gsum pa tshes bco lnga la yab rje rin po che nyid nas sbyin bdag gi tshul gnang ste 'jam mgon ngur smrig bzhes pa bsod nams dbang po'i zhabs tshogs dbur spyan drangs
pa dang bcas khu dbon bzhi ga bzhugs khri gcig la bzhugs nas chos 'khor thog mar bskor ba'i legs mdzad des bstan 'gro spyi'i phan bde gong 'phel du 'gyur ba dang /
skabs de'i 'brel thogs rnams kyis dge rtsa rdzogs byang du bsngo ba'i bden tshig rdo rje'i smon lam dang phyogs kun tu bkra shis kyi me tog sil mas khyab par mdzad/ gzhan
yang de skabs kyi zang zing gi dngos po phal che ba zhig de 'phral nas mchod sbyin gyi yul so sor dga' ston du stsal ba sogs gangs can gyi ljongs su rdzogs ldan gyi nyi
ma ring du shar ba mdzad pa yin no/ /de skabs nyin rjes ma'i gsung bsngo'i mjug tsam la rje 'di nyid nas nges 'byung gi rnam pas spyan chab dang bcas 299"/>a ne a ne zhes
btud mar gsungs ba zhig byung ba phyis su rtog dpyod byung tshe mnga' ris gong ma'i khri lcam rin chen bu khrid zhes sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i sras mo rje 'di nyid
kyis a ne drung gshegs pa dang dus 'grig pas kun ha las par gyur to/ /de nas lo ngo gnyis kyi ring la rgyud gzhung mang po zhig thugs 'dzin dang / rdo rje phur pa'i cho
ga'i khrigs kyi dbyangs rol bris thig sogs la byang chub par mdzad/ skabs shig sku khams cung ma bde ba'i tshe mnal lam zhig tu bud med dmar smug 'jigs gzugs lcags kyi
sbar mo can zhig gis 'ded pa'i thugs snang byung bar/ rje nyid ring stabs su bros phebs pa'i skas zhig 'dug par 'dzegs phebs te thog mkhar phebs dgongs pa dang / bud med
de'i zin la nye ba'i mtshams/ skas mgo de nas mi bong che ba zhig gis phyag nas 'then te bde bar phebs pa zhig byung ba/ dmag zor ma'i cho 'phrul zhig tu 'dug kyang rigs
kyi srung ma gzhan gyis bar gcod srung ba'i ltas bzhin bsnyun yang seng dngas byung /dgung lo bcu pa la 'jam gon bsod nams dbang po phu ri nas spyan drangs te/ yab sras
bzhi gas gtsos chos sde lho byang

gi dge 'dun pa mang rab dang bcas la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ sa lo dang / sngags 'chang chen po/ bsod nams dbang po nyid bcas kyi bka' 'bum rnams dang / rtsa rgyud 'phags chen
bcas kyi lung sogs rgya cher gsan/dgung lo bcu gcig pa spre'u zhes pa me lug lor 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs kyi drung nas rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i yang snying gsung ngag
rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa gsan bzhed kyis yab sras bzhi ga chibs bteg te byas 'gyur du phebs/ lo de'i dbo zla'i tshes brgyad nyin chos thun dbu tshugs par nam
mkha' la 'ja' gur sum tshom gyi dbus su rje btsun dkar po rnam gsum bzhugs pa yab sras thun mong gis gzigs pa dang / me tog gi char sogs dge mtshan brjod du mi langs pa
byung / de skabs bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang bka'i sta gon gyi nub yab rje nyid kyi mnal lam du rgyal yum bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid de nyid khri mthon po zhig la
bzhugs nas yab rje nyid sogs slob tshogs mang por chos 'khor yun ring skor ba zhig mtshan lam du shar bas phyir nang snga mor rje 'di nyid yab kyi drung du phebs ma thag
nged la mdang sum rmi lam ngo mtshar ba byung / sngags 'chang chen po de nyid kyai rdo rje dang / rgyal yum de nyid bdag med ma

dngos yin pa'i brda' ru 'dug cing / khyed kyang nga'i yum de'i sprul sku yin 'dug pas mdang sum khyod la ngas chos zhus so zhes sogs kyang stsal/ 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs
nas rje 'dir khyad par can gyi thugs gtsigs gnang zhing / yab rje rgyan drung gi phyag phyi khong khri thog rgan 'bring gnyis kyis ma chog pa mi 'dug pas/ khyed rang nga'i
phyi la phyiin/ dbus gtsang gi sa dgon che chung rnams dang / sbyin bdag sde dpon che phra kun la nged kyis ngo sprod byas/ ma 'ongs pa na dbus gtsang gi bla gcig ma byed
pa yin mod ces yang yang gsungs pa phyis su rje 'di nyid kyis gdan sa'i thugs khur bsnams nas bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad pa la dgongs pa'i gsung yin 'dug cing /
de skabs khrid kyi dngos gzhi dang / rgyab rten lung gi rim pa sogs dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos spyi bye brag snyan brgyud kyi rim pa lhag med du bzhes nas bstan pa'i srog
shing 'dzin par mdzad/ khyad par sngags 'chang chen po'i rnam thar ljags lung gsan tshe thugs dad bcos min 'khrungs te/ sngags 'chang chen po sbugs rwa bsnams pa zhig dang
mjal e yongs dgongs mi med pa rnams su lan mang phebs bzhugs mdzad pa yin zhes gsung /rje nyid dgung lo bcu gnyis bzhes pa phur bu te sa sprel

lor yab sras bzhi char byas 'gyur tu 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs kyi spyan sngar phebs/ rgyal sras rin po che sku mched gsum ga gzhi bsnyen sku mtshams dam par gnang / 'jam
mgon sku mched gnyis kyang bsnyen rgyab kyis tshul du bzhugs/ de skabs rje 'di'i mnal lam du gzim khang gi ngos la 'ja' 'dra ba'i kha dog khra chem me ba yid du 'ong ba zhig
gi khrod na/ yi dam gyi rigs mang po zhig sku brnyan gsal rgyu rang med pa dang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma shin tu gsal ba zhig gzigs pas de ni bde bar gshegs pa
khri chen de nyid kyis dus mchod la bdag med ma'i sgrub mchod gsar du tshugs pa 'di'i ltas yin 'dra zhes phyis gsungs pa dang / yang mnal ltas su dzo ki gnyis byung ste
nged kyis khyed la gser 'gyur gyi rtsi 'chos lugs 'bul zer ba ltar rje nyid nas zhib par mkhyen snang zhig byung ba ni sgyu lus kyi lcags khams la rim gnyis kyi rtsi thebs
pas zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi gser khams 'grub pa'i brda' rtags ngo mtshar ba dang / gzhan yang sngon dus rdzu 'phrul phug gi glad de na nyin bzhin yong ba'i rbab lam
zhig yod phyis 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabasakyis sgrub sde nyams gso mdzad skabs pu tra la bka' bsgos te re zhig nas rbab lam chad pa yin kyang / de skabs rje

'di'i che ba ston byed ltar du gzim chung theg mchog yang rtser mdzad yod pa'i steng la/ rbab mi tshad tsam zhig 'ur sgra dang bcas phog par/ yab rje sogs kyis gsan pa dang
thugs shin tu zhed nas rje 'di bzhugs sar phebs par/ rje nyid thugs g.yo med du bzhugs 'dug pa'i sku la nyams nga lta ci/ gzims khang gi dral lcam la yang skyon ma dmigs
pas yab rje 'khor bcas thugs ngo mtshar ba mdzad pa sogs drod tshad can gyis dus grangs mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa kha skong sbyin sregs dang bcas gegs med phun tshogs su grub
nas slar yang gdan sar phebs/dgung lo bcu bzhir son pa thun mong zhes pa lcags khyi lor nges 'byung gi dgongs pa brtan po thugs la 'khrungs te thog mar 'jam mgon sa skya
paNDi tar bzhed don gegs med 'grub pa'i gsol 'debs dngos grub mchog stsol zhes pa gsung rtsom gyi thog ma de nyid gnang nas rim gyis lo de nyid kyi zla ba gsum pa'i dkar
phyog tshes dus legs par dpal sa skya'i dbu rtse rnying ma'i gtsug lag tu sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i sku gdung gi drung / bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyis gtsug phud
phul ba'i ston pa'i sku brnyan gyi spyan sngar/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'jam mgon byams pa dpal ngag dbang bsod

dbang po las so thar dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa tshul bzhin du bzhes par mdzad do/ /der 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs nas legs so'i gnang char rten gsum du ma dang
mar me sbar ba dung gcig gzhan yang zang zing gi dngos po rgya chen po rnams gnang nas dung de bus shig phebs par de bzhin mdzad pas skad che bar thon pa sogs rten 'brel
de rnams kyis brda' don ni phyis su rje 'di'i bstan pa rin po che ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa'i mthus mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi grags snyan rgya mtsho'i gos can khyab pas
ris bral skye rgu'i bla mar 'gyur ba'i dge mtshan dang / sngags 'chang chen po'i sku gdung gi drung du rab byung mdzad pa ni slar gangs can phan bde'i rtsa lag tu gos dkar
lcang lo'i brtul zhugs bzhes dgos kyi mtshan mar gsal lo/ /de mtshams re zhig nas 'jam mgon de nyid dang rje 'di sku mched bcas khu dbon bzhi gas bde mchog pho brang
du yab chos rdo rje phur pa'i gsung bsnyen mthar phyin gnang / de dus rje 'di'i mnal lam du lha chen lcags ri la zhabs skor mdzad cing 'dug par lho lcog gi thad mdun phebs
skabs lha khang bla brang gi ngos la 'ja' 'od kyis dbus su thub dbang gnas brtan gnas

g.yog rgyal chen bzhi bcas shin tu gsal ba dang / sa skya'i shang ri gra chung gong khar grags pa'i rtse mor rje btsun birwa pa'i sku shin tu che ba phyag gnyis chos 'chad
can zhabs skyil krung gi zhabs pus g.yas pa ri'i phag tu song nas mi mngon pa/ 'ja' sngon po'i 'od skor la rgyab rten nas bzhugs pa yang gzigs shing de dang mthun pa'i sku
stod 'phags mchog ma mdzad/dgung lo bcu drug pa chu byi lo dang bcu bdun pa chu glang lo gnyis kar dbus gtsang du sde 'khrug langs pas chos rgyal chen po g.yas ru byang
pa/ shar kha ba/ rin spungs ba/ rtse chen pa sogs dang / dbus nas yang rgyab dpon chen/ mnga' ris nas gung thang rgyal po'i chab 'og gi rgyal phran du ma sogs dmangs 'bebs
dang zing lhong che bar byung skabs/ rje 'di nyid nas bstan 'gro'i phan bder dgongs pa'i smon lam dang chos srung rnams la 'phrin bcol lan grangs stsal bas chos rgyal
rgyal phran bcas rnams la yang ha cang rgya ma che rung 'khul tshod kyis chab 'bangs dum bu dang bcas zhod 'jags bde bar bzhugs chog par byung ba yang rje 'di'i sku drin
du nges/ 'dii skabs gcen sgar chen khams phyogs su phebs/ rje 'di sku mched gnyis gan par bdag po dgra 'dul drung gi spyan drangs ngor phebs te zhal ngo rnams la

'dod chos kyi bdud rtsi ngom par stsal/ rje nyid dgung lo bcu bdun du phebs par chu glang gi lor sgar chen khams nas phebs te mtshungs bral rdo rje 'chang mus chen sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan mjal bar phebs gong du yab rje nas gsung shog gnang ba'i lan mus chen rje nas zhu shog tu/ 'di kha'i mkhan po 'os rigs zhabs drung sku gzhon par shar lags
pas zhes sogs dang / sgar chen dang stabs gcig tu phebs gnang thugs rje che ba mkhyen lags zhes sogs dang / rje nyid la zhu shog de dang dbyibs 'dra la 'dir 'byon gong
sngags 'chang chen po'i dngul gdung la snyan dar dang / sgo rum bskyed ltas su bskang gso brgya rtsa zhig cis kyang mdzad nas phebs pa zhu/ zhes sogs 'byor ba'i rkyen byas/
sku tshe snga ma'i 'brel pas gang gi mtshan tsam gsan pa nyid nas rje 'di nyid kyi thugs la dad spro bzod du med pa kho na dang / de rjes rgyal yum bsod nams rgyal mo
de nyid ngam ring mi dbang chen po mjal bar phebs tshe/ rje nyid nas mus chen zhabs drung du gsung shog phul bar/ bdag gi tshe ha cang mi ring ba zhig byung na thos bsam
rgya cher byas pa la don mi 'dug pas tshe ring thung gang 'ong dang / thog mar mdo sngags gang la sbyangs na legs dang / dbu zhwa sogs sku drag phog

pa'i na bza' zhig byin rten du gnang ba dang / sems la phan pa'i bslab ston zhig gnang bar zhu sogs phul ba'i gsung lan du/ sku phywa btab pas sku tshe ring po yong bar gda'/
thugs sbyongs sngon ma mdo mdzad pa dga'/ thugs sbyong gnang gong mi g.yo ba dkang po'i bsnyen pa zhig mdzad na legs par gda' lags/ thugs dam slob gnyer sogs gang mdzad
kyang thugs rtse dkon mchog la gtad/ nges 'byung drag pos rgyud bskul/ sems can thams cad kyi don du sangs rgyas thob 'dod kyi bsam pas mdzad dgos zhes sogs dang / zhwa
mo sogs bdag gi dri phog pa ni 'bul ma nus zhes sogs gnang 'dug de rjes rje 'di nyid kyis mnal lam zhig tu/ byas 'gyur bla brang nub kyi rje btsun chen po'i chos khri na/
rje bla ma mus pa chen po yin zhu ba'i gzi byin can phyag na mi rkang gi gling bu 'bud bzhin pa zhig gi 'di bus pas mgon po mthong yod gin gda' gsung bar/ rje 'dis rkang
gling de bzhes nas 'bud par mdzad pa na skad kyang ha cang ma byung zhing / chos skyong yang gzigs rgyu ma byung mur bla ma de'i mdun nas chu chen po zhig thol gyi rdol
byung bar/ rje nyid kyis sa skyong sogs thabs mkhas kyi bskyil ba'i rdzing bu che tshad gcig byung 'phral nyi ma yang zer gyis bzhud song ba 'dra zhig

byung ba dang mnal sad pas/ ci 'dra zhig yin dgongs pa byung yang / phyis su rkang gling skad cher ma byung ba sogs ni rje mus chen de nyid la chos skyong gi bskor rag bsdus
shig las ma gsan pa dang / chu rdol ba dang rdzing bskyil ba sogs ni gzhan bde kyai gsang gsum sogs zab chos mu mtha' med pa zhig gsan pa dang / nyi ma nub pa ni rgyal
yum de nyid sku ma gshegs bar rje mus chen de nyid ma mjal ba'i rtags su 'dug gsungs/ 'on kyang nyi ma nub pa'i brda' don 'di rje nyid nas rang bstod du 'gyur dogs kyi dgongs
pa can gyi gsung stsal ba ma gtogs/ chu rdol nas rdzing bskyil grub pa dang nyi ma nub pa de nyid mus chen nyid nas zab chos zhal lung cig brgyud kyi rim pa mtha' dag
bum pa gang byo'i tshul du rje 'di nyid la 'bul bar mdzad nas thugs kyi rdzing du bskyil grub pa dang dgongs pa rdzogs te zhi bar gshegs pa'i rtags mtshan ngo mtsha rar
snang ngo / /de nas mi ring bar glang lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bco lngar rgyal yum de nyid sku gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs gsung tshog lam ston sogs zhu ba dang stabs
gcig mus chen gyi drung du gsung shog phul te/ rje nyid kyis mjal thub min sogs brtag pa zhus par gegs med mjal ba'i lung bstan gsal por gnang /

dgung lo bco brgyad du phebs pa kun dga' zhes pa shing stag lo nang du rje mus pa chen po nas yab rje dang rje nyid la'ang zhu shog nan can dang stab gcig dpon chen rin chen
klu dbang dpon g.yog rnams rje nyid spyan 'dren du 'byor bas yab rje sku mched nas kyang dgongs khrol gyi phebs sgo ltar/ byas 'gyur du 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs kyi drung
du byin rlabs zhu bar phebs bka' bsgo bslab ston sogs lhug stsol gnang / de mthun gdan sa nas yab sras gsum char nas kyang thugs 'phreng ba'i gsung dang skabs babs kyi
zhal ta gnang sbyin rgya chen dang bcas lo de'i zla ba dgu pa'i gzhug tu gdan sa nas chibs btegs te/ yongs 'dzin dam pa mjal 'dod kyi thugs bzhed grub pa'i spro nyams
dang bcas rim gyis mus gnas gsar du phebs pa'i tshe/ de skabs sde gzar gyi rkyen la brten yar rgyab dpon chen de phyoT su byon yod pas/ chibs bsu dang bcas pho brang gi rtser
spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur 'bul nod rgya cher byung zhing / phyir tshe dbang sogs 'dod chos du mas rjes 'dzin gnang / de nas kyang phebs te sang rje bla ma dang mjal
rgyu'i nyi/ rab 'byams chos rje ba sogs 'ga' zhig sngon du gnang ste/ rje rin po che khyed bdag rang gi skye ba mang po'i bla ma yin snyam pa'i nges shes

lhang lhang de ka yod pa dang / 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug gi dbu bla yin pa sogs gang sa nas bdag tshor bsu ba la phebs pa dang / phyag len mdzad pa gtan nas mi gnang
ba zhu zhes bka' khyab mdza pa bzhin/ khong rnams kyis gsol bas/ rje'i gsungs las/ a pha de 'dra ci gsungs pa yin/ kar 'brug dge ldan pa sogs kyi grwa slob bu chen rnams
ni khong rang tsho'i sprul skur grags pa re byon pa la la lung mang po brgal nas 'jal du 'gro zhing/ dngos po gang yod 'bul thub pa la dga' spro chen po byed srol bzang
po zhig yod 'dug kyang / rang re sa skya pa'i grwa slob rnams dad gus pho rus shin tu chung bar brten/ skyes bu dam pa gser gyi pha phong sgo 'grim du byon yang ji mi
snyam du 'dug mod/ gang ltar sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud dri ma med pa byon pa la rang re rnams phyag mi 'tshal na gzhan su la'ang tshal ba yin sngar gyis bsam pa la nga rgas
kyang gru gu 'phrang du phebs bsu la yong bsam pa yod kyang / zhabs drung gi dgongs pa la gtan nas med phyin/ da cha bla brang gi nub kyi 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyi chos
khri chos rwa dang bcas pa'i sa der phebs bsu la yong ba yod zhus shig de ring gza' skar bzang ngan ci yod kyang ltos pa med mdangs nub mo nged rang sa skya zhabs drung
dang gnyid

dang 'od gsal 'dres pa'i ngang nas zhib par mjal byung ste khong sku bong che chung ran pa/ zhal dkyil zlum shing dkar la dmar shas che ba'i mdangs dang ldan pa/ spyan gnyis
zlum shing che ba/ shangs gzeng mtho zhing chu sgros legs pa/ zhal sma ra dang zhal brgyan khyug ge yod pa/ sku gzan smug cing sku chos ser ba bzhes pa zhig gsal bar mthong
byung zhes sogs dgyes spro'i gsung du ma stsal/ de nas rje nyid dpon slob nye char phebs tshe der bzhugs 'dus tshogs kyi ser phreng gi phebs bsu gzab par zhus nas 'jam
pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi chos rwar phebs pa'i tshe dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nyid ngur smrig gi bla gos bzhes pa mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan de nyid thugs
dgyes spro dang byin rlabs kyi gzi byiin nyi ma ltar 'bar ba mjal ma thag rje 'di nyid kyis thugs snang gi rtog pa phra rags thams cad 'gags nas lhan skyes spros bral
gyi yi shes ngang la re zhig had der lus par/ sku 'khor rnams kyis snyan bskul zhus pas sad de/ thog mar rje mus chen nas phyag gsum mdzad ring la/ rje 'dis dad pa'i yus
kyis phyag dgu btud du gnang / mjal dar dang bcas byin rlabs dbu mnyam rtse sprod lugs dgongs kyang rje nyid kyi dbu mus chen gyi dbu 'og tu chug nges shig mdzad rgyu byung
bas

thugs tshim par gyur/ de nas bla brang dbang khang du dpon slob nyung bsdus shig la bzhugs gral gnang ring / yas phyir gsung gleng zhib rgyas dang / khyad par rje nyid nas
snga sor gdan sar bka' shog rim 'byor bzhin dang len dang / lta par bdag rang chung ngu nas mgon po khyed kyi zhal mjal gsung thos dus shig nam 'ong ngam bsam pa bzhin/ da
lan rten 'brel phun tshogs 'di bzhin 'grig pas dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos 'khor lo bde chog lu nag dril gsum nA ro mkha' spyod dang bcas pa'i chos skor sogs zhu dgos yod
pa rnams thugs rjes 'dzin par zhu zhes gsung par/ rje mus pa'i gsung las de bzhin ngo mtshar che/ rang re'i gling kha bde ba can gyi dgon ma bu 'di rnams sngon mus chen
sems dpa' chen pos 'di phyogs kyi bya ri dwags nya sgo nga sogs sems can mgon skyabs med pa rnams kyi mgon skyabs su 'debs par mdzad pa nas bzung da lta'i bar du'ang sa
skya pa'i sngags phyogs kyi bshad sgrub bstan pa'i rgyun gzhan las khyad par du 'phags ngos shes pa ma nyams gong 'phel du yod pa 'di legs shing / da ni nged kha rgas lus
gog pa la brten 'dzin bkod de 'dra thub pa'i re ba mi 'dug pas/ dgon gnas 'di rnams khyed sa skya pa'i phyag tu ma 'phrod na dus kyi dbang gi

gzhan su yin gyi zin pa med pas/ zhabs drung nas sa skya'i bstan pa dang / sems can gyi don la khur chen po bzhes nas dgon ma bu 'di rnams zhal bdag gnang ngos lugs gnyis kyi
skyong dar tshul bzhin du mdzad na/ bla ma gong ma'i dgongs pa'ang de gas rdzogs/ nga rgan po'i bsam pa'ang de gas 'grub cing / 'dod chos 'dra dgos gsungs pa/ spyir yang
chos don du gnyer ba 'byung na rang gi gang yong byed pa'i lugs su yod cing / khyad par khyed dgur lo bco brgyad pa sku na phra mo 'di lta bus nged rgan po bsam nas 'di
phyogs su phebs pa ni bka' drin tshad med pas brkyangs pas chos nged rang la yod pa rnams 'bul gang thub rang cis kyang zhu lags zhes sogs dgyes spro'i gsung 'phros gnang
ba'i skabs de dag tu'ang spyan ras shangs kyi rtse mor gzim bur gzigs shing / thugs dam ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyun la yug re 'byams 'gro ba gzigs pas rje 'di'i dgongs pa
la snyan grags dang mthun pa'i bla ma dam pa 'di lta bu dang mjal ba re legs dgongs pa'i dgyes spro tshad med pa zhig 'khrung par gyur to/ /de nas zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes
gsum dkar po nam gru'i 'grub sbyor nyin gling ga bde ba can gyi 'dus tshogs la bla brang de nyid nas mang ja zung 'brel zhig gnang ba'i snga ma'i tshe rje mus

chen nyid tshog dbur phebs par/ rje nyid nas bstan 'gro spyi bye brag gi phan bde la dgongs pa'i gsung bsngo rin po che zhu rten 'bul nod rgya chen dang 'dus tshogs la'ang
dam rdzas ril bus gtsos pa'i 'bul 'gyed gya nom pa stsal/ mus chen nyid nas 'dus tshogs la nged nas sa skya zhabs drung 'di bzhin spyan drangs thub pa yin pas mus nang gi
lha sde mi sde kun la nged drin che ba yod cing / da ni/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas bzhugs bzhin du/ /ston pa gzhan la gus byed pa/ /yan lag brgyad ldan chu 'gram du/ /ba tsha'i
khron pa brko ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yin pas nyi ma de ring nas bzung khyed lha mi kun gyi phyag dang mchod pa 'bul sa/ lugs gnyis kyi bslab bya zhu sa sogs thams
cad sa skya zhabs drung kho na la gyis shig sogs dgyes spro'i bslab bya mang du stsal/ de nas mang ja rjes ma'i thog rje di nyid tshogs dbu bzhugs khrir phebs te/ rje
mus chen nyid nas bkra shis lha'i reg bya dkar po'i tshes dang bcas rgyal ba tshe dpag med kyi sku brnyan phyag nas phyag tu phul bas mtshon zang zing gi 'bul nod rgya chen
po dang bcas mnga' gsol shis brjod kyi me tog sil mas phyogs kun bkang/ rje nyid nas kyang yon bshad spyi 'gre las kyang lhag tu gnas dang gnas min gyi dbye ba sogs

lung rigs 'thad ldan gyi legs bshad gsar pas mdun bsus te 'phags dang so skye'i tshogs kyis bsod nams su byas pa mtha' dag rdzogs byang du bsngo bar mdzad pas der 'dus thams
cad 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul par yid ches pa byung / 'dus tshogs la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang zhig kyang stsal/ de nas kyang nyin gsum gyi ring la bla brang
gi phyi nang phyag rdzas thams cad rtsis 'bul zhus nas gdan tshab tu mnga' gsol ba bzhin bzhes/ slar yang gling kha'i dge 'dun tshogs pa rnams la rdo rje phur pa stod
las kyi dbang dang / dgyes rdor rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa'i lung sogs dbang lung tshan cher stsal/ de rjes rim gyis rje 'di nyid kyis mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa'i drung
nas dbang bka' rnam grangs bcu bdun tsam dang / bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid rim rgyas pa bcu lhag dang / de dag gi rgyab brten lung gi rnam grangs shin tu mang po dang man ngag
snyan brgyud du ma sogs zab chos kyi rgya mcho bzhes par mdzad pa'i tshe bde mchog gi dbang gsan pa'i nub mo mnal lam du rje nyid skyed mo'i tshal zhig na bzhugs 'dug
par/ de ma thag sa skya'i lha khang chen mo'i shar phyogs seng ldeng sgo khra'i thad der bla ma gong ma'i phyag dril dril smyon du grags pa de dkrol bas de'i skad kyis lha
khang chen mo

mer gyis khengs snyam zhig byung ba phyis kyi rten 'brel brda rtags khyad par can du snang / yang de skabs mnal lam zhig tu sgo rum gyi snyan dar rnams yab rje rin po ches
rje nyid la rtsis sprod gnang ba zhig byung bas nang par mus chen la zhu bar mdzad par/ rje'i gsungs las/ rmi lam shin tu bzang / rigs kyi bu la brgyud kyi lha mgo zer ba
de gda'/ byed pa mis byed kyang mdun ma lhas bsgyur ba zhig dgos pa yin khyed rang bsod nams che bas thams cad dbang du 'du zhing / dpal 'byor longs spyod kyang blos mi
'khyud pa tsam dang / sa skya pa kun gyi re ltos 'chol ba zhig 'ong bas de dus 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud 'di rnams gsang sngags bde chen gling du rgyud 'don thabs rgyas
pa re rtsom la 'dzugs thub pa mdzod ces sogs phyis su chos srid bstan pa'i gdugs dkar srid rtser 'degs pa'i lung bstan brda chos mang du gnang / da lo dbus gtsang spyir
'brum nad byung skabs/ gling kha phyogs su'ang shin tu thu bar byung bas/ rje mus chen zhabs nas da lan gyi 'brum pa 'di re lod du 'dug pas zhabs drung nyid nas grwa pa tshor
sna tshogs yum sogs kyi rjes gnang 'dra gnang na legs par 'dug gsungs pa bzhin du tshogs chen la/ gur

mgon dpa' gcig sna tshogs yum/ ri khrod lo ma gyon ma gsum gyi rjes gnang dang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i na bza' dang bcas tshogs pa thams cad la byin rlabs mdzad
pas dgon pa'i 'brum nad rbad chad cing / de skabs su na ba rnams kyang thar bar gyur pas/ rta mo lung pa dang / skyer pa sogs su'ang spyan 'dren zhus pa ltar khrom dbang
mdzad pas nad 'phro chad cing na mu las thar ba sogs ya mtshan dpag tu med pa byung / de nas yun mi ring bar byang pa chos rgyal ngam ring du phebs nas khyab bdag mus pa
chen po dang rje 'di nyid yab sras lhan cig ngam ring du phebs dgos kyi snyan gsol bskyar ma byung bar/ rje'i zhal nas/ kho bo tshe mjug 'dir bsgrub pa rtse gcig tu byed
pa 'di bzhag nas rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi spyan 'dren byung yang mi 'gro ba'i blo thag bcad pa yin pas/ sde sris kyis zhus pa bzhin khyed dpon slob phebs la bstan 'gro'i
don rgya cher mdzad dgos gsungs pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes te phebs bsu cha ba'i tshe dpon slob gnyis ka gzim chung du phebs te mthar thug snying po'i nyams len rgyud sde'i
gnad 'gag du ma zhig lhug stsol gnang bas/ rje nyid kyis thugs la tshe 'dir gdams ngag 'di rnams bsgom nas grub rtags thon pa byed dgos snyam pa

'khrungs/ de rjes brgyud pa'i byin rlabs dang chos srung la bka' bsgo spyi sger gyi bslab ston phun sum tshogs pa stsal te 'bral mi phod pa'i dad spro dang thugs brtse'i ngang
nas chibs bteg te/ ya ma bde ldan dang / rdzong dga' ldan rtse gnyis su zhag shas re bzhugs nas dge 'dun rnams la 'dod chos re skong du stsal/ mus gnas gsar du yar rgyab
dpon chen dang / mdog lhun sdings su sku zhang gdong kha bas spyan drangs ngor so sor phebs te tshe dbang rjes gnang sogs rkyen sel gyi chos bka' legs par gnang / bsnyen
bkur 'bul nod phun sum tshogs pa byung / de nas kyang mdog gzhung gi lu phu/ sgyi chu/ gzhis dgon/ ya ga chos sdings rnams su rim pas phebs te bla ma grwa rigs rnams
kyii 'dod mthun dbang bka' rjes gnang sogs re ba khengs par gnang / ngam ring du rje btsun ngag dbang chos 'dzoms dpon g.yog sogs la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor rjes/ skya bo
kha gdangs su phebs te mi dbang chos kyi dbang phyug de nyid la tshe dbang rigs mi gcig pa brgya tshar du ma dang / rgyal sras lam bzang sogs dbang lung du mas smin grol
gnang tshe chos rgyal de nyid kyang dad spro gting nas g.yos te bsnyen bkur 'bul ba rgya chen po dang bcas da dung gdan sa zhal ngo rnams dang / mus chen sogs

nas bka' chos lhag med gsan nas chos kyi mdzod bzung ste nged tshos zhu gang 'dod bla ma gzhan 'tshol mi dgos par mdzad nas rim gyis rjes su 'dzin par gsol 'debs phul/ de nas
rim phebs kyis gdan sar phebs nye'i tshe/ yab rje rin po che nas gsung shog phebs par/ da lam khyed rang phyogs su 'gro don la byon pa'i thog ma yin pa'i rten 'brel la
bsam ste ser phreng rta bsu sogs rgyas pa'i grabs gshom byas yod pas/ de mthun gyi phebs lugs dgos zhes gnang 'dug pa gzigs pas thugs spro bzhin pa'i ngang nas byon par/
thog mar chebs bsu ba rnams dang / de nas lho byang gi dge 'dun rnams kyi ser phreng gi bkod pa ya mtshan pa dang bcas gzhi thog bla brang du phebs/ gzim chung rab gsal
du yab sras bzhi ga stabs gcig pas yun mi thung bar gzis byes kyi zhal 'phros rgya cher mdzad/ phyir nyin rje nyid la phyag rdzas gang byung yab rje'i zhabs drung du phul
nas gdan phab ste 'gro don 'phrin las kyi rgyun skyong bzhin pa'i ngang nas shing yos lor chos skyong gi gdams skor rnams nyams bzhes gnang skabs mnal lam du/ sku 'khor
zhig gi shar phyogs la gzigs par bskul ba bzhin rje nyid kyi gra chung gi rtse phyogs la gzigs pas nam mkhar 'ja' sprin dang sprin

nag me 'bar ba bcas kyi dbus na gur mgon gtso bo'i sku shin tu gsal zhing lha brgyad 'khor rnams lam pa zhig gzigs pa la brten thugs rgyud la nyams rtogs khyad par can yang
lhag par 'khrungs/ de nas me 'brug gi lor lan gcig yab rje'i zhal nas do nub kha ton grub mtshams nged kyi rtsar shog dang lab rgyu zhig yod gnang ba ltar byon pas/ gong
nas bkra shis pa'i lha dar zung 'brel/ bzang gos lu hang yug dkar yug gcig rnams stsal nas/ 'o da lam lab rgyu'i snying po dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa la gdan sa chen
po 'di nyid kyi 'dzin skyong las khag che ba mi 'dug 'di'i 'dzin skyong yang zhal ngo na rim bzhin gyis gzhon pa la bka' bab pa zhig yod pa dang / lhag par bsam yas chos
skyong chen pos kyang / rdo rje gdan gyi 'dzin skyong rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam 'phrul gyi gzhon pa de la bka' bab yod do zer ba thang gnyis nged rang la yi ge byung ba
sogs gang nas bsam kyang khyed kyis rab byung gi brtul zhugs 'dii dor nas nged rang bzhin bgyis na/ nga yang bsam pa de gas rdzogs shing / nged rang gi gzugs pos nam lcogs
bar khur yang len pa dang / de ltar byas na rang re la dgra gnyen grogs gsum sus kyang bsam ngan sbyor rtsub kyis mi tshugs shing / nged kyis kyang

sngags 'chang chen po'i bka' chems snying la bcang nas/ gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong gi ched du phyi nang gsang gsum nas yid chad gtong ba mang po byung yang bzod rang bsam bsran
bskyed pas sa skya ming ma stong tsam byung ba yin/ da cha khyed kyis nged la mi nyan par 'dzin skyong mi byed na/ nga yang su la bsam nas sdod/ gang na'ang nged kyi sngags
'chang chen po'i bka' chems blos ma thongs pa bzhin/ nged kyi ngag kyang khyed kyis mi gcog pa byed dgos/ de bzhin ma byas na gong ma ye shes kyi spyan ldan rnams kyang
thug khrel 'gro/ da lta blo thag chod chod ltar byas gdung spel ma byas kyang / nga yang gzugs gshis ngan pa dang yun ring e sdod mi shes pas/ bzhi thog bla brang gi gtsug
lag khang dang / rten gsar bzhengs/ nged kyi blo la ji ltar yod pa 'di rnams kyi mjug khyed la bsgril dgos pa yong zhes sogs gsungs pas rje nyid re zhig thugs yed yed
por gyur nas gsung 'byon rgyu ma byung bar lus/ de mtshams nas zhal ras spyan chab kyis sbags bzhin pas bdag gi sa nas gong bzhugs zhabs drung gi bka' gang phebs zhu ba
las ma 'das 'dug kyang / spyir 'jig rten dang 'brel pa'i 'dzin skyong bdag gis mi shes shing / lhag par khyim bdag dang lhan cig gnas pa bdag gi blo la med nges dgongs par

mnga' ba ltar lags pas/ bdag rang gi cha nas chos mthun gyi kha ton gang 'phel dang / ci nus kyi 'chad nyan bgyid pa sogs kyi sgo nas zhabs tog bsgrub chog pa zhig dang / deng
sang zhal bkod gnang ba'i bzhi thog gi lha khang rten bzhengs rnams kyang mthar phyin pa zhig los yong du 'dug pa/ gong bzhugs rang da dung lo brgyar spyi dgos bstan
pa dang sems can gyi don la zhabs pad brtan pa'i thugs 'dun gnang dgos pa'i tshul rgyas par zhu bar mdzad kyang lan gang yang ma gnang bas/ gdan sa'i khur bzhes dgos kyi
bka' stsal bzhin de lo'i kyai rdor dang phur sgrub kyi chog dpon la phebs nas slob ma rjes 'dzin sogs gnang / de dus phur pa'i dbang yon du rgyal ba byams pa'i sku brnyan
li ma byon gtsang zhig 'bul mi byung bar yab rje'i drung du gzigs pa phul bas gsung las/ 'di rten 'brel legs/ byams pa'i bstan pa ma shar bar du gdung spel byas nas sdod
zer ba'i rten 'brel yin gsung nas dgyes tshor gnang / de lo stan mjug gling ga bde ba can gyi dus chos gnang dgos dang / rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas chos 'phro 'ga' zhig
gsan dgos bcas kyi mus phyogs su chibs bsgyur ba'i lam bar du/ ngam ring chos rgyal nas spyan 'dren pa 'byor ba bzhin

phebs nas chos rgyal 'khor bcas dang chos sde'i bla grwa rags bsdus bcas la dbang bka' rjes gnang lung sogs so so'i skal ba bzhin stsal/ 'di skabs shig tu yab rje nas gdan
sa'i 'dzin skyong khag che tshul ngos kyi gleng ba ltar yin zhes sogs kyi bka' shog phebs par brten ngam ring phyogs kyi thugs brel myur chod mdzad nas mus su phebs par phebs
bsu sngar lugs ltar gyis mus chen dang mjal ba'i tshe rje nyid nas snga sor rags rim thob kyang / da lan gsung ngag cha lag yongs rdzogs mtha' chod pa gcig gnang dgos
tshul zhus par mus chen gyi zhal nas/ gser kha bdag po'i dper 'dug pas/ lam 'bras cha lag dang bcas pa zhig cis kyang 'bul spro zhing / de gong zhabs drung nas tshogs chen
la bka' chos zhig gnang dgos zhes gsungs par rje 'dis de kha'i 'dus tshogs dang / gzhan don gnyer mang po bcas la/ tshe 'phel dkar po sogs rjes gnang bcu phrag gsum lhag
so so'i yig cha'i lung bcas gzhan yang dbang lung du ma zhig gnang grub mtshams/ mus chen zhal snga nas kyis/ gsung ngag chen po che cha lag bcas pa/ man ngag gi gnad/
lag len phra mo'i zur rgyan dang bcas mtha' dag dpyis phyin shin tu smin par stsal/ 'on kyang brda' chigbrgyud thun mong ma yin

pa ni slar bsam gtan phug tu rje nyid kho na la sger du gnang ba mdzad do/ /de nas rje mus chen zhabs kyis sngon byung gi lo rgyus 'ga' zhig stsal nas/ de ltar sa skya pa'i
lam 'bras kyi chos rgyun la sems dpa' chen po nas brgyud pa 'di las 'gro phan dang 'phrin las che ba med pas da res kyang khyed sa skya zhabs drung gis gtsos pa'i chos zhu
ba rnams nas gsung ngag gi bshad bsgrub la 'bad pa thon la lam 'bras nya dar chu dar du 'ong ba zhig cis kyang mdzod ces sogs gsungs par/ rje 'di'i dgongs par/ sngon ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsung ngag tshar brgyad cu gya gsum tsam dang / rje sems dpa' chen pos tshar nyer drug tsam dang 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi tshar lnga
bcu nga gcig gnang 'dug pa de rnams sprul pa'i rnam rol du snang bas 'ong dka' yang / rje 'di zhal bzhugs ring tshar gcig gnyis shig ci ltar yang 'chad thub pa dgos 'dug
dgongs pa'i thugs dam gyi go cha btsan po bzhes/ de nas slar yang grub chen shangs pa nas brgyud pa'i ni gu skor gyi chos bka' rgyas pa zhig gnang dgos zhus par ni gu'i
chos bka' rgyas pa'i lugs kyi dbang khrid spel ma'i 'chad lugs 'di bzhin dgos zhes spyi don dmigs phyed pa zhig stsal nas de lta bu zhig rje 'gyur med bde chen sogs shang

chos bzhugs che ba zhig nas gsan pa'i thugs 'dun zhu zhing / da lam zab chos snying po tsam 'bul gsungs nas/ 'jag bsam gnyis kyi ni gu chos drug gi khrid yig so so'i lung khrid
shin tu smin pa dang / de'i rgyab rten du bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gser chos rnams kyi rtsa 'grel so so/ man ngag gi yi ge gsar rnying du ma dang bcas pa'i lung
rnams gnang bar mdzad/ de mtshams gdan sa nas yab rje rin po ches rje nyid la phur sgrub thog tu phebs dgos pa'i thugs dam phebs par brten/ de 'phral gdan sar chibs bsgyur
nye tshe/ rje mus chen gyi gsungs las/ da lo nged lo don gsum yin zhing / de bar nyes skyon mi yong ba'i lung bstan gdeng khel zhig yod kyang / da dung lo re gnyis ma shi
na khyed rang la chos 'phro 'di rnams 'bul thub pa zhig byung na snyam pa yin pas/ sa skya'i mgon khang gong 'og rnams su zhabs drung rang byon nas thugs bsam chos bzhin
du 'grub pa'i phrin bcol rgyas pa re mdzad pa zhu zhes gsungs par/ rje 'di nyid thugs cung zad ma bde bar/ bdag sogs ltos bcas dang bstan 'gro'i don du zhabs pad lo brgyar
brtan par bzhugs dgos pa'i snyan gsol dang / bzhugs gdan legs pa zang zing gi 'bul ba rgya chen po dang bcas brtan bzhugs gsol

'debs shig kyang mdzad do/ /de nas chibs btegs te gdan sar phebs nas bde kyai gsang gsum yo ga bya spyod dang bcas pa'i rgyud man ngag gsan don mtha' dag gi spyi dang rang
gi mtshan nyid phra zhib bcas pa bsam byung gi mkhyen rab kyis gtan la 'bebs par mdzad/ de skabs shig shar kha chos rgyal gyi gdung rigs drung mi pham bdud 'joms dpa' bo
de nyid rkyen 'ga' zhig la brten nas lam dus kyi nyams bzhes chag pa zhig byung bas slar dbang gi chu rgyun 'thud pa'i phyir/ rje 'di'i drung du kyai rdor rgyu lam gyi dbang
gsan par phebs tshe/ de nyid dpon slob rnams kyis kha skong du gzhis byes 'ga' la gnang tshe/ dbang bshad spyi don phul du byung ba zhig stsal ba las rje bdud 'joms de
nyid kyang thugs ha las pa'i ngo mtshar dang bcas de nas bzung ste dad gus mi phyed pa rgyun chags su brtas/ de skabs shig tu gdong dga' ba'i mchis brang dad 'byor ldan
ma tshe sgron bya bas lho byang gi 'dus sder mang skol dang bcas rje nyid tshog dbur spyan drangs te zang zing gya nom pa'i bsnyen bkur zhus par dge rtsa rdzogs byang du
bsngo ba gnang / slar dgung lo nyer gcig sa sprul lo zla ba brgyad pa'i nang

mus phyogs su phebs/ gling kha bde ba can du mus chen nyid dang mjal tshe bka' mchid 'bel gtam gyi tshul du gsung ngag lam 'bras kyis gtsos snga sor chos bka' gnang ba rnams
las brtsams te dri ba mang zhig mdzad par/ rje 'di nyid nas rgyud dang man ngag grub mtha'i gnad zhib gsal tsham tshom med par phul bas rje mus chen nyid nas/ a la la/
sa skya pa'i yab chos gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi khrid gzhung bshad/ man ngag gi gnad zabamo rnams dang / phyag len phra mo tshun chad khyed kyi thugs la par btab pa bzhin
byung 'dug pa ngo mtshar che zhes sogs gsang chen bstan pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa'i sngags brjod mdzad cing / tshogs chen la gsung ngag gcig gnang dgos gsung pa bzhin rje
nyid nas kyang zhal gyis bzhes nas dus tshes dge bar don gnyer brgya phrag du ma la gsung ngag rin po che smin rgyas stsal ba'i tshe man ngag gi 'chad tshul/ rgyud sde
dang 'brel tshul/ dbang byin rlabs phyags len phra mo tsam la'ang 'khrul skyon dang bral bar 'doms par mdzad pas mus chen nyid nas chos nyan pa gnad shes mkhan tshor ga 'dra
'dug dri ba gnang tshe rgyu mtshan sgroo skur med pa zhus pas/ pha la bu skyes 'dug zhes sogs dgyes spro tshad med pa gnang / gsung ngag grol nas bsam gtan phur

mus chen drung du phebs tshe/ sngar phan rje nyid nas nan zhus stabs phyag len sogs gnang gin med kyang de nyin ci zhus kyang ma gsan par bzhugs gdan las har bzhengs te phyag
lan dang bcas gser zho gsum la dar sna lnga kha mang po 'brel pa zhig phul nas 'di khyed kyi gsung ngag gegs med du grol pa la bsgom 'chen gyi gtang rag brda' mtshon pa
legs so zhes sogs gsungs nas slar bzhugs te mus nang gi dgon ma bu rnams sa skya pa'i phyag tu 'phrod pa zhig dang / 'di na zhabs drung gis lam 'bras gnang zhig re ba rmi
lam du sgugs pa de da lan mngon sum byung / da res bar chad ma byung bas / da phyin lam 'bras ci tsam 'chad kyang bar gcod mi 'ong ba nged kyi lung bstan yin zhesasogs
dges pa'i gsung du ma gnang / yang lan cig rje nyid la spyan cher gyis gzigs nas/ rang re dpon slob byang chub bar du mi 'bral lo/ /mi 'bral lo/ /khyed 'jam dbyangs kyi
gdung brgyud yin pas sngon la sangs rgyas na nged drongs zhig ces kyang stsal bas rje 'di nyid kyi thugs la dga' bde tshad med pa 'khrungs/ re zhig nas bsam gtan phug tu
dpon slob gnyis kho na 'gol skabs shig tu yab rje nas gdan sa'i khur bzhes gdung spel dgos tshul 'di bzhin phebs par/ de phral sems

skyo shas kyi brnangs pas gong sa'i gsung lan kyang don smin zhig zhu ma nus pas don la ji ltar legs zhus par/ rje'i zhal nas/ khyed da lta'i rten 'di ga'i steng gnas rgyu
byung na bstan 'gror phan slebs che snyam pa 'dug 'on kyang rim gyis dbyibs tshul la gzigs kyin dgag dgos rtsis pa'i gnang lugs mdzad pa zab ces sogs lung bstan gsal ba 'ga'
zhig gnang / de nas dgung lo nyer gnyis pa rta lo zla ba gnyis pa tshes ma thag tu thub bstan rnam rgyal nas mkhan chen bzod pa rgya mtsho dang / rdzong dga' ldan rtse
nas chos kyi rje 'jam dbyangs chos bzang rnams rje mus chen drung du chos zhur byon skabs/ rje mus chen nas 'di phyogs su bsnyen rdzogs kyi las gral ma byung ba rgyun ring
po 'dug da lam dge bshes du ma 'dus pa'i skabs 'dir las gral zhig byung na bstan rgyun la phan pa zhig gda' gsungs pa ltar rje 'di nyid kyang ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan
bzhes par spro bas zhu bar gsol ba ltar/ zla ba 'di'i yar tshes bzang po'i nyin yang dben bsam gtan phug tu rje mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan nyid kyis mkhan po mdzad
de dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po mngon du bsgrub ste bstan pa la mngon par dga' ba'i lha rnams

kyis 'dzum mdangs ci yang gsal bar mdzad do/ /de nas kyang rje mus chen de nyid las dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rim lnga'i khrid la sogs pa gsan tshe/ thog mar bskyed rim gyi bshad
pa/ paN chen gung ru/ rje nyi zla seng ge sogs kyi rnam bshad kyi steng nas rgyas shing mtha' chod pa dang / rje rdo rje 'chang dang kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i rim lnga'i
yi ge rje blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi zin bris dang bcas pa la gzhan mkhas pa mang po'i legs bshad kyis brgyan pa'i rim lnga'i khrid shin tu smin pa zhig nyams khrid du
gsan nas de dag gi rgyab chos su rgya bod kyi gzhung mang po'i lung bshad rgyas par nod par mdzad cing / de dus rje mus chen gyi gsung las/ gsang 'dus 'phags skor gyi rgya
gzhung 'di rnams gang zag gcig gis nyams su len na gzhung so so'i brjod bya'i don rnams lam rim du bsgrig tshul 'di ltar shes dgos te zhes rgya gzhung so so dbang khrid
nyams len rnams dang sbyar nas rgyas par gsung / de ltar gsang 'dus 'phags skor gyi chos tshul rnams zla ba phyed gnyis tsam la gsan grub pa dang / slar yang bka' gdams
blo sbyong gi chos skor la lha bzhi'i khrid rim sngon du 'gro bas blo sbyong don bdun ma'i nyams khrid dang bka' gdams gong ma rnams kyi rnam thar gzhan yang sum pa lo tsA
nas brgyud pa'i

mkha' 'gro ma'i snyan brgyud man ngag gi khrid dang / khro lo nas brgyud pa'i skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid sogs gsan/ de dag gi skabs gseng la rje nyid nas thub bstan mkhan
chen dang chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos bzang pas gtsos pa gling kha tshogs chen la gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang lan mang dang / rags bsdus shig la mus chen sems dpa'
chen po'i bka' 'bum gyi ljags lung stsal/ de nas gdan sa nas yab rje chos kyi rgyal po sku khams bsnyel po yod pa'i gtam gsan 'phral 'byon bzhed kyi skabs ngam ring nas chos
rgyal chen pos nan zhus byung bas ngo ma chog par 'khor rtsam phebs rtsis kyi tshe/ rje bla ma'i gsungs las/ da res ngam ring phyogs su phebs 'gor gang chung mdzad nas
gdan sar gang myur du 'byon dgos zhes sogs gsungs pa bzhin ngam ring du mi dbang chen po gtso gyur gyi ser skya stong phrag lhag tsam la brgyud pa'i khyad gnyis ldan gyi
cho ga'i sgo nas sems bskyed kyi bka' drin stsal/ sde srid dral lcam dang ngam ring chos sde'i che bgres slob dpon rags rim lo phu dgon pa'i grwa dmangs bcas la gsang 'dus
mi bskyod pa'i dbang cha lan kha yar dang / mi dbang dpon g.yog nyung bsdus la tshe bka' sogs stsal nas bshad rtsol gyis phebs par/ yab rje rin po che de nyid sa ga

zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad la dgongs pa chos dbying su thim nas bcu dgu'i nyin thugs dam grol ba dang rje nyid gdan sar phebs te sku gshegs khar yab rje zhal mjal ma byung bas
thugs shin tu yus pa byung zhing / de nas sku gdung la phyag skor dang dbu btsugs nas thugs smon thugs tshim par gnang / de skabs grub mchog bsod nams dbang po dang gcen
rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal khu dbon gnyis 'khor bcas nas thugs dam gsal 'debs su dgyes rdor sgrub mchod yun ring dang / sku gdung zhugs 'bul nas brtsam
lo zla dus dran gyi mchod rgyun 'dzugs pa'i bar rgya cher gnang zhing / phyis su rje 'di nyid nas sger du rig 'dzin lha khang na bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung khyad 'phags dang
/ bris thang gtso bsdus chen mo sogs gsar bzhengs shin tu mang po dang / rnying pasnying pa nyams gso sogs rnam dkar gyi phrin las rlabs po che'i rgyun bskyangs pa mtha'
dag gtso bor yab rje de nyid kyi dgongs rdzogs su dmigs par mdzad pa sha dag go /de nas yang mus su phebs/ mus chen gyi drung nas sngar ma gsan pa'i zab chos gur mgon gyi
nang khrid/ srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i khrid rgyab chos/ zab mo gcod kyi lung khrid/ thugs

rje chen po tshem bu lugs kyi dmar khrid smin pa sogs chos 'phro rnams gsan cing / rje de nyid nas snyan brgyud bdag por gnang tshul gyi nA ro mkha' spyod kyi bsam mi khyab
thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag dang 'pho ba cheg brgyud ma gnyis kyang rang babs su stsal/ de skabs rje mus pa'i gsung rigs 'ga' zhig la zhing khams gzhan du dgongs pa'i
brda' chos gnang bar rje nyid thugs shin tu ma bde bar brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs rgya cher mdzad nyin nam mkha' 'ja' sprin gyis khebs pas rje 'di'i thugs la brtan bzhugs 'bul
bar 'ja' sprin 'di rang legs rgyu med dam snyam pa 'khrungs/ de nas rje nyid gdan sar chibs bsgyur gnang khar mus chen drung du gang ci'i bslab bya mtha' dag zhu bar
mdzad pas da lta dang ma 'ong ba'i gsung mang du stsal mthar rje 'di nyid la cher gyis gzigs te/ 'o/ tshe 'di glog dang 'dra khyem tsam zhig yin pas/ gzhi sdom gsum rnam
par dag pa la gnas nas thos bsam bsgom gsum la 'bad stsol mdzad de/ ci mdzad bstan dang 'gro ba'i don du 'gyur ba zhig cis kyang gnang dgos/ 'di nas sa skyar phebs 'phral
bde mchog gi bsnyen pa zla drug ma zhig gnang zhes sogs lhug stsol gnang tshe rje nyid shin tu thugs rang ste byang chub bar du thugs

rje'i skyabs 'og tu 'jug pa zhu bar mdzad/ de nas rim gyis gdan sar phebs te chu mig rdzing kha'i bde mchog pho brang du 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i gsung bsnyen la bzhugs
nas rgyang tsam song ba dang / mnal lam zhig tu rje mus chen de nyid gsal por byon nas lam dbang bla rgyud kyi byin rlabs 'dra zhig gnang ba'i tshe/ bram ze chen po sa
ra ha dang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ spyan snga rin po che dkon mchog rgya mtsho rnams kyi mtshan gsal bar gsan pa dang / yang snga dro'i ljags thun skabs shig tu cung
zad mnal bar rje mus chen gyi sku ma gzigs par gsung sbom la zil che ba zhig gis thugs khar thugs rdo rje ma zhes pa tshig gsal du 'jug dgos lags zhes gsung byung bas
mnal sad de rje mus pa nyid 'di na bzhugs yod do snyam pa'i 'jigs pa dang dga' spro zung 'brel du 'khrung zhing / de nas rgyun mi ring ba zhig na rje mus pa de nyid gzugs
sku chos dbyings su thim ste sku gdung zhus pa phal cher ring bsrel dang gdung log tu gyur cing / dbu thod kyi dum bu mi chung tsam zhig rje 'di'i phyag tu phul bar mchod
'buladang gsol 'debs rgya cher mdzad/ dge 'dun rags bsdus kyi 'khor dang bcas pas kyai rdor sgrub mchod dang bla mchod zla gcig lhag tsam gnang / gdan sa'i dge 'dun

'dus tshogs la mang 'gyed rgyas pa dus dran rgyun 'don dang / yab rje rin po che dang mus chen gyi gdung rten thun mong du dngul gdung yid bzhin nor bu ngo mtshar rmad du byung
ba dang / sku brnyan sku tshad ma/ dngul sku che legs bris sku brgya tshar/ lo dus kyi mchod 'bul du rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs sogs snga phyir
dgongs rdzogs kyang phul phyin dang / de nas bde mchog gi gsung bsnyen kha skong sbyin sreg dang bcas legs par grub nas der 'khor rnams la 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i
smin byed kyang stsal to/ /de nas dgung lo nyer gsum du phebs pa sa lug lor snga gong rnams nas ston pa'i zhal skyin lha ldan jo shAka rin po che rnam gnyis dang / sprul
pa'i gtsug lag khang chen bsam yas mi 'grur lhun gyis grub pas gtsos gnas rten rnams mjal bzhed thugs 'dun che bar yod pa'i khar/ dad stobs ldan pa dbu ru yar rgyab dpon
gyi btsun mo nam mkha' mdzod mas snga phyir gdan 'dren nanabaskyar la phebs par zhal gyis bzhes/ zla ba lnga pa'i nang chibs btegs pas mi dbang ka rma phun tshogs rnam rgyal
nas kyang nan zhus ltar phyir lam bsam 'grub rtser phebs/ mi dbang 'khor bcas la tshe bka' sogs rjes gnang du ma stsal/

dad gus kyi 'bul nod dpag tu med pa phul/ de nas rgyal khar rtser phebs/ dpal 'khor bde chen pa'i dge 'dun rnams kyis ser phreng gzab ma zhus/ sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo
sogs rten grags che ba rnams mjal/ chos sder dbang bka' sogs tshims par stsal/ de lo char shin tu dkon skabs la rje 'di gdan sa nas phebs nyin nas char chen 'beb mgo tshugs
pas rgyal khams yongs sku drin che ba shes pa byung / de nas phebs bsu dang bcas gong dkar du byon nas zhag shas bzhugs/ dbang byin rlabs dang mang skol gral 'gyed rgya
cher stsal/ rten gtso thub chen mkhyen btse chen po'i phyag bzo sogs nang mjal gyi rigs zhib par mdzad/ de nas snye thang bkra shis sgang / chos rdzong / 'or rnams na bzhug
pa'i jo bo'i sku 'dra phyag nas ma dang bla ma dam pa'i thugs dam ma'i mgon khang sogs rten mchog rnams zhib mjal dang smon lam gnang / 'di res sgar khrod kyi mi zhig
gis rje'i phyag rdzas la g.yo sgyu brtsams pas/ de'i khog par chos skyong gi 'khor zhig bzhugs nas lab lob mang po byas byung bar nye skor pa tshos byin rten gyis brdung
ba dang / dud pas bdug pa sogs byas pas de na re/ nga de 'dras 'gro mkhan

min/ sa skya nas 'ongs pa yin/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams kyi dar 'bog ma byung bar mi 'gro zer ba la/ da lta ga na yod dris pas dre'u rgya bo'i steng mgo sprel nang la
yod zer ba/ de bzhin don pa dang / da 'di zhabs drung du nged chos 'bul bas song zhig byas par/ da dung zhal mjal nas zhabs dbang zhig ma thob bar mi 'gro zer ba de bzhin
rje nyid la zhus te kho rang yang yus pa'i tshul gyis rgyug 'dral dang bcas byung ste rje'i zhabs la 'jus nas spyi bor bzhag mchi ma mang du btang ste bsangs/ phyis su
rgyu mtshan zhib par gsan yang de 'dra'i las ngan byed pa snying rje gsungs pa ma gtogs nyes chad tsam yang ma mdzad par 'dug lta sar phebs te jo shAka rnam gnyis/ rang
'byon bcu gcig zhal sogs rten gtso rnams la gser gsol snyan dar dkar me sogs mchod sprin rgya cher mdzad/ bstan 'gro spyi'i phan bder dgongs pa'i smon lam phur tshugs dang
/ pho brang dmar po ri dang lcags po rir rten mjal gnang / slob dpon chen po dang 'khon ston klu dbang bsrung ba'i dus kyi bsgrubs gnas phyis su jo bo yab sras kyis chos
'khor bskor ba'i gnas yer pa brag phug mjal du phebs/ yer pa'i dgon gseb tu

jo bo rje'i phyag nas ma'i mchod rten dkar po zhig yod par rgyang nas gzigs dus de'i ngos la kharsa pa Ni'i sku brnyan gsal ba zhig gzigs pas slar mchod rten gyi drung du phebs
nas mjal bar bzhed tshe mi snang ba zhig kyang byung / gnas mjal ba zhib par gnang / de nub mtshan lam du bud med mdzes ma bzhis phyogs bzhi nas dar thag re brkyangs
pa'i dbus na bzhugs gdan zhig 'dug par bzhugs dgos zhus par rje nyid kyang bzhugs snang zhiig byung yang dar thag 'degs pa sogs ni ma byung / phyir nang zhabs 'bring pa
rab 'byams bsod nams 'od zer la de tshul gsungs pas/ mkha' 'gro'i spyan 'dren gyi rnam pa 'dra bas legs rgyu ga 'dra yod dam zhus pas/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ darathag 'degs
pa dang khyer ba'i rnam pa ma byung bas skyon med gnas bzang bas de'i byin rlabs su 'dug gsungs pa bzhin phyis su'ang don du gnas/ de nas bsam yas su chibs bsgyur tshe
bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen po'i phyi nang gi dge 'dun tshogs kyis ser phreng gzab bstar gyis phebs bsu zhus nas pho brang gong du bzhugs/
de nas pe dkar lcog tu phebs pas gnod sbyin chen po yang de ma thag sku phebs/ de skabs rje nyid nas chos skyong la mnyes tshor chen po

zhig gnang gin med kyang / chos skyong nyid nas dad gus chen pos lung bstan zhib gsal mang ba zhig dang / lhag tu gdan sa'i khur bzhes dgos tshul nan zhus dang / khyad par
rten 'brel kyi khyad cig yod pas dge bshes kyi gdug 'dre la rta zhig dgos/ de yang dge bshes gdung spel byas sa dkar po'i gdan gnon na rta bang la mjug ma 'job be ba zhig
khyer shog rab byung gtsang ma byed na gsar la yid 'dzin pa zhig khyer shog zhus par/ rje 'di rab byung la thugs gzhol bas lha rta gtsug rgyan zer ba'i gsar ma sil po zhig
phul nas de mtshungs rab byung rten gyi 'chad nyan nyams bzhes 'gro phan mdzad pa'i 'phrin las sgrub dgos tshul phebs par chos skyong chen po dgongs pa cung ma khengs
par g.ya' sa dkar po'i rus pa 'di ma chad tsam zhig byed na rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam 'phrul gyi dge bshes gzhon pa rang bsam pa rgya che dgos pa yod do zhes zhu ba phul/
de nas rje 'di chos skyong chen pos rdo skas kyi mgor phebs skyel zhus nas dge bshes kyi ring la sa dkar po'i mdangs thon pa'i phyir zab yangs mthil gyi lha mi rnams kyis
lha rgyal thang gsum bos gsungs nas phyag g.yas kyi ral gri nam mkha' la 'phyar thengs gsum mdzad pa dang bstun der tshogs ser skya mi khrom dmar nag gis lha rgyal 'ur

chil ba lan gsum bsgrags/ de nas bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang nye 'gyangs rnams la dkar me snyan dar mang po dang / mchims phur phebs tshe brag dmar ke'u tshang gi phug pa'i
thod las tshe chu mang du babs pas dpon slob thams cad kyis gsol rgyu byung / brag phug de'i logs shig la rnam rgyal mchod rten rang byon gsal po zhig gzigs pas dkon gnyer
la 'di'i dkar chag ga 'dra yod gsungs pas/ sku gnyer de karma pa'i grwa rigs shig yin 'dug kyang ngo mtshar nas 'di bzhin sngar nas med lags/ da lam skyes chen nyid phebs
pas gnas sgo gsar du phye bar 'dug zer ba de bzhin yongs la grags pa byung / 'di skor mkhan slob chos gsum dus kyi sngon gnas rjes dran gyi thugs nyams 'ga' zhig gsal
por 'khrungs/ bsam yas phyogs kyi dad 'dus ser skya tshang mar dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang sogs chos kyi bka' drin yang rgya cher stsal/ de nas slar yang dpal 'byor rab
brtan nas dpon sa nam mkha' mdzod mas rting bskul gdan 'dren 'byor bas rim phebs kyis gra thang du zha lu lo chen gyi gser gdung dang / de nyid kyi thugs dam ma'i dus 'khor
gyi sku brnyan/ paN chen byams pa gling pas bzhengs pa'i mchod rten chen po byams pa'i sku dang

bcas pa mjal/ dpal rab nas phebs bsu'i bkod pa gzab pa dang bcas te der phebs/ dpon sa nyid gtso bor gyur pa'i spyi sger thun mong dang so sor chos bka' rgya cher gnang / khyad
par dpon sa sras yum nas gsol ba nan can btab ngor zab chos kyang 'ga' zhig bstsal/ zhal gyi rjes gnang mdzad tshe/ sras mo chos mdzad ma gcig yod pa a tsa ra lag na
rkyal pa khyer ba sma ra ring po byas pa zhig dang dngos su 'phrad pas thams cad kyis bla ma dang mgon po dbyer med du shes pa'i dad pa thob/ dpal rab steng gi mgon khang
bsil ba'i tshal du grags pa der nyin re bzhin thugs dam bskang 'phrin re dang / zhal gyi man ngag nas 'byung ba bzhin zhal gyi rten rdo zhig gi steng du nas nag gi tshom
bu lnga la brten nas bstan 'gro spyii'i phan bde dang khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa phyogs mthar rgyas pa'i bka' bsgo gnang bas phyis su sgar chen rin po che'i
phyag tu dpal rab kyi chos gzhis byung ba sogs kyang 'di'i nus par nges shing de ras kyang sbyin bdag 'khor bcas dad stobs phul du phyin pas 'bul nod kyang bsam gyis
mi khyab pa byung / de nas rim gyis zla ba dgu pa'i nang gdan sar phebs/ zla bcu pa dang bcu gcig par lo ltar gyi dus rim rnams rgyas par tshugs/

dgung lo nyer bzhi lcags spre lor mus su chibs bsgyur te/ rje btsun mus pa chen po'i nang rten phyi rten thams cad mjal zhu mdzad/ dkar me snyan shal gsol 'debs smon lam shin
tu smin par bstsal/ 'dus tshogs la'ang mang ja gral 'gyed dang / der tshogs la rjes gnang zur bka' bcu phrag sogs chos kyi bka' drin yang mang du bstsal rta mo bde legs
su phebs/ de phyogs sngar sor ser ba shin tu sdang bar rje nyid nas spyan dmigs srung 'khor gnang bas de phyin lo gsum la ser ba gtan nas ma byung / de nas ya ma bde ldan
dang / rjong dga' ldan rtse sogs kyi grwa tshogs la mang bskol dang chos bka' ci rigs par stsal/ smon 'gro nas lha lcam gyis spyan drangs pa bzhin phebs/ tshe bka' brgya
tshar sogs kyi rjes 'dzin gnang ste gdan sar phebs/ 'di lo hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes bco brgyad kyi nub mo gcen rin po che kun dga' dbang rgyal glo bur du zhing brjes pa'i
thugs dam gsal 'debs su rje nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa brgya phrag gi 'khor dang bcas pas kyai rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / gzhan
yang chos sde nye 'gyangs mang por mang 'gyed rgya chen/ khyad par 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po gdan drangs pa dbur bzhugs kyi gzhis byes kyi dge 'dun khri

phrag longs par bsnyen bkur gral 'gyed dang / skye bo'i tshogs mang po la sbyin gtong rgya chen dang lo zla'i dus dran gyi mchod 'bul bcas bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad/ de nas
gsan sa chen po'i gdung brgyud nyag phra bar brten gtso bor 'jam mgon dbang po'i zhabs kyis dngos dang brgyud nas gsung ring thung sna tshogs pa dang / lhag tu chos rgyal
karma phun tshogs rnam rgyal nas kyang bstan 'gror dgongs pa'i zhu nan phur tshugs da nga / phyis kyi 'byung 'gyur 'di dag mngon sum gzigs pa/ yab rje rin po ches zhal
chems lan mang du yod pa dang / zan g.yang chos skyong chen pos kyang dngos dang brgyud pa'i sgo nas sa skya'i gdung 'dzin rigs gsum mgon gyi sku gzhon pa la bka' bab yod
tshul kyi lung bstan lan grangs du ma dang / gdan sa rang gi gros dbang ser skya tshang mas 'di ga'i 'dzin skyong gnang dgos par gsol ba ci drag tu btab pa'i mthar/ rje
nyid nas sku tshe hril po rab byung gi rten gyi 'da' ba'i dgongs gzhi dang mdzad spyod gong du bstan pa bzhin yin na'ang / skabs 'dir bod khams spyi'i bde skyid/ bstan
pa spyi sger gyi dngos gzhi bla ma gong ma rnams kyi dgongs bzhed dang / gdan sa 'di nyid nas lugs gnyis kyi ltos bcas mtha' dag thugs kyis 'dor ma nus par

rgyal sras mchog gi thugs stobs 'khur chen bzhes te ji ltar zhus pa bzhin zhal gyi bzhes/ lo khong 'dir dbu rtse rnying ma'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba dang / sngar rab byung
bzhes dus dbu gtsug phul ba'i thub dbang rdo rje gdan chung ma gnyis stabs gcig tu bzhugs pa'i drung du mchod pa rgya chen po bshams te bslab pa 'bul chog tshul bzhin
gnang nas yongs rdzogs rdo rje dge bsnyen 'dzin pa'irtul zhugs bzhes nas bzung phyis byung sa skya pa'i bstan srid yar zla ltar 'phel ba 'di byung ba lags/ de nas dgung
lo nyer drug bzhes pa chu khyi lor mi dbang karma bstan skyong dbang pos pho brang chen po bsam 'grubartser spyan drangs/ rje 'di nyid nas kyang mi dbang de nyid rgyal sar
'khod nas chos 'brel zhus pa'i thog mar yin pa'i rten 'brel la dgongs te gser zangs kyi rgyal srid sna bdun khyad mtshar sogs legs skyes rgya chen pos mnga' dbul gyi tshul
dang / dpon slob lnga bcu tsam gyis rdul tshon la brten pa'i phur sgrub gnang zhing / mi dbang chen po drung 'khor bcas dang sku rim pa'i dge 'dun brgya phrag la rdo
rje phur pa'i smin byed dang slar yang chos rgyal 'khor bcas la tshe bka' sogs 'dod chos legs par stsal/ sku chas phod ka 'brug ris can sogs zang zing gi 'bul ba bsam

gyis mi khyab phul/ yar lam dar lung du byon te gsung bskang rgyas par gnang / de nas gdan sar phebs te lo star gyi phur sgrub mdzad/ de lo zla ba dgu pa'i nang shar kha mi
dbang bsod nams dbang po'i sde dang / de'i sras chos rje ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa sogs mi chen du ma chos sde lho byang gi dge 'dun du ma bcas mang ba la gsung
ngag zab mos khrid rim cha lag man ngag rgyab chos lung dang bcas pa zla ba gsum gyi khongs su smin rgyas su stsal/ de skabs mnal lam zhig tu/ 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang
pos gur mgon gyi dkyil 'khor du ma'i dbang bskur rnams dus gcig tu stsal ba shar bas bla ma dang chos srung dgyes pa'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar ba dang / khyad par sems
bskyed chen mo'i nyin 'ja' 'od kyi gur dang me tog gi char soT mthun grub tu byung / 'di lo bya yul lo dgon pa nas spyan snga kun dga' don grub nyid rje 'di nyid dang gdan
sa chen po'i gnas rten mjal bzhed yod thog rje 'di nyid nas kyang gdan 'dren mdzad pas phebs te gsung chos tshad med pa gsan pa'i tshe dpal mgon zhal gyi rjes gnang bram
ze mngag gtad gsan pa'i nub mo mnal lam

du/ rje nyid dang spyan snga ba lhan cig tu bzhugs 'dug pa'i drung na/ rnal 'byor pa'i cha lugs byas pa/ gzus bong chen po ral pa'i thor cog can/ lus la rus rgyan dang g.yer
kha'i sgra sil chom me ba dang bcas pa zhig byung bar/ rje nyid kyis spyan snga rin po che'i bsngags pa mang du brjod pas/ de na re/ de bzhin yin las che ste/ nga ni khyed
rang gis spyan hur re gzigs pa de zil che ba zhig yong gi 'dug cing khyed rang lhag bsam pa yod zer ba sogs gnyan mgon rang shugs su 'go ba'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar
ba byung / phar yang zab chos 'ga' zhig stsal/ rje 'di gdan sar lan gsum byon te bka' chos gsan gnang tshad med dang / thugs snang yang shin tu gshin pas phyis su spyan snga
nyid sku gshegs khang yang lo dgon pa'i rten gtso jo bo shAkya mu ne'i bzo phud du bzhengs pa'i thub pa 'od zer 'gyed dang / jo bo bod du byon na bstan 'gror sman par
lung ston pa'i lung bstan sgrol ma gnyis kyang sa skyar 'bul bar mdzad pa yin no/ /de nas dgung lo nyer bdun chu phag sa ga zla ba'i nyer gnyis nas zhag bdun gyi bar dam
rdzas 'chi med ril bu bsgrub pa mdzad tshe/ nyin re bzhin 'ja' sprin dkar pos nam mkha'i khyon gang zhing / mnal lam zhig tu bud med cig gis shing tog mang po phul

ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i mtshan ltas byung / de'i dbyar lha chen rig 'dzin pho brang du 'jigs byed kyi gsung bsnyen smin par mdzad/ de lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du nags
dgon chos rje sbyin pa grags pa don slob zhig gdan sa'i rten dang brten pa mjal bar phebs pa'i tshe/ de nyid mdo sngags kyi yon tan du mas thugs rgyud phyug cing / mus chen
rje'i zhal slob kyi thu bo yin pa sogs chos khungs gtsang mar song stabs chos bka' 'ga' zhig gsan/ phyir yang gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang sogs 'ga' zhig stsal/
dgung lo nyer brgyad shing byi lor zla ba bcu pa'i tshes drug gi tho rangs mnal lam du yab rje chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi sku mdun na rgya ja sogs dngos po mang po zhig
'dug par rje 'di la gzigs te/ dngos po 'di rnams kyi tho yig 'di yin gsungs nas yi ge zhig stsal snyam byung ba dang / lhag par rje nyid kyi thugs la dogs gnas chen po
zhig yod pa de la 'di gyis shig pa'i bslab bya lhug stsol du gnang ba sogs byung / de nas rgyun mi ring ba zhig na 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug khams nas yar phebs
par/ rje nyid dpon slob rnams glang dkar bar du phebs bsur byon pas mjal ma thag rje 'dis mjal dar dang bcas

phyag phul mdzad tshe/ grub mchog de nyid nas kyang sku mched yun ring nas ma mjal ba'i thugs brtse gdung gi shugs dang/ rje 'dis gdan sa chos srid kyi khur bzhes nas 'phrin
las rgyas pa la thugs dgyes spro'i shugs kyis mjal dar dang phyag mdzad pas rje nyid kyi gcen gyi sku la 'khyud nas bshol bar grub mchog nyid nas kho bo na so rgan kyang
khyed rang gi lugs gnyis kyi mkhyen rab phul du phyin pa 'di'i char yang mi phod ces sogs rjes su yi rang gnang nas sku mched lhan cig par chos sde phan tshun nas ser phreng
gi phebs bsu dang bcas thugs nyams spro bar phebs/ sgang chen zhabs drung nas sku brnyan rgya nag ma gyon gtsang ba du ma dang / rol mo/ ja gos dang / rta/ drel sogs
zang zing gi dngos spyad rgya cher phul/ gtsug lag khang so sor snyan dar phon chen dang 'dus sder mang 'gyed sogs lha mi kun la skyes gnang rgya cher stsal/ de lo gdan
sar mi phyed pa'i dad pa can shag pa chos kyi rje kun bzang drung dang / grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug gi zhabs 'bring pa scags la bla ma chos rgya mtsho gnyis kyis
gtsos pa'i dad ldan du ma'i ngor gsung ngag rin po che rgyas par gnang / de rjes kyang lo nas spyan snga rin po che phebs par chos bka' 'ga' zhig gsan/

de nas dgung lo nyer dgu pa shing glang gi dbyar lha khang chen mo dang / dbu rtse sogs na bzhugs pa'i bka' 'gyur rnams ma tshang ba kha skoong dang / lha khang mthil gyi shar
ye'i thugs dam bka' 'gyur de rgyun 'don mdzad rgyur gdong dang lnga brtsegs/ steng du bla bre sogs zhabs tog dang / sngar phan lo rer bka' 'gyur tshar re klog par rje
'di'i tshar gsam re'i rgyun btsugs/ lha khang chen mo'i khyams stod dang phur khang sogs la bla bre dang / lam 'bras bla brgyud kyis bris thang chen mo/ spen bad la rlung
dril brgya phrag nye ba gsar lugs kyis sgron pa sogs gnang / de lo 'dar grang mo che nas rje btsun dbang phyug rab brtan spyan drangs nas dmar po skor gsum sogs gser chos
gtso bor gyur pa'i bzhed chos du ma dang / khyad par zhal gyi man ngag ha la nag po'i be bum zhes pa rje des sngar su la'ang gnang ma phod pa'i snying nang gi khrag lta
bu'i gdams pa zab mo yongs rdzogs 'bul bar mdzad de/ chos bdag la 'phrod gsungs pa sogs dgyes spro'i gsung dang bcas stsal/ dgung lo sum cur phebs pa me stag lor chos sde
lho byang gi dge bshes ched btus brgya phrag longs par mkha' spyod ma'i sdhuin ra'i  dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i byin rlabs sngon du 'gro bas nA

ro mkha' spyod kyi tshes bcu'i sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs gnang / zla ba brgyad par phyogs kyi mi chen don gnyer du ma lho byang gi chos sder bcas la rdo rje phur pa'i stod las
kyis dbang dang / phur pa'i yig skor mang po'i lung dang / rje gnang zur bka' zab cing dkon pa nyi shu lhag pa gnang / dgung lo so gcig pa me yos kyi lor mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa de nyid rje btsun chen po'i skuu brnyan mdzes po 'od zer dpal gyi dbu thod bzhugs pas mdzes thod mar grags pa la zhabs skor
'bum ther gnang bzhed dang rje 'di nyid 'jal bzhed kyis gdan sar phebs par mjal ma thag nas thugs spro snang shin pas sngar phan yongs 'dzin gzhan las ma gsan pa'i chos 'phro
rnams gnang dgos tshul mdzad pa ltar/ mkhan chen de nyid nas kyang chos bka' 'bul bar dgyes spro'i gsung bcas thog mar zhabs skor grangs sogs mdzad de bka' chos dpag
tu med pa zhig stsal nas phebs/ slar zla ba bzhi pa'i nang gdan drangs te sngar gyi chos 'phro mtha' yas pa zhig gsan/ rje nyid kyang mkhan chen de nyid kyis gtsos gzhis
byes mang bar zab chos du ma zhig stsal/ de rjes phur sgrub grol nas mi dbang bstan skyong dbang pos

spyan 'dren nan zhus bzhin phebs te tshe bka' sogs skyon sel gyi dbang bka' 'ga' zhig sku sger dang phur pa grwa tshang gsar btsugs kyi dge 'dun dang drung 'khor drag rim sogs
