mang ba la phur pa'i smad las drag po sgrol dbang gnang tshe rnying ma spyi don sogs gsung bshad cung zad spros pa mdzad pas smon 'groo tshe dbang pa sogs dpyod ldan
rnams kyang yid rang dbang med par 'phrogs/ mi dbang chen mo nas lo mthong bkra shis sbug gi mchod gzhis kyi thog drangs yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ phar lam snar
thang du rten mjal dang / ngor e waM chos ldan nas shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas kyis gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs/ rten mchog rnams la mchod 'bul dang bstan 'gror dgongs
pa'i smon lam mdzad/ 'dus tshogs la mang ja gral 'gyed stsal/ shar chen de nyid dang thar rtse nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis gtsos 'dus tshogs la rje rdo rje 'chang gi bzhugs
khri'i steng nas chos bka' rgya cher gnang ste/ shab dge sdings su phebs khrom tshogs khri phrag brgal bar khrom dbang / yar lam dar lung du gsung bskang / byang khud
kyi yul grong phyag dbang zhu mi'i khrod na bud med sgang yol ske la lba ba chen po can zhig 'dug par phyag dbang nan che zhig gnang / de dgongs bud med lba ba can de zhing
skyong

chen po'i yum chen zhig yin pa 'dra/ lba ba dkyus ma zhig tu mi 'dug gsung / de lo zla ba brgyad pa'i nang Da Di srin po chos rdzong gi mgon khang nas shing mgon sngar dus
gdan sar drangs pa'i tshab 'di lo 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam rten mgon po lcam dral gyi sku brnyan 'do li la spyan drangs pa dang bcas rje nyid phebs te mgon khang
der bzhugs su bcug nas snyan dar dang spyan gzigs rngams brjid ldan pa phul rab gnas mang gsol rgyas pa dang dus gtor rgyun 'dzugs bcas mdzad/ 'di skabs mnal lam du grub
mchog dbang po mtshan can de nyid kyi dgyes pa'i gsung du ma dang lhag par sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i nang gi ku ru kulle'i thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag 'di rnams yin zhes
stsal ba sogs byung bas mgon khang 'di nyid bzhengs par mdzad pa la grub dbang de nyid kyang dgongs pa khyad par can rdzogs par mngon/ de mtshams nas phyogs kyi 'bul skyel
ba gnyer khag bdun gyi dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab pa slebs pas chos skyong dgyes pa'i mtshan ltas kyi rten 'brel yang 'grig de nas gdan sar phebs/ dgung lo so gnyis
pa sa 'brug lor mkhan chen ngag dbang

chos grags gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs pas ser phreng gi bsu ba gnang / dus kyi 'khor los mtshon pas chos bka' zhab cing rgya che ba mtha' yas pa zhig gsan/ phar yang gsang
'dus rim lnga'i dmar khrid 'gos lugs gtsang ma la rgyab chos yig rnying du ma'i lung sogs 'phags skor yongs rdzogs kyi khrid lung bshad bka' mtha' dag bum pa gang byo'i tshul
du gnang bas mkhan chen 'di nyid kyang 'di nas bzung ste gsang 'dus smra ba'i dbang phyug tu gyur/ dgung lo so gsum pa sa sbrul lor lo snga ma'i bzhi thog gi ar po'i
'phro grub par/ li ma lha khang rdo rje'i gdan dang / rgya nag lha khang ri bo rtse lnga dang / dpe khang chos mdzod chen mo rnams su mtshan gsol nas rab gnas smin rgyas
gnang / de dang dus sprel lha khang chen mo'i byang shar gyi lcog btsun mo spe'u yang nyams gso rmang nas bslang bar mdzad tshe mnal lam du sngags 'chang yab sras gsum rje
nyid bcas bsam gling du phebs rgyu'i rnam pas btsun mo lcog gi shar rtsa nas yar 'byon gin 'dug par sngags 'chang chen pos btsun mo spe'ur legs par gzigs rjes rje nyid
la gzigs nas zhal 'dzum shin tu che ba zhig mdzad pa byur bas sngags 'chang chen po yang dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i mtshan mar

mngon/ dgung lo so bzhi pa lcags rta lor yang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags phebs par gshin rje gshed dmar po'i dbang khrid kyis drangs pa'i gshed skor gyi snyan brgyud
man ngag sgrub 'phrin sogs chos bka' dpag med gsan/ de skabs gan par bdag po mthu stobs drung dpon blon thugs 'dod ma legs par brten zla ba bzhi par gan par phebs ste dpon
blon lha gyang sbyor gyi lugs gnang yang bdag po nas thugs 'khon sor ma chud stabs blon po rnams zur 'jog dang phyag phyi skabs babs zhal bkod mdzad cing / phu dmar zhabs
drung dang sku mched gnyis kar bka' chos kyang mang du stsal/ slar gdan sar phebs/ zla ba drug par bsam 'grub rtser gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs/ sde srid yum 'khoor bcas
la bka' chos ci yang stsal/ rtse gdong khri rin po che yang de na bzhugs par dbang lung kha shas gsan/ de skabs mda' dpon sgos lung pas sger mjal dang 'bul ba bcas byang
chub bar du rjes su 'dzin par gsol ba btab/ phyis su'ang kho rang la na tsha sde gzar gang gi skabs kyang 'di nyid la blo phugs gtad pa'i thugs rje byin rlabs mngon gyur
du ma byung bar brten dad gus gong 'phel gyi lo lo bzhin 'bul ba char chen

'bul/ de nas gdan sa'i phur sgrub la phebs/ rtse gdong nas bdag chen sku 'bring gdan sar phebs pa'i zhabs 'bring thub bstan mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan pa'i zhabs rdo rje bcas
'byor/ khong dpon slob rnams la rdo rje phur pa'i dbang nag po rim bzhi'i khrid sogs bzhed chos mang po gnang / dgung grangs so lnga pa lcags lug lor sku khrag rgyas
pa la/ tshal gtar 'gyangs pa'i rnam pas snyun gzhi shin tu thu ba zhig byung bar sku rim zhabs brtan du chos sde lho byang gis gtsos pa'i dgon gnas ris med du mang 'gyed
rgya dpang shin tu che bas phyi nang gi phyag rdzas spong dag lta bu gnang ba'i 'bras bus/ tshal gtar sogs kyang rim 'phrod kyi skabs mnal lam zhig tu 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od
'bar ba rgyun gyi gser zangs kyi mdog 'di ma yin pa'i gur gum gyis byugs pa lta bu'i gser mdangs shig gzigs pa des rje nyid la mchog tu brtse ba'i nyams kyis sku la 'khyud
pa mdzad byung bar rje nyid kyis kyang dad pa'i sgo nas phar sku la 'chang nas gsol 'debs mang du mdzad pa zhig byung ba nas sku khams kyang dwangs skyed che bar byung
/ skabs de'i dga' ston dang slad kyi sku rkyen sel phyir skya ser khri phrag longs par sbyin gtong bla na med par mdzad/ de nas sngon rje btsun kun dga'

grol mchog gi thugs dam ma/ gtso bsdus bris thang rnams gzigs pa'i rkyen byas te 'di gong dgung lo so gsum lo gzhug tsam nas dbu btsugs te gtso bsdus zhal thang sum cu rtsa
lnga gzab bkod sgrub par mdzad pa/ dgung grangs so bdun thog grub par rab gnas smin rgyas gnang skabs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma byung / dgung lo so brgyad shing khyi lor
dpal rab nas grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug spyan drangs de dang stabs gcig spyan snga rin po che yang phebs/ rje nyid nas grub dbang de nyid kyis gsang yum nam mkha'
sgrol ma dang/ rnam rab nas chos rje'i drung lcam sring gnyis sogs gzhis byes mang por gsung / ngag rin po che bka' drin stsal rjes/ spyan snga rin po che las sngar ma
gsan pa'i rnying ma'i zab chos 'ga' zhig sogs chos tshul mang du gsan/ dgung lo so dgu pa/ shing phag lor khams phyogs kyi 'bul dpon pa sogs bla slob grwa rigs mang por sgrub
thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang yongs rdzogs sogs gnang/ dgung lo bzhi bcu pa me byi lor bsam 'grub rtser sde srid kyi sku rim ser tshogs lo star yod pa'i 'di lo'i tshogs
dbur rje

nyid spyan drangs par dpon slob lnga bcu skor phebs pa/ gzhis ka nas phur pa grwa tshang gi bla ma dang / gur pa'i bla ma sogs dpon slob nyer lnga tsam bsnan pas phur bzlog
tshugs te gtor rdzong nyin zor gtor 'phangs pa dang mnyam du bsam rtse'i lho'i ri sdebs nas rlung 'tshub gcig lang ste je cher gyur nas shar phyogs su song bas phyis su
rtags mtshan bzhin gyi thugs rje mngon gyur du byung / rtse gdong nas gdan 'dren 'byor ba bzhin phebs/ 'jam dbyangs byams pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang dpal bzang po sku
mched gsum dang / thub bstan mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje sogs dpon slob mang por tshe bka' sogs chos dang zang zing gi bka' drin tshad med pa stsal/ zhal ngo
rnams kyis kyang zhabs 'degs dang 'bul ba rgya cher mdzad/ yar lam gser mdog can du phebs/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan gyi dngul gdung rin po che sogs rten mchog rnams mjal/
de nas gzhis ka rtser mi dbang nyid kyis phebs bsu bcas byon nam mkha' dngas ba la 'ja' dang me tog gi char sogs ya mtshan pa'i ltas kyang byung / mi dbang chen por
zab chos 'ga' zhig stsal/ rtse gdong khri rin po che las kyang lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi khrid sogs zab cing

dkoon pa du ma gsan/ sde srid kyis phur pa grwa tshang du 'jog rgyu'i gur mgon lcam dral gyi 'chams sku zhig zhal bkod dgos tshul zhus pa ltar zhal bzhes gnang / pho brang
nas chibs bsgyur nyin sde srid nas phebs skyel zhus pa'i bkra shis lhun po'i thang stod de na phebs dus bud med cig gis phyag dbang ma thob pa'i gdung bas skad chen pos ngu
rgyugs byed pa byung ba dang / snar thang la ma phebs bar nub phyogs nas rlung chen shin tu che ba phyug po gzhung khrig gis khengs pa zhig byung bas/ de nub rje'i gsungs
las/ da nang gi bud med ngu rgyugs byed pa de dang / thal rlung byung lugs des nged mchod yon slar mjal 'dzoms legs tshogs che ba zhig ji 'dra yong ngam gsungs/ de rjes
gdan sar 'cham mgon zhal bkod gnang skabs kyang / 'di sde srid rang nas thugs bsam rnam dag gi mdzad sgor 'dug kyang / bsam 'grub rtser 'khyol thub pa zhig ma byung dogs
ka 'dug gsungs pa sogs phyis 'byung sgrib med du gzigs pa'i bka' du ma gnang / de lo gtsang phyogs su 'brum nad gdug pa can zhig byung bas/ gdan sar yang ser skya mang
por 'brum nad kyi thebs par nye skor du rol mo'i sgra sogs shin tu 'dzem dgos kyis phal cher thag chod mtshams su dbu rtser zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid gnang

dus grwa pa 'brum nad las grol 'phral rnams la phyag dbang gnang skabs/ rje nyid nas nga la yang 'brum nad 'gos yong las che zhes sogs gsungs kyang / zhabs 'bring pa rnams
kyis rje 'di sngar mus la bzhugs skabs sku 'brum du ngos bzung ba'i bsnyun zhig byung bar phyis su shangs la 'brum rjes chen po gcig kyang dngos mthong yod bzhin du sku 'brum
gyi dogs pa ga la yod tshul zhus kyang ji ltar yin nam gsungs pa tsam gyi ngang la phur sgrub tshugs pa'i sa 'dul gyi nyin sku khams cung ma bde yang kun gyis dogs pa
ma shar bas sku khams lhod med du gnang / de mus tshes bco lnga'i snga dro sku dang zhal ras la 'brum bu kha shas thon yang 'tsho byed pa rnams kyis sngar gyi de yid la
'jags ches pas 'brum yan yin snyam bag yangs su du bzhag gsung chog la gdangs dbyangs kyang tshe tsam mdzad pas rim gyis snyun cher byung yang sngags 'chang chen po'i dus
mchod 'di khag che dgongs te thugs bsran mdzad pas bcu bdun gyi nyin sku 'brum yin par thag chod nas bco brgyad la dkyil 'khor bsdu gshegs mdzad/ grwa tshang nas sku rim
'dzugs pa sogs gnang bas sku khams rim dngas byung bas nye skor ser skya thams cad kyis 'di lo'i 'brum nad la rnga skad grags tsam yang mi rung ba la gong bzhugs la sku
'chams dang gsungs

dbyangs rol mo de 'dras skyon med pa sku 'brum las grol ba 'di ngo mtshar ba'i grub rtags rang du 'dug zer ba byung / dgung lo zhe gcig pa me glang lor gan sa nas bdag po mthu
stobs drung sku mched 'brum skyon gyis shegs par rje nyid dpon slob rnams shar stabs su phebs/ rtse gdong bdag chen rin po che sogs bla ma mang por bsngo rten dang dgon
sde mang por mang 'gyed/ rje nyid dpon slob nas gsung chog byang zhu sogs smin pa dang / sku mched gsum gar dngul gdung phal thog re lhag yod pa gsum sogs bzhengs pa gnang
ste gdan sar phebs/ zla ba drug pa'i nang mchod sbyin chen mo gnang ba'i dbur grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug spyan drangs te gsung bsngo zhu rten sgrol ma'i dngul
sku mda' tshad tsam gyis thog drangs 'bul ba dpag tu med pa mdzad/ dgung lo zhe gnyis pa sa stag lor sde srid nas mtha' dmag la dmigs pa'i gtor bzlog cig 'dzugs dgos zhus
ngor ngam ring la phebs pa'i phar lam grangs mo cher tshar chen gyi gser gdung sogs rten mjal mdzad/ grwa tshang la mang 'gyed gnang / ngam ring du chos sder mang ja du
ma gser 'gyed bcas dang / tshogs chen la a ra pa tsa'i rjes gnang bstsal/ gong dkar grwa

tshang la sger du mang 'gyed dang 'du khang zhig gsos la phyag nas mdzad/ khrom dbang zhig kyang gnang / ngam ring byams chen dang / rtse'i rten rnams mjal/ tshur lam klu sgrub
sprul pa'i skus gro mo lung du spyan drangs bsnyen bkur rgya chen zhus/ nang par rin chen sding du khrom tshogs ser skya khri phrag longs par tshe dbang stsal nas gdan
sar phebs/ zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes brgyad dkar po nam gru'i 'grub sbyor nyin thugs sras ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku bltams/
dgung lo zhe gsum pa sa yos lor gtsang pa nas lhor dpung 'jug mdzad nas/ 'brug pa'i yon bdag thams cad kyi khang par me rgyag pa sogs 'brug zhabs drung nyid kyang dben
dgon lcags ri la 'khra btsan mdzad dgos shar ba sogs zil che ba byung skabs/ rje nyid nas lus can gyi sdug bsngal la gzigs pa tshad med pas shar stabs su phebs/ bsam rtser
sde srid drung dang / spa gror mda' dpon sgos lung pa bcas phan tshun du dpung tshogs sdud dgos kyi bka' shog gnang ba bzhin gtsang dpung tshur bsdus gtsang 'brug so so
nas log 'gal mi byed pa'i dam rgya mdzad/ de dus phag rir zla gcig tsam gyi bzhugs gnas grub chen thang stong rgyal po'i btab pa'i bsam grub lha khang du

mdzad/ grub chen gyi phyag bzo mchod rten bkra shis sgo mang dang / grub chen nyid kyi sku 'dra nad gcod mar grags pa sogs rten mchog rnams la phyag dang zhabs skor smon lam
phur tshugs su gnang / phag ri de sa khad mtho stabs kyis phal cher kha ba rang 'bab pa sogs spro nyams med kyang / 'di skabs kha ba 'bab res su jo mo lha rir gtor bsngo
'phrin bcol mdzad 'phral chad pa kho na byung / tshur lam la phyi/ gad shing lung / gam pa/ lhog pa na ring sogs su khrom dbang dang thugs rje chen po'i sgom lung re gnang
nas yig drug 'dren par khas len rnams bsher bas dung phyur bzla ba dam bca' byed mi shin tu mang po dang de min bye ba tshun nas brgya phrag phan gyi khas len pa'ang
mang du byung bas lus can de dag la thar pa'i sa bon btab/ gdan sar phebs nas 'di lo bde mchog pho brang zhig gsos kyi rten dang brten pa ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor lta bu 'di
nyid grub par mdzad de gza' tshes legs par bstun rab gnas rgyas par gnang / rgyal sras mchog gi rnams thar phul du byung ba byang pa rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags bzang pa'i
sku gdung bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung lhun sdings su yod pa phyis su chud zos la nye bar rje 'di'i gdan sar spyan drangs te bla brang nyi lder mchod pa'i yo byad du ma dang

bcas bzhugs par mdzad/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags gdung brgyud rin po che mjal du phebs par bka' chos du ma gsan/ dgung lo zhe bzhi pa lcags 'brug
lor rtse gdong bdag chen bsod nams lhun grub yum sras gnyis phebs par mgon po'i dbang lnga dang sa lo'i bka' 'bum sogs zab chos mang po dang zang zing gi gnang skyes rgya
cher bstsal/ dgung lo zhe lnga pa lcags sbrul lor byang phyogs gu shri rgyal po'i dmag dpung slebs te bsam rtse la skor rgyag byas/ gzhis ka'i nye skor stag la sogs la
'grul pa thams cad sogs dmag gis brdung 'phrog tshad med byed pa'i skabs rje 'di nyid kyis bod sog gi 'dun chings la phebs par/ sog pos kyang gnyer pa gu shri bla ma sogs
phebs lam gyi phyag phyi bar btang ba sogs dad gus lhur bzhes chen po byung ngor du re zhig bzhugs nas gtsang sog so sor bka' 'doms gang mang zhig gnang yang / phan tshun
dgongs dbyings mtho stobs gsan bzhes gdeng khel zhig ma gnang bas gdan sar phebs/ de lo bstan 'gro'i phan bder dgongs sbyin gtong chen po gsum pa mdzad/ chu rta zla ba
gsum pa'i nang shar phyogs

su chibs bteg mi rje ka rma bstan skyong dbang por 'phral yun gyi bslab ston lhug 'doms gnang / de nyid nas kyang 'phags pa rin po che'i thug rten mgon po'i sku brnyan si'u
ma thog tshad tsam da lta rgyal po lo gsar gyi mnga' gsol skabs 'grem pa 'di dang / theg chen rin po che'i thugs dam ma sher shing gi gur mgon gyi sku brnyan/ rgya sbug
zhing skyong lha dga' sogs phul/ 'di phyi kun tu rjes su bzung bar gsol ba btab/ sog dmag gis sde srid gtsang pa dbang du bsdus nas ma 'gyangs par gong sa rdo rje 'chang
lnga pa chen po gzhis rtser chibs bsgyur gyis rtsis bzhes mdzad skabs rje 'di dang thog mar zhal rgyas gnang dus de nas bzung gzigs bskyang gi bstod bkur bsngags gsum kho
na rnam thar du kU la'i glegs bam ka pa sogs gsung rab mang por gsal yod cing / gzhis rtse'i thugs brel rnams chod nas gdan sar phebs/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang ngam ring
mkhan chen klu sgrub dar rgyas pas gsol ba btab pa'i ngor chos sde lho byang bcas tshogs chen la gsung ngag rin po che bka' drin bstsal/ sbrul zla lug gsum gyi lo 'di rnams
la gdan sa phu mda' sogs su'ang mi grub chen 'gro 'dug mang skyon gyis phru ma sgrub sde'i sngags 'chang chen po'i sgrub chu gting skam byung ba/ rje nyid

skyed ltas su thugs dam bskang gsor phebs skabs chu shul der phyag nas mdzad pas sngar bzhin babs/ lo 'di gsum la dbus gtsang du mu ge chen po byung ba sems can spyi mthun
gyi las dbang bzlog dkar gyur kyang thugs bskyed rgya chen pos gdan sa'i gtsug lag khang rnams su re mos su phebs te lus can spyi'i phan bder dmigs maNDal thugs smon sogs
smin rgyas dang / mgon khang rnams su'ang yul phyogs la bde skyid 'byung ba'i thugs smon rtag 'grus su gnang / dgung lo zhe bdun pa chu lug lor snron zla'i nyer gcig bla
mchod 'bum thang du gnang nyin/ sa chen dang rtse mo'i sku 'bum gnyid las bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun dngas la mang ba nyin gnyis su babs shing sprel lo nas lo yang shin tu legs/
de nas 'bum thang la zhig gsos phul du byung ba 'di gnang nas gdung rten rnams las sngon dus khrus chu 'byung ba bar skabs rgyun chad kyang de nas bzung deng sang yang
sa chen yab sras gsum gyi sku 'bum las khrus chu rgyun mi 'chad pa'i ngo mtshar 'di byung ngo / /de bzhin du 'phags pa rin po che'i phyi rten gser 'bum gyi gtsug lag khang
rten dang brten pa nyams gso dang mchod pa'i yo byad du ma 'bul bar gnang / de skabs sgo rum du bdun phrag gcig

bcad rgya gnang skabs gzigs snang thun mong ma yin pa 'ga' zhig kyang byung / de lo hor yul nas mi dbang go dan gyi gdung brgyud stobs kyi dbang phyug gong ma bdag po chen
po bho kha tho zhes pa rje 'di nyid kyis snyan pas thugs dad gting nas g.yos te spyan 'dren du btang ba'i zhu yig tu/ dpal ldan sa skya pa chen po'i drung du/ da'i ching
zhes pa'i yul dang rgya cher brtse zhing kun dang mthun pa'i dam pa mchog gi rgyal pos zhu yig 'bul 'bras/ nga sngon gyi rgyal po rnams kyi bka' bzhag bzhin gzhung dang bstan
pa spel bar bsam nas/ 'gro ba mngon par 'dren thub pa'i mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i bla ma spyan 'dren pa'i phyir bang phyin pa btang yod/ bang phyin pa'i ming ni
phyi gan dge slong / pa rAon dge slong / grags pa dge slong / nam phyi dge slong / na ma gan dge slong / bsam gtan dge slong / kun dga' chos rgyal dge slong rnams yin/
gzhan tshig don bang phyin pa'i ngag na gsal/ zhu yig rten mtshon dngul gyi ka to ra gcig dngul gyi gdong mo gcig ma na ho'i phor chung gcig shel gyi phor chung gcig shel
dkar gyi phor chung gsum/ shel dkar gyi dam be gcig gser rgyab pa'i khrab gcig gser rgyab pa'i rmog gcig sag thag rkos ma gcig

mda' gzhu bcas/ gser rgyab pa'i sga srab rkos ma gcig gser gyi kha sgor rgyab pa'i shel gyi ske rags gcig shang lang brkos ma gcig kha thi yug gcig phul/ dam pa'i yon tan mnga'
ba'i gdan sa lo brgyad pa'i chu mo lug gi lo'i dbyar zla 'bring po'i ches lnga la/ zhes pa'i zhu yig dang / zhu yig tu ma 'khod pa'i gos dar gser dngul mu tig sogs dngos
spyad blos mi dpog pa dang / bang phyin gyi gtso bo rgyal po rang gi ti shri bkur ba'i se chen bla mar grags pas sger du 'bul ba rgya chen dang / lhag tu rje 'di'i zhal
mjal thengs re la gzi mdangs mi 'dra ba re mthong bas yid 'phrog ste dad gus dpag tu med pa byas/ 'on kyang de skabs gdan sa'i chos srid kyi thugs khur che bas phebs
thabs ma byung yang lugs gnyis kyi skyes lon thugs kha rdzogs par mdzad/ dgung lo grangs zhe dgu par shing bya lor rgyud sde'i dkyil 'khor bdun cu don gsum/ de dag gi rgyud
rim zhing bkod sogs bris thang thog tshad nyi rtsa gcig ljags bkod phun tshogs su sgrub par mdzad nas rab gnas smin rgyas su gnang / dgung lo lnga bcu pa me khyi lor bsam
yas nas chos skyong chen pos lo 'dir dge bshes la sku dog chen po yod pas rgyab brten ma nyung tsam dgos tshul zhu 'phrin phul ba ltar/ mgo zla'i nang

dgun chos grol ba'i nub mo nas sngar gyi rgyas 'khrugs kyi bsnyun ro langs nas sku khams cher ma bde ba'i skabs gzigs snang du 'phags pa rin po ches phyogs bzhi nas bkra shis
mdzad pa shar shing / tshal gtar nyis brgyud dang gsol sman sogs 'phrod bzhes gseng shor med pa dang / dgon sde brgya lhag la mang 'gyed sogs sku rim stobs che stabs bsnyun
gzhi las grol ba'i dga' ston dang skyon sel thun mong du/ me phag zla ba dang po'i nang ser skya mtha' dag la sbyin gtong rgya chen zhig bstsal ba'i tshogs dbur rje
nyid phebs nas dge rtsa rdzogs byang du bsngo ba gnang / sa byi lor bsam yas chos skyong chen po nas sgar chen rin po che'i drung du yang gong bzhin zhus pa sogs/ gong grub
mchog nyid kyi rnam thar du bshad pa bzhin dang lo khongs 'dir snga mo nas gnas 'brug thugs khang khems che zhing / lha 'brug thugs snang ma dag par brten lha gnas gnyis
ka lho nang nas bton pa bod rgyal po mchod yon la mgo gtad zhus pa bzhin gyi rgyab dpung la bod nas 'brug par dpung 'jug thengs gnyis mdzad par snga mar yang sde pa 'brong
rtse ba sogs bzung btsir khag pos jus legs rang ma byung na'ang / rjes ma zla ba bcu pa'i nang dpung shin tu

mang po bcas thon par rje 'di nyid thugs rje'i shugs kyis chings 'dum la phebs te/ phag rir gu shri rgyal po'i sras dang dga' ldan po brang nas phyag mdzod chen mo mchod yon
zhal 'dzom la bod dpung bsdu dgos tshul gnang bar/ 'brug pa nas dang len yin lugs byung na bka' phebs bzhin byed zhu ba las dpung bsdu bkod ma gnang bar brten/ slar spa
To nang du phebs te lho bod gnyis kar phebs sgo zhib gsed gnang yang go ba 'thebs pa zhig ma byung ba'i skabs/ bod dmag rnams gsang stabs su bsdu bar mdzad pas rta rkang
mgyogs bul gyi bar khyad rta pa phal cher spa To'i stong du 'byor dus/ rkang thang stong phrag tsam yod pa spa To'i skad pa tsam du slebs skabs 'brug dmag gi rjes gnon slebs
te/ lho nang gi mi rnams bod dmag gsod pa la rngams pas thams cad gron chen du gtong rtsis la/ rje 'dis lho'i dmag dpon 'brug pa'i dbu che chos rje la sngon sar bod
dmag rnams gtong dgos tshul phebs pa de nyid nas kyang bka' bstsal dang len gyis da lam khyod tshor srog skyon las thar ba 'di sa skya bdag chen gyi bka' drin yin pas shes
par gyis shig zer nas bde bar btang bas bod dmag rnams kyis kyang sku drin tshad med du shes pa byung / de dus nyid kyi sku dog 'gyur ba'i rnam pas phyag mdzod

chen mo sku ma 'tsho bar rje nyid nas 'pho ba gsol 'debs gsung chog byang bzhu smin pa gnang ba nas bzung / phyis su gdan sar phebs nas pur bzhu grub mtshams rje nyid kyis
rus chog bcas phyag tsha gnang nas khang brtsegs su bzhugs pa dang / re zhig gi bar du grong dus kyi dge rtsa cho ga smon lam bstar chags dang / gzhan yang kun rig cho ga
stong tshar/ bde can smon lam dang bzang spyod 'bum ther sogs rje nyid kyi ye shes kyi gzigs yul dang / gzhan yang brtag pa mngon shes bcas nas mkha' spyod kyi go 'phang
thob ste dag pa'i sprul pa skye nus kyi mtshan ma rnyed kyi bar du blos dpag par dka' ba'i bsags sbyangs bsgrubs par gnang / de rjes chos sde lho byang sogs dad 'dus mang
bar bde gshegs sman bla mched bdun gyi rjes gnang da nga/ mdo chog gi ljags lung sogs bka' chos shin tu mang po bstsal/ ston ka thugs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gtsos gzhis
byes don gnyer snod ldan mang por kyai rdor rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' dang / srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi khrid bka' sogs shin tu gsang ba'i
snyan brgyud skor dpag tu med pa'i dbang khrid lung bcas lhug bstsal gnang / gsang khrid kyi skor

sngar phan snod ldan bcu phrag lhag par mi gnang ba'i bka' rgya yod pa bzhin/ 'di ras kyang bka' yangs dogs kyi mtshan ltas gzigs pa'i mnal lam du 'jam dgon bsod nams dbang
po 'di nyid sku gzi mdangs 'bar bas zhabs gnyis ka rje nyid kyi dbu thog tu bzhag ste brgyud pa'i byin rlabs bka' bsgo smin rgyas stsal ba zhig byung bas ga tsam la gnang
yang 'tshub cha med par thugs thag chod kyang / slar zab chos khrom sgrags kyi rgyun 'byams kyis dgos pas lnga bcu skor la gnang / zla ba bcu pa'i nang du'ang thugs sras
'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gtsos gzhis byes ser skya brgya phrag du mar gur drag gi dbang bskur ba stsal/ dgung lo nga bzhi pa lcags stag lor thugs sras rin po ches gtsor mdzad
gzhis byes shin tu mang po gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa tshogs bshad kyi smin khrid dang / slob bshad lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi lung khrid rgyab
chos lung gi rigs phyag bzhes rnam dag ltar lam sbas bshad ma gtogs smin cing rgyas pa gsang ba bcus rgyas btab dang bcas zla ba gsum gyi bar du zab chos kyi 'khor lo rgya
chen po bskor/ sa chen gyi sku brnyan gser zangs kyis che legs can grub par rab gnas gnang / bcom mda' mkhan po dkon mchog 'phel ba dang slob dpon

byams pa rgyal mtshan dpon slob rnams la kyai rdo rje rgyu dbang / khrid yig sbas don gsal ba/ pod dmar ma'i ljags lung sogs sger du bstsal/ gzhan de rigs 'gro don 'os pa 'ga'
la khrid brgya cha lag bcas sogs gnang / 'di lo mdar grangs mo cher tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho dang thugs sras rta ra ba bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis kyi sku gdung
la rkyen cher med par me mchod bzhes pa'i gdung rus rnams grangs chen dpon slob rnams nas rje 'di nyid kyi phyag tu phul bar rje nyid nas phyag tsha gnang ste dngul gdung
ngo mtshar ba gsar bzhengs su bzhugs nas rab gnas zin pa dang khong dpon slob rnams kyis phyir gdan 'dren zhus/ de gong sku gdung la me shor ba'i gnas tshul sang 'byor rgyu'i
de nub dzA gi sma ra can ras gos gyon pa zhig gis rgya gar gyi phug ron yin zer ba gnyis bzung nas 'di gnyis bzhes dgos zhu bar/ cung zad thugs 'dzems nyams kyis ma
bzhes pa'i bar der phug ron gnyis po ka ba la sbyar song bar gnyis kas ka ba la 'chang nas bsdad 'dug pa dang / dzA ki'i gzhogs na nnghe gzugs bong che ba zhig ngo nong
tsam byas nas cang mi zhu bar 'dug pa zhig byung bar/ dzA ki de tshar chen yab sras gnyis la chos srung 'khor nyams che bas sku gdung

la'ang de bzhin 'khor ba dang / phug ron gtad pa de gdung rus 'byor nas dad bzhes dgos pa dang / bandhe ngam nag de tshar chen nyid la beg tse 'khor nyams shin tu che bas sku
gdung zhu ba de la yid pham tshod du 'dug gsungs/ dgung lo nga lnga lcags yos lor thug sras rin po che 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug zhal snga nas dgungs grangs bcu
bzhi phebs pas khri 'don gyi mdzad tshul 'og 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar dang / de skabs rta zla'i tshes gnyis nas bcu gcig gi
bar la khri ston zhu mi'i gras nas rgyal byang gi zhabs drung bla ma khu dbon/ ngam ring / dwags po grwa tshang / gur pa grwa tshang / kha ba lhas/ rgyas chos/ ya ma bde
ldan sogs kyi bla ma slob dpon grwa dmangs chos 'dod pa mang por khrid brgya cha lag bcas sogs lung khrid rjes gnang gang 'dod re skongs su stsal/ khri ston rjes nyin rje
nyid yab sras lhan cig chos khrir phebs nas de skabs kyi mchod sbyin nam mkha'i mdzod sgo phye ba thams cad bstan 'gro'i bde skyid 'phel zhing / 'brel thogs rnams kyi
dge rtsa rdzogs byang du bsngo bar mdzad/ dgung lo nga drug pa chu 'brug lor thugs sras rin po che sogs dad 'dus skal ldan rnams la sgrub brgya rgyam sogs dbang

lung du ma gnang / dar rtse mdo nas sa yam gnyer pa dpal ye mjal zhu ched gtad du 'bul chen bcas 'byor bar rdo rje phur pa stod las kyi dbang sogs chos kyi bdud rtsi rgya cher
stsal zhing / lha khang chen mo'i khyams stod kyi gyang ris rnams grub ste rab gnas stsal/ nyang stod rtse chen nas bla gra thams cad kyi zhus ngor 'jam dbyangs bsod
nams dbang phyug dral lcam dang / mkhan chen bsam gtan rgya mtsho sogs 'dus tshogs mang por gsang chen mkha' spyod bsgrub pa'i myur lam thun mong ma yin pa nA ro mkha' spyod
kyi byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba sngon du 'gro bas bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid rim rgyas pa lam gyi yan lag rnams gsal zhing khyer bde bar nyams khrid dang /
de dag gi rgyab brten yig cha rnying gsar du ma'i ljags lung / bde mchog rtsa rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa'i lung bshad rgyas pa/ grub brgya'i rjes gnang rtogs brjod
sogs grub brgya'i chos bskor yongs rdzogs/ sbyongs rgyud kyi lung bshad/ gcod yul gyi byin rlabs khrid lung mtha' mchod sogs dbang bka' khrid lung brjod du mi langs pa zhig
gnang / 'di lo byang bdag kun dga' bsod nams grags pa ched phebs kyi gzhis byes kyi chos nyan pa du mar gsung ngag rin po che smin rgyas su gnang /

dgung lo nga bdun pa chu sbrul lor mdo khams nas a li chos rje dpon slob stobs chen zhabs drung du 'bul chen dang chos sder mang 'gyed rgya chen bsgrub par 'byor bar chos dang
zang zing gi re ba bkang / de lo dgun grom pa rgyang nas mkhan chen mang thos grags pa rnam rgyal gdan sa 'dir chos rje sa paN nas brgyud pa'i sdom rgyun 'dzugs par byon
dgos tshul gsungs pa ltar byon skabs byang nas bdag po kun dga' bsod nams grags pa gzhis byes kyi dge 'dun nyis brgya lhag tsam sdom rgyun de nyid kyis bsnyen par rdzogs
par mdzad/ de lo dpyid thog tsam nas phyag sor cung zad ma bde bar/ gsung las 'di bsam yas chos skyong chen pos nged maunggal gyi bu'i skye ba yin zer ba ltar sngon tshe
rabs gzhan zhig na rang gi pha ma gnyis nyin mo dga' mgur spyad pa la ma dad nas yan lag 'dam bu ltar gzhom par bya ba khyod gnyis lta bu'i pha ma dang mi 'phrad par
gyur cig ces byas pa'i 'bras bu tshe rabs thams cad du myong ba'i las kyi lhag ma yin par snang zhes gsungs/ ston ka thub pa 'od zer 'gyed dang lung bstan sgrol ma sogs rten
mchog khyad par can gsar rnying sger btus kyis gtsug lag khang zhig grub na dgongs par gzhan tshos 'di lo khang las mi rung ba'i rgyu mtshan du mas bshol btab

skabs mnal lam du mi zhig gi gser gyi za ma tog mdzes shing 'od 'bar ba zhig phul nas/ 'di sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung bzhug sa pa'i gtsang khang mdzad du gsol zhu ba zhig
byung bas gtsug lag khang mthar phyin 'grub par mkhyen te de 'phral bla ma lha khang dang mgon khang khyad 'phags gnyis bzhengs pa'i mgo btsugs/ lo rjes ma dgung lo nga brgyad
pa shing rta lo'i dbyar ka rten dang brten pa ngo mtshar can 'di nyid grub nas rab gnas rgyas par gnang / 'di lo 'bras spungs nas rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen
po mchod yon gzhis ka rtser phebs par/ rje nyid nas bstan pa spyir sger gyi la rgyar dgongs te bsam 'grub rtser phebs/ rgyal po chos yon so so nas phebs bsu dang zhabs
tog phul phyin mdzad/ rje nyid nas kyang mchod yon so sor gnang skyes rgya dpangs che bar stsal nas mjal phrad kyi tshe phan tshun thugs snang dag pa'i bag phebs kyi gsung
gleng dang / khyad par rgyal dbang mchog dang mdo sngags chos kyi 'bel gtam mdzad pas thugs phrogs te rje 'di nyid la bsngags brjod ci yang mdzad pa ni rgyal mchog de
nyid kyi rnam thar sogs gsung rab na gsal/ de skabs phyogs dus kyi sla dpon ser skya shin tu mang

por ji ltar gsol ba'i 'dod chos re skong du bstsal/ 'bul ba yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / rim gyis bar rnams su chos sbyin bstsol bzhin pas Da Di mgon khang du phebs/
gsung bskang 'phrin bcol rgyas par gnang / de nas gdan sar phebs/ dgung lo nga dgu pa dang drug cu pa gnyis la/ snga phyir byang nas bdag po kun dga' bsod nams grags pa/
sle lung mkhan po/ ngor gyi zur 'chad pa chos rje bsod nams rgya mcho/ lha khang mkhan che bsam gtan rgya mcho/ zangs ldan bla ma byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ rgyal rtse
bla ma rin chen byam pa rgyal mtshan sogs la rgyud sde du ma zhig gi dbang khrid man ngag rjes gnang bshad lung sogs bsam gyis mi khyab zhig stsal ba 'dir brjod du ma
lang / me spre lar khams dar rtse mdo nas mi 'phrog pa'i dad ldan bstan pa'i sbyin bdag mo sa yang mo rtse o rgyan 'tsho mo ma bu gsum g.yog 'khor stobs chen bcas 'byor nas/
gdan sa gzhung du dar gos ja sogs 'bul ba spom mtho ba dang / lha khang chen mos gtsos pa'i gtsug lag khang so sor mchod pa'i yo byad rgya chen/ 'dus tshogs la mang ja
gral 'gyed sogs phal pa'i blos mi 'khyud

pa'i bsnyen bkur byung bar/ bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang khrid/ jo bo'i chos 'byung brgya rtsa/ blo sbyongs sogs zab cing rgya che ba'i chos bka' dpag tu med pas rjes 'dzin
dang dpon g.yog tshang mar zang zing gi gnang stsal rgya chen pos kyang yid spro bar mdzad do/ /skabs shig thub stan nas grwa skor ba byams chos pa kun dga' bsod nams
grwa skor grub nas 'gro grabs la bshol nas chos zhu ba 'ga' dang lhan cig dbang lung khrid bshad rgyun ring gnang grub nas/ byams chos pa la 'o kha sing nas sdod zer ba
yang khyod bstan pa la phan pa zhig e yong bsam pa yin/ gzhon pa tshos kyang bstan pa spyi dang bye brag kun mkhyen chen po'i bstan pa la bsam nas bshad sgrub dang 'chad
nyan sogs la brtson par bya dgos sogs phebs sgo ci mang zhig stsal bar mdzad pa/ de dus byams chos pa 'chad nyan kyi go sa med kyang / phyis su srid gsum rnam rgyal gyi
slob dpon dang / thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi khams pa grwa tshang gi slob dpon bstan pa la phan slebs can byung ba yang 'byung 'grur lung bstan du gsal lo/ /gzhan yang snod
ldan rags bsdus shig la chig brgyud kyi tshul du rje tshar pa'i ha la nag po'i be bum kha bskong dang bcas pa stsal/

zla ba brgyad pa'i nang lho bod sems can spyi mthun gyi las skal snyigs pa'i skyon dang / sa mtshams su gnas pa'i mi re gnyis kyi byed spyod la brten/ dbyings sa nas kyang
thugs rgyal cher bzhengs pa'i gtsang dbus khams gsum hor sog bcas dmag dpung shin tu che bar spa gro'i mthil du brdzangs par/ chos rje 'brug pa phyogs nas kyang / sa btsan
mgo khur lta bus 'gug thub pa zhig ma byung gshis/ bod dmag byings nas mgrin gcig tu rje 'di nyid la gsol ba btab kyang re zhig dus la ma bab par gzigs na'ang dmag mi rnams
dbugs dbyung ba'i phyir sngon la mi sna sbrel po zhig gnang / de rjes rje nyid nas lha dang srung mar gsol smon 'phrin bcol phur tshugs mdzad pa'i skabs mnal lam zhig
du/ nyid kyi sku 'khor 'ga' zhig gis khrol ma chen po bzhi'i nang du bye'u rad rod shi la khad mang pos gang bar phul byung bar/ rje nyid kyis byin rlabs mdzad pas thams
cad gsos te 'phur song ba zhig byung bas/ skabs don gyi phrin las 'grub par thugs thag chod nas zla ba bcu pa'i tshes gsum la chibs bsgyur/ lam bar rnams su zhabs 'degs
dang 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / dad ldan du mar chos kyi sbyin pa re skong du gnang nas/ phag ri bsam grub lha khang du

phebs/ mkhan chen bsam gtan rgya mtsho spa gro'i lho bod gyi dmag dpon so sor skyes gnang dang chings 'dum kyi bka' lung bcas rdzong bda' gnang / phag ri phyogs kyi skye bo
mang por thugs rje chen po tshems bu lugs kyi dmar khrid sogs dbang lung 'khrid rim dpag med gnang / ma Ni dung phyur gyi khas len mang po dang / srog gcod spang ba'i dam
bca' sogs 'gro ba mang po'i rgyud la thar pa'i sa bon shin tu smin par mdzad/ rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams la bskang gso 'phar ma dang / skabs babs kyi 'phrin bcol nar mar
gnang ba'i skabs shig mnal lam du/ gur mgon zhal dkyil 'od du 'bar ba can zhig dang / pu tra zhal khyim zla ba ltar dkar zhing spyan gsum gser mig 'khyil pa zhig gzigs/
yang lan cig zhing skyong bram ze'i gzugs can sku mdog sngon po rol stabs kyi bzhugs pa zhig gzigs pa dang / yang mnal lam zhig tu bya rog shin tu chen po zhig gis gcan
gzan stag gcig sder mos khyer nas lcags mchu rnon pos 'debs bzhin pas stag de shi la khad pa'i ro'i rnam pa de skyed lhas mgon khang gi rgyab kyi brag logs der skyur nas
bya rog de bya rog chen po gnyis su gyur nas zhabs drung du byung bar bshos chang mang po zhig gnang ba byung ba dang / yang mnal lam zhig

tu/ yab rje rin po che'i phyag tu srog chags sdig pa zhig bsnams 'dug pa de dang lhan cig sdom kha brgyad sogs srog chags ma rung ba du ma zhig me la btab song ba dang sngog
dud kyis lung pa khengs shing / me de tshom bar gyi mgon khang du skyol cig gsung ba zhig byung ba/ snga phyi'i mnal lam gyi 'bras bu/ lho bod bde thabs dge 'brug 'ching
'doms bsgrub dgongs pa la log sgrub rnams bla ma lha yis bsgral ba'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar ba'o/ / de mtshams spa gro nas mkhan rin po che sku khams ma bde bar rten sku
tshab gdan sa nas chos las pa bsod nams bkra shis yong dgos pa'i bka' shog gnang ba bzhin zhabs drung du 'byor 'phral gsungs las/ nged kyi rmi lam gyi dbang du song na/
lho bod kyi chings 'dum legs pa zhig 'ong ba yod na'ang sngar phan dge 'brug gnyis ka nas lab sne len pa zhig ni ma byung / spa gro nas mkhan chen 'dir 'byor ba dang bstun/
nged kyang na ring rdzong chung dgon par lus kyi 'tsho skyong dang / brel ba 'ga' zhig gcod par 'gro dgos pa 'dug cing / slar skabs bstun lho nang rang la 'gro dgos
'dug pas/ da ras nas bzung las chen pa rang mgo mjug tshang mar 'gro dgos pas 'jags par gyis zhes sogs gsung shin tu brling ba mang po bstsal/ de nas

zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nyer drug la mkhan chen yang zhabs drung du 'byor bstun/ dgung lo re gcig pa me bya zla ba dang po'i tshesabargyad la chibs bsgyur na ring rdzong chung
du phebs nas zla ba gnyis nyer bzhugs/ de phyogs ser skya khrom tshogs la dbang bka' dang / rags dus sger pa du mar dbang 'khrid chos bka' skal ba dang 'tshams par gnang
/ de skabs byang nas bdag po rin po che zhabs brtan 'bul du 'byor bar gsungs pa las/ nged rang rang lo'i thog yin kyang dog cha med/ mkhan chen la sku rkyen che tsam 'dug
gsungs/ de mtshams sngar gyi gsung 'phros bzhin/ 'gro ba nyams thag gi ched du nag zla'i tshes bcu gnyis la na ring nas chibs bteg ste/ phag rir zla ngo tsam bzhugs nas/
lho bod rdzong sgar so sor chings 'dum gyi bskor yang mdzad kyang / sne len zhig ma byung bar slar zla ba bzhi pa'i nang dpon slob rags bsdus spa gror phebs pas bod dmag
'dzin cha ba rnams srog rnyed pa lta bu'i dga' spror gyur/ spa gro'i mthil gyi bod dmag rnams sa dug dang / tshad nad rims du mas sdug bsngal bar gyur pa'i tshe/ rje nyid
nas sku 'khor rnams la nang re bzhin ljags chab bstsal bas nyes pa gtan nas ma byung zhing / dmag

sgar byings kyi mgo dpon nas kyang chu gtsang la ljags chab zhus rigs stsal bas nad 'phro chad cing na bar 'phral sos gyur pas thugs rje mngon gyur byung / de nas sku dngos
dang / sku tshab kyis hU~M ral kha'i ljongs dang bod sgar gyi bar la bskor yang sna tshogs zhig mdzad pa'i mthar/ rje nyid dang / rtse gdong bdag chen rin po che byams pa
bsod nams lhun grub bcas khu dbon/ skyid shod zhabs drung / ngor dang bkra shis lhun po'i sku tshab bcas rdzong mdun du phebs te rje nyid nas 'brug pa'i kha lo ba rnams
la/ lar sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba la/ sems can la bde skyid dgos/ de la lho bod kyi mi chen rnams dgongs pa mthun dgos/ de byung na lho bod la bde skyid 'ong ba yin
pas/ nged yod thog lho lhor bde ba dang/ bod bod du bde ba mtha' gtsang gi gsal kha zhig ma byung na byas blo tsam gyis chings 'dum byed dgos mi 'dug pas/ de lugs lho bod
gnyis ka nas dgongs pa rgya bskyed dgos pa yin gsungs pa sogs brjid che ba gnang rjes/ 'brug pa'i kha lo pa rnams na re/ dpal sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs mi'i gzugs can mthong
thos 'brel tshad don ldan yin pas nged rnams bsod nams bsags/ sprel mo la tshun chad kyi bod dmag ka cha dang bcas pa nged rang dbang btsan par thob

zin na'ang / sa skya pas bod dmag thugs blos ma mthong bas nged kyi rdzong rtsa 'dir dbu gdugs skya ling nge yang yang phabs pa 'di shin du bag tsha ba'i bka' gnang dang len
gyis bod dmag ka cha dang bcas pa skya pa'i sku ngor 'bul ba yin zer/ de nas kyang rje nyid nas bka' nan mtha' btsan pas lho bod lo lha'i 'ching 'doms mdzad pas lho bod
kyi 'gro ba mtha' dag thar lam la bkod pa ltar dbugs phyin te rje nyid kyi phyogs su phyag 'tshal bskor ba gsol 'debs byed pa du ma byung ngo / /phyis kyang rgyun ring po'i
bar/ spre mo la mo de lcags kyi sgo lcags rang yin pa/ sgo lcags byed mkhan de bla ma sa skya pa yin pa/ zhes 'ur 'don du glu len pa byung zhing / 'brug pa nas kyang
rdzong dpon rigs dang sbyin bdag rnams nas bar 'ching grub pa'i legs 'bul bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'bul/ de nas zla ba drug pa'i ches drug la spa gro nas gdan bteg pas/ bod
dmag gi kha lo pa rnams nas dmag dpung ma rdzogs bar du bzhugs dgos zhus pa ltar/ bod dmag dud 'gro tsam la yang gnod pa med par bde bar phyin rjes rje nyid dpon slob rnams
kyang phebs/ de skabs gsung las/ da lam lho bod kyi sems can mang po la phan pa rgya chen po byung ba 'dir kho bo la nus pa de lta bu med kyang /

bla ma gong ma rnams kyi thugs rje dang chos skyong gi nus mthur snang / nged phar tshur 'gro phyogs la gzigs nas chos skyong rnams kyang mnyam du 'byon pa'i rmi lam rgyun
chags su yong gi 'dug ces gsungs/ dbyings sa phyag mdzod chen mo nas kyang bang phyin 'bul ba bcas pa'i zhu yig tu/ da lam 'gro phan la thugs 'gan tshad med pa bzhes nas
chings 'dum don 'khyol byung ba sku drin shin tu che bas ngos nas mjal thub zhig dgos kyang brel bas ma grub song bas/ slar dbus phyogs su mjal 'dug thog zhib rgyas phul
chog pa zhus/ de nas rim pas bya sper phebs nyin thugs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku 'khoor chab 'bangs bcas phebs bsur byon/ phyir nyin gdan sa nas phebs bsu'i bkod pa rgyas
pa dang bcas phebs nas/ chos sde dag la 'bras 'jam mang 'gyed sogs rgya cher gnang / ston mjug tu yar lung nas bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan sogs la
zab rgyas kyi chos 'khor bar ma chad du skor/ sngar dus mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags la sku tshe brtag par zhus pas drug cu rgal nas re gcig par sku rim skyid ston
sogs dgos tshul ltar 'di lo phyag len du theb par mdzad/

dgung lo re gnyis pa sa khyi lor yang zhabs drung bka' 'gyur ba chen po phebs par chos bka' du ma gnang / de nyid nas kyang rje 'di nyid la pha dam pa'i man ngag la brten pa'i
brtan bzhugs zab mo zhig phul te bstan 'gro'i don du dgung lo brgyad cu bzhugs pa'i zhal bzhes dgos zhes gsol ba btab pas/ rang re gnyis bzhugs na bzhugs mnyam byed gsungs/
lha sa nas rgyal po mchod yon gyi gdan 'dren pa 'byor bar phebs lam gyi sku rim la dgongs te 'dus tshogs la mang 'gyed rgya che ba'i thog tu/ tshe sgrol sher snying
'bum gter sogs gnang / rgyal zla'i nang shar du chibs bsgyur nas rim phebs kyis gzhis ka rtser sde bdag nor bu'i drung gi zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs/ de nas kyang
/ dpal 'khor chos sde/ yar 'brog sna dkar rtse/ skyed tshal 'og gong dkar chos sde sogs kyi bla dpon grwa dmangs rnams nas phebs bsu bsnyen bkur zhabs 'degs phul byung
kho na bsgrubs/ rje nyid nas kyang rang rang mos pa'i ngo bzhin chos sbyin stsal/ chu shul brgyud du ljangs su phebs skabs/ bud med gcig la glo bur du khog zhugs cig byung
te/ nga bsam yas nas bdag nyid chen po phebs bsu la yong ba yin/ zhabs drung du smon lam zhig 'debs par mthong zhes

gzim chung 'gag tu yus pa'i tshul gyis slebs byung bar/ 'gag pas sgor nas/ 'khor rnams kyi snyan 'bul zhus par/ gsung las/ bsam yas su nged 'phral du yong rtsis yod/ da lam
khams dub pas 'phrad mi thub kyis gsungs pa bzhin bka' bsgyur bas de ma thag rang yal du song ba de ni sngar sor dbus 'byon skabs kyi dar 'bog sku mi'i khog tu zhugs te
khung brtol mkhan gyi chos skyong gi 'khor de yin par 'dug gsung / de nas shun rdzong du phebs tshe rgyal dbang mchog mchod yon nas drung 'khor ser skya rags bsdus kyi chibs
su bka' drin bskyangs te lha sar phebs/ zhag gnyis pa'i thog gza' skar legs 'dzoms la rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa dbyings sa phyag mdzod chen mo dang bcas pas mjal
'phrad dga' ston gzab gshom mdzad de/ thugs nang gshin pa'i gsung gleng yang rgyun ring du gnang / sog po'i rgyal po rnams kyis kyang 'bul ba rgya cher phul/ de nas rje
nyid nas lha sa'i jo shAka rnam gnyis/ po ta la'i 'phags pa ba ti dang lo ke shwa ra sogs rten mchog rnams la mchod sprin dang bcas bstan 'gro spyi'i phan bder dgongs pa'i
gsol 'debs thugs smon smin rgyas su gnang / phyogs 'dus kyi sa 'brug rnying lugs bla chen mang podang / sna dkar rtse'i sde srid sogs ser

skya mang pos dad gus rtse gcig pas mjal kha dang bka' chos zhus 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ rje nyid nas smon lam chen mor mang 'gyed rnam bzhag stobs che ba dang
/ dbus phyogs kyi dgon sde che phra mtha' dag la mang 'gyed stsal/ de nas kyang bsam yas chos skyong chen pos 'phral 'byon zhu bar 'byor bstun/ mchod yon la yang de tshul
gnang bar/ rgyal dbang mchog dbyings sa phyag mdzod rin po che bcas nas 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ mchod yon gyi sku 'khor rags bsdus kyis gru kha bar phebs skyel
bka' drin bskyangs gnang cha gya nom pa stsal/bsam yas zung mkhar du phebs tshe mkhan tshang pa sogs phebs bsur 'byor phyir nyin ser phreng gi bkod pas/ skyid shod zhabs
drung nas kyang phebs bsu rgya chen dang bcas pho brang du phebs/ de'i sang nyin pe har lcog gi rtser bsangs mchod rgyas par gnang / chos skyong chen po yang 'phral du
rang phebs byung bar/ rje nyid dpon slob re zhig lcog gi phyir phebs/ chos skyong gi sku chas bzhes grub pa'i brda' sbyor dang bstun slar phebs tshe/ zhal ngo sngon ma rnams
la chos skyong gi phebs bsu rdo skas kyi mgo las byon srol med kyang / de nyin skas len la ring stabs rgyug 'dral dang bcas khyams ra 'og ma'i phyi sgo bar du phebs

bsur byon/ lha mi lhan cig rdo skas rtser phebs tshe/ chos skyong chen pos paNDi tas bstan pa dar ba'i phyir du lha rgyal thang gsum bos gsungs pa bzhin/ der tshogs mi khrom
dmar nag gi lha rgyal thang gsum bos nas lha mi gnyis khri'u chung so sor bzhugs par chos skyong nyid dad gus kyi rnam 'gyur sku 'khril 'khril 'dar ba dang bcas pas gsung
gleng mang du mdzad mthar/ sngon slob dpon padma'i phyag nas can gyi gdug 'dre'i sdig khrab sha gos dang bcas pa 'di la khyed sa skya dge bshes rnams ma gtogs sus kyang
zhig gsos mi gtubs pas da lan kyang de bzhin dgos pa dang / lcog gi yo byad rnams deb tu 'khod nas dge bshes kyi phyag dam 'byar ma dgos gsungs pa ltar 'phral bsgrubs gnang
nas/ deb yig mkhan tshang rab 'byams pa'i lag tu bzhag cing / tshes gsum nyin sku phebs gzab mar khrab gdan/ gsol khrab/ dbu rmog rnams gsol te nyams gso grub pa khrom
tshogs la ngom pa ltar gyi dgyes tshor mdzad/ rje nyid nas kyang rten rdzas yo byad spyan gzigs rgya chen stsal/ skyid shod zhabs drung yang dad spro'i thugs yid 'phrog
pas bka' chos mang po zhus/ sngon dus sa skya nas shi 'dre mang po lus ngan spang ste gnas spar ba'i snyan grags la brten kong po'i phyogs nas kar lugs pa'i zho kha

bla ma zer ba dbyings sa nas dgongs phog gi rkyen gyis stag rtse'i phyogs su shi ba dmod pa log pa'i mthus 'byung po stobs chen gdug pa can zhig tu gyur pas gtsos shi 'dre
mang pos de phyogs la shin tu gnod pas gnas spor ba zhus pa bzhin gsung chog gnang nas byang bu zhus tshe sha chen gyi dri bro ba dang bcas shi 'dre rnams mtho ris su bkod
pas chos skyong chen pos kyang stag rtse phyogs kyi 'byung po de rnams dge bshes kyi gnas spar song bas da phyin lha rten rnams shig mchod yar sogs dgos pa med ces khrom
bsgrags su gsungs/ de phyin chad 'byung po de rigs ming yang mi grags par gyur/ bsam yas rab byung chos sde'i grwa pa dang phyogs kyi don gnyer du mar kyai rdor rgyu dbang
gi gtsos pa'i dbang lung rgyun ring ba dang khrom tshogs khri phrag du mar tshe dbang khrom chos su stsal/ dbu rtse chen mor rab gnas rgyas pa dang / gling bzhi gling
phran nyams gso grub pa rnams la phyag nas smin rgyas mdzad/ dbo zla'i nyer dgu'i snga char chibs bsgyur rnam sras gling du phebs te sras yum la rjes gnang dang lung mtshan
'ga' zhig stsal/ de nas bye rdzing / gra thang / byams pa gling / rgya gling / dol/ ra ba smad/ dwags po grwa tshang / gong dkar rnams so

so nas ser phreng gi phebs bsu gzab bstar kho nas gdan drangs pa bzhin phebs nas mang 'gyed dang bka' chos kyis tshim par mdzad/ khyad par rdo rje gdan du zhag bcu gsum bzhugs
pa'i ring la chos rje bka' 'gyur ba bsod nams mchog ldan gyis dbus dad 'dus rnams la yi dam chos srung gi dbang bka' byin rlabs dpag tu med pa dang / chos sder mang ja
bcu gsum/ dam rdzas/ gser 'gyed sogs phun sum tshogs ba gnang / de nas chos rje bka' 'gyur ba sogs kyis gam pa byang thang bar phebs skyel zhus par/ rje nyid nas bka' 'gyur
ba la/ da 'di kha nas log phebs/ slar dag pa'i zhing du mnyam du 'gro 'on kyang rang re gnyis zla gcig tsam gyis snga phyi 'ong ngam gsungs pa dang sngar brtan bzhugs
phul dus kyi gsung gnyis mtshungs par phyis rje bka' 'gyur ba zhi bar gshegs rjes zhag nyer drug nas rje 'di nyid zhing khams brjes pa yin 'dug cing / phebs lam tu stag
khu spe'i bla grwa mjal bar slebs par chos bka' dang mang 'gyed gnang / skyed tshal du ser phreng bcas spyan drangs pa bzhin mang ja lnga dang 'gyed stobs chen gnang / dpal
de dang sna dkar rtser 'dod chos stsal zhing 'bul nod kyang rgya cher byung / rin spungs su skyed tshal gong ma'i bla grwa 'ga' zhig 'byor bar chos

bka' dang mang 'gyed gnang / rtse gdong du phebs bzhed chos du ma stsal cing zhal ngo thugs nang gcig 'dres kyi dga' ston gnang / rim pas gdan sar phebs/ dbyar smad du byang
nas bdag po rin po che dang / gong dkar nas sog po bla ma sogs gzhis byes mang por rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i nyams 'khrid sogs dbang lung tshan cher gnang / ston ka gser
mdog can mkhan po byon nas paN chen shAka mchog nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras zhus ngor/ 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug yab sras kyis gtsos pa'i chos zhu ba mang por/ gsung
ngag rin po che cha lag dang bcas pa stsal/ dgung lo re gsum pa sa phag lor bzang ldan nas mkhas grub ngag dbang rnam rgyal byon nas gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ 'jam dbyangs
bsod nams dbang phyug yab sras/ rje btsun ma/ rgyal yum zhal ngo rnams kyis gtsos rags bsdus shig la 'jigs byed rwa lugs rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi khrid dang / de'i yig skor
gyi lung sogs rgya cher stsal/ mgon khang srid gsum zil gnon gsar bzhengs grub par rab gnas mdzad/ de rjes nyis thog lha khang bzhengs skabs a tsa ra zhig gis 'jam dpal

nA ga raksha'i li sku khyad mtshar zhig dang / tsa tu rmu kha zer zhing zhal gyi rten rdo ngo mtshar ba rten rdzas bcas phul lo/ /de ltar sku tshe 'di nyid kyi mkhas dang grub
pa'i rnam thar rmad du byung bas bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po mdzad pa'i tshul de dag kyang 'khor lo gsum du mdor bsdu na/ nges don rgyal ba thams cad kyi yab/ dam pa'i
chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug 'phags mchog 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid las gzhan du ma dmigs kyang/ ston pa yang dag pa'i bstan pa'i khyad par rgyu med 'bras bu skye ba'i
snang tshul 'gog pa'i phyir du bslab sbyangs gsan bsam dpag tu med pa zhig mdzad pa'i tshul bstan pa'i rigs kyi bdag po ni 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ yab rje grags
pa blo gros/ grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug sku 'bring kun dga' dbang rgyal/ mus chen 'khor lo sdoms pa/ e waM thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / bdag chen 'jam pa'i
dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan
snga kun dga' don grub ste yongs su 'dzin pa bcu gnyis/ mnyes pa gsum gyi zhabs tog gi sgo nas mdo sngags gsar rnying dam pa'i chos kyi rgya

mtsho ji ltar gsan pa'i tshul ni gsan yig rin po che zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed du gsal ba ltar dang / ji ltar gsan pa de dag kyang thos thob kyi grangs 'dren pa
tsam ma yin par phal cher nyams bzhes smin rgyas su gnang ba yang dgu lo bcu gnyis par kyai rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen mthar phyin mdzad pa nas bzung / dus snga phyi ci rigs
par/ 'khor lo bde mchog phur pa/ 'jigs byed/ sgrol dkar/ rigs gsum mgon po/ gur drag 'jam dpal nag po/ seng gdong ma/ ku ru kulle/ khyung nag tshogs bdag bstan srung gur
zhal rnam gnyis sogs kyi grangs dus mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa bzhugs gdan thog re rer smin rgyas gnang zhing / rgyun gyi thugs dam nar mar yang / tho rengs ldang ba'i rnor nas
bzung tshe sgrub chig brgyud ma/ bir srung / lam zab/ dkar cha bzhi/ lam dus rgyas pa brda' chig brgyud bcas/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i mngon rtogs/ nA ro mkha' spyod 'pho
ba'i rnal 'byor bcas/ 'byung 'dul/ bsrung 'khor brag rdzong ma/ bla ma rin 'byung / zhal gyi tshe sgrub/ seng 'dong rnam 'joms/ dzam nag/ u tsi'i sngags ring thung / sme
brtsegs sogs dang / phyis su li ma lha khang dang rgya nag lha khang sogs gsar bzhengs mdzad zin nas de dag dang / gzim chung

rten gsum sogs la bla ma so so'i gsol 'debs sogs zhal 'don bcas phyag bskor mang pograngs tshad nges can dang / gzhan yang bzang spyod/ byams smon/ bde can smon lam/ mngon
dga'i smon lam gsung rtsom can sogs bshags pa dang smon lam shin tu mang po dang / thugs brel che ba med phyin phyag dpe shog bu re thugs 'dzin chags med dang / phyi dro
yang lam zab lam dus sogs phal cher bsngo smon yan chad dang / dbyug gu ma'i bzlas pa/ phur chung / gtor bsngo/ bskang gso/ de nas gsung bzlas chag med la/ yang dag gi snying
po/ phur pa/ bde mchog/ kyai rdor yabayum gsang 'dus/ gshed dmar 'jigs byed/ gu ru zhi drag gur zhal/ 'jam dpal nag po/ seng gdong ma/ dbyug gu ma/ ku ru kalle/ dzaM
dmar rnams kyis ljags bzlas dang / de nas gcod gdan thog gcig ma bcas 'di rnams dgung lo nyer lnga nas gdan sa'i chos srid kyi thugs 'gan bzhes phyin gyi sku tshe'i ring
gi nyams bzhes chag med phal cher smos pa yin gyis/ nyer lnga yan la de dag nyis ldab sum ldab tu gnang ba zhib pa ni gsung tho zhib par ltar ro/ /de dag gi rgyun bsnyen
nyung thal rnam kyang 'bru 'bum ma song

ba med cing / mgon po'i yi ge bdun la bye ba gnyis tsam/ yi ge bcu gnyis ma dang shA sa na 'bum phrag du ma/ chos srung so so'i bskang gso khri tshar mang po gtsug lag khang
rnams su bla ma'i rnal 'byor la brten pa'i maNDal gsol 'debs smon lam rnams 'bum phrag lhag pa dang / bzang spyod khri tshar phyed gnyis lhag tsam/ sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya
khri phrag du ma rnams zhal 'don dang / gzhan la yon dmar bar gnang nas bsnyen pa byed du 'jug par mdzad pa la oM gsum ma bye ba sum cu/ ma Ni dung tshar nyi shu rtsa
gnyis/ bzang spyod 'bum ther kha shas/ sdig bshags smon lam ljags rtsom ma 'bum ther/ rnam rgyal gyi gzungs ring dang tshe gzungs rnams kyang shin tu mang po bsgrubs pa
sogs thun mong gi rnal 'byor dang / khyad par gnas skabs kyi 'khor yug thams cad du mnyam rjes gnyis su med par snang grags rig gsum yi dam lha'i sku gsung thugs su dgongs
pa'i rim gnyis zab mo'i rnal 'byor la gcig tu goms pa'i 'khrul zad grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar bzang po kho na bdag gir bzhes pas thugs dam lam rtags kyang rtsa
gsum lha'i zhal gzigs lung bstan bar ma chad pa dang / 'gro ba gzhan gyi 'byung 'gyur bde sdug skye gnas lkog gyur mngon par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pa sogs grub

pa mchog gi go 'phang mngon du mdzad na'ang gdul bya dad gus snod dang ldan pa pa rnams spro ba skyed pa'i ched dang / log lta can rnams yang dag pa'i lam du bkri ba'i don
dang / the tshom can rnams nges shes bskyed pa'i dgos pa khyad par can de dag gi skabs su mtshon bstan ni rtogs brjod chen mor gsal zhing / shin tu gsang ba'i gzigs snang
gi skor 'ga' zhig ni der yang bkod du rung bar ma gnang zhing / de min rgyun gyi kun spyod gang zag dkyus ma'i lugs kyis thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan mngon
'gyur ga 'dra zhig yin kyang gnas dus skal ba gzhan la zhal g.yar ba'i kho bo la de 'dra ga la yod gsung nas sbas tshul kho na gnang ngo / /de ltar gsan bsam nyams bzhes
kyis gtan la phab pa'i chos tshul de dag kyang rgyal bstan rin po che'i rgyun la dgongs te gzhis byed thams cad du sku tshegs la ma ltos par chos kyi 'khor lo bar ma chad
du bskor bar mdzad pas 'chad nyan bstan 'gror sman pa'i zhal slob rags par yang rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug rtse gdong bdag chen byams pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen ngag dbang lhun grub mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/

shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar kha chos rje 'phags pa tshul khrims khu dbon/ dgon gsar chos rje ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bzang ldan chos rje kun dga' dpal 'bar/
khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ glang bu chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug ngam ring mkhan chen tshul khrims rgyal po dang / klu grub
dar rgyas gnyis/ ngor e waM chos rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ de nyid dbon po/ zur 'chad pa bsod nams rgya mtsho sogs dang / thub bstan mkhan chen bzod pa rgya mtsho/ kong
ston don grub dpal bzang / mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan rdor sogs dang / gser mdog can mkhan po lcags 'dam pa shAkya bstan 'dzin/ brag dmar mkhan po 'jam dbyangs phun
tshogs/ thub bstan yangs pa can gyi chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos bzang / bya rgod gshong chos rje grags pa rnam rgyal/ lung phu chos rje byams pa rgyal mtshan/ rdzong dga'
ldan gyi gdan sa pa ngag dbang dpal ldan/ sle lung mkhan po sangs rgyas rab brtan/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi rin chen sgang pa/ gser gling chos rje/ nam mkha' mdzod pa/
rnam mkhyen grong pa/ ra ba smad chos rje dkon mchog dpal 'byor/ dgas po grwa tshang gi slob dpon blo gros brtan pa/ bsam

yas rab byung gi gdan sa pa kun dga' bzang po/ gcod yul grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje dgra lha ba/ dar mdo pa yam chos rje kun dga' lhun grub/ lcags la bla ma chos rgya mtsho
rnams dang / sgrub rgyud bstan pa'i mnga' bdag lnga rig smra dbang 'brug pa sangs rgyas rdo rje/ snga 'gyur bstan pa'i gsal byed yol mo sbrul pa'i sku sku mched sogs
grub mtha' gzhan dag gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma dang gdan sa 'di nyid kyi lha khang mkhan rin po che rin chen blo gros/ byams pa phun tshogs rin chen/ byams pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ byams pa bsam gtan rgya mtsho/ byams pa bsod nams bkra shis te mkhan rab snga phyi rnams dang / rgya tsho dpon chos las pa sogs dang / gong du bgrangs pa
de rnams kyang 'gro phan nus pa gtso bor smos pa tsam ste/ chos sde de dag dang gzhan yang / mus/ ya ma bde ldan/ chos 'khor lhun po/ kha ba lha sa/Da Di chos rdzong/ bzhed
ri skyed tshal/ bcom mda'/ rgya skabs nor bu gling rnams kyi so so'i bla ma dbon brgyud/ zur 'chad/ grwa rigs bgrang gis mi lang ba rnams la skal ba dang 'tshams pa'i
chos 'khor skor ba'i rnam grangs brjod kyis mi lang ba sa bcas gtso bor gsung ngag rin po che tshogs bshad cha lag rgyab brten lung dang bcas pa tshar bcu/ gsang chen

slob bshad tshar gsum/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi 'khrid/ bde mchog nag po rim bzhi/ zhen pa bzhi bral/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ gsang 'dus 'gos lugs/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid
tshem bu lugs/ gcod khrid/ blo sbyong rnams lan grangs mang po dang / 'khrid brgya cha lag bcas tshar bdun sogs nyams 'khrid rgya che ba du ma dang / gsang 'khrid gzhan
dang gur mgon phyi nang gsang gsum gyi zab 'khrid sogs kyang snod dang sbyar ba'i tshar mang / gzhan yang lung 'khrid lung bshad nyams 'khrid phran bu sogs shin tu mang
po dang / kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang / rgyu dbang/ lam dbang / bdag med ma'i dbang / gsang bde 'jigs gsum/ yang phur gur drag sogs bla med gsar rnying gi dbang bskur
rigs grangs mang ba dang / byin brlab dang rjes gnang gi rigs ni bgrang bar dka' ba sogs dbang khrid man ngag lung bshad gang yang go rim phyag len gzhung tshad ma 'brel
dgos/ bod gzhung yang rgya gzhung tshad ma dang 'brel dgos/ rgya gzhung yang rgyud dang 'brel dgos gsungs pa'i zhal gdams dang bcas/ bstan pa rin po che'i rgyun 'chol
gyis dogs pa spyan 'bras bzhin du gces spras ngos rtogs bzo sla chos dang mi 'os pa'i rigs 'gre rgyas 'geb phra mo tsam yang mi

mdzad pa mtha' bzhi dang snyan brgyud bzhi sogs kyi bshad pa dang 'brel bar 'doms par mdzad cing / de dag gi phyag bzhes kyi rgyun yang rgya bod mkhas grub rig 'dzin rim brgyud
rje nyid kyi yongs 'dzin rnams kyi bar rgyud gzhung gi dgongs pa bzhin bzhugs pa mi nub pa'i ched dang thun mong ba'i bstan bcos 'ga' zhig bcas gsung rtsom gnang bar
yang / bstod tshogs gsol 'debs smon lam rigs brgya dang nyi shu tsam/ nyams dbyangs zhal gdams chab shog skor chos tshan brgya phrag nye ba/ rje nyid kyi gsan yig glegs
bam gcig bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar rigs nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ mdo phyogs kyi bstan bcos nyi shu rtsa gsum/ chos 'byung pod longs bcu bzhi/ sbyong rgyud kyi tshig 'grel/
brtag gnyis kyi tshig 'grel gnyis/ sgrub thabs dkyil chog gi rnam bshad rigs bdun/ bskyed rdzogs rnam bshad rigs dang 'khrid yig skor bcu bdun/ sgrub thabs dkyil chog dbang
rab gnas sbyin sreg 'chams yig dbyangs rol sogs kyi skor brgyad cu gya gsum/ rjes gnang bskang gso 'phrin bcol sogs chos srung gi skor nyi shu rtsa brgyad/ dkar chag gi
skor bcu bdun/ brda' gsar rnying shan sbyar dang dag yig sogs thor bu du ma bcas gzhung gang dang gang yin pa de dag gi dgongs

pa'i gting lon pa'i sngon med pa'i legs gsung kho na bzhugs pa dang / tsug lag khang gsar bzhengs kyang / li ma lha khang / rgya nag lha khang / phyag dpe lha khang chen mo/
bla ma lha khang / mgon khang khyad 'phags/ nyis thog lha khang / mgon khang srid gsum zil gnon rnams dang / bde mchog pho brang / 'bum thang / 'phags pa rin po che'i phyi
rten lha khang / btsun mo lcog sogs du ma rten dang brten pa zhig gsos rmang nas slang ba dang / lho byang gi gtsug lag khang du ma'i shing rtsi ldebs ris nyams gso gsar
bkod gnang ba ni brjod du ma langs/ rten gsum yang gser zangs kyi 'od dpag med khyad 'phags/ sa chen gyi gser sku bzo bkod phun sum tshogs pa/ dngul gdung mchod rten
rgyu bkod gya nom pa thog tshad phyed gnyis can dang thog tshad can brgyad/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po'i sku tshab dngul sku khyad mtshar/ 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po'i sku
brnyan che chung gnyis/ lam 'bras bla brgyud kyi kha skong mang po rnams gser zangs dang / byin rten dang sman 'dam las grub pa'isku brnyan shin tu mang po/ bris sku gtso
bsdus chen mo zhal thang bcu bdun srid na 'gran zla dang bral ba/ rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs kyi dkyil thang thog tshad nyi shu rtsa gcig sngags thang gras tshar nyi shu rtsa
bdun/ slob dpon

padma'i rnam thar sogs kha thor ba bgrang bar dka' ba rnams sku tshe'i ring la ri mo mkhan lnga re las mi nyung ba'i rgyun bris dang / bka' dang bstan bcos kyi glegs bam rigs
grangs mang dus bzhi 'khor yug tu yig mkhan mang por 'brii mjug par mdzad pa sogs rten gsum so so'i dkar chag tu gsal ba ltar yin zhing / nad mtshon mu ge sogs sems can
la sdug bsngal ba'i rgyu phra mo tsam byur na'ang bzod du med pa'i thugs rje'i shugs kyis rten mchog rnams la phan bde 'byung ba'i thugs smon phur tshugs dang rdo rje'i
chos skyong rnams la 'phrin bcol mdzad cing / phyogs gzhan du phebs dgos kyi rigs rnams la lam ring 'gro dka' ji lta bu zhig yin kyang sku tshegs la ji mi snyam par phebs
pa dang / mtha' 'khob kyi 'gro ba 'ga' dang 'ga' la yig drug sgrog pa dang / srog gcod spong ba'i dam bca' bzhes pa sogs sgo du ma nas lus can rnams la thar pa'i sa bon
ci yang smin par mdzad pa'i sa gnas 'phags chen dam pa'i rnam thar byis blo'i yul las 'das pa mngon par gsal ba dang / sku tshe 'dir rang gzhan ris med kyi skye bo khri
phrag du mar sbyin gtong chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa stsal ba sogs mdzad pa'i cha shas re re yang bskal pa'i bar du brjod kyis mi langs pa zhig gis bstan pa dang sems can

la phan bde rgya chen po sgrub par mdzad do/ /lo de'i zla ba lnga pa'i nang skor nas sku khams cung zad mi dngas pa'i tshul ston gyi sku zungs zhan tsam gyur pas thugs dam
sku mtshams la bzhugs te gsung rtsom rnams kyis mjug bsdu bar mdzad/ sku drung na yod pa'i phyag dpe rnams la gdong dar glegs thag sogs khyad par can bsgrubs nas/ da tshe
'dir dpe cha rnams la bed chod pa zhig yong ba mi 'dug kyang / phyir mi gyar ba chos skyong la 'phrin bcol yod pas dpe khang chen mor skyol dang ma 'ongs na bed chod pa
yong srid gsungs/ de mus su bsnyun gyi rnam pa cher med kyang / 'tsho byed zung nas 'phrod sten sna re tsam bzhes pa dang / 'tsho byed zung nas 'phrod sten sna re tsam bzhes
pa dang / sna rim yang dbus gtsang gi chos sde ris su mchad pa yongs rdzogs la mang 'gyed stobs che ba dang / gdan sa rang du'ang nye bskor gyi dge 'dun rnams bsdu ba
dang bcas zhal grangs stong phrag brgal bar bsnyen bkur 'bul 'gyed rgya chen rgyun ma chad par bsgrubs kyang sku khams la dngas bskyed bzhes pa ni ma byung zhing / bka'
las kyang kho bo ma shi bar du rong ston chos rje dang sngags 'chang chen po bzhin chos 'chad nyan dang bla ma gong ma'i dus dran gyi sgrub mchod rnams la 'gro thub pa byed
snyam pa yod kyang / na tshod dang

bcas lus zungs 'di yang zhan du ka 'gro ba zhig 'dug pas/ nga rang bstan pa'i bya ba yang de tsam yin 'dug cing / ma grub snyam pa'i 'gyod pa yang cher med/ lo gzhon nu nas
chos la dag snang che ba byas pas bla ma rnams kyi spyan 'bras lta bur dgongs pa byung / nged rang gis kyang so so'i bka' bzhin bstan pa rin po che'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum
la ngal ba lhur len bgyis pas da bar bstan 'gro la yang phan pa dga' rab byung zhing / lhag par chos rgyun dkon pa rnams yang spel thub cing / bsngags 'chang chen po'i
bstan pa'i rgyun 'di yang yar ldan kho na byung bas blo bde/ da ni bstan pa'i bya ba mi thub pa'i lus rten 'di brjes na legs sogs zhing khams gzhan du dgongs pa gtad pa'i
gsung kho na byung / de skor zhabs brtan 'bul mi shin tu mang bas/ bzhugs gdan rdo rje'i ri mo can kho na'ang brgya phrag nye bar byung zhing / skabs shig lha khang chen
mo'i dge 'dun byings gling mtshan mthun sdebs dang / spyir las 'dzin sger bcas kyis zhabs brtan phul bas/ grwa pa 'di rnams kyis snga phyir nged bsam pa byas/ da lam yang
do gal chen po byas byung yang / nged la phan pa cher med rung kho rang tshor bla ma gong ma'i byin rlabs 'jug ces sogs

gsungs shin tu smar ba mang po gnang / 'di skor gzigs snang khyad par can 'ga' byung tshod yin 'dug kyang gzhan brda' tsam las dngos su ma gnang / rje btsun rnal 'byor ma dang
/ chos srung zhal dang pu tra yang yang byon pa dngos su gsungs/ lan gcig sa sros mtshams sku 'khor rnams kyis gzim chung steng du phebs ran 'dug zhus pas cung zad lhod
cig gsungs pa'i mu nas/ nga 'das pa'i rjes su me tog gi char kha ba 'bab 'bab yong ba 'dug ces nyis btud du gnang / de skabs sde pa nor bu'i drung zhang tshan glo bur
du bsam rtser byon pa gsan pas/ sku tshe du mar bstan 'gro'i phan bde kho na la gom pa'i thugs kyis ma bzod par mkhan chen bsod nams bkra shis la sde pa zhang tshan la rgyal
dbang mchog nas dgongs pa grol ba yin na legs kyang / ma grol ba yin tshe khong khang tshan nas kyang bshags pa 'bul ba dang / rgyal dbang rin po che nas kyang bshags
pa bzhes dgos tshul zhal bkod zhib 'thems bcas rdzong bar mdzad/ de mus zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes lnga'i nyin 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug zhabs kyis gtsos pa'i rdo
rje'i slob ma nyu shas la zab cing rgya che ba'i bka' gsang rmad du byung ba'i

lung ston dang / rjes su gnang ba'i sgo nas sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa ji ltar 'dzin skyong spel ba'i tshul rnams rgyas par gsungs/ tshes bdun gyi nyin
sku brnyan rnams la 'bul rgyu'i na bza' rnams kyi zhal byang mdzad par chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta'i drung du na bza' 'dis mtshon pa'i dus gsum gyi dge bas sa skya pa
a nanta tshe 'phos 'phral dag pa'i zhing du skyes nas sa lam skad gcig la bgrod de/ slar yang sprul pas bstan pa rin po che dkar 'jam du bya nus pa'i mthu dang ldan par
gyur cig gsungs pa sogs sku brnyan so sor kha bsgyur rgyu'i gsung rtsom gyi tha ma de gnang / de rjes phyag mdzod sku drung du phyin par zur bstan gyis bka' mang zhig dang
/ lhag tu dga' ston sbyin gtong de 'di'i tshes bcu la nges par yong bar gyis sogs 'phral phugs bslab ston ci yang stsal bas/ phyag mdzod nas da dung zhabs pad bstan pa'i
bka' drin ci nas che dgos pa dang / ci ste gsol ba ma thebs phyin bka' bstsal rigs cis kyang bsgrub par zhu zhing bdag sogs skye ba dang tshe rabs su rjes su 'dzin dgos
tshul zhus par/ khyed rnams nam yang brjed mi 'ong sogs rdo rje'i gsung gi zhal bzhes lhug par phebs/ de nas tshes bcu'i nyin thugs dam ljags bzlas kyi rim

par gtor bsngos kyi bar sngar ltar rgyas par gnang rjes gtor ma 'bul grabs kyis gsungs pa dang lhan cig gtor ma la phyag mdzub gtad nas bde kyai gsang gsum la sogs pa'i rtsa
brgyud kyi bla ma yi dam chos skyong srung ma'i tshogs dang bcas pa rnams la 'dis mtshon pa'i dus gsum bsags pa'i dge ba'i dngos po rnams kun tu bzang po'i mchod pa'i sprin
gyi phung po lta bur gyur nas bskal pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du 'bul bar bgyi'o gsungs nas smon lam dang 'phrin bcol mang zhig gnang / de rjes sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya
zhal 'don gnang bzhin pa'i mur tshogs chen gyes song ngam gsungs/ cung ma gyes zhus pas de mus su bzhugs/ de nas tshogs chen grol ba'i bkra shis kyi mjug gi ki sgra gsan
'phral da grol ba yin 'dug thugs dgyes nyams chen po dang bcas gdul bya rtag 'dzin gyi blo can rnams la 'dus byas kyi gnas tshul bstan pa'i phyir mgo zla ba'i yar ngo'i
tshes bcu dpa' bo mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus tshes khyad par can gyi srod kyi char rje btsun grags pa'i 'phel gdung dang sngags 'chang chen po'i dam rdzas shig bsres la khur
shog gsungs gsol grub 'phral zhabs rdo rje skyil krung / phyag gnyis rdo rje khu tshur thugs kar bsnol/ sku rgyab phyogs su cung zad nye nyams kyi rgyud

sde rin po che nas gsungs pa'i 'da' kha ma'i rnal 'byor gsal 'debs par mdzad de hika che ba gnyis dang / chung ngu gcig gnang ste gzugs sku'i bkod pa don dam 'pho 'gyur med
pa'i 'od gsal phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du mnyam par bzhag pa'i tshul bstan no/ /de nas re zhig gi bar du nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa la gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan sogs
kyi rnam pa'i 'ja' tshon gyis khyab pa dang / bser bu ngad 'jam zhing sngar tshor ma myong ba'i dri bzang po 'thul ba dang / skabs su nam mkha' nas rol mo'i sgra 'byin pa
dang / nyin byed kyang lhag par gsal la dro ba sogs snod bcud la byin chags pa byung ba la/ de skabs gtsang dbus zing long gi skabs yin pas re zhig gsang rgya byas kyang
dpyod ldan mang pos snod bcud 'byung ba'i rtags ya mtshan pa de rigs la dpags nas gshegs par shes pa yang byung / tshes bcu gnyis kyi tho rengs kyi tshar 'od gsal las zung
'jug gi skur bzhengs te dbu'i gtsug gtor sor gang tsam 'phags shing byang sems kyi zil pa khrom me ba dang bcas dpa' bo rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pas sku
mdun nas bsus te shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du de bzhin

gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i drung du gshegs so/ /de skabs bzhi thog bla brang gi shar gyi mi mang gi khrod du bu chung lo bzhi lon pa zhig gis thog mar bzhi thog gi steng nas
rim pas shar phyogs kyi nam mkhar 'dzub mo ker nas ya gi na ko bkrol la mang po gnam la song / gong bzhugs kyang phebs song zer ba de rang las sgrib srab pas rje de nyid
dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyi DA ma ru'i sgra dang bcas spyan drangs pa mthong ba yin 'dug de nas sku gdung rin po che chas zhugs dang bcas gdung sgrom du bstsal nas mchod
pa'i yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug zhabs dpon slob rnams kyis bla mchod rgyun ring dang/ gzhan yang rdo rje 'dzin pa
du ma 'dus tshogs dang bcas pa'i zla ngo lnga'i ring la sgrub mchod dang gsol 'debs mchod 'bul sbyin gtong nar mar bsgrubs pa'i zhing dang sbyor ba dngos po'i rnam grangs
bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dir bkod du ma langs pas rags rim tsam zhig rje 'di'i rnam thar kha skong dad pa'i chu rgyun du gsal ba ltar ro/ /de nas nag zla'i bcu gnyis nyin
sku gdung rin po cher zhugs chog phul bar/ sngon gyi gsung bzhin me tog gi char kha

ba bzhin babs pa btsun chung 'ga' res lha khang chen mo'i gling dbar nas btus pa shog thum byas byung ba dang / gdung khang gi drung du mang du babs pa ting phor gang btu rgyu
byung ba mchod rdzas su phul/ dbu thod phal cher ril bor byon par bde mchog dpa' gcig rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ gur mgon/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug rnams kyi sku brnyan dang
/ yig 'bru sogs shin tu gsal ba dang / ring bsrel du ma/ phyis su dung gi tshems shig 'khrungs pa de yang ril por byon pa sogs gdung rten bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon/ gdung
rus lhag ma shel ltar dwangs ba rnams dri bzang gi chus sbyangs te 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug nyid kyis sangs rgyas byang sems bla sku sogs kyi satstsha chig
stong chig brgya nga gsum phyag 'debs la gser zho bcu drug ljib gsol mdzad nas gdung rten rnam rgyal mchod rten 'dzam gling rgyan mchog 'di nyid dang / rje nyid kyi sku tshab
thog tshad ma/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sku brnyan mi tshad tsam pa rnams kyi bzo rgyu gser dngul phra rgyan sogs bsdoms par dngul srang khri phrag gcig lhag pas bzo
bkod khyad par can du bsgrubs pa 'di dag tu gzugs dang byin rten dpag tu med pa bcas bzhugs shing / de dang stabs gcig rgyal ba'i 'khrungs rab dpag bsam 'khri

shing gi bris thang rgyu bkod phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas grub par 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug nyid kyi gtso mdzad rdo rje 'dzin pa sha stag bcu phrag gsum gyi
'khor dang bcas pas dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la brten nas rab tu gnas pas byin rlabs kyi gzi byin 'bar ba bsgrubs/ slad nas dus dran gyi mchod par rgyud 'don bla
mchod sogs dang rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub mchod/ mgo zlar bde mchog nag po lugs kyi sgrub mchod zhag bcu gsum ser 'du bcas/ snron zlar mchod 'bul bla mchod
nyin gang ma sogs dang / gzhan yang ngor/ gong dkar/ nyang stod rtse chen/ gli kha bde ba can/ gser mdog can/ srid gsum rnam rgyal/ yul chen/ nyi shar/ gdong dga'/ bsam
yas rnams su zhag grangs mang por sgrub cing mchod pa sogs rgya chen bgyid pa'i gzhi rten dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab par sbyor bar mdzad do/ /ngag dbang bsod nams dbang
phyugyongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'jam mgon de nyid kyi rigs dang chos kyi thugs sras gcig pu 'jam pa'i dbyangs

ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan snyan srid pa gsum gyi khongs na mngon par gsal ba de nyid kyi dang po sprul gzhi'i ngo bo
ni rgyal ba thams cad kyi gsung rdo rje'i bdag nyid 'od dpag med dam nyid kyi sgyu 'phrul ye shes kyi rol gar mtha' yas pa las phyi ma'i dus su 'bras bu'i theg pa mchog gi
nye lam ston pa'i ched du gsang ba gsum gyi 'od rdul sindhu'i mtshor 'phos pa'i sprul pa'i snang brnyan 'chi med rig 'dzin grub pa loo Dyin thod 'phreng 'chang ba de nyid
sku dngos rnga yab dpal rir bzhugs pa gangs can gdul bya'i mgon du lha rigs 'khon gyi gdung du mii'i srid pa bzung ba ni 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po nyid yin pa rje
de nyid kyi rnam thar skabs 'byung ba bzhin/ de nyid slar yang rang gi rigs dbon du phebs pa rje 'di nyid yin tshul ni/ skyabs mchog 'di nyid dbus phebs kyi skabs gsang
phu nas lkog gyur sgrib bral gzigs pa'i chos skyong chen po bse khrab can gyis rje 'di nyid la/ paNDi ta rang sngon gyi dge bshes 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i
sku'i rnam 'phrul yin ces dang / sku tshe 'di nyid kyi mdzad phrin 'di ltar 'byung gi lung bstan gsal ba bcas maNDal chen po zhig phul ba dang / zha lu rgyan gong du rdo
rje rab brtan sku phebs pa'i

lung bstan du'ang/ sngon rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa la phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa dang / paNDi ta bcas pa'i dam tshig bzhi par smra song dus/ ngas brgyud
bskul drag po btang bas ma rig song / phyag rdor sprul pa lus ngag yid gsum chu ris kyi ri mo ltar yod pa lus sems gnad du phob la 'gro ba sems can gyi don gyis zhes
dang / sngon gyi dus su phyag rdor sprul pa rang gi bkas gnang / paNDi tas bzhengs pa'i mchod rten lam gyi g.yas phyogs pho brang gi nub zur na yod/ de la gzungs ma 'khrul
bar tshud la gzhongs zhes sogs rje di nyid kyi sku tshe sngon ma 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po phyag rdor gyi sprul pa'i paNDi ta zhes pa zha lu mkhan chen te de nyid
Da Di grangs zhig tu sku skye bzhes par zhal ta phebs te mchod rten de bzhengs par gsal la/ 'o na slob dpon padma'i sprul pa yin par 'chad pa'i skabs su phyag na rdo rje'i
sprul par bshad pa ci zhig snyam na/ de ni spyir rgyal ba thams cad kyi ye shes gci gnyid du mar snang ba ltar las don du ris su med pa dang / khyad par rig 'dzin padma
thod phreng nyid la bde skyong yid 'dzin dbang mos skye sprul sogs ci ltar zhus pa'i lan tu/ 'gro re'i mdun du sprul sku'i ston pa 'byon :zhes pa nas/ chos dbyings gnas
su kun du bzang po dang :

stug po bkod par rdo rje 'chang chen po: rdo rje gdan du thub pa chen po nyid: gnyis med padma nga ru lhun gyis grub: ces rdo rje 'chang du dngos bstan la/ rdo rje 'chang dang
rdo rje sems dpa' phyag rdor rnams ni ye shes gcig nyid yin pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che/ /rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa kun/ /rdo rje dang po kun tu bzang / /phyag
'tshal phyag na rdo rje la/ /zhes sogs kyis gsal ba ni 'phros tsam dang / gzhan yang rje de nyid kyis dge sdings su zha lu mkhan chen las gsung ngag rin po cher gsan skabs/
nged sa skya'i bzhi thog gzim chung dugacig pur bsdad pa las/ 'dir gcig pur bsdad pa blo bag phebs shing kha ton 'phel ba dmigs pa gsal ba sogs yong gi 'dug pa snga
sor 'dir sdod yun ring ba yin pa 'dra zhes dang / yang nyin gcig sngo mo nged kyi sbyor drug bsgoms dus kyi gzim chung gting ma gi na yod pas gnam sgo 'di phye dang nged
rang rnams lta bar 'gro gsungs pa bzhin mdzad pas/ gzim chung sgo byang bstan zhig gi shar lho'i sbug zur na gzim mal skyor bcas sogs ji lta ba 'dug pa yang sngar phan gzhan
la rgyus med cing / sku nyid gtan nas phebs 'grul ma myong bar sngon gnas rjes dran gyi zhal bzhes khyad par can sogs mdo tsam brjod nas/ sku tshe 'di

nyid kyi rnam thar thor long ni/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis sde pa lhun rtse ba'i rus brgyud tsha shood mthong smon pa'i rigs skyes bkra shis dpal gyis bu bskyed ces
pa khab tu bzhes par gdung gcig phebs pa sku phra mo nas gshegs/ phyis su 'bro'i sngags 'chang 'jigs bral zhes brtul bzhugs grub pa de'i sras mo ma gcig o rgyan skyabs
ma bzhes par yab rje rin po che dgung grangs zhe gcig bzhes thog rje 'di nyid rgyal yum de nyid kyi lhums su zhugs pa nas yum nyid kyang dus rgyun chos skyong rnams dang
'bral med yod snyam pa'i 'jigs snang dang spro sing nge ba bag dro ba rgyun chags su byung zhing / yab rje'i mnal lam du'ang / dar 'phyar/ dung 'bud/ rol mo 'khrol ba sogs
dge mtshan du ma dang / 'gro mgon sngags 'chang nyid kyang sku srung la rgyun gnas kyi skabs mnal lam zhig tu mi ras gos dkar po can rakSha'i phreng ba thogs pa zhig thal
gyis byung nas/ sa skya par gdung 'byon par yod do/ /'gro mgon ni lhag pas khyer song ngo zhes pa zhig byung ba dang / rtags mthong mkhan gzhan la yang gdan sa'i thad
kyi nam mkhar chos dung zhig yang yang 'khor ba mthong ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma rgyun chags byung ba bzhin du yab rje rin po che dgung grangs zhe gnyis pa 'bru

mang zhes pa sa stag hor zla brgyad pa'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa'i res gza' sbyin byed bla ma dang rgyu skar dkar po nam gru'i 'gyub sbyor phun sum tshogs par bzhi
thog bla brang du gzugs sku'i nyi ma mngon du shar zhing / 'khrungs ma thag nas mdzes sku'i chas shas yongs su rdzogs pa dang / skye mched gsal ba sogs mi las 'das pa'i
mtshan shin tu gsal bar/ yab rje nyid dang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags lhan cig pas tshe dbang rjes gnang bka' bsgo sogs zla shas bar nyin rar bzhin mdzad/ srung ma'i
dbang po rnams la gtang rag dang / chos sde lho byang la mang ja 'dzugs par mdzad pa tshes brgyad 'khrungs jar grags pa da lta'i bar rgyun ma chad pa sogs dga' ston rgyas
par gnang / sku cog la bzhugs nus tsam nas zhal gyi rtsa sngags ring thung gsung nyams mdzad pa dang / gsung mkhyen nas badzra gu ru/ kI la ya/ mgon po'i yi ge bdun ma
sogs thogs med grol du gsungs/ dgung lo bzhi pa nas 'bri klog chos spyod sogs 'bul tshul zhus pa thogs med du mkhyen/ skabs shig sku gcig rkyang tshom dmar na bzhugs skabs
shig tu sku rtsed gsung gleng mang du gnang bar zhabs phyi ba slebs ste gsung zla su yod zhus pas bzhugs khri padma can gyi g.yas phyogs su phyag 'dzub ker te pu tra
pu tra

gsungs pa sogs rigs kyi srung ma dang 'bral med du bzhugs pa'i ngo mtshar dang / dgung grangs brgyad par kyai rdor dkyil chog thugs su chud/ dgu par yab rje dang lhan cig phur
sgrub chen mor phebs/ rim gyis cho ga phyag len dbyangs rol gar 'chams sogs la byang chub par mdzad/ yab rje rin po che las sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur bde kyai sogs
yi dam chos srung bcas pa'i dbang lung man ngag phal cher gsan/ dgung lo bcu gnyis tshun snga phyir de dag gi dkyil chog gtor sgrub mdos bzlog sogs phyag len phra mo
tshun la byang chub par gnang / bcu gsum par yab rje rdo rje 'chang las gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i smiin grol slob bshad lugs lam skor phyi ma brgyad
snyan brgyud man ngag gis rgyan pa rgyab brten lung gi rigs mtha' dag dang bcas par gsan/ phyis su dgung grangs nyer gnyis par rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang lhan cig
par yang gsung ngag rin po che bskyar ma gsan pa yin no/ /dgungs grangs bcu bzhiir son pa lcags yos gsar tshes kyi thog chos kyi khri ga la bar chos kyi rgyal por mnga'
gsol ba'i sgo shar nas dus mdos chen mo yang rgyal zla'i mjug tu bsring ste

gzab spros phun sum tshogs pa snga srol ltar dang / gnam gang la srung ma'i gtang rag sogs rgyas par bsgrubs/ cho 'phrul zla ba'i yar ches dang po'i nyin/ gzhung sa mchod yon
gyis sku tshab/ bkra shis lhun po'i sku tshab/ rtse gdong nas mchod dpon pa/ ngor mgron gnyer sogs che gnyan dmangs phal bcas khri 'bul mnga' gsol ba sa chen po'irdul
bzhin 'khrigs pa lo gsar dus ston dang skabs gcig dga' ston rgya cher stsal/ tshes bcu gnyis kyi bar du yab rje mchog nas phyogs 'dus che gnyan rags bsdus bzhi thog tshoms
chen khri gang ba la khrid brgya sogs kyi chos sbyin re skong stsal/ tshes bcu gsum gyi nyin nyi shar la chos khri chen mo'i nye logs su dge 'dun 'dus tshogs rnams kyis
bkod pa bstar ba dang / rje 'di nyid sku 'khor ser skya du ma'i tshogs bcas sgrigs bkod phun sum tshogs pa'i zhal mdangs nyi ma 'bum gyis gzi byin 'dzum 'ood 'bar bas 'jam
dbyangs rim byon gyi zhabs stegs rdo rje'i khri 'phang dam par zhabs kyi pad mo mngon par bkod de rgyal ba'i sras kyi lam bzang gsal bar byed pa'i bstan bcos chen po thub
pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba'i bka' chos nyin gsum gyi bar du gnang ba dag gsal snyan pa'i dbyangs kyis skye dgu'i yid dbang 'phrog par gyur cing / tshes

bco lnga'i nyin yab rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang lhan cig bzhugs khrir phebs te skabs de'i 'brel zhus rnams kyi dge rtsa rdzogs byang du smin pa dang / bstan 'groo'i phan
bde spel ba'i bden tshig rdo rje'i gsung bsngo rin po che gnang / gzhis byes nas khri 'bul gyi dngos po blo'i ra ba las brgal ba spungs pa phal cher de nyid du mchod sbyin
gyi phyag ring brkyangs pas thams cad chos dang zang zing gi 'byor pa lhan cig pas tshim par gyur/ 'di lo 'dar grangs tshar chen rin po che bla slob kyi sku gdung la zhugs
rkyen byung ba'i gdung rus rnams gdan sar phul ba yab rje mchog nas thugs stsol gyis phyag tsha dngul gdung sogs bzhes par mdzad pa zla drug pa'i nang zin pa'i rab gnas
