kyi nyin yar lung dbon rin po che mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan nas rje 'di nyid kyi khri ston snga sor 'bul ma thub pa skyel mi 'byor bas/ yab rje mchog nas rten 'brel
legs pa'i mnyes tshor gyi gsung mang du gnang ba bzhin/ rje 'dis dus phyis su tshar lugs kyi bzhed srol mtha' dag dar rgyas mdzad pa'i dge mtshan du snang / de lo dgyes
rdor gzhi bsnyen mthar phyin gnang / 'di bskor snga phyi sogs su yab rje rin po che dang gzhan yang rigs kyi bdag po rnams las zab rgyas chos kyi rgya mtsho ji ltar gsan
pa'i tshul ni gsan yig chen mo

thub bstan srid mthar gsal ba'i nyin byed du gsal bar ltar las 'dir tshig tshogs bsdus pa dang / de bzhin du zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi zla grangs sbrel ma dang kha yar du
ma gnang bas bstan pa'i srog 'thud cing 'gro ba grangs med thar lam la bkod pa'i tshul yang mdo tsam 'og tu zhal slob ji ltar byung bas kyang ston par 'gyur ro/ /de nas
rje nyid dgung grangs bcu dgur phebs skabs rje btsun chen po 'dis gangs can phan bde'i rtsa lag gdan sa 'di nyid kyi gdung rabs nor bu'i phreng ba bstar ba'i phyir bdag
chen shar pa'i sras mo ma gcig pad dkar bu khrid ces pa khab tu bzhes par me sprel dbyar ra'i nyer lnga la rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis grags
pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes dri med lung gi bsngags pa'i gling bu srid par snyan pa de nyid 'khrungs nas yangs pa'i rgyal khams ngo mtshar gyi snang bas khyab par
gyur/ de lo yab rje nyid lho bod sems can spyi'i bde thabs 'phaT chen dam pa'i thugs bskyed la zhugs nas lho 'brug phyogs su chibs bsgyur gnang skabs gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong
gi khur 'gel dang lhag tu yab rje nyid tshur phebs kyi bar sku mtshams dang

bskang gso 'phrin bcol 'di ltar dgos tshul phebs pa bzhin/ de 'phral nas thugs dam g.yel med la bzhugs nas rdo rje'i chos srung rnams la yab rje'i dgongs bzhed 'grub pa'i gnyer
gtad shar mar gnang skabs me bya zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu bzhi'i mnal lam du a tsa ra sngo bsangs rgyab la ras 'bog khur ba gnyis slebs nas nged gnyis rgya gar gyi
gnas bsil ba'i tshal nas yin/ da lam yab rje'i sku zhabs nas snga 'gros su 'ong ba yin/ khong dpon slob rnams kyi bzhed don yang myur du 'grub par yod ces yus pa'i rnam
pa dang bcas pa ras 'bog de gnyis kha phye nas 'di dang 'di'i don snying yin ces btsun pa'i mgo gsum snying gnyis/ mi nag pa'i mgo lnga rna ba gnyis rnams gsal por byung
bas lho bod 'khrug rkyen sel 'jug byed mkhan rnams mthu ldan srung ma'i tshogs kyis bsgral bas gong bzhugs dpon slob kyi bzhed don mthar phyin 'grub par thugs thag bde mor
chod pa byung/ rje nyid dgung grangs nyer gnyis su phebs pa sa phag lor gser mdog can gyi mkhan po dpon slob dang / sgom sde pa sogs mang por ljags lung pod long mang po
bka' drin stsal/ 'di lo yab rje 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid dag zhing phebs pa dang

nor bu sde gzar thug pas re zhig gsang rgya'i nas sku rim du kha g.yar ba'i ris med chos sder mang 'gyed rgya cher sogs dgongs rdzogs rten bzhengs dus dran gyi bar rmad du
byung ba bsgrubs pa gong yab rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar dang / dgungs grangs nyer bzhir phebs thog yab rje'i bzhed skong du dmigs sprul pa'i lha
khang chen mo'i ldebs bris mthil zhal nyams gso sogs kyi dbu btsugs/ ldebs bris sngon ma tshang 'grig gsar bris kyi khar/ phyogs gsum char du yab rje rin po che'i sku brnyan
thog tshad re dang / gzhan yang rnam rgyal brgya tshar sogs sangs rgyas byang sems bla brgyud yi dam chos srung gi sku brnyan shin tu mang ba bsnan par sku brnyan rnams
la gser btul ma zho brgya lhag pa ljib gsol dang / bzhugs khri chen mo'i thad kyi ldebs bris la gtso bo 'jam dbyangs dang / sngags 'chang chen po gnyis la rnal 'byor
dbang phyug gong ma lnga/ sa lochen bo/ yab rje rin po che/ rje nyid zhabs 'bring pa bcas dang / gzhan yang gdan sa chen por bsngags pa snyan ngag dbang po'i nyer 'tsho
gdung rabs ya rabs kha brgyan/ yab rje rin po che'i rnam thar rags rim sogs gsar bkod dang / gzhan yang rgyug dra ko dra rdo gcal khyams stod sgo dmar g.yas g.yon gyi g.yab

chos khri chen mo sogs dgung grangs nyer lngar phebs pa chu stag lo dbyar thog tu grub nas rab gnas gnang tshe me tog gi char mthun grub tu byung / bzo rig pa rnams la'ang
gnang sbyin yid khengs pa dang bcas dga' ston nyin dam pa gong ma rgyas pa'i dngos grub rten 'brel bzang por glo bo smad nas dpon drung khro bo rnam rgyal dpon g.yog rnams
kyis gser dngul brgya 'bul/ dar ras/ rta phyugs sogs 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang 'byor/ ston mjug gzim chung rab gsal 'og gi ka rtsi gdung rtsi sogs tshon 'gyed dang
/ tshoms dmar gyi 'gag nas brtsams te g.yab skor gyi tshon rtsi/ sa chen phug dang phag mo phug gnyis la rje nyid de dag gi sku brnyan re las mchod rgyun sogs med par
nyams gso rten bzhengs mchod rgyun phul phyin mdzad/ 'di lo gzhung sa nas lha sa gzhung gi mchod gzhis rnams kyang phyag 'byor byung / dgung grangs nyer drug tu phebs par
khams nas bo tshang dbon po kun dga' bstan 'dzin dpon g.yog gsung ngag rin po che zhu bar 'bul chen dang bcas 'byor ba dang mnyam du/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ rgyal
rtse zhabs drung ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan sogs gzhis byes chos nyan sum brgya

lhag par gsung ngag rin po che'i chos bka' thog mar gnang ba'i rgyud gsum sngon 'gro dbang bskur stsal ba'i ched du ljags bsnyen gsos gnang tshe sngon dus yab rje rdo rje 'chang
bde mchog tu bzhugs skabs pha bong zhig la phyag sor drud sa'i rjes grub chu rdol ba phyis su shwa 'od sogs kyis zub nas ma byung ba/ 'di skabs rang rdol du byung ba
sogs grub pa'i mtshan ma ngo mtshar ba brnyes/ khams sman ji dgon nas bla ma bgres po lam 'bras rdzong lugs lo re bzhin 'chad mkhan zhig yod 'dug pa des chos dung dngul
gshog ma gnyis kyis gtsos 'bul chen phyag 'byor gyis rten 'brel yang legs/ dgung grangs nyer bdun par zha lung mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub bka' chos zhur phebs par zla
ba phyed gnyis tsam gyis ring zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi ji ltar bzhed pa gnang / 'di lo snga phyiir bla brang phun tshogs gling nyams gso dang / dbu rtse rnying mar
mthil zhal/ shing rtsi/ khyad gos zhe gcig pa'i gnam rgyan/ ka 'phan sogs phul phyin mdzad/ dgung grangs nyer brgyad par khams sa dkar nas sbyin bdag sku drung sku skye
dpon g.yog rnams dad mjal dang gsung ngag rin po che zhu bar 'bul stobs che ba bcas 'byor ba bzhin

gzhis byes mang bar gsung ngag rin po che cha lag rag bsdus bcas dang gzhan yang chos bka' 'dod sbyar gnang / de lo byang chub gling sprul pa'i sku yon tan rgya mtshor yang
sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sogs chos bka' rgya cher stsal/ dgungs grangs nyer dgur phebs pa chos sde lho byang la 'dod lha 'ga' zhig gi dbang lung sogs bstan rgyunal dgongs
pa'i chos sbyin rgya cher gnang / rtse gdong zhabs drung bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po phebs par thugs mnyes kyi mjal spro dang bka' chos rgyun ring gnang / bsam yas chos
skyong chen po nas sku rten pa tshe dbang zhu bar brdzangs pa bzhin tshe dbang mdzad/ sgar chen zhabs drung dang yab rje rin po che nas lha khang chen mor phul ba'i gnam
rgyan rnams yar mar spos te rten gtso rnams kyi dbu thog tu khyad gos 'ba' zhig pa'i bla bre rgya chen phul/ dbu rtse rnying mar lam 'bras brgyud pa'i kha skong du yab
rje rin po che'i sman sku yod pa bde chen gling gi rten gtsor bzhugs nas de tshab gser zangs kyis sku brnyan khyad mtshar 'di nyid bzhengs/ dgung grangs sum cu par yang zha
lu mkhan chen de nyid ched phebs ltar dbang chen/ byiin rlabs/ rjes gnang gi rigs bcu phrag tsam dang / dbu sems so so'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga

nyams 'khrid lung 'khrid ljags lung sogs rnam grangs drug cu tsam gyis bzhed don re skong mdzad/ byang bdag rje bsod nams grags pa dang / snye mo rje btsun ma sogs kyis zhus
ngor lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i nyams 'khrid cha lag dang bcas pa yang stsal/  dgung grangs so gcig par rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs chos khrir chen mor mnga' gosal sogs
'og de nyid kyi rnam thar skabs su gsal ba ltar dang dga' ston rgyas par bstsal/ nyin gsum bar yab sras lhan cig phebs te bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel ba'i gsung bsngo bkra
shis kyi me tog sil ma bsnyil ba'i mtha' brgyan/ 'di lo byang bdag po ngag dbang bso nams grags pa sogs mang por kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang bskur yang stsal/ dgung
grangs so gnyis par byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal sku gshegs pa'i sku gdung zhugs 'bul gshegs rdzong sku rten dus mchod sogs phul phyin mdzad/ gzhan yang 'jam dbyangs
bsod nams dbang po'i phyi rten du lha babs mchod rten/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros kyi phyi rten rnam rgyal mchod rten/ yab rje dam pa'i phyi rten byang chub mchod rten
gsum po bde chen gling

stod du bzhengs par/ chos sde'i gong gnon lta bur song ba rang gzugs kyang cung zad 'khrugs pas bsam yas chos skyong chen pos spo dgos tshul lung bstan byung ba bzhin phyi
lo arga'i cho gas spo chog bcas da lta nub phyogs zhol na mchod rten ngo bo gong mtshungs bzhugs pa 'di rnams slar gzungs 'khrul med phyag bstar gyis gsum kar sangs rgyas
kyi 'phel gdung re res gtsos dam rjas byin rten bgrang las 'das pa/ rgyud sde gong 'og gi yi dam gyi sku brnyan li ma shas che'i gser zangs 'dres pa bzhi bcu zhe bdun/ thub
sku li ma gser zangs khyoon drug cu re gcig rje btsun gong ma'i sku kha shas/ bris thang nyi shu tsam/ chos sku'i ring bsrel stod smad bar gsum gyi gzungs sngags rigs
bgrang bar bka' ba/ mchod rten bye ba ma shas che'i li ma gser dngul las grub pa bcas nyi shu sogs da dag gi bzhugs tshul yang mdo sngags kyi phyag len rnam par dag pa'i
lung dang rab gnas smin rgyas du ma bcas byin rlabs kyi phung por bsgrubs/ dbyar thog rig 'dzin pho brang du lha khang mkhan rin po che'i gtsos pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen
brgya phrag tsam la nyin dang po tshugs nyin sta gon bka' sgrub nas slob ma sta gon tsho bzhi gnang / sang snga char dngos gzhi'i bka' sgrub gnang nas/ dngos gzhi tshar
bzhi

bskur ba gnang nas gzhugs chog grub rjes sang dkyil 'khor gang gnang rgyu'i stan gon gyi cho ga skyabs 'gro nas bkra shis bar mdzad rjes/ sang dngos gzhi gang gnang rgyu'i
bka' sgrub kyi grabs yul mdzad nas thugs dam chag med rnams kyis rim pa la 'jug par mdzad de cung zad mnal ba tsam mdzad/ de nas snga dro'i thugs dam zab bzhes rnams gnang
grub rjes sku bzhengs nas dngos gzhi'i bka' sgrub gnang ste bskur ba sogs kyis sgo nas zhag bcu gsum la ngan song sbyongs rgyud nas gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi
dbang bskur rdzogs par mdzad/ yang lo de'i phur sgrub grol rjes rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis gtsos gong mtshungs la zhag bcu gsum ring sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu
gnyis kyi dbang bskur smin rgyas gnang / bde chen gling gi lcags ri/ gra shag sogs nyams gso'i zhal bkod mdzad/ zla ba bcu gcig par lcam sring mo kun dga' chos kyi nyi ma
dag zhing gshegs par dgongs rdzogs phyi nang gi rten dus dran bcas rgya cher gnang / dgungs grangs so gsum par yar lung gnas gsar dbon rin po che/ rje btsun ma bka' 'gyur
ma bcas bka' chos zhu bar 'bul ba rgya chen lha khang spyi sger la gnam rgyan ka 'phan

sogs ltos che bar 'byor bar gsang bde 'jigs gsum gyi gtsos dbang bka' byin rlabs rjes gnang lung 'khrid bcas gnang / bla brang nyi zla'i nyams gso mdzad pa'i mgo btsugs/ 'og
gi gtsug lag khang du byams pa'i sku brnyan thog tshad ma gser ljib byugs kyis gtsos sku brnyan bris 'bur du ma gdung rten gnam rgyan 'phan char dkar me mchod rgyun phun
sum tshogs pa dang / bla brang dge 'phel gyi nyams gso bcas lcags phag lor zin nas rab gnas smin rgyas gnang / de lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes gsum la rgyal yum pad dkar
bu khrid dag zhing gshegs par gshegs rdzong mdzad tshul sogs 'og de sras sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar dang dpyid ka ngor khang gsar dbon
po gnyis sogs don gnyer brgya phrag lhag par gsung ngag rin po che cha lag bcas smin rgyas gnang skabs nye skor 'brum nad byung ba bzhes kyang gsung chos la gtan ma gnod
pas thams cad kyis sngar phan yang lam 'bras gnang thengs re la grub pa'i mtshan ma re yong gin yod pa/ da lan gyi de gdan sa'i nye bskor 'brum nad kyis khyab par sku
nyid la yang cha dang gzhan la yang srog skyon gcig kyang ma byung ba 'di rang yin 'dug ces grags pa byung/ dgun dpyid mtshams bzhi

thog gser khang steng 'og gi thad dang / gsang sngags pho brang gi thad rnams shin tu nyen cher yod pa rnams nyams gso'i las 'go tshugs/ sngon dus yab rje rin po che'i sku
dus kyang gsung brtag mo rtsis sogs la ma chug pa ma gtogs gtsug lag khang khyad 'phags dang / mgon khang khyad 'phags bdud las rnam rgyal gsar bzhengs gnyis kyang byang
rgyud 'dir byung na dgongs pa'i lhag ma bsgrub ched arga'i cho ga gnang ste tshoms bar gyi byang 'dul mgon po sogs thog mar rje nyid kyis bshags pa spyan 'dren mdzad nas
bsgul rjes bsnyen song rnams kyis tshoms chen du spyan drangs pa nas bzung rim gyis gsang sngags pho brang sngar las bzo bkod mi zhan pa dang / steng du gser 'phru gsar bzos/
de'i shar tshoms bar mgon khang sngar 'khyud ltar/ de'i thog mgon khang bdud las rnam rgyal/ de'i steng bla ma lha khang khyad 'phags mthong ba don ldan de'i steng gnas
chu lha khang gi thog tu gser gyi ganydzir dang zur gnyis su gser gyi rgyal mtshan re bcas gsar bzos/ de rnams kyis shar phyogs su spyan gzigs khang / de'i steng shag
skor/ de'i steng dbang khang ka drug ma la gser 'phru gsar bzos dang / gzim chung la shar lho'i phyogs su rgyal mtshan gsar bzos sogs/ byang brgyud shar

nub ka ba nyi shu tsam pa yongs rdzogs gsar bsgrub kyi rtsig ra rmangs gyang skor gnyis tsam gyi bar spang leb kyi nang gyang mtho gang re tsam 'phar ba byung bas mthong mkhan
tshos gzhan la chal sgrog bstan pas de nas ma byung bar grags/ nub byang gi zur nas brtsams te byang brgyud la mgon po/ lha mo/ dpal mgon zhal/ pu tra rnams kyi rgyu
mtshan yig cha ma bu gsal byed dang bcas pa'i nang bzhin rab gnas thugs gsol dang bcas pa dang / gtsug lag khang de dag rnams su sngar bzhugs pa las lhag tu bris 'bur gyi
sku brnyan grangs mangs/ sku rnying la bzhugs khang rgyab yol bzhugs khri gang dgos gnam rgyan sa rgyan mchod rgyun spyan gzigs gtor tshogs sogs gang la gang 'os bag dro
brjid chags pa'i bkod par rab tu gnas pa smin rgyas kyis byin rlabs kyis phung por bsgrubs/ dgung grangs so lnga par gser mdog can gyi mkhan po rgyal ba lhun grub pa sogs
gzhis byes dge ba'i bshes gnyen du mar dbang lung chos 'khor rgya cher stsal/ zha lu mkhan chen rin po che bsod nams mchog grub byon te gong sa rdo rje 'chang rgyal dbang
lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa'i rje 'di nyid yab sras kyi brtan bzhugs tshogs 'dzugs bcas zhabs brtan gyi rten 'brel

mdzad/ phyir yang zab chos rgya cher gnang / de nyid kyi lha khang mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bkra shis las 'jam mgon sa paN nas brgyud pa'i bsnyen rdzogs sdom rgyun bzhes
pa de nyid rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen pos bzhes pa'i bstan rgyun tshugs pa yang rje 'di'i sku drin du shes shing / dgung grangs so drug par rgyal dbang mchog
nas rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde nas gur pa sogs grwa tshang khag bzhi dang / brtse chen nas grwa tshang khag dgu rnams kyis sngar phan dbang rgyun med par sgrub mchod
sogs tshogs 'don gtong gin yod tshod 'dug pas rje nyid nas dbang bka' gnang dgos tshul dang / grwa tshang tshor yang zhu dgos tshul phebs pa ltar grwa tshang rnams kyang
'byor bar rgyud sde gong 'og chos srung sogs kyi dbang bka' shiin tu mang bar gnang / de skabs ngor mkhan chen thar rtse pa gshegs pa'i gdan sa 'os bsdu phul bar thang
dkar dgon na bzhugs pa'i lhun grub dpal ldan par gsung brtag bzang chug byung ba bzhin gzhung sa nas bka' shog lam yig zhus te bang chen bshad stsol gnang bas/ mi ring
bar byon te gdan sar 'khod/ lho nas gangs mchod pa dpon g.yog lnga bcu skor mjal

khar 'byor bar phyag dbang ston mo zab rgyas bka' 'doms che ba gnang / khong tshos kyang lho bod nyes med kyi sems can bde thabs 'ching 'doms gang yong thugs rjes gzigs par
zhus/ dgun spu hreng bla ma kun dga' rgyal mtshan dad mjal 'byor bar dbang lung 'ga' zhig gis rjes 'dzin gnang / dgungs grangs so bdun pa shing stag lor bsam yas nas chos
skyong chen pos gdug 'dre'i gzhal yas khang nyams gsos dang gsar bkod dgos tshul zhu phrin 'byor ba dang / dbus sde srid nas 'di lo rgyal dbang sku zhabs bcad rgya 'dra
min pa'i stabs bde'i skabs 'dir yab sras rin po che lhan cig dbus phebs la lam bar gyi zhabs phyi'i ched du 'di dus phebs snga gsal yang gnang dgos bcas kyi zhu shog 'byor
ba ltar rim gyis phebs pa'i dgongs pa shar/ hor zla dang po'i nang ngor mkhan chen shar pa sher 'byung gis mchod dpon kun dga' legs pa dpon slob rnams kyis gser dngul
brgya 'bul gyis gtsos pa'i chos sder mang 'gyed sogs rgya chen bcas bka' srung gi chos skor zhu ru 'byor ba/ gzab gnad thugs bcud kyi chos bkas re skong dang / rtse gdong
zhabs drung ngag dbang nor bu bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po dpon slob rnams phebs par thugs snang shin tu

spro ba'i ngang nas bka' chos bzhed don rdzogs par gnang / 'di lo rdo rje phur pa'i gos sku chen mo bzhengs par mdzad par chos longs sprul gsum/ bla sku kha shas sogs nas gtso
skur zin tsam la 'phro 'jog par mdzad/ de mtshams gzhung nas phebs lam gyi gra sgrig thogs med gzhis rtse rdzong nas dgos tshul gyi bka' shog phebs pa ltar/ lam gtor
mgon khang nye 'gyangs rnams su 'phrin bcol rgyas pa sogs bsgrubs par mdzad nas zla ba bcu pa'i nang yab sras lhan cig chibs bteg rim gyis chu mig tu ngor gdan sa pa dang
/ bla brang khag rnams nas phebs bsu dang bcas/ tshong 'dus khri khang du zha lu mkhan chen gyi phyag mdzod pas gzhi lan gzab ma zhus par byin rlabs gnang skyes phun sum
tshogs pa stsal/ rin spungs su skyed tshal gong dpon slob rnams mjal phyag tu 'byor/ rong byams chen na 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa'i thugs dam mgon sku'i bzhugs khyim
la gzhung sa'i dam 'byar 'grol bar mdzad nas mjal te slar rje nyid kyis phyag dam gnang / chos sde'i mkhan po'i dkar spro dang 'bul tshan zhus/ gan pa byang thang du zhe
re skyid tshal ba/ gong dkar slob dpon pa grwa slob/ bsam yas mkhan tshang rab 'byams pa rnams kyis mjal zhus la so so'i re skong gi byin

rlabs bka' stsol gnang / chu shur pu stag khu spo/ thar pa gling pa rnams kyis 'bul ba mjal zhus byung bar chos 'brel sogs re skong gnang / de nyin gzhung sa gong nas rta dar/
rta thug rgya gling / 'bog ltsag dbu gdugs/ chibs rags sogasabacas gang 'grig gis 'byon dgos tshul phebs 'byor bzhin sngar rgyun ltar bsgrigs/ rin chen sgang du thab
bsu dang / gzhung rtse shod nas phebs bsu ba rta pa brgyad cu skor 'byor bar gsol ja gnyis kyi ring bzhugs gral gnang rjes yab sras rnams kyis sku'i g.yas phyogs nas phebs
bsu ba rnams dang / g.yon phyogs nas gdan sa'i drung 'khor rnams bsgrigs bkod gzhung gi mgron gnyer rgya phrug pas mdzad cing / lha sar phebs phral gzhung sa nas gsol ja
ja zhus dang / zur chas spom mtho phral 'bul gnang / sang gzhung gi mgron gnyer sogs phebs bsu ba nyi shu bskor gnang ba bcas rtse shod lhan cig dang zhal rgyas byung bar
rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang dang mjal ma thag thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi dgyes spro'i ngang gsol ja bzhi'i yun la gsung mol gnang / de mtshams bka' 'gyur khang du gsol ston
rgyas par stsal rjes phebs skyel dang bcas lha sar phebs te/ jo shAka rin po cher bzang gos kyi snam sbyar gra snam la sangs rgyas kyi sku brnyan

gyis mtshan pa'i khyad can 'bul bar mdzad pa'i mtshon rten mchog rnams la zhal gser snyan shal mar me bdug spos sogs mchod sprin du ma dang bcas bstan 'gro spyi'i phan bder
spyan dmigs kyi smon lam rgya cher gnang / tshes brgyad nyin yang po ta lar gdan 'dren zhus te 'gol mjal thog bka' mchid yun ring dang / rje btsun rin po che dang 'phags
pa rin po che'i dbu thod rnam gnyis sogs nang mjal 'ga' zhig bka' drin brkyangs/ tshes bcur rgyal dbang mchog la brtan bzhugs dang bcas 'bul spom mtho ba dang / grwa gtsang
la mang 'gyed sogs rgya cher stsal/ jo bo lo ke shwa ra dang/ rje btsun la mang 'gyed sogs rgya cher stsal/ jo bo lo ke shwa ra dang / rje btsun grags pa'i sku brnyan
rtsa ris ma sogs rten mchog rnams mjal zhing mchod 'bul smonalam mdzad/ tshes bcu gsum nyin rgyal dbang sku zhabs nas tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes gnang gi rten 'brel bsgrigs
pa dang bcas thon phyag gnang sbyin blos mi 'khyud pa dang / khyad par rje yab sras zur mjal gnang nas na bza' cha tshang / zhal dkar dngul steg can re sogs stsal te
yab sras nas sngar phan yang 'chad nyan gyis bstan srog 'thud pa byung 'dug cing / da dung yang chos tshul spyi dang khyad par mkhan chen kun spangs pa nas gsang chen slob
bshad kyi chos skor rnams

bzhes te spel thub pa gnang dgos/ sa skya zhabs drung rin po che gdan sa na gsung ngag slob bshad gnang gin gdug zer ba thos na nged rang nas kyang zhabs phyi gang 'gyur zhu
rgyu yin gsung pa sogs lugs gnyis nas thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi 'bel mchid lhug par gnang / tshes bco lngar sde srid sku zhabs nas gsol ston 'bul ba phul du byung ba dang
/ rnam rgyal grwa tshang nas kyang klu sbug gling khar gzim gur du spyan drangs te gsol ston 'bul ba rgya chen zhus/ lha sar bzhugs ring chos rje bco brgyad pa sogs bla
chen mi chen dmangs phal bcas la chos sbyin kyang re skong du stsal/ bcu dgu la rtse shod kyis phebs bsu ba rnams chibs skyel bar gnang ba ltar lhan cig chibs btegs/ sku
'bum thang nas gsol ja'i thog phebs skyel ba rnams la byin rlabs dang dngos skyes stsal te rje nyid dpon slob rnams rim gyis phebs/ phyin nyin zung mkhar dang / nyer gcig
nyin snga dro bsam yas nas rab byung mkhan slob/ mkhan tshang rab 'byams pa sku rten pa dpon g.yog sde pa skyi shod pa'i drung 'khor mang po bcas pas phebs bsu 'byor ba
dang lhan cig dal la gong nas rdo mchod phreng bar sku rten par chos skyong phebs grabs kyis rig pa mi gnas par nye tshe/ rje nyid nas nged dang chos skyong mjal ba'i

thog ma yin pas zla ba mar ngo la mi yong gsungs phral gzhi med du dngas/ bsam yas gtsug lag khang dang nye bar phebs tshe sngon sgar chen rin po ches bzhengs pa'i 'chams mgon
byin ldan/ rab byung grwa tshang gi gser phreng / skye bo pho mos gzhas glu bcas pho brang gong du phebs/ zla smad der yul phyogs kyi ser skya dad 'dus du mar dbang lung
chos bka' 'jal kha gang 'tshams gnang / yar lung rje dbon drung 'di nas bzung ste gong dkar bar zhabs phyir phebs nas bka' chos gsan/ zla mjug tu rje yab sras dbu bzhugs
kyi bsam yas rab byung mkhan pos zor las pa byas te dpon slob lnga bcu bskor gyis dmigs yul zhig la ched gtad kyi mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog 'phen par mdzad/ nub
me 'bar ba dang dur khrod bdag po keng rus gzugs can ltad mo bas mthun snang du mthong ba sogs mngon spyod kyi rtags mtshan ngo mtshar ba bzhin dmigs yul de yang ma 'gyang
par pha rol gyi ltad mor song ba'i bsngo rten 'byor bas tshar gcod rjes 'dzin lhan cig grub par mdzad/ hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i yar tshes gnyis kyi nyin rje yab sras dpon
slob kyis lcog gi rtser lha bsangs rgyas par gnang / dkar me khang du phebs te mkhan tshang dpon slob rnams kyis chos skyong spyan 'dren

zhus par 'phral phebs kyis rje yab sras rgyal sgo byang nas phebs pa dang / chos skyong chen po yang ring stabs kyis rdo skas rtsa bar phebs bsu 'byor nas rje yab sras la g.yas
bskor dang bcas lha mi lhan cig rdo skas 'gor phebs pa dang / chos skyong chen pos sa dkar po'i yul gyis bstan pa dar ba'i phyir lha rgyal thengs gsum 'then gsungs pa
bzhin/ der 'dus khrom gyis lha rgyal 'ur chil ba lan gsum 'then/ de mtshams sprul pa'i chos rgyal chen po yang sku phebs kyis rdo skas khar phebs bsur byon pa dang / sngon
bzhin lha rgyal bskul ba sogs mdzad/ rje yab sras nas kyang sgron dar sna lnga/ gser phud srang gang / chibs pa sga 'khor sogs mthun rdzas rnam grangs bco lnga tsam phul/
chos skyong chen po nas kyang pheb lam bskor sogs gang cir phun sum tshogs bzhin pa nas bsam yas su phebs pa legs pa legs tshul dang gdug 'dre'i gnas gzhi 'di ngo dod
pa gcig dang / rgyal posku lnga'i rten 'dzugs gcig byung na bod khams kyi bde skyid la phan pa yod byas pa yin kyang / da bar 'gyangs shing / 'on kyang da cha dang len
dgos tshul sogs gsungs par rje nyid nas kyang zhal bzhes mdzad/ slar yang tshes brgyad la sku phebs thog snga phyi'i 'phros du ma dang bcas bsam yas gtsug lag khang gtso
phal la

rgyud sde dang mthun pa'i rab gnas mdzad dgos gsungs pa bzhin/ phyi nyin rten mjal dang lhan cig mchod sprin du ma spro ba dang bcas pas lha khang thams cad la rab tu gnas
pa yang gnang / mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i bzhugs khri'i thog nas khrom tshogs shin tu che bar tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / rigs gsum mgon po'i rjes gnang stsal/ de thog
rab byung grwa tshang dang 'phrang 'go zhi ba grwa tshang rnams nas yo byad kyi 'bul dngos che phra rang 'khos dang bstun zhabs brtan zab rgyas phul/ tshes bco lngar yang
chos skyong chen po sku phebs kyis lcog gi nyams gso dgos tshul sogs bskyar zhus dang / chos skyong chen po nas 'bul ba dgu tshan bcu gsum tsam phul nas bzhes pa nan zhus
phul yang / bsod btags gcig dang gsol dkar gcig ma gtogs lcog rang du 'jog par gnang / gzhan yang mgon khang phu mda' gtor gzhi 'dzugs pa dang rab byung grwa tshang la
mang 'gyed thog sgrigs lam kun spyod kyi zhal bkod brjid 'doms che ba phebs/ rdo rje brag rig 'dzin chen po dpon slob dad mjal chos zhur byon par thugs bzhed 'grub par gnang
/ nyer gnyis la chibs bteg te de skabs dgun grang ngad che ba'i stabs kyis phyi dro gru sgrol ba sogs dka' bar brten/ de nub

gtsang po pha kar 'byon stabs ma bde bar/ rje nyid nas dos rnams pha kar phyin tsam byung na sku nyid bcas ko bar phebs chog tshul sogs gnang ba ltar gru khar phebs phral gnam
yul dro bas de nub gra phyir phebs pa na byings dmangs kyis sngar dus las nyi ma nyis 'gyur du ring ba byung bas rje yab sras kyis nyi ma bzung bar 'dug ces grags pa
byung ba ltar don la'ang gnas/ de phyogs ser skya khrom tshogs bcas la chos sbyin rgya cher stsal/ de kha'i gtsug lag khang du mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor gyi thugs ring
bsrel 'byon bzhin pa zhig yod pa de rje 'di'i phyag tu bzhes ma thag ring bsrel mang bar babs shing / ring bsrel gcig sgra dang bcas nas rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi
phyag tu babs pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i rtags mtshan kun la gsal bar byung / gra thang du phebs grwa pa mngon shes kyi chos khri'i thog nas khrom chen la tshe dbang gnang
/ gter bdag gling pa chen po yang mjal kha dang bka' chos zhu bar phebs par kyai rdor rgyu lam gyi dbang sogs bzhed skong bstsal/ de skabs ngan rkyen gyi dbyen sbyor la
brten sgrub sde nam mkha' mdzod pa sdang sner yod skabs la gter ston rin po che nas 'di don gzhung sa yas phyin la snyan lhon thog sor chud yong thabs nan bskul dang / rje
nyid

kyang sgrub gra khyad thon yin stabs thugs kyis ma bzod de chos skyong rnams la bka' sgo 'phrin bcol drag po mdzad pas ngan rkyen byed pa rnams la rtsub 'gyur byung bar brten
rgyal dbang mchog nas kyang bka' drin chen pos sgrub sde de nyid sngar mkhos bde 'jags stsal/ de nas gdung phud chos 'khor du bzhugs zhag bzhi'i ring la grwa tshang tshang
mar lugs gnyis brtse gzigs kyi re bskong gnang / khrom tshogs la tshe dbang stsal/ mgon khang du gtor gzhi gsar 'dzugs mdzad/ de skabs rgyal po sku lnga'i shar phyogs
rgyal po yin zer ba'i khog zhugs gcig yang yang byung bar/ lan gcig rje nyid nas khyod shar phyogs rgyal po yin na khyod rang gi sngon gyi lo rgyus shod cig gsung sa par
thogs med bshad byung bas thugs yid ches te gtor ma dang 'phrin bcol bcas khag gcig dang ral gri gcig gnang ba de sogs gzugs med lha 'dres kyang zhabs la btud pa'i rnam
thar ya mtshan pa'ang mang du byung / skyid gshong ra ba smad du lha mi'i bsu ba dang bcas te rdo gcal du phebs skabs chos skyong nas dge bshes rang gi stan dmar things
shig gsungs pa ltar der bzhugs par chos skyong nas mjal dar phul te phebs lam nas sku gsung thugs la ngal ba ma mchis sam zhes sogs bsnyun rmed

phul/ rje yab sras nas kyang sgron dar sna lnga gnang / phyi nyin rje yab sras dpon slob sku rten pa dang bcas gtsug lag khang gi thog lha bsangs rgyas par gnang thog chos
skyong sku phebs grabs byung bar rje nyid nas phyag nas zhig gnang bas bsangs grol mtshams bar ma phebs shing de nas phebs te rje yab sras la chos skyong nas dbu gdugs dkar
po zhig phul/ phar yang sgron dar/ khrab gdan/ phyag ral sogs spyan gzigs rgya chen stsal te bstan 'gro spyi sger gyi phan bde'i 'phrin bcol gnang ba ltar chos skyong
nas kyang zhal bzhes mdzad/ rje nyid grub mchog bsod nams dbang po'i rnam 'phrul dang / rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid sgar chen rin po che'i skye sprul yin tshul lung
bstan dang / rgyal mtshan bzhi sogs 'bul ba mang po dang phyag phyi drung 'khor rnams la brtan bzhugs 'bul dngos 'byor bstun phul/ rjes gnang ljags lung sogs chos bka' rgya
cher bstsal/ khrom tshogs la tshe dbang grub rgyal lugs dang / mgon khang steng 'og tu brtan gtor 'dzugs pa dang gsung bskang 'phrin bcol gnang / de nas chibs bteg nyin
chos skyong nas kyang dgon gshams bar du phebs skyel dang bcas/ dge bshes slar yang nyi ma

dbus phyogs su rta pho'i kha lo bsgyur ba'i rten 'brel du gdug 'dres gtsug lag khang gi rtse nas g.yab mo lan gsum byed pas/ dge bshes nas rta pho'i kha lo g.yas su bsgyur
ba re mdzod gsungs nas nas chos skyong yar phebs te gtsug lag khang gi steng nas ki sgra dang bcas pa'i mda' dar gyis g.yab mo lan gsum mdzad pa dang rje dpon slob rnams
kyang chibs kha g.yas su bsgyur ba re gnang / rnam rab tu grwa tshang gis gtsug lag khang du gdan drangs nas 'bul ba gang 'byor bcas zhabs brtan phul/ mgon khang du gtor
gzhi 'dzugs pa dang 'phrin bcol gnang / de nas phebs lam du chu rags rnams la phyag nas mdzad pas de phyin chu'i gnod pa ma byung ba dang rnam rab phyag 'debs la lo tog rgyun
zhes la phyag nas gnang bas de phyin shin tu lo legs byung ba dang / tshe dbang gi tshe bum nor bu tshe ring la gnang ba las bdud rtsi chal chil du 'babs pa sogs byin
rlabs kyi mtshan ma ngo mtshar ba yongs su grags/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan du phebs bsu rgya chen dang bcas phebs nyin 'ja' 'od kyi gur dang me tog gi char mthun grub tu
byung / gsang ba'i mgon khang dam 'byar dkrol te rgyun gtor 'dzugs pa dang gsung bskang 'phrin bcol gnang /

'dus tshogs kyis gsol ba btab ngor rje nyid nas yang dag dang / rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs nas phur pa lha khra'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang bskur la slob ma nyi
shu rtsa lnga'i grangs bcad dngos sta re mos nyin zhag bco lnga tsam la g.yel med gnang / de skabs yar 'brog gling zhabs drung rin po che phebs nas 'bul chen dang bcas yang
phur gyi dbang bka' zhus/ chos sdes kyang zhabs brtan dang sbrel ba'i dngos porgya cher phul/ dad ldan sbyin bdag ser skya du mar re skong gi chos dang zang zing gnang
/ 'dus tshogs kyis rgyud sde du ma'i sgrub mchod dang / gur gar sogs phyag len gyi rgyun rnams gzigs 'bul zhus/ de skabs 'bras spungs grwa tshang la dar rgyas cher med
stabs chibs bteg khar phyag nas zhus pas de phyin dar rgyas byung / de nas rim gyis rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sder phebs te ser skya phyogs 'dus la chos dang zang zing gis
spro ba mchog gi dga' ston stsal/ 'bul nod bsnyen bkur dpag tu med pa dang / zha lur phebs nas bzhugs/ zhag bzhii'i ring la chos sbyiin mang 'gyed sogs stsal/ ngor du
phebs nas khang gsar bla brang du bzhugs gdan 'jags/ de skabs chab gzhi ma 'phrod pa'i rnams pas rje nyid sku khams cung zad ma snyoms pa'i sku rim du dbu mdzad chen

mos zor las byas te 'jigs byed drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog nyin gang zhig kyang gnang / snga phyir nan zhus ngor rdo rje 'chang gi bzhugs khri'i thog nas rje nyid kyis 'dus tshogs
la bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs dang / gnas bcu'i rjes gnang / phyi'i chos khri'i steng nas khrom la tshe dbang / shab dge sdings su'ang de bzhin te/ de ltar gdan
sa nas chibs btegs nas bzung yas mar phebs lam ris med kyi chos sde skyed tshal gong 'og jo gdan/ byams chen grwa tshang khag gnyis/ ngur smrig lha sa nas rnam rgyal grwa
tshang / ser 'bras/ tshal gung thang / bsam yas rab byung grwa tshang / grwa phyi/ gra thang / gdung phud chos 'khor/ skyid gshong ra ba smad/ dwags po grwa tshang /
gong dkar rdo rje gdan/ rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde/ brtse chen/ zha lu/ ngor e waM/ Da Di chos rdzong rnams gtsor smos la mang 'gyed rgya cher gnang ba dang / chu mig
gtsug lag khang / byams chen mgon khang / ngur smrig lha khang dang sa chen zhabs rjes/ snye thang jo rje'i gnas bzhi'i gtsug lag khang / chos rje bla ma'i phyi rten jo
bo'i gdung thal gyi sku 'bum/ bkra shis sgang mkhan chen grags seng ge chos khri/ 'phags sde'i nang rten/ lha sa'i jo shAka rin po che rnam gnyis kyi gtsos pa'i rten mchog
mtha' dag

po ta la'i nang mjal gyi rigs/ tshal gung thang gi phyi nang gi rten rnams/ bsam yas gtsug lag khang / gra phyi/ gra thang / gong dkar rdo rje gdan/ thong lcags mgon khang/
gnas gsar zha lu/ ngor e waM chos ldan rnams kyi rten gsum grags chen byin rten sogs kyis gtsos phyi nang gi rten rnams la snyan shal mchod sprin dang bcas bstan 'gro spyi'i
phan bder dgongs pa'i gsung smon phur tshugs gnang / nang don gyi btab pa'i skye bo mang po la zhal mjal phyag dbang tsam gyis bar gcod 'phral sel mdzad/ skal ldan gyi
skye 'gro bgrangs las 'das pa thar pa'i lam srol la bkod nas slar yang gdan sar phebs/ lha khang mkhan chen sogs phebs bsu ba las 'dzin rnams la gnang skyes dang / 'dus
tshogs la mang 'gyed/ mgon khang rnams su gtang rag sogs rgya cher gnang / dgung grangs so brgyad pa shing yos zla ba gsum pa tshes nas sngar ljags bkod kyi 'phros gos
sku chen mo dang / gnas bcu lha khang gi ldebs ris sogs las mgo btsugs nas mi ring bar grub ste rab tu gnas par mdzad/ de nas rgyal dbang mchog nas snga sor dngos mjal skabs
gsung bskul bzhiin chab chu bzang khyad kyi zha lu mkhan chen gdan sa bar du gdan drangs

nas bka' chos gsan pa 'thad tshul dang / gdan sa'i mgon khang nye 'gyangs rnams su skyes chen dam pa dag chos gsung gsan la gegs 'tshe med pa'i 'phrin bcol can gyi snyan shal
sogs dang lhan cig rje 'di nyid la gsung shog gnang bar/ ganggA'i rdul snyed las 'das rgyal rnams kyi/ /yon tan thugs bskyed drod kyis rigs kun bdag/ /gser sgong yongs
smin sdee bzhi'i zhal sgo can/ /chos phung rgya mtsho'i 'byung gnas mes po cher/ /zhes rgyal ba thams cad kyi yon tan gcig tu bsdus pa las rje 'di byung ba dam chos kyi
'byung gnas yin pa dpe can dang / gser gyi sgo nga las tshangs pa skyes pa chu bo ganggA'i 'byung gnas dper bkod de ldan pa'i gzugs can gyi rgyan du mdzad pa dang / nye ba'i
char yang lha sngags ye shes kyi/ /gsang gsum mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lo'i gar/ /'dzam gling skye dgu'i bsod nams mchod sde dung / /bsgyur 'di yid kyi kun dga' bskyed
pa'i gsos/ /zhes nges pa lnga ldan gyi zhing du sku lha gsung sngags/ thugs ye shes kyi rang bzhin mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lor bzhugs pa'i sprul pa'i snang brnyan rje 'di
nyid kyi rnam par shar ba bsam pa rgya che ba'i rgyan/

ring nas bdud bzhi'i dmag dpung mthar byas pa'i/ /mtshan dpe'i lang tsho bkra ba'i lus brtas par/ /bsnyun 'dri byis blor nges mod tshul bstan tsam/ /med de skal bzang lus can
legs byas dpyid/ /ces sku khams rnyog pa med pa ya mtshan du ci zhig 'dzin te phung po'i bdud sogs thog ma nas bcom zin pa nyid kyis bsngags pa rgyu yis 'gog pa'i rgyan/
'di na phra mo'i na tshod zla tshes nas/ /thos bsam 'phel 'grib byed pa'i blo dman bdag /srid pa'i nyes skyon mthong bzhin chos brgyad gdon/ /snying btab smyon pa'i gar
mkhan lta bur gnas/ /zhes rgyal dbang sku nyid thos bsam sogs 'phel 'grib byed pa zla ba dkar nag gi phyogs kyi dpe gzugs can dang / srid pa'i nyes skyon mthong yang 'dor
ma nus pa smyon pa lta bu zhes dpe rgyan sogs rgyan 'dres pa rab spel du mdzad nas rang nyid dman sa 'dzin pa dam pa'i rnam thar dang / 'od gsal lha rigs tshangs pa'i
ral klung nas/ /'jam dbyangs thugs rje'i yan lag brgyad ldan chab/ /gangs can bstan pa'i khyab 'jug zhabs bsil du/ /chad med lung rtogs rgya mtshor 'khyil pa rmad/ /ces 'jam
dbyangs 'khon gyi gdung las rje 'di nyid thub bstan lung rtogs kyi dpal du byon

pa dpe can dang / tshangs pa'i ral pa nas chu bo ganggA khyab 'jug gi zhabs bsil du phabs pa rgya mtshor babs pa dper mdzad pa'i mtha' dag gzugs can dang / gtan bde'i nor bu
don gnyer mgron po rnams/ /brtse chen bla ma'i thugs bcud gru gzings la/ /brten nas thar pa'i rin chen gling khrid pa'i/ /ded dpon mchog de khyod min gzhan na ci/ /zhes
thar pa don gnyer mchis na rje 'di la gsol ba btab phyin brtse chen snying po'i thugs bcud snyan brgyud la brten nas thar gling du khrid nus pa ni/ rin chen don du gnyer
ba rnams nged dpon mkhas pa la brten na gru gzings su bcug nas rin chen gling du sleb pa'i dpes rgyan snga ma ltar dang / yang srid nyer lnga 'jam pa'i rdo rje yis/ /rjes
bzung lnga rig 'chad snyan sgra bo che/ /sa skya lo tsA'i bstan pa gangs can kun/ /yongs khyab spel bar bsam bzhin byon na snyam/ /zhes mi nas mir gyur yang srid nyer lngar
'jam mgon gyis rjes su bzung ba'i sa skya paN chen de nyid slar yang rang gi bstan pa spel ba'i ched du rje 'dir sprul nas phebs par yin nam snyam zhes rje 'di nyid
mkhas pa'i tshul la bsngags pa rab rtog snyam sgra

can dang / chos rgyal 'phags pa'i gdan khri pad can steng / /zhabs rdul dmar 'od lhung ba'i 'dren pa khyod/ /sa gsum skye dgu'i tshogs kyi gtsug gtor rtser/ /rdo rje'i skyil
krung gcig gis khyab pa 'dra/ zhes kun gyi gtsug rgyan du gyur pa chos rgyal 'phags pa dang mtshungs par bsngags pa la skyil krung rgya che drags pas srid pa gsum mnan
pa 'dra zhes rab rtogs 'dra ba'i sgra can sogs daNDi'i gzhung lugs las drangs pa rgyal dbang nyid kyi chab shog glegs bam du gsal ba bzhin gnang ba ni/ slob dpon klu sgrub
kyis/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan ni/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mkhyen/ /sa gzhi yi ni lci ba'i tshad/ mtha' yas nyid kyis shes par 'gyur/ /zhes pa ltar snang zhing
/ de lta bu'i snyan phrin gyis lam nas gsung ngag rin po che gsan bskul gnang 'byor dang / mkhan chen drung du'ang gsung ngag slob bshad gnang thub pa dgos tshul de bzhin
yod 'dug pa bcas yos lo snron zla'i nyer lnga la chibs bteg shab dge sdings su phebs pa'i phyi nyin nas mkhan chen yang byon pa dang / gzhan yang dbon rin po che ngag
dbang blo gsal mchog ldan/ sgra pa bshes gnyen rnam rgyal/ bya tshang rje drung sogs kyang

'byor ba nas drug pa'i tshes gsum la bka' chos kyi dbu tshugasate zhag bdun song mtshams rje 'di'i mnal lam du a tsa ra mdog sngo bsangs g.yon na rwa dung zhig bzung / g.yas
pas glegs bam zhig rje nyid la phul nas lam 'bras rdo rje'i tshig rkang dgos na 'di yin zer bas phyag brkyangs nas bzhes par brtsams kyang glegs bam phyag tu ma byung bar
mnal sad pa zhig byung ba 'di res chos mtha' mi rdzogs pa'i ltas su snang / de nas snang gsum rdzogs nas rje nyid gdan sa gong du phur sgrub la phebs shing / rgyal dbang
sku zhabs su lam 'bras tshugs tshul sogs zhu yig 'bul mi gnang / mkhan chen nyid ljags bsnyen zhal gsos la bzhugs/ rgyal dbang mchog nas bka' lan du bka' chos tshugs pa
legs tshul dang / slar yang phur sgrub grol mtshams gzhan dbang la ma song ba'i chos 'phro bzhes thub dgos tshul sogs dang / gdan sa dang mkhan chen gnyis kar bka' chos
tshul pa'i dga' ston la mchod gzhis re gnang bar rje 'di nyid la brag dkar bkra shis bsam 'grub sogs gtan 'jags kyi bka' khra bcas gnang ba yin zhing / de mur mkhan chen
sku khams bsnyel bar phur sgrub grol 'phral rje nyid phebs te rkyen sel bka' dbang sogs gnang / chos 'phro bshol te mkhan chen

nyid re zhig zha lur phebs/ rje nyid nas dbon drung sogs la dbang 'khrid chos bka' rgya cher gnang / dbon drung gdan sar byon par dmar po bskor gsum sogs zab chos 'ga' zhig
sger du'ang bstsal/ de skabs kyang mon pa a chog sogs kyi dkrug rkyen la brten pa'i lho bod zing long la 'gro phan du dgongs te bla ma sangs rgyas 'phel 'ching gi sku tshab
la brdzong bda' mdzad/ gzhung du'ang de tshul gyi zhu shog phul bar bka' lan du/ lho'i zhu 'ching skor la dpon slob khag rnams bgros pa'i rdzong bda' gnang ba sems can
gyi bde thabs la phan pa tsam yong las che zhes sogs bka' shog ma bu 'byor/ chos las pa shes rab rgyal mtshan la zhal bkod bca' yig dang bcas zangs ldan chos sder bsko
'ja' gnang / gzhung sa chen po nas sde pa khri 'don gyi legs 'bul du phyag mdzod rdzong bda' gnang ba dang / lhan cig zangs ldan mkhan po yang phyag 'bul la thegs/ gzhis
byes dge 'dun 'dus tshogs mang ba rnams la gsang bde 'jigs gsum sogs kyis chos 'khor rgya chen bskor/ be tshang dbon pos gser gar lugs kyis 'jam dbyangs gtso 'khor lnga'i
sku brnyan sogs 'bul chen dang bcas gsol ba btab ngor 'jigs byed ra lugs sogs dbang bka' rjes

gnang byin rlabs ljags lung du ma re skong du bstsal/ de mtshams gsung ngag gsan lhag mkhan chen nas gnang ma thub stabs ka spe rje drung ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas grangs
chen gdan sa dgongs zhus dang / gsung ngag slob bshad kyang de nas gsan na 'os min sogs la rgyal dbang sku zhabs su zhu shog gnang ba'i bka' lan snga phyir/ snga sor gdan
sa bar du bka' chos tshugs pa mthar phyin byung na legs tshogs che rung chos mtshams gnang dgos shar bar/ grwa chen mkhan po khur len dgongs khrol yong ba dang bstun
rje nyid nas slob bshad kha gtsang zhig kyang gsan rgyu mdzad na mi 'os pa med cing / slar mkhan chen nas kyang bskyar ma gsan thub pa e yong sogs phebs pa 'byor 'phral dgyes
tshor dang bcas thugs la shin tu bcags kyang / lha bod kyis 'dun 'ching la sku tshab rang gis 'ching mi thub dogs dang / bsam yas lcog gi rten 'dzugs sogs 'gyang dgos
kyis chos skyong chen por gang spyi'i gsol mchod 'bul mi gnang ba'i lan du/ dge bshes rang gi las kyi skal ba byed dgos la/ phyi nang gsang gsum gyi rten rdzas kyi bye
brag dang / sku lnga 'khor bcas kyi rgyud gzhung bye brag dang mthun pa'i yid lus kyi gzugs ri mor 'khod pa/ hor zla gsum pa'i lha

tshes gcig la las 'go tshugs pa zhig dgos/ zhes sogs zhu phrin nan cher 'byor bstun sprul sku padma dbang rgyal gyis gtsos pa'i gsum 'phral brdzong gnang / snga sor lcog gi
zhig gsos gnang rgyu'i thog mar las mi sogs la nyes skyon mi 'ong ba dgos tshul phrin bcol gnang ba'i lan du/ gzhal yas khang gi nyams gsos 'di/ /bkod pa sngon nas byas
pa bzhin/ /dus kyi rten 'brel ma 'griig pas/ /las byed pho nya mtha' dag la/ /bar gcod mi 'byung dka' na yang / /'khor du gtogs pa'i sde brgyad po/ /dkar phyogs lha dang
nag po'i bdud/ /phyed mar yod pas 'chun par dka'/ /'on kyang dpal chen khrag 'thung gi /bka' zhin dam las mi 'gal bar/ /dam bsgrags byed pas go bar gyis/ /yang bskyar bkod
pa'i sna gcig la/ /gzugs med gdug pa sde brgyad rnams/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa spel ba dang / /dkon mchog dbu 'phang bstod pa dang / /gnas gzhi gtsug la skyong ba la/ /la
la dga' ste la la khro/ /de yi bkod pa skor phyir du/ /li yul lcang ra smug po dang / /byang phyogs shambha la sogs par/ /gdug 'dres khrid nas mgo skor byed/ /gzags can
la 'tsher med tsam zhig /e 'ong lta bas nges par gyis/ /zhes zhu lan byung ba dang bstun

las mi nas rje nyid la zhig gsos 'dzugs khar 'thor rgyu'i phyag nas shig zhus pa gnang ste/ sa bshig ral byed rgyu'i snga nyin thor cig par bka' stsal ba bzhin byas pas de
nub tsheg sgra 'ur chom sogs skyel byed pa'i rnam pa 'tshub cher byung bas/ phyi nyin thams cad 'jigs shing bshig phral gyi sna bstad byed nus mkhan ma byung ba la/ zung
mkhar bar pa zhig gis las sne gtod pa bcas mthar phyin gyis bar du ar mi 'go pa gcig la'ang nyes skyon ma byung ni snga sor zhal bzhes dam bca' phul ba bzhin gnas/ dgung
grangs so dgu par lho bod mtshams su zing bun che tsam byung bar rgyal dbang sku zhabs su g.yul 'khrugs sogs bshol ba'i bka' sde srid la phebs dgos tshul dang / sde srid
la'ang de bzhin 'bul bar mdzad par sku zhabs rtse nas bka' lan du phan tshun gnyis lo'i chings mtshams byung na sde par yang mtha' skyel du ma song ba dgos tshul 'di nas
kyang 'phros pa byed cing / bar bzhugs khag nas kyang sems can gyi bde thabs la dgongs pa'i phan skor thabs sgo gang zab gnang dgos tshul sogs phebs/ de skabs dbus dpung
gling bzhi brgyud nas brdzangs/ gtsang dpung gis sa dkar la dang spre mo la brgyud/

dpung khag gnyis mtsho sna dang bum thang sogs brgyud pas 'chings khag rnams bya byed dang bral bar gyur/ skye 'gro kun gyis kyang chings mtshams 'dir sa skya bdag chen rin
po che phebs ma thub na sems can gyi bde skyid zad pa yin zhes mgrin gcig tu gleng ba dang / rje nyid kyi kyang thugs rje gting nas g.yos pas phebs par bzhed de bsam yas
mdo sde mchod 'bul dang lhan cig chos skyong chen por yang lung zhu dang 'phrin bcol gnang ba'i bka' lan du/ nag po bdud kyis kha bsgyur ba'i gzugs can re 'gas sems can
gyi bde skyid 'di dkrug 'dug pas gdug 'dres de dag la lnga sor nas kha gnon re byed kyin yod pas/ dge bshes kyi re ba ltar sems can smin grol gyi lam du 'god pa'i sdong grogs
'bad rtsol byed ces phebs pa dang bstun/ lam gtor mgon khang rnams su gsung bskang 'phrin bcol gnang zhing / ra ba smad chos skyong la'ang 'phrin bcol rten gnang bar
yang gzhis byes su gegs 'tshe mi 'byung ba'i lung gsal 'byor ba bzhin zla ba bcu par chibs bteg lam bar gyi gdul bya du ma smin grol la 'god bzhin pas phag rir phebs mtshams
bkra shis lhun po dang stag bde zhabs drung gnyis sogs chings khag bzhan yang 'dzoms pa nas spre mo la phar rgyab kyi sho smug tu

bzhugs sgar gnang / de mtshams rtse gdong zhabs drung yang phebs pas thams cad bka' 'gros thog nas phan skor gang drag dang khyad par rje nyid nas sems can spyi'i bde thabs
la 'o brgyal khyad bsad kyis rong la 'byon thengs bcu gcig tsam mdzad kyang dmag dpon rnams kha shin tu mkhrang bas yun ring byung mtshams/ dkrug rkyen gtor shing byed mi
rnams la rdo rje'i chos srung rnams kyi bka' chad rtags mtshan cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung ba dang / bsam yas chos skyong chen po nas kyang bzhed don 'grub 'gyur gyi lung
bstan dang / ra ba smad bse khrab can nas kyang log lta can kun la la ni sa bdag gi nad kyis btab ste rgyun bcad yod/ la la ni mkha' dbyings nas khrom mda' lha ma yin
gyis lcags zhu btab nas gum par bgyis yod/ la la ni rgyal po'i smyo 'bog gis byings te gnas dog mor bcug nas bzhag pa de kun sa dkar po'i steng gi dge bshes 'jam pa'i rdo
rjes gzigs shing gsan pa de bzhin legs mod ces sogs byung ba bzhiin bzhed don mi ring bar 'grub pa'i rten 'brel du ma 'grig pa nas/ sbrul lo zla ba dgu pa'i nang rgyal dbang
sku zhabs su bslab ston zhu bar chibs bsgyur gnang nas gan pa byang thang bar phebs thog gzhung sa nas zhabs 'gyel zhus bstun chings

'tshams zhib gsed zhu shog phul ba'i bka' lan du/ da lan khad nyer phebs pas 'jal 'dod shin tu che yang / la rgya'i stabs mjal 'dzoms ma bde bsam yas phyogs su rten 'dzugs
rab gnas sogs kyis stabs myur bar zhal 'dzom yong ba sogs dang zhib par mgron gnyer skyar po ba'i gdung du gsal tshul zhib lhug dang zur chas dpang mtho bcas phebs pa bzhin
slar skor te spre mo la rgyab bcas sga zer bar bzhugs sgar gnang nas/ phan tshun du 'phen skor mdzad pas de mtshams so so nas dang len don smin byung bas/ dgung grangs
zhe gcig pa sa rta zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes gsum la lho par dbu rtsi gnang thog lho pas 'bul spom blos mi 'khyud pa phul zhing / tshes bzhir gzhung du dbu rtsi phul bar yang
gos dar ja sogs legs 'bul bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ phan tshun mi nor gyi sprod lan bde 'jags mdzad/ lho pa yon bdag rnams dang / spyi bla 'bul dpon pa/ spe shing pa/
'phang ye dgon/ waM gzhung/ spa gro gzhung brgyud sogs nas kyang rang mkhos dang bstun pa'i 'bul ba che chung dang bcas dad mjal du 'byor bar rang rang mos 'dun bzhin
gyi dbang rjes gnang / o rgyan rin po che'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ ma Ni'i bzlas lung sogs stsal

zhing/ khrom tshogs nas kyang badzra gu ru dang ma Ni 'dren pa srog gcod rku jag spong ba sogs kyi dam bca' phul/ de ltar lho bod du zla ba bco brgyad tsam gyi ring la gzhan
phan thugs rje'i shugs kyis dka' ba dang bzhes mdzad cing gdul bya rnams yid drangs pa'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod pa yang mang du ston par mdzad/ chings khag gzhan rnams
byer rjes mon phyogs kyi sprod lan phral chod ma byung bar rje nyid dpon slob rnams phag rir bzhugs/ de skabs kyang gdul bya dpag med la chos sbyin gnang / de mtshams
chibs bteg pa'i na ring rdzong chung ngu dbang chen zhig bstsal/ thub bstan rin chen gling du gtsug lag khang dang mgon khang rnams la mchod tshogs rgya cher mdzad skabs
mgon khang gi trag shad yab yum gyis zhal 'bag rje 'di'i phyag tu bzhes par spyan mtshams nas dngul chu lta bu'i bdud rtsi thig la khad mang po byung gsung bskang 'phrin
bcol sogs rgyas par stsal/ rma bya/ lha gdong / bdud pho brag sgrub sde rnams su phebs/ brag po che mgon khang du gtor ma la byi bas gnod pa byung tshul rje nyid la zhus
pas/ der sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros kyi thugs dam ma'i gur mgon gyi sku zhig yod pa de kha'i phu mdar 'pho skyes byas skyon yin pas da phyin bsgul bskyod ma byed gsungs
pa bzhin

byas pa de phyin byi ba'i gnod pa gtan ma byung / de ltar sbyin pa rnam bzhi'i lus can mtha' dag la phral dang yun gyi phan bde'i sgo brgya phye bar mdzad nas/ zla ba bzhi
pa'i tshes gcig la rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs 'khor bcas bya spe na khar chibs bsur phebs pas mtshon phebs bsu'i bkod pa nye 'gyangs ngo mtshar ba dang bcas gdan sa chen
por phyag phebs/ chos sder mang ja dang gzhan pa rnams la gnang sbyin/ mgon khang nye 'gyangs rnams su btang rag phun sum tshogs pa mdzad/ sngon dus rnams su'ang lho bod
kyi chings 'dum la gdan sa'i zhal ngo phebs res rnams su dkar phyogs kyilha dang nag phyogs kyi bdud stobs 'gran pa'i stabs kyis sku rkyen 'gyur ba'i rnam pa phal cher 'byu
nga stabs/ 'di skabs kyang lha khang mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bkra shis sku khams shin tu log par byung bas/ rje nyid nas cag thon dgos tshul phebs par zhu ngag
tu kha sang ka spe rje drung nas bdag gi nad zo gzigs pas cag thon dgos pa'i bslab ston gnang byung yang / bdag gi gong ma rin po che ma phebs bar du bdag 'chi mi 'ong zhus
pa kha pho don la gnas pa byung / da bdag la mi 'ong re mi 'dug kyang rje nyid bzhed don grub nas phebs pas blo bde/ bdag ma shi bar du

mkhan po'i 'os gzigs shig bka' drin brkyangs pa zhus pa bzhin bse dgon drung du lung zhus dang thugs brtag sgo bstun chos las pa ngag dbang kun rgyal bzang chug byung ba ltar
bka' stsal gnang bas thugs bder gyur pa'i mur mkhan chen de nyid zla ba bzhi pa phyi ma'i tshes gcig la sku gshegs pa'i gshegs rdzong tshogs dbur phebs pa dang / phyi
rten nang rten bzhengs pa sogs kyi bslab ston stsal/ zla ba de kha'i tshes bcu gsum dus tshes bzang 'dzom la mkhan chen ngag dbang kun rgyal nyid lha chen chos khrir mnga'
gsol gnang/ bsam yas su rten mdos 'dzugs dgos la phyag len tshul bzhin dgos gal che bar dgongs te/ mnga' bdag chen po'i dngos slob chu spe steng par skor gyi yig cha phyag
lan phra mo tshun chad mtha' mchod thugs bzhes mdzad nas slar rgyal dbang sku zhabs su phyag dpe gzigs 'bul dang 'di thog nas brten 'dzugs mdzad na yong min zhus lan
du/ pe dkar gyi skor dgongs par bcags pa bzhin/ shel phreng g.yu phreng lcags phreng sogs rgyud man ngag bka' gter gyi gzhung rnying du ma yod tshul 'dug kyang / da lan 'di
thog nas rten mdos 'dzugs pa gnang tshe rgyas bsdus 'tshams pa sogs nas gsar skyes kyi

snyan 'bul ma dgos tshul zhib rgyas phebs/ bsam yas chos skyong chen po nas kyang gzhal yas khang gi rten gso dang rab gnas la zla ba dgu pa'i nang tshun la rten 'brel sgrig
dgos pa dang/ lho bod 'dun 'ching gi dan mtha' lho phyogs btsan po nas sor gnang byung yang / byang phyogs btsan po nas gtam sar gyi bkod pa du ma zhig tsam 'dug pas de
dag gi dogs pa gcod pa dang zung 'brel du rta po'i kha lo bsgyur ba dgos tshul nan bskyar 'byor bar brten/ hor zla dgu pa'i tshes lngar chibs bsgyur gnang nyin gzhung sa
nas kyang mon shar gyi don rnams chod pa'i chod yig gnang bar phebs par 'gab tshul kyang 'byor/ rim gyis dpal 'khor chos sder phebs/ mkhan chen kun spangs pa'ang lo gsum
bcad rgya mdzad bzhin pa dang mjal/ rgyal dbang mchog gi sman bla mchod chog ljags 'khrigs dang mthun pa'i sku brnyan rnams bal po spi la jus gser zangs las bzhengs pa dpal
'khor chos sdersdar gnang 'dug pa gtsor smos gtsug lag khang la rab gnas rgyas par stsal/ bal po bza' mi rnams kyis bzo phud du bzhengs pa'i 'jam dbyangs kyi sku'i gtsos
pa'i 'bul ba rgya cher byung / gangs ru sgang mkhar chos sde/ la phyi dgon/ phag ri rnams su dbang bka' chos sbyiin gnang nas/

bca'bcas sgar bzhugs nas 'ching gzhug gi sprod len dang mjug sdom chod yig gnang zhing chings 'dum bskor mthar phyin par mdzad/ de skabs kyang dad ldan ser skya du mar chos
sbyin stsal ba dang / dad 'bul yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / de nas chibs 'khor te gdan sar phebs nye tshe rigs sras khri rin po ches gtsos pa'i ser skya dmangs mi'i
phebs bsu'i bkod pa dang bcas bzhi thog chos kyi pho brang du phebs/ mnga' zhabs lha sde mi sde bcas par gnang skyes dang / mgon khang rnams su gtang rag gi bskang gso
gnang grub bstun/ shar la chibs bsgyur mdzad tshe/ slob dpon rin po ches gsang ba'i lung bstan gab rgya can las/ pe dkar gling du rgyal po'i rtse mdos dang : gnod sbyin mchod
cing byang shar mtshams su gtong : sngags pa brgya yis zor 'phang drag bsngags bzlas: dge 'dun brgya yis bden tshig brjod pa na: bsam yas rje dpon dgra las rgyal bar
'gyur: mtha' yis dmang kyang lo nur zla nur 'gyur: zhes pa'i lung bstan dus babs kyis/ rgyal dbang sku zhabs nas kyang bsam yas chos skyong gi lung bstan du sa skya zhabs
drung gis lha sar rab gnas dang / bsam yas su phur bzlog rab gnas bcas khra 'brug tu rab gnas rnams mdzad na bod spyi'i bde

thabs la phan gsungs pa byung bas thugs khur bzhes dgos phebs pa ltar/ dgung grangs zhe gnyis pa mchu zla'i nyer gcig la chibs bteg/ lam bar gyi gdul bya rnams rjes su 'dzin
bzhin pas zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad nyin gzhung sa nas phebs bsu sogs sngar lugs bzhin gyi lha sar phebs/ phyi nyin yang bsu ba dang bcas po ta lar spyan drangs/ sde
srid kyang gzim chung 'gag tu phebs bsur byon pa bcas nas mjal spro yun ring gnang / tshes bcu gcig gi nyin jo bo'i sku mdun du kyai rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas smin rgyas
bstsal ba'i yon sgo'i sku tshab du bka' blon rtar mdongs pa dang / drung yig dar rgyas bkra shis gnyis byon/ ston mo dang legs 'bul zur gnang bcas phal pa'i blor mi
shong ba dang / bcu gsum nyin rgyal dbang sku zhabs su zhabs pad brtan bzhugs rgyas par phul zhing / dmar po skor gsum mgon po che chung sogs kyi 'khor lo'i phyag len gsal
byed kyi ljags lung sogs gsan/ po ta la dang lha sa'i rten mchog rnams la mchod mjal zhib pa smon lam phur tshugs gnang/ tshes bcu dgur rgyal dbang sku zhabs nas bzhugs
gral gnang thog sngon mar legs po dang / da dung bod khams spyi rim du

bsam yas su phur sgrub zhag bdun/ phur zlog zhag gsum/ rab gnas nyin gsum ma/ khra 'brug tu rab gnas nyin gsum ma zhig gnang dgos tshul sogs kyi nyer mkho'i yo byad dang /
gnang skyes zur bstsal bcas rgya dpangs che ba/ sde srid sku zhabs nas kyang ston mo 'bul ba rgya chen/ sku zhabs grwa tshang gis gtsos pa'i bla dpon dad 'dus kyi bsnyen
bkur bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / tshes nyi shu la phebs skyel dang bcas chib bteg skyid chu kha nas phebs skyel ba rnams la gnang cha bcas/ lho brgyud du phebs lam gyi
zhabs phyir sku tshab stod lung gros chung ba dang / kong po tsha bar a bo gnyis rdzong bda' gnang ba dang lhan cig/ nyer gnyis nyin bsam yas lha mi'i phebs bsu ring thung
sogs sngar bkod ltar pho brang gong du phebs/ nyer gsum nyin lcog gi rtser lha bsangs gnang / chos skyong dpon slob sku phebs dang phebs bsu lha rgyal bskul ba sogs sngar
bzhin dang / rje nyid nas kyang sgron dar/ ja phud/ gser phud/ dbu 'chings/ khrab gdan/ zhabs rgyan zhabs sgrogrog khrab rmog phyag ral/ zhags pa/ stag gzig sogs kyi mgo
brnyan bcu gsum/ gser zangs kyi rgyal mtshan bcu gsum/ zur bzhi la dril bu/ maNDal/ lha rta sga bcas sogs spyan gzigs rgya

cher bstsal/ chos skyong chen po nas kyang phebs lam gegs 'tshe med pa nas gdug 'dres bskul ma byas pa bzhin lha sar rab gnas tshugs pa legs tshul sogs zhib lhug dang / rje
nyid nas kyang lcog gi nyams gso rten 'dzugs sogs sgrub dgos de bzhin yin na'ang lho bod sems can bde thabs su 'gro dgos shar bar yun 'gyang tsam song yang / rtsa brgyud
bla ma lha dang khyed chos skyong ye shes kyi spyan ldan rnams kyi mthus legs rab byung tshul sogs lha mi bka' mchid nang bshin par gnang/ de'i phyi nyin nas phur sgrub
kyi bca' gzhi tshugs pa nas sku 'tshams gnang nyin bsam yas kyi mtha' phyogs char rgyun dang bcas pa'i sprin gyis khebs kyang / sku 'tshams ma grol bar char pa gtan nas ma
byung / rim pas phur bzlog rab gnas/ byang shar mtshams su mdos rdzong bar khang steng du brten mdos 'dzugs pa sogs zhib rgyas 'phral sel dang / klu gnyan sa bdag rnams
la'ang klu gtor bka' sgo sogs gnang bar brten/ 'di lo lo tog kyang phun sum tshogs pa byung / chos skyong chen po nas kyang rten 'dzugs sogs grub par legs so rgya cher phul/
khrom tshogs la tshe dbang gnang / zla ba gsum pa'i nyer bzhir khra 'brug tu chibs bsgyur nas

der yang rab gnas nyin gsum ma rgyas par gnang / bkra shis chos sde nas gdan 'dren zhus par 'byon bzhed shar yang chos sder phebs stabs ma bde bas grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan
dang sbrel ba'i 'bul dngos rgya chen phul/ khra 'brug nas phebs khar kha sang nas 'dir sngod ring la bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis sku zhig 'ong bsam pa byung
yang de snga ma byung / da de ring ni mi yong ngam gsung byung ba dang / chibs skyel ba rnams la slog cha gnang ba'i tshe/ yar lung 'dir snga sor dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa dang / yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ de dag phar slob tshur slob yin pas/ seng rgyal ba'i phyag bzo bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi sku sbyin rlabs can khyed
rnams la med dam gsungs par/ rtse tshogs pa'i grwa pa gcig gis bdag la chos rje bla ma dam pa'i shangs mtshal las grub pa'i yar lung pa de nyid kyi phyag bzo 'khrul med
dkar me 'dzin nges byin ldan zhig yod pas cis kyang bul spro zer ba bzhin la thugs shin tu mnyes te byin rlabs gnang skyes legs par stsal zhing / sku de nyid gzim chung
ngu bzhugs su gsol/ de gong lha sa nas gsang phu mchos khang bla ma mjal du byung ba khyed la sa paN gyi zhun thigs las grub pa'i rnam rgyal gyi sku zhig yod gdug

pa de nged la bslang gsung pa na gus pa dang bcas phul ba sku la 'bral med du bcang bar mdzad/ gra phyi ru phebs skabs chos skyong gi lcog rtsar phebs bsu ba'i grwa pa gcig
rta thog nas dran med du 'gyel bar rje nyid nas chos skyong gi sku gsung thugs la nyes 'gel byung ba bshags pa bzhes dgos gsungs pas/ chos skyong gi sha ngar zhig thongs
da lan dge bshes kyi ngo la srog skyon mi gtong zer ba bzhin bde bar gyur/ chos skyong nas rje nyid la mjal dar dang bcas dbus phebs sngon ma'i skabs 'dug 'dre'i lus khog
rgas pas dge bshes dang phrad ma thub kyang / dge bshes kyis phyag nas gnang bas lus sems bde ba byung zhes sogs dad gus kyi zhu mchid mang pa zhus pa dang / 'dus tshogs
nas zhabs brtan bcas 'bul ba rgya cher phul/ gter bdag gling pa chen po yang mjal khar phebs pas thugs spro gnang / sding po che'i sprul sku ngag dbang snyan grags bzang
po yang 'bul chen dang bcas chos 'brel zhu bar byon pas khong thugs gzu bor gnas pa la mnyes tshor dang bcas zhen pa bzhi bral gyi rtsa tshig gnang / khrom chen la dbang
bka' bstsal/ sgrub sde nam mkha' mdzod pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyer lnga bka' 'brel zhu bar 'byor bar chos bka' kha shas dang slob dpon

chen por ja mchod zhig ljags rtsom mdzad nas lung bcas bstsal/ gdungs phud du lam 'bras lha khang gsar bzhengs la phyag nas khrom dbang sogs re bskong du gnang / skyid gshong
ra ba smad du phebs bsu'i bkod pa chos skyong nyid nas gnang ste/ ser phreng gi rjes su me long khyer ba lnga/ bum pa kha rgyan bcud ldan khyer ba lnga/ ral gri khyer
ba lnga/ zhags pa khyer ba lnga/ mda' dar khyer ba lnga/ rgyal mtshan khyer ba lnga/ khrab can mdung dar khyer ba lnga/ gzig lpags khyer ba lnga/ rol cha khyer ba lnga rnams
'asgrigs/ chos skyong rang ser phreng gi dkyil du byon nas/ de nyid du mjal dar phul/ rje nyid nas kyang sgron dar gnang ste lhan cig phebs/ de skabs chos skyong chen
pos sems can spyi'i bde thabs 'di dkrug pa'i dam nyams shig gdug 'dres bsgral ba dge bshes la spyan lam du 'beb rgyu yod gsungs pas rje nyid kyis khyed chos skyong rnams
bstan dang bstan 'dzin srung skyong gi las byed pa yin pas tshul de shin tu legs/ da dung khyed dus gsum sgrib med gzigs pa'i ye shes kyi spyan dang ldan pas bstan dgra
rnams myur du sgrol dgos gsungs pas/ de las phyis tsam na chos skyong nyid kyis lcog gi sgo'i g.yon phyogs su stag lpags shig

bting/ lcog nas zhags pa zhig de'i khar brkyangs/ sang sku phebs skabs bsdu bar mdzad song bas/ gsang ba'i dgra bo zhig tshe 'phos pa'i bsngo rten 'bul mi 'byor bas de la blta
bar 'dug gsungs / de skor chos skyong nas bka' zhib bgros dang rten 'brel rgya cher bsgrig par mdzad/ skya ser khrom tshogs la dbang bka' byin rlabs sogs sku drin rgya
cher bstsal/ dgas po grwa tshang nas gsan drangs 'bul ba sogs gzab rgyas zhus/ gong dkar du phebs te li ma lha khang du bzhugs/ nang so lhun grub rab brtan pas 'bul bar
rgya cher zhus/ bka' las khyed rang sngar phan chos sde 'di kha'i sbyin bdag yin 'dug gshis de las mi g.yo ba dgos lugs phebs pa dang / khong pas kyang deng sang phan chad
shi gson gyi skyabs gnas sa lugs yin zhing da dung yang zhu zer ba'i dam bca' skyabs 'jug phul/ skya ser khrom chen la dbang bka' bstsal/ khyad par thams cad mkhyen pa
chen po'i sku gdung ril po bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung mjal bar mdzad tshe/ 'du khang nas ring bsrel zhig sgra dang bcas te sku pang du babs/ rim gyis phebs te/ yar 'brog sde
pa bgres gzhon thugs nang ma gshin pa lugs legs dgos tshul dam tshig gi sgrel ba'i

ched du kyai rdor rgyu lam gyis dbang gnang bas de phyin nang gtsang du gyur/ rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde nas kyang 'bul nod bsnyen bkur bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung zhing
/ de phyogs ser skya bgrang las 'das pa thar pa'i go 'phang la bkod/ ngor du phebs lam phebs bsu ba phyag dbang zhu mi mang po'i nang nas bud med gcig gi mthong snang la
rje'i chibs gzhogs g.yas g.yon na spyang 'dra ba'i sems can 'jug ma ring po can gnyis 'dug pa mthong bas bred nas brgyal ba'i gnas tshul rim gyis snyan du dwangs bar/ ngor
pa'i phebs bsu ba rnams dang lhan cig dpal mgon zhal yang nged bsu ba la phebs pa yin 'dug gsungs pa de skabs dpal mgon dngos su gzigs pa yin 'dug ngor khang gsar bla
brang du bzhugs/ bla brang so so nas kyang 'bul nod rgya cher phul/ ser skya bgrang ba bka' ba la chos sbyin dbang bka' gnang / rim gyis shab dge sdengs brgyud nas phebs
'di res kyang phebs lam gyis ris med chos sde ser 'bras/ yar lung bkra shis chos sde/ ras chung phug/ yar lung shel brag rtse tshogs/ gra phyi/ sdings po che/ sgrub sde
nam mkha' mdzod/ gdung phud ra ba smad/ dwags po grwa tshang / gong dkar rdo rje gdan/ thar gling / rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos

sde/ brtse chen/ ngor e waM/ Da Ti chos rdzong sogs la mang 'gyed rgya cher stsal te thugs dgongs spro bzhin pa'i ngang nas gdan sa chen por phebs bsu'i bkod pa sngar rgyun
bzhin bcas bzhi thog pho brang du phebs/ lha mi mtha' dag la gtang rag dga' ston phun sum tshogs pa stsal/ thub bstan yangs can mkhan po shAkya bzang po'i zhus ngor chos
sde lho byang rags bsdus bcas la gsung ngag rin po che'i gzhung rgyas pa cha lag gtso bsdus bcas gnang/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang lho bod phan tshun mi nor gte'u 'dzin sogs
bslogs pa dang / zlos rtsa rnams gcod 'doms la phebs te nod 'jags su mdzad nas chibs 'khor/ dgung grangs zhe gsum par chos kyi rje byams pa ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas
gdan drangs nas gsung ngag slob bshad snang gsum zhib rgyas gsan/ sngags lam tshugs nye ba nas dpon slob rnams byas 'gyur du phebs te rgyud gsum gsan pa gegs med du grub/
ston dgun rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis gtsos phyogs 'dus kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen du mar chos 'khor bar med du bskor/ skyed lhas su bzhugs pa'i dpal mgon bram gzugs
kyi sku brnyan dang / gtso bo dus gsum sangs rgyas

can gyi gos thang chen mo yang bzhengs pa'i 'go btsugs/ dgung grangs zhe lnga par gos thang chen mo rab gnas bcas grub/ kyai rdor nag po lugs kyi sku gsung thugs snying po
kyai rdo rje dkyil 'khor bzhir phye ba'i dbang rgyun de nyid ngor du bar skabs chad pa 'di lo ngor mkhan po lhun grub dpal ldan pa la rgyun gso ba'i phyir gnang ba sogs gzhan
yang dbang lung gi rgyun rgya cher spel/ chos skyong skor gyi sku thang che tshad bdun bkod pa gnang ba yang grub/ de phan gyi rten gsar bzhengs rnams la mgon po la
brten pa'i rab gnas zhag bdun ma zhig gnang ba'i mtshan lam du/ yab rje rin po de nyid sku zil che zhing sku gzan ser po'i thu ba shing tog gis bskang pa zhig bsnams te/
khyed kyi rten 'di rnams la rab gnas byas pa yin nam gsungs byung bar yin lags zhus pas de legs 'dug gsungs te shing tog nas rten rnams la 'thor ba mdzad pa'i thugs snang
shin tu gsal bar byung ba ni gdan sa 'di nyid kyi phrin las rgyas pa'i rtags su mngon/ yang gong ma rnam lnga sgrol dkar nor lha sogs rtsa gsum 'ga' zhig gi zhal thang dgu
gras bzhengs te dbang khang du bzhugs su gsol/ dgung grangs zhe drug par rten bzhengs dang bka' chos

gnang bar lngar las thugs rtsol che bar mdzad/ chos gzhis mnga' 'bangs kun la'ang gdan sa 'di nyid kyis gtsug lag khang gi nyams gso'i las sne du ma byed dgos stabs smon rngod
ma gtogs khral rigs gtan med kyi bka' shog rgyal dbang mchog nas gnang ba sogs sde bstan pa bcas la rje 'di nyid lhag tu sku driin che ba lta bu byung/ dgung grangs zhe
bdun par zangs ldan mkhan pos zhus ngor chos sde lho byang gi dge 'dun mang po dang bcas la gsung ngag rin po che bka' drin gnang / bzhi thog bla brang gis rten dang brten
pa bzhengs pa'i mjug sgrig mtshams rab gnas dang / las rgyab pa bzo rigs sogs la dga' ston gnang sbyin rgyas pa bstsal/ ston ka yab rje rin po che'i sku dus kyi sngags
thang chen mo'i lugs kyi sngags thang gras mtshungs kyis dbu btsugs/ gsang ba'i mgon khang / mgon khang nub/ shab dge sdings kyi gnas bcu/ Da Di mgon khang / khru ma lha
khang / sgrol ma lha khang rnams kyi nyams gso mthil phyin mdzad/ hor zla dgu pa'i nang bsam yas chos skyong chen po nas yang bskyar rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub pa dang gtor
bzlog la 'bad pa gal che/ bstan pa dang sde'i skyid sdug de la rag las pa yod do gsungs pas/ lung bstan legs rgyu

rang mi 'dug dgongs pas spyan gzigs dang bcas bskyar zhus mdzad pas gsal dod rang ma byung yang / dgon che phra mang por mang bskol/ bka' 'gyur klog sgrog mdo sgrol tshe gzungs
'bum ther/ rnam rgyal stong mchod grangs mangs/ rje nyid kyi zor las mdzad pa'i phur bzlog dang / mgon po'i gtor zlog sgrol dkar tshe bsnyen bdun phrag gsum/ sde dmangs
la sbyin gtong grong khal thob rtsis sogs sku rim rgya cher mdzad/ 'brug thams cad mkhyen pa zhal mjal chos zhur byon par dud gsol skor sogs zab chos mang du stsal/ dgungs
grangs zhe brgyad pa/ lha khang chen mo'i rgya mthong gi zangs dra sogs la thugs stsol dang chos sbyin kyang rgya cher gnang / chos sde lho byang rnams na bar skabs
su bsnyen rdzogs ma thob pa yod rigs la 'di lo thugs rtsol gyi las gral bsgrigs par te bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ mkhan chen ngag dbang kun rgyal sku gshegs pa'i
rjes thog tu bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po byams pa don grub legs bzang nyid thub bstan lha chen gyi chos khrier mnga' gsool/ zur sbug bla mas zhus par brten bskal bzang
'ga' la chos 'khor rgya cher skor/ de ltar mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i rdo rje slob dpon rnams nas zab rgyas kyi chos tshul

gang gang gsan pa nas bzung gsan don snying por dril ba'i rgyun gyi nyams bzhes la'ang / tho rengs lhag pa'i lha'i ldang ba'i rnal 'byor gyis bzhengs nas/ zhal gyi tshe sgub
gur bdun ma nas bzung / bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang yi dam gyi bdag bskyed bcu phrag lhag pa/ lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dang / gong ma lnga bstod sogs bla ma brgyud
pa'i gsol 'debs rigs bcu gcig tsam dang / yab rje rin po che'i gsol 'debs 'jam dbyangs rigs thig ma'i sho lo ka dang po brgya tshar dang yongs rjogs char re/ sgrol ma'i
mtshan rgya/ kyai rdor bstod pa/ daNDa ka rnams dang / gtor ma brgya rtsa/ dbyug gu ma/ 'byung bzhi gtor ma/ sher snying bdud bzlog tshar gsum re/ bshags pa smon lam thugs
brel dang bstun/ phur chung gtor bsngo chos skyong rnams la gsung bskang rgyas bsdus skabs bstun/ beg tse lcam dral gyi bskang gso dang / dgongs lo lam dus 'bring po/ zhal
gyi tshe sgrub/ rdo rje'i brag rdzong ma/ 'jigs byed/ lam zab nang ma/ gshin rje tshe bdag gi bzlog pa rnams dang / gzhan yang skabs gseng rnams su mchog mthun gyi yi
dam du ma'i bskyed rdzogs ljags bzlas bar med du gnang / don du rigs kun bdag po'i ye shes brnyes pa'i tshur mthong gis snang ngor ma

ltos kyang / gdul bya rnams yid drangs pa'i phyir nges gsang rgyud sde'i lam rtags dang mthun pa'i mngon mkhyen dang grub pa'i mtshan ma brnyes pa'i tshul yang gong du 'ga'
zhig bstan pa ltar dang gzhan yang gong dkar du nang pa dpal gling pa'i zhal ngo ma chen gyis 'bul chen phul te bdag rgas pas da ni mi 'jal zhes smre sngags bton pas/ skyon
med lo bzhi nas 'phrad 'ong gsungs pa de kho na ltar byang thang bkra shis gling du mjal ba dang yar 'brog sna skar ba'i rgad po zhig nad drag po'i 'chi bar thug pa'i
tshe 'bul ba dang bcas bdag 'chi bar 'dug pas thugs rjes 'dzin dgos zhus pas/ dogs sel gyi rim gro 'di rnams kyis dang mi yul spang mi dgos phebs pa ltar nad las grol bas
bka' shogs de gzhan la bstan nas bla ma zer na sa skya pa yin mod/ nga rang 'chi thag chod pa la mngon mkhyen 'di 'dra zer ba byung ba dang / phyug po stod lung pa'i rgad
po long ba zhig la mig thur 'byed sogs ma byed par gzhog dang rang bye 'ong gsungs par/ kho g.yol chung nas mig ya gcig gtan long du song zhing / ya gcig rang phye byung
ba dang tshong dpon bsod nams mgon po dar mdor shi nas bang phyin ma slebs skabs tshong dpon de rta dkar po zhig la zhon zhu lung du song ba mnal lam du

gzigs pas bsod mgon gyi skye ba zhu lung du yong bar gsungs pa phyis su yin nges rtags mtshan gsal ba bcas byung ba sogs dang / chos skyong bran du khol bas 'gal byed tshar
gcod rjes 'dzin lhan cig mdzad pa'i tshul yang / gdong na smon 'gro ba dang mchod gzhis sa khad 'brel nyi'i stabs rtsi med kyi spyod ngan byung bar/ gdan sa nas btso nyis
sbrel thon pa kho pa'i gur gla tshal gyi gseb na yod pa'i steng du babs pa dang / gdong sna'i gling gsebs tu mi rkang gi sgra lan mang thos pa sogs nas mi ring ba gtan
brlag tu song ba dang / phu dmar phyogs su bstan dgra zhig gi khang thog tu mtshan mo bong bus bro 'khrab pa mthong ba'i phyi nyin der gtor skam kha yar byung bas bred nas
bshags pa rgya cher phul ba dang / yang log lta can zhig gis zhabs 'dren che tsam zhus par ma 'gyang par gdan sa'i nang gso'i rtsa khang gi sbug na dgra bo de mig gnyis
phyir thon lus thams cad sbos nas e khyer khyer 'dug pas khams pa a khu bla ma zer ba des mthong 'phral kun la bshad pa bzhin mi ring bar dgra bo yang de kho na ltar gyur
nas shi ba dang / phu ri'i 'brog par skye bo mi srun pa zhig gis 'tshe bar byung bar gdan sa'i thad nas btso mang po rgyugs te kho'i sbra thad du babs cing / nye sar pha
bong chen po zhig

la btso babs pa kun gyis mthong bas pha bong de tshal par gas shing gnod byed de la'ang mngon spyod kyi rtags mtshan 'gyang med du byung ba sogs brjod kyis mi langs pa dang
/ gzhan yang rje 'di nyid kyis dag pa ye shes kyi sku 'khon gyi gdung du phebs par yang dpal mgon zhal gyis bskul ba yin tshul yab rje nyid kyi gsungs pa dang/ sku tshe
'dir yang shin tu 'khor nyams che zhing / skyed lhas mgon khang du sku mtshams bdun phrag dang bcas dam tshig bskang gso dang gtor bzlog gnang skabs gzigs snang khyad par
can byung zhing / gsung las kyang da lan dam tshig bskang gso btang ba 'dir dpal mgon thugs mnyes mdog kha mo byung song ba/ thugs rab tu mnyes na 'phral du zhal bzhi pa'i
sku zhig 'bul mi 'ong / 'bring tsam mnyes na bram gzugs kyi sku zhig 'bul mi 'ong / ma mnyes na gang yang mi 'ong gsungs nas/ mang mkhar chab tshan la phebs skabs mus
pa bkra shis lhun grub kyis zhal gyi bris sku'i gtsos 'bul dngos rgya cher phul ba sogs mtha' yas shing / zhal gzigs sogs du ma 'ong ba'i gsung zur thol byung du thon pa'ang
slar gzhan du zhal bsgyur ba sogs sbas tshul kho na gnang bstan pa rin po che thugs dgongs su bcangs nas bstan rgyun 'thud phyir 'chad

pa'i rim pa'ang gsung ngag rin po che tshar bdun gyis gtsos pa'i bstan srid kyi khur bzhes phyin gyis gnas skabs phal cher chos kyi sbyin pas 'da' bar mdzad pa'i rnam grangs
so sor brjod du ma langs na'ang zab rgyas kyi bdud rtsi de dag gsol ba'i zhal slob 'chad nyan nus pa rags rim ni gtso bor 'dzam gling bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rigs sras 'jam
pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rtse gdong dbon rin po che bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po/ bdag chen ngag dbang nor bu
bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po/ rgyan mchog ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan te gdan sa gong 'og gi gdung brgyud rin po che zhal ngo bzhi/ lung rtogs rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag byams
pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyal rtse bdag po ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bzang ldan mkhan po bsod nams grags pa/ ngor
mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ grangs chen mkhan po ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas/ bsgyi chu'i mkhan po ngag dbang dpal bzang po ste bla slob zung 'jug tu gnang ba bdun/
yar lung dbon riin po che bsod nams mchog ldan/ ngag dbang blo gsal mchog ldan gnyis/ ngor mkhan chen bsod nams rgya

mtsho sogs de skabs kyi bla ma thams cad dang / thub bstan rnam rgyal/ mkhan po kun dga' bsod nams/ dpal 'byor rnam rgyal/ bzang po rgyal mtshan/ gser mdog can mkhan po rgyal
ba lhun grub/ btson 'grus phun tshogs/ shAkya phun tshogs sogs dang / thub bstan yangs can mkhan po ngag dbang bkra shis sogs dang / bya gshongs mkhan po mang thos dge
byed sogs gsum dang / ya ga chos sding mkhan po sogs ngam ring grwa tshang so so'i bla ma/ gzhis dgon mkhan po bkra shis lhun grub sogs dang / lu phu dang bsgyi chu'i mkhan
po byams pa dge ba'i dbang po/ gling kha bde ba can zur 'chad pa ngag dbang chos 'phel/ bzang ldan mkhan po rje drung dpal brtse ba sogs dang / ngam ring mkhan chen klu
grub dar rgyas/ nub dgon chen bla ma kun dga' legs pa/ spe shing dbon po kun dga' 'phrin las rgya mtsho sogs dang / gdan sa 'di nyid kyi lha khang mkhan chen byams pa
bsam gtan rgya mtsho/ byams pa bsod nams bkra shis/ byams pa dag dbang kun rgyal/ byams pa don grub legs bzang sogs dang / gzhan yang zha lu mkhan po/ gur pa bla ma/ chos
'khor lhun po/ kha ba lhas/ byang chub gling / brtse chen brag dmar rnams kyi bla ma dang / gong dkar rdo rje

gdan gyi zur 'chad pa rin chen rgya mtsho sogs de skabs kyi grwa tshang so so'i bla ma/ gzhad ri skyed tshal/ ra ba smad/ dgas po grwa tshang rnams kyi bla ma bsam yas rab
byung mkhan po snga phyi rnams dang / chos rje bco brgyad pa byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ gsang phu gling stod zhabs drung / rtse thang lnga mchod mkhan po/ gdungs phud
chos 'khor bla ma/ 'brug thams cad mkhyen pa/ gter bdag gling pa chen po/ rdo rje brag rig 'dzin chen po/ 'bro'i sngags 'chang rig 'dzin dbang rgyal sogs grub pa'i gong
'phang brnyes pa du ma dang / rtse chen mi dbang rnam rgyal rdo rje/ 'dar sde pa tshe'i dbang po/ gling sde pa bsod nams lhun grub/ sna skar rtse'i sde pa/ sde dge dbon po
sangs rgyas bstan pa/ kun dga' rab brtan/ tshe dbang rdo rje sogs dang / sa skar drung pa/ 'dam thog bla ma/ rgya skabs nor bu gling bla ma/ ri khud dgon bla ma/ a li chos
rje sogs che long tsam zhig smos pa ste/ gzhan du gsung gi bdud rtsi'i ngom pa'i bla chen dpon chen kho na'ang bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ /rtsom pa'i bstan bcos kyang rje
btsun gong ma rnams kyi gsung du ma 'thus pa mi 'dug gsung nas de dag gi bstan rgyun spel ba gtso bor mdzad pa las spros pa cher mi gnang yang / kun

rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang chog lho sgo bar do'i chos bshad bcas/ tshar lugs rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dkyil chog yang dag mar me dgu pa'i mtho yig kyai rdor bka' babs
bzhi'i dbang chog mdos chung skyid sbug pa'i rnal 'byor ma'i bsgom bzlas tshogs 'khor dang bcas pa'i dris lan sogs chos tshan bcu bzhi tsam gnang/ de ltar sku tshe'i ring
du bstan 'gro'i phan bde sgo du ma nas spel ba'i rgyal sras mchog gi rnam par thar pa kho nas dus 'da' bzhin pa nas dgung grangs zhe brgyad pa de nyid du lho bod kyi
'ching gi dus mtshams rdzogs pas thugs brtse bas kun nas bslangs te phebs bzhed kyi skabs shig mnal lam du/ dpal mgon zhal gyi sprul pa yin rgyu'i zhabs 'bring ba'i grwa
pa gcig gi rnam pas/ gnas khams gsum 'khor ba'i mun dkyil du/ /lus dal 'byor bco brgyad tshang ba 'di/ /las ma 'bad 'grub pa ngo mtshar che/ /'di yun ring mi sdod mi rtag
pa/ /zhes pa zhig gsan nas mnal sad pa na mi rtag pa bskul ba'i tshig de legs rgyu rang med dam dgongs pa byung / de nas chibs bsgyur nye ba na/ gdan sa'i bla ma slob dpon
las tshan gra rigs bsam gnas rags bsdus bcas la

zhal bkod du/ lha khang chen mo'i zangs dra 'gel rtsis sogs byed dgos med/ gzhan zangs skud sogs gang 'thon gyis/ chos sde lho byang bca' yig dang mthun pa'i sgrigs bkod sogs
g.yel med 'bad pa thon zhes dang / lhag tu rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs la sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa 'dzin skyong spel ba'i bka' stsal dang / gzhis byes kyi
rkyen bzlog la sku mtshams bcad rgya sogs 'di bzhin dang / phur pa sgrub mchod kyang bla brang bzhi thog tu dgos tshul sogs zhib 'them gnang nas zla ba drug pa'i tshes
lnga la chibs bteg ste rim gyis phag rir phebs/ zla ba bdun pa tshes nas snyan mi gsang ba dang sku khams pa bsnyun dmigs rang med pa'i sku ngal ba'i rnam pa lta bu'i cung
zad mi dngas pa zhig byung mur zla ba brgyad pa shar ba dang / sku 'khor rnams kyis rje nyid kyi sku khams 'di bskor gdan sa na spyir yang khri rin po cher snyan 'bul zhu
dgos 'dug pa dang / sku rim sogs kyi'ang khyad 'dug tshul zhus pas dgongs khrol ma gnang yang / lho khog gi dgon sde bcu gcig tsam la mang skol zhig gnang / zla ba de'i
tshes bcu skor nas chab chu'i rnam pa lta bus zhabs mgo phran tsam sbos pa sogs byung bar 'tsho byed rnams nas 'phrod

bsten sogs phul yang dngas skyed rang med pa nas/ bcu gsum nyin chings pa rnams bka' bgros zhal 'dzom zhig gnang / bcu bdun la 'brug pa sku tshab dang zhal 'dzom gnang rgyu'i
tho rengs khrag rlung gi snyun gzhi lta bu zhig gis sku khams ma bde bas lho pa dang mjal 'dzom ma bde bar/ mdzod pa sku tshab tu gnang / nyin phyed bskor nas sku khams
dngas skyed che bar byung bas 'tsho byed rnams kyis kyang sems can gyi skal ba zad pa 'dra yod na ma gtogs da lan skyon rang yong mdog ma kha zer ba sogs byung / de skabs
rje nyid nas bka' ma grol yang zhabs rim pa rnams kyis gdan sar gnas tshul dang sku rim sogs gnang dgos zhu 'phrin brdzangs pa'i bang phyin yang lam nas na te dus stong
ma khel ba dang / gzhan yang snga gong rnams nas zhing khams gzhan du gdul bya'i skal bar dgongs pa'i gsung rigs du ma byung ba dang nye skor du phyi nang 'byung ba'i rten
'brel legs rgyu med pa'i nyi zla'i mdangs mi gsal ba dang / sa chen po g.yo ba dang / gangs ri rtags can gi ngos nas gzhom pa dang / gdan sa'i shar ngos bra chung gi
bye ma rtags can nyil ba dang / grum chu mdog 'gyur ba sogs ltas lod sna tshogs dang / thag nye nas bzhugs sgar gyi thad kar 'ja' sna tshogs shar ba dang / thag

ring nas gzims gur gyi thog tu 'ja' sna tshogs zug pa dang / shing bzo ba rdo rje zer ba sgar thog nas gdan sar log grabs la/ rje nyid nas re zhig sdod dgos gsungs pa la slar
gdung sgrom byed dgos kyi dgongs gzhi sogs dang / rje nyid kyang thugs zhi ba chen po'i ngang nas thugs dam g.yel med du bzhugs pa'i skabs 'gar snga sor yab rje dam pa/
rje btsun drung / zhabs drung ngag dbang rnam rgyal rnams kyi sku gdung la zhabs tog 'di bzhin bsgrubs pa yin lugs kyi 'phros kun la go rgyur gnang ba dang / nyin gcig
nye bskor na bya rog gnyis 'bros 'ded byed pa gzigs pas nga nad 'di las grol yang sgar 'di nas mi gcig 'chi bar 'dug gsungs par/ zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis rje nyid kyi sku
la nyes skyon ma byung na su shi na'ang chog legs zhus pas/ lho bod gnyis kyi mtshams su dpung shom ma dgos tsam gyis chings 'dum 'di byung na de kas yong gsungs/ yang
lan gcig da lan phan yon chen po yong ba 'dug gzhan gyis don du srog gtong ba zhes pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnam thar ltar da lan lho bod sems can bde thabs kyi ched du
nged rang gis lus sems kyi dka' ba 'di bzhin spyad pa yin gsungs/ tshes bcu dgu la zhabs 'bring sku 'khor ban gtsang

ba rnams kyis zhabs pad brtan dgos kyi gsol ba nan tan btab/ nyer gcig nyin de ring tshes grangs gang yin gsungs par khong tshos de bzhin zhus pas bzhes gong mo bde sing nge
'gro gsung / de phral gzim gur gyi thod la gzigs nas maNDal 'bul ba dang / phyag thal mo sbyar nas bzhugs par gang gdug zhus pas/ rje btsun gong ma lnga byon byung gsungs/
gzhan yang sngags 'chang chen po yab sras dang / yab rje chos kyi rgyal po sogs zhal gzigs pa'i gsung byon/ nyer gsum gyi nyin phyag mdzod la da lan nged la mi 'ong re
mi 'dug pas gang sar 'di bzhin dgos kyi ljags bkod dang / nged kyi sngags thang gi mjug lus 'di bzhin sgril cig sogs zhal bkod lhug par gnang / 'brub pa'i sku tshab la
nged chings khag rnams rang don sger pa gang yang med kyang sems can spyi'i bde thabs la bsam nas dka' ba dang len 'di bzhin byas pa yin rung nged kyi khams kyis ma lcogs
yang / 'phen skor 'di don smin pa rang zhig byed dgos kyi bka' shog byin rten sogs bstsal/ de nas thugs dam nyams bzhes kyi ngang las oM gsum ma'i gsung bzlas gzim gur gyi
phyi nas dir dir tshor ba rang gnang mur/ zhabs 'bring pa rnams la dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed phur pa bde kyai

gsang gsum chos skyong gur zhal sogs 'di bzhin byon byung gsungs/ nyer bzhi'i nyin nyi ma ma zhud tsam la phyag mdzod gsol gzim gsum la/ da khyed gsum 'dod pa gcig tu byas
pa'i phyag mdzod kyi ngag bzhin hur thag dgos lugs sogs lugs gnyis kyi bslab bya ma 'ong lung bstan ci mang zhig stsal rjes/ 'phel gdung dang gong ma'i dam rdzas gdung rus
