khyung po'i thugs las byon pa'i ring bsrel sogs sbyar ba bzhes phral/ zhing 'di'i mdzad pa re zhig rdzogs nas zhing khams gzhan du 'phrin las kyis 'jug pa yangs par dgongs
te rgyud sde rin po che nas gsungs pa'i 'da' ka ma'i rnal 'byor gsal 'debs dang bcas gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdu bar mdzad nas nyer lnga phyi ma'i nyi ma phyed yol
bar du gsal stong zung 'jug spros bral phyag rgya chen po'i dgongs par mnyam par bzhag nas de mtshams dbu gtsug nas dbu thod gtsug tor gyi tshul du thag sgra shin tu che
ba dang bcas 'phags te byang sems kyi zil pa nyil le ba dang bcas 'od gsal las bzhengs nas dpal bo rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs kyis mkha' spyod dag pa'i zhing du spyan drangs
par gyur to/ / de tshe rjes 'jug thams cad ci bya gtol med du lus pa'i

ngang nas kun gyi rje nyid kyi zhal chems bzhin ban tshang ba rnams kyis bla ma mchod chog dang bcas pas gdung mchod rgya cher zhus/ gdan sar gnas tshul phral 'bul dang / gdung
sgrom gyi gra bsgrigs sogs bsgrubs/ de tshe nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa las me tog gi char dang / rol mo'i sgra sogs rnal 'byor mchog gi lam rtags rmad du byung bar gyur/
de nas sku gdung rin chen mchod pa'i yo byad sna tshogs dang bcas gdung sgrom du stsal te/ gdan dren nyin phag ri nas gdan sa'i bar du 'ja' dkar po zhig drang thal du zug
pa dang lu ma khar phebs pa'i skabs gdung sgrom gang du 'dren pa'i phyogs su 'ja' kha dog sna tshogs lhan cig 'gro bar byu nga bzhin pa'i mu nas/ zla ba dgu pa'i tshes
gcig la sku gdung rin po che gdan sar phebs/ gdan sar gnas tshul nyer brgyad la 'byor 'phral chos sde khag gsum la mang ja 'bras 'jam 'gyed bcas kyi thog mchod 'bul smon
lam rgya chen dang / nyer dgu nas bzung lha khang mkhan rin po ches gtsos pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa bcu phrag bzhi lhag gis dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi sgrub mchod dang / dgung
tshigs dang por rigs sras khri rin po che nyid kyi gzim chung sger nas lha khang chen mor 'bras 'jam mang ja sbyor sbrel thog brgya

mchod sogs mchod tshogs bla ma slob dpon so sor bsngo rten tshan grangs spyi 'gyed sogs rgya chen dang / sku gdung rin po cher chos rje ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas kyis rgyud
sde dri ma med pa nas gsung pa'i sku spur gyi zhabs tog phyag len mdzad de/ zla ngo gsum gyi ring mchod pa'i zhing du bzhugs su gsol ba'i sku mdun du chos rje de nyid
kyi mchod 'bul rgyun bzhugs pa mdzad/ dgung tshigs bzhi pa'i thog phyag mdzod/ gsol gzims/ gnyer mchod dpon sogs zhabs gras rnams kyi dgongs rdzogs zhal 'debs mang 'gyed
sogs bsgrub/ dgung tshig lnga par 'jam mgon khri rin po che nas yab rje'i sku bstod gsol 'debs tshogs mjug mang ja 'phar ma sogs dgung zhag gi ring phal cher gzhi tshogs
kyis mchod 'bul la mang 'gyed rgyun chags lta bur mdzad pa sogs mtha' yas/ gzhung sa chen po nas gdung mchod 'bul bar dngos po gtos che ba brgyad tshan drug/gzhan yang
rtse gdong / bkra shis lhun po/ zangs ri sde srid/ ngor e waM sogs phyogs kyi lha sde mi sde che phra du ma dang / rang zhabs kyi ser skya mtha' dag gis kyang 'byor bstun
gyis dngos po dpag tu med pa phul/ rgyal dbang rin po che'i sku zhabs su

mchod bsngo rten dang / gzhan yang ngor e waM/ thub bstan gong 'og gser mdog can/ ngam ring/ zangs ldan/ rtse gdong / bkra shis lhun po/ zha lu/ se ra/ 'bras spungs/ dge ldan/
rnam rgyal grwa tshang / nA lendra/ bsam yas sogs dgon sde ris med sum brgyar nye bar mang 'gyed mchod bsngo rten tshan grangs rgya che ba dang / dgongs rdzogs dngos
gzhi hor zla dgu pa'i nyer gnyis nyin gdan sa'i chos sde lho byang gis gtsos/ chos 'khor lhun po/ gdong dga'/ 'dar grang mo che/ thub bstan dge 'phel/ bsam 'grub dgon gsar/
bya gshongs sogs nye bskor dgon sde rnams kyi bla ma slob dpon grwa btsun pho mo stong phrag gsum lhag pas nyin gsum bar lha khang chen mor mchod 'bul bsam gyis mi khyab
pa phul ba'i mang tshogs la nyin re bzhin 'bras 'jam dang mang ja bzang ja sbyor bzhi re/ nyin dang por 'gyed ya ju dngul phor re/ nyin gnyis par chu thog dngul phor re/
nyin gsum par grwa pa drug re dang / btsun ma bcu gnyis re la gser zho re/ bla ma slob dpon so sor tshan grangs dgu tshan nas bdun tshan gyi bar skabs sbyar dang / dgongs
rdzogs thang ston nyer lnga'i nyin gdan sa 'di nyid kyis gtsug lag khang rnams su skar me snyan shal sogs mchod sprin

tshad las 'das pa phul/ bla ma las tshan zur 'bul 'os pa rnams la tshan grangs stobs chen/ gzhis byes kyi 'gyes skal blang mi ser skya khri phrag phyed gnyis longs par mang
ja bzang ja sbyor bzhi re/ 'gyed chos sde lho byang dang lto zan rnams la nas dkar legs pa khal re/ dge 'dun gzhan rnams la ya ju dngul phor re/ skya 'gyed la dkyus ja dngul
phor re sogs mchod sbyin rgya chen stsal ba'i dge rtsa yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs pa'i mchod bsngo 'jam dbyangs khri rin po che nyid
chos khri chen mo'i steng du phebs nas gnang / de bzhin du mus gling kha la'ang dge 'dun brgya lhag gis zhag nyer lnga'i ring dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub mchod dang / mus
nang gi dgon sde so so'i 'dus tshogs stong phrag brgal bar mang 'gyed spom mtho ba dang / ser skya bgrang bar dka' bar sbyin gtong rgya cher stsal/ dus dran gyi mchod
pa yang gdan sa rang du nyer bzhi byung res kyi brtag gnyis rgyud 'don/ nyer lngar rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub mchod/ tshogs chen dus ja/ zla ba brgyad pa'i bcu gnyis nas
nyer drug bar gsang 'dus sgrub mchod chen mo sogs dang / phyogs kyi dgon sde 'gar yang bstan pa nam gnas kyi bar mchod rgyun btsugs tshul yi ges

'jigs pas 'dir ma bkod kyang rnam thar chen mo dang / gdan sa deb chen las shes par bya'o/ /zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer gcig la chos kyi rje ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas kyis
rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgo nas sku gdung rin po che mchod sprin rgya chen dang bcas zhugs mchod phul skabs 'ja' 'ood kyi gur dang / me tog char/ lha rdzas kyi
spos dri zhim po sogs 'jig rten thams cad ngo mtshar gyis khyab/ bdun phrag gcig gi bar du mchod 'bul gsol 'debs zhus te de mtshams gdung khang zhal phye bar phal cher
gdung log tu gyur cing / sku'i rje ngar gyi rus pa gcig la rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sku brnyan shin tu gsal bar byon pa sogs rang byon dang ring bsrel gyi rigs ma gtogs gdung
rus thams cad 'dul sbyangs kyis 'jam mgon khri chen nyid nas bla ma sangs rgyas rgyud sde gong 'og gi yi dam chos skyong sogs kyi sku brnyan dang mchod rten sAtstsha bdun
khri sum stong drug brgya don bdun la gser zho sum cu so brgyad ljib gsol mdzad/ phyi nang gi rten yang rje de nyid kyi sku tshab gser zangs kyi 'dra sku sku tshad can
dang / gzim mal sman sku/ bu ston gyi thig 'gros ltar gyi rnam rgyal mchod rten thog tshad phyed gsum lhag pa bang rim man dang bre rgyan dang

gdugs 'degs thugs rje mdo gzungs yan chad rnams gser zangs/ bum sdir dang bre dngul ljang brdung / chos 'khor bcu gsum pho 'khor mo 'khor gser zangs spel ma la rin chen khyad
nor bgrang bar dka' ba'i phra rgyan sogs bzo bkod 'gran zla med pa dang / rten rnams kyis bzo phud du rje nyid kyi sku 'dra pad sbrags khru gang bcas sku 'dra dang mchod
rten de dag gi rgyu chas rags pa la zangs khal lnga bcu nga bzhi dang / gser 'gur zho bdun brgya dang bcu/ dngul srang bdun brgya sum cu sogs song / bde gshegs mchod rten
brgyad kyi bum ldir dngul/ gzhan rnams gser zangs las grub pa khru do'i tshad gras mnyam/ phyi rten rnam rgyal mchod rten mthong grol chen mor grags pa rnams kyi nang
rten la sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyi ring bsrel/ gong du smos pa'i gdung tshwa de dag dang rje de nyid kyi sku bal rigs sogs byin rten dang gzungs
bzhugs dpag tu med pas phyur bur gtams/ gzhan yang 'jigs byed dang phur pa'i bla brgyud kyi sman sku mi tshad bdun bcu don drug rje de nyid kyis dgongs pa'i lhag ma sngags
thang chen mo nyer lnga/ gos bzang sgrigs kyi lha khang chen mo'i khyams stod dbus kyi gdung khebs su dus gsum sangs rgyas

balhung bshags sangs rgyas so lngas bskor ba/ slob dpon rin po che la gu ru mtshan brgyad kyis bskor ba sogs bris thang mang po la zhal khebs gong bshams 'ja' ris tog la sogs
pa khyad du 'phags pa bsgrubs pa'i phyi nang gi rten bris 'bur rigs grub rim nas 'jam mgon khri rin po che nyid dang chos kyi rje ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas dpon slob
sbrel mas rab gnas yang yang gnang/ lo ngo gsum gyi nang dgongs rdzogs su dmigs pa'i rten bzhengs thams cad grub mtshams me yos hor zla gsum pa'i dus tshes dge bar 'jam
mgon khri rin po che nyid rig pa 'dzin pa'i 'khor tshogs sum cu skor dang bcas pas dpal kyai rdo rje la rten pa'i rab tu gnas pa smin rgyas kyis byin rlabs kyi gzi byin
'bar bar bsgrubs nas sa gsum skye dgu'i bsod nams kyi rten du bzhugs so/ /ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ de ltar mkhas dang grub pa'i rtse mor byon pa de nyid kyi rigs sras
'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis

grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan gyi gling bu srid na snyan pa 'di nyid ni rgyu mtshan gzhan dag gi sgo nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga'
rin chen nyid kyi sprul par grags che zhing / gzhan du mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa'i sprul pa'i skur yang rtags mtshan du ma'i sgo nas
gsal te/ de dag gi sprul gzhi sku phreng sogs ni gzhan du gsal ba bzhin la/ 'phags chen dam pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' gcig tu ma nges pas thugs rgyud gcig pagcig ba sogs
su mi 'gal yang / 'dir khyad par du bod kyi lha btsan po khri srong lde btsan gyi sku ring la/ phal cher rgya gar gyi paNDi ta lha dbang byang chub dang / dA na shI la
sogs dang paN lo mdzad nas dam pa'i chos dpag tu med pa bsgrur ba'i 'jig rten gyi mig gcig tu zhang gi lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde zhes pa de nyid dag pa'i skye ba du ma
brgyud pa'i tha ma rgyal ba gzhan gyis spangs pa'i rtsod dus gdul dka'i gangs can 'gro la ched du gzigs pa'i rgyal sras mchog gi snying stobs brling ba rje 'di nyid yin
pa ni/ rtsod bral dus bab kyi gter chen lo chen bai ro'i rnam sprul rig 'dzin gter bdag gling pa chen po 'gyur med rdo rje'i sha 'ug gi gter byon zab lam thugs rje chen
po bde gshegs kun

'dus kyi lung byang du/ ye shes sde sprul mchog gi snying stobs canaH 'khon gyi rigs las mang ga'i ming can 'byung : zhes 'khrul med lung gi yi ge dus gsum sgrib thogs bral
ba'i smyug gus bris pa phyogs kyi rtsigs logs su gsal bar shar ba 'di nyid ni yab rje dam pa ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug de nyid dgung grangs bco brgyad du phebs tshe/
rgyal yum dam pa bla brang shar pa'i lcam gcig pad dkar bu khrid ces bya ba'i lhums su zhugs pa nas bzung yum nyid la byams dang snying rje rang shugs su 'khrungs pa
dang / dbul phongs la rjes su brtse ba'i sbyin pa lhug gtong sogs rnam dkar la thugs spro zhing mnal ltas su'ang lus las 'od kha dog lnga 'phros pa'i dkar po de cher 'phel
nas 'jig rten thams cad khyabs snyam byed pa dang / de skabs dngos su'ang nyin bzhin gsol tshigs grol mtshams sbrang bu yid du 'ong ba zhig gis sku lus thams cad nyug bstar
chags su byung ba/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs la yum rang gis rgyu mtshan zhu bar mdzad pa'i tshe/ byang chub sems pa'i sprul pa khyad par can zhig lhums su zhugs par lha
rnams kyis khrus gsol ba'i rtags su 'dug gsungs pa sogs phyi nang gi ngo mtshar ba'i dge ltas rgyun mi chad pa nas me spre sa ga zla ba'i dus tshes dge bar

rgyal yum dam pa'i sku la nyam nga med par bltams shing / de 'phral nas zhal khyim dngas ba sogs 'jig rten phal pa las 'das pa'i snang tshul dang / rim gyis sku skyed bsring
ba'i gzhon nu nyid nas kyang yab yum la gus shing ngang tshul bzang ba dang / sku rtsed phal cher yang chos 'chad pa dang / dbang bskur ba sogs rnam dkar gyi bag chag sad
pa kho na las tha mal byis pa'i ngang tshul gtan nas mi mnga'/ rim gyis 'dri klog sogs phul bas kyang tshegs med du mkhyen/ lan gcig yum sras 'khor bcas lha khang chen
mo'i yang steng sngags 'chang chen pos bzhengs bar mdzad pa'i lam 'bras bla ma lha khang gi 'og gi mgon khang du phebs skabs mgon khang 'dir sku 'di ga yin nam gsungs/ yum
gyis 'di las mi gda' zhus pas/ da dung mgon po lcam dral gyi sku zhig yod pa 'dir mi 'dug gsungs pa dang / sku 'khor zhig gis Da Di chos rdzong na mgon po lcam dral gyi
sku brnyan zhig yod pa 'di nas gdan drangs pa yin 'dug pa de e yin lags zhus pas/ de ga yin gsungs/ rje 'di nyid sku 'khrungs pa nas bzung 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kun dga'
bsod nams nyid nas khrus gsol tshe dbang sogs phal cher dang / yab chos yang phur/ gsung ngag rin

po cha lag bcas/ chos srung skor sogs mtha' yas pa zhig bstsal/ 'di skabs dgung grangs drug bdun tsam gyi skabs yin kyang chos bka' gsan pa la thugs dgyes nyams ngo mtshar
bar bzhugs/ rdo rje phur pa'i chog bsgrigs tshang ma thugs 'dzin dang / phyag len dbyangs rol gar 'chams sogs kyang tshegs med du mkhyen/ dgungs grangs brgyad par pu tra
dmar nag gi zhal 'bag phyag bzo mdzad pa da lta e wam dang dbang khang phur bzhugs pa 'di yin/ lo der yab rje rin po che dang lhan cig phur sgrub tu phebs pa gnang dang de
loo nas bzung dgung grangs bcu gnyis bar/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyi drung nas yab sras lhan cig pas dbang khrid che rim drug cu skoor tsam gsan/ dgung grangs bcu
gsum pa sa spre gnam lo gsar tshes la 'jam dbyangs gdung brgyud rim phebs kyiis dam pa chos kyi khri chen por gtsug lag gnyis kyi phrin las la dbang sgyur bar mnga' gsol
ba'i sgo dod de/ sngar rgyun bzhin phyogs mthar de tshul dril bsgrags/ dus mdos chen mo yang rgyal zla'i gzhug tu bsring ste gzab spros mdzad/ cho 'phrul gyi tshes gcig
nyin phyogs

'dus che gnyen du ma dang bcas par lo gsar gyi dga' ston rgya cher bstsal/ khri 'don dngos gzhi zla ba de ga'i tshes lnga'i snga dro chos dung chen mo lan bcu gsum bar du bskul
ba'i gzhis byes kyi dge 'dun sindhu ra'i chu gter 'khyil pa lta bu bzhugs khri chen mo'i mdun logs su 'khod pa'i mthar dad ldan gyi skye bo du ma'i khrom tshogs kyis
bskor ba'i dbus su rje 'di nyid ngo mtshar ba'i bkod pa mdzes shing brjid dang ldan pas rdo rje'i zhabs stegs ga la bar zhabs kyi pad mo mngon par bkod nas nyin gsum la
rgyal sras mchog gi lam bzang thub pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba'i bstan bcos sbyor dngos rjes tshang dag gsal snyan pa'i gsung gis skye dgu'i yid dbang 'phrog cing thar
pa'i sa bon rgyud la smin nus can stsal ba'i skabs gseng rnams su gtso bor gong sa rin po che phyag na pad mo lnga pa chen po'i sku zhabs nas dar dkar yug gsum/ zhal dkar
dngul stegs/ dngul gyi bzed zhal/ dngul gyi maNDal/ dngul mdong / gos yug du ma sogs gtos che bas drang pa/ dbyings zhabs dang sog po'i rgyal po gnyis sogs lha sde mi sde
mchog dman kun nas khri 'bul dpag tu med pa byung ba nyin gsum gyi khongs der 'bul thub pa byas pa'i nyin phyi mar yab rje rin po che yang lhan cig bzhugs

khrir phebs nas de skabs kyi lhag bsam dag pa'i 'brel thogs rnams kyi dge rtsa bstan 'gro spyi'i phan bde'i dpal du gsung bsngo rin po ches rgyas 'debs dang / khri 'bul gyi
dngos po phal cher mchod sbyin du bstsal/ dgung lo bco lnga tshun la gdan sa chen po'i sgrub mchod rgyud 'don dus rim bskang zlog rigs nyi shu skor thugs 'dzin phyag len
bcas byang chub par mdzad/ bcu drug par rdo rje gzhon nu'i gsung bsnyen smin rgyas gnang / 'di skabs cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes gcig la rgyal yum dam pa de nyid sku gshegs
par thugs ngal gyi rnam pa dpag tu med pa gnang zhing rgyal yum nyid kyi dgongs pa dag pa'i zhing du rdzogs pa'i gsung smon rtse gcig pa dang / bsags sbyang mchod sbyin
sger pa rgya cher mdzad/ dgung grangs bcu bdun par mgon khang rnams su phrin bcol rgyas pa dang bcas kyai rdo rje'i bzhi bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i khongs su thun mong dang thun
mong ma yin pa'i zab lam du ma'i sgo nas lus sbyong 'khrul 'khor sogs kyang smin par gnang ba'i ngang nas kha skong sbyin sreg bcas gnang tshe rim pa gnyis kyi lam la
goms pa mthar son rtags tha mal gyi snang grags rig gsum lha

sngags ye shes kyi rol pa'i ting 'dzin la 'byams pa byung / dgung grangs bcu dgu par yab rje dam pa'i dgongs bzhed ltar rgyal dbang rin po che mjal zhu sogs dbus phebs kyi
sgo shar bas yab sras lhan cig chibs bsgyur gnang ba'i lam bar gyi 'gro ba rnams phan bde'i dpal la 'god bzhin par/ gzhung sa nas phebs bsu bkur gzos bcas lha sar phebs/

phul du phyin pa gnang / lha sa dang po ta la'i phyi nang gi rten rnams zhib mjal mchod 'bul smon lam bcas mdzad nas gzhung zhabs phebs skyel ba dang bcas bsam yas phyogs
su chibs btegs/ sku 'bum thang nas phebs skyel ba rnams phyir slog/bsam yas su phebs nye'i tshe lha mi'i bsu ba ya mtshan dang pho brang gong du phebs/ de skabs khrom
tshogs la rje 'di nyid nas 'jam dpal nag po'i rjes gnang / gtor ma brgya rtsa dang / 'jam dpal mtshan brjod kyi ljags lung rnams bstsal/ rim gyis yar lam gsang phu ra ba
smad du phebs tshe chos skyong chen mo bse khrab can gyis rje 'di nyid la bskor ba thengs gsum mdzad

nas de ring gu ru padma dngos su mjal zhes sogs gus spro'i gsung bcas me long dang lha dar tshon tshogs zhig phul te/ me long g.ya' dag pa 'di 'gro don la sgrib g.yogs med
cing phrin las ches cher gsal ba'i brda' yin/ lha rdzas tshon tshogs ring zhing bkrag mdangs che ba 'di zhi rgyas dbang drag gi phrin las rgyun ring por gnas pa'i brda' yin
pas pad ma'i rnam sprul gyis go a byung sogs shin tu dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur mdzad/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan du rje nyid nas tshogs chen la rdo rje phur pa'i stod las byang
chub sgrub pa'i bka' dbang gnang / de skabs shig tu gong dkar ba'i grwa rigs 'ga' zhig gis mthong bar rje 'di'i phyag tu 'bru dum pa zhig bsnams 'dug pa yud tsam nas 'bru
rnams gcig tu 'jim pa bzhin brdzi bar mdzad pa phyag gnyis kyis ring por 'then nas yab rje la gzigs phul bar zhal 'dzum pa zhig mdzad pa'i mthar khri rtsa der g.yug par
mdzad song ba gong dkar grwa rigs tshos btsal yang ma rnyed zer ba'i grub pa'i mtshan ma'ang bstan/ de nas rim gyis chibs btegs te ring por ma thogs par gdan sa chen por
phebs/ mgon khang rnams su gtang rag gi gsol mchod rgya cher gnang / dgung grangs nyer gcig par bde mchog gi ljags bsnyen

zla drug smin rgyas gnang ba'i skabs gzim chung gi phyi nang nye skor bcas par lha rdzas kyi dri bsung sngar tshor ma myong bas khyab pa dang / mchod gzhi'i ting phor khar
lha'i me tog 'dab ma bzhi pa lan grangs du mar bab pa byung / thugs dam ting nge 'dzin gyi bogs kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa thon/ gzhan yang snga phyi ci rigs par 'jam dbyangs
nag po/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/ gur drag seng ge sgra/ 'byung 'dul/ sgrol dkar/ khros nag mgon po/ seng gdong ma sogs kyi ljags bsnyen rnams mthar phyin
par mdzad/ skabs 'dir dgung grangs nyer gnyis nas nyer lnga bar lo ngo bzhi'i rnam thar sa bon mi snang / dgung grangs nyer drug par rje 'di nyid dang / lcam bkra shis
dbang mo/ 'dar rje drung / 'dar sde pa/ rag rdzong bla ma/ chos grwa lho byang kyi dge 'dun sogs mang ba dang bcas pas yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs drung du gsung ngag
rin po che'i lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa slob bshad smin 'khrid cha lag rgyab brten lung gi tshogs dang bcas pa mtha' rgyas su gsan/ nyer bdun par ngor e waM chos ldan gyi
mkhan rin chen lhun grub dpal ldan pa'i drung nas 'jigs byed sa lugs sogs

dbang bka' kha shas gsan zhing phar yang ku ru kulle sogs rjes gnang dang lung du ma bstsal/ nyer dgu par 'jigs byed ljags bsnyen thun mtshams rnams su pu tra chen po'i zhal
'bag phyag bzo mdzad par yab rje rin po che nas rab gnas smin rgyas mdzad dus pu tra dngos su zim par gzigs pa de da lta dbang khang na bzhugs pa 'di yin zhing / yang yab
rje nyid kyi bkas bskul te pu tra dmar nag gnyis kyi zhal brnyan phrag bzo 'phral bsgrubs mdzad de phul ba yang mgon khang khyad 'phags su bzhugs pa 'di nyid do/ /dgung
grangs sum cu par khros nag gi sku mtshams shig gnang / de skabs seng ldeng gi DA ma ru dang / rkang gling / sgom thag sogs la thugs rtsis chen po mdzad pa zhig byung 'dug
pa sngon gyi sku 'phreng zhig gi bag chags sad tshod du 'dug 'di lo yab rje rin po che nas bka' phebs kyis lo lo bzhin bstan pa spyi rim du gtor zlog gnyis re gnang ba'i
zor las su phebs pa'i gsung bsnyen zhal gso'i skabs rnams su dngos nyams 'dres mar gaNDe las sprul gyi pho nya rnams kyi dbyibs 'dra bas gzim chung khrig mer gang ba
dang / 'ga' res yus kyi rnam pas rje nyid kyi bzhugs gdan sogs 'brad pa'i rnam 'gyur shar/

yang phur zlog gi dngos gzhi'i gtor zlog gi skabs shig tu gtso gtor la tshag sgra chen po kun gyis tshor ba zhig byung ba dang lhan cig gtor rtse sor bzhi tsam zhig gas 'dug
pa de nas ma 'gyangs par dam nyams kha shas la rtags mtshan mngon gyur byung / bsam yas su chos skyong chen po glo bur du sku phebs nas bka' shog cig phebs nang 'dus byas
thams cad mi rtag pa'i rgyur 'gro ba'i brda' tshig de e go sogs dang / zlog thabs la rdo rje phur pa drug cu sogs kyi gtor zlog tshe sgrub sogs dgos tshul 'dug pas rje
nyid nas yab rje dang nged rang su la sku dogs yod kyang da lan hur thag dgos pa 'dug gsungs te tshe sgrub sogs kyi thugs dam la g.yel med brtson pa dang / gzim chung rang
nas phyag rdzas bton pa'i yon sprad nas rdo rje 'dzin pa gzhan la yang tshe sgrub srung bzlog rgya cher bsgrub 'jug pa gnang / zla ba drug pa'i nang yab rje rin po che
lho bod kyi 'dum chings la phebs rjes/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ 'di lo blo mi bde zhing / yab rje yang sku'i rnam 'gyur sogs sngar dang mi 'dra ba zhig mdzad 'dug pa ji ltar
yin ma shes pas sku rim la 'bad dgos gsungs pa gnang / phyogs kyi 'bul sdud bla ma sogs la 'dod sbyor gyi dbang bka' sogs stsol bzhin

pa'i skabs phag ri bzhugs sgar nas bang chen slebs gdong yab rje rin po che sku khams rnyog tshul 'dug par de 'phral zhabs phyi rnams la rang gzhan phyogs mthar mang skol gtor
bzlog sogs sku rim gyi bkod pa dang / rje nyid nas kyang zhabs brtan 'bul mi 'phral rdzong mdzad rtsis kyis bzhugs gdan gos sprin dang me tog sogs kyi ri mo med pa nor
bu cha bdun dang shing 'bras sogs kyi ri mo byas par drub na rten 'brel zhig e 'grig sogs ci drag gi thugs khur dang / bka' las kyang spyi sger bstan pa rin chen dang /
sgos su sa skya'i rigs rus bdag sogs rnams nyams thag par yong nyen che gsungs pa sogs thugs las kyi ngang du yod tshe bang chen yang skyar slebs nas sku khams shin tu rnyog
tshul 'byor bar rje nyid nas da cha sku rim la 'bad kyang don chen yod mdog ma kha/ 'on kyang nga rang sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung du brtag pa zhig la 'gro gsungs
nas gsung bskang tshugs te brtag bsgril gnang tshe yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid zhing gzhan du phebs yod 'dug gsungs pa dang / bse dgon la spyan cher gyis gzigs te dus
gnas kun tu mchod cing bstod pa la khyed rnams las byas chung ba sogs thugs chad bka' bsgo mang zhig gnang /

de rjes gtam ngan skyel ba'i bang chen rting ma slebs tshe dpon slob thams cad dran med du had pa'i murathams cad kyis yab rje de nyid kyi sku drin rjes dran pa'i dgongs pa
rdzogs thabs la blo kha chig sgril gyis rig pa hur bton rje nyid nas sku gdung rin po che 'dir ma phebs bar nga rang gi gzim chung nas gser dngul ja gos dar sogs gang yod
mchod 'bul du 'gro ba gyis gsungs pa nas bzung / sku gdung phebs nas zla ba gsum gyi bar mchog gi rdo rje 'dzin pa rje drung bstan pa rab rgyas kyi gtsos pa'i dge 'dun
tshogs nas gdung mchod rgyun ma chad pa dang / dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi bdun phrag re re'i mtshams mang 'gyed rgya che ba dang / phyogs mthar yang mchod bsngo dang mang skol
dpag tu med pa bstsal/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i gzhug tu sku gdung rin po che zhugs sbyangs zhus te gdung rten dngul gdung mthong ba don ldan bzo bkod khyad 'phags thog so
gsum pas gtsos phyi nang gi rten bzhengs rgya cher bsgrubs pa rnams gong yab rje'i rnam thar du gsal ba bzhin dang / 'di la dbus gtsang phyogs khyab tu 'brum nad byung
bar rje nyid nas khyed rang rnams bag tsha mi dgos nga la 'brum pa'i gnod pas mi tshugs zhes yang bskyar phebs pa dang / srung ma bse khrab can gyis kyang

sku nyid la 'brum dogs mi yong tshul 'byor yang gzhan gyi kha na ma tho 'gog phyir re zhig bcad rgyar bzhugs pa'i khongs su rje drung bstan pa rab rgyas nas chos bka' lhag
ma rnams mthar phyin par gsan/ de skabs shig tu 'od gsal dag pa'i gzigs mor yab rje rin po che de nyid phebs nas 'byung 'gyur lung bstan 'ga' zhig gnang bar brten yab rje
nyid kyi sku bstod zhal gsungs ma rgyal ba gnyis pa sho lo ka gcig thog mar yod pa'i gsol 'debs 'di gsar rtsom gnang / zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i gzhug tsam nas sa skya'i yul
grong la'ang 'brum skyon re gnyis byung tshe sgo rum du thugs brtag gnang bar sku nyid la nyes skyon ngo ma shar yang gzhan ngor nyes med du dgongs nas re zhig byas 'gyur
du phebs/ sang nyin der mchod dpon ngag dbang chos ldan la 'phags mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i drung 'dir mchod gtor dam rdzas bkod legs shig gyis dang / nged rnams kyis mi
dbang rnam rgyal rdo rje sngon 'di phyogs su phebs ma myong bar rten gnas ngo sprod byed gsungs te phug pa so sor thugs rgyus shar mar mkhyen pas 'di nas 'di na shog gsungs
pa dang bcas rten gnas thams cad thogs med du ngo

sprod pa gnang / nyin bzhin zhabs bskor la phebs mur skabs shig byas 'gyur rgyal sgo thon tsam nas sku nyid tal mar sngon la phebs te slar tshur phebs pa nyin kha shas byung
bas nyin gcig phyag mdzod sogs nas gang yin bltar phyin pas brag ngos shig nas tir mchu nas thon pa'i tshad tsam gyi chu dkar dwangs shig 'bab kyin 'dug pa rje nyid la
gang yin zhus pas kha lud 'dra bskyur ba'i shul las thon pa yin nam gang ltar der lcog gcig btsugs na legs gsung / sang yang sngar ltar phebs rjes zhabs phyi rnams kyi kyang
slebs pas chu de nas nyid kyis kyang gsol 'khor rnams la'ang gnang bar mdzad/ re zhig nas nyams grib can zhig gi rkyen lta bus chu de chad pa'i shul du 'khyag pa sbom
tsam zhig las mi 'dug pa de don phyis su brtags tshe rten 'brel cung ma 'grig pa ma gtogs lcam bkra shis dbang mo de nyid la yab rje rin po che'i rnam 'phrul zhig 'khrungs
rgyu yin tshod kyi brda' ltas gzhan yang de dang dus mtshungs mang du byung 'dug nyin gcig 'phags mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i na bza' thams cad g.yas g.yon du bsal nas sku
rjen par lho phyogs su zhal cher gcus pa zhig byung bas sngon sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug khams la phebs skabs su pu tra chen po zhal shar 'chus byung

'dug pa bzhin da lo yang rang re rnams lhor 'gro dgos pa yin nam gsungs pa bzhin zhag shas nas dbyings zhabs rin po che nas lhor 'ching la phebs na legs tshul gyi bka' shog
'byor/ de nas zla ba gsum pa'i tshes legs par byas 'gyur bla brang nub kyi bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi thugs dam ma'i mgon sku ldebs bris ma'i drung du gsungs bskang 'phrin
bcol mdzad pa'i snyan shal bris sku'i sku dpung g.yas pa'i steng du zla ba kha shas bar gnas pa byung / zla ba de ga'i tshes bcu la gdan sar phebs/ nye 'gyangs mgon khang
so sor bzhed don 'grub pa'i kha byang can gyi snyan shal bcas gsung bskang gnang / khyad par bse mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i drung du gtor gzhi gsar 'dzugs sogs gnang bar
bse mgon chen po sku bongs che zhing snum bag ldan la zhal mkhur gnyis las 'od 'phro zhing dra sgo phyogs su sku btud nyams che ba sogs ngo mtshar bar byung / de nas yab
rje chos kyi rgyal po'i phyi rten mthong grol chen mo'i sa gzhi dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi sa chog gi sgo nas byin gyis brlabs/ dngul gdung rin po che'i srog
shing gtsug tor dri med nas byung ba bzhin gyi 'dzugs chog mdzad/ bzo bo rnams la sngar grub gyi legs so dang / slad ma'i zhal bkod gnang phebs

'grul la bsnams rgyu'i rnga thug gnyis la tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi ru mtshon 'dzugs pa'i cho ga'i sgo nas thug gsol smin par mdzad/ zla ba de'i nyi shu gsum la gdan sa
nas chibs btegs te bkra shis yang rtser bzhugs/ de dgong 'dam thog phyogs kyi sbyin bdag a bkra zer ba 'bul ba dang bcas dad mjal du 'byor bar phyag dbang sogs re skong du
bstsal/ rim gyis phag rir phebs nas gzhung 'brug gi sku tshab so sor pang?bang yig re gnang / tshes dgur chings khag gzhan rnams dang phyogs 'doms sho smug tu bzhugs sgar
bteg ste phan tshun 'phen skor ci yang zhig mdzad kyang gzhung 'brug thugs 'dod cher ma snyoms pas bzhugs 'gor skabs gseng du don gnyer rnams la chos bka' rgya cher gnang
/ bla ma gong ma mang po la gsol 'debs sho lo ka re re tsam thugs rtsom gnang zhing bla ma lha dang srung ma'i tshogs la sems can spyi'i bde thabs myur 'grub kyi thugs
smon rtse gcig tu mdzad/ phag ri thang du yab rje rin po che zhi bar gshegs pa'i gnas der gong ma de nyid dgongs pa rdzogs pa dang skye dgu'i bsod nams gsog pa'i phyi rten
du khang bu brtsegs pa'i mchod rten che legs shig kyang bzhengs pa'i zhal bkod

gnang ste tshegs med grub nas rab tu gnas pa smin rgyas mdzad skabs 'ja' 'od kyi gur dang me tog gi char sogs ya mtshan mthun sgrub tu byung / mchod rten de la nyams gso sku
dkar sogs rgyun gnas dkar leb dgon pas dgos pa'i rten gser phag zho bzhi/ dngul dang / ja sogs sbyor 'jags gnang / 'dum 'chings kyi don phan tshun nas ngos len zhig ma
byung bas 'ching pa rnams stong log tu nye tshe/ rje nyid dpon slob rtse gdong zhabs drung khri chen bcas shar nang la phebs pa'i gces sgar bzhugs skabs char che'i sgang
yin pas/ de ga'i gzhi bdag bdud po la gtor ma 'phrin bcol gnang bas sang shar nang du ma phebs bar char thigs gcig kyang ma babs pas ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su byung / 'brug
sku tshab rnams la khe nyen gyi mtha' 'doms lhug gnang mdzad pas khong rnams kyis kyang bka' dang len gyi 'dzom dus sogs ngo thon zhus/ slar bzhugs sgar du phebs pa'i lam
bar thugs rje chen po'i brag zer ba der phebs tshe 'di na gter zhig yod par 'dug gsungs/ de nas rim gyis rje nyid dang bla ma lha yi thugs rjes phan tshun gyi sku tshab
ngo bo/ lho bod kyi sa sne'i rdzong gnyer 'dus che ba rnams la ye shes chos skyong dpang 'dzugs kyi dbu rtsi sogs mtha' 'doms grub pas/

thams cad kyis bla ma sa skya pas sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal las bskyabs nas bde ba la bkod song zer ba'i gtam lab 'ur ding ding bcas legs 'bul gya nom pa stobs
pa'ang byung / yos lo hor zla gnyis pa'i tshes gsum la phag ri nas chibs kha bsgyur te bzhugs ring dang phebs lam thams cad du skye dgu mtha' dag smin grol la bkod cing
dgon gnas rnams la mang 'gyed sogs mchod sbyin phul du byung ba stsal bzhin pa nas tshes bcu'i nyin gdan sa chen por ngo mtshar ba'i bkod pa rgya chen dang bcas phebs/
mgon khang so sor gtang rag rgya cher gnang / dus rim drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog dang bstun sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung du bcad rgya gdun phrag gcig mdzad/ lo de'i mjug
tu ngor mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs 'bul ba rgya chen dang bcas byon par bka' chos sogs lugs gnyis thugs gnyes par mdzad/ 'brug lo'i nang ngor mkhan chen lhun grun
dpal ldan gdan drangs par spyan mi gsal tshul gyis dgongs zhus byung bar skyon med 'byon dgos bskyar mar phebs pa ltar byon pa lam 'bras tshogs bshad smin rgyas gsan pa
grub mtshams rgya gar gyi

sman pa am dznyi dha na 'jun bya ba lag rtsal che zhing mig 'byed la mkhas pa de 'byor bas rten 'brel rang 'grig ngos rje nyid nas mkhan chen la spyan dbye mdzad dgos shing
bar gcod mi 'ong tshul phebs par mkhan chen nas da na so rgas pa sogs nas mig gi dgos pa cher med kyang bka' bzhin dbye bar zhus pa ltar phye bas ji phebs ltar 'phral zug
tsam yang ma byung bar gsung chos gzhan yang rgya cher gsan pa mthar phyin par mdzad/ phar yang bka' chos du ma gnang/ thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi mkhan chen bzang po rgyal
mtshan spyan drangs te gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum gyi lung gsan pa'i dbu btsugs/ re zhig nas chos mtshams mdzad de phyis su gang phebs nas bka' 'bum 'phros dang / gzhan
yang snga phyir mkhan chen 'di nyid las chos bka' dpag tu med pa zhig gsan pa'ang gsan yig tu gsal/ phan phyi dpon dpal 'byor bsam 'grub pas gser dngul/ dar gos/ byi ru/
spos shel/ rta phyugs/ sman ltang / mar ltang sogs dngos po'i 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa bcas dad mjal du 'byor bar bka' chos sogs re skong du bstsal/ khong rang dad pa
dbang med du skyes pa'i shugs kyi maNDal skabs gser dngul mchod par gtor ba'i rdog po mchod dpon

sogs kyis khyor ba gang btu rgyu byung ba slob ma dad 'byor ldan pa'i lugs su 'dug dpon de 'dir 'byor thog mig kyang mi gsal zhing lus byings dang rkang pa mi bde ba 'dug pa
mjal phyag thob rjes nas rim dngas kyis thon khar mig gsal zhingalus yang bas gling skor gnyis re tsam thogs med du 'khor ba byung bas byin rlabs dngos su zhugs par gsal/
mang mkhar chab tshan la phebs tshe chab khar rlung chen langs pa gzhi bdag gtor ma zhig gnang bas rlung po rang sar zhi zhing / gung tshigs thog sku mdun du sbrul ljang
khu zhig byung bar gzigs nas gzhi bdag dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur zhig tu 'dug gsungs nas der bzhugs ring gzhi bdag gtor ma chag med gnang / gdan sar phebs nas dam rdzas ril
sgrub gnang ba'i 'phrin bcol du sgo rum du phebs par bse mgon rin po che'i zhal ras snum bag sogs dgyes nyams mthun sgrub tu byung / de skabs mnal lam zhig tu/ bud med
rgyan khral le ba zhig gi rol mo zhig thogs te 'di grog khad cig na 'dug pa khyer 'ong ba yin pas zhing skyong dgyes pa'i chas zhu zer nas phul ba zhig byung ba/ phyir nyin
bal po rol mo khur ba zhig gis bdag gi rol mo 'di 'khyags pa la 'dred nas rdeb thang gnyis shor bar brten mthar chag nyen

'dug pas gsol ras gang gnang mdzad nas 'jags par zhu zer ba zhig slebs pa snyan du dwangs 'phral de spus dga' lod gang yod kyang nyo dgos gnang bar dngul srang brgyad kyis
khugs pa'i rol mo de la zhing skyong 'brug sgrar 'dogs par mdzad bsam brling du 'byon skabs lung pa 'ja' sprin gyis gang ba dang / jo mo rtags mtshan ma'i re rtse nas 'ja'
kha dog lnga rje nyid kyi phyogs su zug pa sogs dge ltas ya mtshan pa byung / skabs der kyai rdor zhal thang / bitlba pa grub brgyas bskor ba/ sa chen gyi sku thang / sa
pan gyi rnam thar zhal thang rnams 'bul mi byung ba sogs rten 'brel legs pa dang bcas dam rdzas sgrub pa tshugs nas gsang sngags bde chen gling gi 'khor yug thams cad dri
bzang gi khyab par byung / dgung grangs so bzhi par hor zla lnga pa'i nang du sku nyid kyi rkyen sel la bcad rgya bdun phrag gsum pa zhig mdzad/ zla mjug tu sku rkyang
gis mgon po khro bcu'i gtor bzlog cig kyang gnang / skabs 'dir rgyal ltas 'tshub cheer byung ba rje nyid nas sgo rum du ljags bzlas nyin gsum mdzad rjes mgon po'i sgo nas
drag po'i sbyin sreg mdzad par brtsams pas gzhan gyi rmi lam du 'dab chags sogs srog chags 'ga' zhig zin nas mer

bskyur ba dang / ral gri me 'bar bas nam mkha'i mthongs myul ba sogs byung ba dang mthun par rgyal 'gong gi gnod pa'ang rang zhir song / gzhan yang gdug 'dre 'ga' zhig ting
nge 'dzin gyis bkug ste lam bstan chos bshad mdzad nas ma rungs pa'i skye rgyun gcod par mdzad/ de rjes sku mtshams bdun phrag cig gnang skabs/ gur mgon gyi sku brnyan gsal
po zhig byung gsungs pa'i sang der gzhan zhig gis gsol ras zhu rten gur mgon gyi sku brnyan khru gang ba zhig 'bul mi byung / lha khang chen mo'i btsun chung rnams la
chos spyod rgyugs bzhes mdzad de thugs dgyes nyams chen pos thams cad la 'bras sil shing tog rigs sogs bya dga' gnang / rab byung gi sder phyag mdzad pa sogs bstan pa'i
la rgyar khyab gang che mdzad/ dgung grangs so lnga par gong ma yab mes rin po che rnam pa gnyis gyis gtsos pa'i sngon byon rnams kyi dgongs pa rdzogs byed dang bstan pa'i
btsas su dgongs pa'i chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i gser 'bum mthong grol chen mor nyams gsos dang gser chab gsar gsol/ 'dra sku rme ba can la dpe byas pa'i sku
brnyan dang / yab rje rin po che'i sku brnyan gsar bzhengs/ gser 'bum gyi chos 'khor yan la gser zangs bskyar 'bul/

gser phibs shing bsgrigs nas bzung bskyar 'gel/ gnam rgyan/ sa rgyan/ rol cha/ mchod rdzas mar me'i rgyun 'dzugs pa sogs kyis mtshon mchod rten maN khang kagni sogs snga yod
nyams gso dang gsar bzhengs gzugangs 'bul rab gnas skyor ba sogs du ma zhig mdzad/ 'di skabs kyang mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan phebs par dbang khrid lung gi rigs dpag
tu med pa zhig gsan pa'i mthar mkhan chen de nyid nas rje nyid la zhabs drung nas 'chad rtsom gnang ba rnams gdul bya shin tu rmongs pa yin na ma gtogs nyams rtogs legs
pa ci rigs pa re mi skye ba ma mthong zhing / deng sang dbus gtsang gnyis la zab chos bzhugs tshogs che ba sku nyid 'gran zla ma mchis gshis chos bka' spyi dang khyad
par sa skya'i yab chos yang zab 'di rnams rgyun spel mi nyams pa sngar rgyun bzhin rtag 'grus gnang dgos gsungs pas/ rje nyid nas deng dus chos la don gnyer nyung zhing kha
cig za chog mkho bed tsam gyi chos zhur byung yang rkyen phra mo tsam yang mi theg par lkog dngos gang rung nas bla mar 'bar shar gtong ba'i dam sel nyams grib kyis srid
pa'i ma mo 'khrugs pas 'jig rten na mi dge ba 'byung ba'i rgyu las mi 'dug pas phal cher brgyud pa lhad med nas thob pa'i chos bka' rnams rang gi nyams

len gang lcogs lro dge rtsa sems can la bsngo smon byas pa rang phan yon che 'dra snyam mod/ 'on kyang rnam 'dren bla ma'i bka' stsal mi gcog pas dam ldan 'os rigs byung tshe
de bzhin zhu gsung / de skabs mdo smad ri khud dgon sku skye ngag dbang kun dga' dang / gdong dga' bla ma bsod nams chaso 'phel/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi zur 'chad pa
sogs snod ldan 'ga' zhig gis gsol ba btab ngor/ kyai rdor rgyu lam gyi dbang sogs smin grol zab rgyas du ma zhig bstsal/ dgung grangs so drug par chos rje bco brgyad pa
mkhyen rab ngag dbang byams pa lhun grub gdan drangs te mdo sngags gsar rnying lung 'khrid man ngag dbang bka' snyan brgyud zab mo dpag tu med pa zhig gsan/ phar yang chos
rje rin po che de nyid kyis gtsos pa 'ga' la chos bka' rgya cher gnang / gdan sa dan gyi nub phyogs dpon chen shAkyang bzang po'i gser 'bum bzhugs pa'i skor dang / sa
la dbang phyug grags sogs kyi gtsug lag khang phyi nang gog stobs che bar thog mar arga'i cho ga nas bzung zhig gsos mdzad/ pa la ba'i nang rten mchod rten gnyis kyi gdugs
'khor yan nyams gso dang / mchod rten gcig rtsa ba nas gsar bzhengs/ sku brnyan re gnyis ma gtogs ldebs bris

tshang ma gsar bzhengs/ sngar med gser zangs kyi sku brnyan/ rten gsar rnying la gzungs 'bul tshul ldan rab gnas smin rgyas gnam sa'i rgyan mchod pa'i rgyun sogs rmad du byung
ba bskrun/ chos khri chen mo'i mdun gyi rdo gcal lcags ri chen mo yang dngos mi gtsang bas lo lo bzhin nyams gso dgos 'dug par 'gram brtsig rmang nas bslang ba'i 'khor
yangs brtan brling spang bad g.yam bsgrigs sogs khyad mtshar bsgrubs nas pu tra ming sring la bcol gtam gnang bas chu dang khad nye sogs la dogs pa gtan nas med pa byung
/ gzhan yang dbu rtse rnying ma dang bla brang phun tshogs gling sogs kyi'ang spen bad bcad g.yam sogs 'ga' zhig nyams gso mdzad/ lo phyi ma'i dgung keg gi dogs sel la
thugs dam zam mo 'ga' zhig kyang 'phar ma rgyun ring gnang / dgung grangs so bdun par zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis dgung keg stabs bcad rgya gnang bar zhus pas/ keg skyon med
pa ngas khag 'khur/ khyed rang tsho zhig gsos sngar 'phros rnams dang khyad par bde mchog pho brang gi nyams gsos 'di bzhin dgos tshul sogs phebs/ theg chen chos rje'i
phyi rten dang / gser khang rnying ma'i lam 'bras brgyud pa'i sku brnyan rnams dang / grags blo mgon chen rig 'dzin lha khang /

lha khang rtse/ sgrol ma lha khang / mngon dga' bde ldan/ sgo rum bla ma lha khang / rdzong chung lha khang / nyi lde bla brang / bde chen gling mgon khang / g.yu thog mgon
khang / rin chen sgang lha khang bla brang grangs mo che/ lha khang chen mo'i khyams chen gyi ko dra rgyug dra sgog hral du song ba rnams sogs nyams gso gang dgos dang gsar
bzhengs bris 'bur mchod rgyun sogs mthar phyin par gnang / de nas phur sgrub dang khyad nye'i skabs gnam char sogs kyi rkyen cher med par glo bur du shal kha phyogs nas
chu log chen po zhig rdol ba'i gdan sa'i mdun gyi zam pa rnams kyang khyer/ byang rgyud kyi khang pa rnams la'ang nyen grabs byung bar phyag nas gnang bas 'phral du chu
bri ba'i ya mtshan byung yang / kun gyis khrom chu 'di ltar byung ba sku de dag gi ngo yin thag chod pas sku rim la 'bad pa dang phur sgrub kyi tshogs dbur mi phebs pa
legs tshul mgrin gcig zhus par/ nged la re zhig gegs dang bar gcod med/ chu log 'di ni 'byung ba'i rang shugs sam/ gzhan gyi rbod gtong gi rnam rtog bslang ched cig yin las
che yang nged rang la ya nga bag tsha med pas rang khag rang gis theg phur sgrub la 'gro ba rang sku rim yin pas cis kyang 'gro/ khyed rang tshos zam pa 'dzugs grabs kyis
dang

tshegs med tshugs yong gsungs pa bzhin nyin gsum gyi ring la zam pa gsum char brtan brling legs par tshugs/ de skor bka' phebs ji lta ba bzhin gegs 'tshe sogs ma byung bas
phyis zhig sku rtsed kyi tshul du khyed rnams bla ma la yid mi ches pa'i skyon zhig yod/ da yid ches sam sogs kyang gnang / de nas theg chen rin po chee'i thugs dam ma'i
kyai rdor blos bslang gi nyams gso rab gnas sogs mdzad/ dgung grangs so brgyad par mdar stod nas chos rje ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas pa zhi bar gshegs tshul gsan 'phral
gzim dpon bsod nams blo gros sku gdung gi zhabs tog tu brdzangs par mdzad de bslabs ston nang bzhin gdung mchod zhugs sbyangs bcas mtha' gtsang bsgrubs pa'i gdung byon
yig 'bru sogs khyad par ba rnams zur btus kyi gdung rus rnams gdan sar rje nyid kyi drung du phul bas zla shas bar mchod pa'i rten du bzhugs su gsol zhing de mtshams nas
sbyangs btul la phyag tsha gnang ste rnam 'dren de nyid kyi 'dra sku bzhengs pa sogs dgongs rdzogs rgya cher mdzad/ de lo byang chub gling gi sprul sku yon tan rgya mtsho
sku gshegs pa'i zhal chems su khong gi gdung rus rnams gdan sar phul la

nga rang gi 'dra 'bag gcig mgo 'dren zhus gsungs 'dug pa ltar 'byor bas rje nyid nas sa lam gyi bar gcod zhi ba'i skyabs 'jug dang 'dra sku gsar bzhengs la gzungs bzhugs dang
rab gnas smin rgyas bcas gnang ba'i 'thor nas 'bru gsum sku 'dra'i thugs kar 'dzin pa sogs ngo mtshar ba byung / rtse gdong nas zhabs drung a mi drung kun dga' tshe dbang
rig 'dzin bka' chos 'ga' zhig zhu bar phebs par yang grub rgyal tshe dbang / lcags sdong ma/ mda' 'phel ma rnams kyis thog drangs/ yab chos yang phur gnyis kyis gtsos
pa'i dbang lung dpag tu med pa zhig bstsal/ chos sde lho byang 'dus tshogs rnams la sngon 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi sku ring tshugs pa'i sa paN gyi sdom rgyun ltar nyi shur
slebs pa rnams la bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dngos po bsgrub dgos bka' phebs bzhin mkhan chen bsam gtan lhun pos gra gsar lnga bcu skor ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan 'dzin par
bsgrubs pa'i las gral mdzad/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan khams su phebs rgyur nyer mkho'i chos bka' phyag len du ma zhig dang / zang zing gi gnang cha dpag med bstsal/
mkhan chen nyid nas kyang tshe dbang brgya rtsa dang / zhabs brtan 'bul ba spom mthor phul te

dpon slob nang thugs gshin pa'i phebs sgo du ma gnang / dgung grangs so dgu par lha khang chen mo'i lcags ri'i byang spe nyams gso dang / de dag tu bstan pa rin po che phyogs
mthar rgyas pa'i bum gter kha shas 'jug pa gnang / 'bum thang gi dpal chen 'od po/ zangs tsha/ ba ri lo tsA ba rnams kyi phyi rten 'ga' zhig hrul ba la arga'i cho ga nas
brtsams nyams gsos rmang nas bslang bar mdzad pa de skabs than pa che bas skye dgu nyam thag pa'i skabs yin pa la ar po tshugs nas char rgyun legs par babs pas rten 'brel
phun sum tshogs pa byung/ rten rnams kyi nang bzhugs sngar yod la gser chab gsol ba dang / gsar 'bul tshad med pa phyag len rnam par dag pa'i sgo nas bstsal te rab gnas
smin rgyas bcas mthar phyin par mdzad/ srung ma bse khrab can gyis lung bstan bzhin/ dpon chen shAkya bzang po'i gser 'bum thog gi dbang khang ka drug mar tshe dpag med
kyi 'bur sku bcu gsum bris sku brgya dang lnga bcu rnams gsar bzhengs/ mchod rdzas du ma dang bcas bskrun par mdzad/ gong du smos pa ltar rig 'dzin gter bdag gling pa chen
pos/ thugs rje chen po bde gshegs kun 'dus gter nas gdan drangs pa'i lo bdun tshun la gsan bzhes grub na legs

tshogs che yang rim 'gyang du song ba 'di lo gter ston rin po cher zhu yig gnang ba ltar gter chen de nyid kyi gcung sha 'ug gi chos bdag lung zin lo chen ngag dbang chos dpal
zab chos sgo skyel gyi tshul du phebs par sne len bkur gzos rgya chen dang bcas rtsa ba'i zab chos de nyid dang gzhan yang rnying lugs kyi chos bka' dpag tu med pa zhig
gsan/ lo chen la'ang yang dag mar me dgu pas gtsos pa'i zab chos dpag med gnang / de nas lho bod mtshams kyi skye bo mi srun pa rnams kyi dkrug gzhi dang / lha sa'i blon
chen pad ma rgyal po 'khor bcas 'brug phyogs la ngo bltas pa'i rkyen byas/ a 'dzin bod zhabs su yod par 'brug phyogs nas rgyab gnyer sogs la dga' ldan pho brang pa thugs
ma song bas zing long du nye ba na/ rje nyid kyi thugs bskyed rmad du byung bas 'dum chings la chibs bsgyur/ lam bar du'ang chos kyi sbyin pa stsal bzhin pas chu mig shel
mgor phebs dus gnas 'dir ma 'ongs pa na dam chig nyams pa'i snga ltas shig 'dug gsungs pa phyis su padma rgyal po khu mtshan chings mtshams las 'das nas dmar gsod byung
ba de yin tshod 'dug rim gyis phebs te spre mo la'i lha khang ka gnyis kyi nub phyogs su bzhugs sgar gdan chags pa'i skabs shig gsungs las/ nged

'dir bsdad pas gzhi bdag 'ga' re dga' ba dang 'ga' re mi dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur 'dug ces phebs/ de skabs rje nyid bzhugs sgar gyi phyi nang gar phebs la 'ja' tshon gyi 'od sgor
rang byung bar/ phyag mdzod nas nyin bzhin 'ja' sgor 'di yid snang bde rgyu rang zhig mi 'dug pas/ chings khag gzhan dang lhan cig phag rir phebs na mi 'thad dam zhus
pas/ deng sang nam zla drod gsher stabs 'ja' sprin yong ba la nyes pa rang med dam gsungs/ 'on kyang phyag mdzod nas gdan sar sku rim gyi bang yig dang / dgon khag gzhan
la'ang mang bskol sogs brdzangs mur phag ri'i bsnyen gnas ma rnams la thugs rje chen po'i rjes gnang dang bsgoom lung gnang ba'i sku grib kyi nyen bslangs sku khams ltem
pa zhig byung bas/ nye skor gyi dgon sder sku rim yang bskyar rgya che ba dang / ban tshang ba rnams kyis bskang gso/ sri mnan/ sri thar sogs gseng sher med par bsgrubs/
bzhugs sgar sho smug tu spos nas 'brug pa dang mjal 'dzom zhig mdzad dgos byung bar sku 'khor rnams nas phebs pa bshol yang / da lan thog mar yin gshis rten 'brel gyis rib
tsam zhig 'gro/ lab rgyu sogs mdzod pa rang nas zhib tshags

gyis dang skyon mi 'ong phebs pa bzhin don gnas byung / de skabs rje nyid kyi mnal lam du/ sku nyid sa phyogs spang gshong zhig na bzhugs pa'i nye phyogs su ban de mgo skya
zhig gis gzan nyis lteb cig bting ste de'i khar bzhugs zer bar bzhugs pa la thugs mi spro ba zhig byung nas gzhan zhig tu phebs par phebs lam rnams su khos gzan de bting
nas zhabs rdzis thebs thabs rang byed par/ rje nyid nas thugs zon mdzad pa'i mur/ mchod rten dkar po zhig la sgo zhig 'dug pa'i nang du phebs pas seng khri'i nang lam 'bras
bla brgyud sku 'dra gzi byin ldan pa gsung 'byon nye ba'i nyams can gyi mtha' skor du mchod pa sna tshogs shig bshams 'dug pa'i sku re re la byiin rlabs zhu bar mdzad/
bum ldir du byon pa'i tshe/ rig 'dzin brgyud pa gong bzhin bzhugs 'dug pa rnams la'ang byin rlabs zhu bar mdzad pas 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po gzhan las kyang zil che ba
zhig gis byin rlabs gnang ba dang bstun rigs kyi bu mchog dang ldan pa khyod da lam bsnyun gzhi 'di las myur du grol bar yod do/ /sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa spel la sems can
gyi don mdzod cig gsungs pa'i mur mnal sad pa dang sku khams dngas shing thugs bde mas shar/ gdan sa nas dpon tshang

bstan 'phel ba yang bshad rtsol gyis 'byor pas 'phral du gsol sman phul/ khong la phyag mdzod nas bsnyun gzhi'i bab dris pas skyon rang mi 'dug tsha ba ma smin pa la bsil bcos
thal ba'i skyon du 'dug zer ba bzhin ngos gsal gyis rim dngas su gyur pas dus tshes dge bar lha dang srung mar gtang rag gi bsangs gsol rgyas pa sogs gnang/ de nas 'chings
mtshams rim gyis 'phen skor mdzad kyang / phan tshun gnyis ka nas 'phral len zhig ma byung ba'i skabs/ phag ri bas bsos pa 'brog pa'i nor phyugs tshan che ba ded pa'i
rgyus btsan gdong ba dang 'khon rkyen gyi phag ri rdzong dpon stod lung zhing mo che bas/ ngan zhe bzhag gis rje'i bzhugs sgar thog tu btsan gdong ba'i tshong pa thor
bu yod pa la bkab pas rje nyid thugs dam gyi mur hab 'gros kyis bzhengs nas bar mdzad kyang phag ri yul don pa rnams kyis brtsi med kyi btsan gdong ba'i mi bcu gnyis bzung
'khrid kyis bzhugs sgar la sma 'bebs byas par thugs rgyal bzheengs te chos srung la drag po'i las bskul gnang bas/ de ma thag ngan sbyor ba rnams la dmar bshal gyi nad
yams lta bu'i zhag re'i nad kyis sha rus tshal par tshad pa zhig byung ste 'chi khar khog zhugs kyis/ bsam yas chos skyong

yin/ gnod sbyin beg rtse yin/ nged tsho gur gyi mgon pos sdod du mi ster/ gur gyi mgon po sa skya 'jam dbyangs khros pas sdod du mi ster zer ba sogs kyi rtags mtshan mngonasum
du gyur pas tshar bcad/ zla ba dang po'i nang phag btsan gyi mi rta sprod len du rong la phebs nas zla ba phyed gnyis lhag 'gor gyi skabs mnal lam du yab rje rin po che
de nyid kyi phyag na nor bu'i rigs kha dog sna tshogs pa zhig bsnams nas rje nyid la gnang ba dang mnyam du thugs dgyes nyams dang bcas te nged kyi rnam thar de shin tu
legs po byung 'dug ngo mtshar che ba'i nang nas rgyal mtshan 'dzugs pa'i cho ga de ngo mtshar che bar yod gsungs pa zhig byung / de mtshams srung ma'i tshogs la 'phrin
bcol bcas thugs bskyed rnam par dag pa'i mthus 'brug phyogs nas pad rgyal khu mtshan phyogs gtogs mi grangs bzhi stong lhag pa phyir slog dang / bod phyogs nas kyang a 'dzin
char gtogs bcas pa rtsod zlos med pa bcas gzhung 'brug so so nas gsal mdzad pas rje nyid nas legs spel gyi khra ma 'doms che ba'i dbu rtsi bzhes pas mchog dman thams
cad yid bde'i gnas su gyur/ de nas phag ri nas chibs btegs te rim gyis phebs pa'i

lam bar du sngon chos rgyal 'phags pas btab pa'i sram dgon gsar zhes pa'i gtsug lag khang nyams gog ches par nyams gso'i rten dang gnyer bdag tu sram pa sngags 'chang bsko
bzhag mdzad/ lam bar gyi 'gro ba rnams phan bder sbyor bzhin pa nas phebs bsu ring thung sogs sngar rgyun bzhin gyi gdan sa chen por phebs te srung ma'i tshogs la gtang rag
sogs rim sel mdzad/ sde dge bla ma sangs rgyas dpal bzang dpon g.yog rnams 'bul chen bcas 'byor ba dang / re zhig nas ngor mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyang phebs
pa bcas gzhi byes chos zhu ba du mar bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang dang / chos srung skor du ma/ 'khrid brgya sogs chos 'khor rgyun ring du bskor/ gdung rgyud myur
byon sku rim sgo rum skyed lhas sogs su sku mtshams bdun phrag re gnang / dgung grangs zhe gsum par gong sa rin po che drug pa chen po mjal bzhed sogs kyis dbus phyogs su
chibs bsgyur/ rong dga' bder phebs tshe khong rnams la gdon rkyen drag po zhig gis mi grangs mang po shi chad dang cho 'phrul btud ma la nus ldan grags chen du mar skyabs
zhus byas kyang phan med kyi khar srung rim mkhan rnams rkyen dbang du 'gro ba'i brtol med cig byung

'dug par skyabs 'jug zhus pas/ rje nyid nas bgegs skrod dang / tshe rta sbrel ba'i dbang zhig gnang ba nas bzung 'tshub lhong gtan chad pas phyis su'ang dad spros gsol ba 'debs
pa byung / de nas skyed tshal klu sdings nye bar gzhung sa mchod yon nas thab 'dzin dang phebs bsu bcas ja sbyor gnyis yun la bzhugs gral gnang / lha sar rag kha gling
du bzhugs sgar mdzad/ 'di skabs lha sar sib bu sogs nad yams du ma zhig yod pa'ang rim gyis chad/ de nas rgyal dbang mchod yon lhan rgyas nas 'byor thon sbrags ma'i mjal
kha bsdus pa bzhin zhabs brtan gyi 'bul nod sogs rgyas par mdzad/ po ta la'i gnas rten zhib mjal dang / gser gdung 'dzam gling rgyan gcig mjal bar mdzad tshe rgyal dbang
de nyid kyi thugs brtse dran pas gsol 'debs shig kyang 'phral rtsom mdzad/ jo shAka rnam gnyis sogs zhib mjal dgongs pas phebs kyang jo bo rin po che ma gtogs phebs lam
gzhan du phyag dbang zhu mis 'gags te phebs ma thub/ yer pa zla ba phug gi gnas gzigs la phebs te zhib mjal mchod 'bul bcas de dgongs phyir 'khor mdzad/ lha sa'i gzhi gnas
phyogs 'dus bcas nas gdan sa'i zhal ngo

rim phebs las kyang rje 'di nyid la dad spro 'bul mjal tshan che ba byung / de nas rtse shod nas gnang cha phebs skyel sogs sngar rgyun bzhin gyi bsam yas phyogs su chibs bteg
bsam yas rab byung chos sde'i 'cham mgon ser phreng gi bkod pa bcas phebs bsu zhus nas pho brang gong du bzhugs/ 'di skabs shig nas gnod sbyin chen po'i sku rten par
skabs re 'byung po gzhan zhig kyang 'bab rdzu yong ba zhig byung bas lha tshes dang bstun pa'i chos skyong yin zer ba de khog 'bebs byas pa'i mjal 'phrad sogs yab mes kyi
srol rgyun ltar mdzad/ chos skyong des kyang lha rgyal bskul ba sogs sngar lugs bzhin byung / dkar zhal mthil du ser skya grangs las 'das par tshe dbang zhig khrom chos
su gnang nyin rgyal po shing bya can sku phebs kyis rje nyid la ched du brjod pa'i bstod tshig du ma dang bcas gdugs dkar po zhig phul te lha rgyal lan gsum bskul bar mdzad/
rje nyid nas kyang sgron dar gnang / sgrags su gnas gzigs la phebs te sgrub phug so so zhib mjal dang bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs gnang / dkon gnyer gyi ngag nas kha sang
zhag shas nas khog zhugs cig gis sa gnas kyi skyes bu dam pa zhig gnas gzigs la 'byon pa yod

pas phebs lam sogs 'chos dgos rnams bde bar gyis shig zer byung ba rje 'di nyid phebs pas yin par 'dug zer/ sang rdor brag rig 'dzin chen po dpon slob mjal khar 'byon par thugs
spro gnang / gter ston 'dud 'dul gling pa chen pos kyang rje nyid chos bdag yin tshul bcas 'byon par thugs dgyes mdzad/ slar yang bsam yas su phebs/ stag rtse sde pa
lha rgyal rab brtan drung gis spyan drangs te gsol ston dang 'bul nod gzab pa zhus/ de 'phral mchod yon lhan cig dbu rtser gnas gzigs dang khrus gsol rab gnas bcas gnang
/ bco lngar mdo sde mchod pa gzigs/ de nas chibs bsgrur te 'bras gling du phebs/ grwa pa zhig gis klu 'jim las grub pa'i ston pa'i mdzad bcu shel sgo can ngo mtshar ba phul
bas thugs shin tu mnyes nas rten gsum mchod cha 'gang che rigs byung na gdan sa chen por phebs pa'i 'os yin sogs gsungs/ khra 'brug tu phebs te mchod 'bul smon lam rgyas
par mdzad/ rdo skas mgo'i sgrol ma'i bris sku la snyan shal 'bul bar mdzad pas bzhes par grags/ yar klung dbon rin po che nas gdan 'dren zhus par

phebs lam du chos rgyal 'phags pa sku 'khrungs pa'i gtam snyan sa paN gyis gsan pa'i gtam snyan chos khri la bkras btags kyi dar lcog cig gnang / yum bu bla mkhar gnas gzigs/
de 'tshams bkra shis chos sde nas phebs bsu'i bkod pa tshar du dngar ba dang bcas bla brang du phebs/ dkar spro gzab ma zhabs brtan 'bul ba rgya cher phul/ yar klung shel
brag tu gnas gzigs la phebs/ de skor gyi tshes bcu ba rnams la le'u bdun ma'i ljags lung gnang / btsan thang lha khang dang / bya sa lha khang gnas gzigs/ smin grol gling
nas gdan 'dren 'byor ba bzhin phebs nye'i tshe lo chen rin po che dpon g.yog gis chibs bsu dang / ser phreng gi bkod pa rmad du byung bas phebs bsu bcas thugs spro'i
ngang nas zhag shas bzhugs/ gter chen rin po che sku mched yab sras so sor legs skyes rgya cher bstsal/ gter chen rin po che yab sras la tshe dpag dkar po dang / gur mgon
lha brgyad/ pu tra'i zur bka' rnams gnang / gter chen rin po che'i zhabs drung du thugs rje chen po bde gshegs kun 'dus kyi chos skor tshang ma smin rgyas gsan/ sku 'bum
mthong grol chen mo sogs gnas rten rnams la phyag nas dang phan tshun thugs nang gcig 'dres kyi dgyes spro mdzad/ dngos

po'i 'bul ba rgya chen dang bcas gter chen rin po che nas slar yang mjal ba'i smon lam dang skyel thung gnang/ gra thang du zhang blon lha g.yag gi bsu ba la snyan shal gnang
/ sne chung chos mdzad nas rgya sbug phrin las mkha' khyab kyi gtsos 'bul chen dang bcas rnam kun thugs rjes gzung bar gsol ba btab/ ra ba smad du lha mi'i bsu ba ngo
mtshar ba bcas phebs/ sang nyin bsangs mchod rgyas pa'i thog chos skyong dang mjal 'phrad mdzad de/ rje nyid nas dbu 'ching / sgron dar sna lnga/ gser skye mas srang gang
/ gzhan yang spyan gzigs sgo mtshon lha rta sogs rgya cher bstsal/ chos skyong gi gsung las dge bshes chen po nyi ma'i 'od zer 'bangs 'khor du ma'i tshogs bcas pa dkar po'i
gnas nas bzung ra sa 'phrul snang brgyud 'gro ba mang po'i rgyud byin gyis brlabs nas gnas 'dir 'byor ba legs po dga' rab yin/ srung ma bswe'i khrab can nga rang yang
dregs pa'i chas su zhugs te lus dang grib bzhin res sngon la 'ong / res rjes la 'ong byas pa dge bshes rang gi gsal nang ltar yin sogs zhus pas/ rje nyid nas kyang de ltar
yin tshul dang / da dung yang bstan dang bstan 'dzin skyong pa dgos tshul sogs phebs/ chos skyong nas

zhus ngor gnas der bzhugs zhag gsum mdzad/ 'dus sder mang 'gyed gya nom pa dang khrom dbang gnang ba'i skabs chos skyong nyid nas gos chen gyi rgyal mtshan zhig la bkras btags
btags pa zhig phul te sku phebs thog nas chos gsan/ lcog tu gsungs bskang bcas bkra shis 'thor nas sogs chos skyong gi dgongs bzhed ltar gnang mtshams chos skyong nas
kyang dar dkar gser srang sogs 'bul ba rgya chen dang bcas chos srid rim gyis dar zhing gegs dang bar gcod med pa sogs kyi lung bstan phul/ de nas chibs btegs pas chos skyong
nas skyel thung dang lcog gi rtse nas dar dkar g.yab mo sogs kyi rten 'brel bsgrig gong dkar chos sder bzhugs zhag gsum du nyin re bzhin mang 'gyed rgyas pa re dang
khrom dbang sogs bstsal/ phyi nang gi rten rnams la mchod 'bul bcas zhib mjal mdzad/ grwa tshang spyi sger nas kyang zhabs brtan dang sbrel ba'i 'bul nod tshan che ba byung
/ gsang ba'i mgon khang du gtor gzhi gsar 'dzugs bcas gsung bskang 'phrin bcol rgyas par gnang / de nas chibs btegs te thar pa gling du gling zhabs drung dpon g.yog mjal
khar 'byor bar chos 'brel sogs thugs mnyes mdzad/ de ga'i mkhan grwa nang legs rang med par zhal ta phebs pas de phyin

lugs legs su gyur/ 'brong rtse zhal ngo dpon g.yog 'bul chen bcas 'byor bar phyag dbang zhal mjal gnang / rtsi'i gnas gsar gyi dgon gnas dang / 'jam dbyangs sa paN gyis byin
gyis brlabs pa'i rkyang 'dul bde ba can du phebs/ ngor du mang 'gyed dang 'du khang chen mor tshogs chos kyang bstsal/ spyi sger nas 'bul nod dang bsnyen bkur bsam gyis
mi khyab pa phul/ de ltar yas phyir phebs lam du dgon gnas che phra rnams su mang ja 'gyed dang bcas bstsal ba yang / gser mdog can/ yer pa'i dgon sde/ gung thang chos sde/
bsam yas rab byung grwa tshang / sgrags gi sgrub sde/ 'bras gling / bkra shis chos sde/ shel brag smin grol gling / gra phyi/ gra thang / gdung phud chos 'khor/ dwags
po grwa tshang / gong dkar/ thar pa gling / gur pa grwa tshang / rtse chen/ rtsi'i gnas gsar/ rkyang 'dul bde ba can/ ngor rnams te de dag tu gnas gzigs rten mjal la phebs
pa dang / chos bka' yang phal cher la bstsal zhing / chos sde che gras de rigs dang 'dab 'byor yul grong la'ang khrom dbang yang lnga drug gnang ste 'brel thogs thar lam
bkod cing gzugs can gzugs med kyi zhabs tog blo'i ra ba

las 'das pa byung / rim gyis gdan sar phebs/ 'di lo khams gser mdog bla ma dang sku skye sogs kyis gsol ba btab ngor gsung ngag rin po che khrid gzhung smin rgyas la rgyab
brten lung gi skor che long bcas bka' drin bstsal/ gsung ngag grol nyin smon grol gling gter chen rin po che nas gsungs shog dang ratna gling pa'i gter byon slob dpon gyi
sku mthong grol chen mo 'bul mi 'byor ba'ang dngos grub tu dgongs/ de mtshams shab tu chibs bsgyur gnang ste dge sdings pho brang gi gsang ba'i mgon khang dang Da Di'i mgon

bka' sku drin bstsal/ sa phyogs zhabs kyis bcags shing phyag nas 'thor bas byin gyis brlabs par mdzad nas gdan sar phebs/ dgung grangs zhe bzhi par gzhung sa mchod yon
nas lo ngo gsum la ar po che chung sogs byas mi chog pa'i rgya sdem mdzad par rje nyid nas dgongs khrol zhu bar mdzad de gsang sngags bde chen gling gi lcags ri gra shag
rnams dang / grags seng sku 'bum/ lha khang chen mo'i steng g.yab/ khor yug ldeb mthil

zhal ba logs bris bcas/ glo 'bur zur chen gnyis su gser gyi rgyal mtshan phal thog phyed gsum re yod pa dang / glo 'bur dbus kyi gser 'phru che ba/ gan mdzod chen mor dngos
grub 'byung ba'i lha'i sku brnyan du mar sku rgyu dang gzungs 'bul tshad ldan rnams rab gnas smin rgyas bcas bsgrub gnang gi gnam sa'i rgyan dang mchod rgyun sogs rmad du
byung ba mdzad/ gur pa bla ma dpon g.yog rnams kyis gsol ba btab ngor rdo rje gzhon nu'i stod las kyi dbang / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang sogs re skong du bstsal/ zla
ba drug pa'i nang chos grwa lho byang gtsor gyur gyi mang ba rnams la gsang 'dus kyi dbang chen bka' drin bskyang tshe/ dgong cig mnal lam du yab rje dam pa de nyid gsal
por mjal ba'i zhal nas/ zhabs drung deng sang ci mdzad kyin yod gsungs par/ rje nyid nas bdag deng sang gsang 'dus kyi dbang zhig byed skabs lags zhus pas/ de shin tu legs
'on kyang snyigs dus 'dir chos sgrub la bar gcod che yang / khyed rang gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rjes rjes su bzung bas mkha' 'gro sde lngas 'bral med gegs dang bar gcod srung
bar 'dug pas skyon mi 'byung / da dung chos 'chad pa la rem mdzod gsungs nas/

gos ljang gu la dril ba'i bse sgam zhig gi nang shel bum nor bu'i kha rgyan can zhig gi kha rgyan gyi mtshams nas bdud rtsi chil chil lud pa zhig gnang byung / bdud rtsi de

sa rang min nam snyam pas bag tsha mi dgos/ 'on kyang zla mjug 'dir phur bzlog cig dang drug cu pa zhig tshugs na rnam rtog gi 'gal rkyen sod pa yod do gsungs pa bzhin
bsgrubs/ de rjes thang stong lugs kyi tshe sgrub bdun phrag gcig dang / gter gsar gar dbang tshe sgrub bdun phrag gcig bcad rgya mdzad/ mthar tshogs

brgya zhig gnang nyin rtse gdong nas gnam lcags rdo rje rtse dgu rtse lnga gnyis dang rol mo sogs 'bul mi 'byor ba yang rten 'brel legs tshogs su dgongs/ dbyar kha 'jam dbyangs
gzi 'od 'bar ba'i dbu thog gi rgya phibs shing brtsegs gsar 'bubs/ gser zangs nyams gso phul phyin dang nang so pu tra khang gi lho phyogs kyi gyang la skyon zhugs pa'i
'ag na 'degs kyi gyang skyor zheng che ba thog la reg pa sogs brtan brling mdzad/ ngor mkhan chen tshul khrims dpal bzang sku khams cung zad rnyog par thugs dam skyabs
'jug zhu rten bsil ba tshal gyi rdo nag las grub pa'i gur mgon gyi sku brnyan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i thugs dam rten zhal gyi bris thang / mgon po me 'bar ma sogs
rten gsum 'gangs che ba mang pos drangs pa'i 'bul chen zhu yig bcas 'byor bas/ gsungs las da lam ngor mkhan chen sku khams ga 'dra 'tsho'am gsungs pa bzhin ma 'gyangs par
sku gshegs tshul byung ba bzhin ngor du dgongs rdzogs rten gnang ba dang / rje nyid nas kyang sa lam gyi gegs sel gsung bsngo thugs gtad gnang rjes kha'us chab tshan dang
chabs cig byas 'gyur nyams gso'i rab gnas sogs la phebs/ slar gdan sar phebs nas mgon khang nye 'gyang du 'phrin bcol sngon gro'i dam

rdzas ril sgrub mthar phyin btang rag bcas gnang / 'di lo lha mo mchod pa'i spyan gzigs gsar 'bul mang ba dang / khyad par mngon rtogs dang mthun pa'i dre'u'i sga chas mi mgoo'i
gzugs kyi sga ru/ nad rkyal/ byang khres/ sho rdo/ tshon dru/ khram shing / g.yang gzhi/ sbrul gyi gong smad sogs bzo bkod legs pa dang / nyi zla rma bya'i gdugs sogs
zhal bkod mdzad/ zla ba lnga pa'i gzhug nas rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs la gsung chos kyi 'phro mang zhig rgyun ring po'i bar gnang / glo bo rgyal po'i sras zhig rab byung
gsan 'dod kyi mkhan po zhus par chos las pa dbang phyug chos bshad rdzong bda' gnang / mnga' zhabs su dngos spyad bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sbyin gtong rgya chen dang
/ chos 'khor rgyun ring bskor ba mdzad mur phyag zhabs la bsnyun zhig byung bar rang gzhan phyogs mthar zhabs brtan sku rim bsam gyis mi khyab zhig bsgrubs/ grub thob thang
stong pa'i dbon brgyud gra thang mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs bka' chos zhu bar phebs par khong rigs chos gnyis ka'i brgyud pa khyad par can du 'dug gshis
rkyen sel grub thob tshe dbang brgya rtsa zhig gsan pas de ras kyi sku khams dang skyed byung / mgon po mnga' gsol gyi thugs dam bskang ba'i rten du

gtso thang kyai rdo rje la mgon po gur zhal lcam dral 'khor bcas nor lha sogs zhal thang khyad 'phags bdun gyi gtsos/ gzhan yang tsan dan dmar po las slob dpon mtshan brgyad
khru tshad zhe 'gro dang / thugs rje chen po bde gshegs kun 'dus kyi lha grangs rnams gzungs 'bul tshad ldan rab gnas smin rgyas bcas gnang mur lho bod zing bun 'dum la
sku dog stabs rje nyid phebs ma thub par 'ching 'doms su mdzod pa rdzong gnang mdzad/ sku nyid bde mchog pho brang du gar dbang tshe dpag med kyi ljags bsnyen them par gnang
/ ngor thar rtse dbon po dpon g.yog rnams byon par phyag rdor u tsarma'i rjes gnang zhig gnang rjes deng skabs nged la dngos po zhig 'bul mi yong ba yod do gsungs pa
dang / ma 'gyang bar la stod ding ri'i phyogs nas ban de zhig gis gnam lcagasakyi rdo rje rtse lnga pa ngo mtshar can zhig phul bas/ kha sang dngos po zhig yong ba yod byas
pa 'di yin gsungs nas dgyes tshor chen po gnang/ dgung grangs nga drug pa lcags yos lor rigs sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs gtso bor gyur pa'i snod ldan dmigs btus la bde mchog
lU nag dril gsum gyi chos skor yongs rdzogs kyi gtsos pa'i dbang lung bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig stsal lo/ /de ltar

khams gsum 'gro ba'i bla ma chen po mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug 'di nyid kyis thog mar yongs 'dzin rigs kyi bdag po yab mes rin po che?rin che po rnam gnyis/ byams pa
ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ ka spe bstan pa rab rgyas/ ngor mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bco brgyad pa mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang
lhun grub rnams las thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i dam pa'i chos kyi bang mdzod bzung nas/ ris med pa'i gdul bya'i skal bar 'tshams pa'i gsung ngag rin po che
tshar gsum gyis gtsos chos sgo dpag med phye bas/ thar pa'i lam sna zin pa brjod du mi lang zhing / bstan rgyun 'chad nyan nus pa'i zhal slob che gnyan rags rim gong gi skabs
so sor gsal ba bzhin dang / gsan don snying por dril ba'i rtsa ba gsum gyis ljags bsnyen bzhugs gdan thog gcig tu nyams bzhes mdzad tshul smos zin pa dang / nyams bzhed
nar mar yang tho rengs nas bzung nyin re bzhin gyi snga char/ sgrol dkar tshe sgrub/ lam bzang phyi nang / bir bsrung gnyis/ lam dus rgyas 'bring / rnal 'byor ma lus
dkyil bcas/ o rgyan bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bar gcod lam sel/ bde mchog nag po pa/ 'jigs byed/ brag rdzong ma/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ sgrol

ma maNDal bzhi pa/ thugs dam bskang gso/ ne gu chos drug seng gdong bsgom bzlas/ nang gi brag rdzong ma sogs rgyun gyi nyams bzhes rnams dang / gzhan yang bar skabs rnams su
lhag pa'i lha du ma zhig gi nyams bzhes skabs babs gnang ba ni brjod du mi langs pas kun rdzob snang ba dkyil 'khor gyi bdag po'i sku gsung thugs kyi rnal 'byor dang nam
yang 'bral ba med pa'i mthus bzung 'dzin spros pa'i chos kun dag pa ye shes kyi 'khor lor shar ba'i lkog gyur rjen par 'char ba sogs grub pa'i snang tshul ci rigs par bstan
pa las phyogs tsam gong du smos pa rnams kyis mtshon pa dang / bstan 'gror dge ba'i ljags rtsom gyi rim par yang 'jam mgon kun dga' bsod nams la gsol 'debs don gnyis
lhun grub/ yab rje rin po che la gsol 'debs dngos grub 'byung ba sogs gsol 'debs kyi rigs du ma dang / yab rje rin po che'i rnam thar byin rlabs me tog char 'bebs/ chag
med bzhi'i nyams len bya tshul/ srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i sgrub thabs bklags chog yid bzhin nor bu/ bstan pa gso chog sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i chog tshe sbyin yid bzhin
'khor lo'i sgrub thabs bsam 'phel don grub sogs tshe sgrub skor mang ba/ 'jam dkar sgrub thabs/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i

sgrub thabs/ de'i rgyun khyer sogs don bzang sdeb legs 'khyer bde phan pa lhur len lugs kyi bstan bcos kyang bka' 'bum glegs bam du gsal ba bzhin bskrun par mdzad pa sogs bstan
dang 'gro ba yongs la sman pa'i sku drin mtshon du med pa nas sku dngos kyi zhing 'di'i 'gro don rdzogs su nye ba na de lo zla ba bzhi pa tsam nas sku khams rim gyis
ltem bar gyur tshe/ sku rim snga gong nas rgyun mthud kyi mur tsha drag tu bsgrub cing / rje nyid nas lho nang phyag mdzod par yang de kha'i chings mtshams legs grub bstun
'gyang med yong dgos tshul gi bka' shog kyang bstsal ba bzhin phyag mdzod nas kyang rje nyid kyis 'phrin las grub ste ma 'gyangs par 'khor bstun/ slar yang sku rim sgo
gang zab la 'bad kyang ngo thon gang yang ma byung ba'i mur gro bzhin zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad nyin zhabs 'bring rnams la de ring de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'phel gdung zhig
dang rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi dam rdzas shig sbyor zhig gsungs/ phyir nyin nyi ma rgyang tsam song mtshams shig tu zhabs 'bring pa la nged kyi gdan 'di shar du bsgyur
cig gsung pa ltar zhus pas der spyan yun ring gzigs shing / slar yang phyogs gzhan gsum la yang de bzhin gnang rjes nged kyi rtsa 'dir mi bong che ba

zhig dang / gzhan yang mang po slebs byung gsungs/ yang gsung shub bu zhig gis ma hA kA la dang mkha' spyod ma bcas zhi khro'i lha tshogs rnams so/ /zhes kyang gsungs mur sngar
nyin dam rdzas sbyar ba de nas dum gcig bzhes te tshes bcu dgu'i nyin phyed yol bar rgyud sde rin po che nas ji ltar bstan pa'i 'da' ka ma'i rnal 'byor gsal 'debs par
mdzad de kun rdzob spros pa'i gzugs sku'i rnam pa de nyid/ don dam spros bral chos kyi sku 'pho 'gyur med pa'i dgongs par bsngu bar mdzad song 'phral sku 'khor thams cad
mya ngan gyi gdung ba drag pos so sor 'gyel zhing bub nas re zhig brgyal te dran pa rnyed 'phral mchi mas brnang bzhin du sku gdung mchod pa'i grabs gshom la zhugs pa'i
tshe/ gzugs sku bsdus pa las slar yang bzhengs te gsol ja zhig bzhes nas lung bstan 'ga' zhig bstsal rjes thugs rje chen po sems nyid ngal gso'i sku'i bzhugs stangs kyi
rnam pas sprul snang de nyid chos dbyings su thim tshul mdzad par/ sku tshe'i ring nas mnyam rjes 'khor yug gi dgongs pas 'od gsal ma bu 'dres bzhin pa las lhag tu skabs
'dir ting nge 'dzin la 'jug cing ldang ba med pas de ma thag tu dbu'i gtsug tor gsal por 'phags te mkha' spyod du gshegs pa las thugs dam du bzhugs

par ma gnang ba nas/ phyir nyin der sku gdung rin po che la rdo rje 'dzin pa du mas lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang rjes su mthun par mchod 'bul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhus
shing / nyer gcig nyin dri bzang po'i shing gi za ma tog tu sku gdung rin po che chas gzhug phyag len rnam par dag pa'i lugs su gsol nas gzim chung ka bzhi mar mchod sprin
gyi dbus su spyan drangs te bzhugs su gsol nas chos sde lho byang gi rdo rje 'dzin pa bsnyen song rags bsdus kyi mchod 'bul rgyun mi chad pa dang / gtsug lag khang rnams
su snyan shal gser chab dkar me rgya chen po dang / 'dus tshogs shin tu mang bar mang ja dngos 'gyed blos mi 'khyud ba bcas bsgrub cing / de mtshams sku gdung rin po che
dgyes pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i zhugs sbyong phul bar/ gdung la zhugs rang bzhes lta bus yud kyis zhu zhing / spur khang 'ja' dkar pos bskor ba dang / me
lce yang rtsa ba pad 'dab lartse mo bkra shis rtags kyi rnam pa sogs su 'bar ba dang nam mkha' la 'ja' tshon gyi bla bre dang me tog gi char sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dpag
tu med pa byung / gdung khang la zhag gsum rgyas btab pa'i ring gdung khang gi shar lho'i phyogs der me lce 'dzub mo tsam nyug nyug pa zhig rgyun

du bsdad thar khag gsum gyi mtshan mo gdung khang nas du ba'i rnam pa cher thon pa ni mi ma yin rnams kyis gdung skal mchod pa'i rten du gdan drangs tshod du 'dug cing / de
mtshams gdung khang zhal phye bas/ dbu thod ril por byon pa dang / rang byon rigs kyang du ma bzhugs pa gdung rus rnams so sor zhib par bsal te mchod sprin gyis dbus su
bzhugs/ dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi gung tshigs gsum pa'i thog/ chos sde lho byang gis gtsos rang zhabs nye skor dgon sde bcu gsum tsam kyi 'dus tshogs zhal grangs khri phrag
nye bar nyin bdun la snga dro 'bras 'jam dang mang ja bzhi ri'i thog/ 'bru 'gyed/ dngul 'gyed/ ja dar gos snam/ go khrab/ thabs spyad sogs rgya dpangs che ba kho na dang
/ thang ston chen mor sngar gyi steng du gser skya bgrang bar dka' ba la sngar rgyun gyi mchod sbyin dpag tu med pa rnams bsgrubs/ gzhan yang rgyal dbang rin po ches dbu
mdzad 'dreen mchog rnams la mchod bsngo rten dang / dbus gtsang gi chos sde ris med la bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa phul/ sku gdung rin po che mchod pa'i cha rkyen du
gzhung sa mchod yon nas kha Ta mthing khra drug gis sna drangs/ ral gri drug gis mtha' brten pa'i brgyad tshan gtos che ba drug sogs phyogs

mtha'i che gnyen dmangs phal nas kyang dgongs rdzogs zhal 'debs dpag tu med pa 'byor/ de nas rigs sras dam pa rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams dang bcas pas gdung rus gtsang mar sbyangs
btul la byin rten dpag med pa dang lhan cig pa'i 'jim pa las rje de nyid kyi sku brnyan gyi gtsos pa'i rgyal ba sras bcas kyi satstsha shin tu mang ba rnams la gser zho
sum cu ljib gsol la/ gdung rten rnam rgyal mchod rten phal thog bzhi lhag gi bum pa bum gdan bang rim rnam dngul ljang brdungs la de lhag gser zangs las bsgrubs pa'i bzo
bkod khra rgyan gangs can 'di na 'gran zla med pa lta bus ngo mtshar can gyi bum sgor gser zangs las rje de nyid kyi 'dra sku skum khru gang pa dang / gzhan yang gser
zangs kyi sku tshab 'dra sku/ de dag gi bzo phud gser zangs kyi rin chen 'byung ldan gyi sku 'dom phyed tsam pa rnams dang / phyi rten bde gshegs mchod rten gong mtshungs
phal thog brgyad sleb bre man chad gnas chen du ma'i sa sna rdo sna sogasakyi rgyu dang / gdug 'degs yan chad gser zangs las bsgrubs pa de rnams kyis nang bzhugs sangs rgyas
kyi ring bsrel dang gong gi gdung tshas gtsos pa'i gzungs 'bul byin rten so so'i dkar chag tu gsal ba bzhin gzhugs par rgyud sde kun la mnga' dbang

'byor pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa du mas rab tu gnas pas byin rlabs kyi gzi byin 'bar bar bsgrubs par mdzad do/ /de ltar sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa rgyas sras sems
dpa' chen po dmur rgod 'dul dka'i dpa' bo 'di nyid ni mkhas grub kun gyi rtse mor son pas rnams thar ngo mtshar dpag yas mchis mod kyang / mdzod 'dzin pa nam mkha' bsam 'grub
dang/ shes rab ngag dbang gnyis kyis rje 'di'i rtogs brjod pod longs brtsams rung brjod bya zab cing rgya che ba/ rjod byed tshig nyog gi chud zos su btang zhing chad
lhag mang bas bla ma'i zhabs tog dang mkhas pa dgyes pa'i legs bshad du mi rung mod/ bdag sogs gnas dus kyi skal ba rnams la zin thor rung tsam mchis pa nas/ 'dir nyung
ngur bsdus shing zhib pa ni kho bos gsol btab kyi ngor mus chen grub pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams dpal bzang gi gsung rtsom gnang ba zhig yod kyang zhu dag nan chen dgos 'dug
pas slad nas grub dbang nyid dang mkhas grub gzhan gyi zhu dag par mdzad pa de las rtogs par bya'o/ /

ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen/yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag rgyal sras sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de nyid kyi sras bdag gi drin chen rtsa ba'i bla
ma dam pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang bdud kyi stobs 'phrog ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan gyi
dge legs srid zhi'i gdung sel du 'phro pa de nyid ni/ yab rje mangga'i mtshan can de nyid dgung lo sum bcu pa shing glang khrum zla'i nang yab rje 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
dbang phyug gshegs nas ring por ma lon par mnal ltas su yab rje dam pa bsod nams dbang phyug de nyid byon nas lung bstan mtha' yas bstsal ba zhig shar ba'i tshe rje de
nyid kyi gsol 'debs zhal gsung ma/ rgyal ba gnyis pa sho lo ka gcig sngon 'gro'i rigs brgya'i khyab bdag sogs sho lo ka drug gsung rtsom gyi gdung shugs drag po mdzad pa'i
mthu dang / grub dbang de nyid kyis thugs bskyed rmad du byung ba bcas gdung sras su 'byon nges pa'i mtshan

ma shar ba bzhin lcam sne'u gdong ma bkra shis dbang mo dang bcas byas 'gyur sgrub sder me stag rta zla'i bco lnga nas bzung rgyang tsam 'brum yol la bzhugs skabs mtshan stas
su yab rje de nyid re zhig byas 'gyur du bzhugs rgyu lta bus dges spro chen po mdzad pa zhig gsal ba dang / de skabs ka spe chos rje ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas kyi
mnal ltas su'ang 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug shin tu gsal bar gang nas phebs/ gang du phebs rgyu yin zhu bar mdzad pa'i lan du sngar 'di phyogs su bsdad da byas 'gyur
la 'gro/ de nas 'di la rag las gsungs te phyag dpung g.yas la skud pa zhig btags par phyag 'dzub btsugs pa'i mnal ltas shar ba sogs grub dbang de nyid kyi sprul sku phebs
pa'i mtshan ma shar zhing byas 'gyur du bzhugs ring da lta'i sgrub chu khyad par can 'di gsar 'don gnang skabs/ zhabs phyi rnams nas gang yin dogs gcod zhus par mchil
ma zhig skyur shul du byung ba yin nam gang ltar der dar cog zhig btsugs na legs phebs kyang / spyi sger bstan 'gro'i gegs dbang gi zom lus su gyur pas chu 'babs rgyu ma
byung bar 'khyag pa tsam lus pa ni/ lcam bkra shis dbang mor gdung phebs bzhed gegs dbang rten 'brel gyi phebs ma thub kyang ma 'ong pa na rgyun ma chad tsam

gyi snga ltas shar ba bzhin slar yang dgung lo so gnyis par chos rje bco brgyad pa'i lcam bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo khab tu bzhes tshul ni bco brgyad chen mo mkhyen rab
byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyi rnam thar zhal gsung ma shel dkar phreng ba las/ me yos lor/ gdan sa chen po nas sne gdong gi lcam la gdung ma phebs pas/ khams gsum chos
kyi rgyal po'i bslab don bcas phyag mdzod bsod nams rgyal mtshan lha sar phyag dbang dang sdong nas phebs/ bco brgyad du 'bog gong la byon pa'i lcam gyi mched bstan 'dzin
zer ba zhig yod 'dug pas de kha sa skyar bzhes na ji ltar legs kyi snyan 'bul mdzad 'dug par gzhung sa nas de kha legs tshul gyi bslab don bka' drin bskyang 'dug pa
dang / phran bur yang grub mtha' sogs gang ci nas babs 'brel shin tu che bas 'phral 'bul dgos tshul gyii bka' shog rin po che phebs/ 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' shog
phyag mdzod rang gi sa skya nas gsung ba drag babs tshul gang spyi'i bslab don zhib pa gser srang gang chibs gsar ma legs pas gtsos gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba bcas gzim
dpon nam mkha' bsam grub dang mi nyag dbon po nyis sbrel sku tshab gdong nas lcam 'bul dgos tshul gyi bslab don gnang byung bar/

nged rang tsho sa skya pa'i gdung phebs par shin tu dung ba dang / bslab don phebs phyin bka' dang blang zhu ba gzhir bcas zhus nas/ sku tshab phyir slog dang lan 'debs phul
bas zhag shas nas sa skya phyag mdzod rgyun gyi dbang por phebs/ bzhugs sa sgrub sder mdzad/ nyin re bzhin bla brang du phebs nas gsung gleng zhib rgyas dang / nang mjal
sogs zhib par mdzad/ gzhis len rgyas pa zhus/ nged kyis gzhis su phyin/ phyi nyin phyag mdzod dpon g.yog phebs bsur gzhis khar phebs/ gzhis len dang tshan grangs rgyas
par gnang / ma nas lcam 'di dkyus ma zhig min 'dug pas/ mgon po mjal ba na snyan dar babs pa zhal khebs ma gsal ba phye ba sogs lo phyi nang du ltas ya mtshan pa byung 'dug
cing / nged rang la yang rmi ltas su nyi ma shar ba/ dar po che btsugs pa/ chu bo 'babs pa sogs legs pa byung / gza' tshes legs par gzhis nas gdan sar skya ser du ma dang
bcas rdzong bda' zhus/ zhes gsungs pa bzhin ma 'ong ba na bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid phebs pa'i dge mtshan gsal yang thog mar gdung sras gnyis byon pa ma bzhugs
pas dus ngan ci 'dra zhig mthong 'ong ngam zhes spyi sger skye 'gro rnams smre sngags sgrog pa'i tshe lha bla ma mo rtsis sogs kyi

lung babs sku rim rnams rgya che rgyun 'khyongs su mdzad pa'i byiin rlabs dang / khyad par bskal bzang sangs rgyas rnams kyi nang nas bdag cag gi ston pa dmu rgod 'gro la rjes
su brtse ba ltar/ dam pa de nyid nas lnga bdo'i mthar thug 'di ka gdul bya'i zhing du gzigs te/ sngar gyi mtshan ltas bzhin grub dbang I shA ra'i mtshan can de nyid slar
yang dpal sa skya'i gdung du bsam bzhin srid pa 'dzin par bzhed de sngags 'chang dam pa'i mtshan can dgung grangs bzhi bcur phebs skabs lho rong du zing bun gyi 'jug
phag tsan mi rta sprod bzhes la zla ba phyed gnyis tsam bzhugs mgor dus lan gcig mnal ltas su yab rje bsod nams dbang phyug gi phyag nas nor bu kha dog sna tshogs pa rje
nyid la gnang ste dgyes nyams kyi gsungs las/ nged kyii rnam thar de shin tu legs po byung 'dug ngo mtshar che ba'i nang nas rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog de ngo mtshar che ba
yod gsungs pa zhig shar ba dang / yang zhe bzhir phebs pa'i lo chu stod zla nang chos gra lho byang sogs la gsang 'dus dbang gnang skabs mnal ltas su yab rje bsod nams dbang
phyug gis deng sang zhabs drung ci mdzad kyin yod gsungs par bdag deng gsang 'dus kyi dbang byed skabs lags gsungs pas/ de shin tu legs 'on kyang snyigs dus

'dir chos sgrub pa la bar gcod che yang khyed rang gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rjes rjes su bzung bas mkha' 'gro sde lngas 'bral med gegs dang bar gcod srung bar 'dug pas skyon mi
'byung / da dung chos 'chad pa la rem mdzod gsung nas / gos ljang khu la dril ba'i bse sgam zhig gi nang shel bum nor bu'i kha rgyan can zhig gi kha rgyan mtshams nas bdud
rtsi chil chil lud pa zhig gnang byung bas/ bdud rtsi de gsol bas ro mngar nyams dang mchog thun dngos grub thob pa yin snyam pa'i thugs la bde spro dpag tu med pa zhig
byung ba shar ba 'di dag la bsam na mnal ltas sngon ma nor bu gnang shing rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog ngo mtshar gsung pa de nor bu lta bus gdung byon nas rgyal mtshan lta
bus ngo mtshar 'byung gsung rgyu dang phyi ma nyid kyi sras la chos bka' du ma gnang thub cing phrin las sna tshogs 'grub pa dang dbang gi chu rgyun mi nub cing bdud rtsi
gsol bas ro mngar dang bde spro'i thugs nyams gdung 'byon pa'i ltas 'khrul pa med do/ /rgyu mtshan de'i phyir/ rgyal yum dam pa bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo'am/ bstan
'dzin bu khrid du grags pa la thog mar zhal du med pa'i yon tan du ma la dbang 'byor ba rje btsun kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma de nyid 'khrungs shing / de nas

bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid 'byon pa'i snga ltas su skabs shig yum gyi mtshan ltas la/ dza lung rig 'dzin chen po de nyid yin snyam pa zhig gis dar sna tshogs kyis
dril ba'i lcags kyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa 'od 'tsher ba zhig dang / dam rdzas las grub pa'i gu ru padma'i sku zhig gnang ste/ 'di gong ma rin po che'i skyes su bstsal ba
yin pas thugs bcag gang dag mdzod gsung ba dang / yar lan gcig mnal stas su dpal rtse zhabs drung kun dga' bkra shis de yin snyam pa zhig gis rdo smug po'i spar bu dam rdzas
kyi gang ba zhig grangs ji tsam yod ltos gsung ba bzhin bgrang pas sum cu brgal tsam bgrang zin pa na/ mnal bsad pa ni snyigs dus dmu rgod gdul bya'i dbang gis dgung
grangs de tsam las mi bzhugs pa'i mtshan ma dang / yang lan gcig zhabs drung de yin snyam pa zhig gis byas 'gyur pu tra sbab len ma'i brag seng nas lcags rdor rtse lnga
dang lcags phur phur dar la dpal mgon zhal bzhi bris pa zhig gnang ste/ rigs 'dzin pho brang rang du bzhugs la sku rim 'di rnams nges par mdzad dgos yod do/ /zhes sku rim
