gyi brda' sbyor zhig byung yod tshod 'dug kyang de skabs kyi zin bris dang rgyus yod kyi mi med pas ji bzhin ma rtogs/ yang lan cig 'phan yul du bud med mang po dang 'grogs
nas byon te/

chu bo ri'i gru yin snyam pa zhig la mi mang po yum nyid kyis sgrol 'don mdzad pas chu'i pha rol ri sgang zhig nas shes la rang byon spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal gyi sku zhig
rnyed pa thugs tshags mdzad pa'i gnang ba byung ba sogs mnal ltas ngo mtshar can du ma dang / dngos su'ang sku lus yangs shing byams snying rje byang chub kyi sems dang
ting nge 'dzin khyad par can thug sa rgyud la 'khrungs pa byung yod 'dug cing / yang snye thang dge slong kun dga' bstan 'dzin zhes 'dar pa paNDi ta sogs mkhas grub du
ma'i slob ma rig gnas la mkhas shing 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug gi thugs rtsis can rje btsun mkha' spyod dbang mor thugs dam snying por mdzad pa des gdung sras myur
'byon sku rim mnal ltas dang bstun par gu ru rin po che'i phyag na rdo rje'i rnam sprul 'byon pa la the tshom med gsungs pa dang / bla ma dkon mchog rgyal pos rje 'di
la rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang 'bul skabs rje 'di'i gsung 'phros kyi zur zhig la/ slon dpon padma nga rang yin zhes thogs med kyis stsal ba dang / gong dkar mkhas grub dam
pa blo gros dbang phyug gi mtshan ltas su/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo'i rnam sprul yin pa shin tu gsal bas drung yig kun dga' sangs rgyas la de'i gnas tshul

gsung ba dang bcas/ rang re rnams nas zhabs phyi tshul bzhin byung na/ ngan song du mi skye ba'i khag theg zhes gsung 'dug pa dang / yang yol mo sprul sku rin po che bstan
'dzin nor bus a mes zhabs la lung bstan phul ba de'i gsham na/ sku tshe 'di la mdzad pa mi rdzogs pas/ /da dung skye srid gnyis ni nges par 'dzin/ /zhes 'byung ba'i dang
po rtse gdong zhabs drung kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin yin tshul dang / gnyis pa bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid yin tshul gong kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin gyi
rnam thar du bshad pa ltar dang / yang lce rigs rje btsun dam pa mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub zhes snyigs dus mkhas grub 'gran bral de nyid kyi rnam sprul 'khrul
med yin pa ni bco brgyad chen mo de nyid kyi rnam thar shel dkar phreng bar/ lcags lugs lo sa skyar phebs skabs kyi 'phros las/ bstan srung rgya mtsho'i bzhugs gnas kha'u
brag rdzong mjal bar phyin/ spyan gzigs snyan dar phul bskang ba rgyas par byas skabs sgra chen po zhig dang lhan du/ dpal mgon bram gzugs sku mdog mthing nag ral pa'i
thor gtsug can rgyan phyag mtshan sogs zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs ltar drag shugs mi zad pa dang ldan pa zhig zhal

mngon sum du bstan pa'i tshe/ sems thog mar 'jigs zhum pa dang / de nas bde ba dang ldan pa zhig byung zhes dang / yang de nyid las sa skyar rjes phebs kyi skabs nged rang
gi lcam gyi gzim chung du phyin phral yun du phan pa'i bslab bya byas shing / rten 'brel gyi stabs gzim chung gi sgo nang nas bzhugs zhus pa bzhin mdzad song / zhabs phyi
rnams kyi skyel ma sogs shin tu rgyas par gnang zhing / dar rgyas sogs chibs skyel ba mang tsam gyis la rtse'i bar skyel ma byas shing so sor ster cha byas/ dpal mgon gyi
bla rdor kha'ur mthong snang byung ba bzhin briis pa de lus shing char bab pa sogs ltas kyang legs snyam pa mang dag byung zhes dang yang de nyid kyi rnam thar smad cha
bskal ldan rna ba'i bdud rtsi zhes bco brgyad tshogs gnyis rgya mtshos mdzad pa las zhing rje kha ma'i lo rgyus de gras su hor zla lnga pa'i tshes gcig gi nyin sprul pa'i
chos skyong dpon blon la slar lung bstan zhib tu zhus par che bas sngon gyi sku rim rnams bsgrub par gzhan dang mi 'dra ba byung 'dug sogs 'phral ltar snang la legs legs
'dra ba'i gsung 'ga' las 'di yong gi gsal kha mi 'dug gsung zhing chung bas da cha dbu thog tu rgyal mtshan dkar po zhig tshugs/ bzhugs gdan kyang mtho ru mthong gsung
ba/ chos skyong dpon blon gyi gsung de rigs nged

so skye rnams kyi rtogs par ma gyur gshis pha bla ma rigs kun bdag po nyid la rgyu mtshan rnams zhib tu zhus par zhal 'dzum mdangs dang bcas rgad pos kyang thegs pa yin 'dug
phebs pa phyis su bsam tshe de nas ring por ma lon par bla brang 'di nyid du sku tshe'i mdzad pa'i mtha' mar gyur cing / gdan sar dri med 'khon gyi gdung du sku bltams
te 'gro ba'i don rlabs po che spyod pa'i lung bstan du 'dug chos skyong gi lung bstan lan gnang mur/ de bzhin yin tshe gnangs nyin tshes gsum la bla brang steng du rgyal
mtshan dkar po zhig 'dzugs pa dang / nged kyi gdan la phying dkar dri ma med pa zhig gsar du thing / khyed rang gzim khang gong du thugs gsol rgyas pa zhig thongs shig phebs
byung ba ltar phyin te thugs gsol grub 'phral sku zhabs su bcar skabs nyin ltar dang mi 'dra ba'i sku zor yang la dgyed nyams gzhan las che ba zhig 'dug lo 'di dang sngon
mar bsam yas nas shing bya can dang rgyal po nyi ma'i 'od zer gnyis kyi lung bstan kha lta ngan pa phyag mtshan gas chag yod pa 'ba' zhig bskur ba sogs yang yang byung
ba bzlog cing sku rim 'dra sgrub na dang bskyed e yong gi re ba'i gtso bor chos rgyal dpon blon dang / gong gi chos skyong gnyis bcas

so sor snyan shal gser skyems tshogs 'khor sngon nas dgos tshul byung ba'i rta mdzo bskur te lung bstan zhu mi ched du brdzangs pa'i phyir phebs la chos skyong chen pos zhing
'di'i mdzad pa phal cher rdzogs pas 'di lo rang zhing 'dir bzhugs pa mi yong kyang / slad nas bstan pa la phan thogs yong zhes gsungs pa rdo rje'i gsung bla na ma mchis
par 'dug zhes 'byung ba ltar/ rgyal mtshan dkar po 'dzugs pa sku tshe phyi mar lngags 'chang gos dkar can du 'khrungs par shin tu gsal ba ste rab byung la ngur smrig gi
rgyal mtshan 'dzin par grags pas rtogs nus shing / phying gdan dkar por mdzad pa myur du 'khrungs rtags dang / slad nas bstan par phan thogs yong ba'i lung bstan kyang don
la gnas/ gang ltar chu lug lo snron zla'i gnam gang gting mar dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim tshul bstan/ de nas ma 'gyangs par gang gi dbon ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab
brtan gyi tshe yi dngos grub stsol mdzad bde ldan mgon zhes sogs zhabs brtan sho lo ka gsum po 'di bka' rtsom mdzad byang las zhes zhabs brtan tshigs bcad 'di yang tshe
rab du mar dpal ldan bla ma nyid kyi sku drin gyi 'tsho ba'i lha btsun ngag dbang mkhyen brtses sug bris su rgyun gyi dbang po nas gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab ste phul ba
dge

legs 'phel bar gyur cig zhes gsungs rtsom mdzad/ sa skyar bang mi ched gnang gi gsung shog tu/ bstan 'dzin bu khrid la sras phebs pa yod pas de bar thum bu 'di kha ma phye
zhig zhes pa'i gnang rten dang bcas bstsal/ gang ltar de nas yab rje dgung grangs lnga bcu bzhes shing / yum so gsum pa sa skyong zhes pa shing mo bya lo cho 'phrul rta zla'i
tshes bcu/ res gza' bkra shis dang skar ma ri dgas mgo 'dzoms pa'i stobs ldan bkra shis kyi sbyor ba shar ba'i mtho rang sprul pa'i lha khang chen mo'i zur lcog rig
'dzin pho brang du bde chen chos dbyings kyi lhums las gzugs sku'i nyin byed shar nye ba na/ gzim chung phu mda' thams cad dri bzang gi gang ba der yod kun gyis rtogs shing
/ tshoms chen du chos skyong gi sprul pa lta bus bya rog babs pa dang yum gyi gzigs snang la 'od zer sna tshogs khrod nas bum med mdog mi 'dra ba du ma dang / mi nag a
tsa ra sogs shar zhing / dkar dung sgrigs pa'i skad mang po gsan pa dang bcas zhabs gnyis sngon phebs kyis sku bltams pa de bzhin gyi gsan tshul phyis yab rje rdo rje 'chang
gi gsan pa na/ sngon rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan yang tshul 'di lta bus sgo nas sku bltams pa yin gsung zhing / de nyin nam mkha' 'ja' 'od kyis gang ba dang /

me tog gi char 'babs pa sogs dge mtshan du mas snod bcud thams cad la byin chags pa ltar gyur to/ /de skabs 'khrungs ston gtang rag sogs dang sku gnang gces stabs gsang rgya
sogs mdzad tshul lo rgyus 'ga' re yod 'gro yang zin bris ma mthong zhing / yab rje mchog nas tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs 'bul bar mdzad cing / sku rim spyi dang khyad par
dus mdos zab ma gegs med mthar phyiin / de nas rim gyis zhabs gom phebs tsam du gyur pa'i skabs zhig pho brang gi steng la sku rkyang du phebs pa na bya rog gnyis kyis
na bza'i sne mo nas bzung ste zhabs 'bring pa'i tshul byed/ yang sku rkyang du bzhugs skabs shig 'tsho byed bsod nams dbang phyug gi zhabs phyir phyin pas/ gzims sgo mnan
pa lta bus ma phye bar sgo 'gram du bsdad pas gsung gleng dar dir mu nas shog phebs pa bzhin/ phyin te sku drung na su yod lags zhus pas rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi bris
sku de la spyan cher gzigs pas/ 'tsho byed bsod dbang gi bsam par rje nyid la stobs kyi mgon po dngos su gyur nas zab dgu'i gdams ngag stsol ba zhig yin nam snyam pa shar/
yang yum gyi zhal sta ma zhig gis mthong snang la/ sras kyi dbu sngas mgor mon phrug gsum gral bsgrigs pa mthong bas/ yum la

sras kyi dbu sngas mgo na pu tra lcam sring phebs 'dug zhus pas/ mon phrug gcig gis gang yang ma zer zhes pa'i lag brda byed pa sogs chos srung spyi dang khyad par las mkhan
chen po nyid skad cig kyang mi 'bral ba'i mtshan ma shar/ de nas 'dri klog sogs gsan bzhes ran pa na brgya dpon bsod nams bsam 'phel gyi sku mched gnyis kar yi ge'i ma
mo chos spyod sogs rim bzhin zhi drag du mas phul bas rgyun bar slob dpon la 'jigs tshul gnang yang skabs shig chu tshan la byon dus lcam sring gnyis nas 'bral mi phod pa'i
tshul gyi spyan chab kyang bsil ba byung zhes grags/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang la snga phyir gsung gi bdud rtsi gsol ba rnams 'dir phyogs gcig tu bkod na thogamar grub chen
dze tA ri'i lugs mgon po tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang / rje btsun sgro dkar gyi rjes gnang / bla ma zhi khro'i tshe dbang rnams dang / yang smin byed dbang gi skor la/
kyai rdor man ngag lugs yab bka' yum bka' rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor steng nas dbang / gsung ngag rin po che las 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i tshogs bshad smin 'khrid/ slob
bshad lung 'khrid de'i gdam pa yongs su rdzogs pa las tshogs bshad snang gsum dang 'brel ba'i lung gi rnam grangs la/ lam 'bras phyag mchod/ brgyud 'debs gnas

sbyar ma kha skong bcas/ bla ma rgya bod kyi rnam thar/ rje btsun gong ma lnga/ tshogs nyan/ dkar brag zhang brag bla ma dam pa/ ri khrod pa/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen ye rgyal/
budha shI/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ rgyal tshab/ kun mkhyen/ yongs 'dzin/ rje sangs rin/ sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ bdag chen/ rdo rings pa/ sngags 'chang chen po/ tshar
chen lam glu/ rta ra ba/ ngag dbang chos grags/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon bcas kyi rnam thar dang / gsung ngag khog phug legs bshad 'dus pa'i rgya mtsho/ gsung ngag byon
tshul gsung ngag rin po che bstan pa'i pad tshal bzhad pa/ lung khrid gsung ngag slob bshad snang gsum 'khrid yig zla ba bdud rtsi'i thig phreng / bla chen 'brog ma'i
rnam thar brda' grol bka' rgya ma/ bla ma lnga bcu pa/ 'grel pa rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa/ snang gsum mdzes rgyan/ snang gsum snying po/ brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi sems
bskyed chen mo/ rgyal sras lam bzang gi lung / slob ma rjes 'dzin/ mngon par rtogs pa bdun nam brgyad dang ldan pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba/ rtsa sngags aShTa'i bzlas
lung / lam dus kyi dbang / yi ge brgya pa'i bzlas lung / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i sindha ra'i byin rlabs/ lam zab phyi nang /

bir bsrung mthun mong dang mthun mong ma yin pa/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sindhu ra'i byin rlabs/ tshar gsum khug pa/ bla ma rin 'byung / brda' don gsal ba/ brda'
chig brgyud/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ lam sbas shad/ mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang / dngos gzhi 'khor 'das dbyer med kyis lta ba/ dbang bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i lam bskyed rim
phyi nang gtum mo pho nya rba rlabs mda' kha ma/ 'bras bu sku lnga mngon du 'gyur ba'i tshul/ de rnams kyi rgyab rten lam 'bras glegs bam pod ser pod dmar pod nag/rgyud
gsum mdzes rgyan/ kyai rdor bskyed rim/ rnam bshad nyams rtogs gong 'phel/ gsung ngag slob bshad sngags lam gyi 'khrid yig nye gzhon gsar pa'i thig phreng / rgyud gsum snying
po'i legs bshad/ dam tshig rnam bshad/ lam sbas bshad kyi zin bris/ slob ma zin bris bya tshul/ aShTa'i bzlas lung / brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ tshar gsum
khug pa/ bdag med ma'i byin rlabs/ lam zab phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung / bir bsrung gnyis kyi byin rlabs/ brda' don gsal ba/ lam sbas bshad/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ mgon
rkyang gi rjes gnang yi ge gnyis las gsum byung gi go don/ lam dbang mtha' bcad rnams

mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ bir bsrung phyi ma'i yi ge sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/ bir bsrung mthun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge lam zab nang ma'i yi ge
kyai rdo rje'i bskyed rim bshad pa zab don gnad kyi gsung bgros dang / lus dkyil gyi rnam bshad bde chen bcud kyi snying po/ kyai rdor bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad blo gsal
bde 'jug rnams kyi lung / lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi 'khrid/ sgrub pa lung sbyiin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas btab/ gur mgon lha brgyad/ dzam ser nag rnam kyi rjes gnang / yang
phur ras bris kyi dbang / yang phur man ngag a ti glegs bam gyi lung / gu ru brag dmar gyi dbang / sgrub thabs rgya rgyam gyi rjes gnang rgya gzhung bod gzhung gi lung
bcas sgrol ma nyer cig 'byung 'dul/ zhal bzhi bsnyen dus/ mgon po khro bcu/ dur khrod bdag po/ dkar bdud lcam dral/ grub rgyal tshe dbang / blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral
gyi nyams 'khrid/ de'i yig cha kha shas dang / 'jam dpal mtshan brjood/ rtsa brgyud brtag gnyis/ tshe mdo/ sher snying / rdor gcod/ smon lam rnam gsum/ byams pa'i dam bcas
pa'i gzung / spyod 'jug rje dgon pa ba'i bstod pa yon tan mchog mnga' ma sogs bstod pa du ma/ phar tshad brgyud 'debs/ nA ro mkha'

spyod kyi brgyud 'debs rgyal ba rgya mtsho rnams kyi lung / yang dpal 'khoor lo bde mchog lu nag dril gsum gyis ras bris dang lus dkyil du dbang bskur ba/ nag po lugs kyi 'khor
lo sdom pa'i bskyed rim gyis bshad pa shin tu zhib pa dang sems 'dzin gyi 'khrid/ rdzogs rim zab mo nag po rim bzhi dang / dpyid thig gi khrid/ de dag gi rgyab rten
bde mchog nyung ngu/ nag po gzhung drug sa chen gyi nag po mngon rtogs/ nag po dkyil chog lu nag dril gsum gyi sgrub thabs kyi rnam bshad rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i bstan pa
rgyas pa'i nyin byed/ nag po gzhung drug gi tho yig gam Tikka sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ chos byung bde mchog chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed/ sa lo/ sngags 'chang gnyis kyis mdzad
pa'i nag po sgrub dkyil lhan gcig sdebs pa gsar bu'i blo chen 'jug bde/ dril bu lugs kyi lus dkyil gyi bshad pa shiin tu mtha' chod pa dang sems 'dzin gyi 'khrid zab
mo/ dril bu rim lnga'i sngon 'gro'i byin rlabs/ lu hi pa'i smad lngar grags pa rnams dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi khrid/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i be bum/ gur mgon lcam dral
gyi bskang ba nag po mchod rten/ chos nyi ma/ bstan srung spyi bskang cho ga dngos grub rgya mtsho/ sku dang gsung thugs ma/ gtum chen ma/ lha mo'i bskang ba dngos

grub rol mtsho/ zhal gyi bskang ba lha mchog ma dang stobs 'phrog ma/ dmag zor bstod bskul 'phris myur sgrub/ dur khrod bdag po'i bskang bshags bzlog bskul bstod pa dang bcas
pa 'phrin las mkha' khyab/ pu tra'i sgos bskang / dkar bdud bskang ba rgyas bsdus/ chos skyong rnams la bskang ba 'phrin bcol rig 'dzin mur 'byon/ bdud rtsi lnga mchod
kyi lung sogs smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa du ma gsan pa las/ gsung ngag gsan dus dgung grangs lnga pa yin 'dug kyang nyin gcig gsung las/ snang ba gsum gyi lam gyi gzhi
byas te/ /nyams blang ma lus rgyud gsum dag gi shes/ /zhes thol byung du phebs/ de dus rgyu dbang sta gon skabs mus gling kha nas gsung ngag pod ser ma/ ngag dbang chos
grags kyis mdzad pa'i snang rgyud 'khrid yig khog phub rnam bshad/ byin rlabs cha lag bcas pa/ dbang chog rjes gnang sna tshogs/ ni gu'i chos skor bcas pu ti bzhi yab rjer
'bul mi byung ba dang / rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor yang je cher gyur pa sogs spyir rten 'brel legs shing / bye brag sprul pa'i dal du rgyu dbang gsan pa lta bu byung
/ gzhan yang 'khor lo bde mchog gi bka' zab mo gsan dus/ nyin gcig glo bur du rlung 'tshub chen po zhig gi 'tshub mas

gzim chung khengs par dam pa nyis nas/ yab rje mchog la/ dur khrod bdag po dang mi nag mang po slebs byung zhes gsung zhing/ gzhan yang yab rje'i gsung las/ sngags 'chang chen
po de nyid la dpal mgon zhal pu tra dmar nag 'dod khams ma bcas kyi phrin las rtsol med du sgrub cing mngon spyod kyi las sogs la nus pa che ba yong zhes phebs/ yang
skabs shig yab rje mchog nas phun tshogs gling du sku mched gnyis la mnyes spro sogs nyin gang lta bus sku mdun du rgyun ring bzhugs nas slar rigs 'dzin pho brang la phebs
khar thub pa dgongs gsal gyi glegs bam dang / sgar sbug khyad mtshar chung ngu de gnang nas hur bskyed mdzad dgos kyi bka' phebs pas thugs phreng po byung zhes rje de nyid
rang gi gsung las dngos su thos/ de nas dgung grangs bdun du phebs pa lcags yos lor yab rje rdo rje 'chang zhing khams gzhan du phebs nye'i skabs mchod dpon dkon mchog
rgyal po la spyan cher gzigs nas/ sngags 'chang chen po 'di nyid kyi sku tshe'i stod la 'o brgyal po yong bar 'dug pas kho bos 'bul ma thub pa'i chos 'phro rnams dkon mchog
rgyal pos phul zhes gsung nas spyan rig 'dzin pho brang phyogs la

gzigs shing sras la thugs phreng ba'i rnam pa mdzad de/ gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan/ lo rgyus 'di la bltas na yum sras rnams rig 'dzin pho brang nas yab
rje'i sku mdun la skabs re las yang yang mi 'byon zhing / yab rje'ang bka' chos gnang skabs ma gtogs yum sras kyi sar 'byon mi bde ba sogs sngon bod kyi chos rgyal rnams
sdig blon la 'dzems dgos ltar gzhan dbang sna tshogs yod tshod 'dug gang ltar dgongs rdzogs sogs yum sras rnams la sku dbang yod med ci ltar kyang byas byas mang po shes
rab ngag dbang gis brtsams pa'i mangga'i mtshan can gyi rnam thar na 'dug rung / don la ni yum sras rnams la 'o brgyal rang byung zhing mangga'i mtshan can gyi rje 'di'i
sku tshe'i stod la 'o brgyal yong gsung ba de yang bshad ma thag pa dang / 'og 'byong dus sogs yin 'dra/ re zhig nas gdan sa 'dis rten mchog rnams la mchod 'bul thog mjal
bar phebs pa'i thog mar lha mthil gtsug lag khang du phebs pa'i tshe de'i rten rnams gzigs mur grub dbang bsod nams dbang phyug gi 'dra sku ldebs bris ma zhig la ya gi
nga'i sku 'dra yin/ dar 'di bzhes 'gro gsung 'bul bar gnang bas sku des zhag du ma'i bar du bzhes/

yang sgo rum mjal bar phebs skabs/ bse mgon chen po'i drung gsung las/ 'di'i spyan gyi gsang thag nyams bzo byed skabs/ zla bo gzhan rnams gros nas ma byung zhes phebs pa/
sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos nyams bzo gnang dus sku 'di snga thog rang du song bas spyan gyi 'phrul sogs ji 'dra yod gzigs pas gsang thag rnams nur nur po'i stabs
ha cang gi 'grig pa ma byung tshe thag sgra shin tu che ba zhig byung bar/ sku 'khor rnams ha las te dra sgo'i phyir bros skabs/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gzigs snang la/
bse mgon chen po nyid kyi phyag gnyis dkrug cing thugs khar steng 'og sogs su ma bsgrigs rang 'grig tu byung ba'i skabs kyi mdzad bzang de la dgongs sam yang na 'jam dbyangs
bsod nams dbang po'i gnas bshad na'ang nyams bzo'i skabs dkon gnyer rin pa rnam pa 'jigs nas bros tshul sogs yod snyam pas sngags 'chang yab sras gang rung zhig tu
zhal gyi bzhes par mngon no/ /dgung grangs brgyad thog chu 'brug lor phur sgrub tshogs dbur phebs bzhed kyis phyag len rnams ban tshang dbu byed dkon mchog seng ge las bzhes
shing byang chub par mdzad/ sku zhang bco brgyad zhabs drung ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan sku

mched rnams nas phur sgrub rtsa 'chams kyi skabs legs 'bul phun tshogs rten 'brel sgrig par dgongs nas phebs te thog mar zhabs drung des 'dren pa dam pa lcam sring gnyis gtso
gyur gyi chos grwa lho byang gi dge 'dun phal cher la sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang sogs 'bul bar mdzad pa'i skabs shig bla ma de nyid kyis 'dren mchog dam pa 'di nyid
spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal dngos dang / yang rjes gnang zhig 'bul skabs phyag rdor dngos su gzigs/ de nas rim bzhin mgon khang steng 'og tu 'phrin bcol gnang skabs
skyed lhas dus brag sgo'i nang na dril chung gser kha'i skad mang po 'dug gsungs pa sogs ngo mtshar du ma byung yod tshod du 'dug de nas rim bzhin phur sgrub tshugs pa'i
sa skya tshogs su rtsa 'chams thog sku zhang mkhyen brtse dpon g.yog nas legs 'bul mdzad yod dam snyam/ bcu dgu'i nub bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po'i mtshan ltas su/ yab sras
dge 'dun 'khor tshogs kyi zhabs phyi bcas zhabs bskor la phebs rjes dbang khang smin grol bzhugs khrir bzhugs par mangga'i mtshan can nyid shin tu dges pa'i 'dzum mdangs
dang bcas gzigs nas/ dkon mchog rgyal po sdug bsngal byed mi dgos 'di ga rang yin gsung sras mchog dam pa la

thim nas dbyer med du gyur pa zhig byung gsungs pa ltar/ yab rje'i zhabs brtan ngag gi dbang phyug ma dang / phyogs las rnam rgyal ma gnyis gang gi yul nas sras kyi zhabs brtan
gsol 'debs su 'dzugs par mdzad/ phur sgrub skor gegs med du grub/ de skabs tsam la lcags zam grub dbon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs de nyid las snga phyir gsung
gi bdud rtsi gsol ba rnams phyogs gcig tu bkod na tshe dbang bla ma zhi khro mda' 'phel dang grub rgyal lugs/ bsam pa lhun grub kyi sgrub thabs tshom bu'i dkyil 'khor/
ku ru ku llelha lnga/ gso byed bdud rtsi bum chen/ mi 'khrugs pa zlum po bzhi dbang / gur mgon gri gug lha lnga lugs gnyis/ lha brgyad/ bcu gnyis/ bcu bdun/ rigs gsum spyi
dbang / kyai rdor mtsho skyes lugs/ nag po lugs/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor/ gshed mar lha lnga/ 'jigs byed ro lang brgyad skor rnams kyis dbang / rdo rje khyung khra'i thun
mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang bkru byab srung ba mtha' rten gtor dbang dang bcas pa/ sna tshogs yum/ rnam 'joms ba ri lugs/ phyag rdor u tsa/ seng gdong dmar mo/ sme brtsegs
dud kha/ rta mgrin shwa na bzhi bskor/ phag dkar/

shes rab gsal byed/ sgrol ma dmar po/ dzam dmar sa lugs/ dzam bha la dkar po/ rta mgrin skyer sgang / mgon po phyag drug phyag bzhi/ beng dmar/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ ri khrod
ma/ phyag rdor gtum po/ sme brtsegs ljang nag/ mi g.yo ba sngo dkar/ thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug dmag zor rgyal mo/ dur bdag dkar bdud/ sgrol ma tshe sbyin ma/ phyag
rdor 'gro bzang / rta mgrin dbyug tho can/ thugs rje chen po skyer sgang lugs/ rta mgrin lcags ral/ 'jam dbyangs smra seng / tshe dpag med dkar po/ gur mgon gtor dbang /
gur lcam dral lha gsum/ brgyad/ dgu/ bcu gnyis ma rnams dang sprin zhabs ma/ ber gcer/ pu tra/ bran bdud/ zhal bsnyen dus/ gsang sgrub/ las gzhi'i mgon po rnams dang / dud
sol thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ dmar chung bskor gsum/ tshogs bdag thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ khyad par dang bcas pa/ 'dod rgyal thun mong dang thun mong
ma yin pa/ rnam sras sprin gseb/ mdung dmar can gnyis/ rta sngon rnams kyi rjes gnang/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ grub dbon nyid kyi mdzad pa'i yig lung / sa skya'i
rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum la sa chen gyi gnyis/ rtse mo'i gsum/ rje

btsun gyi gsum/ sa paN gyi gsum/ 'phags pa'i bzhi rnams dang / byams chos sde lnga / rdo rje phur pa'i 'grel chen 'bum nag rnams kyi lung / yang ne gu'i chos skor la 'jug sgo
yon tan kun 'byung / bde mchog dbang bzhi'i lus bsgrigs/ chos drug gi sgos bka' so so/ phyag len ga'u ma'i byin rlabs/ bla ma yi dam lam khyer/ mkha' spyod dkar dmar/
mkha' spyod gsum phrugs/ lha bzhi dril sgrub rnams kyi byin rlabs/ 'khrid yig snying po kun 'dus kyi steng nas nyams khrid rgyab rten lung yongs su rdzogs pa/ sa skya pa'i
gser chos khyung pod/ yang gur mgon brag rdzong ma'i khrid phyi nang gsang gsum/ rtsa gsum 'khor lo bzhi la brten pa'i nang khrid/ gsang ba'i las sbyor spu gri so 'debs/
mgon dkar tshe 'khrid/ lung la mgon pod me 'bar ma/ snyan brgyud po ti glegs bam der bzhugs pa dang ma bzhugs pa/ sgo rum pa/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ bod mkhar ba/ rta
ra ba/ dbang phyug rab rtan/ ngag dbang chos grags/ kun dga' bsod nams/ grub dbon chen po nyid rnams kyis mdzad pa'i 'di'i skor gyi chos sna 'ga'i lung / yang stobs 'phrog
dbang po'i man ngag lus la gnad du snun pas rdo rje 'dzin pa'i go 'phang mngon du byed pa'i gsang 'khrid/ tshe

sgrub gur bdun ma'i nyams 'khrid lung la zhal pod yongs rdzogs dang / snying thig ha la'i be bum/ dud sol ma'i chos skor glegs bam yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / yang gter bdag
gling pa chen po'i gter gsar bla ma drag po dang / rig 'dzin thugs tig gi dbang lung beg tse 'khor mang gi rjes gnang / chos sna'i lung / nag po chen po rnam gnyis kyi
zab gnad mdud 'grol rin chen lde mig dang snying bcud zil mngar 'khor lo bri yig mthong ba don gsal dang snying gi khrag thig dmar po skor gsum gyi 'khor lo'i gsal byed dang
/ bka' gnad mdud 'grol/ rnas sras dbang drag gi be bum sogs du ma gsan no/ /bstan 'gro spyi sger gyi 'phel rgyas la dgongs 'dren mchog dam pa 'di nyid nas grub dbon chen
por chos gra lho byang gi dge 'dun rnams la gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad gnang dgos tshul phebs pa bzhin slob bshad zab mo cha lag dang bcas pa smin rgyas su stsal/
gzhan yang dam pa kha shas las gsan bzhes mdzad tshul 'ga' zhig 'dir brjod na/ yang chos gter gling pa ngag dbang kun bzang rang grol las 'chi med sku gsum rigs 'dus dang
/ zab lam thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho bde gshegs kun 'dus kyi skor sogs gsan no/ /yang rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po dkon

mchog rgyal po las bla ma zhi khro dang / lcags gdong ma'i tshe dbang rdo rje phreng ba/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje/ rdo rje phur pa'i smad las drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang/
phur pa'i brgyud 'debs/ sgrub thabs klags pas don grub/ dkyil mchog yid 'ong blo gros kha 'byed/ gter bzlog dgra bgegs kun 'dzoms kyi lhan thabs gnam lcags rdo rje'i
me dbal/ drug cu pa'i cho ga dgra bgegs gnad gcod kyi spu gri/ tshe sgrub gur bdun ma'i nyams len/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi'i drag po'i gtor chen bsam don lhun grub 'khrid brgya
rnams kyi lung dang/ g.yu thog snying thig gi skor sogs gsan/ yang grub dbang bsod nams chos 'phel las tshe dbang mda' 'phel dang grub rgyal lugs/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum
ma dang mgon po'i dbang chen lnga / dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ yang lung la dpal kye rdo rje'i chos skor gtso che'i chos sna sum cu rtsa dgur grags pa/
mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi bka' 'bum/ rgyas sras bka' 'bum/ blo sbyong legs bshad kun 'dus dang chig chod chen mo/ mgon pos me da'abar ma/ snyan brgyud glegs bam/
rdo rje brag rdzong ma bar chad kun sel/ rnam bshad zab don snyan brgyud rol mtsho/

gtor ma gsum gyi zhal shes/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i khyad par gyi lde kha'i zhal shes/ brag rdzong ma'i phyi rol rdzas kyi sbyor ba'i zhal shes/ nag po chen po'i gsang sgrub
kyi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i gsung bgros/ nag po chen po'i nang sgrub skabs kyi gnad kyi zin bris/ gtor ma'i gsad las/ dbang gi dngos grub sgrub pa/ bsnyen pa byed tshul
gyi yi ge thun mong ma yin pa/ gur gyi mgon po'i bsnyen pa'i zhal gdams/ mgon po'i dbang gii sbyin bsreg gi zhal shes/ drag po sngags rgod/ brag rdzong ma'i dam tshig
'khor lo'i zhal shes/ sngags pa nang rgyas/ dri chu la brten nas rims nad bsrung ba/ dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar/ 'khrid yig 'dod dgu'i dpal ster rnams dang / tshe sgrub
gur bdun ma/ nor lha dbyug gu mched gsum gyi man ngag gi yi ge sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams kyi mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / mkhas grub khyung po nas brgyud pa'i ne gu'i
be bum lung dang byin rlabs kha shas/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi 'khrid/ ra 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud sogs gsan no/ /yang stag rtse byams pa lha dbang
rig 'dzin las/ grub rgyal tshe dbang / mi 'khrugs lha dgu'i dbang / sgrol dkar rjes gnang dang khrid/ gnyan sgrol/ seng ge sgra/ tshe dpag

med dkar po/ rdo rje khyung khra/ phyag rdor gtum po/ dmag zor rgyal mo rnams kyi rjes gnang / rab gnas kyi cho ga dngos grub 'byung ba/ drug cu pa'i cho ga dgra bgegs gnad
gcod kyi spu gri/ gtor chen byang tshul/ mgon po'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sngags 'chang kun bsod kyi mdzad pa/ gza' bcos rje g.ya' bzang ba'i man ngag rnams kyi lung / ma gcig
mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi chos skor sogs gsan no/ /lo de'i nang du drung yig dbang phyug bkra shis mdzod par 'khod/ rje btsun kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi mas dges pa rdo
rje'i ljags bsnyen gnang ste dam rdzas 'chi med ril bu sgrub pa sogs bstan pa'i 'khur chen gang mtshams re zhig bzhes/ dgung grangs dgu tsam nas rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis
bde kyai gsang gsum sogs sgrub dkyil so so bla ma mchod tshogs sogs la thos bsam mthar phyin gyi sgo nas sgrub mchod sogs la slob dpon min pa'i tshogs dbur phebs/ dgu grangs
bcur phebs pa shing rta la chos grwa lho byang dge 'dun mang po la dge slong gi sdom pa 'bogs pa'i mthun rkyen bzang po bstsal te/ mkhan chen byams pa kun dga' bstan
'dzin gyis de bzhin dang len mdzad/ lo der lho bod shin tu gzar

ba'i chings sgrig tu mdzod pa rdzong bda' gnang ste mkha' 'gro chos srung la bka' bsgo phrin bcol drag tu stsal ba'i byin rlabs la brten zla ba bcu gcig tsam nas gtan chings
legs 'grig gi spyi bye brag skye 'gro rnams bde skyid kyi dpal dang ldan par gyur/ de nas rgyal sras lam bzang thugs 'dzin dges spro chen pos myur bar thugs mtshor gtams/
dkon mchog seng ges pu tra 'chams su grags pa'i phyag khrid phul/ de'i tshe la lar ma phul yang 'khrul med du mkhyen pa byung / dgung grangs bcu gnyis su phebs pa me spre
lo chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i chos kyi khrir zhabs zung bkod de rgyal tshab chen por mnga' gsol ba'i sngon 'gro dus rim zab spros che ba dang bcas tshugs/
nyer brgyad nyin pu tra chen po'i 'chams gral du phebs te/ lam 'gros nas bzung dgu rdung gi bar phyag bzhes su gnang bas kun ngo mtshar du gyur/ nyer dgur gtor zor 'phen/
gnam gang la bskang ba brgya tshar/ rta zla'i tshes gcig la gtang rag mnga' gsol dang gnam lo gsar tshes kyi dga' ston shin tu gzab par gnang / tshes gnyis nas bzhi'i
bar la phyogs nas khri ston legs 'bul ba rnams dang / sku 'khor rags bsdus dag la dga' ston rgya chen pos tshim par

mdzad/ tshes lnga'i nyin rtse la chos dung dkar po rgyang grags gsung bskul gyi/ gzhis byes/ dge 'dun khri phrag tsam du long pa dang / skye bo'i tshogs rnams chos grwar 'dus
'khod grub pa dang / chos khrims pa sogs las sne 'dzin pa'i spyan 'dren pa rnams dang / las mtshan bcu gsum gras sogs 'gro 'os rnams sngon 'gro'i bdag cag gi rnam 'dren
dam pa de nyid mtshan dpe'i gzi 'od 'bar zhing sngags 'chang mdzes brjid kyi rnam par bzhengs pa'i nye 'khor kun tu ser skya zhabs 'bring pa'i tshogs rang rang gi cha lugs
lhun chags shing bag dro ba dang bcas ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa skye dgu'i bsod nams kyi mgron du gdugs tshod la spyan drangs pa ltar bzhi thog pho brang chen mo nas
rim gyis snga srol bzang po'i lugs ltar phebs te/ bzhugs khri chen mor bzhugs grub 'phral ser skya tshogs chen gyi chos phyag mdo klog bdud bzlog maNDal sogs sngar gyi phyag
srol bzhin mdzad zin pa dang / sems bskyed gsal 'debs bstan chos rtsom pa po'i che ba'i yon tan gsung ba sngon 'gro'i rgyal sras lam bzang rgya skad nas rtsom bsam gtan
gyi phar phyin bshad pa yan chad nyin gnyis par sngar 'phros shes rab kyi phar phyin bshad pa nas/ sku gsum ye shes kyi rnam bzhag yan/ nyin gsum par sngar 'phros nas
bzung mjug

sbyar byang gi bar tshang la ma nor ba yongs su rdzogs pa dag gsal snyan pa'i dbyangs kyi legs par bstsal bas 'dus tshogs thams cad shin tu ya mtshan ngo mtshar gyi dpal la
bkod/ nyin gsum po de'i ring gsung chos kyi bar rnams la gsol ja'i thog legs skyes thog mar rgyal dbang rin poo che nas dgu tshan dgu/ shod nas dgu tshan lnga/ sku zhang
chos rje bco brgyad pa'i 'bul tshan nyer lnga/ 'od chog sprul sku rin po ches dgu tshan nyer gcig smin grol gling nas dgu tshan gsum/ rdo rje brag nas dgu tshan gsum/ bsam
yas chos skyong chen po'i dgu tshan bzhi/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan sogs dbus kyi dgon khag so so'i bla spyi sogs nas kyang 'bul dpangs rgya chen po dang / ngor e wam chos
ldan mkhan rin po che nas dgu tshan bzhi/ bdun tshan gcig ngor spyi so'i tshan grangs gsum/ bla brang khag rnams nas kyang dngos 'bul rgya chen po dang / thub bstan rnam
rgyal gyi mkhan po rin po che nas dgu tshan lnga/ grwa tshang nas kyang dngos 'bul rgya chen/ gzhis rtse rdzong dpon khrus phu nas sogs rdzong dpon gyi rigs mang po dang/
'dar bsam grub pa sogs sde dpon rigs/ drung 'khor/ gzhis rgan/ khyim bdag rang kha ba bcas so so nas kyang 'bul dngos shin tu gtsang ba/ rje btsun

a lce lags/ yum drung / mdzod pa dbang phyug bkra shis/ gnyer dpon/ gnas slob/ gsol gzim/ mchod dpon sogs sku 'khor ser mo ba'i rigs/ drung yig mgron gnyer/ gnyer tshang pa/
gzim 'gag pa/ rtswa shing gnyer pa sogs sku 'khor skya rigs rnams nas rang rang gi 'byor ba dang bstun pa'i chos yon/ chos grwa lho byang gi mkhan chen byams pa kun dga'
bstan 'dzin gyis dgu tshan lnga/ spyi pa nas dgu tshan bdun/ spyi chen/ las thog pa/ dbu chos/ ban tshang bsnyen song / sgrigs pa yan/ 'bul sdud bla ma gsar rnying / sku
gnyer so so/ sgrub sde gong 'og chos lhun bcas kyi bla grwa rnams dang / gzhan yang gzhis khag rnams kyi gnyer rgan bcu dmangs sogs ser skya drag zhan so so nas kyang rten
gsum gser dngul gos dar sogs rang la ji ltar mnga' ba rnams legs skyes su phul/ sngar srol ltar ngo mtshar ba'i rten bzhi'i thog drangs/ gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang
rnams su dkar me/ zhal zas/ spos/ bla bre/ 'phan/ snyan shal sogs kun bzang mchod sprin lta bu'i mchod 'bul bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / der bzhugs bla ma dge ba'i bshes
gnyen sogs la rnam bzhag dge 'dun 'dus pa'i tshogs gzhi grwa'i rigs la 'bru khal re dang / gzhan yang /

zhib mar thud rnams kyi 'gyed sogs bsnyen bkur gya nom pa dang / skye bo'i tshogs bgrangs las 'das pa rnams la mar 'bru/ tshwa sogs sbyin pa rgya chen bcas yab mes gong ma'i
khri ston rnams las kyang ches zab par gnang ba rnams 'khor gsum yongs dag gi gsung bsngo bla na med pa'i byang chub tu rgyas 'debs kyang rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid rang
nas bka' drin skyang rjes/ bla ma slob dpon dge 'dun 'dus tshogs dang bcas pas/ me tog gi char dang bcas bkra shis mnga' gsol gyi sgo nas/ mdzad 'phrin bzang po gegs med
lhun grub 'byung ba'i rten 'brel legs par bsgrigs pas bstan 'gro spyi sger la 'phral yun gyi phan bde nyi ma shar ba ltar gyur to/ /de nas dgung grangs bcu gsum du phebs
pa me bya lor ljongs 'di shin tu gzir ba byung tshe/ skye bo'i gleng brjod kyi rigs sna tshogs la rten/ yum dang mdzod pa sogs tab tob po'i rang bzhiin du gyur kyang/ rje
'di'i mchod dpon dkon mchog rgyal po la/ da lam rang re'i bstan srid sogs la skyon mi 'dug slob dpon bye ma a krong gi sku 'di'i thugs kha nas 'od zer gsal la 'tsher ba
zhig nged rang la shar ba'i tshe/ 'jigs skrag gang yang med cing / bde gsal mi rtog pa'i ngang nas lus bde cham 'gro

yin 'dug zhes phebs pa bzhin 'dar bsam grub par zhib dpyod mi 'ga' 'dir 'byor bar mjal phyag zhu ba ltar bcos nas sku mdun la bcar skabs gri ring rnams btags bzhin du 'ong
ste phyag sogs me byed kyang zhal mjal ba tsam gyi snang ba 'gyur te/ de 'phral phyir thon nas gri rnams dor dar dkar gyi phyag rten bcas phyag 'tshal zhing phyag dbang zhus
te sku mdun 'khod pa'i ston mo'i thog dad pa gyur med thob te/ zhwa dmar gyi bla ma rang du ma song na/ 'di las rnam dpyod che ba ma mthong zhes dngos rdzas kyi 'bul
ba dang bcas skyar nas mjal phyag sgo gsum dang bas zhu ba byung zhing / gzhan yang dmag mi spyi bye brag nas thugs bsun med par/ kun mkhyen lnga ba chen po sogs nas stsal
ba'i bka' gtan rim can gyi dgongs don bzhin mdzad chog pa byung ngo / /de skabs grib rkyen zhig la brten pa'i mgur 'cham shin tu lod pa dang / spyan nad sogs rgyun ring
zhig byung ba na/ skabs shig 'dren mchog dam pa 'di nyid nas mdangs rmi lam du yab rje dam pa de nyid kyi tshe dbang dang / ljags chab kyang gnang byung bas/ da myur du
phan 'gro bar 'dug zhes bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po la phebs pa bzhin/ snyung gzhi yang 'phral du dngas ba

sogs bla ma yi dam chos srung gi zhal bstan tshul/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po dang / mdzod pa bsod nams bstan pa'i rdo rje la lan gcig min pa yang yang stsol ba mdzad yod 'dug
kyang zin bris ji bzhin ma 'khod/ de nas dgung grangs bcu bzhir phebs pa sa khyi lor chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i gser 'bum bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang gi
gser phibs kyi mdog 'don shing cha gsar spo skya rnams rmangs nas bzung nyams gso dang / chos grwa byang gi dge 'dun 'du ba'i kun ra dri gtsang khang bcas rtsa ba nas bzung
gsar bzhengs lta bu dang de tsam la rdzong chung bla brang gi shar skya gsar spo sogs chos srid mdzad pa kha shas yod 'gro yang zin bris ma snyed/ de nas dgung grangs
bco lnga pa sa phag lor da lta dbu rtser bzhugs pa'i gang gi yab rje mchog gi sku brnyan 'di dang mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i sku lugs ma rgya bzo bas kyang lhag
pa lta bu byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba da lta gzim chung shar mgon khang nang bzhugs pa 'di sogs gsar bzhengs mdzad/ lo 'di gnyis la dus dbang gi phur sgrub bshol nas
bde mchog sgrub mchod gnang dgos byung bas 'tshub lhong lta bu yin nam/

gtor 'bul zhig gi skabs rol mo stong gsum 'brug sgra glo bur du chag khyi lo lha mthim khyams smad lho'i ka ba zhig skyon cung zad kyang med par tshag sgra dang bcas byer/
sgo srung rta mgrin gyi phyag g.yon ma gyang logs nas sa phag phog pa'i gas skyon dang / de'i rjes tsam la g.yas kyi phyag mtshan pad dbyug lhung ba sogs mtshan ma mi shes
pa kha shas kyang byung 'dug de skabs tsam la yin nam 'byung 'dul phur pa gur mgon rnams kyi ljags bsnyen mdzad dus phur pa'i skabs rdo rje gzhon nu'i sku 'di las 'od shin
tu che ba zhig yong gin 'dug zhes dang / mgon po'i skabs mgon sku 'di las me stag mang po 'thon gyin 'dug zhes dge rgan bsod nams bsam 'phel la gsung 'dug yang bcom ldan
'das dpal kyai rdo rje'i grangs dus kyi ljags bsnyen gsol dpon thugs rje bkra shis dang lhan du mdzad pa'i gsol tshan gzhu lung pa bsod nams mchog ldan gyis zhus par/
skabs gcig 'bul gtor tshang ma ma phul bar/ zhabs drung du phyin pas de 'dra ma byed gsung pa'i brda' dang / gzhan yang spyan lta stangs su gzigs nas 'od gsal gyi ngang
la bzhugs pa lta bu kha shas dang / gsung las kyang / yab rje de nyid dang kyai rdor dbyer med du 'dug zhes dge rgan bsod nams bsam 'phel la gsung ba

sogs mtshan ma'i bsnyen rtags kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung yod tshod du 'dug go /de ltar gsung bsnyen sbyin sreg bcas grub pa nas bzung yab mes gong ma'i dus mchod/ bde
kyai gsang gsum/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ rdo rje bdag med ma/ rdo rje gzhon nu/ kun rig sogs sgrub mchod 'dus tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i gtor bzlog drug
cu pa sogs kyi zor las/ lo gnang dus kyi dam rdzas sgrub pa/ tshugs sgrub mchod/ dkar mo dus ja sogs rnam dkar dge 'thebs stod smad lho byang sogs su 'bul sdud bla khag
tshong pa bcas 'dzin skyong spel gsum gyi sgo nas/ yab mes kyi phyag srol bzang po mi nyams zhing ches cher gong nas gong du 'phel zhing rgyas pa'i dbu tshugs par gyur/
dgung grangs bcu drug tu phebs pa lcags kyi lor/ dbus phyogs la chibs bsgyur bar bzhed de mgon khang steng 'og sogs la 'phrin 'chol gsung bskang snyan shal bcas gnang / hor
zla bcu pa'i dmar phyogs la/ gzhung sa'i sku tshab sgang chen nas dang bcas chibs rags drug cu bskor chibs kha bsgyur te/ dgon rgyas/ lcang gshong / rgya mdud/ srad rgod/
snar thang sogs su rim phebs kyi thog snar thang du gnas gzigs snyan

shal mchod 'bul smon lam sogs dang / gzhis rtser phebs skabs zla ba 'dii'i tshes bdun la paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa dbus phyogs la chibs bsgyur bas phyag mdzod sku tshab
nas ja zhus/ rdzong nas zur gsos sogs phul/ gser mdog can du dgong zhag gcig bzhugs/ bla brang / 'du khang / gur zhal dang / pu tra'i bla mtsho'i rgyun yod pa'i mgon khang
/ gos sku khyad can bcas la mchod 'bul gnas gzigs/ bla spyi 'dus tshogs nas zur gsol legs 'bul de nas rim bzhin zhang pa brag gdong du/ 'bras yul skyed tshal nas legs 'bul/
rin spungs rdzong nas phebs bsu/ zur gsos leegs 'bul/ byams chen gnas gzigs 'phags pa'i thugs dam gur mgon gyi bzhugs sgam zhal dbye/ ngur smrig brgyud ram par phebs
skabs rlung che ba zhig gis dbu gur ma gtogs gzhan rnams 'gyel ba'i tshe/ nged rang ban tshang pa bcas nas bskang gso byed dgos phebs pa bzhin/ nyams bzhes gnang bas/ gtor
bsngo grol phral 'tshub ma rang zhir gyur/ yar 'brog dpal de ba dang mig pa bcas nas zur gsos legs 'bul/ gam pa la brgyud gsal byed rdor gling / snye thang du chos rje
bla ma dam pa'i phyi rten/ jo bo rje'i gdung thal las grub pa'i sku 'bum/ lung bstan sgrol ma sogs

gnas rten rnams la mchod 'bulathugs smon bcas/ snye thang 'phags sder gnas gzigs/ gsol tshigs khang du mchod yon chen po nas gzim gur bzhugs khri thab 'dzin/ rtse shod kyi
sku 'khor ser skya lnga bcu tsam gyis phebs bsu/ gsol ja gnyis kyi ring la bka' 'dri ji ltar 'tshams pa gnang rjes/ dpal gyi chos 'khor lha sar phebs te/ g.yu thog khang
gsar du bzhugs/ der mchod yon chen po nas yo byad mkho dgus phebs bar thon gsum gyi zur gsos shin tu che ba gnang / rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i mthong bzos
bdag rkyen bla na med pa'i dbu 'don bka' drin che ba'ang gong sa rin po che de nyid kyi rtogs brjod dpag bsam rin chen snye ma zhes lcang skya rdo rje 'chang ye shes bstan
pa'i sgron me'i bka' rtsom de nyid las mgo zla'i tshes drug la gangs ri'i ljongs kyi thub pa'i ring lugs pa rnams kyi nang nas rdo rje theg pa'i bshad sgrub kyi bya ba
rgya cher spel ba la mchog tu bsngags pa dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud dri ma med pa dang yum rje btsun ma bcas mjal khar phebs par bkur bzos sogs sngar srol ma nyams
pa'i bdag rkyen dang rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i skor las brtsams pa'i gsung gleng yang mang du mdzad/ bdag chen sku 'khor dang bcas pa rnams nas kyang sku gsung

thugs rten gyi gtsos pa'i 'bul ba'i rnam grangs tshan che bar phul zhes gsungs pa ltar/ legs 'bul dngos gzhi tshom chen rnying mar 'bul bar mdzad thog kyang gsol ston shin
tu zab pa sku 'khor nang gras rnams kyis rje nyid la mjal dar phyag dang bcas te phyag dbang zhu bar byung ba la/ thugs shin tu mdzangs pa'i rnam pas phyag dbang gnang ma
nus par mkhyen gzigs rin po che nas/ 'khor 'di sogs skye 'gro spyi bye brag la mjal phyag gsung chos sogs brtse gzigs sgrib med gnang dgos pa'i bka' lhug stsol phebs par
rten/ gsum skas mdun du skye 'gro drag zhan khri phrag tsam la shur phyag gnang/ de ltar lha ldan du bzhugs zhag bco brgyad tsam gyi ringrin paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa
dang mjal 'dzoms mdzad tshul ni de nyid kyi rnam thar zhal gsung ma 'od dkar can gyi phreng ba'i lcags byi rgyal zla'i skabs kyi gsung 'phros las nyer gnyis kyi nyin sa
skya bdag po chen po yum lcam sring 'khor bcas ngos phrad la pheb sapar gsol ja bzhugs gral thog gnang skyes gya nom pa ltar zhing lan 'debs bzang po sogs bzos sgo gang che'i
sgo nas mnyes par byas zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /gzhan yang che btsan par zhan gyi rigasal tshe bka' sogs 'dod chos mjal kha phyag dbang sogs gang 'tshams sku

ngal med du gnang zhing dad ldan rnams nas kyang 'bul dngos gtsang zhing kha lar mi khyud pa lta bu'i stobs shin tu che ba byung / de bar la po ta la dang lha sa'i rten rnams
la gos bzang las grub pa'i na bza' snyan shal/ gser chab/ sna lnga'i rgya mchod sogs dang bcas mchod mjal thog gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi thugs smon smin rgyas mdzad/
rgya dpon gtsang jun/ gung tshe dbang dpal mi sogs che btsan rnams dang zhal rgyas kyi 'brel ba zab cing / khyad par gtsang jun zhabs gras rgya mi rnams rje 'di'i bzhugs
khri'i mtha' 'khor du thal sbyar gus 'dud kyis langs te zhal dkyil la ngom pa med par lta zhing khong dpon g.yog rgya yul du log 'byon dus rje dpon g.yog nas sku 'bum
thang bar phebs skyel mdzad pas rgya mi mang pos gtam du ma gleng ba na bdud rtsi ril bu byin phebs pa bzhin byas pas thams cad mgu zhing ci yang mi smra ba gyur pa sogs
gdul bya'i re ba skong bar mdzad do/ /de nas mchod yon gyi thon phyag kyang gzim chung nyi 'khyil du gnang thog gsol ston gos dar/ dngul dpyad sna tshogs/ snam cha ther phrug
rgya ja'i rigs sogs dpag dka'i dngos bzang stsol ba dang bcas/ spyir bstan 'gro'i don rlabs chen dang / lhag par sngon dus bzhin lho kha sogs la

chibs bsgyur kyis 'gro don thugs mdzangs med par dgos lugs kyi bka' phebs/ lha ldan nas chibs bsgyur te yer par bzhugs zhag gi gnas gzigs zhib rgyas/ sang de sgo mo dgon gyi
gnas gzigs mdzad nas de'i la brgyud 'phan yul rgyal chen gzhol du bzhugs bzhag sang nyin glang thang brgyud phebs par glang thang chos skyong sku phebs kyis bsu ba dang
bcas rje nyid la dar gyi rgyal mtshan/ lcang ram mdud ldan bcas phyag rten du phul/ nA landra'i dge 'dun rnams kyis ser phreng / chos skyong sku phebs/ skye bo'i tshogs
kyi phebs bsu bcas bco brgyad bla brang du zhag bdun skor bzhugs pa'i bar la zhabs drung sogs la gsung chos kyi 'brel pa skye bo'i tshogs la khrom dbang stsal tshe nyin gang
la mi grub par gleng yang nyi ma gzhan las ring ba zhig byung bas 'dzin par mdzad par grags/ bco brgyad bla brang nas kyang zur gsos gsol ston snga phyi bar gsum du rgya
dpangs shin tu che ba nyin re bzhin skye bo dpag med la phyag dbang gnang/ dgung grangs bcu bdun du phebs pa lcags glang lo'i rgyal po lo gsar kyang gnas de nyid du mdzad/
nA lendra'i chos grwa/ 'du khang / kun mkhyen rong ston gyi 'dra sku/ gdung rten mgon khang sogs kyi gnas gzigs/ dpal ldan rtser thugs dam

bskang ba smin rgyas mdzad de/ 'phan yul mda' skor gyi glang thang dgon gyi gnas gzigs thog chos skyong sku phebs mjal 'phrad/ dga' mngon kha dang / dga' ldan gyi gzhung brgyud/
'brom ston me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang gras brag la dpal mgon zhal rang 'byon yod pa'i mgon khang gnas gzigs grub nas/ phebs lam du phyag dbang zhu mi 'dus khrod bud
med mche ba gtsigs pa zhig la phyag 'dzub gtad par/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal pos bud med pha gi ci 'dra zhig legs zhus pas/ yum chen zhig yin 'dra phebs/ de nas chang tshugs
su bzhugs zhag dgod kha la'am rgod dkar la brgyud bsam yas phu sngas mgor bzhugs dus bsam yas mkhan tshang rab 'byams pa sogs chibs bsu 'byor/ de'i sang rtses po khar
bsam yas sku rten pa rdzong dpon sku tshab sogs kyi chibs bsu/ thab 'dzin/ ja zhus pa rnams kyis phebs sna drangs te bsam yas su bzhugs sgar klu sding du mdzad/ sang nyin
de lcog khar lha bsangs smin rgyas gnang rjes/ chos skyong sku phebs kyi rdo skas mgor phebs bsur byon pa'i phyag ral 'phyar te/ lha mi kun gyi lha rgyal 'bod sgra chen
po thengs gsum mdzad pa dang / rje nyid la mjal dar che legs zhig phul/ rje nyid nas

kyang / sgron dar gser phud bcas gnang zhing / bka' sgo 'phrin bcol mdzad pa na/ bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i brtags dbu gug lan gsum mdzad pa na/ lcog nang gsang bkod kyi lung bstan
'dra phebs yod pa 'dra yang sngar phan yig rigs ma mthong / chos skyong rang gi rten rdzas nang mjal bcas yun ring gnang / dbu rtse rigs gsum la rgya mchod/ gzhan la
lnga mchod snyan shal sogs dang bcas/ de skor gyi rten gsum rnams zhib mjal/ nyin re bzhin che btsan gyi mjal kha zhu mi dang / shur phyag zhu mi sa gzhi khebs pa lta bu'i
dngos 'bul shin tu che ba byung / sku rten lha dbang dar rgyas nas dbang gzhi bteg te khrom dbang stsal/ so so nas rang la ci yod kyi dngos rigs rje nyid la gus 'bul rtse
gcig tu brtson par gyur te kun 'phral yun gyi legs lam la sbyor bar mdzad/ bsam yas chibs bsgyur/ rdo mda' brgyud rtse thang 'bras gling / dben dgon bsam gtan gling gi
chos bsrung gur zhal chos rje bla ma'i thugs dam ma sogs gzigs/ de dus de na khog zhugs byed sa zhig kyang yod tshod kyi kho par de 'phral bab te gus 'dud byas mthar gdug
'dre byang chub bar du rjes su bzung zhes skad chen po dang bcas zhags pa'i sne gcig rje nyid kyi phyag

tu phul/ lcags kyu yod pa'i sne gcig de rang gi phod ka'i rdor gong la rgyab pa rjes su gtan nas ma grol bas zhags pa rdor gong bcas sa skyar 'byor ba lo du mar tshoms dmar
du bzhag tshod du 'dug khra 'brug tu phebs lam khar nag dkyil zhig nas byi'u phur ba'i rnam pa 'dra ba la sa gzhi yoms pa lta bu'i chibs rags 'ur la khad pa byung bar gang
yin zhus pas bsrung ma bse khrab can gyi 'tshub lhong yin 'dra gsung / dar tsam nas ra smad grwa tshang chos skyong bcas kyi gdan 'dren gyi bang mi 'byor/ khra 'brug gnas
gzigs thog de kha'i chos skyong sku phebs kyis rje nyid la mjal dar dang / me tog 'thor zhing lcog nang gdan drangs thog rje nyid nas kyang sgron dar gser phud sogs 'bul
bar mdzad/ chos skyong nas gur zhal spyi dang / khyad par zhal gyi bskang ba khri tshar sku rim su sgrub dgos lugs kyi lung phul/ de'i sang phebs lam du bkra shis chos
sde sogs kyi chibs bsu bcas/ sngon chos rje sa paN dbus phyogs su rgyun ring bzhugs skabs/ chos 'khor skor ba'i bzhugs khri der bzhugs dus zhig la sa skyar 'phags pa rin
po che'i sku 'khrungs pa'i gtam snyan 'bul mi 'byor bas/ gtam snyan bzhugs khrir grags par dar 'dzugs dang / yum bu bla mkhar gnas gzigs/ yar lung bkra shis

chos sder gser phreng sogs zabs rgyas thog phebs bzhugs rin mchod khang so so'i gnas gzigs/ mgon khang du thugs dam bskang gso/ khong tshos gar 'cham bkra shis chog mang dus
mdzad pa ha lam gzigs 'bul dang / der bzhugs dpon slob sbyin bdag bcas kyi zhabs tog zan chas/ chos sde nas dbang gzhi bteg pa'i skye bo'i tshogs la khrom dbang dang gnas
gsang rdo rje 'chang de nyid dgung grang bco brgyad du phebs skabs yin 'dug kyang mdzad bzang la thugs spro'i yar lung dbon rin po che zhes phyis su'ang gtsigs chen mdzad
cing / gnas gsar gong ma'i thugs dam ma mgon sku byin chen zhig dang thun ru khyad mtshar sogs 'bul bar mdzad 'dug cing / zhal rgyas lo rgyus kha shas yod tshod 'dug
kyang zin bris ma rnyed/ de skor gyi thugs brel rnams grub nas chibs bsgrur te/ btsan thang lha khang gnas gzigs/ tshe chu 'bum pa'i tshe chu nas dpon slob tshang mas bzhes/
de nas rim phebs kyis bya sa dang / rnam sras gling du bzhugs zhag gra phyir ser phreng chos skyong sku phebs sogs kyi spyan drangs te dgon der phebs/ rten gsum spyi
dang / khyad par mkhas grub khyung po'i thugs dang / kha che paN chen gyi rdza sku phyag nas mar grags pa sogs gzigs/ gra

thang du ser phreng chos skyong sku phebs bcas gong bzhin/ khyad par zhang blon rdo rje bdud 'dul dngos su thim par grags pa'i mgon g.yag byin can gyii phebs bsu/ gnas gzigs
khrom dbang phyag dbang zhabs tog sogs gong bzhin/ kyai rdo rje'i sbyin sreg mchod gar sogs gzigs 'bul/ gra byams gling gnas gzigs/ gdung phud chos 'khor du'ang phebs bsu
sku phebs sogs gong bzhin/ rang rang 'byor pa dang bstun pa'i dngos 'bul dang khyad par dol bsam mkhar bas dbang gzhi bteg ste khrom dbang gnang skabs tshe chu stobs cher
bab pas nye 'khor phal cher la 'thung rgyu byung / ra ba smad du ser phreng chos skyong sku phebs kyi phebs bsu/ gnas gzigs lcog tu lha bsangs/ thugs dam bskang ba lha
bsangs kyi spyan 'dren skabs chos skyong dngos su gzigs pa lta bu'i gzigs stangs mdzad mur/ sku rten par chos skyong sku phebs rtsis kyis su sgra chen po byung ba la rje
nyid nas re zhig ma phebs zhes pa'i phyag brda' zhig mdzad song bar phebs 'phror g.yal kha shas dang bcas re zhig yal/ slar phebs par chos skyong gzhan las thugs nang gshin
pa'i gsung gleng sogs legs lam che zhing / de skabs rmor chen chos kyi rgyal po dang mjal tshul ni/ rmor

chen gyi rnam thar sgeg mo'i me long las/ lcags glang zla ba dang por rang lo re brgyad pa'i steng gdan sa chen po nas sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen
gong gi mjal phyag grub nas bsam yas brgyud lho kha phyogs su chibs kha brgyur ba ra ba smad du tshes drug la phebs pa'i sgo dod zhes dang / de 'phros lcags zam pa'i skor
gsung mthar/ tshes drug gi nub lcags zam pa'i sku mdun nas thon par mdzad de gong dkar du phebs/ de nas ra ba smad du phebs tshul ni/ yang gong gi rnam thar las/ de nas
mgyogs par yong bas ra ba smad du nyi ma kha 'bol la 'byor/ tshes drug gi nyin blo gsal kyang phebs bsur phyin pa'i mgron gnyer la tshes bdun la grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan
yin gshis brgyad la phul chog pa snyan gsan phul 'dug don ltar de nyin grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan gyi dung brda' gtong ba dang slebs pa dus mnyam du byung / mjal phyag
kyang tshogs rang du shar mar zhus par gong ma rin po che khri thog nas bzhengs pa'i dgyes tshor che bar zhal 'dzum bcas gnang / dpon slob nas tshe dpag med rong ston brgyud
par sbyar chog pa'i chog khrigs nged rang nas bgyis pa de 'dzugs sa gnang bar gsung chog kyang shin tu 'grig pa sku gsung thugs rten la bdag gi bshad pa bgyis nas dpon
slob

kyis rim gyis btegs nas phyag tu 'bul ba gnang / zhal bzhes nged kyi zhus par tshogs pas maNDal 'bul ba sogs dang spyi sger thams cad nas 'bul dpangs shin tu mtho bar 'dug
de'i sang nyin snga ma ji lta ba bzhin gsung chog grwa tshang nas mang ja gnyis thog nas gnang bar nged rang nas sku rten bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal gyi zhal gzigs kyi
sgrol ma'i sku mtho gang pa/ gsung rten bdag nyid chen po'i phyag dpe rgya nag ma padma rA ga dang margad sogs kyi khra ldan ba so'i glegs shing 'gangs che ba/ thugs rten
gdung rten lcags rtse ma/ mdzod btags 'dom 'khor ma bcas phyag tu phul/ mdzod btags bsod btags rtags brgyad bcas legs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu'i phon gyi mgo byas pa'i bcu
gsum tshan rdo rje gsang lam ma dmar po legs pas mgo byas pa/ sangs rgyas so lnga'i sku thang gra tshar spus legs bco lngas 'go byas pa/ sbug chol rnying ma shubs bcas kyis
'go byas pa/ 'di thams cad la dril gtan nas med/ mjug tu nya lcibs kyi me tog chas 'go byas pa sogs gang yod thog nas dngos gtsang bar phul/ rmor pa'i spyi so grangs
so so'i 'bul ba yang nad khyag yod/ de mjug tu rab brtan gyi btsun ma rnams kyis spyi 'bul dang sger 'bul/ byang kha rgyud kyi sbyin bdag rnams

kyang 'thud pas bag dro bar byung / steng du sger mjal la yang mdzod btags phon che ba dang / yum drung dang phyag mdzod la yang phyag mjal gya nom pa phul/ yar lung sogs nas
nged kyi lag tu gnam lcags kyi rdo rje yongs grags de yod pa snyan du 'bul mi byung stabs phyag mdzod nas de 'dra yod 'dug pa spus bsgyur dgos nan gyis gnang byung bar
thog mar de 'dra'i rigs med ces sku rtsed zhus par nan bskyed gnang byung bar / de 'dra yod pa sngar sor nas 'bul rtsis yin rung bdag rkyen ma gnang na chud zos dogs byung
kyang thugs la gtang na cis kyang 'bul spro zhes mthing khra dang khags kyi na bza' bcas bdag chen rin po che rang gi phyag tu phul bas shin tu dgyes pa'i rtser gson/
bdag ni nor bdag po'i phyag tu 'phrod snyam dga' ba thob/ da dung de rigs lag tu 'khor byung na cis kyang dgos zhes bka' gnang zhing yum nas kyang nan bcags che bar byung
/ sku zhabs rin po che nas dam rdzas stong rdo brgya rdo gnyis bsil ma phon che ba phyag mdud bcas dang / dngul sogs tshan grangs gnang ba ma zhus kyang / de nub phyag mdzod
nas rdo rje'i legs so yin gnang ba'i dngul srang sum cu kha btags bcas gnang bar/ de la ltas nas phul ba min pas dam rdzas byung na gang byung zhu dgos

zhus par tha ma'ang phyed bzhes gnang kyang ma zhus/ da lam 'di khar dam rdzas mdzangs pas tshan che ba med slar 'bul gnang bas zhogs pa dam rdzas brgya rdo sil ma bcas mang
bar byung / de nas gra tshang dpon slob dang nged gsum/ dbu chos zhol gling drung 'khor bcas chibs skyel tshan che ba bcas sgang seb bar chibs skyel zhus/ nged de nub ra
ba smad du bsdad/ sang nyin rang gnas su log de skabs skyid gshongs su yum drung nas sa skyar lung bstan rgya can ma'i phyag dpe med gshis sngar phan stsol ba byas kyang
ma byung bas/ da lam de kha gzhan dang ma 'dra ba'i thugs 'dris che stabs phyag na yod na dang / de min thugs stsol dgos tshul gnang byung bar nged rang la khyad par 'phags
pa zhig yod pa sku zhabs su phul tshar bas gong chos tshun la 'bul thub pa yong zhus nas 'di kha nas rgya can rtsa ba dang / bla ma mal gyi thugs dam rten 'khor lo bde
mchog nag po lugs kyi sku brnyan rdo nag las grub pa sa chen gyi phyag tu byung ba phyis dpon ag len la gnang ba'i sna dkar rtse'i nang rten du bzhugs pa phyis rdor drag
gi phyag tu 'byor bar gtor dus 'khyar ba nged rang gi lag tu 'byor ba'i khyad can de dang bcas 'bul bar blo gsal btang / gong dkar chos sder zhu yig bcas phul bas shin
tu dgyes/

bka' lan rgyas pa dam rdzas mang ba bcas gnang zhing / da dung de rigs byung na dgos tshul bka' drin che ba bcas sku zhabs yum phyag mdzod bcas thams cad nas rgyas par gnang
/ zhes gsungs so/ /rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas sku dang gsung rten bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal gyi zhal gzigs dang thugs dam ma 'bul ba gnang ba ni gdung rabs myur
'byon rten 'brel thugs bsam che skyed rang yin 'dug de ltar ra ba smad kyi thugs brel rnams chod nas/ dwags po grwa tshang du phebs bsu bsnyen bkur mjal phyag khrom dbang
sogs stsal/ der gnyan mkhar nas kyi gdan 'dren thog dwags gra nas chibs bsgyur te gong dkar chos sde nas phebs bsu sogs zab rgyas kyi bla brang du gdan 'dren zhus/ dge
'dun yon bdag che btsan bcas la mjal kha phyag dbang skye bo mtha' yas la shur phyag 'dus tshogs nas kyai rdor gur rigs bsdus sogs/ chog gra nyer bdun lhag tsam gyi sgrub
mchod cho ga'i yan lag sbyin bsreg mchod gar/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i grub 'chams/ gur gyi mgon po'i las mkhan ru 'dren gyi gar 'chams rnams gzigs phul/ lha khang steng shod
bar gsum thun mong dang / thun mong

ma yin pa'i mgon khang sogs kyi gnas gzigs/ khrom dbang / rdzong nas kyang sger dang dbyings sa nas stsal ba'i bka' 'dzin nang ltar gyi zur gsos dang / sngon rdo rje gdan pas
dbyen dgon du btab pa'i bde chen chos 'khor bshad sgrub gling sogs rang gzhan gyi dgon sde rnams nas legs 'bul phun sum tshogs pa byung / de skabs rtse gdong zhabs drung
nor bu rgyal mtshan la zhu shog zur gsos sogs 'bul bar mdzad tshul gong de nyid kyi rnam thar du bshad pa ltar ro/ /gong dkar nas chibs bsgyur te chu ri gru brgyud stag
khu spo bas phebs bsu sogs dang bcas de'i bla brang du bzhugs 'tsher gnang / dge 'dun rnams dang / nye 'khor che btsan rnams la mjal phyag skye bo'i tshogs la shur phyag
khrom dbang gnang skabs tshe bum las tshe chu'i rgyun shin tu che ba babs nye 'dab chos 'khor yang rtse nas legs 'bul sogs rgya chen/ khrus sde zhal ngo rnams nas gsol
ston legs 'bul/ de nas zhe re skyed tshal du phebs bsu/ legs 'bul sogs rgya chen dang / khrom dbang sogs gnang / chu ri'i gru dang gan pa la brgyud/ dpal der phebs/ zhal
ngo rnams kyi zur gsos gsol ston legs 'bul/ sna dkar rtse rdzong dang stag lung mgon khang du gur zhal gyi bskang

chas kyang bzang bar stsal/ de nas thar gling du phebs bzhugs zhag gi ring mang 'gyed khrom dbang sogs stsol bar mdzad/ de nas rja ra dang / kha ro la brgyud phebs pa na/ ra
lung kha mo dgon sogs nas legs 'bul/ mthong lcags rdzong mgon khang du bskang chas phul/ rgyab khra nas skyor ngar phebs/ zhal ngo rnams nas bsnyen bkur/ rgyal rtse dpal
'khor chos sde dang nye bar gur pa/ mngon dga' ba/ khang gsar ba/ bde ba can pa rnams kyi bla spyi dbu chos sogs nas chibs bsu/ grwa tshang / de bzhi dang rgyal rdzong
bcas nas zur chas bzhugs ring grwa tshang gi bla spyi/ dbu chos dge 'dun sogs dang nye bskor gyi drung 'khor che btsan rnams la mjal phyag dang / shur phyag/ khrom dbang
/ der bzhugs rten gsum rnams dang / ri khrod dga' ldan/ mchod rten mthong grol chen moo bcas la gnas gzigs sogs grub nas phebs/ rtse chen zhol du grwa tshang nas gzigs gur
dang bcas/ gsol ston legs 'bul phun sum tshogs pa byung zhing / thong lcags mgon khang gi sku gnyer gur pa'i grwa pa bcos med 'dra ba zhig gis drung yig kun sangs lags
kyi phyag nas 'jus te/ mchi ma gtong zhing ngu ma lab 'phros su/ 'dren mchog dam pa 'di

nyid la bltas te/ yid bzhin nor bu 'di star yong ngo / / zhes yang yang zhu ba zhig byung 'dug pas rjes su drung yig lags nas/ da tshod bsam tshe srid zhi'i 'dod dgu kun stsol
yin no zhes/ brda' sprod nges shes skyes pa zhig byung gsung / de nas 'brong rtse nas gsol ston zur gsos legs 'bul/ nye 'khor gyi che btsan dang / skye bo'i tshogs la
spyi phyag sger phyag sogs/ 'brong rtse chos sde sogs dgon rigs rnams nas kyang legs 'bul byung zhing / gnas gsar rgyal khang gi gnas gzigs mchod 'bul smon lam sogs mdzad/
skye bo'i tshogs nas 'bul ba shin tu stobs che bas zhabs phyi rnams nas bsdu ma thub par bag med 'jog dgos lta bu byung / de nas 'dus chung skyid sbug nas gsol ston legs
'bul dang khrom dbang zhus/ skyang 'dur bde ba can tu phebs gsol ston legs 'bul gnas gzigs che btsan skye bo'i tshogs la phyag dbang khrom dbang / nub gling brgyud tshal
du bzhugs sgar gsol ston legs 'bul/ che btsan dmangs bcas la phyag dbang / pad tshal mchod khang du dkar spro gsol ston/ de nas chibs bsgyur ste/ zhwa lu rgyan gong gi
gnas gzigs dus lha mo sku phebs kyi lung byung tshul zhig a Ni lags de nas

gsung byung yang ma nges/ zhwa lu mthil du bzhugs sgar grwa tshang spyi dang / dkar poo grwa tshang nas gang ci'i legs cha rnams grangs rgya chen zhus/ ri sbug tu phebs gnas
gzigs mchod 'bul ga ya dha ra'i bum chu zhal phye'i sku khrus dang / grwa tshang nas kyang legs 'bul/ de nas lcags la brgyud e wam chos ldan nas mkhan chen rin po che khang
gsar ba khri pa'i dbus/ thar rtse/ klung sdings dpon slob/ gzhis gnyer sogs chibs bsu ba rnams dang bcas phebs te/ klu sdings bla brang du bzhugs/ bla brang gzhung sger
so so nas gsol ston legs 'bul zhag bdun skor bzhugs pa'i ring gnas gzigs che btsan sogs la phyag dbang / skye bo'i tshogs la khrom dbang / de nas chibs bsgyur te bzhugs
zhag gnas su mdzad/ mi ser sogs la mjal phyag brag skye rer dge sdings nas thab 'dzin/ Da Di kha ba lhas kyi bla ma dbu chos/ shab gnyer rgan po sogs kyi chibs bsu'i khro
phur phebs byams chen sku 'bum rnam sras bcas gnas gzigs mdzad rjes/ dge sdings gzim chung du gdan drangs te/ gsol ston legs 'bul che btsan la mjal phyag khrom dbang
/ dge sdings/ Da Ti'i gnas gzigs sogs grub nas chibs bsgyur te rgya mdud brgyud dkyil

stod rgya rgan nas kyi zur gsos gsol ston legs 'bul/ nyung bsdus la tshe dbang dang mjal phyag shur phyag sogs gnang / lcang gshongs sogs brgyud ser phreng gi phebs bsu dang
bcas dgon rgyas su bzhugs zhag gnang / dgon de dang phun sum chos sde nas legs 'bul zhus de ltar chibs bsgyur mar yar phebs lam rnams su gtsug lag khang 'brel mtshungs
rnams la mchod 'bul snyan shal dge 'dun gyi sde rnams la mang 'gyed dbul phongs la sbyin pa sogs lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i mdzad phrin bsam gyis mi khyab par gyur to/ /de
nas chibs bsgyur ste ga ra bkra shis dar rgyas su bzhugs zhag mdzad/ lcags glang zla ba gsum pa'i yar tshes gza' skar legs 'dzoms nyin dpal ldan sa skyar phebs rgyu'i snga
char/ bkra shis dar rgyas su chos grwa lho byang gi mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan sogs zab spros dang bcas phebs bsur 'byor ste/ gling bu'i sgra
dang spos kyi phebs sne drangs thabs su ja zhus rim gyis dpal sa skyar chos grwa lho byang gi ser phreng 'cham sku'i phebs su/ skye bo'i glu bro sogs spyan 'dren bkod
pa du ma dang bcas bzhi thog bla brang chen por dge legs kyi dpal 'bar bar phebs so/ /

sang nyin bzhi thog tshoms chen du legs phebs dga' ston legs 'bul/ de nas rim bzhin mgon khang rnams su gtang rag mdzad de chos srid yar rgyas su gyur/ dbus phyogs nas phebs
'phral 'gro mgon 'phags pa rin po che'i sbyin bdag gong ma se chen gan gyi gdung rigs khal kha rje btsun dam pa'i sku'i dbon don grub wang dpon g.yog rnams 'byor te/ gus
'dud shin tu che ba dang bcas/ dngul gos dar sogs 'bul ba rgya chen po dang / gnas gzigs mchod 'bul/ 'dus tshogs la mang 'gyed bcas mdzad par lugs zung gi sgo nas khong
dpon blon dgyed pa'i rtser gyur/ de nas ma 'gyangs par go shri bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung rgyud e bus pa'i li dpon g.yog 'khor bcas mjal phyag tu phebs pa la'ang
gong bzhin bdag rkyen phu dud chen po'i sgo nas thugs tshim par mdzad/ lo 'di'i nang phyag mdzod dbang phyug bkra shis 'das par/ gsung byang dang / rgyal ba yab sras
sogs la skyabs 'jug zhu rten 'bul bar mdzad cing dgon sde kha shas la mang ja sogs mdzad do/ /de nas lha bzo bkra shis don grub de tshab tu bsko gnang gis ma 'gyangs par
rje btsun sa skya pa'i chos srid la gnad shin tu che ba gdung rabs rin po che mi nyams dar rgyas su

spel bar bzhed de bdag chen shar pa'i sras mo lcam lha mdzes bu khrid gsang yum du bzhes/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen par zhabs brtan gsol 'debs zhu shog rten gsum sogs 'bul
ba dang bcas mdzod pa bkra shis don grub rdzong bda' mdzad par gzhung zhabs rin po che nas mgo 'dren brtse gzigs kyi legs lam phun sum tshogs pa dang / de skabs phul byung
rgyab byang pa'ang sngar shul du stsal ba dang bcas mdzod pas las phyag bde bar 'khor/ de nas chu stod zla ba'i tshes bco lngar gong dkar rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang
phyug gi drung du skyabs gsum 'dzin pa dang yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa gnyis/ cho ga byed do lugs bzhin gyi sgo nas so sor thar pa'i sdom pa dang / theg chen
dbu sems gnyis kyi cho ga'i sngo nas sems bskyed/ gso sbyong bsnyen gnas yan lag brgyad pa te byang sems kyi sdom pa dang / yang de nyid kyi drung du 'chi med rnga sgra/
a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ gza' yum lha bcu bzhi rnam 'joms/ ber lugs/ dgra nag lha bcu gsum ma/ gdong drug lha nyer gcig dus 'khor byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun gong ma gong
chen gshed dmar lha lnga dang bcu gsum ma/ bsrung ba lnga / gur rigs bsdus/ 'jigs byed zhe dgu

ma dang sa lugs/ bde mchog dril bu lugs phyi nang/ gur sgrol lha bcu gcig rgyu ma chen mo lha lnga/ yang dag mar me dgu pa/ gdugs dkar zhe gnyis/ bcu bdun ma nyer bdun ma/
rtsi mo rigs bsdus/ dri med rnam gnyis/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ kyai rdor 'grel lugs/ phag mo so bdun ma sogs dbang du ma/ tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ nyi sbas lugs kyi sgrol
ma nyer gcig sgrub thabs rin 'byung / 'jam dbyangs dang sa paN sbrags sgrub/ sgrol dkar/ rdo rje shugs/ dbyangs can dkar dmar/ 'jam dpal gang blo ma'i rig gtad/ sangs
rgyas klu dbang/ bcu gcig zhal/ gtsug gtor rnam rgyal/ mi g.yo ba dkar po/ phyag rdor gos sngon/ sme brtsegs bdud kha/ 'jigs byed dpa' gcig i ndra mkha' spyod/ mai tri mkha'
spyod/ dmar chen skor gsum/ dmar chung skor gsum/ rnam sras rigs chen bco lnga/ phyag rdor khang brtsegs/ zhang blon rdo rje bdud 'dul phyi nang gsang gsum/ las gshin
sogs rjes gnang gi rigs du ma/ lam 'bras rdo rje'i tshiig rkang gi bshad pa man ngag bshad mdzod steng nas 'dzin chos/ dag ldan snye ma'i steng nas rtag gnyis rgyud bshad
'dzin chos sbas don gsal ba'i steng nas gsung ngag lam 'bras gsan par pod nag ma lam bskor phyi ma

brgyad / gtso che'i chos sna so dgu rnams kyi lung / yab yum rgyu lam gyi dbang lam zab/ bir bsrung / sgrub pa lung sbyin rnams dang / gzhan yang aShTa'i byad bzlog rten 'brel
bsrung ba/ go cha lnga'i bsrung ba/ gur mgon lcam dral lha gsum sbags sgrub/ gur lha dgu ma/ gur mgon chos skor kha skong glegs bam gyi ljang glegs bam/ gong dkar mgon
pod rnamasakyi lung / brag rdzong ma'i nyams khrid/ gsang khrid thun mong ma yin pa/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi gsang sgrub dang sgrub dus thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i
rjes gnang zhal pod kyi lung / de'i gsang 'khrid thun mong ma yin pa/ 'od dpag med kyi nyal 'pho 'khrid brgya/ g.yu thog snying thig bskor sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan
no/ /gzhan yang yongs 'dzin dam pa snga phyi rnams 'dir phyogs gcig tu brjod na khang gsar zhabs drung bsod nams bzang po/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha'i mtshan can/
thub bstan rnam rgyal mkhan chen dbang phyug phun tshogs/ dza lung rig 'dzin chen po padma 'phrin las dang / 'gyur med gsang sngags bstan 'phel sogs mdor na yongs 'dzin
dam pa chos bzhin du spyod pa du ma'i zhal sgo las zab pa dang rgya che ba'i zab mo'i chos

grangs dang tshad las 'das pa zhig gsan pas/ bod gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir dus phyis byon pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa zhig la bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid
rang gsan rgya che zhing dam pa'i chos mtha' dag gi bdag po lta bur gyur te/ rim pa gnyis la lam dus su gus pa dang rtag pa'i sbyor bas nan tan du bsrung sdom mdzad pa
la brten nas rtsa ba dang yan lag gi nyes lhung phra mos kyang ma gos shing tha mal gyi thugs rtog gang gis kyang rdzi bar mi nus pa'i bskyed rdzogs ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyun
bzang la dbang 'byor pa sogs sdom pa gsum gyi thugs mtsho legs par bltams pa'i sgo nas gsum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur to/ /hor zla brgyad
pa'i gza' skar legs 'dzom nyin nas dpal sa skya'i ngo mtshar rten bzhi'i gras rnam rgyal sku 'bum la nyams gso gsar pa lta bus dbu btsugs te/ mchod rten la sa rdo'i zhal
gso gang dgos mdzes brling dang / steng 'og gi shing sgrig rtser gser bzang kyi rgya phebs zur drug pa gdugs 'khor char khebs tog bcas/ 'og seng khri'i steng gi mu khyud
la rdo g.yam shing sogs sgrigs rgyugs mdzes brtan/ nye skor du gtsug lag khang ka gnyis rnams grub/

dgung grangs bco brgyad par rnam rgyal lha dgu'i sku brnyan sogs sku gsum gyi rten kha shas der bzhugs par gnam sa bar gsum gyi mchod rdzas spyi dang mar me'i rgyun sbar yon
chab zhal zas mchod rol gyis sprad pa 'di bzhin phyag bzhes dus las gra tshugs pa nas nam mkha' dngas shing 'ja' sna tshogs me tog gi char sogs kun gyi mthun snang du gyur/
chu stag lor 'dren mchog dam pa 'di nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa bcu phrag lhag tsam gyis 'khor tshogasadang bcas pas/ dpal kyai rdo rje la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa smin rgyas
dang / gong dkar ba chen po blo gros dbang phyug nas kyang rab gnas mdzad/ de nas bzung zla rer rnam rgyal stong mchod bcas dang / yang de skabs phur ba'i ljags bsnyen
zhig kyang gnang tshod kyi sam Tar rje nyid kyi phyag bris ma zhig las/ lags dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i rtsa sngags dag po bgrang pa'i 'bum phrag brgyad dang / yum rang gi
spyan gsal po rang cig yong ba'i phyir du kI la ya khri phrag gsum bcas zhus lags zhes dang / yang phyag bris zhig las chu stag zla ba gsum pa'i tshes gnyis la nyal ba'i
rnal 'byor skabs rmi ltas su lcags kyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa gcig dang / rtse lnga pa gcig lcags phur gcig bcas 'grub pa'i rtags byung lags zhes yum drung la 'bul bar

mdzad 'dug de nas dA ching ba dur 'bul ba stobs chen dang bcas dad mjal du byon par mjal phyag tshe dbang sogs lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas mnyes par mdzad cing/ dpon de nyid nas
gdan sa 'di bstan pa'i 'byung khungs yin pas chos srid gang sar rnam spyod dod pa zhig gnang dgos zhus pa bzhin/ chos grwa lho byang du bca' yig chen mo'i zur 'debs smar
thus re gnang ba sogs chos srid rim bzhin yar ldan 'byung ba'i thugs 'khur che bzhes bka' drin kyang dus de tsam la gu ru padma'i ma 'ong lugs byang 'ga' na sa skya'i sa
gnad rnams su rigs gsum mchod rten kakNi dang bdud 'dul mchod rten rnams bzhengs pas bstan 'gro spyi sger la phan par lung bstan yod mod kyi de bzhin bzhengs par mdzad par
rgyu sa 'bum chos 'khor gdugs tog gser zangs mdzes byed dril bu kha shas kyi rgyan pa rnamasal gzungs ring bsrel rnam bzhi dang / gong sa rin po cher ched du zhu gnang
gi 'dod gsol bcas bzhugs su gsol ba la rje nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa'i 'khor dang bcas pa'i rab gnas dang gong dkar ba chen po blo gros mtshan can gyis kyang de bzhin du mdzad
cing gzhan yang de dus chos srung rnams la 'phrin 'chol 'dod gsol zhig kyang gong

sa rin po cher bka' rtsom zhu bar mdzad do/ /lo de'i ston dpal sa skya'i dbu rtse'i gtsug lag khang 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba sogs sku gsung thugs rten byiin can bgrang
yas bzhugs pa'i drung du bdag nyid chen po 'di'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len mtha' dag gcig tu 'dus shing zab pa'i mthar
thug gsung ngag rin po che smin grol cha lag 'ga' zhig dang bcas stsal/ dad 'dus kyi slob ma rje btsun kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma/ yum bstan 'dziin bsod nams bzang mo/ lcam
lha mdzes bu khrid/ bdag gi drin chen rtsa ba'i bla ma brag rtsa ba chen po/ chos grwa rnam gnyis kyi mkhan chen smon bde ba glo bo lha btsun/ chos grwa lho byang / chos
lhun/ sgrub sde gong 'og gdong dga' phu gsum sogs nas 'dus pa'i chos nyan pa gsum brgya lhag tsam smin grol mchog gi lam la dkri bar mdzad pa'i skabs su bla ma rgya bod
kyi rnam thar sogs rnam thar rags bsdus gsung ngag khog phub sogs snang gsum dang 'brel ba'i lung du ma sems skyed chen mo lha mthil rdo chal du bstsal zhing slob ma rjes
'dzin kha gso'i ljags bsnyen sogs rgyu dbang mngon rtogs bdun ldan pod ser pod dmar sogs ljags lung stobs chen lta ba phyi bskyed rim lam dbang nang

bskyed rim dbang gong ma gsum dang 'brel ba'i gtum mo pho nya/ rba rlabs kyi 'khrid rnams skabs su babs pa'i ljags bshad dang bcas bstsal shing rjes 'brel lam zab bir bsrung
rnams kyang bka' drin che bar bir bsrung dus slob ma phal char gyis bla ma sku mdangs dmar zhing spyan zlum pa zil chen rnal 'byor dbang phyug dngos lta bur mthong ngo
/ /de ltar zla ba gsum lhag tsam gyi ring chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ de sngon tsam nas bzung da lta'i shugs ldan rtsal 'di'i cho 'phrul gyi rnam pas dngos su rdo che chung
sna tshogs bskyur ba dang 'ga' zhig la mthong snang nyams myong 'dra min byung tshod du 'dug dgung grangs bcu dgu pa chu yos lor rnam rgyal sku 'bum du nyin re bzhiin mchod
'bum gzungs 'don pa bzhi sde 'dzugs par mdzad/ sngon bla ma bdag nyid chen po dpal la gong ma'i lung gi dpal sa skya'i gdan sa bzung ba'i gdung spel bar mngags pa na dpon
chen ag glan sogs dad can rnams kyi ngor btsun mo bdun bzhes pa ltar de skabs chu stod zla nang tsam la bdag la sku drin shin tu che ba'i ma drung bsod nams dpal gyi
dbang mo kha bzhes bka' drin che bar ma lags de rang la lkog gyur rjen gsal gyi mnal ltas 'ga' zhig byung 'dug pa 'og kho

bo'i rang mtshang ston pa'i skabs su 'dri'o/ bsam brling lha mo gsol mchod kyi mdung dar bzhes spro spus gtsang 'di rnams bzo bar mdzad/ ma lag de sgam yer bzhugs skabs rje
'di gdal chur chab bdugs la phebs dus gsung las kha sang chu bdugs kyi yas tsam rdo dkyil pha gir bltos dang gsungs bzhin mdzad pas/ rdo ngos legs zhig la zhabs rjes gzigs
pa bzhin bla ma mchod dpon sar gsung sgros byung bas rdo pha ga'i thad 'od mthong yang snang med du bzhag pa de 'di yin 'dug gzhan la ma gsung bar de khar bzhag gnang
ba bzhin ma lags de nas phyis su nged rang la'ang ston par mdzad byung bas zhabs 'dred shor ba'i rjes lta bu zhig 'dug dgung grangs nyi shu par shing 'brug lor dbo zla'i
tshes 'gor phur bzlog zor 'dzin gyi sku 'tshams la bzhugs mur drug cu gtor bzlog 'phar ma zhig gi bskul gyi bsam ma tshugs pa dang / mgon khang de'i 'tshams mgon rngul ris
ma sku yongs rdzogs phyir phebs shing gtor ma thebs nas nang du byon pa'i gzigs snang dang / gong du bshad pa'i lha mthil 'khyams smad lho'i ka ba gas grum can 'degs 'khrul
gyi bzo bzhed gang ci'i skor gzhan gyi blos ma 'khyud par gsung brtag zhus pa'i lan ljags mthun gyi

dbar la phyir phebs su nged rang gi spyi steng na rigs 'dzin bla ma rnams mtho brtsegs su bzhugs par thugs rjes byin rlabs bskul te dregs byed rnams las la 'byon pa yod/ 'on
kyang thun yungs 'di de khul phyogs kun gtor nas the tshom med pa'i las hur thogs dga' rab yong phebs pa bzhin sgrub pas de kho na bzhin gyur pa'i ka mgor mr-i ta'i phyag
tshwa/ sangs rgyas 'phel gdung / sa chen gong ma'i bdud rtsi ril bu sogs byin rten/ 'phral yun phan bde'i 'dod gsol bcas bzhugs par slad nas rje nyid kyis phyag nas mdzad
cing / de dang chabs gcig shing bzo dar po kho nas zla gsum khongs phur khang shar skyor shing sgrigs tshegs med du 'grub/ de dus gdab las kyi dam rdzas mdzod pa bka'
bzhi bas phul ba'i mthong snang du mi nag gnyis kyi dam rdzas tshom tsam khur ba shar zhing / dngos su'ang snod nas cung zad bo zhes thos la/ yum drung bstan 'dzin bsod
nams bzang mo'i thugs bzhed bzhin rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che gser chos gsar bzhengs gis 'char gzhi dang lo de'i chu stod zla nang nas rgyun 'dzugs kyi sgo rum ye shes
mgon po'i drung du zla ba byung ngo cog gi bcu dgu la tshogs yongs nas bskang gso dang / nyin ltar bzhi gra'i bskang rgyun gdung rabs myur byon gyi sku rim

du 'dzugs par mdzad de skabs skyed lhas su'ang gser tog dang maNDal zhig kyang 'bul sbyor gnang/ dgung grangs nyer gcig pa shing sbrul lor a lce drung skyid skyid tshe ring
ngam kun dga' bsod nams bstan pa'i nyi ma btsas/ bka' 'gyur gsar bzhengs kyi shog bu gser snyu gu bris pa rnams la rgyud sde nas 'byung ba'i byin rlabs mdzad/ ma dpe rgyal
rtse them spang ma'i bu lo chen thugs rje dpal bas zhu dag ma chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun po nas g.yar zhus la thugs 'dod bzhin bka' driin che bas bsnyen bkur spyan
'dren ngos/ mthing shog pa sum cu skor gser 'dul ba bcu lhag gser yig pa brgya dang bcu gcig glegs shing bzo rtsi gdong dar zhal khebs na bza' bzo pa bcu/ gzhan yang las
pa du ma dang bcas zla grangs bzhi tsam gyi khong du bskrun par gzhung sger gyi mang ja bskor bshal ston mo sogs kyi bdag rkyen dang / zhu dag bris pa rnams kyi tshar
gcig zhus chen pa rnams kyi sbyar klog sogs thengs gsum bcas lan bzhi'i rjes su gong gi na bza' sogs kyis spras shing gos bzang gi bla bre yol ba mchod pa'i yo byad du ma'i
dbus su bzhugs pa la rab gnas mdor bsdus yang yang mdzad yod dam snyam zhing da lta gro bzhin bcu dgu'i dus chen sogs la 'don

pa'i gdugs rgyal mtshan sogs rgyu bkod khyad mtshar 'di rnams gsar bskrun mdzad/ dgung grangs nyer gnyis pa me rta lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i yar tshes dge bar lha khang chen mo'i
khyams stod du rje 'di rdo rje 'dzin pa'i 'khor tshogs dang bcas pas/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po sgrub mchod dang 'brel ba'i rab gnas rgyas
pa nyin bdun ma zhi rgyas sbyin sreg dang bcas pa'i mthar gong gi mchod phreng gsar pa sngon 'gro'i phyi bskor la phebs te me tog gi char 'bebs pa sogs mdzad pas sngar
nas glegs bam rnams gser mdangs zhan yang de nas bzung yig 'bru rnams mdangs legs shing 'od 'tsher ba sogs gsung rnam par dag pa sor rtog ye shes dngos su bzhugs pa'i mtshan
ma shar yum drung sku drin can de nyid dang / gdam sa gzhung bcas nas gsung bskul yang yang bka' drin che ba dang / nged rang gi thog la'ang tshar kha shas gsung bskul
zhus shing / khyad par gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs drung du glegs bam 'di thog nas ljags lung bka' drin nos pas gdan sa chen po 'di nyid du dus phyis dpal
sa skya'i gdung bka' 'gyur gyi lung yongs rdzogs gsan pa kho bo mched tsam yin pas rgyu mtshan des nas yum sras gnyis nas

ma 'ongs pa na gdung gi lung rgyun nod pa'i tshe glegs bam gsar pa 'di mkho che bar 'gyur ro zhes pa'i thugs mkhyen yin byas kyang chog go /nag zla'i nang lha chen khyams stod
byang gi 'jag khang dang / dus mchod bla brang phu mda' sde yangs sogs nyams bzo dbu tshugs/ de'i dbyar bsnyen rdzogs las gra zhal bkod mthun rkyen bcas kyi sgo nas chos
grwa lho byang gi dge 'dun 'os su gyur pa rnams dge slong gi dngos por mdzad pa sogs bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel bar mdzad do/ /yang de dus thub bstan dge 'phel gyi rje
btsun grags pa dang tshar chen sku drung tshe sgrub dgos pa mnal ltas su shar yang phebs skabs ma byung bas sku tshab las chen pa bstan pa rab rgyas nas de bzhin zhus dus
rmi ltas su rang gi snying kha na rje 'di bzhugs par khyod rang nas sgom pa'i bla ma 'di ni slob dpon padma dngos yin no zer ba'i sgra lhang gi thos pa shar/ de skabs
tsam la dge 'brug dgong rtse ma mthun par leg spel du mdzod pa rdzong bda' gnang bas 'phral 'grig byung / de nas dgung grangs nyer gsum pa me lug lor nged rang gi a lce gzhon
pa sangs rgyas bu khrid dam/ chos ming kun dga' bstan pa'i sgron me'am/ phyis su rkyen 'ga' zhig gi mchog gsum

phrin las dbang mor btags pa de btsas pas bla ma dkon mchog rgyal pos da rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung mi mthong ba 'dra gsungs nas zhing khams brjes/ lha chen/ khyams stod
gong ma lnga sogs kyi sku'i sa khri rnams shing khri bang rim can gser shog tshon rtsi sogs kyi mdzes par rol sil sgrig sgo bcas gsar bskrun la sku dang mchod cha rnams bzhugs
su gsol/ 'jag khang dus mchod sogs kyi nyams gso mthar phyiin par 'dren mchog dam pa 'di nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa pa'i 'khor tshogs dang bcas pas rdo rje phur pa'i rab
gnas zhag bdun ma gnang dus rtse dmar gyi sprul pa lta bus a tsa ra cotso khan bha ti zer ba zhig gis dung dkar/ me long dar dmar can/ raksha gdong drug pa/ bcu gcig pa/
nyi shu ba rnams dang / thal chen/ ganggA'i chu lbal gu gang bcas phul te de rang tshe nam gnas bar zhabs phyi nang gras thugs rtsis can du mdzad/ stod phyogs kyi dpon us
tshing no yon phun tshogs bde legs 'khor bcas 'bul chen dang bcas mjal phyag tshe dbang zhu bar 'byor bas re ba rdzogs par mdzad/ bzhi thog pho brang gi sde yangs kun dga'
ra chung gi bskor rnams bzo bkod phun sum tshogs par mdzad de mthar phyin pa na/ 'dren mchog dam pa 'khor tshogs dang bcas pas rig 'dzin lha khang du rab

gnas kyi cho ga don gnyis lhun grub bzhin gyi me tog kun ra sogs gsar bkod rnams la 'thor bar mdzad/ sgo rum du gur mgon la brten pa'i rab gnas sogs / ngo mtshar rten bzhi/
skyed lhas byas 'gyur/ bsam gling sogs su snga phyir rab gnas lan mang stsol ba'i tshe/ byas 'gyur du rje btsun grags pa'i sgrub chu lud cing yab rje mangga'i mtshan can
gyi sgrub chu sngar bzhin rang rdol dang / gzigs snang du sgrub sde'i lho phyogs rtag 'tsher ma'i thad kyi nam mkhar 'ja' sprin gyi dbus su slob dpon padma yab rje mangga'i
mtshan can/ rdo rje gzhon nu/ dkar bdud gnyis/ khyad par gur gyi mgon po nyid ring stabs su phebs pa bcas gzigs pa las/ bla ma gnyis kyi sku yongs rdzogs gsal zhing /
gzhan rnams sprin sbugs su bzhugs pa lta bu'i cung mi gsal ba zhig byung zhes mdzod pa bkra shis don grub la gsungs shing / phru mar yang sngags 'chang chen pos sgrub chu
sor chud sogs dgon gnas khyad par can 'di 'phel rgyas su mdzad do/ /de nas ljongs 'dir bstan 'gro'i gegs chags kyi dbus gtsang gzir gong tsam la mnal ltas su lha sa'i jo
shAka rin po che'i sku mdun chu klong du gyur pa la jo bo zhal phub tu lhung la khad par/ thugs ngal bzod med kyi brtan bzhugs mdzad pas

sngar shul du bzhugs pa zhig gzigs pa 'di ni dbus gtsang dus 'khrug des rgyal ba yab sras sogs bstan 'dzin gyi skyes chen rnams la sku gegs che ngor rje nyid sogs kyis sku
rim la rtag 'grus mdzad pas ma skyon tsam byung ba 'di yang shes ldan gzur gnas rnams ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /de nas chu stod bco brgyad nyin lha sa bla brang du lum pa
nga phod sogs dbus drung nga rgyal can rnams kyis khang chen nas dA ching ba dur nga rgyal can dkrong pas dbus gtsang dgra gshed kyi brlag res la bstan don yin tshul gyi
ming snyan thogs pa byung 'dug kyang nyams myong can rnams kyi gzigs dang bka' bstan lugs kyi bstan bcos bcas nas 'byung ba'i bstan don byed lugs rnams kyang 'di 'dra yin
