pa 'dug gam/ gang ltar so sor chings sgrig du phan re'i mdzod pa phral rdzong la/ chings re bral bas log par snying rus kyis mi sdod pa gsung ba'i bka' nan dang zhag shas
nas mgron gnyer bsod nams bsam grub gzim chung du 'bod gnang gi chings la 'gro dgos tshul phebs par yang / chings re med tshul zhus pas sems can re gnyis kyi srog skyobs
byung na'ang chog pas cis kyang 'gro dgos gsung pa bzhin phyin pa na mi brgya phrag du ma'i srog skyobs byung ba yin zhes mgron gnyer

des gleng skad thos shing / bstan 'gro spyi rim bka' 'gyur gsung sgrogs/ sgrol sher 'bum ther/ chos bsrung la bskang ba 'phrin 'chol sogs lan mang bstsal zhing / rje nyid nas
kyang gsol 'debs 'phrin 'chol nan tan bka' drin che ba'i dbus gtsang sogs rgyal khams sems can thams cad phan tshun tshe rabs mang po'i pha ma nye 'brel du gyur pa'i drin
dran shes kyi bde 'jags thugs 'dun rtse gcig gnang mur khrums zla'i nang kha'u chab tshan khar kong po rgyas bskor ba der 'byor gyi mjal phyag tshe dbang zhus skabs tshe
chu mang bar babs cing khong pas dus gzir las 'phros pa'i chags sdang brjod rigs sna tshogs zhus par phyogs ris su mched pa'i gsung 'phros gang yang ma gnang bas gnas
skabs su gsung 'phros mi mkhyen pa ltar gyur kyang / rgyas sras rnams la gser dang bong ba mtshungs pa'i rnam thar dang ma 'ong pa'ang gzigs par mngon no/ /de nas dgung
grangs nyer bzhi pa sa spre snon zla'i nyer drug la rgyal pham so sor phye/ dbyug zla'i nang tsam la gang rgyal bar gong ma chen po'i bdag rkyen bka' drin che bas pho lha
nas mi'i dbang pos ljongs 'dir lung rgyugs nas ring por ma lon par legs 'bul du mdzod pa rdzong bda' gnang bas mchod yon dam pa

rnams gnyis nas gzigs pa dge ba'i 'dod don 'grub thog 'dir 'phral 'byor gyi bka' tham gnang rten bcas legs lam shin tu che ba'ang skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi thugs bskyed du
go /sa bya lo'i lha sa smon lam chen mor dge 'dun zhal grangs chig khri chig stong sum brgya nga bdun tsam la mang 'gyed kyi bsnyen bkur mdzad cing / mkhar kha nas rje btsun
dam pa'i dgongs rdzogs mi sna'i gdong zhu shog rten sgrags rgya chen dang / 'dus sder mang ja/ grwa rer dngul srang re'i 'gyed dang bcas 'byor bar lugs gnyis kyi gnang
skyes rgya chen bstsal/ rgya sog mang pos dge tshul slong zhus par/ mkhan chen dbang phyug phun tshogs la bka' gnang ste de bzhin du mdzad/ skyed lhas mgon khang du zhag
bdun tshe sgrub nyams bzhes dus/ sku khams nyog pa dang dus mtshungs nged rang gi ma lags de'i mnal ltas su skyed lhas nas yin zer ba'i btsun ma skra sil bur 'phyang ba/
mche ba gtsigs pa zhing byung nas/ gong ma rin po che sku khams shin tu mi bde ba'i sku gegs chen po 'dug par zhabs brtan sku rim gang drag dang / lhag tu da lam tshes
brgyad nyin sgrol 'don bya zhing / gsol 'debs tshigs bcad 'di zhabs brtan du thon zer nas shog ril zhig gtad pa shar ba bzhin sgrub pas sku khams kyang

'phral dngas byung / nag zla'i tshes bcu gcig la kho bo btsas/ de nas sa ga'i bdud rtsi ril sgrub nyer brgyad nyin ma lags de nas zhabs brtan gsol 'debs dngos phran 'phul bar
byon pas ril sgril ba'i tshogs dbur rje nyid bzhugs pa bi rWa pa'i rnam pa can la bud med mdog mi 'dra bas bskor ba zhig tu gzigs pa dang / phur dbang thog mar gsan skabs
tsam la yin nam phur dbang zhig gi dus bla ma'i sku las 'od sngon po 'phros pa ma lags rang la phog pas sbrid cing bzhugs mi thub pa lta bus 'dar bun gyi spyan zhal chu
'phrug bde stong gi thugs nyams shar ba dang / gnas skabs de dag tu ngos rnams la tshe dbang zhig stsol tshe zan bum las tshe chu kha dog sna tshogs phebs shing / yang
btsun mor bdag cag rnams la mgon po gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang zhig stsal dus rab gsal gyi bya gdang khar bya rog babs nas skad snyan sgrog cing rjes gnang zhu mi rnams
la lta ba dang / gdal chur chab bzhugs zhig gi dus pu tras bskur byung gsung ba'i rdo gri ka to'i dbyis can logs la las mkhan gyi bla rdo pha wang long bu kha shas 'byar
ba zhig kho bor gnang ba nang so nyams bzo'i dus su pu tra'i gzungs la phul lo/ /yang yab rje mangga'i mtshan can nas rje 'di'i drag las

mngon spyod 'grub par lung bstan ltar skabs shig bsam yas chos skyong chen po thog phebs kyi lung las/ sa skya dge bshes nas nged kyi gnas khang der snron zla'i nya la ngos
kyi gsol kha drag bskul bcas thong / 'dres kyang bstan dgra gdug can tshar gcod pa'i grogs byed gsung ba bzhin mdzad pas/ lcog gi sgo 'gram du sgra chen po dang bcas khrag
phor gang stor byung bas sgo logs su'ang dmar chil gyi byung ba dang bstun rje 'di'i gzigs snang la lcog nang du me lce lhab kyi byung ba zhig shar bas dus der bdud sprul
'ga' der bsgral lam snyam/ yang gzhung zhabs rin po che nas bstan 'gro'i spyi rim du gtor bzlog dgos tshul phebs pa'i zor 'dzin mdzad skabs 'phen nyin skyed lhas phyogs
nas 'brug sgra dang ser rkang 'khyug cing char mun shin tu che khrod rje nyid sku bong rgyun dang mi 'dra ba'i che bar las mkhan 'khor bcas kyi bskor ba lta bus gzugs
med kyi sgra sna tshogs dang bcas phal cher gyi snang bar shar zhing/ char gyi stabs zhabs lham 'dam gyi gsher yod snyam gzims dpon dkon mchog yar 'phel gyi phyi bar brtsam
pa na/ rlan cung zad kyang med pa byung zhing / dgun grang dus kyang gtor zor mi 'khyag pa/ gtor slang la drod skye ba/ dgug gzhug mdzad pas zan ling mdog 'gyur ba ni
kho bo

gzhon nu'i skabs dbang khang du phur bzlog sku rkyang gi sgrub pa mdzad mthar gdab las tshogs yongs dang bcas phyir mdzad dus yang 'brel so drug ma tshar bar la lingga bag
phye rang mdog tu yod pa la/ dgug gzhug rjes ma nas bzung zangs g.ya' sogs kyis byugs pa lha bu'i ljang khur gyur pa zhig shin tu gsal bar mthong ba sogs mngon spyod kyi
las 'grub pa'i mtshan ma 'di bzhin dang / 'og tu'ang rim bzhin 'chad par 'gyur ro/ /de tsam nas yongs 'du'i gnyer khang nas gnyer thog las 'dzin bsod nams mchog ldan gyi
bstan pa gdung brgyud sde bcas kyi zhabs tog tu dmigs g.yul thang gyang rtser ma Ni g.yam brkos steng spen bad sogs kyis spras shing ma Ni lag bskor du ma dang / rnam snang
/ sbyongs rgyal/ rgyal mchog shAkya/ cher rgyas rnams la kun rig rtsa lha so bdun/ byang sems nyan rang sgo ba bcu drug gis bskor ba/ dus gsum sangs rgyas la cho 'phrul
bstan pa'i mdo bkod kyis bskor ba/ bde ba can mngon dga'i zhing bkod sogs bris thang mang ba/ sgrol ma 'jigs pa brgyad skyobs sogs 'bur sku'i rigs/ rje btsun gong ma lnga
sogs sku par du ma/ brgya mchod kyi kong bu ting spos 'dzin mchod khri bcas kha shas/ rgyun gyi yon chab 'bul snod/ dngul ting

bdun cha gsum/ khyams stod phur khang tshoms chen lho byang / dbu rtse/ g.yul thang / dge tsha/ phur bzlog sogs kyi tshogs gdan spus gtsang du ma/ dge tsha'i gur chen sogs
legs byas rgya chen po rim bzhin rgyun bsrings te spel/ de nas dgung grangs nyer drug pa lcags khyi lor gu ru'i ma 'ong lung bstan zhig tu/ lcags pho khyi la hor dmag bod
du lhungs bzhes yod pas/ 'di lo nyen mi 'ong ngam zhes gong dkar dam po blo gros dbang phyug la gzhan 'dras zhus pas/ rang re rnams skyabs mgon dam pa 'di la gsol ba rtse
gcig thob dang skyon mi 'ong gsungs pa bzhin don la gnas/ de dus rje 'dis gzigs snang la sa skya'i chos srung rnams zhal nub gzigs su phebs pa zhig shar bas/ de nas bzung
dus mdos kyi zor kha nub tu bsgyur bar mdzad/ mdzod pa bkra shis don grub dgongs zhu grol tshab gzim dpon bsod nams bstan pa'i rdo rje mdzod par 'khod/ 'di pa gzim 'gag
skya bo'i dus 'gag pa bkra shis su grags shing / lo dar mar chos byas te gzim dpon du 'khod skya ser gnas skabs kun tu zhabs 'gyur che zhing thugs rtsis lhag par yang che/
mchod yon du las phyag zhus dus thugs la btags shing sku drung dpal brtse ba 'khor bcas mchod gzhis

su gnang / lo de'i nang mkhas pa zil gnon chos khri chen mo'i mtha' bskor lcags ri shar nub la sgo nyis hral gnyis re 'phral phugs brling mdzes kyi nyams gso/ dus mdos gzab
ma'i rdor gong / phod ka zhwa nag bse theb/ rnga chung pa'i gar chas/ gser rnga/ rmog khrab/ gri dong / bud med chas gos chen las grub pa sogs dang / tshoms chen gdung khebs
gos kyi lce sgrigs/ gzhung zhabs rin po ches stsal ba'i gos yol khyad mtshar/ gur lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i ru mtshon sogs bca' sgrigs kyi dus mdos gzab ma zhig
kyang bka' drin bskyang ngo / /dgung grangs nyer bdun pa lcags phag lor nged rang gi ma lags de la zas min lta bus snyun gzhi thu mo gdon rgyab bcas byung bar nyin gcig
rje 'dis drag dmar nyams bzhes thog nas bgegs bskrod mdzad pas/ ma lags de'i gzigs ngor btsun mo'i thog tshad dang mnyam pa'i drag dmar gyi sku las me stag du ma 'phros
pas sku lus tshig nyams shar ba dang/ de rjes lhun grub pho brang du drag po sgrol dbang gsan skabs ma lags de'i gzigs ngor rje 'di rdo rje phur pa'i skur gyur pa'i phyag
mtshan rnams rang la bsnun nyams kyi dud khu rnag khrag sogs thon pa'i thugs snang

shar ba bzhin bsnyun las myur du grol zhing/ nged rang gi nu bo sngon ma de btsas dus bu chung sku lus la rma du ma yod pa zhig byung bas gso thabs rkyen sel sogs thugs brtson
mdzad kyang zhag nyi shu nas dus mthar gyur pa'i spur btsun mo rab gsal 'og sa 'bum nang du lo kha shas bzhugs so/ /de nas bla brang phun tshogs gling gi sa chen sku
'dra rin po che bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang brtse chen lha khang du grags pa 'di 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug gi sku thog la bzhengs pa mdzad 'phral lta bu yin 'dug kyang
/ nyams gso byang bskyed sogs kyi snang tshul shar bas de bzhin du mdzad skabs/ kho bos sngon gzhan gnod bskyal ba'i 'bras bu dang / 'phral rkyen klu zhig gi gdug rtsub
'dzoms pas lus thams cad shu thor gyi mnar bar/ rje 'di'i gsung las/ ar po byed bzhin pa 'di'i rtsig bskyed tsam na rdo sgam 'dra bar gnas pa'i sa bdag gi gnod ngo shar
bas de phab la dkyil khang du klu mkhar bzos pa'i nang chug phebs pa bzhin sgrub pas shu ba'ang rim gyis gsos/ de lo'i ril sgrub 'dam la phyag bzo mdzad pa'i phag gzugs
chung ngu zhig bsrung bar bstsal ba bzhin/ phyis su 'og 'don gyi gnod pa phal cher bsrung thub/ de ltar nyams gso mthar phyin skabs rje

nyid ban tshang pa dang bcas pa'i rdo rje phur pa'i rab gnas zhag bdun sbyin sreg phyi skor me tog 'thor ba bcas mdzad dus/ mtshan ltas su gter chos sna tshogs kyi glegs bam
zhig dang / dge slong gzi chen zhig gis pag ril nang nas rin chen ril bu 'khrul med yin zer ba zhig phul ba gzigs pa ni slad nas rin chen ril bu lta bus 'gro phan can du
mas mchog thun dngos grub stsol ba'i mtshan ltas yang dag par mngon no/ /de nas ston nang tsam la ma lags bdag spun bcas gsang sngags pho brang du slebs/ tshoms dmar bzhugs
khri padma can gyi steng nas gsung ngag rin po che'i chos 'khor gnyis pa bskor ba'i slob mar/ ma lags/ rig 'dzin mthu stobs dbang po/ gzims 'og sprul sku/ chos grwa
lho byang gi dge 'dun bcas 'dus par/ ma lags kyi gzigs snang du nyin gcig tshoms dmar gyi nang smugs pas gang ba lta bus chos zhu ba rnams ma gzigs kyang / rje 'di 'ja' 'od
kyi dkyil na rdo rje skyil krung gis bzhugs pa lta bu zhig gsal ba dang / 'gro mgon dpon slob kyi gzigs ngor skabs shig me 'theb sor tsam tshoms dmar phyi nang thams cad
la rgyu bar gzigs pa na/ gnyis kas legs min gsung brtag zhus par/ so so'i nyams snang las byung ba'i 'char sgo yin pas

skyon med gsungs/ gsung ngag rin po che smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa mthar phyin nas chos grwa lho byang gi dge 'dun rags bsdus la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang lung
bcas bstsal/ de nas dgung grangs nyer brgyad du phebs pa chu byi'i dpyid mdzod pa bsod nams dus yol gyi nyin bzhi thog bla ma lha khang gi zangs dra'i nang 'ug pa byung
ba sogs than ltas ngan pa bzlog phyiir phur bzlog glo bur du 'phangs/ mdzod pa de dus las yol bar thugs las shin tu che bar/ ma lags dang bdag cag spun nas thugs gso zhabs
brtan gsol 'debs zhus pa'i phyir phebs su khong lo lnga bcu tsam sdod dgos yod kyang so bdun las ma thub pas nga yang de tsam las mi sdod pa 'dra zhes phebs pa phyis mngon
du gyur/ byang bu lam ston dbu mdzad bzod pa bkra shis kyi spur sbyong gi thod par hU~M yig gsal zhing 'dus tshogs kyi kun rig cho ga nyin gsum dang / e wam chos ldan
sogs la bsnyen bkur/ lo ja'i 'thebs su kha btags Dam brgya sbyor 'jags/ da lta lha mthil rten gras kyi dngul gdung chung ngu 'di sogs bskrun par mdzad/ dbo zla'i nang yum
drung bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo'i thugs bzhed du rin sgang gtsug lag khang du ra sa 'phrul

snang gi gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i thugs rje chen po rang byon bcu gcig zhal dang sku tshad mnya ma pa'i bcu gcig zhal gyi sku bzhengs bzhed kyi sku rgyur dpal sa skya'i
rten 'dam dpe bral ma gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen po dang / 'bras ljongs chos rgyal phyag rdor rnam rgyal gyi rten 'dam klu 'jim rgya bod gnas chen gyi sa sna
rdo sna khyad par dam rdzas sman spos stobs che ba dang bcas par dbo zla'i bcu gnyis srong btsan sgam po'i dus chen nyin rje 'di nyid nas rten gsar par bya ba'i arga'i cho
ga'i byin rlabs dang / gnod sbyin 'khor lo sgrub par mdzad de bzo pa rnams kyis bcu gcig zhal gyi sku rigs lnga dang bcas pa bzhengs pa'i nang bzhugs ring bsrel rnam bzhi
spyi dang khyad par bcu gcig zhal dang don yod zhags pa'i gzugs ring grangs mang / yi ge drug ma dung du nye bar bzhugs te rten gyi bya ba yongs rdzogs zla ba gsum gyi
khongs su grub pa la sku brgyan na bza' mchod chas kyi spras te bzhugs/ yang de dus lha khang chen mo nas spyi bsod la 'byon mi dge 'dun rnams kyi gsungs brtag zhus par
tshigs bcad du bstsal ba'i tshig rigs de las/ /gzhan yang dog gzhi che ba'i ngo zhig la/ /brag ri chu srin gdong pa 'dra ba yi/ /rtsa bar mtsho ni nya mig tsam zhig yod/
/zhes sogs dog gnas

gsungs pa bzhin/ rong chung gi lam de 'dra ba zhig tu bsod nams bzang po rbab la shor tshad pas lag khrid la mdzo zhig yod pa de shor bas rbab tu lhung / snron zla'i tshes
bdun la rgyal mtshan rin chen mdzod par 'khod 'phral gzhung zhabs rin po cher las phyag zhu ba'i thon phyag thog skyabs 'jug sogs gang ci'i snyan sgron zhus par/ rje nyid
nas gegs chags med cing phun sum tshogs par yongs phebs don ltar/ skyon med mjal kha shin tu spro zhing gtan tshigs lon pa sogs legs lam byung / gung sku zhabs rkyen sel
zhu bar chibs bskyod la phur sgrub tshogs dbur phebs skabs mjal 'dzoms dang / gzhan yang dpon g.yog kun la lha dgu'i tshe dbang / sku dngos la byad 'grol sogs lugs gnyis
dang 'brel ba'i thugs bzhed bskong bar mdzad/ phebs zhor mang mkhar chab bzhugs dus mdzod pa yar 'byor mang mkhar du mjal zhur phyin pas gsung 'phros las bdag chen rin po
ches bcos thabs gnang ba'i thugs rjes yar bskyed la chu tshan 'di yang shin tu 'phrod par byung zhes dgos nyams gnang bar ma zad/ de nas bzung sku khams cung zad snyom
par gyur/ gang ltar zla ba de'i bcu gnyis srong btsan sgam po'i tshes mchod thog rje nyid chos grwa rnam

gnyis kyi mkhan chen sogs rdo rje 'dzin pa'i tshogs dang bcas pas rab gnas 'bring po'i cho ga don gnyis lhun grub bzhin mdzad pas rang 'dra'i ye shes pa spyan 'dren gyi tshe
mkhan rin poche dbang phyug phun tshogs kyi gzigs snang la/ nub phyogs bde ba can gyi zhing khams nas ye shes sems dpa' 'od dkar po'i rnam pa can rten gyi thugs dkar thim
pa'i snang ba shar ba bcas byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba 'di nyid kyi drung du btsun ma rgan gzhon bzhi re mos kyis zla drug re bcu gcig zhal dpal mo lugs kyi cho ga
ltar chags su sgrub pa 'di bzhin bskrun par mdzad cing / sring mo rgan pa mchog pa'i kun dga' chos kyi nyi ma btsas/ de nas dgung grangs nyer dgu pa chu glang lo sa ga zla
nang shing bzo rta ra ba ngo g.yog gnyis/ sa skya rang gi bzo pa lnga bcas kyi shing las dang / bal po a ti ka la bcas mi gnyis/ shel dkar zangs bzo ra lam pa dang lha
btsan bcas mi bco lnga/ bar sbug bkras sgang pa sogs mi lnga/ gdong dga' yul chen bcas kyi lcags bzo ba mi bzhi sogs kyis chos khri'i rgya phibs kyi las gra tshugs par 'dzugs
ston sogs rgya cher gnang ste thugs bzhed mthar phyin/ a li chos rje kun dga' bsod nams dpon

g.yog du ma mjal phyag tu 'byor ba'i dngos dpyad khyad mtshar du ma dang / khyad par rje nyid kyi gsung bskang rgyun dkrol dkar mo 'brug sgra phul zhing / chos sde rnam gnyis
kyi mkhan chen dbang phyug phun tshogs las bsnyen rdzogs zhu mi mang du byung ba ni nged rang gi thog phyogs der sa lugs bshad sgrub 'phel ba'i rten 'brel/ a Ni drung
kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma'i yum mchog bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo'i sku rim gyis mtshon 'brel thogs shi gson kun gyi tshogs bsog sgrib sbyongs su mkha' spyod rdo rje
btsun mo'i sku nA ro lugs rin chen du ma bsres pa'i rgyu las gar bu khyad mtshar 'di nyid la thog mar rje btsun drung de nyid nas mkha' spyod mar sbyar ba'i rab gnas dang
/ phyis su rje 'di nyid kyis kyai rdor rab gnas 'bring po bka' drin che bas byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar bzhugs pa 'di yin la/ gong gi las 'phros chos khri'i rgya phibs
steng shod nang gi bla ma yi dam chos bsrung nor lha'i bris sku shing rtsi bcas legs par grub/ de nas dgung grangs sum cur phebs pa shing stag lor chos khri thang mo che'i
rdo chol du gzims gur bsam grub pho brang phubs te rje nyid rdo rje 'dzin pa'i tshogs dang bcas pas dges rdor la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i yon bsgor nger rang dang
phyag

gnyer gnyis bcas bcar ba'i bkra shis rdzas brgyad kyi shis brjod dang bcas kyi mthar dga' ston rgya che ba'i thog gzhis byes nas legs 'bul bzo rigs pa rnams la gla yon gnang
cha gya nom gnang / de dang rjes 'brel mon chung pu tra khang du bskang rgyun gsar 'dzugs la rje nyid phebs pa'i tshe/ sgo rtsar a tsa ra gcig 'byor ba des mjal dar dkar
po zhig phul bar bha la phyag phebs gsung bas/ des kyang rgya skad du lan phul/ gsung bskang skabs sku drung du 'bod pa gnang rjes pho brang du 'khrid par gnang byung bas/
gcer bu 'dom dkris ral lcog can sngo nag lus gnad bcas nas 'dug pa zhig nged rang nas kyang 'khris su mthong gnang cha gzab par bstsal/ tshul 'di ni pu tra nyid dngos
su byon pa yin nam snyam mo/ /lo 'di'i sa ga zla nang khyad 'phags byang mgon khang na pu tra'i mdos bskang tshogs dbur rje nyid phebs mur tshes bcu'i snga dro kha ba tshan
chen 'babs pa dang chabs cig kho bo'i nu bo phyi ma tshangs mchog gam/ ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams mthu stobs dbang phyug bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po 'khrungs par tshe dbang sogs byin rlabs bstsal/ de skabs bstan pa'i gegs chags lta bu yin nam phur sgrub sogs kyi skabs

zhal ngo rnams tsho du mar bzhugs dgos byung bas phun tshogs gling na yum sku drin can de nyid dang a ni lags bzhugs/ rje de nyid lha khang rtse/ ma lags dang ngos spun bdag
mo lha mdzes bu khrid rnams bzhi thog na yod skabs phur sgrub tshugs thog gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang phebs thengs gnyis pa dang / rta nag mkhan chen ngag dbang tshul khrims
bzang po'ang byon/ rigs cha dang bdun pa'i bka' 'gyur zla stod la tshugs pa las rig grwa'i gzigs mor yang rgyal yum de nyid kyis nan tan mdzad/ bka' 'gyur khyams smad
byang du tshugs skabs lha mthil mchod mjal la 'byon zhor bka' 'gyur tshogs gsham nas sku na bgres mo des brgya phyag brgal tsam thugs smon dang bcas mdzad/ zla ba de'i nyer
drug chad pa'i nyer dgu la phun tshogs gling gzim chung du gsung gtor mdzad mur steng grib 'dra ba'i bsnyun gzhi glo bur ba zhig bzhes par phur sgrub gung seng thog de'i
gnas tshul rje nyid la zhus pa bzhin rkyen sel sogs gang ci'i zhal bkod gnang yod 'gro yang zhib par ma nges/ de nas dgongs myul tsam la rgyal yum sku drin can bstan 'dzin
bsod nams bzang mo de nyid dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan par rje sku mched nas kyang skyabs 'jug yang dag bka' drin

bskyang zhing / mtshan 'bum gsung sgrogs dge 'dun bzhi rgyun chog dpon slob shes rab 'od zer dang rab 'byams pa bdun bcas kyi mdzad cing / sku mched nas byang bu lam ston/
thub bstan mkhan chen de nyid nas kyang gsung chog sogs gang 'tshams/ 'dus tshogs nas kun rig sgrub mchod zhag dgu/ gzhan yang mang ja mchod 'bul sogs gzhis su sgrub 'os
rnams dang / gong sa rgyal ba yab sras la skyabs 'jug zhu bar mdzad pa sogs phyogs su sgrub 'os rnams tshang ma mdzad cing / lo mchod khrums zla'i tshes 'gor tshogs chen
cho ga'i rgyun 'dzugs par mdzad do/ /rgya mtshan de dag la dpags na thog mar yum de nyid bco brgyad nas 'byon skabs bco brgyad chen mo'i gsung gong du bkod pa bzhin dkyus
ma dang mi 'dra ba zhig ste/ rang lugs bstan pa'i rtsa ba dpal sa skya pa'i gdung chad la nye skabs bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid bskrun par mdzad pas da lta'i bar
du rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud la re ba byed rgyu byung ba 'di bzhin dang / rje de nyid sku nar ma son par yab rje gshegs pas rang re'i chos srid la rgya'i skor
phyi nang gang sar zhal bkod khyab pa'i 'dzin skyong yang dag dang / bka' 'gyur rin po che gser

chos su bskrun pa dang / dge 'dun gyi sde dang btsun ma'i dgon pa rnams la mthun sbyor phun sum tshogs mdzad pa dang khyad par chu byi lor rgyal yum nyid kyis sngon 'gro lta
bur rin sgang bcu gcig zhal gsar bzhengs gnang zhing / gshegs khar bka' 'gyur 'dus tshogs la phyag bcas thugs smon mdzad pa 'di bzhin la blo ldan rnams kyis dpyad pas dus
gsum mkhyen pa'i ngo mtshar dang zhing brjes nas yang srid kyang da lta'i bar du rang re la phan nges zhig nged rang la gsal po yod kyang re zhig mi spro'o/ /dgung grangs
so gcig tu phebs shing yos lor bla brang shar gyi gzim khang rnying ma ser mor grags pa la nyams gso mgon khang gsar bzhengs rten gtso zhal bram gzugs kyi skur dbu zhabs
bar gsum gyi gzungs cha tshang / 'khor lo 'dod gsol sogs ring bsrel rnam bzhi'iphyur por bkang ba la rab gnas thun mong ba dang khyad par ba mdzad/ sa ga zla nang lha
mdzes bu khrid kyi sras sngon ma 'khrungs kyang ma bzhugs/ snron zla'i yar tshes gza' skar dge bar rje de nyid nas kho bo slob gnyer gyi sgor rjes su bzung bar zhag bcu
lhag nas gnas slob de nyid kyi sku zhabs rin po che thugs brel rgya che bas gdung la sku yon slob gnang dka' ba bcas kho bos zhabs 'gyur zhus na

gsungs ba bzhiin bka' drin bskyangs te bzhugs/ g.yab shar slob gnyer khang du sger chod thog nyin re bzhin sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang dang sa skya bka' 'bum ljags
lung khyug tsam re bstsal/ lo de'i nang du sde dge chos kyi rgyal po bstan pa tshe ring nas bka' 'gyur rin po che gsar bzhengs kyi par phud gdan sa chen po 'dir 'bul sbyor
bka' drin che bar 'dus tshogs nas mchod pa'i yo byad du mas spyan 'dren zhal kod bka' drin bskyangs/ rje nyid la stong 'bul dang / sde dger bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad
bzhengs rgyu'i tsan dan sgrub yon stong dngul la nye bar phebs pa bzhin de 'phral thugs brtson gyis bal yul du don gnyer bka' drin che bar tsan dan sdong dum pang du theg
tshad du ma 'byor ba 'di yang rje nyid dang chos rgyal de nyid bcas kyi ngo mtshar rnam thar du mngon zhing bstan pa spyi sger gyi sku rim du mgon po drug cu'i gtor bzlog
zhu gnang bzhin zor las bka' drin che bar 'phen nyin tshoms chen rgya mthong nas pu tra dang bran bdud yul mi lta ba bzhin stang gis gzigs pa zhig dang / phyir phebs skabs
seng ge sgor sgo ma seng gdong ma yul gyi gzigs pa lta bu zhig byung zhing / sde dge'i sku tshab bstan pa bzang po dang

tshe ring 'phel 'khor bcas la'ang lugs gnyis bdag rgyan bka' drin che bar bstsal/ bka' 'grur bzhugs sa'i kun ra dang snar thang bka' 'gyur kyang par 'debs mdzad pa bcas lha
chen bkra shis lha khang du bzhugs/ bdag sogs skal dman gyi ngor zhabs 'bam gyi bsnyun gzhi lci mo bzhed tshul gyi mjug 'phrod bzhes su kha'u sman chab la phebs skabs skyed
lhas su gsol tsha sgrub nas chibs thog phebs shin tu dka' bar chibs chen chos 'phel rag pas nyal stabs su 'dug nas da chibs shig lta bu'i rnam 'gyur bstan pa bzhin chibs
pas yang sug bzhi dal bus srang nas 'gros dal brel ran pos sku la ngal ba mi 'byung ba'i sgo nas gdan 'dren zhus pas kun ha las/ dus de tsam la mi dang yab sras rnams
yas mar chibs bsgyur thog mjal zhur mdzod pa lha rtse gcan lung gzhis rtse sogs su lan mang 'gro dgos byung / de nas dgung grangs so gnyis su phebs pa me 'brug lor lha mdzes
dbu khrid kyi sras rjes ma 'khrungs kyang zhag shas nas gshegs/ nged rang phur sgrub la thog mar 'gro shag yin kyang / phur sgrub tshugs nyer sgo rum du brtag sgril
byed gsungs nas mdzad pas mthon/ de lo lha chen khyams stod ag glen ka brgyad

kyi ya gyal ka ring gsum nyen gtsong dogs gnas gang yang med par hor zla bdun pa'i tshes bcu gsum nyin 'gyel pa'i glo bur rdib gzhom byung bas ris med dgon la mang bkol zhig
btang ba'i nyams bzo 'phral tshugs kyi gnang ba bzhin/ zhig gso bris rtsi sogs gsar bskrun rab gnas bcas dgongs bzhed bzhin 'grub/ ma 'gyangs par rgyal ba yab sras mi dbang
sku zhabs rnams zhal rgyas la bla brang rgyal mtshan mthon por phebs pas mnga' ris nas gung sku zhabs gu ge chos rgyal gzhan yang dpon khag kha shas bcas stong phrag
skor mjal zhur phebs zhor sa skyar yang byon pas chibs bsu thab 'dzin ser phreng sogs dang bcas phebs 'phral 'byor phyag gsol ston zab rgyas bzhugs sgar bya khra mar gnang
/ bzhugs zhag gsum gyi nyin bar mar zhabs brtan thog gung sku zhabs nas dgu tshan nyer lnga/ gu ge chos rgyal mnga' ris dpon sogs zhabs 'bring rnams nas kyang 'bul chen
bcas/ dpon g.yog drag bsdus la rdo rje phur pa'i stod las byang chub sgrub dbang/ sa skyong nyid la mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang tshe dbang grub rgyal ma sogs gnang/ dbang
yon kyang dngul srang brgya skor 'bul bar mdzad/ thon phyag bzhugs gral zab rgyas kyi thog legs cha'i dngos 'bul rgya che ba

bstsal te gzhis rtser phebs/ de nas dbyug zla'i tshes dgu la rje nyid kyang chibs bsgrur te gzhis rtser phebs par rgyal ba yab sras mi dbang chen po bcas nas sngar srol bzhin
gyi bskur bzo bka' drin bskyangs/ 'on kyang rgyun gtan sku gcong che khar sku grib la nyan blang bag ge'i bsnyun bzhes tshul gyi sku nyams zhan cing phebs mi thub pa tsam
byung yang thugs rus kyi mchod yon mjal zhur phebs pas mjal dar rtse sprod bzhugs khri sogs rnam gzhag bzang po sngar srol bzhiin gyi dbu 'phangs bstod par mdzad/ phan
tshun 'bul gnang nam mkha' mdzod sgo phye zhing khyad par gong sa mchog nas mgar thar nas yar phebs sku 'khyos su sgo rum nang so skyed lhas bsam brling sogs mgon khang
kha shas su sngar ma mthong ba'i nang mdzod sgron dar sna lnga khyad mtshar/ shel dpyad khyad 'phags du ma/ ljon ja spus legs phon che ba sogs bstsal zhing gzhan gyi gsol
ston ring sku mdun du bzhugs par gsol zas bsod pa du mas bsnyen bkur che skabs sku 'khris na dge lugs bla ma kham chen zhig bzhugs pa des rje 'di nyid la na bza' bco ba
sogs thugs nye dpe med mdzad de gsol ston grol/ bar skabs shig tu klu sdings sa su mi dbang yab sras mjal bar phebs pas dkar spro'i thog

'bul ba rgya cher gnang zhing gsung 'phros ci ris mthar bka' sgo skyabs 'jug zhu bar mdzad pa sogs gus 'dud bka' drin bskyangs/ zhabs phyi byings la dbu gur phyir shur phyag
mchod yon nas phebs phyag kyang zab par stsal/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen par mjal phyag skabs kyang bdag rgyan rtsis chen bka' drin che zhing gsolaras gya nom gnang / phyis
su rje nyid kyi bka' las kho bo gzhis rtser na skabs paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa mjal bas bder song zhes gsung dngos las thos gzhis rdzong sprel po sogs mjal zhu ba
dang shur phyag zhu mi grangs med byung / thar rtse rdo rje 'chang dang rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku yang phebs par thar rtse rje'i gsungs las rje 'di mchod yon mjal zhur sku
nyams zhan pos phebs pa gzigs pas spyan chab dbang med shor byung phebs shing de dus kyang tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs 'bul bar mdzad/ de dang dus mtshungs dbus nas chos
skyong zhig gi lung la dbyug zla'i tshes bco lngar dge bshes la sku dog yod pas sku rim zab dgos zhes phul ba dang ma lags der glo bur spyan la sha 'dzer byung bar gnas
slob bzod pa bkra shis nas bse mgon chen por khrus gsol du byon pas zhal 'bag yongs rdzogs dar

gyis bstums nas bzhugs 'dug pas gung sku zhabs kyi snyan dar sgron pa yin nam snyam zhing mda' sogs kyi zhal khebs bsal nas mar byon dus gsung las sngar dpon chen zhig gis
kyang mgon por dngul gyi lkog stegs phul bas lkog ma skrangs pa bzhin da lam kyang zhal ras bstums pa des skyon yin 'dug pas gdangs 'gro gsungs pa bzhin mngon du gyur cing
phyis su de rang gi rtog par thog mar zhal ras dar bstums rje de nyid gzhis rtser zhing brje nye la 'og tu bshad pa'i rten 'brel rnams 'grig pas re zhig zhabs pad brtan
pa yin nam snyam ste ma lags de'i mnal ltas su ban de lus bong can zhig nas dbyug zla'i bco lngar sku zhabs rin po che la gsol ba ma btab na mkha' 'gros gdan 'dren par 'dug
go zer mur rje de nyid dang ma lags chos grwa lho byang gi dge 'dun bcas phyi skor du byon pa'i mthar bzhi thog dbang khang bzhugs khrir rje nyid bzhugs song bas/ ma
lags rang gi zhal 'don bskulbskus bas 'dus tshogs nas gsol 'debs mdzad pa zhig shar ba bzhin gzhis rtser bang phyin shad rdzong gi bco lngar slebs pa dang gong gi chos skyong
lung bstan de'ang 'byor zhing / 'dir yang bka' 'gyur gsungs sgrogs/ tshe mchog bskang ba/ sgrol 'don sogs zhabs brtan sku rim 'phral

sgrub zhus pas/ gzhis rtser yang sku la dngas bskyed byung 'dug pas na bse mgon chen pos gnas slob de la rgyud bskul 'dra mos zhal khebs bsal du 'jug par mdzad dam snyam zhing
'bras bu'ang de bzhin no/ /de ltar gzhis rtse'i thugs brel rnams chod pas yar phebs zhor ngor du spyan 'dren mdzad pa bzhin chibs bsgyur gyi phebs lam thog lha chung
sgang rgyud pa'i nang la phyag nas bstsal/ de nas ngor pa'i chibs bsu thab bsu'i sna drangs dgon pa dang khad nyer 'dus tshogs nas ser phreng gi spyan drangs 'phral bla brang
nas bsnyen bkur grub rjes thar rtser bzhugs/ zhag lnga'i ring la bla brang khag sor sor spyan 'dren dang bzhugs tsher sogs su nye mkho'i zhabs tog phul phyin bcas gnas
gzigs mchod 'bul mang 'gyed khrom dbang nang dbang mjal phyag zhu mi spyi sger tshang ma'i re ba 'grub par mdzad cing / gdan sa pa 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong de nyid
lugs zung mkhyen spyan yangs shing zhabs drung yas man sku dngos dang sku tshab gzhan yang dgon pa'i las sne rnams mkhyen rab dang pher yongs can du bzhugs pas/ phan
tshun gnyis ka'i legs lam rang 'grig byung zhing / khyad par thar rtse rdo rje 'chang de nyid nas tshe dbang gur mgon khro

bcu'i rjes gnang sogs 'bul bar mdzad cing bzhugs 'tsher shin tu spro bar byung 'dug ngor nas chibs bsgyur gyi gnas su bzhugs zhag gi de khul la mjal phyag bstsal zhing chu
mig sogasal phyag nas mdzad pas chu rgyun bzang por gyur/ de nas chibs bsgyur gyi Da Di kha lhas bla ma mgon khang dpon slob/ gnyer rgan sogs kyi rta thab bsu sngon 'gro'i
shab dge sdings bla brang dang nye bar ser phreng glu gzhas sogs kyi spyan 'dren gyi gzim chung du phebs 'phral dang bzhugs zhag ring gsol ston legs 'bul bsnyen bkur mjal
phyag gsung bskang phyag nas sgrub 'thor mang 'gyed khrom dbang sogs bka' drin skyang ste rim gyis chibs bsgyur ngos gdan sar phebs nye'i skabs sa skyar yang de sngon
nas bag ge yod mur nged rang gi nu bo de yang bag ge'i na skabs yin pas kun tsher zhing rje 'di phebs pa'i dga' spro zung sbrel thog nas smin drug zla nang phebs nyin snga
dro bkra shis dar rgyas dang gdan sar phebs skabs kyi bca' sgrigs rnams sngar srol bzhin bgyis pa'i nged rang dang a lce spun nas bla brang zam gdong du phebs bsu mjal
dar phyag 'bul phyag dbang zhus te dam pa gang gi bsti gnas su phebs pa'i sang nyin tshoms chen du gsol ston legs 'bul de nas mgon khang rnams la gtang rag sku 'khyos

gsool ras gya nom mang 'gyed sogs bka' drin bskyangs/ rang rang gi las ngan smin pa lta bu'i ma lags dang bdag cag spun rnams bag ge dogs bcas kyi 'chi la khad du gyur dus
rkyen sel bka' dbang rjes gnang byabs khrus ljags chu glud rdzong sogs sgo du mas dus min 'chi ba las bskyabs pa 'di kho na'i sku drin kyang gzhal dka' 'o/ /de ltar bdag
sogs nad las grol mur bdag mo lha mdzes bu khrid kyang nad des smyung bar bcos dang rim gro sogs rtse skyong gnang rung sku gegs kyi rnam pas lnga lam du gshegs khar dbu
mgoor phebs pa'i skyabs 'jug dang spur sbyong rjes sgrub dge tshogs rgya cher bka' drin bskyangs shing / khyad par byang bu lam ston rje nyid nas gnang skabs kho bo'ang yod
pas dri rten byang 'dzin snyug ma sogs la drod tsha chil ba bcas sku dngos la lam ston mdzad pa lta bu byung zhing / spur tshwa dang ring bsrel rnam bzhi bzhugs pa'i 'od
dpag med kyi 'jim sku che ba la rab gnas dang mchod pa sogs bstar/ lo shas dus mchod lta bur mkha' spyod ma'i tshes bcu'i cho ga dge 'dun kha shas la gnang ngo / /de nas
