gi bka' sgrub zhabs phyir kho bos kyang blor yod rnams mnyam 'don zhu bar stsal bas/ skal pa mchog tu bzang bar gyur to/ /

de nas smin drug zla nang tsam la nad 'khrun yongs rdzogs chod pas mgo zla'i bde mchog sgrub mchod dang dus mdos sogs la kho bos phyin par dus mdos nyer gsum nyin 'cham sku
rnams la snyan shal 'bul bar rje nyid phebs nas tshogs gsham du tshogs phyag mdzad byung bas khri thog tu sdod mi nus pa lta bu byung zhing / 'di skabs chig sgrub kyi zhal
gtor bzlog zhig kyang gnang ngo / /de ltar dgung grangs so drug yan gyi ngo mtshar mdzad pa rnams rags tsam las zhib pa ni zin bris med pas rnam thar chen mor yang ma
'khod cing rje nyid la gzhan gyi rtogs brjod gsung bar zhus kyang kho bor rnam thar mi dgos gsung pas 'di tsam las spro bar ma nus shing / dgung grangs so bdun pa ni dgos
pa'i dbang gi 'og tu 'chad do/ /gang ltar gong smos ltar bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa 'di nyid kyi gsan bsam mthar phyin nas/ bsgom pas thugs nyams su star tshul ni kyai
rdor rdo rje phur pa/ mgur mgon rnams kyi gzhi bsnyen sbyin sreg bcas mthar phyin zhing de rnams kyi kha gso'i ljags bsnyen grangs mang dang / gzhan tshe sgrub rigs kha
shas/ rta mgriin skyer sgang pa sogs yi dam du ma'i ljags bsnyen zla zhag grangs bcad 'ga' re yod 'dra yang kho bos ma rtogs/

nyin zhag phrug re'i nyams bzhes ni ldang ba'i rnal 'byor gyi bzhengs te/ tshe dpag lha dgu/ bla ma bzhi khro/ grub rgyal lugs gur mgon dkar po rnams kyi tshe sgrub mdzad kyang
ljags bzlas kyi grangs ma nges/ gur bdun mar tshe sngags phreng 'khor/ srung sngags rnams nyer gcig sogs/ dkar cha bzhi/ dbyug gu mar 'chang bu/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i
sbyin sreg lam dus rgyas par skyabs 'gro dang srung sngags nyer cig yig brgya lnga bcu bskor/ rtsa sngags phreng 'khor/ snying po/ nye snying / yum dang 'khor sngags rnams
kyang grangs bcad re yod 'dra/ lam dus 'bring po yang de dang cha 'dra/ lam zab phyi ma dang bir bsrung phyi mar ang ku li grangs bcad sogs mdzad de/ gzims khri nas bzhengs
skabs sku rags 'ching ba soogs na bza' bzhes ring tshe sgrub gur bdun brgyud 'debs dang yab rje'i sku bstod/ sa skya nad grol/ gu ru'i gsol 'debs bod 'bangs bde ba'i
dpal ster/ badzragu ru phreng 'khor tsam gsungs pa der rang nas nges shing / gzhan yang yod dam/ de nas mjal phyag/ tshogs dbu phyag dpe thugs rtog chos 'chad/ gsung byang
/ thugs brtag zhal bkod sogs gnang dgos yod na de bzhin dang / gung tshigs grol nas gsung bskang sogs mdzad/ rgyun par de

nas bdag bskyed phur chung gtor bsngo chen mo'i steng beg tse rdo rje rab brtan ma dmag zor bran bdud rgyal chen rnams la gtor bsngo/ yig brgya lnga bcu tsam/ mgo gnon nyer
gcig chos skyong rnams kyis sngags lnga bcu sogs grangs mang nyung sna tshogs mdzad nas bskyang ba thugs dam ma/ brgyad bcu bzhi/ nyer gsum nyer dgu sogs la gong gi steng
bskang gsar so so'i dus gtor/ gung tshigs rjes sAtstsha'am zan par ci rigs/ gsol zas gang gnang yang lus kyi lha gdan gsum tshang ba mchod zhes dang / chos skyong 'ga'
re'i mtshan gsung zhing / spyan dmigs zengs mdzad pa lan cig min pa yang yang mthong thos byung bas 'di la dpags na 'dod yon lam khyer gyi dgongs pas nyes pa dang lung ma
stan gyi bag med du 'gro ba'i skabs mi srid dam snyam/ nyi phyed man nas srod phyi mo'i bar thugs dam gnang ba zhig 'dug pas/ lam zab bir bsrung nang ma 'jam nag sme brtsegs
dud ljang rdo rje khrab ring / seng gdong sngon mo/ rta mgrin skyer sgang 'byung 'dul/ dregs 'dul/ gur drag khyung nag phur pa gong khug ma rnams kyi ljags bzlas grangs
ma nges shing / bsrung 'khor brag rdzong mar yi ge bdun ma dang bcu gnyis ma phreng 'khor/ shA sa na drug cu sogs dang bcas mdor na thugs dam 'khor

yug lta bu dang / gzhan yang chos spyod smon lam 'ga' zhig kyang gnang zhing / ljags chu/ srung ba/ ser srung / char 'bebs/ rlung gnon/ sri gnon/ gtad hrul/ lha bsangs/ chab
klu/ seng ge sgra'i cho ga glud rdzong rigs du ma/ gto bcos/ phyag mo sogs gdul bya gang la gang 'dul de la der ston gyi dus 'da' bar mdzad/ chags sdang gi gsung sgros
sam/ kha 'jam sems gdug g.yo rgyu sogs ngan spyod dri tsam yang mi mnga' zhing / 'gro ba spyi dang khyad par rgya bod shugs ring mgron po phyug zhan/ gnas skor ba sprang
'khyam/ mi drag zhan khos ka med rigs la lhag par yang brtse zhing / sku gsung thugs kyi rang bzhin drang po las nged rang lta bu gdug rtsub ye mi mnga' 'o/ /de ltar rtogs
pa mngon du gyur nas bstan 'gro'i don du gsung chos stsol ba'ang / bde kyai gsang gsum bdag med ma kun rig tshe dpag lha dgu rnams kyi dbang grangs mang / rdo rje phur
pa'i stod las dbang shin tu mang ba/ smad las rjes gnang bcur nye ba gur drag dbang kha shas sbyongs dkyil bcu gnyis sogs dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa tshar kha shas/ bla
ma zhi khro/ lcags sdong / grub rgyal rnams kyi tshe dbang grangs mang mda' 'phel ma kha shas/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser 'byung 'dul rnam

'joms/ sme brtsegs lugs gnyis rta mgrin skyer sgang / seng gdong sngon mo/ 'jam nag khyung khra nag rnam rgyal sogs yi dam du ma'i rjes gnang dang / gur lha brgyad/ khro bcu/
zhal bsnyen dus/ dur khrod bdag po/ pu tra'i rjes gnang le tshan bran bdud dkar bdud sogs bstan srung rjes gnang du ma/ dug dbang rdo rje pha lam/ phyag rdor gtum po'i
dug dbyung / bsnub lugs byad 'grol/ seng ge sgra'i gdon 'grol/ mkha' 'gro grib sel sogs rkyen sel du ma/ sa skya bka' 'bum sogs ljags lung du ma/ gsung ngag tshar gsum sogs
'khrid du ma te smin grol lam bzang gi dga' ston ci yang 'gyed par mdzad pas/ zhal slob gyi gtso bo thar rtse rdo rje 'chang / gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang / brag rtsa rdo
rje 'chang / thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims mtshan can/ zhe dgon bum 'dzin rab brtan bzang po/ gong dkar mkhas grub blo gros dbang phyug bla ma mchod dpon/ chos grwa
rnam gnyis kyi mkhan thog shas/ ngor gyi dbon mkhas grub thor tsam/ chos grwa lho byang dge 'dun khyod nas lugs gnyis la pher yongs can rags rim dang khyad par sku thog
de la bka' ram sgrigs pa sogs blo gsal yon tan can mang po dang/ byang pa rnams kyang cho ga phyag len gzhan las nges pa lho

byang gnyis ka gsung gra bzang ba sogs bla ma'i byin rlabs gzhugs pa 'dra mo dang / gzhan yang rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku sogs bu slob phyogs tha dad na bzhugs pa du ma dang
/ grub mtha' ris med mkhas grub kha shas/ mnga' ris gtsang lho byang mon 'brog dbus dgas kong khams sogs rigs rgya nag sogs kyi sku drag du ma sogs gtsug lag zung ldan rnams
nas bstan 'gro'i don gdul bya so so'i skal ba dang 'tshams pa'i sgo nas 'phral yun phan bde spel ba rgya cher bskrun par mdzad de rang snang klong du phebs pas gzhan
snang zil gyis gnon pa chos nyid bzhin skye dgu du ma'i gtsug la zhabs rdul dmar 'od kyi khyab par mdzad pa gong ma bdag po chen po g.yung Ting rgyal pos bka' glegs rin
po che srid na mngon par btsan pa'i phyag rgya dbang mdangs gzi 'bar gyis spras pa'i nam mkha' mdzod sgo phye ba lta bu'i gsol ras gya nom lan gnyis tsam phebs par zhu lan
byin rten dang rje nyid kyi sku skal du gyur pa'i dngos po bzang dgu stobs par mdzad/ gong ma chen po'i sku tshab lha sar bzhugs mi zhig gis kyang mdzod pa lha sar 'gro
zhor zhig la sa skya'i gnas tshul zhiib dris kyi rje 'di nyid la mi phyed dad pa brtan pos thal mo sbyor zhing de skabs zhabs 'bam gyi snyun tshul gsan pas spyan chab

sil ba tsam gyi gdung shugs bcas zab bzhes 'thus ma shor ba dgos tshul nan slob mdzad pa'i rgya nag lugs kyi zhabs la 'byar sman bu ram 'dra mo shog bu dang gos kyi rgyab sha
can bcu lhag tsam 'bul 'byor byung ba dang bod kyi mi rje btsan po rim nas phu dud zhus shing mdzum li rgyal po'i mi sna/ 'brug pa'i sde srid rim byon sogs chen po mang
pos gus 'dud dbu 'phang bstod chos skyong dang lha 'dre dregs pa can rnams kyang dbang du mdzad pa lta bu'i bka' sgo dang springs yig thos pa tsam gyi gzhan la phan thogs/
kha sbyor yan lag bdun ldan mngon du mdzad pas rdzu 'phrul thugs mkhyen sogs kyi lo rgyus smra ba byis pa mtshar bskyed du zad mod/ 'on kyang gong seb tshags rnams su
thor re ba rnams dang 'dir yang cung zad smos na skabs shig shangs phyogs nas 'ong pa'i slong mo ba mig long ba zhig byung bar thugs rje tshad med g.yos pa'i phyag dbang
ljags chab gnang ma thag rang phye byung yang de bzhin gshegs pa dang lha byin gyi dpe ltar phyis su sku drin khyad gsod byas skad thos/ sku na phra skabs sgrol dbang bka'
sgrub zhig gi gseng dbar gsol dpon thugs rje bkra shis kyi zhag phor dkar yol yu thung steng zhabs gnyis kyi ljid 'gel bar mdzad kyang gas chag ma byung ba dang/ rgya
dpon bla brang du gtor spod

la phebs skabs zhig bla ma mnyam med pa'i khrung sing rdza snod de mjal bar mdzad pas mthil nang nas bdud rtsi rang rdol gyi rje nyid dang zhabs phyi kha shas bcas la khyor
ba re tsam bzhes rgyu byung ba dang / rab 'byams pa dge 'dun dpal bzang gi kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen phreng bar byin rlabs mdzad pas dri bzang thul ba sogs byung zhing / yang
sde dge bla ma bkra shis yar 'phel nas lan cig rje 'dir 'byung 'dul sku zhig 'bul grabs yod dus sku mdun du ma 'byor tsam la rje 'di'i de'i phyag rgya yang yang mdzad zhes
thos shing / shing stag rta zla'i nang gzims shar mgon khang du zhal bskang khri tshar mdzad dus mon phrug mang pos shing 'bras sgog btsong sogs phul ba'i gzigs snang
ma lags der shar ba las 'phros pa yin nam/ yang na de sngon gang yin kyang gong gi dpon slob de'i phros zhig la gzims shar mgon khang du rje 'di la yum chen sring mo bzhi
'dra ba'i 'bras mchan phul ba yin zhes lung bstan phal cher gab tshig lta bur stsol bar mdzad pa bzhin bdag gi bla ma 'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes de nyid nas gsung brtag
zhu lan du rong dang stag gzig sogs la gras pa'i gab tshig mthar sku rim rnams phebs pa bzhin 'gyangs min nas rkyen 'ga' zhig

gi mgul par skrang chen zhig byung dus sku rim rnam grangs du ma mdzad kyang skyed ma byung bar rje 'di'i gsung brtag de la thugs rtog gnang bas de nang nas 'jigs byed drug
cu 'phen dgos de las 'dug pas 'phral tshugs kyi phangs pa na gtor ma phyir 'gro ba dang mgul skrang glo bur du rdol zhes ngor chen de nyid kyis gsung las thos shing / dbus
gtsang zing bun dus rgyal rtse mes srong nas yas mas su phyogs pa 'am gang du'ang ma the ba legs min gsung brtag zhus par dbus phyogs bgyis na rtsa ba nas stong / gang
yang ma byas na pha gzhis dang bral/ gtsang phyogs byas na byus legs bzhin rim gro bcas bstsal bas mngon du gyur zhes khong sde pa tsho gsung/ 'brog skar mgon na mur 'tsho
min zhus par nyi ma la rtsar slebs pas bcos med 'on kyang rim 'gro phran tsam phebs pa bzhiin 'gyangs min nas dus chos su gyur/ lu spe kun dpal thar rtser 'jigs byed chos
bka' zhu bar 'gro dus sa gtsang min gyi the tshom la sang rang thon pa rgyug gnang bas/ thar rtse rje sang sku mtshams gnang bzhed kyi do nub 'byor bas sku mtshams 'gyang
thog nas 'dod chos thob pa'i yar 'byor/ 'di kha'i 'bul sdud 'phang ye bla ma bstan pa'i skye ba gdan sa'i shar gyi sde khrod yong phebs pa bzhin tshong dpon gzhung mgron
gyi bu

ban tshang pa bstan pa de byis pa'i skabs shin tu gsal ba sogs mang du yod 'dra/ yang mi min gyi phrin las sgrub tshul ni/ skyed lhas su bcad rgya'i skabs shig gang nas 'ong
med pa'i bande smug ring zhig gi thub dbang 'dud 'dul ma'i sku seng khri rdo snying 'dra zhing sku dngos do lo g.yang kri 'dra bar sku dang bzhugs khri rang grub ma zhig
gzim dpon rdo rong pa brgyud phul bar ga nas yin dang gar 'gro dris la bdag rgyan gyis gsung pa bzhin de 'phral rtsad pas/ su la'ang mthong thos med pa yal ba ltar gyur/
'di ni sngon 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos bsam yas su zhal 'bag smug chung nyams gso mdzad dus bande zhig gis rgya tshal dang ba so'i mi mgo rlon gzugs bcu dgu phul
nas gar song med pa dang 'dra zhing thub sku khyad can de nyid zhal byang 'byar ba deng sang kho bos spyil bu 'dzam gling phun tshogs dpal 'bar gyi rten gras la bzhugs/
gzhan gong du bshad pa ltar bse mgon chen po'i thugs rten gnam lcags rdo rje'i mtshon sku gsung thugs rten byin can khyad mtshar mang po dang / rgya sbug log 'dren tshar
gcod sogs rol cha spus legs du ma sogs rten dang mchod cha'ang bla ma gong ma rnams dang mtshungs par phyag 'byor byung ba sogs rnam dkar phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab

po/ /de nas dgung grangs so bdun pa lcags bya rta zla'i nang sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung dgung keg rkyen sel sku tshe sgrub pa'i bcad rgyar dad ldan rnams kyi gsol btab
bzhin phebs dus ma lags de nas zhabs pad brtan dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan zhu bar mdzad cing sku mtshams dus gzims 'od dang 'gag pa dpal dar nas kyang gsol ba btab par sngar
gyi sa gtsang min des thugs sbyong byung ba sogs snyigs dus rgyu mtshan du mar thugs skyo kho na'i gsung 'byon mur slar yang lam sdem sku tshab slebs pa gzhan gyis zhu ma
nus kyang sku gnyer rtogs ldan du grags pa'i rtog med rang bzhiin gyi 'phros su zhus pas thugs lhag par yang skyo bzhes kyis de 'phral tshe sgrub sdud par mdzad nas pho
brang du byon skabs spyan ltas bzang min sogs phros zhu ba rnams la ltas kyang bzang du rang ma byung shing bzlas pa 'gro chung bse mgon bzhugs khyim du bas grib pa lta bus
mi mthong zhing / yab rje de nyid yang yang dmigs ltas su phebs pas shin tu dran pa zhig byung / gdung spun la gsung ngag slob bshad 'di 'phral du phrod re byed gsungs/
de nas thugs brel gzhan gyi mur dpyid zla zhig la kha'u chab

la phebs pa'i zhag bzhi'i nub gur 'di rmugs pa 'dra ba zhig gis gang byung ltad mo yang che tsam byung phebs pa zhig kyang byung 'dug pas tshul 'di mus chen sems dpa' chen
po dang sngags 'chang chen po sogs zhing rje nye'i gsung dang khyad ma mchis/ lha chen byang shar lcags ri'i spang bad nyams gso gnang / nag zla'i mjug tsam la gzims shar
mgon khang du pu tra'i mdos zor sgrub gnang gi rol mo kho bos zhabs phyi zhus shing phyir 'phen gyi zhabs rjes su'ang yod/ sa kar ril sgrub la phebs dus shog gnang yang
gsang 'dus sgrub mchod la thog mar 'gro ba dang thug pas dgongs pa zhus/ ril sgrub mdzad skabs phal cher du 'di lo'i ril bu g.yer du thon zhig byed yag po 'dug gam zhes sku
'khrigs pa rnams la gsung par gzim 'od nas 'phel stobs che bas ka pA la rnams nas lud cing mdog shin tu bzang bar gda' zhus/ de skabs tsam la rtag tsher gangs mog por
song ba dang / mus gling kha'i ru khang chu mig lud pa/ khyad 'phags lho'i mgon khang thug po chag pa/ wa rgyal dang 'ug pa'i skad ngan 'don pa/ lcags spre'i dgun rig 'dziin
pho brang rab gsal steng bya rog tshang bsags pa/ mchod shing kha shas sgo ral ba/ ma lags de nyid kyi mnal ltas su nyi ma phyed yol la nub pa/ thod mdzes

dkyil stor ba/ spyan long ba sogs byung zhing nang so'i gtor mar byi skyon che zhing bla mtsho mdog mog por byung ba/ glo bur thar rtse nas gsung shog ched mngags 'di lo skyabs
mgon mchog la phebs 'grul zhig phral du yong nye 'dug pas sku rim gnang dgos gsung par dngos su 'grul mi 'ong gzhan gang shes gnang bas ma lags dang phyag gnyer gzims
'od sogs kyi do dam gyi tshe chog rnam rgyal bskang phrin gsung sgrogs mang ja sgrol 'don seng ge sgra'i cho ga brgya bzhi sogs 'dir sgrub 'os dang mus nang gzhi dgon ngor
bya gling bsam yas rab gra sog la'ang sku rim 'phral thon gyii zhabs brtan 'bad sgrub ring nas snron zla'i lha mo mchod ran pas ma phebs na legs tshul ma lags nas zhu
bar mdzad par 'di lo cis kyang 'gro slar mi shes zhes phebs shing / lha mchod la phebs pas rtsa sked kyi thad tsam du rgyu mtshan med par thugs la skyo shas drag po byung
zhes gsung las dngos su thos/ de'i sang tshoms chen du sa bcud bum gter phon chen sgrub gnang thog ser ma thor bu'i rnam pa 'dra ba'i sku la 'dar bun sogs gsung chog mdzad
ma thub pas yar phebs 'phros rnams mchod dpon pas sdus/ de nas rim bzhin gsol sman sku rim gsol zas sogs gang sar sman pa'i ngag bzhin 'gyod med dang

mkha' 'gro bsu bzlog bcas tshang mas sgrim khul yin kyang 'di yin med pa'i snyun gzhi sku shed chag stobs che zhing gsol dang je zhan la 'gro ba las snyun zug sogs gang yang
ma byung bas rim gyis dngas bzhes yong re dang rje nyid nas kyang gsung ngag slob bshad gnang shag gi mur brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang dang thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims
bzang po byon pas brag rtsa rjer mjal kha dang / thub bstan mkhan chen la sngar nas rkyen sel bzhes mu yin pas de skabs kyang tshe dbang gur drag dbang gur khro bcu'i
rjes gnang sogs gsan par/ gzim chung nas 'do ler gdan 'dren zhus pa thub bstan mkhan chen des gzigs pas a kha gsung zhi nga spyan chab mdzad de dus gsung 'phros rang bzhin
skabs nged nas chos rnams ma 'phrod pa byung na thar rtse dang / brag rtsa ba sogs la zhus shig gsung / 'o na de dus gnas gsar rje sogs mi gsung ba ci yin snyam na/ thar
rtse dang brag rtsa rjes tho mar rjes su bzung nas bla ma de gnyis kyi gzhan ston par mdzad dgos kyi rten 'brel zhig yod par sems/ gang ltar tshes dgur snyun tshul bzhes
nas bcu gsum bar dngas lod res 'jog dang de nas je zhan du phebs pas gzhung sger nas zhabs brtan sku rim btud mar sgrub bcu dgu nas

thugs dam nyams bzhes rnams sngar las yun ring bar mdzad/ mgul glo dang mnal yer ba sogs byung bas zhal dkar ba dang gzim chung pa'i em ji gnyis nas glo gcog mnal 'gugs kyi
gto dang / kho bor sngags 'bul dgos bka' phebs kyi lan ngag sdus su da nas 'byung ba'i sngags dang gto sogs so so skye bos sangs rgyas la dbu skor 'bul ba ltar gyur kyang
/ bla ma mnyes byed gang yin bya zhees pa ltar sems dge ba la nyes med tsam byung e yod/ gang na'ang nyer bzhi'i nyin bzhugs g.yab tu bzhugs gdan gyi zhal phyogs bzhir
sgyur gsung zhing spyan nam mkhar gzigs pa dang / ma lags/ gzim 'od 'gag pa dpal dar rnams 'das dus spun du gyur nas rje nyid drung smon lam btab gras da lta sku mdun 'dzom
pa bzhin mtha' ma'i gzim khri'i zhabs 'gyur yang khong tshos byed dgos phebs pas/ yang skyar ma lags nas zhabs brtan 'bul bar mdzad zhor ngos spun rnams nas kyang phyag
'tshal gyi zhabs pad yun brtan gsol ba btab par 'dun pa gang drag byed gsungs pa las gzhan ci yang mi gsung / de skabs snron zla'i mchod 'bul nyer lngar mdzad skabs yin
pas nyer lnga'i nyin chos grwa lho byang nas de mdzad/ nged kyi mgon de'i zla rer chag med gnang ba'i gur drag 'phrin gzhung sku

tshab byas nas btang ba'i nyi phyed yan la gsar 'gyur med kyang / de nas ljags dbugs sna thung zhing brel bas bzhugs g.yab du ma bzhugs par gzim khrir gdan 'dren dang ma lags
sogs zhabs drung du 'khod pa rnams kyi phyag 'tshal bcas zhabs brtan gsol 'debs phur btsugs dang / dpa' chen zhig me long la ltar bcug par gzim khri yongs rdzogs 'ja'
'od 'dra bas thum nas mi mthong zer skad thos de mtshams nas nged rang gzim chung mdo'i g.yab na yod par gnas slob de spyan chab mdzad cing 'dug pas gang yin zhus par da
zhabs pad mi brtan pa 'dra gsung byung bas snying gas pa lta bu'i sdug bsngal gyi skad chen por ngus pas rtabs shogs dang sdug bsngal gnyid ka 'dom pa lta bu spun gzhan rnams
kyang ngu zhing gzim shar na yod par dum tsam zhig nas gzim chung du shog gsung byung bas de phral snying rus skyed nas phyin pas gzhan tsho zhabs brtan gsol 'debs byed
mur 'dug cing khyad par mdzod pa des rgyun mtshan du ma zhu gin 'dug kyang spyir lo gzhon shing khyad par sdug bsngal gyis mnar bas ma nges/ 'on kyang de lan zhal gsal
ni gang yang byung ma song shing / nged la spyan cher gzigs te sna grang mor song ba dang dbugs 'di'i stabs bcas nas nam phyed tsam las mi thub pa 'dra

gsung byung bas hon thor ba lta bus ngu yang ma dran de nas nged rnams log zhabs phyir bcar sdod rnams yod pas srod nas dum tsam mnal du phebs de nas mnal sad pa dang nam ji
tsam slebs gsung par phyed ma zin tsam gda' zhus pas de nas bzung mnal ye med par spyan hu rer bzhugs shing / phyag rtsa gnang bas cung zad mi bde bas gsol sman bzhes na
zhus par re zhig 'then tsam gyis phebs gzim 'od la gzigs shing phyag grang mo des yun ring 'chang bar mdzad pa ni gzim 'od rang skal ba bzang ngam snyam/ de dus gzim chung
zang drar 'od khyug dang zang dra skad 'byin pa 'dra mo byung ba ni las ma dag pas de bzhin mthong yang don la mkha' 'gro'i 'od dang sgra sogs yin 'dra zhing gsung las
rtogs ldan chos nyid rang grol byon byung bzhugs gdan things gsung pas ser ma yin 'dra bzhes thug gnang mi dgos sam zhus pas ci yang mi dgos gsung / de nas thor mgo ma
zin tsam la dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim tshul gyi dbu las rlangs pa du ma thon pas dbu zhwa chu rgyun can du gyur/ spur chas rnams rim gsol gyi mchod tshogs dbus su bzhugs
su gsol/ phyis su thar rtse rje'i gsungs las de nyin nged zhwa lu brgyan gong thad der 'grul zhig la 'gro yin yod pas mig khrig cing sems ma dga'

long byed mu nas nyi ma 'byon khar nub du ltas pas 'ja' tshon zhig shar byung bas gang yin nam mnyam par slad nas bsam tshe yab rje chos kyi rgyal po de gshegs nyin yin 'dug
gsungs shing mgul khril nas gsung phro'ang chad song / sang snga mor nged rang nas gzims shar du phyin pas gzim 'od lha bshos kha shas bzo zhing gzhan tsho mun rub pas
bsdad 'dug pas rtse zim byas byung yang gshegs min rtog pa gang yang ma byung / ma lags de gzim mal na dran med lta bur bzhugs pa'i phyag bdag gi lag par bcang ste gnas tshul
gsung byung bas hon ne ba zhig la da dgongs rdzogs rnams gang drag mdzod zhus nas ster du gzim chung la phyin pas lho byang gi bar la sprin dkar snam yug rkyang pa lha
bu zhig las gzhan g.ya' dag pa ltar sngo seng yid skyo lhang byed pa zhig 'dug nang na gzim khri yol bas bltum pa'i lho ngos na sku gdung rin po che skyil krung mnyam
bzhag 'dra mo dbu sku mdun la dud nyams kyi bzhugs drung mchod pa gshom dang bsham rgyu kha shas bcas gnas slob des dkar cha bzhi sogs thugs dam rnams gsol 'debs mdzad 'khul
du 'dug nyi dros la nged spun dang bkra shis rgyal mtshan de bcas nas gnas bcur bla mchod zhus pas dran drags ngu ma lab kho na las 'don ma thub rgyun du ni rtsed

mo dang lab la yengs pas sdug bsngal yang rjed/ 'don pa zhig tshugs na bla ma bcos min dran pas ngu ba kho na byung / de nas nyer brgyad bar thugs dam la bzhugs shing de las
grol ba na dbu ltor phyogs shangs nas byang sems dkar dmar gyi rgyun dang sku las chab ser stobs chen zags pa sogs rtags shin tu gsal bas spur zhu phral sgrub zhus kyang
yongs tshod 'dug kyang / dbyar du song bas mi rung zer ma zad paN chen thams cad mkhyeen pa'i mchog sprul rin po che gdan pa bkra shis lhun por gdan 'dren nye'i mi dbang
sku zhabs gtsang la chibs bsgyur dang thug pasaskabs su ma che zhing dgongs skor ma 'gug pas gsang rgya dam bsgrags kyi spur sgrom du gdan 'dren shar yang bzo ma bde bar
de sngon nas chos lhun mkhan chen lha btsun dpal 'bar gshegs dus bsngo rten du phul bas sgam rtsi tshon gser shog yul le ba de dbang khang du yun ring las pa/ de skabs
su babs pa ni rang rang gi thugs bskyed smon lam dbang gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i bshos mtha' ma mgar ba'i bu tsundas phul ba dang 'dra'am snyam zhing / de gyen slang nang
spur chas tsan phye sogs dri bzang du ma'i khrod du bzhugs par phyi nas dar yug sna tshogs kyi spras pa mchod pa'i dbus su 'khod cing / phyag cha rdor dril ka pA la

sogs sku mdun du bkod par dus mtha' nas bshad pa'i spur bskyed chog zhus/ gnas slob des slob dpon mdzad pa'i nged rang mi lnga tsam gyi kyai rdor ras bris sgrub mchod dgung
zhag zhe dgu 'dzin pa'i dbu tshugs/ nam mkha' g.ya' dag cing me tog char sogs byung bas 'ga' zhig gi blo la zhing rjes pa min nam snyam pa shar yang zer ma nus/ sku rim
yin khul gyi mang ja mchod 'bul 'ga' re byas/ nged rang nas drug pa'i bdag med sgrub mchod la phyin pas dga' mo yod 'dra snyam pa yang gzhan blor shar de nas dgongs skor
'gug par skabs su babs pa'i gsung sngon 'gro'i gsang rgya mi dgos pa'i zhal bzang bstsal bas de ma thag gsang rdol ba'i yab yum de gnyis rang gi gzim chung dngos thog nas
'dus sder 'bras 'jam mang 'gyed shin tu zab pa/ lha chen khyams stod sogs su brgya mchod sogs grangs mang/ rig 'dzin lha khang du brgya mchod sogs dang bcas 'dus sde'i bla
mchod tshar kha shas/ gtsang dbus gnas rten la mchod 'bul dgon du mar mang skol sogs dang / gdan sa gzhung nas 'dus tshogs la bde kyai gsang gsum bdag med mkha' spyod
kun rig rnams kyi sgrub mchod zhag bcu gcig tshugs par/ 'bras 'jam ja drug

tsha thug zhib 'bo re/ mar rgyar spor te/ thud zhogs gnyis rnams dang mchod gtor zab gshom grol nyin gzhim chung nas 'gyed bzang ba/ yang mang ja 'gyed bzang bcas gzhung nas
sgrub pa dang zhal ngo so so chos sde rnam gnyis drung 'khor ser skya bla khag tshong khag mi ser sogs nas rang 'byor dang bstun pa'i dge sgrub gdung 'bul rten bzhengs
zhal 'debs sogs dpag med sgrub/ yang gro bzhin zla nang gzhung nas ser 'du nyin gnyis la 'bras 'jam re mang ja bzhi nyin dang por nang tshogs la bzang ja dang / byings la
dkyus ja dngul phor re/ nyin gnyis par nang tshogs la Tam gnyis re dang phyi tshogs la Tam re/ gsum par thang ston mchod 'bul bsnyen bkur sbyin gtong sogs bla ma gong ma'i
dgongs rdzogs dang cha 'dra'i tshogs dbu bsngo smon sogs la nged spun nas stong min bgyis khul dang / gzhan yang 'phral yun gyi dgongs rdzogs sgrub tshul 'ga' zhig yod
kyang re zhig de tsam mo/ /gzhan yang gzhis byes nas ngos tshor sems gso dang / dgongs rdzogs mdzad pa du ma byung zhing khyad par thar rtse rje nas de phral phyag mdzod
ched mngags rdzong gnang gi bka' shog sems gso dngos po bcas dang 'gyang min sku dngos phebs pa'i gang

ci'i mtshams la zhal bkod sogs mdor na rgyal tshab lta bu'i sgo nas rjes su bzung ba sogs rje 'di'i sku drin 'khor mtha' ma mchis so/ /de nas nged rang gi sems la dgongs skor
'gug phral spur sbyongs zhabs tog zhu snyam yang gzhan dbang gis de bzhin ma byung bar smiin zla'i nang thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi tshoms dmar du spur zhu bka' drin bskyangs
par 'ja' dang me tog char sogs mthun snang du grub cing sku gdung kyang byis pa lo brgyad tshod las med pas me mchod phral bzhes byung zhing thar rtse rje'i mnal
ltas su re zhig mngon dga'i zhing du phebs nas slar yang sprul pa 'byon par gsungs/ de dus nged kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen sngon ma'i skabs yin pas spur zhu'i nub rmi ltas su
gser khang steng gi nam mkhar nyi zla'i 'og tsam na 'ja' sprin dmar po'i dbus bzhugs gdan la rje de nyid sku mdangs dmar zhing sngags 'chang chas la sku bem dmar po dang
sa zhu bzhes shing g.yon skyabs sbyin g.yas gos dmar la lam zab bir srung sogs kyi phyag dpe yin bsam pa zhig dril nas sku 'khris nye gnas brgyud rang la bstsal nyams can
bzhugs pa la bzhugs g.yab g.yam skyor shar 'khris na'ang rje de nyid bzhengs nas nam mkha'i rje rang gi sku la bshad pa mdzad pa

zhig shar/ nged lta bu'i skal dman la'ang snang tshul de 'dra 'char na gzhan skyes bu dam pa'am skal rnams la dngos brgyud dag snang zhal gzigs yong ba the tshom med kyang
gsung mkhan ni mi 'dug pas gong gi tshul de/ chu phran rtag tu ku co che/ /rgya mtsho ca co ga la sgrog /zhes pa'i gras su ma gyur cig /de dus spur sgam nas sku rus rdog
tsam zhig byung ba da lta bdag gi byin rten gras la yod par bsam tshe dus phyis gdung 'dzin nged la dgos pa dang / phugs kyi rten 'brel la'ang bsam bzhin stsol bar mdzad
pa zhig yin 'dug pas rjes 'jug rnams nas thugs bcag gang dag zhu/ gdung rus zhu la phul ba rnams btul nas mchod dgu bla ma yi dam sogs kyi sku par 'jim pa dang bsres te grangs
mang gser mtshal sogs kyi bsgyur ba rnams 'og gi rten bzhengs rnams kyi gzungs dang rten sgam nang du bsri dgos gdung 'gyed sogs bgyis shing / 'on kyang nged rang na
phra skabs yin pas bkod pa ma thub pa des skyon yin nam ha cang gis 'gad gtsang rang ni ma byung / zhabs rjes phyi rten sa 'bum gdugs chos 'khor gser zangs nang rten dngul
gdung che ba phra rgyan can/ dbu rtser gser zangs kyi rje de nyid kyi sku sgros gtsang che ba sku thang kha shas dus mchod du thub dbang gnas rten sogs

'jim sku/ dus ja zla tshes dus dran mchod 'bul kyai rdor sgrub mchod zhag dgu ser 'du bcas pa sogs so so'i dkar chag dang gtong deb tu gsal ba bzhin dang gzhan yang nged rang
gi lus longs spyod dus gsum dge tshogs rje de nyid kyi zab dgongs chos dbyings su rdzogs thabs kho nar 'bul rtsis yin pa bzhin mgon de'i gdul bya skal ldan gzhan nas kyang
de bzhin mdzad yod 'gro yang sku drin gyi cha shas tsam yang 'khyer ba'i go skabs mchis pas bdag gzhan sgo gsum bgyi ba rnam kun don yod dam pa khyed nyid dges pa'i
rgyur 'gyur ba'ang gcig mchog rgyal po nyid la gsol ba 'debs na de de bzhin du 'gyur bar byin gyi brlabs tu gsol/ rang gi dad pa ma bslus na bla ma'i byin rlabs kyi mi bslu
bas zhing brjes nas kyang bdag la dges pa'i 'dzum zhal bstan pa gong 'khod bzhin dang gzhan yang rang lo nyer gsum tsam gyi nag zla'i tshes zhig la'ang rje de nyid nas
rang sems lhag lhar ngo sprod mdzad pa zhig shar yang de tsam gyis chog cing da lta'i bar du bag chags dang dgos pa khyad par cankhyar par can gyi yang yang rmi ltas su
phebs pa zhig 'dug cing / 'od zer la'ang skabs zhig rmi ltas su rje de nyid phebs par gdung shugs kyi rjes su 'dziin dgos tshul zhus pas nub phyogs na ltung bshags sangs

rgyas so lnga'i sku zhig 'dug par phyag 'dzub gtad de gsol ba thob gsung pa lta bu shar ba sogs gzhan la'ang de bas lhag pa'i dngos nyams rmi ltas byung yod 'gro bas bdag cag
gi rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid snying rus bstan 'gro spyi dang bye brag rje btsun sa skya pa'i ring lugs yang sgos bdag sogs gdul bya'i dpal mgon dam par bsam bzhin byon
pa zhig go /'dir smras pa/ mtha' yas 'gro la dpag yas rjes chags kyis/ /bsam yas thugs bskyed bgrang yas phrin las bzhi'i/ /tshad med gzigs pa sgrib med 'jug pa yis/ /yengs
med rjes 'dzin dpag med mgon des skyongs/ /zhes so/ /kha skong 'di rtsom pa po kun dga' blo gros dang / gcung mthu stobs dbang phyugde ltar byang phyogs thub pa'i rgyal
tshab de nyid kyi khyad par gyi gdul bya 'khor 'khyams bdag cag spun rnams rjes su bzung bas drin chen bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo las sras gsum

dang sras mo bzhi ste bdun byung ba'i gsum pa bdag gi rang 'tshang ni dgos pa'i dbang gis 'og tu 'chad la 'dir drug pa bdag gi nu bo gzhon pa de ni sems chung ba dang lhag
bsam dkar ba tsam las gzhan mkhas btsun bzang po'i rtogs brjod 'di yin zhu rgyu med kyang gdung rabs kha skong gras la gnas tshul 'dri mi 'os pa'ang med pas de nyid rgyu
mtshan du byas te lo rgyus cung zad zhu ba ni/ ma lags de'i sku la 'khril dus mnal lam ngo mtshar can mang po byung byung gi yi ge zhig 'dug pa des las rags tsam bsdus pa
ni/ de yang chu glang lo mngal du zhugs pa na nub gcig mnal ltas su yab yum lhan rgyas gda' chur sku khrus la byon song bas rdzing bu kha dog sna tshogs pa zhig la khrus
mdzad pas chu dkyil na yab rje de nyid yin rgyu'i khul la rnam pa phyag na rdo rje'i sku che ba zhig 'dug pa/ des rdo rje bsnun pas lus las srog chags dang rnag khrag zags
pa dang / yang skabs shig ma he skad gtong ba yin snyam pa'i rtse gsum pa rkang gling thogs pa zhig 'ongs nas 'brang lcag gis brabs pas sku gzugs phyi nang me kha dog
sna tshogs kyis gang ba dang / yang lo de'i khrum zla'i nang zhal ta ma bsod nams chos 'dziin yin snyam pas btsun ma zhig dang bud med bzhi'i skyed lhas lho'i spang ri la
lug khyu 'tsho zhing 'dug pas

ma mo gnyis la lug gu dkar po re btsas pas btsun ma des lug gu zhig ma lags rang la sprad/ gcig bsam brling du skyel rgyu yin kyang bdag mi thub bam zer tshul lam skyed lhas
brag gseb la smug rtse'i me tog khrod nas byams mgon gyi sku dmar po rnyed pa zhig kyang byung 'dug pas 'di ni lkog gyur rjen gsal 'dra mo zhig te/ de dus lha mdzes bu
khrid kyi sras sngon ma de'ang sku lus la yod kyang slar 'khrungs 'phral gshegs pa der mngon zhing yang bye rdzing tshogs kyi gtsug lag khang na khyung po'i ring bsrel yod
pa gsan pa'i bag chags kyis der phebs 'dug pa na ring bsrel de yin zer ba'i ngang sgong 'dra po seeer po zhig la byiin rlabs zhu bar mdzad pas ring bsrel gnyis brul bas
gcig mchod gcig gnyer ba dang / yang rong ngur smrig yin zer bar pha bong dril bu 'dra ba'i ngos nas spyan ras gzigs kyi sku dang ma Ni rang byon btus nas mchod pa dang
/ yang sngar nas yang yang mnal lam du 'ong ba'i btsun ma padma chos dpal yin zer ba des nang rtsa lhas dang phyir mgron bu'i g.yogs pa'i cham rtse 'dra ba zhig phul nas
'di gyon gribs bsrung yong zer ba dang / yang gzhi dgon bum 'dzin byams pa rab brtan bzang po zhes ra lo'i rnam 'phrul du grags pa der tshe sgrub yang yang zhu bar mdzad
pas/ lan gcig

sgrub tho gnang nyin 'byor rgyu'i do nub grwa pa zhig gis gzhi dgon dpon slob kyi yin zer ba'i bum pa g.yu khra ma chus gang ba'i dkyil nas ljang pa thon pa zhig dang thod
phreng g.yer khas spras pa phul ba zhig shar zhing de dus sgrub tho de las ngos kyi rmi ltas su dung bus pa bum pa las 'bras snye thon pa sa skya'i lung pa 'jam dbyangs me
tog gis khengs pa dpon po ri la zhal gyi sngags 'bur du thon pa nyi zla shar ba sogs byung bas gur zhal 'khor bcas la bskang khrus dgra lha dpangs bstod dang khyad par
zhal gyi bskang ba khri tshar mdzod gsungs pa ltar/ dbus phyogs chos skyong rnams nas kyang zhal bskang khri tshar dgos pa'i lung rnams mthun pa bzhin yab rje rdo rje 'chang
nas yun bsrings te bsog gnang gi snga phyir khri tshar gsum lhag bka' drin bskyangs/ yang btsa' rgyu'i zla ba de'i tshes dgur yab rje 'dus tshogs nas drug cu yin snyam
pa'i gtor bskul phyir mdzad byung bas gur zhal gyi sngags dang A li kA li dbyangs dir dir yod pa yod pa shar ba dang / yang btsun ma zhig nas lnga dus la dog zer bas gang
yin 'dri bar mdzad pas zhag lnga zla lnga lo lngar dog zer ba shar ba ni de dus sgra ji bzhin yin shag mdzad kyang / phyis su nged rang nas bsam tshe lnga gsum bco lnga
yin 'dug pas bco lnga'i lo sa

'brug nag zlar khrag rlung mthu mo zhig gi mi 'tsho ba tsam du gyur dus 'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes kyi 'chi bslu sogs rim gro dang sman sogs kyis lhogs tsam byung ba de
yin 'dra/ gzhan yang mnal lam yin yin mang po byung 'dug kyang 'dir de tsam mo/ /gang ltar de nas shing stag sa ga'i tshes bcur kha ba 'bab cing btsas par yab rje rdo rje
'chang nas ljags chu tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs bstsal zhing gtang rag lha bsangs gsung bskang sogs dang rim gro spyi sger nas sgrub yod 'gro zhing/ legs so ster ba'i dngos
po ni du ma byung / gso sla zhing nyan pas yab yum nas thugs rtsis lhag par che/ ming zhus pas yab rje nas ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams mthu stobs dbang phyug bkra
shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang poor bstsal/ gces ming la tshangs pa mchog pa zer bas zla bo tshos bla ma tshangs mchog lags zer/ ming la mthu stobs dbang phyug yod
pas sgar chen rnam sprul yin zer bas cal sgrog byung bas de rang yang sgar chen yin rgyu'i khul byed/ smra shes tsam la yab rjes zhabs 'bam bzhes dus 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
dbang pos phyag mkhar bsnams pa mthong bas rgan nyams dang mkhar ba 'khur ba'i tshul byed/ yab

rje las rkyen sel kha shas dang mkhan chen dbang phyug phun tshogs la yang tshe dpag lha dgu dang grub rgyal ma'i dbang lan 'gar yang thob cing / smin byed thog ma yab rje
las rdo rje phur pa'i dbang ras bris steng nas thob pa dang / gur drag dbang sogs thob pas gnas skabs de dag tu nged spun rgan pa rnams chos gral du'ang rtsed mos sdod mi
zug kyang chung ngu de yab yum gyi zhal la lta zhing chos nyan khul dang skabs rer phyag rgya 'dra mo byed/ rgan nyams kyi phreng ba 'khur nas sngags 'dren tshul dang /
srogs chags la byams sems kyi nged rnams nas sems can bzung na bsad dogs dang / gzhan gyis gzhan la sdigs pa ltar byas na mchi ma 'don zhing / bskang gso dang gur drag chag
med byed khul las gzhan rang bag chags cher ma mchis/ lo bzhi par phur sgrub thog phun tshogs gling la 'gro rgyu'i gong tshoms chen mgon khang / dbu rtse/ sgo rum/ nang
so rnams mjal bas nang sor pu tra slebs byung zer/ thab spos dus drung 'khor gyi bzhas sogs byas/ khal kha byang chub rdo rje'i 'bul chen 'byor bas bsod nams che ngo byung
/ skabs zhig thar rtse rdo rje 'chang sa skyar phebs dus tshang mas rkyen sel gsan par tshe dbang zhig stsol dus yab rjer sgrol dkar/ nged la dbyangs

can lha mo nu bo der zhal sgrub dus mgon po'i sku thang gnang bas nged gnyis kyi thang khar gong gsham mi 'dug pas gong gsham gsol dus gos spu ma 'brug ris sogs 'bur thon tshon
snas spras pa zhig byung song bas bsrung ma 'di kun tu 'go zhing 'phrin las sgrub pa'i rten 'brel yin nam snyam zhing / de dus tshe dbang gnang dus tshe bum zan bzo
las tshe chu dngos su phebs pas yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid la nyung ngu dang / nged la thigs grangs mang tsam/ nu bo de dang ma lags la gtan nas ma byung bas phyis kyi
rten 'brel kyang de ltar du gyur/ yang de dus tshe dpag lha dgu'i sgo nas 'chi bslu dang rjes 'brel dbang yang bstsal zhing me tog dkyil 'khor la 'bul du 'jug par mdzad
pas/ yab rje'i de sangs rgyas tshe dpag med la babs/ nged kyii de rin chen tshe dpag med la babs/ nu bo de dang ma lags de gzhal yas khang nang du lhung tsam byung / gur
khro bcu dang zhal bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang kyang bstsal/  de nas rim gyis lo bdun par slebs dus nged gnyis chos khri thang mo cher che 'don lhan du gnang bas rgan gzhon
khyad thub pa dgongs gsal nged kyi skyar/ mnga' gsol phyag nas ni gnyis ka byung bas skal ba bzang snyam yin/ ka bzla sum cu

nas bzung slob gnyer byed rgyu'i thog ma yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas bka' drin skyang ste dgongs gzhi khyad par can gyi gsung ngag rdo rje'i tshig rkang dang lam dus 'bring
po gsung slob gnang zhing shes pa'ang sla mo byung bas sngar thugs mthong che khar lhag par yang byams rtse bka' drin che/ de nas 'brum nad kyi mnar ba sogs skal ngan dang
/ gsung ngag lam 'bras thob pa sogs skal bzang myongs/ de nas 'gyang min yab rje chos dbyings su gshegs pas slob gnyer 'phro rnams gnas slob bzod pa bkra shis des slob
grogs mdzad pas stabs bde thog nas sgrigs rgyug rim bzhin byung song zhing de lo nged gzhi bsnyen ring sbyin bdag dang sgar khag sogs ngos phrad dgos pa rnams 'gan len mur
thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang po byon par ngos 'phrad dang rkyen sel zhus shing thar rtse rje'ang bzhugs yod pas gnyid ka nu bo der dgyes so dpe med gnang /
gang ltar thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi bka' chos bstsal ba phal cher nged dang dbyer med thob/ khyi lo'i dpyid brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs la btugs dus dbang rjes gnang
dang lung 'ga' re zhur yod cing bka' khrid rnams la ni med/ de'i dgun sde dge nas sa skyong bsod nams mgon po 'khor bcas byon pas ngos phrad zhus/ chung

ngur phur sgrub sogs la phyin zhing / phag lor nged dbus gtsang sogs la song dus re zhig sngar bzhin mjal kha sogs btang zhing ston mjug nas dge rgan dang lhan cig 'byung 'dul
bsnyen pa byas/ de nas nged rang 'grul nas 'khor ba'i brel ba rnams grub phral nas zla ba kha shas mtshams la bsdad/ char 'phar brel mu nas byi lo'i dgun gnas gsar rdo
rje 'chang gi zhabs la btugs pas nged spun rnams la thob yig pod chen byung yang bsam sgom rang ni ga 'dra byung yod dam/ de sngon tsam nas bzung a Ni drung de nyid dang
nged rang las kyang chos kha shas thob/ glang loo'i ston dge rgan dang lhan cig phur bsnyen sbyin sreg bcas bgyis/ rgyud 'don dang bla mchod ni tshar 'ga' re las med phur
pa/ bde kyai gsang gsum/ bdag med ma/ bskang ba gtor bzlog sogs la slob dpon bgyis dang ma bgyis sna tshogs kyi phyin/ chos 'chad thog ma gnas gsar rjer 'jam dbyangs dmar
ser rjes gnang phul dus mgo bshad ngos kyi gsar sgrigs bcas rgyas tsam phul bas thugs shin tu dges/ stag lo sogs la lo rgyus 'dra yod 'gro yang ma dran/ yos lo'i ston
gzim dpon kun phun dang lhan cig kyai rdor gzhi

bsnyen la sdod rgyu'i mgon khang khag bzhir 'phrin 'chol ngos dbang khang mdor mtshams chas rnams sgrigs pas a tsar gnyis nas shel bum che ba zhig tu gangga'i chu 'khur zhing
phrad par yam bu dang gor kha'i lo rgyus las gzhan ni mi 'dug mtshams thog gung 'gyur med tshe brtan dpon g.yog rnams phebs par ngos kyi phun tshogs gling du bsdad nas
zhal ya zhus/ nu bo de mtshams la yod tshul zhus kyang ma gsan par sku rkyang la ngos phrad dgos lugs nan bskyed mdzad pas mtshams 'og tu ma chug bzhin du mi mjal ka med
byung bas des mtshams ral bar song ba yin nam bsnyen pa gsum gnyis tsam song thog khrag rlung lta bu nad kyi mi khyol ba byung yang sbyin sreg bcas mthar phyin pa'i dga'
ston du yul chen ban tshang pas las mgon ru 'dren sogs kyi 'chams byas/ 'brug lor nged rang lhan nas gur mgon bsnyen pa zla gang bgyis/ 'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes nas
grub thob brgyad bcu nyi sbas sgrol ma/ snar thang brgya rtsa/ sa skya bka' 'bum ljags lung sogs rgya cher stsol dus kyang phal cher la yod cing gong du bshad pa'i na tsha
thu mo de'ang byung bas ngor pa dpon slob rnams kyis 'jigs byed drug cu rnam rgyal stong mchod sogs dang chos grwa lho byang nas kyang rim gro gang 'grub mdzad cing /
de rang

tshe sgrub sogs la brtson par byas pas re zhig nas lus las 'bu mtho gang tsam zhig mngon sum thoon pas nad grol zhing / nged rang gzhis rtsee rin rtse sogs la 'gro skabs dang
mdzod pa na mur yod/ nu bo des sa skyar khur bzung de'i dgun dge rgan kyang gshegs/ sbrul lo'i snron zla tsam nas nu bo des khyad 'phags byang mgon khang du gur mgon brag
rdzong ma'i bsnyen pa zla gang sbyin bsreg bcas bgyis/ nged kyi phur sgrub bshad las dang mdos chung / sku rim chen po'i gzor las bgyid rgyu'i mtshams rnams mu sbrel
tshul gong nu bo des dbyug zla'i nang sgo rum bla ma lha khang du sdod yul byas nas bse mgon chen po'i drung zhag shas bskang ba kho nar 'bad dus/ nyin gcig bse mgon bzhugs
yul nas sku mdun la nyang mdzad pa lta bu dang / nyin gcig sa lo'i phyag rnga brdung mur lpags ldebs la 'od khyug pa de rang dang gzim dpoon kun phun gnyis kas mthong
/ yang de skabs mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus zhig la nged kyi pu tra'i thun mong min pa'i gsang rten gnyis gsar bzo'i skang ba sogs dbang khang mdor srod chen thog bgyis nub 'gag
pa rab brtan gyi rmi ltas su bzhi thog rtse'i thog kha'i sgo der sgo lcags byed rgyu yin bsam pa

la mi mgo rlon pa khrag 'dzag 'gel bzhin 'dug pas 'jigs snang shar ba dang / sgo rum 'khor tshom du sdir chom du ma'i tshig gsal ba la g.ya' g.ya' zer bas don chen de bla ma
lha khang mdor nyal ma nus pa gzhan du bros/ dum tsam zhig nas mkhar rngar sor mo bsnun pa lta bu'i sgra zhig byung nas ldir chom rnams yar 'ong te dbu rtse rnying ma'i
gser phur khar yang khrag rlon thor re ba dang 'khor tshom lho 'gram la che ba rta dang chung ba ra lug gi rmig rjes 'dra mo gdan nas la mang du byung/ zla mjug der ngeed
rang mtshams la sdod khar shar phyogs nas don med zer bsog mang pos rgyud 'khrugs bzhin du sdod dgos byung / de nas rim bzhin bod dpon sku mched dus gzar je gsal gyi thams
cad ya nga la bya thabs zad cing 'jigs zhum zla sbrel skabs dus mdos gtor pod sogs kyi slob dpon nu bo de bgyis zhing / chos 'chad kyang re gnyis byas tshod yiin cing
phur chen lhag ma de'i dkyil chog sogs kyi phyi dbyangs nang dbyangs bskang ba bstod pa rnams kyi dbyangs sogs zur 'chad rje drung la bslab 'dug/ de dus stod phyogs bros
shor rnams byung dogs dang / 'dar sde pa sku mched la srog skyob zhu ba sogs

gang sa nas 'tsher ba'i rang bzhin dang / bsam yas sku rten pa 'byor bar ngo 'dzin chos 'brel sogs kyang nu bo des byas shiing sku brten pa'i lha khang rtse'i sngags 'chang
chen po'i sku la smon lam btab pa'i dbu mtshams nas zil pa thon pas bzang ngan gang yin ni ma shes/ sbrul zhug rta mgor sde dge blo gros rgyal mtshan sku mched 'khor bcas
byon par ngos spun nas dgongs bzhed gang 'grub zhus shing nu bo des chos 'brel yang le tshan kha yar byas tshod yiin/ lcags rta'i snron zla sogs la ngos kyi gzhis rtser
phyin skabs dang lo de'i dgun mjug nas nged rang kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen lan gnyis par sdod skabs rnams la sgrub mchod tshogs dbu sogs 'gan phal cher des khur zhing khyad
par lcags lug lo'i bdud rtsi ril sgrub kyang des byas lo de'i ston kho bos rtse gdong du phur sgrub 'dzugs pa sogs brel ba rnams la zla shas g.yeng dus dang / yar slebs nas
zhal zor las bsnyen skabs sogs la'ang des dus mdos sogs kyi mgo byas chu spre sos phral thabs lhor spos nag zla'i nang nged spun nas brag rdzong ma'i las tshogs shwa bzlog
phon cher sgrub pa dang/ sa gar thar rtse rje'i sku rim drug cu pa zhig kyang sgrub dus gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang yang sa skyar phebs shing

tshoms dmar gnyer tshang sogs kyi zhig gso phal cher grub/ dbyar thog der gnas gsar rjer nged rang nas sger pa'i sras mo nu bo'i lcam du 'os tshul zhus pa bzhiin mdzod pa sogs
tshang ma gros mthun gyi thag chod/ dbyug zla'i nang nged spun nas tshoms dmar dang dngos grub gling la rab gnas 'bring po dang / phur pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa bgyis de
sngon nas rje btsun drung sku khams nyog mu yin pas sku mdun la yang yang bcar shing gang ci zhu 'os slad kyi 'char gzhi bcas zhib zhus thog nas thar rtse rje'i bka' bzhin
ngos spun gur drag bsnyen pa bdun phrag la sdod pa'i dbyug zla'i nyer dgur a ni lags gshegs zhabs rjes rnams kyi bkod pa dang gur drag drag po'i sbyin bsreg bgyis te dgongs
rdzogs skor phal cher grub pa'i tshes mgor bdag mo bsu ba'i sngon 'gro mgon khang khag la 'phrin 'chol dang khyad par skyed lhas su rtag gtor 'dzugs par nged spun phyin
pa'i zhag shas ring de bzhin byas skabs tho rengs shig kho bo spyod khung la rkang pa shor bas lham yu sgrog bcas g.yam rnon gyi stub pa'i pus g.yas 'og tsam du rus
pa mthong tshod rma bcos byung yang sran skyed pas sdug skam la song zhing nu bo der yang 'khrugs nyams glo thu mos zhag shas na ba dang kho bor rmi ltas byung tshul ras
byang la bris te gtor sgam

der btags yod pas de dus nas 'tshub nyams byung zhing / mthar rtse rjes ma lags de la bdag mo'i dga' ston sogs la g.yeng ba med par mtshams mdzad na legs tshul phebs pa ma
'ong sgrib med gzigs pa'i lung du 'dug de nas smin zla'i bcu gsum la bdag mo 'byor ba'i ston mo gzhas sogs gzab 'phyor dang / khyad par gong sa rin po che nas gzims 'gag
'od 'jo sku tshab tu ched gnang gi legs so tshad med bstsal ba sogs gzhis byes gong 'og kun nas go babs de las lhag pa mdzad rgyu med kyang sngon las 'phral rkyen lta bu'i
mi shis pa'i mtshan mar bdag mo byon phral dbus zhabs zhig nas bzhi thog tshoms chen rtser dar lcog zhig btsugs song ba de phral rlung gis khyer ba'i gar song cha med byung
song zhing / mon 'khyams mya ngan gyi non pa lta bu 'ga' rer gling bu ngu skad 'don pa lta bu bsgyur ba sogs sems tsha lhang nge byung yang rmu gab kyi bcings pas rim
gro gang yang ma dran/ de dus zhol khang chol mdzad sku tshab tu byon pa'i gzhung sa'i sku rim bskang ba nyin gang ma zhag shas tshom chen du tshugs pa'i dbu dang mdos
chung mdos chen sogs la'ang des phyin/ de nas chu bya rta zla'i tshes gcig la rlung chen tshod med byung

bas bal yul nas gzhan la me mjug byas par glang mang mkhar gnas gsar bas 'chams sogs rnam gzhag dpe med byas/ de nas nged kyi gsung ngag thog ma 'chad pa'i slob ma'i gtso bo
nu bo de yin pas de skabs chos kyi rnam grangs thob tshul ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i snang rgyud khrid yig khog phub/ dam tshig gi rnam
bshad/ phyi nang bskyed rim bshad pa/ a mes zhabs kyi rlung bshad rnams gung bsgrigs thog nas 'chad par sems bskyed chen mo/ slob ma rjes 'dzin/ rgyu dbang mngon rtogs
bdun ldan/ lam dbang bdag med ma'i byin rlabs/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab rnams dang bcas pa'i rgyab chos lung skor la bla ma rgya bod rnam thar/ gong ma
lnga nas mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i bar gong yab rje'i stsal skabs bzhin/ de nas kun mkhyen sangs rgyas rin chen/ yongs 'dzin/ sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang
yab sras gsum/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang rnams kyi rtogs brjod/ rtsa rgyud rtags gnyis pod ser ma/ de gras mngon rtogs yan lag bzhi drug dbang
chu/ yum gyi mngon rtogs byin rlabs rtsa ltung 'khrul spong / tshogs 'khor 'bring po/ sbyin bsreg lam skor phyi ma brgyad/

pod dmar ma/ pod nag ma/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gsung bskyed rim rnam bshad/ lus dkyil rtsod spong / gtor chog dang bstod pa nyi shu'i bshad pa/ tshogs 'khor kun
bzang rnam rol rnams dang / kun mkhyen gyi gsung zla zer rtsod spong / lus dkyil dang dbang chu'i rnam bshad/ mngon rtogs tshul bcu bzhi/ lam dbang yi ge sa lo'i gsung
glo bo mkhan chen dang zha lu lo chen la bstod pa/ sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya/ dus 'khor maNDal/ dkon mchog lhun grub kyi rnam rgyal stong mchod/ rgyud gsum brgyud 'debs/ sngags
'chang chen po'i rgyu dbang 'tsham sbyor/ bsod nams dbang po'i nyams rtogs gong 'phel/ grags pa blo gros kyi lam 'bras khrid yid/ a mes zhabs kyi gsung ngag lam 'bras
bla brgyud rnam thar mdor bsdus dang sbyar ba'i rgyud 'debs/ bir bstod gnyis/ kun mkhyen sku bstod/ lam 'bras khog phub chen mo/ rdor dril phreng ba dgang blugs bum pa
rnams kyi bshad pa le tshan/ bde kyai phur pa bdag med ma/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ kun rig tshe chog rnams kyi mngon dkyil/ bdag med dbang gi 'tsham sbyor/ rab gnas don gnyis
lhun grub/ seng ge sgra'i cho ga chab klu kun rig bsnyen thabs/ rnam sras bskang ba rnams dang / ngag dbang chos

grags kyi kyai rdor phyi dkyil rnam bshad dang kun rig lho go'i lhan thabs/ sgrub khang pa'i las bzhi'i sbyin bsreg rnam bshad/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi gsung ngag 'chad
tho dang ngor gdan rabs/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis kyi dam rdzas sman tho/ bstan pa gso chog/kun rig brgyud 'debs/ dam pa dang grags blo bas mdzad pa'i mgon po mnga'
gsol/ nged rang nas brtsams gras yab rje'i sku bstod dus gsum rgyal ba/ thar rtse dang gnas gsar rje'i zhabs brtan dang gsol 'debs/ a Ni drung / brag rtsa rje/ rje sangs
rgyas ye shes/ gnam kha'u pa/ shAkya mchog rje btsun sgrol ma rnams la bstod pa/ kyai rdor rnam bshad sngags 'chang mgul rgyan/ 'jam rdor sgrub dkyil/ dam tshig rdo rje'i
bsgom bzlas/ zhal gyi mnga' gsol/ beg rtse'i gzungs mchog phyag gnyer gyi bskul ba'i ring 'tsho'i bden tshig rnams kyi lung / rjes gnang skor la ri khrod ma/ rnam 'jom
sme brtsegs ljang dud/ sman bla mched bdun/ gnas bcu/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon/ 'jam dpal dkar smra seng / gang blo rig gtad/ sher phyin dkar mo/ dbyangs can dkar dmar/ nor
rgyun ser mo/ 'byung 'dul le tshan/ sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bde mchog lhan rgyas/ 'jigs byed dpa' gcig

seng mdong sngo dmar/ 'jam nag rdo rje shugs/ khyung khra nag sna tshogs yum/ gtsug gtor 'bar ba/ drag dmar/ so 'brang dkar mo/ tshe dpag sprul sku/ khro mo rme rtsegs/ sgrol
dkar/ gnyan sgrol/ sgrol dmar/ bcu gcig zhal/ don zhags lha lnga/ sengge sgra/ phyag rdor dbu tsa/ phyag rdor gtum po/ phyag rdor khang brtsegs/ rtan mgrin jo lugs/ ras
chung lugs/ skyer sgang lugs/ zla rgyal lugs/ dzam ser nag dmar po lugs gnyis/ dkar po lha lnga/ a pa ra tsi ta/ zhang blon/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ mgon po phyag drug dkar
nag legs ldan mched gsum/ beng dmar/ rdo rje rab brtan ma/ tshe ring mched lnga/ sgrol ma nyer gcig nyi sbas lugs rnams bgyis so/ /de ltar zla gsum lhag tsam bgyis shing
/ snron zla'i nang tsam la phun tshogs gling du phyin nas chu stod nang de rang gi gzugs gcong 'phrod rten tu stong chen nas sman chu blang ba'i sbyongs byed skabs nged
rig byed ma'i char 'beb byed cing yod pas zla bo nas glo bur rdo rje sbug tu shog zer byung phral tab tab por rgyugs pas rlung gi rnam pa 'dra mos dran med 'chi la khad
du song 'dug pas thabs gang drag brtson pa bskyed pas dar tsam nas

dbugs kyi rgyu ba slebs kyang dran med kho nar lus pas de skabs thar rtse dang gnas gsar gnyis ka bzhugs yod pas skyabs 'jug ljags gul gsung rtag zhus par gnyis ka nas 'phral
'tshub las skyon mi 'ong gnang ba bzhin dgong ja tsam nas thugs dam byed khul byung yang mi ngo shes shing gtam mi smra bas nged rang car sdod kyi nyin gang 'khyol/ mtshan
mo zla bo rnam drung du bzhag nas nged rang rdo rje sbug gi mdor bsdad pas nam phyed tsam nas gnyid bde mor 'khugs pas da mi lto 'am zer sang nam langs phral gam du
phyin pas 'don pa thub tsam 'dug pas de nyin gnas gsar rjer tshe dbang zhus shing de nas rim gsos kyi phur sgrub sogs la pher tsam byung / de dus thar rtse rdo rje 'chang
dang gnas gsar rje gnyis kas bdag mor dngos po'i gnang sbyin bcas legs slob zal lta rtsol bar btsun mo spe'ur sku dngos phebs/ ston 'gor thar rtse rje ngor du phebs skabs
rig 'dzin pho brang gi sgo sgrigs sogs shin tu 'grig par mdzad de phebs skyel zhu mir de'i gnas tshul yin rgyu'i rnam pa mdzad nas da ni gzim chung ya gir yang de tsam
mo gsung pa 'gyang min nas zhing rje ba'i gsung du gnang / ston nas dgun 'goo'i bar gnas gsar rjes gsar rnying

du ma'i chos bka' bstsal mthar dbus la phebs/ dgun brel char 'phar rnams dang shing khyi'i dpyid ngos nas lam 'bras chos 'chad gnyis pa grub phral nged spun nas tshoms dmar
du zhal gyi dam tshig skang ba nam lang sa rub lta bur sgrub dus nged rang gnyis nas skul ras byas/ de nas 'bum thang zhig gso'i skor dang dbyar tsam nas ma lags de bsnyun
gyis rim bzhin bzung bas phur sgrub dus bzhi thog tu bzhugs/ nged kyi phur sgrub skabs snga phyi sna tshogs su 'bum thang gzungs bzhugs 'od zer dri med dkyil chog bsags
shing bzhi thog tu re gnyis yong dus nged gnyis nas ma lags kyi drung du rkyen sel sogs gang yong zhus pas skabs zhig do nub bzhi thog tu bzhugs la sang tshoT dung du byung
nas byon gsungs pa bzhin byas pas 'gro khar shog gsung / sku mdun du phyin pas da lam nad 'di'i kha nas thar ba zhig mi yong 'dra bas des na nyid rang ni dar bab gang
sa nas blo kyog mi dgos 'on kyang sku 'khrugs ma byung bar mdzod/ gcung po 'di thugs sems chung la sku gcong che zhing bdag mo gyong ba sogs 'o rgyal byung dogs dang sku
tshe'ang ha cang ring ba zhig ma byung dogs pas nam bzhugs bar sku mched da lta bzhin thugs mthun pa dang dbu 'doon yang dag mdzod/ gzhan rje btsun ma rnams dang zhabs

phyi rnams kyi bab gang sa nas zhal mngag du ma gnang mthar rgan mo nga'i 'das shul gang mdzad na'ang nyid rang nas mkhyen pas des ma thus pa gang yang zhu rgyu med gsung byung
bas blo khol yang snying rus skyed nas da dung sku rim 'phrod bzhes rim nas zhu bas dngas bskyed bzhes thub tsam e yong ci ste ji gsung bzhin thog bab shar tshe gang
spyi'i zhal chems 'gyod med zhu zhus pas dgongs par shin tu bab song zhing nu bo de ni mid pa 'khril ba yin nam gang yang zhus ma song / de nas phur sgrub ring dang khrums
zla'i bcu gsum par res 'jog gi de nyin ngos spun dbang khang na 'jam rdor sgrub mchod byed mur nyi dros la da gshegs grabs 'dug pas byon zer ba bzhin phyin pas mi ngo
mi mkhyen cing spyan phan tshun du gzigs thub tsam 'dug pas nged rang nas bdud rtsi ril bu khrus chur sbyar bar sangs rgyas 'phel gdung bcas zhus pas dar tsam nas cung zad
thugs gsal du song nged gnyis kyi sgrub mchod grol grub phral 'on seng gang dgos gra sgrigs kyi cag char re bsdad pas bcu bzhi 'i shar mda' btang tsam la char chen sgrub
mchod tshogs drung gsan pas phyag thal mo sbyar nas chos dbyings su thim phral zhal chems bzhin 'od zer nas mkha' spyod ma'i 'pho ba gsol

'debs sogs rjes sgrub rnams zhus/ de'i dgun 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong dang mjal/ rgyal zla'i bcu gnyis la/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang zhing rjes pas dgongs rdzogs sgrub
mchod rnams nged gnyis nas gang lcogs zhus/ shing phag nag zla'i tshes mgo nas chu stod zla skyed bar ngos la khrag rlung nad gzhi thu min sna tshogs bstud mar byung bas
'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gi rim gro'i zhal bkod dang rkyen sel stsal/ de lo'i ril sgrub nu bo des bgyis shing rje btsun gong ma'i bdud rtsi ril bu'i rta rnams mang
du spel/ chu stod zla nang nas ngos kyis thub bstan mkhan rin po che bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan/ ri khud sprul sku bsod nams dbang phyug sogs la chos 'chad byas/ deng dus
kyang dbang sogs kha shas la nu bo de yang yod pas de las 'phros 'dir yang nged rang las snga phyir chos thob tshul 'ga' zhig smos na bde mchog nag po pa/ dril bu phyi nang
/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ ye shes zhabs lugs/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ mi 'khrug lha dgu/ rigs gsum spyi dbang / sbyongs dkyil bcu gnyis/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ dra med rnam
gnyis/ gur drag a ra pa tsa lha lnga/ yang dag phur pa'i stod smad/ rta mgrin yang gsang sogs kyi dbang / tshe dbang grub

rgyal bla ma zhi khro/ lcags sdong / lha mang / lcags sdong 'chi med 'dod 'jo lugs/ lcags sdong ngag chos lugs/ rdo rje'i srog shing / yang snying kun 'dus/ sgra mi snyan/
tshe'i rdzong chung / gur lha brgyad/ khro bcu/ hrakshad/ dmag zor/ zhal bsnyen ngus/ beg rtse/ dur khrod bdag po/ pu tra/ bran bdud/ dkar bdud las gshin rigs gsum/ dmar
po skor gsum/ rnam sras/ phyag rdor khang brtsegs/ zhang blon/ tshogs bdag chags pa rdo rje sogs rjes gnang kha shas/ gzhan yang lung sogs mang tsam thob chod yin/ de nas
lo de'i ston dang me byi'i dpyid bar nged gnyis nas gtsang dbus mchod yul rnams mjal bar phyin dus sa skya nas thon skabs nu bo des da lam nga'am mthu stobs gang rung zhig
gi phung po dbus su bzhag 'gro zer/ gang ltar de dus gong sa rin po che sku ltem tshul bzhes skabs yiin pas mjal phyag ji 'dra 'ong 'am zer mu dang rong sner slebs dus
rgyal rtser 'brum dogs sogs gang sa nas 'tsher dung nge phyin pas rgyal ba yab sras bka' blon rin po che rnams sogs che gnyan tshang mas spyan skyang bka' drin skyang zhing
/ spyi sger lha sde mi sdes byams pa sogs sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma'i sku drin la 'khor mtha' ma mchis shing /

lhag par gru 'dzin pho brang mchog nas kun gzigs bdun pa chen pos bdag rgyan mgo 'dren mchog gi rjes su bzung bas spyir bag dro zhing / yang dgos de sngon gzhan nas mjal phyag
zhus pa'i nyen blang sku khams la gnod pa 'dra yang byung yod tshod 'dug kyang / 'byor phyag zhus nub mtshan gzim 'jam pa dang / zhabs brtan phul ba nas sku la dang skyed
bzhes pa sogs gong sa rin po che de nyid kyi rnam thar lcang skya rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rtsom de na'ang bsngags brjod bcas 'khod pa gnang 'dug pas nged spun la de
'dra'i nus pa ma mchis kyang grub mtha' ris med mkhas grub la gus shing/ khyad parkhyad pa rgyal ba yab sras 'di rnams snyigs dus bstan 'gro'i mgon du bsam bzhin phebs pa
yin snyam pa'i dad pa rjes zlos min pa rang byung du yod pas rten 'brel de'i gnad dang gong sa rin po che nyid kyi thugs rjes gzigs pa la ni the tshom med pas 'di tsam zhig
sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma'i zhabs tog tu rngo thogs/ de dus chos 'chad phal cher kho bos byas pas go chod 'on kyang nu bo de nas phran tsam byas gras lha sar spo ra
sde bgres la lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang kyai rdor bsnyen thabs kyi lung phul gong ma'i sku tshab shu am sa ngos phrad la phebs byung bas nu bo de bcos med rang yin
pas lha par mnyes nged jo bo drung rab

gnas chig sgrub dus nu bo des gzim chung khams gsum du rme rtsegs khrus bgyiis dus gong sa rin po cher sku dog rtags byung 'dug kyang zhu ma nus/ gong du smos pa bzhin gzim
dpon mthu stobs kun dga' rgyas 'khrugs kyi na bas lha sar lus thog nas dus chos su gyur pa'i rjes sgrub rnams la nu bo de rang nas bskul ma bgyid pa sogs byas shes drin
zo ya rabs kyi rtags ni dga' mo 'dug bco brgyad du sku ngo rnams la sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog de'i mtshan brgya/ gnas gsar rje'i sku bstod/ nged rang mched ring 'tsho'i bden
tshig rnams kyi lung / bsam las su kyai rdor rgyu dbang tshar drug rta mgrin skyer sgang rjes gnang / dbu rtse rigs gsum gling bzhi gling phran gtsug lag khang rnams
la rab gnas cho ga'i sgo nas me tog gtor song bar thal rlung byung bas rang gzhan la mi shis pa 'dra gter ston rin po che kun bzang bde chen rgyal por gang ci'i gsung brtag
zhus pas nu bo de khong gi chos bdag gter lung las/ nub nas sa skya'i gdung brgyud byang chub sems/ /zhes lung zin de yin 'dug gsung zhing tshe tshad ma nges gsungs pas
lung bstan thig po yin 'dug cing/ lo de'i mgo zla'i nyer gnyis la bdag mor 'chi med bu khrid dam/

chos ming 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma 'di btsas tshul gnyer dpon bgres pos bsam yas su yi ge skur byung / bsam yas nas rtse thang du thon khar sger yum grong / rtse thang 'bras
gling na grwa pa zhig la chos skyong yin khul zhig 'babs 'dug pa ngos nas sngar med kyi srol gsar mi dgos byas pas kho pa tshig za'i zhe nag gis nged kyi nu bo 'das dus
kyang gnod 'khyol tshul ngo so byed pa dang / gzhan yang 'bras gling par mi shes pa gang byung yang kho pas yin tshul dang / rtse thang lung spyir yang char pa bsrung
tshul sogs byas shing lus g.yar kho rang nas kyang grwa tshang dkrug shing byed pa sogs zhing bcu tshang ba'i las la mthu rtsal yin pa'i kha po ston skad 'dug pas dgra bgegs
ngo mtshar can shAkya'i bstan la rgyab kyi phyogs pa zhig yin pa la nii the tshom mi 'dug bzang ngan gang yin na'ang yin du chug rang rang gi thog tu rnam smin khur nas
'gro dgos yin 'dug go gang ltar de khul brel ba chod nas yar lung du gnas gsar rjes lugs gnyis bdag rgyan tshad med bskyang / shel brag gnas skor grub nas sger par sdod
rtsis kyi lam zhor btsan thang lha khang du nyi ma ma zhud tsam la 'byor/ de nas sger par 'gro lam du sa sros khrom rnams nas lha rgyal 'then pas rta 'ur la khad byung
sger pas gzab gshom dpe med byung yang

gshegs mo'i zhe dgu 'dzin skabs yin 'dug cing / ngos spun nas kyang gshegs bzhugs tshang mar bab 'brel gang yong bgyis nas gra phyi sogs su rim thon dus sger pa nas rnam sras
gling bar thal rlung kho na dang sger pa'i yab la shangs khrag byung ba sogs mi shis pa'i mtshan ma byung / bye tshogs su kyai rdor rgyu dbang tshar gnyis/ grwa thang
du 'jam dbyangs dmar ser kyi rjes gnang / dad chu ma dang gong ma lnga bstod kyi lung / gdung phud du bla ma zhi khro dang / yar lam yar 'brog thar gling du kyai rdor rgyu
dbang tshar gnyis/ ngor tshogs chen la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang / thar rtser tshe dpag dkar po'i rjes gnang rnams byas song / de nas shab dang bo gdong sogs brgyud sa
skyar 'byor zhing / dga' ston gtang rag sogs byas te/ sa ga zla nang ban tshang par dam tshig bskang gso btsugs pa'i tshogs dbur nged gnyis nas phyin pas tshugs dgong gtso
gtor mdun rgyab bye nas zhig pa'i gtor dar mchod me'i khar lhung grub kyi me nyan kyang chen po byung 'dug kyang mtshan gang ma shes sang bskang gso 'tshog khar mchod
dpon la ti tshab lang 'dug kyang bya thabs ma byung zhing nged rnams bdag bskyed byed skabs gtor ma bye ba de

sbyor du bcug nas bskang ba byed dgos byung ba lo de'i ston bdag mo'i zhe gyong skor dang phyi lo nu bo de mi sdod pa'i ltas su 'dug snron zla nas chu stod zla nang bar nged
kyis tshe dpag lha dgu'i gzhi bsnyen sbyin bsreg bcas bgyis dus nu bo de tshogs dbur 'gro mu yin pas bde mchog sgrub mchod thog de gras gra gzhon zhig bud/ kyai rdor sgrub
mchod dang bstun rgyu dbang byed skabs dbang yol shor bas dkyil 'khor phyed tsam la skyon pa sogs mi dge ba'i ltas du ma byung/ de dus chu stod tshes bzhi'i dge tshar
'gro gong nged thun la yod thog rdo rje rgya gram gyi stan dang dngos po'i ster cha thogs nas ring 'tsho'i rten 'brel sgrig par slebs byung bas phyag 'tshal dang bcas smon
lam mang po zhig byas mthar khong rang gi rgyun 'don phreng ba nged la gtad nas dge tshar song bas ci yin nam snyam yang phyi lo zla tshes de la zhing rje rgyu yin 'dug
pas de'i brda ston 'dra mo byung / de nas gong dkar rdo rje 'chang chos dbang rgya mtshos bka' chos gnang ba'i mgo tshugs/ phur sgrub skabs tsam nas bzung bdag mos dbus
la gnyen phrad 'gro rgyur rnyed 'os min du mar nged rang spun nas bstun phyogs rang byas rung je lod du song / khrums zla nas ngos kyi klu sdings zhabs drung rin po cher

dbang lung khrid sogs ci nus 'bul skabs dang / gong dkar rje nas dpal rtse sogs yog dkyil chen mo rnamasakyi dbang bstsal ba'am spun lhan du thob/ de dus kyai rdor gzhi bsnyen
skyar rtsis kyi dam tshig rdor dril byin rlabs sogs de rang nas bgyis shing mgon khang bzhir phrin 'chol rim gro sogs sngon 'gro'i 'cham la 'jug gong bdag mor phral phugs
kyi gleng 'os tshang ma byas tshod yin kyang dag pa ster ba zhig ma byung 'dug go /gang ltar 'dir nu bo des rgyun 'don rnams smos na/ lam zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi
nang / lam dus rgyas 'bring / bde mchog dril bu nang dkyil/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ 'jigs byed/ yang phur/ gur drag lcags sdong ma/ 'chi bdag 'jom pa/ gur bdun ma/ brag
rdzong ma/ kyai rdor/ bde mchog gur zhal sogs gtor bsngo chen mo bzhin/ dkar cha bzhi/ dbyug gu chang bu/ dzam dmar srog sgrub chu sbyin/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin bsreg
na ro mkha' spyod dang tshe dpag med ma gtogs gdan sa'i sgrub dkyil tshang ma rgyugs shing/ shing khyi nas me byi khrums zla bar nyin ltar satstsha dri med snying po can
bcu gcig re/ lcags lugs lo tsam nas gtor ma brgya rtsa/ chab klu/ 'byung gzhi lan gtor rnams zla rer gang 'grub re/ lcags rta nas bzung rnam sras

dus gtor/ brgyad bcu bzhi/ nyer gsum/ nyer drug nas gnam gang bar gyi dus gtor phyag len bzhin 'don cha dbyangs rol tshang ma/ nye lngar gur drag phrin gzhung / kha 'don de
rnams kyi gtso bo kyai phur gur drag rang yin zhing / khyad par gur drag ni byis pa'i dus klog me shes gong nas byed khul rang byed kyi yod pas skabs shing brag rtsa rdo
rje 'chang nas de'i dpal gtor phyag bzo ma zhig kyang gsol ras gnang ngo / /gzhan yang gong du bshad pa ltar gdan sa'i 'khur rags rim kyang byas pas gshin po du mar lam
ston dang chos 'chad sogs kyang phran bu byas/ yab yum sku drin can rnams las kyang ngos la mthong che bar byed cing / 'di phyi'i skyid sdug legs nyes gang byung yang nged
la re ba lta bu yin zhing nged rang nas kyang dbu 'don gang yong khul yin kyang long bas long ba khrid pa lta bu yong nyen yod 'dug de ltar rigs khyad can du skyes/ gzhon
nu nas dam pa'i mgon du ma dang mjal zhing / sangs rgyas bstan pa'i nying khu rje btsun sa skya pa'i bka' srol gdan sa bcas bzung chog pa 'di ni bdag cag spun gnyis nas
rnyeed pa'i mchog legs par brnyed pa zhig lags zhes 'phros don du bkod nas/ gong gi 'phros de nas me khyi khrums zla'i nyer gsum nas gzhi

bsnyen la 'dug thun tshang mar 'jur zhing thun mtshams rnams su rgyun 'don rnams kyang ma chag par byed mu nas dbyug zla'i tshes mgor bdag mos dbus la log phyin pa'i rkyen
byas thog mar srog rlung 'dra mos bde ba nas rim bzhin lus mi bde ba bstud mar byung yang snying rus kyi 'tsham hur theg byas shing / nged rang ni chos 'chad dang brel ba
char 'phar mang thog bdag mo'i skor la 'khrun gcod sna tshogs byed dgos dang rim gro'i bkod pa sogs la g.yeng mu nas dus mdos phrin 'chol tshugs pa'i nang sa'i phrin 'chol
grub nas rta mgrin yang gsang dbang sgrub bgyid skabs sa skya tshogs kyi dar chen la rlung gnon sgrog theg 'dogs mi dar chen logs nas lhung pa'i tshe'i dus byas par tshang
ma ya nga zhing rnam rtog za ba zhig byung bas rjes su bsam tshe/ me glang lo'i dpyid rgyal ba rin po che dang dbyar nu bo de zhing brje ba'i ltas su 'dug cing / de'i
rgyal zla'i nang tsam la yin tshod kyi gang ltar dbu rtser ngos spun gyi rgyun tsha rnams la bla ma ngag dbang lags nas rab gnas brgyad tshar mdzad skabs nyin gcig 'jam
dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i spyan gnyis nas chab babs pa'ang me shes pa'i ltas yin 'dug cing / dgun thog der bsnyen pa'i sgang pha lam lus sems me bde bzhin du phyogs/

rta zla'i nang tsam la ngor bas 'jigs byed drug bcu sogs dang / gong dkar dpon slob rin po ches kyang gtor bzlog du ma gnang / me glang dbo zla'i tshes bzhir rgyal ba rin po
che chos dbyings su thim tshul bzhes pa'i dgongs rdzogs 'bul bar mdzod pa lha sar thon/ ngos kyis bde kyai gsang gsum sogs kyi sgrub mchod dgongs rdzogs su btang / klu
sdings zhabs drung rin po che zhabs 'bam gyi snyun lci mo bzhes pas 'di nas ngor du 'do ler spyan 'dren zhus/ de'i zla bskyed tsam la gang nas 'ong med pa'i bum med sprul
gzugs 'dra mo lung pa du ma'i mi nor ngo shes pa zhig kyang byung bas dus rtags lta bu yin 'dra/ mdzod pa dbus nas 'khor nyer nu bo der chu bsags kyi mgo zug bye rdzing
tshogs nas sku brten pa 'byor/ nag zla'i nyer gcig srod 'od zer la rlung log gi nad mthu mo srog la 'bab nye byung / de sngon nas bla ma dam pa du ma dang chos skyong kha
shas mo brtag rtsis sogs la babs pa'i rkyen sel tshe dbang rjes gnang sogs gang dgos nged rang nas bgyis shing / tshe chog gtor ma'i rigs bka' bstan sogs gsung sgrogs/ mdos
dang / gtor bzlog bskang ba sbyin bsreg satstsha sogs sgrub 'os rnams chos grwa lho byang ngor chos lhun zha lu sogs dgon pa kha shas su zhus shing sngags

bon rtsis sogs kyi gto bcos gang dgos bcas 'bad sgrub bgyis kyang tshang ma ma dran zhing sgrub tho rnams kyang de tsho de dus la dag pas khra gzhi'ang med/ mdzod pa dang bye
tshogs pa slebs 'phral lha khang rtser ngos 'gro'i sku gsol thog lung nan zhu byas pas rbad gtong gi cho 'phrul yin tshul gyi 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gi gsung
brtag nang bzhin bgyis thus bcas byung mthar phan gnod kyi gsal gang yang med par phad bu zhig tu lcags slang / gser/ kha btags/ zas sna bcug mda' dar gyi g.yab re gnyis
mdzad mthar gong gi gshom rnams zhabs 'og tu mnan zhags pas bcings te brag chung gi rir gnon la de khar mchod rten byiin can zhog zhes dang / yang nam mkhar yul gyi gzigs
te lam gyi bzhi mdor lha babs mchod rten bzhengs/ gzim chung gtso bo'i shar lhor rgyal mtshan dkar po 'od ldan 'tshugs gsung srog skyon yong min nges sbyar zhus kyang lan
med par yal song bas gang yiin nam zer bzhin rim gro rnams ni byas phad bu gshom bcas kyi don ni ma go rgyal mtshan dkar po 'dzugs rgyu de nged rang gzims shar na sdod
skabs yin pas gzim chung gtso bo yin khul byas nas zla bo tshos de'i thog kha'i shar lhor btsugs 'dug pa 'gyang min nas skya chas su 'gro bar

brtags shing / mchod rten g.yul thang gsham gyi 'di yin pas lha bab ni ma 'ong pa na rigs brgyud 'byung bar brtag pas bye tshogs chos skyong gi lung gsal po yin 'dra/ de nas
sa ga'i tshes 'gor mtshams grol shing sbyin bsreg ni ma thub/ nged rang nas tshe chog brgya tshar bsog dbu tshugs khams la bde bskyed med pas mtshams khang dog skyon gyi
bcos byed mi bde bas g.yab shar du sdod gnas kyi sman zas spyod tshang mar brtson pa bskyed kyang phan ngo len pa ni ma byung bas zhal ngor/ chos grwa lho byang drung 'khor
ser skya 'bul sdud tshong khag ser mi ser sogs spyi sger nas brtan bzhugs stobs pa mang zhing phyogs nas kyang 'ga' yar byung yang phan tshun bsun pa las rgyu mtshan
gzhan mi 'dug/ skabs shig nged rang gi rmi stas su sger rum bse mgon chen po yin snyam pa'i mgon po'i zhal 'bag sngo thal char lhags kyi brdung pa 'dra ba zhig ltag sgo
rdo skas mgor gzhan la 'gro tshul du 'dug pas sems khral dpe med byas pa zhig dang / yang lan cig bse mgon bzhugs khyim na mal lo'i thugs dam ma yin zer ba'i rus krang gzi
brjid can zhig 'dug pas da bse mgon ma bzhugs pa'i tshab yin 'dra bsam pa zhig dang / yang lan cig

nu bo de dang lag sbrel byas nas 'gro yi 'dug pas skye ba de'i rnam pa med par byis pa loo lnga'i tshod tsam zhig 'dug pa'i mthar rgya dkar nag lha khang gi thog khri zhig
bzhag song bar mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi skur 'gyur/ yang lan cig chos dung nu bo des bzung 'dug par 'jim rlon bzhin zhig pa sogs rmi lam ngan pa btud cing / de
rang la bsnyen pa'i skabs rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i gras dran pa nam mkha'i skye ba yin khul gyi gter zhig ston song bar gro kha dang dar dmar la gter chos dhA ki dhA ki zer
ba'i glegs bam bsnyed pa rmis shing / yang lan cig khog nang na byis pa mche ba skya zing nge ba zhig skye grabs yod bsam pa dang / yang lan cig thun gyi sgang la spyi
bo nas rang sems kyai rdor yab yum gyi rnam pa mtho gang tsam zhig rlangs pa bun ne thon nyams byung bas skyo lhang lhang byung zer zhing da nged gcong can 'di'i gdung gi
go sa mi yong bas gang ci'i mtshams la bla ma rin po che rang thugs bsam che bskyed mdzad dgos zhes sa skya pa'i gdung 'dzin kyang nged la bcol zhing / skabs 'gar sman
dang rim 'gro sogs kyi dga' mo yong 'gro zhes sems gso'i tshul byas na/ lan du zla ba brgyad par dri med rnam gnyis mi 'khrugs pa'i gsung chog rnams gtong rogs mdzod zer/

gang ltar yang skyed yong re bral yang re ba kho nas 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong mchod gnas su spyan drangs pas dbang rjes gnang sogs dang 'chi blu 'phrin 'chol zhal bkod
gang la gang 'tshams sogs nyin mtshan rtag 'grus 'dra mo bka' drin bskyang / gsung brtag yang skyar zhus par nu bo der rim gro phran tsam mdzad nas 'u gu 'di bas sku zhabs
gcen gyi zhabs brtan sku rim la brtson dgos 'dug go zhes nu bo de mi 'tsho ba dang nged la rkyen sel dgos pa'i lung gsal de 'dra stsal yang ha ma go bas/ gzhan nas ci
gsung gcung rin po cher gsung rtag zhus na gcen por sku rim mdzod gsung ba ya mtshan zhes sgrogs/ 'jam mgon de nyid lan cig khyad 'phags byang du gsung bskang la byon dus
mgon khang du phebs ma thag chos skyong rnams la bka' skyon 'dra mor sngags 'chang ya gi'i sku lus la dngas bskyed bzhes pa zhig dgos rgyu yin kyang ma byung bas khyed
rnams bag zas pa la'ang ngo ma tsha'i gsung pas sku mdun pa rnams 'jigs zhum pa zhig byung zhes thos nged rang nas rkyen sel mang du byas/ de rnams nang nas phyag rdor u
tsaraya'i rjes gnang byas dus sha pags kyi hrag la tsha khyug du ma byung zer/ mkha' 'gro bsu zlog zhu ba mkha' 'gro ma rnams mtshon byed 'jim gzugs lha mo mdog dang lag
cha

sna tshogs 'dziin pa rnams yol ba'i phyir bzhag nas dmigs pa brtan pos zhu ba lan rnams nged rang nas byas pa'i rdzong chog byas pas bsu ba rnams phyir log pa'i mtshan ma mus
chen bsod nams dpal bzang la shar bas da sku dngas skyed bzhes thub tsam e yong gsungs shing gdugs dkar byed 'grol sogs mdzad/ zha lu nas bla grwa nyi shu lhag tsam la
byon zhus pa'i bu lugs bzlog chen bzhi/ tshe chog don yod zhags pa'i gzung chog sogs rim gro 'ga' re zhus dus kho bo'i bla ma ye shes grags pa de nyid kyis slob dpon mdzad
pas gdugs dkar mdos chen 'phen rgyu'i sngo dro khrag rlung bsnyun thu mos stems pas/ da mdos 'di tshar bar ma shi tsam byung na de nas shi yang bla gsung ba sogs 'tshub
nyam rang byung / rnam grong rdo rje 'chang nas kyang tshe bka' sogs bstsal te nged rang tshor sems las srung thabs dga' mo yong rgyu'i khul mdzad kyang thugs kyi tshar
gzhi dngos ni mi 'tsho ba khoo nar dgongs pa'i dbus la 'phral du phebs dgos tshul nan stsol bzhin zhus pas snron zla'i mjug la gong dkar du phebs skabs gsung las kho bos
rjes su gdan sa'i sku gegs thams cad 'brang nas 'dir thugs phan thogs pa zhig byung na de ka 'bad gsung ba sogs ma 'ong mkhyen pa'i lung bcas phral phebs

bka' drin skyang / bde mchog nas a lce mched byon na gsungs par ngos kyi rgyang tsam ma byon par ston ka tsam byon pas mthus byas pa yin zhes 'phros pas ston dgug long mi yong
zer/ nged kyang de skabs chu tshan ston dpyid gnyis chag med byed dgos yod kyang dpyid chu 'gyang zhing gtar kha'ang de lo nas bzung ji srid 'tsho'i bar mi rung zhes
'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong nas gsung pas chu gtar ka med par phur sgrub 'gan blang na rkang nad yong tshul sman pa rnams nas zer bas chu stod zla nang kha'u chu tshan
la 'gro rgyu'i nyer bsdogs tshang ma grub pa'i de'i tshes lnga'i nyin 'gro shag yin kyang gdang ma khel bas tshes bzhi'i nyin zhal dkar dkon mchog rgyal mtshan la gang
ci'i mtshams zhib dris kyi bcos sogs sngar mu bzhin gang la gang 'tshams byed grogs dang ma nges pa'i ya yud byung tshe sangs rgyas 'phel gdung rje btsun gong ma'i byin phye
'di rnams zhu thub pa zhig dang gang ci'i 'tshams la khyab che mdzod byas pas da nang phyag rtsa ha cang gdeng khel zhig mi 'dug pas da lam chab tshan bshol ba gnang
na zer/ 'on kyang ring bsrel sogs zhal dkar bar bskur nas nged rang yang de'i drung du phyin pas zla bo zi kholakhol dang rgyal tshing mchi ma 'don zhing 'dug pas zhal dkar
bas 'phel

gdung sogs gtad byung ba bzhin byin/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong spyan 'dren zhus pas ljags dbugs hal zhing shar rgyus su byon nas spyan chab nyil mdzad de da sku zhabs
rin po che rang 'dir ma bzhugs shig khyed zhabs phyi zhig nas rje btsun gong ma yi dam lha tshogs bcas la gsol ba rtse gcig 'debs par zhu zhus gsungs pa bzhin byed mu nas
mya ngan las 'das/ nged rang ni rkyen sel rim gro sman zas spyod de tsam byas kyang ngo mi lta ba snyam pa'i zhe sdang nag thom pa las sems khral yang ma byung / de nas
nged rang gi nang du log ste tshig pa za hrug ge bsdad pas 'od zer sogs zla bo rnams nas sems gso byed khul dang dgongs rdzogs skor zhal bkod rnams rim zhu zhus chog pa
dang de nyid kyi sku bstod zhig kyang byung na zer bzhin de ring mang ja zhig dang gzhan rnams 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong sogs la zhu rtsis yin cing gsol 'debs da lta
'ong byas/ 'gro la rjes brtse ma 'di blo la thogs med 'char 'dug pas gang dran de rang brtsams/ de'i tshig ris la kye ma thub dbang bstan pa'i sogs sho lo ka gcig ni lo
de'i dpyid gong sa rin po che gshegs pa sogs bstan 'dzin gzhan gshegs pa'ang dran pa'i tshig yin/

de nas dar tsam zhig nas 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong spyan chab gnang ba tsam gyi gsung 'dar bzhin du de ring bdag sogs gdul bya kun gyi bsod nams dus gcig zad pa'i gnas
tshul ngan pa de 'dra mthong byung bas/ da cha skyabs mgon dam pa nyid zhabs pad yun bzhugs kyi dgongs pa g.yel med nas bstan don la rgya tshang mar thugs bskyed zab sgron
zhu dgos la'ang rim bzhin gsan bzhes thugs rje che dgos zhes dngos po'i gsol ras phyag 'tshal du ma bcas gnang byung bas spyir bdag rang bsod nams dman pas gzhon nu nas
yab rje rdo rje 'chang gshegs gdan sa'i khur mi yong bzhiin du bab/ bar skabs su ya hud yong la khad kyi gnas tshul du ma'a'ang byung / khyad par nu bo de bdag rang la
khri zhing gdan sa 'dzin par med ka med rang yin kyang / sdod ring lus gcong zhing da lo nad yun ring por gang yang thus ma shor ba bskyang khul dang khyad par sku zhabs
nyid nas thugs brtson de tsam bka' drin skyang song yang gegs chags bzlog med kyi snang tshul 'dir bdag ni tshig pa za rang drags kyang bya thabs mi 'dug pas sku zhabs nas
de lta'i thugs ngal mi bzhes par phral yun gang cir 'di nas kyang zhu cha mang du mchis pas/ de bzhin thugs 'khur che bzhes zhu zhus

pas thugs gso lta bur gyur nas gnas skabs kyi gsung 'phros dum tsam byung / de dus drug pa tshes bzhi'i dge tsha nyi ma phyed yol la grol skabs yin pas mang ja'ang de tsam
la yong tshod yin/ de nub nas bzung 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gi spur drung thugs dam gsol 'debs sogs dang dus mtha'i zhal bkod tshang ma gnang/ nged rang nas kyang
rgyun 'don phal cher skabs kyang rtsis gang zin dang khyad par tshes lnga nas kyai rdor sgrub mchod tshugs/ gzhung nas tshes drug bdun rnams la mang ja gnyis re de nas zhag
bzhi'i bar mang ja re/ yang tshes nas bdun zhag gsum ring chos grwa lho byang dge 'dun drug cu re bdun tsam gyi kun rig sgrub mchod nyin gsum la cho ga tshar gnyis re
'jam ja/ thud/ mar rgyar/ bur mar/ tsam nas sogs kyi gtong sgo dang yon dngul 'gyed bcas/ yang tshes lnga nas ban tshang pas kyai rdor sgrub mchod dang chos grwa lho nas
nyin re bzhin grwa mang nyung sna tshogs bzang spyod 'bum bsog gi dbu tshugs/ zhag gsum bar thugs dam khul dang de nas grol rtags je gsal du song bas 'jam mgon dpal ldan
chos skyong mus chen bla ma ngag dbang rnams nas gsung chog bcas tshes bdun la spur chas zhal bkod

gad gtsang spur zhu'i gnas kha shas sngar nas rtag sgril byas par phun tshogs gling tshoms chen thon pa bzhin der spur zhu'i bca' sgrigs nged rang nas brag rtsa rje'i dgongs
rdzogs 'char can bgyis/ tshes brgyad snga dro mchod phreng rgyas pas spur khyer bas phun gling sgo 'phyor du nye bskor skya ser tshang ma'i 'dod pa bzhin byin rlabs zhur
