mo bco lnga/ gur/ sam/ he ru ka'i yig brgya/ rig byed ma/ dus 'khor snying po/ nye snying / bde mchog yab yum gyi rtsa sngags/ snying po/ nye snying/ 'khor lo lnga'i lha
sngags/ go cha gnyis/ mkha' spyod ma'i oM gsum ma/ 'khor lo bsgyur drug sangs rgyas thod pa/ ma hA ma ya/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ phur pa rtsa dum/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/
'jam rdor spyan gzigs/ gshed dmar/ dgra gdong 'jigs gsum/ rnam snang rgyu dra/ phyag rdor 'khor chen/ gtum po/ yo ga rdor dbyings/ sbyongs rgyud 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor
drug chos dbyings gsung dbang / khams gsum rnam rgyal/ dpal mchog de nyid 'dus pa'i yig brgya/ gdugs dkar/ rnam snang mngon byang/ a ra pa tsa lha lnga/ dpa' bo chig grub/
rgyal po rol pa/ yan lag med pa/ ngag gi rgyal po/ shes rab 'khor lo/ a ma ra Ni/ bcu gcig zhal/ sengge sgra/ sa bcu pa/ byang sems gzi brjid chen po/ 'od zer can/ sman
bla/ mi bskyod pa/ stobs po che/ phyag rdor gzungs ring / mi g.yo ba/ rnam 'joms rnams kyi sngags so so nas lnga

brgya bcu gsum re dang tshang ma gser bris gcig dmar po skor gsum/ nor rgyun tog gzungs nas 'byung ba'i 'bru nor 'phel ba'i gzung ste rgyud sde bzhi'i gzungs rags bsdus dang
/ khyad par gtsug nor rnam rgyal/ gtsug rdor dri med/ gsang ba ring bsrel/ byang chub rgyan 'bum/ rten 'brel snying po ste gzungs chen sde lngar grags pa dang / rab gnas
rgyud gzungs tshul khrims rnam dag srog shing brtan sngags/ rdor dbyings/ chos dbyings/ sngags dbyings/ tshe gzungs/ byams pa'i dam bcas/ sangs rgyas stong gi snying po/
mdzod bu nor bu/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yig brgya/ mtshams med sgrib sbyongs/ don yod grub pa'i gzungs/ shes snying dang sngags/ nam mkha' mdzod gzungs rnams so so nas lnga
stong chig brgya nga gcig dang gser bris re/ rig phug 'dod gsol du ma/ gsang 'dus/ 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar/ rta mgrin skyer sgang / drag mthing / drag dmar/ phur pa/ yang
dag rig byed ma/ mkha' spyod ma/ bde mchog dus 'khor/ kyai rdor gyi sku rnams sdoms dgu stong nyis brgya zhe bdun/ de nas bum thog bre nang du srog shing la zhal phyogs
shing 'khor mor bzhugs pa yab rje rdo rje 'chang dang brag rtsa rdo rje

'chang gnyis 'jim sku/ kyai rdor li sku/ bde mchog dang thub dbang gnyis klu 'jim/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i 'jim sku/ gu ru chos dbang gi gter bzhes gu ru'i sku/ birlba pa/ dkar
po rnam gsum/ kha che paN chen/ chos rje khu dbon/ bu ston rin po che/ rdo ring rin po che/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ ngor chen
dkon mchog lhun grub/ tshar chen rin po che/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs/ gzims shag chos rje ngag dbang rnam
rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis rnams kyis sku las/ kha che paN chen dang bu ston rin po che nas bzung so so'i phyag nas ma/
sngags 'chang chen po'i zhal thang chung ngu byin can/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi mgur 'bum sngags 'chang chen po'i phyag bris ma/ sangs rgyas 'od srung gi tshems
dum/ byangs sems chos 'phags dang chibs ngang pa gser ldan gyi tshems dum/ jo bo'i phyag tsha'i dum bu/ 'brog mi'i spur thal/ dam pa rgya gar gyi tshems/ rje btsun grags
pa'i gdung rus/ sa paN spur thal dbon ston skyer sgang pa'i spur rus/ theg chen spur sha 'jam dbyangs

nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyi spur rus/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po'i spur rus spur thal/ rgyal tshab zhun thigs/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge'i spur rus/ mus chen sangs rgyas
rin chen gyi spur rus/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags kyi spur tsha/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi spur spos/ sangs rgyas sengge'i spur thal/ tshar chen dbu thod dum/
sngags 'chang chen po'i zhun thigs chab ser ril bu/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i spur rus/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho'i dbu thod dum/ gzhon nu blo gros kyi spur tsha/ grags
blo ba'i spur rus chab ser ril bu/ dkon mchog dpal ldan gyi spur rus/ shes rab 'byung gnas kyi spur rus/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang sgar chen gnyis kyi dbu thod
dum/ klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i spur rus/ ngag dbang chos grags kyi gdung thal/ a mes zhabs kyi thugs dum gdung rus/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyi gdung rus/ ngag dbang
rnam rgyal gyi dbu thod dum/ bsod nams dbang phyug gi gdung rus/ bstan pa rab rgyas kyi tshems ring bsrel can gyi dum bu/ bzang po rgyal mtshan gyi gdung rus/ sngag 'chang
kun dga' bkra shis kyi gdung rus gdung thal/ mtshal gtar ril bu/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi spur cha zegs 'dam rnams

dang / yang rgyal po 'od zer go cha/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po yab sras/ 'u yug pa rig pa'i sengge/ ngor chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgyal tshab/ lha mchog 'phags chen/ sa lo/
dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga ngag chos/ bdag chen kun legs/ sngags 'chang yab sras/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ nam mkha' dpa' bzang / dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang
chos grags/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon bco brgyad chen moo khu dbon/ bzang po rgyal mtshan/ ka spe ba/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang rnams kyi dbu lo/ gzhan yang gong du bshad
pa'i bla ma de rnams kyi na bza'i dum bu/ gong ma lnga/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang/ sa lo/ spyan snga/ grol mchog tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ sngags 'chang yab sras gsum/ shes
rab 'byung gnas/ ngag chos/ rtse gdong khri chen khu dbon/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ tshul khrims dpal bzang/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang/ nged rang
spun bcas kyi bdud rtsi ril bu phon che ba/ thang stong rgyal por tshe dpag med kyi dngos su bstsal ba'i tshe ril/ mkhyen brtse'i skye bdun ril bu sogs skye bdun du ma/
jo bo'i phyag dpe phyag bris ma'i dum bu/ bla ma gong ma'i gtor skam sne 'dus/ 'jam dbyangs ril bu/ rten 'dam ril nar sogs/

ba so'i dbang bum byin can rnams/ chos 'khor nang yab rje rdo rje 'chang/ a mes zhabs sngags 'chang chen po/ tshar chen/ go ram rje/ rdo rje gdan pa/ rdzong pa kun rgyal/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang / gong ma lnga/ lo chen/ a ti sha birlbapa/ bo dhi sa twa/ padma 'byung gnas/ 'phags pa klu grub/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang gi sku bcas bsdoms chig
khri chig brgya don gcig dbu gzungs lam zab/ kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi/ bdag med ma/ gur/ sam/ dus 'khor sa lugs/ bde mchog lu nag dril gsum/ sa phur/ gsang 'dus 'phags
lugs/ 'jigs byed sa lugs/ kun rig a ra pa tsa lha lnga/ tshe dpag lha dgu/ sems bskyed dbu lugs/ so thar/ gur zhal rnams kyi bla brgyud mtshan byang dang/ sa skya'i gdung
rabs rnams brgya bcu gsum dang/ gser bris tshar gcig steng grub chen brgyad cu/ yang dag sa lugs/ dri med rnam gnyis kyi brgyud pa rnams bzhugs pa'i rtser sangs rgyas ring
bsrel nged rang gi lag babs bco lnga/ de skabs phral 'byor nyer lnga/ khyung po'i thugs byon ring bsrel gsum/ gtsug gtor rnam rgyal gyi gzungs/ 'od zer dri med kyi gzungs/
mdo yug bris gdugs dkar sku gzungs 'khor lo rnams bzhugs par/ nged rang nas rgyal

mtshan 'dzugs chog rab gnas bsdus pa du ma rgyas pa kyai rdor dkyiil chog dang 'brel pa zhi rgyas sbyin sreg bcas bgyis dus shangs 'ba' ra sprul sku'i bum pa bcud can kha brgyan
can gyi thog drang dngos po'i skyes bcas ngos phrad la byon pa'ang mchod sdong drung du blang zhing / da 'u dpon don yod nas gser srang brgya'i 'bul ba'ang zhi ba'i
sbyin sreg thog 'grig pa sogs la nye bzang po de'i bum pa da lta tshogs chen rnam rgyal sogs la mdzad pa 'di yin cing / gser de las bum sgo'i gser sku rdo rje 'chang sogs
bzhengs/ dpon la kho bos dge bsnyen gyi sdoom pa 'phog ste kun dga' rgyal mtshan du btags/ ring 'tsho'i bden tshig rtsom bskul byung bas byon dang 'byon 'gyur sa skya'i
gdung rabs kun gyi zhabs brtan gsol 'debs bkra shis 'gyur med g.yung drung brtsams nas re zhig tshogs 'don la ma btsugs pa slar chu lug lo nas bton chog byung ba sogs dge
'bras phral du byung dra yang bying nge sdod pa kun gyi srol yin/ gang ltar gser dngul sogs kyi g.yogs ma grub pa'i shing 'bum de nyid la tshes dang gza' skar 'phrod dge
ba nas bzung thub bstan lha chen gyi gdan rabs nyer bzhi pa mkhan chen brtson 'grus ye shes kyi kyai rdor rab

gnas 'bring po brgya kha yar/ sa yos dpyid nas gser sku rdo rje 'chang gi bzo grwa tshugs/ rta zla'i nyis brtsegs kyi sngon ma'i bcu bdun la sde dger 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos
skyong gshegs/ de skabs snga dro nyi dros tsam la sa skya'i nam mkha' mthongs gang thams cad sprin kha dog lnga ldan sngar mthong ma myong bas gang / phyi ma'i bco brgyad
la nged rang gi lcam sngon ma 'das pa sogs sdug bsngal kun spung/ de'i dbyar lcam phyi ma len rgyu'i rim gro sogs bgyis/ de tsam nas bzung gong gi shing 'bum la gser
dngul phra brgyan gos yug skon sogs grub cing / gser sku rdo rje 'chang gi bzo tshugs pa khrum zla'i stod tsam la 'dril bas gzungs bzhugs kyi gtso bo gur ru rin po che'i
sku tshab gter lnga'i nang tshan bye ma a krong gi sku gu ru yab yum gyi byang sems dkar dmar 'dres shing phyag nas ma ring bsrel 'byon bzhin pa sde srid gtsang pa'i nang
rten gras 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i phyag babs de dang / gnyan phul byung ba gtsug tor rgyal po'i bzheng bar mdzad pa'i sa 'jam zhal sprod sa chen gyi phyag nas
brgya tshar dang rje btsun sku mched kyi phyag nas dang thugs dam rten byin can/ sngon gyi bla ma kha shas kyi mngon rtogs mus srad pas 'dri bar mdzad pa de'ang 'di la

gzigs nas yin 'dug pas de lta'i bris de gong gsham zhal khebs bcas bzhengs stabs nar mor sgril ba srog shing dang lhan cig sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung lnga rnams kyi thog drang
ring bsrel rnam bzhi grangs mang nyung tsam ma gtogs mchod sdong nyid dang cha 'dra bzhugs par rab gnas tshar kha shas bgyis te/ bum sgor bzhugs pa 'di yang gdan sa
chen po'i gdung brgyud rgyun mi chad pa 'byung ba'i rten 'brel du zung 'jug gi rnam pa can dang thar thug kha sbyor yan lag bdun ldan rdo rje theg pa'i 'bras bu sems can
kun la stsol ba mtshon byed du bzhengs te khrum zla'i gza' skar dge ba nas bzung 'thor nas sgrub cing nged rang gi rdo rje slob dpon dang mkhan chen bde chen gling pa tshogs
yongs kyi kye rdo rje'i dkyil chog dang rjes 'brel rab gnas zhag bdun ma rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg 'o thog sgrub pa rnam lnga'i mchod pa gtsug lag khang rnams su 'bul ba
dge 'dun bsnyen bkur mchod phreng phyi skor me tog 'thor ba phan sku zhal dbye/ ston mo'i thog spyi sger legs skyes len pa/ bzo par ster cha/ zhal sogs cha lag dang zhi ba'i
sbyin sreg mnga' zhabs la 'bru 'gyed bcas rgyas par bsgrubs pa'i rten 'di nyid la mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur gyi tshul du gser sku rdo rje 'chang la dar gyi na bza' dang
/ rin po che'i

rdo shal/ mchod rten gdugs 'khor 'og nas 'phyang ba'i dril bu/ bzang gos spus legs kha dog sna tshogs yug bco brgyad kyi na gza'/ bkral btags kyi bla re/ mchod khri gser shog
ma'i steng theg chen gan dril/ gshegs po'i rgyun bskul gan dkar/ dngul stegs/ bzed zhal/ phud phor/ si yang ho'i lcog rtse/ shel sngon gyi lhung bzed sogs shel dpyad sna
tshogs bco lnga/ yu ring rtags bcas nyi shu/ rdo dril bcu gnyis/ dngul gyi bya ma bum dang ldong mo cha/ zangs bum cha mgul 'ching kha brgyan bcas/ dngul srang lnga bcu
ma'i ting 'gag gzugs ma bcu gcig rnams dang / de nas mdo zur sbug dang pha sgar sogs su mchod rdzas dkar dpyad don gnyer bgyis par sbyin bdag dad can rnams kyi phul gras
la dkar yol gyi lhung bzed gcig me dam kha dog mi 'dra ba che chung sna tshogs spus legs nyer brgyad/ dkar yol yu thung che chung sna tshogs nga gsum/ gu sha'i par bu sogs
bcu gnyis/ dkar seng khyi sogs bco lnga/ ne tso'i gzugs bcu/ rgya mi/ spre'u/ sbal gzugs sogs bcu gnyis/ rgyu sna tshogs las grub pa'i me tog phon bcas lcags 'brug lo
nang 'byor ba bzhin slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ chos rje khu dbon 'jam mgon a mes

zhabs sogs kyi dus chen 'go zla'i bcu gnyis zhabs skor la nged rang bzhi thog nas 'gro gdong khyer te mchod sdong drung du phul zhing smon lam btab bo/ /de ltar 'di skabs kyi
rnam thar gzhan las rjes sgrub skor spyi dang / mchod sdong gser sku bcas kyi lo rgyus zhib tsam bris pa ni gshegs po de la 'di dag cung ngo mtshar che ba yod pas dge
ba la rjes su yi rang bsam pa skye ba'i ched yin zhing / de las byung ba'i dge ba ni gzhan las khyad par 'phags pa zhig ste/ 'phags pa sdud pa las/ stong gsum ri rab srang
la gzhal ba'i tshad bzung rung / /rjes su yi rang dge ba de ni de lta min/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bus mtshon nus pas bstan 'gro'i don du 'di lta'i dge ba'i sems ma gyur 'gro
ba kun la skye bar gyur cig /ces tshig sgra legs po des sgro bkur dang bral ba'i lo rgyus drang por bshad nas/ de ltar bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid kyi rjes su
bzung ba'i spun rnams las drug pa'i lo rgyus mdor bsdus de bzhin dang / sras gsum pa kho bo cag ni tsandan sdong shul yor mos bzung ba'am/ rta lam bong bu'i 'gegs pa'am
mgrin bzang gzig lpags gyon pa lta bu ste/ de'i tshul ni 'di ltar ro/ /

ngag dbang rigs thig 'khon ston sa skya pa/ /kun mkhyen 'gro rnams dga' mdzad gdung rabs su/ /blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan zhes/ /ming snyan dpal ldan bzang
po thob gyur kyang / / 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum mkhas pa'i yon tan med/ /sgo gsum bag yod btsun pa'i khyur ma tshud/ /bstan 'gro'i re skong bzang po'i gras ma pher/ /lugs
gnyis blang dor gsal ba'i rnam gzhag bral/ /smin grol las byung grub pa'i sne ma zin/ /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug nor gyi phyug /nga rgyal phrag dog gzi 'od 'bar ba la/
/bstan 'dzin bla ma'i ming gog las kyi thogs/ /de phyir yang dag rtogs brjod bdag la med/ 'on kyang skyabs gnas dam pa'i thugs rje yis/ /dge 'bras da lta'i dal 'byor lus
rten 'di/ /'dzam gling bstan pa'i bdag po'i gdung du skyes/ /skyes tsam nyid nas 'dren mchog du ma mjal/ /mjal bar ma zad rgyas zab gsung bcud myong / /myong bas lhag bsam
dkar ba kho bo'i gshis/ /gshis lugs de ltar yin yang dad gshin dkor/ /dkor rdzas mi 'ju bzhin du dpa' nyams byed/ byed pa 'di 'dras nam zhig a tsa ma/ /ma gyur 'gro la
dkon mchog thugs rjes gzigs/ /gzigs pa ji bzhin rang mtshang 'di ltar

ro/ /zhes mdor bstan du bkod nas/ de yang thog ma'i dus 'di tsam nas yin zhes tshad bzung med pa zhig nas bdag gi sems rang bzhin 'od gsal shel khams 'dra mo de bzung 'dzin
khrul par a 'thas kyi las sna tshogs bsags pas tshon kha dog du mas bsgyur ba ltar mi dge ba'i 'bras bu ngan song gsum dang khyad par dmyar bar bskal pa du mar thar med
sdug bsngal drag po myong ba yang tshad med/ skabs 'gar dge ba'i 'bras bu mtho ris gsum dang khyad par mi yul du res 'ga' bla ma mkhan slob rab byung sngags pa sogs su skyes
nas chos dang mi mthun pa dang mthun pa'ang byas/ la lar rgyal po dang dpon sogs kha drag dbang chen du skyes nas mi dge ba dang dge ba'ang du ma byas/ de bzhin skyes
pa bud med rigs rus mtho min mang dag tu skyes nas phyug po don ldan don med sna tshogs dang / dbul po snyom chung dang gshed can rku jag pa'ang byas/ bum med kyi lus rten
yang bzang zhan byed spyod mi mtshungs pa dang/ res 'ga' btsun ma sdig can 'ga' rer chos tshul ldan pa sogs mtha' gcig miin pa'i skye ba bzo tshun rgyud du 'khor zhing
'khor ba las skye ba 'di'i sngon ma 'di nas yin zhes zhu rgyu med de kha sang byas pa de ring mi dran na gzhan dran pa lta ci smos/ 'on kyang

yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas kho bo'i ming la ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa blo gros zhes bstsal bas mi rnams kyis sgro btags nas grags blo ba'i sku skye yin zer yang
mi bden nam/ bden nges na grags blo ba'i bag chags yong rgyur 'dug kyang de'i dri tsam yang ma bro/ sgro mo lung pa mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel gyi sku skyer ngos 'dzin
byed cing rang yang de yin khul gyi gnas gsar rje'i rnam thar na'ang ham lab tshad med bris yod kyang kho bo sa spre snron zla'i tshes 'gor mngal bzung / dpon slob de
sa spre rgyal zla'i nang du gshegs pas sku skye yin min des ka shes bsam/ me lug nas sa spre'i bar dbus gtsang zing bun thog mi dang dud 'gro tshad med shi ba'i bar do yang
grangs med du ma zad/ 'bu gcig bur skye 'gyur gyi bar do'i sems can la'ang thug pa med pas de 'dra zhig nas dge ba'i bag chags sad pa dang dam pa de nyid kyi gdul bya
sras kyi gras su rjes su bzung ba dus la babs pa na go sa mthoon po 'di 'dra ru skye ba mngon sum tshad mas grub ste/ dper na srang dbar du 'khyams pa'i bya spu'am rtsa
dang sbun pa skye bo du ma'i rdog 'og tu 'grim zhing mi gtsang bas gos pa rnams kyang skabs 'gar rlung chen gyi mthon por bteg sgo glo dkar mthong khung sogs nas dkon mchog
gi rten

gral dang / rgyal po'i bzhugs khri sogs go sa gnyan po rnams 'grim pa dang khyad med dam snyam/ 'on kyang 'khon gyi gdung rabs dus gsum byon dang 'byon 'gyur gzhan ni skyes
bu dam pa phyag mchod kyi gnas yin pa la the tshom nam yang ma dgos/ nged rang gi skye lugs de ltar yin pa da lta'i kun spyod thams cad kyi gzigs pa 'di'i los mkhyen/ gang
ltar sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud 'byon dkar mor kho bo ma lags de nyid la 'khril bas thams cad gu dog sel thabs ni byung 'dug pas de dus ma lags de rang la mnal ltas ngo
mtshar mang po byung tshul shog ril rtse rgyong 'dra mo 'dri bar mdzad 'dug kyang bdag cag spun rnams la brtse gzigs tshad med/ bka' drin che khyun de'i rang mdangs 'gog
med 'grig 'grig mang po thugs bsam bzhes nas 'dri bar mdzad pa yin nam/ don la byung ba gang ltar na'ang lo rgyus de'i 'go na chu yos chu stod zla ba'i tshes lnga'i mnal
lam du/ sa skya nas mgron gnyer kun bzang dbang po yin zer ba'i rgyal lu chas la dar dmar thod can zhig nas gdan sar yong dgos zer ba la/ ci yin gsungs pas/ rigs gsum lha
khang sku gnyer byed dgos yin 'dug zer bas kho mos mchod gshom mi shes pas dgongs pa zhu grogs mdzod

gsungs pas/ de 'dra ma zer sngon nas bskos pa yin pas dgongs pa zhu re med zer phyag mdud dmar ljang dkar gsum phul byung bas gtsug lag khang de gang na yod gsungs par sgrol
ma'i gtsug lag khang gi steng na yod zer ba shar ba'i sang de gnyer tshang pa rnam sras nas 'gro mgon yab yum rnams la sras mo sa skyar 'byon dgos tshul zhus/ yang 'byon
grabs skabs mnal lam du ko cag gi jo bo sku rgyab zer ba'i ri de'i 'gram sher gling zam pa'i thad nas nor bu yin zer ba'i rdo ril kha dog mi 'dra ba gsum rnyed pas kho
mo 'gro ba'i gtsug lag khang der 'bul rgyu yong 'dra bsam sku phrag tu bsnams par shar bas rigs gsum lha khang sku gnyer mdzad dgos zer ba ni rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung
rabs la rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa 'byon par sngon gyi yi ge du ma na bshad 'dug pas gdung rabs de gras kho bo cag gdung gsum tsam skyed skal yod zer ba yin gyi rigs gsum
sprul pa 'byon zer ba ni min/ de bzhin nor bu kha dog mi 'dra ba gsum snyed pa'ang gdung tshe ring thung mi 'dra ba gsum yong ba'i brda yin 'dra bas gong du yab rje rdo
rje 'chang gi rnam thar na ma lags de rang la lkog gyur rjen gsal gyi mnal lam byung 'dug zhes smos pa de 'di yin/

dbus nas bsam yas chos skyong dang ra smad bse khrab chos skyong gi lung las yul dbus su mchod rten khang brtsegs dang jo dar btsugs pas gdung 'byung bar lung bstan pa bzhin
gong dkar dam pa blo gros dbang phyug gi sa dpyad gzigs pas sgrol ma lha khang dang jo mo thags ra gnyis yul dbus su 'dug pas mchod rten sgrol ma gtsug lag khang gi rgyab
dang / jo dar jo mo thags rar btsugs pas dar shing las yal ga khru gang tsam gsum skyes skad dang / sa spre dbo zla'i nang mnal lam du skyed lhas mgon khang yin snyam
zhig na shing leb la bram gzugs bla brgyud kyi mtshan zhal gyi sngags bcas 'dug pa sku srung du bcang ba dang/ yang lo de'i sa ga zla nang gzungs gra lnga thugs las bton
pa tshar gnyis byung ba ni kho bos 'di'i rig gtad thob nas sa skya'i gdung srid mtha'i bar du myur 'byon sku rim gra lnga sgrub mchod phyed nyis brgya rgal tsam blo thog
nas bton pa dang gtso mo lnga'i sgom bzlas rgyun ring rab byas shing 'di rnams kyis lugs sku khri rgyab can gtsug lag khang bcas 'grub pa dang par sku grangs mang 'grub pa'i
mnal lam gsal po yin 'dug pas rjes su yi rang zhing 'di skor gdan sa chen po 'dir nged rang shogs thon par yod/

yang gong dkar dam pa de nyid la so 'brang rjes gnang gsan nas/ de'i sgom bzlas zhag bdun bcad rgya'i thog nas mdzad pa'i mnal lam du bud med padma chos dpal gyi 'bras snye
gsum dang a ru ra rnam rgyal yin zer ba'i a ru mdzog tsam zhig phul nas 'bras snye'i 'phros mang mkhar mu khu lung nas yong zer de dang dus mtshungs gzim dpon bsod nams
mang mkhar chu zhor mu gu lung mjal bar phyin pa'i de nas gro snye rtsa ba gcig la snye phon gsum re yod pa sbar chag gang tsam phul 'dug pa 'di gsung ngag zab mo sloob bshad
yongs rjogs gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang las kho bos thob pa dang myong 'gyur gyi ltas shig yin 'dra/ yang lan cig lha khang rtse'i ga ya dhA ra'i bum chu'i drung na byon
mur bla ma mchod dpon yin snyam pa zhig nas bum chu 'di'i bdag po lha mo rig byed ma yin gsung par bud med dmar mo zhig gis chu zhig zhus pa dang / yang bum med zhig gis
a ma dgra lha ma'i yin zer ba'i ril dkar thum dang shel gyi mchod rten rgya phibs can gyi nang shel bum du rigs lnga'i bum chu yin zer ba zhig phul ba shar bas mnal lam
de gnyis kho bo rig byed ma'i chos skor la byang chub pa dang / dze TA ri'i lugs kyi tshe chog

grangs mang byed cing gdung sku mched sogs la 'di'i dbang mang po 'bul thub pa 'dir rtag pa 'dra zhing / yang rtag tsher gangs rtser phebs 'dug pas de na gur dkar nang khri
mthon po'i 'gram bum med mang po 'dug par/ khri 'dir su bzhugs kyi yod gsung pas 'dir bzhug mkhan phyi lo yong zer za btung mang po zhus gangs la dar lcog btsugs pa'i mnal
lam byung ba de ni kho bo rang la'ang sa yos dpyiid rmi ltas su rtag tsher gangs rtser slebs 'dug pas spang gshongs lhas ra 'dra mo na skyes bud med mang po glu gzhas
byed pa zhig byung bas de dang mthun zhing / gangs mchod gsar rtsom 'di yang de dus byas pa yin/ lo de'i ston khrum zla'i nang yab rje rdo rje 'chang kha'u chab la phebs
pa dang chabs cig skyed lhas mgon khang tu mtshams zhag bdun dang thug 'dzugs sogs gnang ba'i mtshan lam tu mchod rten zhig gi logs nas raksha gdong gcig mang po dang / dung
chung / rtse gsum rdo rje rnams phyag tu babs pa shar ba ni gong gi ma lags kyi mnal lam dang mthun pas ding sang mgon po 'di'i chos bskor tshang ma sngon gyi phyag len
dang mthun par thob pa kho bo tsam yin 'dug pas 'di kho na'i sku drin kyang khyer thabs ma mchis pas gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang de byang chub snying po'i bar du

bdag gi lus srog longs spyod kun gyi mchod nas dges pa chen pos rjes su 'dzin cing mgon de'i rnam thar bzang po skyong thub pa'i 'phrin las stobs 'phrog dbang pos mdzad du
gsol zhes shugs byung ngo / /yang go zla'i nang gong dkar dam pa de nyid kyis bu rdzi ma'i mdos 'dzugs gnang ba'i mtshan ltas su/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi spos snang dpal
dang / skal bzang sangs rgyas stong / rigs gsum mgon po'i sku rnams gser thang tu bzhengs pas gtung 'byung gsung pa bzhin phral bzhengs thang sku rnams da lta mkha' spyod
lha khang na bzhugs shing / de dus mdos kyi zas sna'i dkyil tu nas ljang mtho gang tsam thon/ yang mgon de'i rgyal zla'i nang btsun mo'i steng du ru mtshon 'dzugs chog
mdzad dus 'bras chang dgos gsung bar sngar btso myong med kyang khrung dpon phur pas ji 'dra yong ngam zer zhing btsos pas gnang dus nas chang bas ldab 'gyur gyi zhim pa
byung / yang zla ba de nang mnal lam du zha lu brgyan gong mgon khang na byon 'dug par bud med zhig gi bro sder gang nang dung chung gcig ba so'i brgya phreng dril bu g.yer
khas brgyan pa rus brgyan drug cha tshang zhig phul nas lte bsgyur yong bas gnyer gyis zer ba byung bas rten 'brel

khyad zha lu sku zhang la lte bsgyur 'khor lo zhu bar mdzad/ sa bya dbo zla'i nang yab rje rdo rje 'chang gis bzhi thog gzim shar mgon khang du chos skyong gtso bsdus la gdung
lus khril gegs med btsa' thub pa'i 'phrin 'chol bka' drin skyong skabs rdo rje rab brtan ma'i thang sku'i nu ma g.yas nas 'o ma byon 'dug pas mnal lam dang rtags mtshan
de ni kho bo la zhwa lu'i bag chag bsad rgyu 'dug pa bzhin der bzhugs sgrub dkyil 'gran med dpe hrul sus kyang nyams gso ma thub pa rnams sde dger par gyi mgo 'dren zhus
pa bzhin ring mo zhig nas tshang 'grig zha lur phul ba dang / dgon gnas khyad can de na gso sbyong sogs 'dul ba'i rnam gzhag la 'du skabs chos kyi gaNDi tshad ldan mi
'du pas gaNDi tshad ldan phul zhing phan 'gyur snyan sgron yang yang zhu ba sogs shugs byung gi byed pa 'di la blta ba 'dra/ sa bya nag zla sngon ma'i tshes bcu mchod pa
mdzad dus tshogs chang lud/ dpal gtor dngos grub tshul du rang gzhan gyis myang pas bu ram gyi ro 'dra ba byung gsung 'dug pa ni de dus ma zad phyis su nged rang dran gsos
nas tshes bcu'i mchod pa mdzad pa kha shas la'ang gtor ma'i ro bu ram 'dra ba nged kyis kyang myong shing tshogs chang lud pa lan gcig byung bsam/ de'i nam phyed

tsam nas btsa' ran grabs byung ba'i mnal lam du mi pho mo sna tshogs gzab 'phyor gyis sa skya'i phyi skor la 'gro zhing badzra gu ru rigs gsum mgon po'i gzungs rnams la rgyun
bzhin gdang byed mur ma lags de rang gzims yod snyam par padma chos dpal gyi phyag nas 'then cing yar bzhengs bcug nas da lam gyi bu chung 'di la bzang po mchog tu thogs
shig zer ba shar/ bcu gcig gi nyi shar spen skeg lang 'tsho sbyor thog btsas/ 'ja' dang me tog char byung gsung ba 'dug kyang / phyis su gzhan nas 'phros byed par de nyin
smad zhing la sa bon btab/ thal rlung che tsam byung zer bas kho bo de dus nas thal ba hur re skyes yod 'dug go /gang ltar de dus kyi mnal lam rnams la zla tshes bkod
pa'i shog ril de re zhig ma rnyed pas slar yang thugs dran gsos pa rnams 'dri bar mdzad 'dug cing/ phyis su shog ril sngon ma brnyed pas phal cher 'dra zhing re gnyis zla
tshes nor ba dang lo rgyus kyang mi 'dra bar mchis/ gzhan yang sku gsung thugs rten du ma gzigs tshul 'dug kyang 'dir ma bris so/ /mngal nas thon phral lce la dri bzang
phye mas dhIH par rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sin dkyil ltar btab/ srung ba dang zas gos g.yog sogs gces spras bka' drin rkyang zhing / yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas btang

rag sogs gang ci'i mtshams la bka' khyab thugs rje che yod 'gro yang nges pa zhig ma byung / byis pa chung ngu de gti mug shas che bas nyin mtshan phal cher gnyid byed cing
yan lag rkyang skum yang cher mi byed pas sha hrag rnams la rul g.ya' zug kyang ma lags sogs nye 'khor rnams bstod ra mdzad snying 'dod grags rdo rje 'chang gi bzhugs stangs
yin 'dug gleng/ 'dod chags shas che bas 'o ma bag med du 'thung dgos par ma lags de chab zho rgyas pa dang thug pas ngom med 'thung ste khar lud nas skya nyog ge sdod
pa'ang byung / zhe sdang shas chung 'dra bas ngu skad drag po mi 'don zhing shin tu nyan pa zhig yod 'dug pas bu rdzi rgan mo bkra shis rab mdzes des bla ma 'di'i skyid
du bcud zhes bsngags brjod byed/ legs so ster ba'ang byung yod 'gro yang phros mi 'dug mdzod pa bka' zhi ba de yon tan dga' mo yod 'dug pa kho bo'i ring 'tsho'i bden tshig
la snga ba ngag la dbang bsgyur ma rtsam 'dug spyir tshig sgra legs shing khyad par thugs kyi bzhed don 'gyur med zhabs brtan shog zer ba 'di nged la gzhan las rten 'brel
dge bar yin 'dug cing sbyar byang du'ang yin mdog gang yang ma byas par sa skya pa'i rje btsun gong ma'i zhal lung la dad pa thob pa skal bzang ser mo'i gral gsham du
'dud pa bdag gi rmongs

zhen gyi sgo nas phul zer ba 'dug pas snyom chung skyag po rang cig yin 'dug yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs yang yang stsol zhing lo ngo gnyis thog
tsam la yin nam smin byed dbang gi thog ma gsang 'dus 'phags lugs ras dkyil nas bka' drin skyang ste chos skyong gi rjes gnang yang kha shas bstsal yod 'dra/ 'on kyang rang
lugs rgyu dbang de bla med dkyil 'khor gang nas yin kyang rdul tshon dkyil steng nas thob dgos pas 'og tu 'chad pa bzhin no/ /de dus tsam la yin nam nged rang dran par
btsun mo'i thabs tshang sgo 'gag byang de nas shar gzigs la bla ma rab byung bgres po zhig gi dbang gnang ba'i dril lce la lag pa tham pa zhig dran pas phyis su rgyus yod
la dris par gong dkar dam pa de nyid yin 'dug zer yang yin min ma shes/ btsun mo'i steng gi g.yab theb chag de'i logs bris la lha sku mdog khra bo zhig mthong ba phyis
su khyung khra yin 'dug yang de dus nub phyogs la ljag kheb zhig yod pas de'i srub nas bltas pas mi gzugs phra ring khyom me ba lnga tsam gar byed pa mthong / gu ge chos
rgyal g.yul thang du bzhugs dus de e yin/ kho bo lo gnyis pa lcags khyi lo de hor dmag yong ngo yod 'dug kyang bod kyi sku rim spyi sger

gyis srung thub pa 'dra/ dus mdos zabs ma'i 'cham chas sgros gtsang 'di rnams thog mar gyon nas mdzad pa yin 'dug cing / de dus sam phur sgrub skabs gang la mthong ba yin kyang
kho bo bu rdzi'i rgyab la 'khur nas btsun mo'i thog steng byang de na yod dus lhas ra 'dra mo zhig na keng rus 'cham byed pa mthong ba ni dur khrod bdag po 'cham mdzad
pa de mthong ba yin nam/ yang 'cham sku yin bsam pa de 'dra lho gzugs la 'byon 'dug par gyon mi rnams kyi stag lham bsam yas chos skyong gi zhabs chags 'dra ba gyon 'dug
yang nang lho'i glo dkar de nas bltas skabs 'ga' rer khris kyi groong pa dbon po ba'i thong khung lho de na gra pa mgoo med zhig gul gul 'dug par mthong / lo gsum pa tsam
la yin nam gang ltar ma lags de snyung skabs zhig sku rim yin rgyu'i khul byas nas btsun mo'i thabs tshang de them pa shin tu tho bar yod pas de la stod nyang byas them
phyir ja shog ser po lingga yin pa'i lugs byas nas hU~M mdzad phyag rgya ma shes pas byang chub mchog rgyu 'dra mo bcas nas sangs rgyas kyi bka' bden pa dang zhes sogs
dgug gzhug gi rnam pa byas te shog bu blang nas thabs sgor sreg pa dran/ lus la gyon gos kyang dkar dmar las gzhan mi gyon khul byed par lan gcig phyu pa gzi khra bkon pas
ngus

nas gtan nas ma gyon/ gzhan chos dang mthun pa'i spyod pa 'di byas ni ma dran/ 'jig rten lugs la rig pa bkra bar yod pa nam mi tshos byed lugs ni/ kho 'di byed kho 'di byed
zhes lad mo byas pa rnams 'dra mo yod pa 'dra/ 'di 'dra'i mi dran dgu dran mkhyen pa zer ba mang po byung / de nas shu lum la song skor yab rje'i rnam thar du bshad pa ltar
yin zhing / de dus phun tshogs gling na ma lags bzhugs yod pa yin nam de'i g.yab tu byug sman spyi dang dres thag mer sbyangs thal ba skus pa tsha mo byung zhing rkang
lag zing zing sdud pa zhig dran/ de tsam la yin nam thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi rtse chen lha khang du gsung bskang gnang ba dang / bka' dbang zhig la rdor le mda' gzhu'i
'khor lo skor ba bya gsung pa dran pas 'jigs byed dug dbang gi bskur tshig zhig la rdo rje mda' gzhu'i zer ba 'dra ni med dam/ yang lan cig tshogs khang gral gdan mang
po zhig na khro 'bag ka bar sgrags pa mjal yang 'di yin nges mi 'dug yang lan cig nam zir yin bsam pa zhig la bu rdzi'i rgyab la khur/ ma lags dang a lce spun bcas gtsug
lag khang sgo shar ltas sgo steng na seng ge dang mdo na rdo chal dbus shing sdong yod cing 'dogs khyi skad lhang lhang byed pa zhig tu slebs byung ste su la'ang 'di yin
